MAT 1:1 Eneshi Ersa Mexihani xienrenlai niereni jilasan shu wo. Hheshi Iburaheimu, Dawudeni houdei wo.
MAT 1:2 Iburaheimude Isagheini oluwo. Isagheide Yagebuni oluwo. Yagebude Yuda, gaijiulaini oluwo.
MAT 1:3 TamaYudade Falesi, Xiela ghualai oluwo. Faleside Xisilunni oluwo. Xisilunde Lanni oluwo.
MAT 1:4 Lande Yaminadani oluwo. Yaminadade Nashunni oluwo. Nashunde Samenni oluwo.
MAT 1:5 LaheSamende Boasini oluwo. LudeBoaside Ebeideni oluwo. Ebeidede Yexini oluwo.
MAT 1:6 Yexide Dawude honshanni oluwo. Uliyani bierei Dawudede Sulumaneni oluwo.
MAT 1:7 Sulumanede Loboanni oluwo. Loboande Yabiyani oluwo. Yabiyade Yasani oluwo.
MAT 1:8 Yasade Yeshafani oluwo. Yeshafade Yelanni oluwo. Yelande Uxiyani oluwo.
MAT 1:9 Uxiyade Yetanni oluwo. Yetande Yahasini oluwo. Yahaside Xixijiani oluwo.
MAT 1:10 Xixijiade Manaxini oluwo. Manaxide Yamenni oluwo. Yamende Yexiyani oluwo.
MAT 1:11 Bexinlai Babilunde touzhi echikude Yexiyade Yegeniya, gaijiulani oluwo.
MAT 1:12 Touzhi Babilunde echidene Yegeniyade Salaqieni oluwo. Salaqiede Solobaboni oluwo.
MAT 1:13 Solobabode Yabiini oluwo. Yabiide Iliyajinni oluwo. Iliyajinde Yasoni oluwo.
MAT 1:14 Yasode Saduni oluwo. Sadude Yajinni oluwo. Yajinde Ilini oluwo.
MAT 1:15 Ilide Iliyasani oluwo. Iliyasade Madanni oluwo. Madande Yagebuni oluwo.
MAT 1:16 Yagebude Yusufuni oluwo. Yusufushi Mereiyenni zhanguiji wo. Mereiyen Mexiha giesan Ersai oluwo.
MAT 1:17 Ingiese Iburaheimuse Dawudeshi 14 dai wo. Dawudese bexinlai touzhi Babilunde echikude 14 dai wo. Touzhi Babilunde echidene Mexihashi 14 dai wo.
MAT 1:18 Ersa Mexihai olusan shiqinshi imutui wo. Hhei anai Mereiyenni Yusufude boluzho. Dou ese agikude Mereiyen Shenlinghala kewosi laiwo.
MAT 1:19 Hhei zhanguijini Yusufushi nie gou kun wo. Hhei minminji shizheghaku duran uwo. Qioqioji siraghane giezho.
MAT 1:20 Hhe zhen ene shiqinni sumulakude Ezhanni qienxien zhoujindei xienjighazhi kieliewo, "Dawudeni houdei Yusufu, chi bu ayidene Mereiyenni agizhi ire. Hhe Shenlinghala kewosi laiwo.
MAT 1:21 Hhe nie kewon olune. Niereini Ersa giezhi ogi. Hhe bexinlane zui dundase jiuine."
MAT 1:22 Ene shiqinla man fashen giekushi Ezhan xienzhini tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho,
MAT 1:23 "Nie ese dafalasan oqin kewon laizhi olune. Niereini Imaneili giene." Imaneilini isishi Huda matanre hhantu wo.
MAT 1:24 Yusufu xiereidene Ezhanni qienxien fenfulasan mutun biereii agizhi irewoma,
MAT 1:25 kewosi ese olutula ghuala hhantu ese kijiezho. Kewonni oludene hhende Ersa giezhi niere ogiwo.
MAT 2:1 Hherode honshan danlakude Ersai Yudayani Bolihende oluwo. Dunbangiese aghelitu kunla Yelusalende ire asawo,
MAT 2:2 "Olusan hhe nie Yutai kunni honshan khala wine? Bijien dunbangiese hodunyini chanladene hhei beiile irewo."
MAT 2:3 Hherode honshan enei sonosudene zhughedeni nanran uwo. Nie Yelusalenni kunladeye nanran uwo.
MAT 2:4 Ingie honshan bexinlai fugie buwa, jinwun hanjialai man uruzhi hhantulagha asazho, "Mexihani khala olune?"
MAT 2:5 Hhela kieliewo, "Yudayani Bolihende olune. Xienzhini shu jiere huaizho,
MAT 2:6 'Yuda oronni Bolihenya, chi Yudani chenshi dundase zui gani pusho. Mii bexin Isilieyi uduruchen nie lindao chii hhense khizhene.'"
MAT 2:7 Ingie Hherode aghelitu kunlai ghulazhi uru iredene hodun yan xienzide khizhesei xianxide asazho.
MAT 2:8 Ingiedene hhelai Bolihende peizhi echigha kieliewo, "Ta echidene xianxide hhe kewonni daqinla. Ereizhi oludene made kieliele ire. Biye hhei beiile echine."
MAT 2:9 Hhela honshanyi kielienyi chenliedene echiwo. Dunbangiese chanlasan hhe hodun hhelai melie yozho. Izhi hhe kewonyi qiorun qiende yozhi echi beiwo.
MAT 2:10 Hhela hodunni chanladene hende bayasuzho.
MAT 2:11 Giedoura orose kewonni, anaini Mereiyenyi chanlawo, papaladene hhe kewonni beiiwo. Boubei xiaxiane keighadene antan, xian, guizhuntu caoyeni mure ogiwo.
MAT 2:12 Huda aghelitu kunlai zhoujinde Hherodei ochirale bu echi giezhi mejieghase psedu mose goya orondene echiwo.
MAT 2:13 Hhela echidene Ezhanni qienxien Yusufui zhoujinde xienjizhi kieliewo, "Chi bosizhedene kewon, anaini uduruzhi Aijide piile echi. Bi fenfulatula hhende sou. Ene kewonni Hherode ereizhi alane giezho!"
MAT 2:14 Ingie Yusufu xienidei bosizhedene kewon, anaini uduruzhi Aijide echi
MAT 2:15 Hherode fugutula hhende souwo. Ingiekushi Ezhan xienzhii tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho, "Bi kewonne Aijise uruzhi khizhewo."
MAT 2:16 Aghelitu kunla piendasei Hherode mejiedene hende hokuzho. Ingiedene aghelitu kunlase hodun kaishi giezhi khizhesan shijienni mejiedene kun peizhi Bolihen chenshi pse zhouwidedu ghuase meilani kewonlai man alawo.
MAT 2:17 Ingiese Ezhan Yelimi xienzhii tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholuwo,
MAT 2:18 "Ramade nango giezhi hende wilasan shenqini sonosuwo. Lajie kesiladene oluzhi wilazho. Kesilani man widase sidaghazhi kieliesei ese chenliewo."
MAT 2:19 Hherode fugudene Ezhanyi qienxien Aijide Yusufuni zhoujinde xienjighazhi kieliewo,
MAT 2:20 "Chi bosizhedene kewosi, anaini uduruzhi Isilie oronde echi. Kewonni alane giesan kunla ijin fuguwo."
MAT 2:21 Ingie Yusufu bosizhedene kewosi, anaini uduruzhi Isilie oronde khareizhi irewo.
MAT 2:22 YajilaoHherode adane oronde Yudayani honshan danlasei Yusufu sonosudene hhende echikuse ayizho. Ingie zhoujindeni Ezhan mejieghase Jialili oronde echidene
MAT 2:23 Nasale giesan chenshide souwo. Ingiekushi Ezhan xienzhilai tungo giezhi, "Hhei Nasale kun giezhi urune." giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho.
MAT 3:1 Hhe xienzide xili gieghasan YaheiyaYudayani hontande khizhedene chonjizhi kieliewo,
MAT 3:2 "Ta geizhen giendu, asiman gojia chadashiwo!"
MAT 3:3 Eneshi Isaiya xienzhi kieliesan hhe kun wo. "Hontande nie kun waradazho. 'Ezhanni moni zhunbei gie! Hhei moni zhidagha!'"
MAT 3:4 Yaheiya loto noghosunghala giesan jienyi musizhi arasunni pixie pixieliezho. Hhe ijiesanshi machazi, shimei wo.
MAT 3:5 Yelusalen, Yudayani go oron, Yedanheni idou oronlade sousan kunla man Yaheiyai hhende echidene
MAT 3:6 zuine renjizhi Yedanhede Yaheiyase xili jienliezho.
MAT 3:7 Yaheiya olon Falisai kun, Sadugai kunla xili jienliele iresei chanladene kieliewo, "Du mogheini zhunzhughala, kien tande jianlai ireku Hudai hokukuse anda shidane giezhi kieliewo?
MAT 3:8 Ta geizhen giesanne giekughala zhenmin gie.
MAT 3:9 Iburaheimushi bijienyi xienren wo giezhi ta zhughedene bu sumula. Bi tande kielieye, Huda ene tashilani Iburaheimuni houdei gholugha shidane!
MAT 3:10 Ede sugiei mutun genzide teiwo. Gou alima ulie souku mutunlani man chizhidene khande teine.
MAT 3:11 Bi tai geizhen gieghane giezhi usughala xili gieghazhoma, mase khuina iresan kun mase nenli fugie wo. Bi hhende maheini qilaseye pei dane. Hhe Shenlin, khanghala tai xili gieghane.
MAT 3:12 Hhe khadene baqi bareizhi tughonni boudeii baqiliezhi agidene cankude zhonlone. Arasunlai ulie xinieku khande teine."
MAT 3:13 Hhe shihoude ErsaJialilise Yedanhede irezhi Yaheiyase xili jienliene giezho.
MAT 3:14 Yaheiya hhei danlazhi kieliewo, "Bi indan chase xilii jienliese oluzho. Chi matugie mase jienliele irewo?"
MAT 3:15 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi dain gie. Matan ingiezhi giedene gounilai man chenjighakui wo." Ingiese Yaheiya dain giewo.
MAT 3:16 Ersa xilii jienliedene dei ususe khizhekude asiman menzhali keizhi Hudai Ruhher ghoghochen mutun bouzhezhi goyai jiere luisei chanlawo.
MAT 3:17 Pse asiman jierese shenqi irezhi kieliewo, "Eneshi bi oresan kewon wo. Bi hhende xiqi wo."
MAT 4:1 Ingiedene Shenlin Ersai udurusenu hontande echise Ibilisi hhei shiizho.
MAT 4:2 Ersa 40 qiende xieni udu orozo bareidene oliesuzho.
MAT 4:3 Shiichen iredene Ersade kieliewo, "Chi Hudai kewon enbese enezighan tashii fenfulazhi ginan gholugha."
MAT 4:4 Ersa kieliewo, "Jinwun jiere huaizho, 'Kun amitushi zinie ginande ulie kouine. Hudai amanse khizhesan soyuji kieliende kouine.'"
MAT 4:5 Ingie Ibilisi Ersai uduruzhi zhiguitu chenshi Yelusalende echi mechii zui undu oronde beigha
MAT 4:6 kieliewo, "Chi Hudai kewon enbese jiuli bou. Jinwun jiere, 'Hhe chade oluzhi qienxienladene fenfulazhi khaghalani chii feizhi konnichii tashi jiere ulie mughughane.' giezhi huaizho."
MAT 4:7 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "'Ezhan Hudane bu shii.' giezhi jinwun jiereye huaizho."
MAT 4:8 Ibilisi pse hhei uduruzhi tebie undu ula jiere khireidene duyani soyuji gojia, pse gojialani henni man uzheghazhi
MAT 4:9 kieliewo, "Chi papalazhi mii beiise enelai man chade ogiye."
MAT 4:10 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Ibilisi, chi yola! Jinwun jiere huaizho, 'Zinie Ezhan Hudane beiizhi hhei shunji.'"
MAT 4:11 Ingie Ibilisi Ersase likai gie, qienxienla irezhi hhei ushilazho.
MAT 4:12 ErsaYaheiyai barei echisei mejiedene Jialilide khareiwo.
MAT 4:13 Khuinashi Jialilini Nasalese likai gie Jiabainunde echi souwo. Eneshi Xibulun, Nafutalidedu Jialilihaini kouisan oron wo.
MAT 4:14 Ingiekushi Ezhan Isaiya xienzhini tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho,
MAT 4:15 "Xibulun, Nafutalidedu kunla, haibienzini mo jiere, Yedanheni hhemiende niman kunlai Jialilide sousan kunla,
MAT 4:16 Hhe khara oronde sousan bexinla fugie gonni chanlawo. Fugusan oronde sousan kunlade gon zhouiwo."
MAT 4:17 Hhe shihouse kaishi giezhi Ersa chonjizhi kieliewo, "Ta geizhen giendu. Asiman gojia chadashiwo."
MAT 4:18 ErsaJialilihai bienzide yokude Beduru giesan Ximun, jiuni Andelie ghuala haide on xiaisei chanlawo. Hhelashi zhaghasun bareisan kun wo.
MAT 4:19 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta iredene mii dagha. Bi tai zhaghasun bareiku mutun kun bareichen gholughane."
MAT 4:20 Hhela onni deigo jiedene hhei daghawo.
MAT 4:21 Ersa hhense melie yodene pse gaijiu ghualai chanlawo. Hhelashi Xibitaini kewon Yagebu, Yagebui jiuni Yaheiya wo. Hhela adarene hhantu chon jiere on huduzho. Ersa hhelai uruse
MAT 4:22 hhela deigo chon, adasene likai gie hhei daghawo.
MAT 4:23 ErsaJialilini gochude man yozhi hhelai huitanlade sughazhi Hudai gojiai gouxioxini chonjizhi bexinlai yanyanji gien nouzhi giemeresanlai goudaghazho.
MAT 4:24 Ersai minshen Xiliyade man chonji kuruwo. Kunla yanyanji gientulai uduruzhi irese Ersa goudaghawo. Yanyanji giemerezhi tendun shouisan, sheitan heisan, yanjiofen nousan, tanhon giesanlai man ireghazho.
MAT 4:25 Tebieji olon kunla Jialili, Jijiapoli, Yelusalen, Yudaya, Yedanheni dunmiense hhei daghawo.
MAT 5:1 Ersa olon kunlai chujieghedene ulade khirei souwo. Tujilani melie irese
MAT 5:2 hhelade sughazhi kielie qiiwo.
MAT 5:3 "Zhughede nanxin kunlade fuqi wine, asiman gojiashi hhelanughun wo.
MAT 5:4 Nango giechen kunlade fuqi wine, hhelai sidaghazhi kieliene.
MAT 5:5 Goyane meilade uzhechen kunlade fuqi wine, hhela ghazhai jienliene.
MAT 5:6 Gundanni giene giezhi oliesuzhi undasuchen kunlade fuqi wine, hhelade kurughane.
MAT 5:7 Ubali xiichen kunlade fuqi wine, hhelade ubali xiine.
MAT 5:8 Zhughe ganjintu kunlade fuqi wine, hhela Hudai chujieghene.
MAT 5:9 Heqishighachen kunlade fuqi wine, hhelai Hudai kewosi giezhi urune.
MAT 5:10 Gundannide oluzhi heikui shouisan kunlade fuqi wine, asiman gojiashi hhelanughun wo."
MAT 5:11 "Mii yenyinghala kunla tai shizheghazhi, heizhi, shiheni doghunnighala ghudan kieliezhi tai sugiese tande fuqi wine.
MAT 5:12 Ta hende bayasundu, asiman jiere tande ogiku jianli fugie wo. Tanse melieshiku xienzhilaiye ingiezhi biizhi daozho."
MAT 5:13 "Tashi duyai dansun wo. Dansunde widao widase matugie koudaghane? Yamade inji dadene bendase kunla taine."
MAT 5:14 "Tashi duyai gon wo. Ula jiere beighasan chenshini niuigha dane.
MAT 5:15 Kun zhulai jienjise ighaghala ulie komorone, zhula teiku teizi jiere jiene. Ingiese nie gie kunlade gieghan wo.
MAT 5:16 Ingiezhi ta gonne kunlai melie zhouidene kunla ta goude giesei chanlazhi asiman jieredu adadene kuaikui ogigha."
MAT 5:17 "Bi irese guijin, xienzhilai shuni widaghane giekui ta bu sumula. Bi guijinni widaghale ese irezho, chengun olughale irezho.
MAT 5:18 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, asiman zemin widatula guijin jieredu nie jienjien nie bihuada ulie widazhi man chengun olune.
MAT 5:19 Ingiese kienliuzhe enezighan minlin jieredu zui ganii ulie zunjizhi kunlade ulie zunjise olune giezhi sughase asiman gojiade zui gani giezhi urune. Kienliuzhe minlinyi zunjizhi kunlade sughase asiman gojiade fugieni giezhi urune.
MAT 5:20 Bi tande kielieye, tai gouni jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlase ulie daose jiedui asiman gojiade oro dane."
MAT 5:21 "'Kun bu ala! Kun alase panjine.' giezhi eqighanku kunlade kieliesei ta chenliezhi daozhoma,
MAT 5:22 bi tande kielieye, gaijiudene hokuse panjine. Gaijiune, 'Guazi' giese zui fugie fayende lai echine. 'Yanhunzi' giezhi sugiese dozoheini khande orone.
MAT 5:23 Ingiese chi sidagha gieku teizi jiere mure ogikude gaijiuchii chade hokusei sumula irese
MAT 5:24 mureni sidagha gieku teizi konde jiesenu gaijiughalane xien goudadene mure ogile ire.
MAT 5:25 Chi duitoughalane zhale echikude mo jiere ghujighan hheghala gouda. Pse duitou chii panjiku noyende jiuise panjiku noyen chii gunnande jiuizhi bafanzide khane.
MAT 5:26 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, chi 1 fen baerniliuzhe honjizhi ulie qindaghase bafanzise khizhe dane."
MAT 5:27 "'Piofen bu gie.' giesan kielienyi ta chenliezhi daozhoma,
MAT 5:28 bi tande kielieye, biereini uzhezhi hu sumulase ijin zhughedeni piofen giewo.
MAT 5:29 Chii borun nudun chii zui fanjighase waidene benda. Chii beyese iyanzi widazhi beyechii man dozode orokuse gou wo!
MAT 5:30 Chii borun kha chii zui fanjighase chizhidene benda. Chii beyese iyanzi widazhi beyechii man dozode orokuse gou wo!"
MAT 5:31 "Pse, 'Biereine ulie kerese hhende lihun qiuzi ogikuni wo.' giezhi kieliezhoma,
MAT 5:32 bi tande kielieye, biereini lon kijieku yenyinse chugo lihun giese biereini piofen gieghazho. Pse lihun giesan biereini agisan kunye piofen giezho."
MAT 5:33 "Pse, 'Fayen giesanne bu fura. Ezhande fayen giesanne zunji.' giezhi eqighanku kunlade kieliesei ta chenliezhi daozhoma,
MAT 5:34 bi tande kielieye, yama fayen bu gie. Asimanyi zhiizhi fayen bu gie. Hheshi Hudai baozo wo.
MAT 5:35 Zeminyi zhiizhi fayen bu gie. Hheshi Ezhan kon teiku bandou wo. Yelusalenyi zhiizhi fayen bu gie. Hheshi fugie honshanni chenshi wo.
MAT 5:36 Qiorunne zhiizhi fayen bu gie. Chi qiorun jieredu nie ganzi usunne chighashigha dazhi kharalagha dane.
MAT 5:37 Tai kielien enbeneshi enbene gie, pushoshi pusho gie. Enense olon kieliese Ibilisinughun wo."
MAT 5:38 "'Nudunde nudun honji, shidunde shidun honji.' giesan kielienyi ta chenliezhi daozhoma,
MAT 5:39 bi tande kielieye, doghun kunlare zodui bu gie. Kunla borun khizhaichii eghise soghei khizhaneye eghigha.
MAT 5:40 Kunla chii zhazhi chii lizii jienni kerene giese mienzine jienniye ogi.
MAT 5:41 Kunla chii biizhi 1 li mo yoghase hhere hhantu 2 li mo yo.
MAT 5:42 Chii xiahua giezhi kerese ogi. Chase dunxi ghuise uwo giezhi bu kielie."
MAT 5:43 "'Ta giebeidene ore, duitoune henji.' giesan kielienyi chenliezhi daozhoma,
MAT 5:44 bi tande kielieye, duitoudene ore, tai heisanlade oluzhi onxian gie.
MAT 5:45 Ingiezhi giese ta asimanni Adadene kewosi danlane. Hhe naranne doghun kun, gou kunni jiere man zhouighazho. Ghurani gou kun, gou witu kunde man bouzheghazho.
MAT 5:46 Ta zinie tande oresan kunlade orese tande yan jianli ogine? Lien shui shanjisan kunlaye ingiezhi giene.
MAT 5:47 Ta zinie gaijiudene zhaohu daise kunlase giedun gou wo? Lien niman kunlaye ingiezhi giene.
MAT 5:48 Ingiese asiman jieredu Adatai onqien biku mutun taye onqienshi."
MAT 6:1 "Ta gouni giekude xioxin giezhi kunlai melie uzheghane giezhi bu gie. Qingiezhi giese asiman jieredu tai Adase yama jianli jienlie dane.
MAT 6:2 Chi nanxin kunlade ogikude jiazhon giesan kunla mutun bu gie. Hhela goyane kuaighane giezhi huitan, geidoude fugiede tunguliene. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, hhelade jianli ijin ogiwo.
MAT 6:3 Chi nanxin kunlade ogikude borun kha giesei soghei khade bu mejiegha.
MAT 6:4 Chi ogisanne kunlade bu mejiegha. Beichazide uzhesan Adachii tande jianli ogine."
MAT 6:5 "Ta onxian giekude jiazhon giesan kunla mutun bu gie. Hhela kunlade uzheghane giezhi huitan, shizilukoude beidene onxian giekude xiqi wo. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, hhelade jianli ijin ogiwo.
MAT 6:6 Ta onxian giekude giedera orodene wijienyi khadene beichazide bisan Adasene onxian gie. Beichazide uzhesan Adachii jianli ogine.
MAT 6:7 Ta onxian giekude niman kunla mutun touchan erchanji yama isi witu kielienyi bu kielie. Hhela sumulase ologhan kieliese chenliemu giezho.
MAT 6:8 Ta hhela mutun bu gie. Ta xiahua gieku melie ta yan keresei Adatai mejiene."
MAT 6:9 "Ingiese ta ingiezhi onxian gie, 'Asiman jieredu mai Ada, chi nierene zhiguishigha.
MAT 6:10 Chii gojiai iregha. Chi isine asiman jiere mutun zemin jiere chenjigha.
MAT 6:11 Niudunieku ijiuni enedu bijiende ogi.
MAT 6:12 Bijiende codasan kunlai bijien rouliesan mutun bijien codasei roulie.
MAT 6:13 Bijienyi shiikude bu echighazhi Ibilisii khase khizhegha. Gojia, qienli, famashi chanqi chinughun wo. Amine!'
MAT 6:14 Kunla codasei ta rouliese asiman jieredu Adataiye tai rouliene.
MAT 6:15 Kunla codasei ta ulie rouliese asiman jieredu Adataiye tai ulie rouliene."
MAT 6:16 "Ta orozo bareikude jiazhon giesan kunla mutun uxinne bu bougha. Hhela orozo bareisei kunlade mejieghane giezhi guyide ghuniraku yanzi khizheghane. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, hhelade jianli ijin ogiwo.
MAT 6:17 Chi orozo bareikude qiorunne sanlazhi nune waghadene
MAT 6:18 orozo bareisei kunlade bu chujiegheghazhi beichazide bisan Adadene uzhegha. Ingiese beichazide uzhesan Adachii chade jianli ogine."
MAT 6:19 "Goyadene oluzhi boubeini zemin jiere bu sunji. Zemin jiere ghughei ghazhazhi xiuqirane. Ghughei nudurun waizhi ghulane.
MAT 6:20 Boubeini asiman jiere sunji. Asiman jiere ghughei ghazha dane, ulie xiuqirane. Ghughei nudurun waizhi ghula dane.
MAT 6:21 Chii boubei khalashi zhughechiiye khala wo."
MAT 6:22 "Nudunchiishi beyeni zhula wo. Nudunchii goushi beyechii man gieghan wo.
MAT 6:23 Nudunchii gou wise beyechii man khara wo. Chii sudorodu gon kharashi hhe kharani zhengiejia fugie wo.
MAT 6:24 Kienliuzhe ghua ezhanni shunji dane. Ene niede henjise hhe niede orene. Ene niede gundushi hhe niede gongien wo. Ta Huda baer ghualai hhantu shunji dane."
MAT 6:25 "Ingiese bi tande kielieye, ta amindene oluzhi yan ijiene, ochine giezhi munan bu gie. Beyedene oluzhi yan musine giezhi munan bu gie. Amin ijiekuse zhunyo uwonu? Beye musikuse zhunyo uwonu?
MAT 6:26 Ta asiman jieredu bunzhulai nie sumula, hhela ulie tareine, ulie ghurane, cankude ulie sunjine, tai asiman jieredu ada hhelai qiezhene. Ta bunzhulase zhunyo uwonu?
MAT 6:27 Tani dunda kien zhughe chilakughala aminne niecha fududagha shidane?
MAT 6:28 Musikude yangiezhi munan giezho? Ta banche jieredu baihe chizhe matugie osisei nie sumula, hhela ulie khishilane, bosiye ulie giene.
MAT 6:29 Bi tande kielieye, Sulumane honshan zui henni xienzide musisanla ene nie chizhede ulie kurune.
MAT 6:30 Ta goude xianxin ulie giechen kunla, banche jieredu osun enedu wine, maghashijie luzide teiliuzhe Huda dou ingiezhi dabalaghazho. Tai qingie ulie gienu?
MAT 6:31 Ingiese, 'Ta yan ijiene? Yan ochine? Yan musine?' giezhi zhughe bu chila.
MAT 6:32 Enelashi man niman kunla xiahua giekuni wo. Asiman jieredu Adatai tande enezighan chaisanlai man mejiene.
MAT 6:33 Ta xien Hudai gojia, hhei gundanni xiahua gie, ingiese enelai man tande ogine.
MAT 6:34 Ingiese ta maghashijiekude munan bu gie. Maghashijiekude maghashijie munan giekui wine. Niuduku chijiani niudushi kuruzho."
MAT 7:1 "Ta kunlai bu kielie, pse taiye kieliene.
MAT 7:2 Ta kunlai matui kieliese taiye qingiezhi kieliene. Ta yanghala nanjizhi ogise tandeye yanghala nanjizhi ogine.
MAT 7:3 Chi yangiezhi gaijiune nudundedu osun zhazhai chanlane, goya nudundedu lianni chanla dane?
MAT 7:4 Chii nudunde lian bidene matui gaijiudene, 'Bi chini nudundedu osun zhazhai agiye.' giezhi kieliene?
MAT 7:5 Chi ene jiazhon giesan kun, xien goya nudundedu lianni agidene uzhezhi qinchu olusenu gaijiune nudundedu osun zhazhai agi."
MAT 7:6 "Zhiguitu dunxini nogheide bu ogi. Ochira daozhese tai zhoune. Manouni khigheini melie bu tei. Khigheila manouni taine."
MAT 7:7 "Ta xiahua gie, tande ogine. Erei, ereizhi olune. Wijienni eghi, tande niene.
MAT 7:8 Xiahua giechen kunlade ogine. Ereichen kunla ereizhi olune. Wijienni eghichen kunlade niene.
MAT 7:9 Tai dunda yan kunyi kewon ginan kerese tashi ogine?
MAT 7:10 Zhaghasun kerese moghei ogine?
MAT 7:11 Ta gou wiliuzhe kesiladene gouni ogikuni mejiene, asiman jieredu Adatai xiahua giechen kunlade gou dunxini genjia ulie oginu?
MAT 7:12 Ingiese ta kunlai goyadene matugie gieghaku duranshi taye kunlade qingiezhi gie. Eneshi guijin, xienzhilai shu wo."
MAT 7:13 "Ta witan wijiense oro. Fugughakude uduruku wijien fugie wo. Mo aghui wo. Orochen kun olon wo.
MAT 7:14 Aminde uduruku wijien witan wo. Mo yozhi chijia wo. Ereizhi oluchen kun choghon wo."
MAT 7:15 "Ta jia xienzhilai fangula. Hhela ghoni arasunyi zhozhi tai enende irene, sudoroni wizha zhanghei wo.
MAT 7:16 Hhelai alimaghala hhelai tanine. Eghesun jierese putou zhei shidanu? Osun jierese uhuago zhei shidanu?
MAT 7:17 Jien gou mutun jiere gou alima soune. Langan mutun jiere langan alima soune.
MAT 7:18 Gou mutun jiere langan alima sou dane. Langan mutun jiere gou alima sou dane.
MAT 7:19 Jien gou alima ulie souku mutunlai chizhidene khande teine.
MAT 7:20 Ingiese hhelai alimaghala hhelai tanine."
MAT 7:21 "Mii, 'Ezhan, Ezhan!' giezhi waradachen kunla man asiman gojiade orokui pusho. Zinie asimandedu Adaimi kielien mutun giechen kunla orone.
MAT 7:22 Hhe zuihouku udude olon kunla made kieliene, 'Ezhan, Ezhan, bijien chini niereghala chonjiwola? Chini niereghala sheitanlai touwola? Chini niereghala olon nenlitu shiqin giewola?'
MAT 7:23 Hhe shihoude bi mindaminji hhelade kieliene, 'Bi tai tani dane. Ta enezighan uhun kunla, mase likai gie!'"
MAT 7:24 "Ingiese mii enezighan kielienyi chenliedene giesan kunshi jienzha kun wo. Hoxian gieni fugie tashi jiere giesanghala niekielien wo.
MAT 7:25 Ghura bou, fugie usu chunji, kei hende feiliezhi eghiliuzhe gieni ulie enbereine. Gieni jigunni fugie tashi jiere giezho.
MAT 7:26 Mii enezighan kielienyi chenliedene ulie giesan kunshi men kun wo. Hoxian gieni shazi jiere giesanghala niekielien wo.
MAT 7:27 Ghura bou, fugie usu chunji, kei hende feiliezhi eghise gie enbereine. Da enbereisan fugie wo."
MAT 7:28 Ersa enezighan kielienyi jianji baraghase olon kunla hhe sughasande ghanirazho.
MAT 7:29 Ersa hhelade sughadan hhelai jinwun hanjialai buxian wo, nie qienlitu kunni xianli.
MAT 8:1 Ersa ula jierese bouzhi irese tebieji olon kunla hhei daghawo.
MAT 8:2 Ingiekude nie pifugientu Ersai melie ire papaladene kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi duran bise mini ganjinragha shidane."
MAT 8:3 Ersa khane zhighazhi hhei maqizhi kieliewo, "Bi duran wine. Chi ganjinra!" Ingiese hhei pifugienni deigo ganjinrawo.
MAT 8:4 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi kiemade bu kieliedene echizhi beyene buwade uzhegha. Musai shu jiere fenfulasan mutun Hudade mure ogizhi kunlade ganzhen bei."
MAT 8:5 ErsaJiabainunde orose nie baifuzhan melieni irezhi Ersai xiahua giezhi kieliewo,
MAT 8:6 "Ezhan, hojimi tanhon giesenu giede kijiedene tendun shouizho."
MAT 8:7 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Bi hhei goudaghale yoye."
MAT 8:8 Baifuzhan kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi mii giede irese bi pei dane. Chii nie aman kielienshi hojimi goudane.
MAT 8:9 Biye kunlai kha doura wo, buduila mii kha doura wo. Bi buduiladene, 'Echi!' giese echine, 'Ire!' giese irene, 'Enei gie!' giese hhe giene."
MAT 8:10 Ersa chenliedene ghanirazhi daghasan kunlade kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, bi intu xianxin giekui Isiliede uzhezhi uye daozho.
MAT 8:11 Bi tande kielieye, dunmien ximiense olon niman kunla irezhi asiman gojiade Iburaheimu, Isaghei, Yagebure hhantu xi soune.
MAT 8:12 Kharei Isilie kunlai tousenu ghadanedu kharanide echighase hhela hhende shidunne zhouzhi wilane."
MAT 8:13 Ingie Ersa baifuzhande kieliewo, "Chi kharei. Chi xianxin giesan mutun gholu gie." Hhe shihoude hojini goudawo.
MAT 8:14 ErsaBedurui giede echise Bedurui ghadunmekieni fashao giedene kijiesei chanlawo.
MAT 8:15 Ersa hhei khani nie maqise fashao giesan daodene hhe bosizhe Ersai ushilawo.
MAT 8:16 Khara oluse kunla sheitan heisan olon kunlai Ersai shida uduru irewo. Ersa nie aman kielienghala sheitanlai tou khighawo. Pse gien wineku kunlai man goudaghawo.
MAT 8:17 Ingiekushi Ezhan Isaiya xienzhii tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho, "Hhe matanyi bixinni deilawo. Matanyi gienlai danjiwo."
MAT 8:18 Ersa olon kunla hhei wiqisei chujieghedene, "Hai duimiende daoye!" giezhi fenfulawo.
MAT 8:19 Nie jinwun hanjia melie ire hhende kieliewo, "Loushi, chi khala echise bi chii daghane."
MAT 8:20 Ersa kieliewo, "Funieghede dun wine, asiman jieredu bunzhude ho wine, Kunnikewonde nie zhentou teiku oronda uwo."
MAT 8:21 Pse nie tuji iredene Ersade kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi xien adane bulale echiye."
MAT 8:22 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Fugusan kun fugusan kunlane bulale echi gie. Chi mii dagha."
MAT 8:23 Ersa chon jiere khireise tujilani hhei daghazho.
MAT 8:24 Menzhali hai jiere fugie kei bosiwo. Lan chabudu chonni unaghane. Ersa da hhunturazho.
MAT 8:25 Tujilani echizhi Ersai uru xiereigha kieliewo, "Ezhan, bijienyi jiui! Bijienyi amin widane giezho!"
MAT 8:26 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta ene Hudai gou xianxin ulie giechen kunla, yangiezhi ayizho?" Ingie bosizhedene kei, haini nie sugiese nanranghane gholuwo.
MAT 8:27 Kunla ghaniradene kieliewo, "Eneshi yan kun wo? Kei, haiye kielienyini chenliene."
MAT 8:28 Ersa hai duimiende daosenu Jiadala kunyi oronde irewo. Ghua sheitan heisan kun mezase khizhedene hhei shida texien wizhashi kiemada hhe mose yo dazho.
MAT 8:29 Hhela deigo warada qiiwo, "Hudai kewon, chi bijienyi jiohoro bu gie. Shihou da uye kuruzho, chi enende irezhi bijienyi zayalanu?"
MAT 8:30 Hhelase gouji gholode idaban khighei ijiezhi souzho.
MAT 8:31 Sheitanla Ersai xiahua giezhi chi bijienyi tou khighane giese bijienyi khighei jiere echigha giewo.
MAT 8:32 Ingie Ersa echi giese sheitanla khizhedene khigheilai jiere khiwo. Menzhali khigheila egheide chunji bou, haide yenji alawo.
MAT 8:33 Khighei adulasan kunla holudene chenshide echi sheitan heisan ene kunlai shiqinyi kunlade man kieliewo.
MAT 8:34 Ingiese nie chenshini kunla man Ersai ochirale khizhewo. Hhei uzhedene, "Enense likai gie." giezhi xiahua giewo.
MAT 9:1 Ersa chon jiere khirei hai hhemiende daozhi goya chenshidene irewo.
MAT 9:2 Ingiekude kunla nie tanhon giesan gientui ruzide qienlie Ersai shida irewo. Ersa hhelai xianxin giekui uzhedene tanhon giesan gientude kieliewo, "Gaijiu, zhughene tei, chii zuini mienliewo."
MAT 9:3 Ingiekude giedun jinwun hanjiala zhughedene kieliezho, "Ene kun kufurei fanjizho!"
MAT 9:4 Ersa hhela yan sumulasei mejiedene kieliewo, "Ta zhughedene yale doghunni sumulane?
MAT 9:5 'Chii zuini mienliewo.' giese sunfan onu, 'Bosizhe yo.' giese sunfan wo?
MAT 9:6 Kunnikewon duyade zuini mienlieku qienli bikui tande mejieghane giezho." Ingiedene tanhon giesan gientude kieliewo, "Bosidene ruzine agi, giedene echi!"
MAT 9:7 Hhe kun bosidene giedene echiwo.
MAT 9:8 Kunla chanladene man ayizho. Imutu fugie qienlini kunlade ogiwo giezhi Hudai kuaizho.
MAT 9:9 Ersa hhense melie yose Matai giesan nie kun shui shanjisan oronde sousei chanlawo. Hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii dagha." Ingie hhe bosizhedene Ersai daghawo.
MAT 9:10 Ersa giedera ijiekude olon shui shanjisan kun, zuirenla Ersa, Ersai tujilare man hhantu soudene ijienduzho.
MAT 9:11 Falisai kunla chanladene Ersai tujilade kieliezho, "Tai loushi yale shui shanjisan kun, zuirenlare hhantu ijiene?"
MAT 9:12 Ersa sonosudene kieliewo, "Gien witu kunla deifu ulie kerene, gientula deifu kerene.
MAT 9:13 Ta echidene, 'Bi ubali xiikude xiqi wo, murede xiqi uwo.' giesan jinwun jieredu ene kielienyi isii suru. Bi gou kunlai ereile ese irezho. Zuirenlai ereile irezho."
MAT 9:14 Ingiekude Yaheiyani tujila Ersai ochirale ire kieliewo, "Bijien, pse Falisai kunla chan orozo bareizho, chii tujila yale orozo ulie bareine?"
MAT 9:15 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ghurunde iresan zhochenla shini khughon bikude matugie nango giene? Shini khughonni kunla lai echiku udu kuzhene. Hhe shihoude hhela orozo bareine.
MAT 9:16 Shini popui khuichen jien jiere huduchen kun uwo. Qingiese hudusan oron jienni qida olughane, tanturasan pse fugiedane.
MAT 9:17 Shini jiuni khuichen tulunde zhonlochen kun uwo. Qingie zhonlose tulun ghaluzhi jiu usuru khizhese tulunye qida olune. Shini jiuni shini tulunde zhonlose ghuala gou wo."
MAT 9:18 Ersa hhelade zhen ene kielienyi kieliekude nie huitan gonjisan kun ire papalazhi kieliewo, "Mii oqin jian duya ijiewo. Chi yodene hhei jiere khane teizhi onxian giema, hhe aminne olune."
MAT 9:19 Ersa bosizhedene tujilarene hhantu hhei daghazhi echiwo.
MAT 9:20 Zhen qingiekude nie chusun usuruzhi 12 nien olusan bierei Ersai khuina iredene jien ghizhaseni nie maqiwo.
MAT 9:21 Hhe "Ersai jienni nie maqise gienni goudane." giezhi zhughedene sumulazho.
MAT 9:22 Ersa ochira daozhe hhei uzhezhi kieliewo, "Funi, zhughene tei! Chii xianxin gieku chii jiuiwo." Hhe shihoude bierei goudawo.
MAT 9:23 Ersa gonjisan kunni giede kuruse kunla fugusan kunde xiu feiliezhi lon chouisei chanlawo.
MAT 9:24 Ingie kieliewo, "Daodu. Oqin ese duya ijiezho, hhunturazho." Ingiese hhela Ersai uzhezhi xiniezho.
MAT 9:25 Kunlai khighadene Ersa oro echi oqinni khase nie laise oqin bosizhewo.
MAT 9:26 Ene xioxi hhe oronde man chonji kuruwo.
MAT 9:27 Ersa hhense melie yose ghua sugho hhei daghadene waradazho, "Dawudeni houdei, bijiende ubali nie xii!"
MAT 9:28 Ersa giedera orose sughola hhei melie irewo. Ersa kieliewo, "Bi ene shiqinyi gie shidakui ta xianxin gienu?" Hhela kieliewo, "Ezhan, bijien xianxin giene!"
MAT 9:29 Ersa hhelai nudunyi moizhi kieliewo, "Ta xianxin giesan mutun gholu gie."
MAT 9:30 Ingiese hhelai nudun goudawo. Ersa hhelade hende fenfulazhi, "Ta ene shiqinyi kunlade bu mejiegha." giewo.
MAT 9:31 Ingieliuzhe hhela khizhi echidene Ersai xioxii hhe oronde man chonji kurughawo.
MAT 9:32 Hhela khizhi echikude kunla nie sheitan heisan yabai Ersai shida uduru irewo.
MAT 9:33 Sheitanni touzhi khighase yaba kielien kielie qiiwo. Kunla man ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Isiliede intu shiqin uzhezhi ese daowo!"
MAT 9:34 Falisai kunla kieliezho, "Hhe sheitanni touzii kouizhi sheitan touzho."
MAT 9:35 Ersa go chenshi, aghinlai yo baraghazhi hhelai huitanlade kunlade sughazhi asiman gojiani gouxioxini chonjizho. Yanyanji gien nouzhi giemeresanlai goudaghazho.
MAT 9:36 Olon kunlai chanladene ubali xiizho. Hhela kunnan wo, banman giechen uwo. Ghonide asuchi uwokughala niekielien wo.
MAT 9:37 Ingie tujiladene kieliewo, "Zhonjia olon wo, wiliechi choghon wo.
MAT 9:38 Ta zhonjiani ezhanyi xiahua giezhi wiliechilai peidene zhonjiane ghuragha gie."
MAT 10:1 Ersa 12 gie tujine uruzhi iresenu hhelade zannan ruhher touzhi yanyanji gien nouzhi giemeresanlai goudaghaku qienli ogiwo.

MAT 10:3 Feili, Badolomai, Doma, shui shanjisan Matai, Yalefeini kewon Yagebu, Datai,
MAT 10:4 Rexinpaini Ximun, pse Ersai ghudandusan Jialie kun Yuda wo.

MAT 10:7 Xien yo xien chonjizhi kielie, 'Asiman gojia chadashiwo!'

MAT 10:9 Kakadene antan, miengu, baer bu barei.
MAT 10:10 Mo yose kuabao, ghua jien, mahei, zhugun bu barei. Wilie giechen kunla ijiuni indan jienliekuni wo.
MAT 10:11 Ta alinie chenshi, aghinde echise gou kun khala bikui daqinladene likai gietula hhei giede sou.
MAT 10:12 Hheni giede orokude salan gie.
MAT 10:13 Hhe giei kunla tai pei shidase ta onxian giesan pinnan hhelai jiere wo. Pei dase ta onxian giesan pinnan yen tai jiere irene.
MAT 10:14 Kien tai ulie jienliezhi kielienyi ulie chenliese hhei gie, hhe chenshise likai giekude kon jieredu turane kui bougha.
MAT 10:15 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, panjiku udude hhe chenshi shouiku zeinan Sodoma, Emola oronse da fugie wo!"
MAT 10:16 "Uzhe, bi tai peizhi echighase ghonilai zhanghei dunda echighasan niekielien wo. Ingiese ta moghei mutun jienzharazhi ghoghochen mutun ganjinra.
MAT 10:17 Ta kunlai xioxin gie. Kunla tai zui fugie fayende jiuine. Hhelai huitanlade mabienzighala eghine.
MAT 10:18 Mii yenyinghala tai shenzhan, honshanlai melie lai echine. Ta hhelai melie, niman kunlai melie made ganzhen beine.
MAT 10:19 Kunla tai jiuikude ta matui, yan kieliekui munan bu gie. Hhe shihoude yan kieliekui tande mejieghane.
MAT 10:20 Kieliesanshi ta pusho, Adaitai Ruhher tai sudoro kieliezho.
MAT 10:21 Gaijiu gaijiune, ada kewosine ghudanduzhi fugughakude jiuine. Kesila ada, anane zodui giezhi fugughakude kune.
MAT 10:22 Mii yenyinghala soyuji kunla tai henjine. Ingieliuzhe rennai giezhi zuihou kusanlai jiuine.
MAT 10:23 Kunla tai ene chenshide heise da nie chenshide holu. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, Isilieni chenshilai ta yozhi baraghatula Kunnikewon irene."
MAT 10:24 "Xieshen loushise fugie uwo, hoji ezhanse fugie uwo.
MAT 10:25 Xieshen loushighala niekielien, hoji ezhanghala niekielien gholuse kuruwo. Kunla gieni zhanguijini, 'Sheitanni touzi.' giezhi sugiese gieni kunlai genjia ulie sugienu?"
MAT 10:26 "Ingiese ta hhelase bu ayi. Khaghasanlai ulie khizheghakui uwo. Niuighasanlai ulie mejieghakui uwo.
MAT 10:27 Bi tande beichazide kieliesei ta mindamin kielie. Ta chighindene chenliesei gie jierese fugiede kielie.
MAT 10:28 Beyeni alane, ruhherni ala dachen hhelase bu ayi. Zinie beye, ruhher ghualai widaghadene dozoheide echigha shidachen hhense ayi.
MAT 10:29 Ghua bunzhui 1 mao baer huinela? Ingieliuzhe asimanni adatai dain ulie giese nieda andazhi bouzhe dane.
MAT 10:30 Tai kieliese tai qiorun jieredu usunniliuzhe toulazhi agizho.
MAT 10:31 Ingiese ta bu ayi, ta olon bunzhulase zhunyo wo."
MAT 10:32 "Kien kunlai melie mini renjise biye asiman jieredu adane melie hhei renjine.
MAT 10:33 Kien kunlai melie mini ulie renjise biye asiman jieredu adane melie hhei ulie renjine."
MAT 10:34 "Bi irekushi zemin jiere pinnan deilazhi iresei ta bu sumula. Bi irekushi pinnan deilazhi ese iredene khudogho deilazhi irezho.
MAT 10:35 Bi irekushi, 'Kun adarene, oqin anarene, konbierei ghadunmekierene zodui gieghale irezho.
MAT 10:36 Kunni duitoushi gieni kun wo.'
MAT 10:37 Ada anadene mase olon orese mii pei dane. Kesiladene mase olon orese mii pei dane.
MAT 10:38 Kien shizijiane beiliezhi mii ulie daghase mii pei dane.
MAT 10:39 Aminne ulie widaghane giese aminne widaghane. Made oluzhi aminne widaghase aminne ulie widaghane."
MAT 10:40 "Kun tai jienliese mii jienliezho. Mii jienliese mii peizhi ireghasan hhei jienliezho.
MAT 10:41 Kien xienzhini xienzhi danlaghazhi jienliese xienzhini jianlini linlane. Kien gou kunni gou kun danlaghazhi jienliese gou kunni jianlini linlane.
MAT 10:42 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kien mii tujila dundadu zui ganide mii tuji danlaghazhi nie beizi usu ogiliuzhe hhende jianli kenjin ogine."
MAT 11:1 Ersa 12 gie tujidene fenfulazhi baludene hhense likai gie hhelai go chenshilade echizhi kunlade sughazhi chonjizho.
MAT 11:2 Yaheiya bafanzise Mexiha giesan shiqinyi sonosudene tujilane peizhi echighawo.
MAT 11:3 Hhela Ersade asawo, "Hhe irene giesanshi chi onu, bijien pse niei saghei?"
MAT 11:4 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta echidene sonosusanyi, chanlasanyi Yaheiyade kielie.
MAT 11:5 Sugho chanlasanyi, dogholon yosanyi, pifugientui goudaghasanyi, dulei sonosusanyi, fugusan kun aminne olusanyi, pse nanxin kunlade gouxioxi chonjikui kielie.
MAT 11:6 Mii inxin ulie giechen kunde fuqi wine."
MAT 11:7 Yaheiyai tujila yoladene Ersa kunlade Yaheiyai kieliezho, "Ta hontande yan kunyi uzhele echiwo? Kei feiliezhi gojiolusan ghulusun mutun zholien kunyi uzhele echiwu? Pusho!
MAT 11:8 Ta yan kunyi uzhele echiwo? Seighan jien musisan kunyi uzhele echiwu? Seighan jien musisan kunla hongunde wo!
MAT 11:9 Ta jiujin yan kunyi uzhele echiwo? Xienzhii uzhele echiwu? Enbene! Bi tande kielieye, hheshi xienzhise da fugieni wo.
MAT 11:10 Jinwun jiere, 'Uzhe, bi qinsi kunne chii melie peizhi chii moni zhunbei gieghane.' giezhi huaisanshi ene kun wo.
MAT 11:11 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, biereila olusan kun dunda xili gieghasan Yaheiyase fugieni nieda uwoma, asiman gojiade zui meila kun hhense fugie wo.
MAT 11:12 Yaheiyani hhe xienzise eli kutula asiman gojiani hende eghizho, lihaitu kun hhei qianlazho.
MAT 11:13 Soyuji xienzhishu, guijinshu jiere melie kieliesanlashi man Yaheiyase jieshu oluwo.
MAT 11:14 Kieliesanlai ta xianxin giene giese Yaheiyashi irene giesan Iliya enbene.
MAT 11:15 Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"
MAT 11:16 "Bi ene idai kunlai yanghala bilane? Hoxian geidoude souzhi nadusan kesilai xianli. Hhela nieniedene waradazhi kieliene,
MAT 11:17 'Bijien tande bierei agiku xiu feiliese ta ulie jiuline. Kun fuguwo giezhi wilase ta ulie wilane.'
MAT 11:18 Yaheiya iredene ulie ijiezhi ulie ochise kunla hhei jiere sheitan wine giezhi kieliene.
MAT 11:19 Kunnikewon iredene ijiezhi ochise kunla ene kun jin ijiezhi ochikure wo. Shui shanjisan kun, zuirenlani zhanlien wo giezhi kieliene. Ingieliuzhe aghelishi giekughala olusan bikuni zhenmin giene."
MAT 11:20 Hhe xienzide Ersa nenlitu shiqin olon giese chenshii kunla geizhen ese giese hhelade jingao giezhi kieliewo,
MAT 11:21 "Gelaxin, Bosaida, tande gou widawo! Tai dunda giesan nenlitu shiqinni Tuilo, Xidunde giewoshi hhela eqighanse madei zhodene jierene funiesun teizhi geizhen giewo.
MAT 11:22 Bi tande kielieye, panjiku udude ta shouiku zeinan Tuilo, Xidunse da fugie wo!
MAT 11:23 Jiabainun, chii undudaghazhi asiman jiere khireighanu? Chii dozoheide anda boughane. Chii hhende giesan nenlitu shiqinni Sodomade giezhoshi hhe chenshi eli kutula wine.
MAT 11:24 Bi tande kielieye, panjiku udude ta shouiku zeinan Sodomase da fugie wo!"
MAT 11:25 Hhe xienzide Ersa kieliewo, "Asiman zeminni Ezhan, Ada, chii mafan gieghawo. Chi ene shiqinlani agheli, erlintu kunlade niuighazhi ga kewosi mutun kunlade mejieghawo.
MAT 11:26 Ada, enbene, eneshi chi duranghalane giesanwo.
MAT 11:27 Yanniliuzhe Adami made ogiwo. Adase chugo kiema kewonni mejie dane. Kewon, pse kewon yenyi mejieghasan kunse chugo kiema Adai mejie dane.
MAT 11:28 Jien khishulazhi gunduni beiliesan kunla man mii shida ire. Bi tai hhamuraghaye.
MAT 11:29 Ta mii jiabanyi jierene zhozhi mase suru. Mii zhughede renyi, meilade uzhekui wine. Tai zhughe hhamura shidane.
MAT 11:30 Mii jiaban sunfan wo. Mii danzi gongien wo."
MAT 12:1 Hhe xienzide Ersa hhamuraku udude boudei ghazhaghun yozhi daozho. Tujilani oliesuse boudei qiorunni sidazhi ijiezho.
MAT 12:2 Falisai kunla chanladene Ersade kieliewo, "Uzhe, chii tujila hhamuraku udude ulie giekui giezho!"
MAT 12:3 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Dawude, hhantuku kunlarene oliesukude giesan shiqinyi ta onshizhi ese daowu?
MAT 12:4 Hhe mechide orodene Hudade ogiku ginanyi ijiewo. Ene ginanyi hhe, pse hhantuku kunlai ijiezhi ulie olune. Zinie buwa ijiese olune.
MAT 12:5 Pse buwala hhamuraku udude mechide hhamuraku udui guijinni fanjiliuzhe zui ulie sanakui ta guijinshu jiere onshizhi ese daowu?
MAT 12:6 Bi tande kielieye, enende nie kun mechise da fugie wo.
MAT 12:7 'Bi ubali xiikude xiqi wo. Murede xiqi uwo.' giesan ene kielienyi isii ta mejiese zui witude zui ulie soughane.
MAT 12:8 Kunnikewonshi hhamuraku uduni Ezhan wo."
MAT 12:9 Ersa hhe oronse likai gie huitande orowo.
MAT 12:10 Hhende nie khani ghosan kun wine. Kunla Ersai zhane giezhi, "Hhamuraku udude goudaghase olunulie?" giezhi asawo.
MAT 12:11 Ersa kieliewo, "Tai dunda kien hhamuraku udude ghoni nokiende anda bouse laizhi ulie khizhenu?
MAT 12:12 Kun ghonise giedughon zhigui wo. Ingiese hhamuraku udude gouni giese oluzho."
MAT 12:13 Ingie, "Hhe kunde khane khizhegha." giezhi kieliewo. Hhe khane khizheghase khani goudazhi da nie khaghalai niekielien gholuwo.
MAT 12:14 Falisai kunla khizhi echidene "Ersai matugie widaghane?" giezhi shanlian giewo.
MAT 12:15 Ersa mejiedene hhense likai giewo. Tebieji olon kunla hhei daghazho. Hhe gientulai man goudaghadene
MAT 12:16 hhelade, "Hheshi kien bikui bu kielie!" giezhi minlin xiaiwo.
MAT 12:17 Ingiekushi Ezhan Isaiya xienzhini tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho,
MAT 12:18 "Uzhe, eneshi bi sunghusan mii hoji wo. Bi hhende orezhi xiqi hen wo. Bi ruhherne hhende ogine. Ingiedene hhe gundanni minzulade chonjine.
MAT 12:19 Hhe ulie zhenjindune, ulie onghonone. Geidoude hhei shenqini kiema sonosu dane.
MAT 12:20 Ghurane giesan ghulusunyi hhe ulie ghuraghane. Xiniene giesan zhulai ulie xinieghane. Izhi gundanni injitula giene.
MAT 12:21 Minzula hhei nierei xiwon giene."
MAT 12:22 Ingiekude kunla nie sheitan heisan sugho, yabai Ersai shida uduru irewo. Ersa hheni goudaghase hhe kielien kieliezhi chanlawo.
MAT 12:23 Kunla man ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Eneshi Dawudeni houdei enbeneba?"
MAT 12:24 Falisai kunla chenliedene kieliewo, "Ene kun sheitanni touzi Biexibui ulie kouise sheitan tou dane."
MAT 12:25 Ersa hhela yan sumulasei mejiedene kieliewo, "Alinie gojia goyalane eghinduse hontan gholune. Alinie chenshiwonu, alinie giei kunla goyalane eghinduse bei dane.
MAT 12:26 Ibilisi Ibilisine touse goyalane eghinduzho, hhei gojia matugie beine?
MAT 12:27 Bi Biexibuni kouizhi sheitan touse tai tujila kienyi kouizhi sheitan touzho? Ingiese tai tujila zhenmin giese tanughun codazho.
MAT 12:28 Bi Hudai Ruhherghala sheitan touse Hudai gojia tande irezho.
MAT 12:29 Pse kun liliantu kunyi giede orozhi dunxilai qianlane giese xien liliantu kunyi ulie banlase matugie man qianla echine?
MAT 12:30 Mii miende ulie beise mii duitou wo. Mare ulie hhantulachen kunshi sandachen kun wo.
MAT 12:31 Ingiese bi tande kielieye, yanyanji zui, hu kieliesanlai man roulienema, Shenlinni hu kieliese ulie rouliene.
MAT 12:32 Kunnikewonni fandui giezhi kieliese roulienema, Shenlinni fandui giezhi kieliese duyade ulie rouliene, houshideye ulie rouliene."
MAT 12:33 "Mutun goushi alima gou wo. Mutun bixinshi alimaye bixin wo. Alimaghala mutunni mejiene.
MAT 12:34 Ta ene du mogheini zhunzhughala, ta doghunshi matugie gou kielien kieliezhi khizheghane? Zhughede durusei amande kielie khizheghane.
MAT 12:35 Gou kunlai zhughede gounishi yen gouni khizheghane. Doghun kunlai zhughede doghunnishi yen doghunni khizheghane.
MAT 12:36 Bi tande kielieye, xienhua kieliechen kunlai panjiku udude nie aman nie amanji renjighane.
MAT 12:37 Tai kielienghala tai gounii sanane. Tai kielienghala tai zuini jinjine."
MAT 12:38 Ingiekude giedun jinwun hanjia, Falisai kun Ersade kieliewo, "Loushi, chi gieku ghudureqini bijien uzhene giezho."
MAT 12:39 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ene idaini kunla doghun nefuxin giezho, ta dou ghudureqi kerezhoma, xienzhi Yunusii ghudureqise chugo uzheghaku ghudureqi uwo.
MAT 12:40 Yunusi ghurudu ghuran xii fugie zhaghasunyi kielide wo. Kunnikewonye ghurudu ghuran xii zemin jizide beine.
MAT 12:41 Panjiku udude Niniwi kunla bosizhezhi ene idai kunlai zuini jinjine. Ingiekushi Niniwi kunla Yunusi chonjisei chenliedene geizhen giewo. Uzhe, enende Yunusise pse fugieni wine!
MAT 12:42 Panjiku udude nanfanni bierei honshan bosizhedene ene idai kunlai zuini jinjine. Ingiekushi hhe gholose Sulumaneni aghelini chenliele irewo. Uzhe, enende Sulumanese pse fugieni wine!"
MAT 12:43 "Nie zannan ruhher kunni jierese likai giedene usu witu oronde izhigie yozhi hhamuraku oron ereizho. Ereizhi olu dadene
MAT 12:44 kieliewo, 'Bi yen khizhesan hhe giedene echine.' Khareizhi echi nie uzhese kunkunji shuzhi goudagha jiezho.
MAT 12:45 Ingie khizhi echi goyasene dolon doghun ruhheryi uduruzhi ire souwo. Ingiese hhe kunni qinkon melieshidakude pse ese kuruwo. Ene idaini doghun kunlaye eneghala niekielien gholune."
MAT 12:46 Ersa kunlade kieliekude ana, gaijiulani iredene ghadane beizhi hhere kielien kieliene giezho.
MAT 12:47 Nie kun hhende kieliewo, "Uzhe, anachii, gaijiulachii ghadane sagheizhi chare kielien kieliene giezho."
MAT 12:48 Ersa khareizhi hhe kieliesan kunde kieliewo, "Kienshi mii ana wo? Kienshi mii gaijiula wo?"
MAT 12:49 Ingie tujilane zhiizhi kieliewo, "Uzhe, mii ana, mii gaijiula wo.
MAT 12:50 Asiman jieredu adaimi isii zunjizhi giesan kunlashi mii gaijiu, eghechijiu, ana wo."
MAT 13:1 Yen hhe udude Ersa giederase khizhedene haibienzide souwo.
MAT 13:2 Tebieji olon kunla hhei shida irezhi hhantulase hhe chon jiere khirei souwo. Kunla man haibienzide beizho.
MAT 13:3 Ersa kunlade bilazhi olon kieliewo, "Nie kun shizhile echiwo.
MAT 13:4 Shizhikudeni niezhanla mo jiere luise bunzhula ire ijie agiwo.
MAT 13:5 Niezhanla tura olon witu tashitu oronde luise tura ninkienshi niazi faizhi ghujin woma,
MAT 13:6 genzi uwoshi naran khizhe nie xiese ghowo.
MAT 13:7 Pse niezhanla eghesun dunda luise eghesun khizhezhi hhei jigheidawo.
MAT 13:8 Da niezhanla gou ghazhade luise 100 pei, 60 pei, 30 pei zhonjia souwo.
MAT 13:9 Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"

MAT 13:11 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Hudai gojiai mimii zinie tande mejieghawoma, hhelade ese mejieghawo.
MAT 13:12 Bichen kunde pse olon ogizhi feilieghane. Wichen kunse bisanlainiye agi echine.
MAT 13:13 Bi hhelade bilazhi kieliekushi hhela uzhese qinchu olu dane, chenliese sonosu dazhi minbai olu dane.
MAT 13:14 Isaiya melie kieliesan kielien mutun hhelai jiere shuhua gholuwo, 'Ta izhi chenliezhoma, dunjire dane. Ta izhi uzhezhoma, minbai olu dane.
MAT 13:15 Ene bexinlai zhughe khiduzhezhi chighin beidazhi nudunne hameizho. Pse nudunni chanlazhi chighinni sonosuzhi zhughedeni minbai oludene kharei daorese Bi hhelai goudaghakuse ayizho.'
MAT 13:16 Ingieliuzhe tande fuqi wine. Tai nudunde chanlazhi chighinde sonosuzho.
MAT 13:17 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, olon xienzhi, gou kunla ta uzhesei uzhene giezhoma, uzhe dazho. Ta chenliesei chenliene giezhoma, chenlie dazho."
MAT 13:18 "Ingiese ta ene fure shizhisan kunni bilasei chenlie.
MAT 13:19 Kienliuzhe asiman gojiani kielienyi chenliedene dunjire dase Ibilisi iredene zhughedeni shizhisei agi echine. Eneshi mo jiere luisan fure wo.
MAT 13:20 Tashitu oronde luisanshi kielienyi chenliedene bayasuzhi deigo jienliewoma,
MAT 13:21 zhughedeni genzi wise niechaku wo. Kielienyi yenyinghala zeinan onu heiku kuzhese deigo furawo.
MAT 13:22 Eghesun dunda luisanshi kielienyi chenliewoma, duyai munan gieku, baer miise kielienyi jigheidazhi yama sou dawo.
MAT 13:23 Gou ghazhade luisanshi kielienyi chenliezhi dunjiresan kun wo. 100 pei, 60 pei, 30 pei zhonjia souwo."
MAT 13:24 Ersa hhelade pse bilazhi kieliewo, "Asiman gojia hoxian kun ghazhadene boudei fure shizhisei xianli.
MAT 13:25 Ashighala hhunturakude duitouni iredene yemeini boudei dundani shizhi yolawo.
MAT 13:26 Boudei osizhi qiorun khise yemeiye khizhewo.
MAT 13:27 Hojilani iredene ezhandene kieliewo, 'Ezhan, chi boudei fureni ghazhade ese tareiwu? Khalase iresan yemei wo?'
MAT 13:28 Ezhan hhelade kieliewo, 'Eneshi duitou giesan wo.' Hojilani kieliewo, 'Bijien echidene xi agimu?'
MAT 13:29 Ezhanni kieliewo, 'Bu echi, yemeini xise boudeiniye xi khizhene.
MAT 13:30 Ghuala hhantu osi gie. Sagheizhi xiku shihoude bi ghurachen kunlade kielieye, "Xien yemeii xisenu chouladene khan tei. Boudeini yanchidene cankude ghura." giezhi.'"
MAT 13:31 Ersa hhelade pse bilazhi kieliewo, "Asiman gojia nie caizi furei xianli. Kun agizhi echi ghazhadene tareiwo.
MAT 13:32 Eneshi fure dundase zui gani woma, osizhi khizhese yan caiseliuzhe fugie wo. Mutun gholudene bunzhula chala jiereni holiene."
MAT 13:33 Pse hhelade bilazhi kieliewo, "Asiman gojia hoxian kuniegheni xianli. Nie bierei agizhi echidene nie deizi ghurunde teizhi man faighawo."
MAT 13:34 Enelashi man Ersa olon kunlade bilazhi kieliesan wo. Bilazhi ulie kieliese hhelade ulie kieliene.
MAT 13:35 Ingiekushi Ezhan xienzhini tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholughane giezho, "Bi bilazhi kielieye. Duyai zhayaghasanse niuighasan shiqinlai kieliezhi khizheghaye."
MAT 13:36 Ingiedene Ersa kunlase likai gie giedera orowo. Tujila shidani ire kieliewo, "Ghazha jieredu yemeini bilasei bijiende mejiegha."
MAT 13:37 Hhe kieliewo, "Boudei furei shizhisanshi Kunnikewon wo.
MAT 13:38 Ghazhashi duya wo. Boudei fureshi asiman gojiai kunla wo. Yemeishi hhe doghunnii kunla wo.
MAT 13:39 Yemei shizhisan duitoushi Ibilisi wo. Ghuraku shihoushi duya baraku shihou wo. Ghurachenshi qienxienla wo.
MAT 13:40 Yemeini xi agidene khande sideraghaku mutun duya barakudeye ingiene.
MAT 13:41 Kunnikewon qienxienlane peizhi zui fanjighasanlai, uhunni giesanlai man asiman gojiasene zhiizhi khizhedene
MAT 13:42 fugie khantu nokiende benda oroghase hhende shidunne zhouzhi wilane.
MAT 13:43 Ingiekude gou kunla adane gojiade naran nudun mutun gieran faine. Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"
MAT 13:44 "Asiman gojia hoxian ghazhade niuighasan boubeini xianli. Nie kun hhei chanladene niuighawo. Bayasuzhi echidene goyane dunxilai man huisenu ene ghazhai agiwo."
MAT 13:45 "Pse asiman gojia hoxian nie meimei kun zhiguitu manou ereisei xianli.
MAT 13:46 Nie fugie jiagetu manoui penjise echidene goya dunxilane man huisenu ene manoui agiwo."
MAT 13:47 "Pse asiman gojia hoxian haide xiaisan onni xianli. Yanyanji zhaghasunlai bareizhi
MAT 13:48 on duruse usu bienzide laizhi khizhedene sousenu gounilai sunghuzhi tunzide teine. Bixinnilai bendane.
MAT 13:49 Duya barakudeye ingiene. Qienxienla irese doghun kunni gou kun dundase sunghu khizhedene
MAT 13:50 fugie khantu nokiende bendase hhende shidunne zhouzhi wilane."
MAT 13:51 Ersa kieliewo, "Enezighan kielienyi ta man dunjirewoye?" Hhela huida giewo, "Bijien dunjirewo."
MAT 13:52 Ersa kieliewo, "Jien asiman gojiade tuji danlasan jinwun hanjiala hoxian gieni zhanguijii xianli. Hhe kufansene shini, khuichen dunxilai agi khizhene."
MAT 13:53 Ersa enezighan bilasei kielie baraghadene hhense likai giewo.

MAT 13:55 Eneshi mujianyi kewon pushonu? Hhei ananishi Mereiyen pushonu? Gaijiulanishi Yagebu, Yusufu, Ximun, Yuda pushonu?

MAT 14:1 Hhe xienzide Hherode on Ersai shiqinyi sonosudene
MAT 14:2 kha dourashiku kunlade kieliewo, "Eneshi xili gieghasan Yaheiya wo. Hhe fugudene aminne oluwo. Ingiese ene nenlitu shiqinla hhei jierese khizhezho."
MAT 14:3 Eneshi Hherode jiu biereine Xilojini yenyinghala Yaheiyai bareidene banlasenu bafanzide khazho. Hherodei jiushi Feili wo.
MAT 14:4 YaheiyaHherodede, "Chi hhei agise ese oluzho." giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 14:5 Ingiese HherodeYaheiyani alane giezhoma, bexinla hhei xienzhi wo giese hhelase ayizho.
MAT 14:6 Hherodeni olusan udu kuzhese xi beilazhi Xilojini oqin kunlai melie wu jiulizho. Hherode hende bayasuzho,
MAT 14:7 ingiese fayen giezhi oqinde yan kerese yan ogiye giezhi dain giewo.
MAT 14:8 Anani oqinne, "Xili gieghasan Yaheiyani qiorunyi hhamusade teidene made iregha." giezhi kielieghase oqin kieliewo.
MAT 14:9 Hherode hende munan giezho. Ingieliuzhe olon kunlai melie fayen giese fenfulazhi hhende ogine giewo.
MAT 14:10 Ingie kun peidene bafanzide Yaheiyai qiorunyi chizhighawo.
MAT 14:11 Qiorunyini hhamusade agi ire oqinde ogiwo. Oqin pse anadene ogiwo.
MAT 14:12 Yaheiyai tujila iredene beyeini linlasenu buladene Ersade echi kieliewo.
MAT 14:13 Ersa enei mejiedene chon souzhi hhense likai gie niezheghan hontande echiwo. Olon kunla Ersa yolasei mejiedene chenshilase yozhi hhei daghazho.
MAT 14:14 Ersa chon jierese bouzhese tebieji olon kunlai chanladene ubali xiiwo. Hhelai giemeresan kunlai goudaghawo.
MAT 14:15 Khara olukude tujilani hhei shida ire kieliewo, "Eneshi hontan wo. Shihou eqie widawo. Kunlai sandaghazhi hhela goyalane aghinlade agizhi ijiele echigieba."
MAT 14:16 Ersa kieliewo, "Hhelai echighaku biyo uwo. Ta hhelade ogizhi ijiegha."
MAT 14:17 Tujilani kieliewo, "Matai enende zi tawun ginanji ghua zhaghasun wo."
MAT 14:18 Ersa kieliewo, "Mii enende agizhi iregha."
MAT 14:19 Ingie olon kunlai fenfulazhi osuntu oronde soughawo. Pse tawun ginan, ghua zhaghasunyi barei, asimanyi uzhe Hudade mafan kieliedene ghulusenu tujilade ogise tujila kunlade ogiwo.
MAT 14:20 Dajiala man ijiedene chuduwo. Tujila feiliesan zhazhai hhantulaghase 12 gie lanzi zhonlowo.
MAT 14:21 Ijiesan kun dunda bierei kewosilai ulie sanase chabudu 5000 ere kun wo.
MAT 14:22 Ersa deigo tujilai biizhi chon jiere khighadene xien hai duimiende daogha goyane olon kunlai sandaghawo.
MAT 14:23 Kunlai sandaghadene ulade niezheghan onxian giele echiwo. Khara oluse hhende niezheghan wo.
MAT 14:24 Qingiekude chon haibienzise gholo wo. Kei shun wise lan chonni eghizhi yuqighazho.
MAT 14:25 Xieni 3 jiense 6 jienni shihoude Ersa tujilai hhende echine giezhi haini usu jiere yozho.
MAT 14:26 Tujila hai jiere hhe yosei chanladene jindazhi ayidene waradawo, "Perei wo!"
MAT 14:27 Ersa deigo hhelade kieliewo, "Ta zhughelane tei. Bi wo. Bu ayi!"
MAT 14:28 Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi enbese minlin xiaizhi mii hai jiereghun goyane hhende yozhi echigha."
MAT 14:29 Ersa, "Chi ire." giezhi kieliese Beduru chon jierese boudene Ersai hhende echine giezhi hai jiereghun yo qiiwo.
MAT 14:30 Kei fugiede feiliesei chanla ayidene haide anda boune giese waradazhi kieliewo, "Ezhan, mii jiui!"
MAT 14:31 Ersa deigo khaghalane laidene kieliezho, "Chi ene xianxin gieku zhughe gajitu kun. Yangiezhi inxin giezho?"
MAT 14:32 ErsaBedurughala chon jiere khise kei beiwo.

MAT 15:1 Ingiekude Falisai kun, jinwun hanjiala Yelusalense Ersai hhende ire asawo,
MAT 15:2 "Chii tujila yangiezhi xienrenla sughasan xigonni ulie zunjine? Hhela ijiekude khane ulie wagha ijiezho."
MAT 15:3 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi goya xigonghalane Hudai minlinni ulie zunjine?
MAT 15:4 Huda, 'Ada anane zunji', 'Ada anane sugiesan kunni ala.' giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 15:5 Ingieliuzhe ta kieliene, 'Kien ada anadene bi tande ogi shidakui Hudade ogiwo.' giezhi kieliese
MAT 15:6 hhe kun adane ulie zunjise olune giezho. Ingiezhi ta goya xigonghalane Hudai kielienyi widaghazho.
MAT 15:7 Jiazhon giesan kunlaya, Isaiya tai zhiizhi melieshida kieliesan ese codazho. Hhe kieliezho,
MAT 15:8 'Ene bexinla amanghalane mii zunjine. Zhugheni mase gholo wo.
MAT 15:9 Hhela kunni guijinyi zhenzhenji daoli mutun kunlade sughazho. Ingiese mii beiise yama oronde uwo.'"
MAT 15:10 Ersa kunlai uruzhi ire hhelade kieliewo, "Ta chenliezhi minbai olu,
MAT 15:11 amanse orosan kunyi ulie zannanshighanema, amanse khizhesan kunyi zannanshighane."
MAT 15:12 Ingie tujila hhei melie ire kieliewo, "Falisai kun ene kielienyi chenliese hokusanni chi mejielie?"
MAT 15:13 Ersa kieliewo, "Asiman jieredu adami zeilasan pushoshi man xi khizhene.
MAT 15:14 Hhelai bu gonji. Hhelashi sughoi uduruchen sugho wo. Sugho sughone uduruse ghuala nokiende anda boune."
MAT 15:15 BeduruErsade kieliewo, "Ene bilazhi kieliesei bijiende kieliezhi minbai olugha."
MAT 15:16 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta dou minbai olu dawu?
MAT 15:17 Amande orosan kielighun mekiende echisei ta ulie mejienu?
MAT 15:18 Amanse khizhesanshi zhughese khizhesanwo. Ene caigie kunni zannanshighane.
MAT 15:19 Zhughese khizhesanshi doghunde sumulaku, alaku, piofen gieku, lon kijieku, ghulaku, jia ganzhen beiku, sugieku wo.
MAT 15:20 Enela man kunni zannanshighane. Khane ulie wagha ijiese kunni ulie zannanshighane."
MAT 15:21 Ersa hhense likai giedene Tuilo, Xidunni oronde echiwo.
MAT 15:22 Nie niman kunyi bierei hhe oronse khizhedene waradazhi kieliewo, "Ezhan, Dawudeni houdei, made ubali nie xii! Mii oqinyi sheitan heisan hen wo."
MAT 15:23 Ingieliuzhe Ersa yama huida ese giezho. Tujilani melie ire xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Hhei khareighaba. Ene bierei mai khuinase waradazho."
MAT 15:24 Ersa kieliewo, "Mii peizhi zinie Isilieni kunlai dundadu miisan ghonilade oluzhi ireghazho."
MAT 15:25 Hhe bierei ire Ersai beiizhi kieliewo, "Ezhan, made banman nie gie!"
MAT 15:26 Ersa kieliewo, "Kesilai ginanyi ga nogheide bendazhi ogise ese oluzho."
MAT 15:27 Hhe bierei kieliewo, "Ezhan, oluzhoma, nogheiye ezhanne shire doura bousan zhazhai ijiene."
MAT 15:28 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Funi, chii xianxin gieku fugie wo. Chi keresan mutun chade gholu gie." Hhe shihoude oqinni goudawo.
MAT 15:29 Ersa hhense likai giezhi Jialilihai bienzide iredene ulade khirei souwo.
MAT 15:30 Tebieji olon kunla hhei hhende iredene dogholon, sugho, sanfei, yaba, pse olon gientulai hhei konshida jiese hhe goudaghawo.
MAT 15:31 Yaba kielien kielie, sanfei gouda, dogholon yo, sugho chanlasei olon kunla uzhedene ghanirazhi Isilieni Hudai kuaiwo.
MAT 15:32 Ersa tujilane uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Ene kunla mare hhantu ghurudu oluzho, hhelade ijiekui widazho. Bi hhelade ubali xiizho. Bi hhelai oliesuzhi echighaku duran uwo. Mo jiere echise injirekuse ayizho."
MAT 15:33 Tujila hhende kieliewo, "Ene hontande imeghei kunlade ijie chudughaku ginan bijiende khalase irene?"
MAT 15:34 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Tande ginan giedughon wo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Dolon wo, pse giedun ga zhaghasun wo."
MAT 15:35 Ersa olon kunlai fenfulazhi zemin jiere soughadene
MAT 15:36 dolon ginan, giedun zhaghasunyi barei mafan kieliedene ghulu tujilade ogise tujila olon kunlade ogiwo.
MAT 15:37 Dajiala man ijiezhi chududene feiliesan zhazhai dolon lanzi zhonlowo.
MAT 15:38 Ijiesan kun dunda bierei kewosilai ulie sanase 4000 ere kun wo.
MAT 15:39 Ersa kunlai sandaghadene chon jiere khirei Majiadan oronde echiwo.
MAT 16:1 Falisai kun, Sadugai kunla Ersai shida iredene hhei shiizhi asiman jierese iresan ghudureqi uzhegha giezhi yoqiu giezho.
MAT 16:2 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Khara olukude olien shouizhi daose, 'Maghashijie arulune.' giezhi ta kieliene.
MAT 16:3 Eqiemagha olien shouizhi dao dase, 'Enedu kei feiliezhi ghura boune.' giezhi kieliene. Ta asimanni qinkonyi fenjine, ene shidaini ghudureqini fenji dane.
MAT 16:4 Ene idaini kunla, doghun nefuxin giezho, ta dou ghudureqi kerezhoma, Yunusii ghudureqise chugo uzheghaku ghudureqi uwo." Ingiedene hhelase likai giewo.
MAT 16:5 Tujila hai duimiende daose ginan bareikui matazho.
MAT 16:6 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta Falisai kun, Sadugai kunlai kuniegheni jinxin giezhi fangula."
MAT 16:7 Tujila nieniedene kielienduzho, "Matan ginan ese bareise ingiezhi kieliezhoba."
MAT 16:8 Ersa mejiedene kieliewo, "Ta ene xianxin gieku zhughe gajitu kunla, ta yangiezhi ginan wikui kielienduzho?
MAT 16:9 Ta dou minbai olu dazhou? Tawun ginanyi 5000 kunde ogizhi giedun lanzi zhonlosei jila danu?
MAT 16:10 Pse dolon ginanyi 4000 kunde ogizhi giedun lanzi zhonlosei jila danu?
MAT 16:11 Bi kieliesanshi ginanyi ese kieliesei ta matugie mejie dane? Ta jinxin giezhi Falisai kun, Sadugai kunlai kuniegheni fangula."
MAT 16:12 Ingiekude tujila Ersa ginan kuniegheni ese kieliezhi Falisai kun, Sadugai kunla surughasei fangula giesei mejiewo.
MAT 16:13 ErsaKaisaliya-Feilibi oronde iredene tujiladene asazho, "Kunla kieliese Kunnikewonshi kien wo giezho?"
MAT 16:14 Hhela kieliewo, "Kunla kieliese xili gieghasan Yaheiya wo giezho. Niezhan kunla kieliese Iliya wo giezho. Pse niezhan kunla kieliese Yelimi onu, xienzhi dundadu nie wo giezho."
MAT 16:15 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta kieliese bishi kien wo?"
MAT 16:16 Ximun-Beduru kieliewo, "Chishi Mexiha wo. Chanqiku Hudai kewon wo."
MAT 16:17 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Ximun-Bayena, chade fuqi wine! Enei chade mejieghasanshi kun pusho, asiman jieredu adami wo.
MAT 16:18 Bi pse chade kielieye, chishi Beduru wo. Bi jiohuine ene tashi jiere giene. Dozoni lilian hhense inji dane.
MAT 16:19 Bi asiman gojiani yeshii chade ogiye. Chi zemin jiere yan banlase asiman jiereye yan banlane. Chi zemin jiere yan andaghase asiman jiereye yan andaghane."
MAT 16:20 Ingiedene Ersa, "Goyaneshi Mexiha bikui kiemade bu kielie!" giezhi tujilade fenfulawo.
MAT 16:21 Hhe shihouse Ersa matugieseda Yelusalende echidene zhanlao, fugie buwa, jinwun hanjialase hende shouku giezhi goyai aladene ghurudude aminne olukui tujiladene kielie qiiwo.
MAT 16:22 BeduruErsai laidene kheila qiiwo, "Ezhan, ulie olune! Intui chii jiere ulie irene."
MAT 16:23 Ersa ochira daore Bedurude kieliewo, "Ibilisi, mii khuina dao! Chi mii unaghane. Chi Hudai isii ulie sumulazhi kunni isii sumulane."
MAT 16:24 Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Kien mii daghane giese goyane sheidene shizijiane beiliezhi mii daghakuni wo.
MAT 16:25 Kien aminne jiuine giese aminne widaghane. Made oluzhi aminne widaghase aminne ulie widaghane.
MAT 16:26 Kun duyani man zhenjidene goya aminne widaghase yande gou wo? Kun pse yanghala aminne arunzhane?
MAT 16:27 Kunnikewon qienxienlarene hhantu hhei adani fama dunda irene. Ingiekude zhao kunni giekughala jien kunde kharulune.
MAT 16:28 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, enende beisan kun dunda niezhanla Kunnikewon qienline bareizhi irekui ulie chanlatula ulie fugune."
MAT 17:1 Zhighudu daose ErsaBeduru, Yagebu, Yagebui jiuni Yaheiyai danxin uduru undu ulade khireidene
MAT 17:2 hhelai melie bienjiwo. Ungieni naran mutun gieghan wo, jienni chighande gon niekielien wo.
MAT 17:3 Menzhali Musa, Iliyaghala Ersare kielien kieliesei hhela chujieghewo.
MAT 17:4 BeduruErsade kieliezho, "Ezhan, matan enende gou wo. Chi duran bise bi enende ghuran zhanfan daiye. Niei chade, niei Musade, niei Iliyade."
MAT 17:5 Beduru kieliekude menzhali niegieda gon faisan olien iredene hhelai khawo. Oliense shenqi irezhi kieliewo, "Eneshi bi oresan mii kewon wo. Bi hhende xiqi wo. Ta hhei kielienyi chenlie!"
MAT 17:6 Tujila sonosudene hende ayizhi zemin jiere papalawo.
MAT 17:7 Ersa melie iredene hhelai maqizhi kieliewo, "Bosizhe, bu ayi."
MAT 17:8 Hhela qiorunne qila uzhese Ersase chugo kiemai ese chanlawo.
MAT 17:9 Ulase boukude Ersa hhelade fenfulazhi kieliewo, "Kunnikewon fugusan kun dundase aminne ulie olutula ta chanlasei kiemade bu kielie."
MAT 17:10 Tujila Ersade asawo, "Qinse jinwun hanjiala yangiezhi Iliya ijinyo xien irene giezhi kieliezho?"
MAT 17:11 Ersa kieliewo, "Iliya irezhi man erchan gie goudaghanema,
MAT 17:12 bi tande kielieye, hhe ijin irezhoma, kunla hhei tani dazhi shimatu giezho. Kunnikewonniye niekielienji zayalane."
MAT 17:13 Ersa xili gieghasan Yaheiyai zhiizhi kieliesei tujila caigie minbai oluzho.
MAT 17:14 Ersa tujilarene iban kunlai shida irese nie kun Ersai melie ire xiutuliezhi kieliewo,
MAT 17:15 "Ezhan, mii kewonde ubali nie xii! Hhende kharalaku gien kurudene tendun fugie wo. Haojihui khande usude anda bouzho.
MAT 17:16 Bi udurudene tujila shidachii echise hhela goudagha dane."
MAT 17:17 Ersa kieliewo, "Ai, ta ene xianxin gieku witu, xiemecha yochen kunla, bi tanse rennai giezhi giedoghoncha beine? Kewonni uduruzhi mii enende ire!"
MAT 17:18 Ersa sheitanyi nie sugiese sheitan khizhewo. Hhe shihoude kewon goudawo.
MAT 17:19 Ingiekude tujila Ersai shida konkonji ire asawo, "Bijien yangiezhi ene sheitanyi khigha dane?"
MAT 17:20 Ersa kieliewo, "Tai xianxin gieku texien gaji wo. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, tande caizi fure chigei xianxin gieku bise ta ene ulade enense noidene hhende dao giezhi kieliese daone, ingiese ta yama gie dakui uwo."
MAT 17:22 Hhela Jialilide hhantulakude Ersa tujilade kieliewo, "Kunnikewonni kunlai khade jiuidene
MAT 17:23 hhela alase ghurudude aminne olune." Ingiese tujila hende yuchou giezho.
MAT 17:24 Hhela Jiabainunde irese mechide shui shanjisan kunla Bedurui melie ire kieliewo, "Tai loushi shui ulie jiuinu?"
MAT 17:25 Beduru kieliewo, "Jiuine." Beduru giedoura orose Ersa xien hhende asawo, "Ximun, chii isi matugiezho? Duyani honshanla kiense shui, baer ghurazho? Goya kunlase onu, niman kunlase wo?"
MAT 17:26 Beduru kieliezho, "Niman kunlase wo." Ersa kieliezho, "Qingiese goya kunlanughunne mienlienema,
MAT 17:27 matan reikusene ayine, chi haibienzide echisenu zhaghasun barei. Touchan bareisan amanyini keighama, nie miengui chanlane. Chi agizhi echidene matan ghualanughunyi jiui."
MAT 18:1 Hhe shihoude tujilani Ersai shida ire asawo, "Asiman gojiade kien zui fugie wo?"
MAT 18:2 Ersa nie kewosii uruzhi ire hhelai dunda beighadene kieliewo,
MAT 18:3 "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ta geizhen giezhi kewosi mutun ulie gholuse asiman gojiade oro dane.
MAT 18:4 Ingiese kien ene kewosi mutun goyane meilade uzhese asiman gojiade zui fugie wo.
MAT 18:5 Kien mii niereghala intu kewosii jienliese mii jienliezho."
MAT 18:6 "Kien mii xianxin giesan enezighan ga kun dundadu niei zui fanjighase ghuzhundeni qiemanshai banladene haini gunde boughase da gou wo.
MAT 18:7 Zui fanjiku yenyinghala ene duyade gou widawo. Zui fanjighaku shiqin chan winema, kunlai zui fanjighasan hhe kunde gou widawo!
MAT 18:8 Chii nie kha onu nie kon chii zui fanjighase chizhidene benda! Ghua kha ghua kon bidene chanqiku khande bendatula nie kha onu nie kon feiliedene chanqi amitukude orose da gou wo.
MAT 18:9 Chii nie nudun chii zui fanjighase waidene benda! Ghua nudun bidene dozoheini khande bendatula nie nudun feiliedene chanqi amitukude orose da gou wo."
MAT 18:10 "Ta xioxin giezhi enezighan ga kun dundase nieiliuzhe meilade bu uzhe. Bi tande kielieye, hhelai qienxienla asiman jieredu adaimi shida chanqi wine.
MAT 18:12 Nie kunde 100 gie ghoni wo. Nieni yo widase ta sumulase matugiene? 99 gieni ulade jiesenu widasan ghonii ereile ulie echinu?
MAT 18:13 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, hhe ereizhi oluse uye widasan 99 giese da olon bayasune.
MAT 18:14 Tai asiman jieredu adaye niekielien wo. Enezighan ga kun dundadu nieiliuzhe widaghaku duran uwo."
MAT 18:15 "Gaijiuchii zui fanjise hhei hhende echizhi zinie ta ghuala bikude codaseini kielie. Hhe chii kielienyi chenliese chade nie gaijiu olodowo.
MAT 18:16 Hhe ulie chenliese kun nie ghua urudene tanghala echi. Ingiese 'jien zhasan shiqinlai ghua, ghuran kunni ganzhenghala shidaghane.'
MAT 18:17 Hhe pse ulie chenliese jiohuide kielie. Jiohuini kunlanughunyiye ulie chenliese niman kun, shui shanjisan kun mutun uzhe.
MAT 18:18 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ta zemin jiere yan banlase, asiman jiereye yan banlane. Ta zemin jiere yan andaghase asiman jiereye yan andaghane.
MAT 18:19 Bi pse tande kielieye, tai dunda ghuala hhantulazhi nie zhugheghala zemin jiere onxian giesanlai asiman jiereshiku adami man chenjighane.
MAT 18:20 Ghua ghuran kun mii niereghala khala hhantulase bi hhelai dunda wine."
MAT 18:21 Ingiekude Beduru shidani ire kieliewo, "Ezhan, jiumi made gieduifa zui fanjise bi gieduifa hhei rouliene? Doleifashi kurulie?"
MAT 18:22 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chade kielieye, doleifa ulie kurune, 70 gie doleifa wo.
MAT 18:23 Ingiese asiman gojiashi hoxian honshan hojilarene zhan sanaku niekielien wo.
MAT 18:24 Sanazhi qiikude 50 on antan chaisan kunyi uduruzhi irewo.
MAT 18:25 Hhende yama honjikui uwo, ezhanni minlin xiaizhi hhei, biereiini, kesilaini, pse bisanlaini man huidene honji giezho.
MAT 18:26 Hhe hoji papaladene, 'Made shijien pse gouji ogi, bi man honjine.' giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 18:27 Ezhanni hhende ubali xiidene andaghazhi chaisan baerni man rouliewo."
MAT 18:28 "Ene hoji khizhedene hhende hharan miengu chaisan hhantuku kunyi penjidene bareizhi ghuzhunsei nieqidene, 'Chaisan baerni iregha.' giezho.
MAT 18:29 Hhantuku kunni papaladene 'Shijien gouji ogima, bi honjiye.' giezhi xiahua giezho.
MAT 18:30 Hhe kun ulie olune giedene chaisan baerni honjitula bafanzide khazho.
MAT 18:31 Pseshiku hojila enei chanladene hende nango giedene echi ene shiqinyi man ezhandene huibao giewo.
MAT 18:32 Ingie ezhanni hhe kunyi uru iredene kieliewo, 'Chi ene doghun hoji! Chi mii xiahua giese bi chi chaisanlai man rouliewo.
MAT 18:33 Bi chade ubali xiizho giezhi chi hhantuku kundene qingiezhi indan ubali xiise ulie olunu?'
MAT 18:34 Ezhanni hende hokudene chaisan baerni man honjitula bafanzi sagheisan kunlade jiuizhi eghighazho.
MAT 18:35 Ta gaijiune zhughesene ingiezhi ulie rouliese asiman jieredu adamiye tande ingiezhi giene."
MAT 19:1 Ersa ene kielienlai kielie baraghadene Jialilise likai giezhi Yedanhe duimienni Yudaya oronde irewo.
MAT 19:2 Tebieji olon kunla hhei daghazho, Ersa hhende kunlai goudaghawo.
MAT 19:3 Falisai kunla ire Ersai shiizhi asazho, "Kun yan yenyinghalaliuzhe biereine lihun gieghase olunulie?"
MAT 19:4 Ersa kieliewo, "Kunyi zhayaghasan Huda dei qiikude ere kun, eme kunyi zhayaghawo giezho.
MAT 19:5 Pse, 'Ingiese kun ada anasene likai giedene biereighalane hhantulazhi ghuala nie beye gholune.' giezhi kieliesan jinwunni ta onshizhi ese daowu?
MAT 19:6 Hhela ghua pusho, nie wo. Ingiese Huda hhantulaghasei kun fenkai gieghase ulie olune."
MAT 19:7 Falisai kunla asawo, "Qinse Musa yangiezhi lihun qiuzi ogidene lihun gie giezhi fenfulawo?"
MAT 19:8 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Tai zhughe khidunshi Musa ta biereine lihun gieghase olune giezhoma, dei qiikude ingie ese giezho.
MAT 19:9 Bi tande kielieye, kien lon kijieku yenyinse chugo biereighalane lihun giedene pse agise piofen giezho."
MAT 19:10 Tujilani Ersade kieliewo, "Ere kun bierei kunyi gonxi imutuishi jiehun ulie giese da gou wo."
MAT 19:11 Ersa kieliewo, "Ene kielienyi kienliuzhe man jienlie shidaku pusho, kiende nengou ogise kien jienliene.
MAT 19:12 Niezhan kunla olusanse jiehun gie dane. Niezhan kunlai kunla ataladene jiehun gie dane. Pse niezhan kunla asiman gojiade oluzhi goyane jiehun ulie giene. Ene kielienyi kien jienlie shidase jienliedu."
MAT 19:13 Ingiekude kunla kesilane uduruzhi Ersai melie ire hhelai jiere kha teizhi onxian gieghane giese tujila hhelai sugiezho.
MAT 19:14 Ingiese Ersa kieliezho, "Kesilai bu dui, mii shida ire gie. Asiman gojiashi imutu kunlanughun wo."
MAT 19:15 Ersa hhelai jiere khane teidene hhense likai giewo.
MAT 19:16 Nie kun Ersai melie iredene kieliewo, "Loushi, bi yan gouni giese chanqiku amin wine?"
MAT 19:17 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi made yangiezhi gouni asane? Zi niekozishi gouni wo. Chi chanqiku aminyi jienliene giese minlinni zunji."
MAT 19:18 Hhe asawo, "Yan minlin wo?" Ersa kieliewo, "Kun bu ala, piofen bu gie, bu ghula, jia ganzhen bu bei,
MAT 19:19 ada anane zunji, goyadene mutun giebeidene ore."
MAT 19:20 Nasuchighan kun kieliewo, "Enelai bi man zunjiwo, pse yan chaizho?"
MAT 19:21 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi man qiendaghaku duran bise echidene bisanlane man huizhi nanxin kunlade ogi. Ingiese chii boubei asiman jiere wo. Ingiedene irezhi mii dagha."
MAT 19:22 Nasuchighan kunde caichan olonshi ene kielienyi chenliedene yuchourazhi yolawo.
MAT 19:23 Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, bayan kun asiman gojiade oroku chijia wo.
MAT 19:24 Bi tande pse kielieye, loto zhun boghose daoku bayan kun Hudai gojiade orokuse da sunfan wo."
MAT 19:25 Tujila enei chenliedene ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Ingiese kienyi jiui shidane?"
MAT 19:26 Ersa hhelai uzhedene kieliewo, "Kun enei gie danema, Huda yanniliuzhe giene."
MAT 19:27 Ingiekude Beduru kieliewo, "Uzhe, bijien man bendadene chii daghazho. Jianlai bijiende yan wine?"
MAT 19:28 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, shini duyade Kunnikewon goyane famatu baozo jiere soukude, ta enezighan mii daghasan kunlaye 12 gie baozo jiere souzhi Isilieni 12 gie paini gonjine.
MAT 19:29 Kien mii nierede oluzhi gie, gaijiu, eghechijiu, ada, ana, kesila, ghazhane bendase 100 pei ogine, da chanqiku aminni jienliene.
MAT 19:30 Ingiese olon melieshikula khuinashilane, khuinashikula melieshilane."
MAT 20:1 "Asiman gojia hoxian nie gieni zhanguijii xianli. Eqiemagha eqie khizhi echizhi kun guidene putou yenzidene wilie gieghane giezho.
MAT 20:2 Wiliechilaghala niudu nie miengu ogikui kielie goudaghadene hhelai putou yenzide echighawo.
MAT 20:3 Eqiemagha 9 jien olukude zhanguiji khizhi echise jide xien beisan kunyi chanladene
MAT 20:4 hhelade kieliewo, 'Taye putou yenzide ire, tande heshide baer ogine.'
MAT 20:5 Ingie hhela echiwo. Xiawu 12 jien, pse 3 jien olukude zhanguiji khizhi echidene ye ingiezhi giewo.
MAT 20:6 Hhe xiawu 5 jien olukude pse khizhi echise dou xien beisan kunni chanladene hhelade asawo, 'Ta niudu enende beizhi wilie giele yale ese echizho?'
MAT 20:7 Hhela kieliewo, 'Bijienyi kieme ese guizho.' Hhe kieliewo, 'Taye putou yenzide ire.'
MAT 20:8 Khara oluse putou yenzii zhanguiji duizhande kieliewo, 'Wilie giesan kunlai uruzhedene zui khuina iresanse baerlaini ogizhi zui melie kuru.'
MAT 20:9 Xiawu 5 jien olukude iresan kunla nie kun nie miengu linlawo.
MAT 20:10 Zui melie iresan kun iredene olon ogimu giezhoma, yen nie kun nie miengu linlawo.
MAT 20:11 Hhela linladene zhanguijide boxin giezhi kieliezho,
MAT 20:12 'Bijien khara naran doura niudu khishilazho. Enezighan khuina iredene nie zhuntou wilie giesan kunlai bijienre niekielien uzhezho.'
MAT 20:13 Ingiese zhanguiji hhelai dundashiku nie kunde kieliewo, 'Zhanlien, bi chii ese kuighazho. Matan ghuala kieliesanshi nie miengu wola?
MAT 20:14 Goyanughunne agidene echi. Zui khuina iresan hhe kunde chade ogisanghala niekielien ogise bi yenyi wo.
MAT 20:15 Bi duranghalane baerne injise ulie olunu? Bi gou kun danlase chi dubilienu?'
MAT 20:16 Ingiese khuinashikula melieshilane, melieshikula khuinashilane."

MAT 20:18 "Uzhe, matan Yelusalende khireine. Kunnikewonyi fugie buwa, jinwun hanjialade jiuise hhela hhei sixin panjidene
MAT 20:19 niman kunlade jiuine. Hhela hhei xilun giene, mabienzighala eghine, shizijia jiere ghada alane. Ingie ghurudude aminne olune."
MAT 20:20 Ingiekude Xibitaini bierei ghua kewonne uduruzhi Ersai melie ire xiutuliezhi xiahua giezho.
MAT 20:21 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi yan kerene?" Hhe kieliewo, "Mii onxianshi ghua kewonyimi chii gojiade niei chii borun miende niei soghei miende sougha."
MAT 20:22 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta ghuala yan keresanne ulie mejiene. Bi shouiku kuni ta shoui shidanu?" Hhela kieliewo, "Shouine."
MAT 20:23 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi shouiku kuni ta shouinema, mii lianmien kanzide soughakui bi ogiku pusho. Adami kiende zhunbei giezhoshi kiende ogine."
MAT 20:24 Psedu hharan tujini sonosudene hhe gaijiughalade hokuzho.
MAT 20:25 Ersa hhelai uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Niman kunlai dunda lindao, noyenla qienli bareizhi kunlai gonjisei ta mejiene.
MAT 20:26 Ta niekielien pusho, tai dunda kien fugieni danlane giese tande ushilachen kun danlakuni wo.
MAT 20:27 Tai dunda kien laoda danlane giese tande hoji danlakuni wo.
MAT 20:28 Kunnikewon irekushi kunlai ushilaghale ese irezho. Kharei kunlai ushilazhi aminne sheidene olon kunlade shuiku Jiage danlale irezho."
MAT 20:29 Hhela Yeligese likai giekude tebieji olon kunla Ersai daghazho.
MAT 20:30 Ghua sugho mo bienzide souzho. Ersa daosei sonosudene waradazho, "Ezhan, Dawudeni houdei, bijiende ubali nie xii!"

MAT 21:22 Ta xianxin giedene xiahua giezhi onxian giese man ogine."
MAT 21:23 Ersa mechide orodene kunlade sughakude fugie buwa, bexinlai zhanlaola hhei shida ire kieliezho, "Chi yan qienlighala ene shiqinlai giezho? Kien chade ene qienlii ogizho?"

MAT 21:26 Kunlase wo giese matan bexinlase ayizho, hhela man Yaheiyashi xienzhi wo giezho."
MAT 21:27 Ingie Ersade kieliewo, "Bijien ulie mejiene." Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Biye tande yan qienlighala ene shiqinlai giesei ulie kieliene."

MAT 21:32 Yaheiya tai hhende irekude gou moni uzheghazho. Ta hhei xianxin ulie giene, shui shanjisan kun, biozila hhei xianxin giezho. Ta hhela xianxin giesei uzhedene dou geizhen ulie giezhi xianxin ulie giene."
MAT 21:33 "Ta pse nie bilasei chenlie. Nie gieni zhanguiji nie yenzi putou zeiladene izhonyini qienjiwo. Sudoroni jiu daruku chizi waizhi yenzi uzheku teizi giedene kunlade bouizhi ogi, gholode echiwo.

MAT 21:38 Bouisan kunla kewonyini chanladene nieniedene kielienduzho, 'Eneshi jiachanni jienliechen wo. Matan enei aladene jiachanni zhanjiye!'
MAT 21:39 Ingie hhei bareidene putou yenzise tungu khigha alawo.
MAT 21:40 Ingiese putou yenzii zhanguiji irekude bouisan kunlai matugiene?"

MAT 22:1 Ersa hhelade pse bilazhi kieliewo,

MAT 23:1 Ingiedene Ersa olon kunlade, tujiladene kieliewo,
MAT 23:2 "Jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunla Musani guijinyi jieshi gieku qienli bareizho.
MAT 23:3 Ingiese hhela tande sughasei ta man zunjizhi giema, hhelai giekuni bu dagha. Hhela sughasanne ulie giene.
MAT 23:4 Hhela banlasan gundu danzilani kunlai dalou jiere jiedene goyala nie kha ghurunneliuzhe ulie gojiolughane.
MAT 23:5 Hhela giesan soyuji shiqinlane kunlade uzheghane giezhi giezho. Hhela zhoku jinwun xiaxiani giezhi fugiedaghazho. Jienni sasuiye giezhi fududaghazho.
MAT 23:6 Hhela xini shanxide, huitanni undu wizide soukude xiqi wo.
MAT 23:7 Giedoude kunla hhelade kielien asazhi loushi giezhi urukude xiqi wo.
MAT 23:8 Ta kunlai goyane loushi giezhi bu urugha, tande zi niekozi loushi wo, ta manshi gaijiu wo.

MAT 23:11 Tai dunda zui fugienishi tande hoji danlakuni wo.
MAT 23:12 Kien goyane undudaghase boghonidaghane. Goyane boghonidaghase undudaghane."
MAT 23:13 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta kunlade asiman gojiani wijienyi khazhi goyalane ese orozho, orone giechen kunlaiye ese oroghazho."
MAT 23:15 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta nie kunyi jiopaidene oroghane giezhi zemin haini yo baraghane. Hhei jiopaidene oroghadene dozoheini kun gholughazhi tanse da olon doghunshighane."
MAT 23:16 "Ta mo udurusan sugholade gou widawo! Ta kieliese mechii zhiizhi fayen giese yama ulie sananema, mechii antanni zhiizhi fayen giese kieliendene kuru giezho.
MAT 23:17 Sughotu guazila, alinieshi zhunyoni wo? Antan onu? Antanni zhiguishighasan mechi wo?
MAT 23:18 Ta pse kieliese sidagha gieku teizini zhiizhi fayen giese yama ulie sananema, sidagha gieku teizi jieredu dunxilai zhiizhi fayen giese kieliendene kuru giezho.
MAT 23:19 Sughola, daoji mure zhunyo onu mureni zhiguishighaku sidagha gieku teizi zhunyo wo?
MAT 23:20 Ingiese kien sidagha gieku teizini zhiizhi fayen giese sidagha gieku teizi, sidagha gieku teizi jiereshiku dunxilani man zhiizhi fayen giezho;
MAT 23:21 Kien mechii zhiizhi fayen giese mechi sudoro sousan Hudai zhiizhi fayen giezho.
MAT 23:22 Kien asimanyi zhiizhi fayen giese Hudai baozo, baozo jiere sousan Hudai zhiizhi fayen giezho."
MAT 23:23 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta bohe, huajio, ziranlasene Hudade ushirei ogizhoma, guijin jieredu gundande gieku, ubali xiiku, kekaoni enezighan genjia zhunyoni ulie giene. Enelai ta indan giekui wo, psedulaiye ulie giekui pusho.
MAT 23:24 Ta mo udurusan sughola, ta meiyen ghugheini liizhi khizheghane, lotoni hulun yenjine."
MAT 23:25 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta beizi, jiezilai mienzii wagha arughazhoma, sudoroni tanxin gieku, lon giekula duruzho.
MAT 23:26 Ta sughotu Falisai kunla, xien beizi sudorodui waghazhi arugha, mienziye arune."
MAT 23:27 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta fenshua giesan mezai xianli, ghadanese uzhese gou wo, sudoro fugusan kunyi yasun, yanyanji zannanni duruzho.
MAT 23:28 Taiye kunla mienzise uzhese gou wo, sudorotai jiazhon gieku, mouxienni duruzho."
MAT 23:29 "Ta jiazhon giesan jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunlade gou widawo! Ta xienzhilai mezai giezho, gou kunni jilaku peizii giezhi mezai goudaghadene
MAT 23:30 'Xienrenlane hhe xienzide bijien bizhoshi xienzhii chusunyi xienrenlarene hhantu ulie usurughane.' giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 23:31 Ingiezhi ta xienzhilani alasan kunlai houdei bikui zhenmin giezho.
MAT 23:32 Ta xienrenlane zuini giezhi baraghale echi!
MAT 23:33 Ta enezighan moghei, du mogheini zhunzhugha. Ta matugie dozoheini faikuse andane?
MAT 23:34 Ingiese bi xienzhi, aghelitu, jinwun hanjialai tai enende peizhi ireghane. Ta niezhanlai alane, niezhanlai shizijia jiere ghadane, pse niezhanlai huitande mabienzighala eghine, ene chenshise touzhi hhe chenshide echighane.
MAT 23:35 Ingiese gou kun Hhabise qiizhi izhi dajienji sidagha gieku teizi dunda alasan Balajiani kewon Sajialiyai zuini guide kurutula soyuji gou kunla usurusan chusunni guini man tai jiere ireghane.
MAT 23:36 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene guini man ene idai kunlai jiere ireghane."

MAT 24:1 Ersa mechise khizhedene yokude tujilani ire mechii loulani hhende zhiizhi uzheghawo.

MAT 24:3 ErsaGanlanshande soukude tujila konkonji ire asazho, "Yan xienzide ene shiqinla fashen giene? Chi irezhi duya barakude yan zunji bikui bijiende nie kielie."

MAT 24:12 Mouxienni olodozhi kunlai oreku zhughe widane.
MAT 24:13 Ingieliuzhe rennai giezhi zuihou kusanlai jiuine.
MAT 24:14 Asiman gojiani gouxioxini qienxiade chonji kurughazhi soyuji minzulade ganzhen beidene caigie duya baraku kuzhene."
MAT 24:15 "Ingiese Danyili xienzhi kieliesan hhe pohai giezhi hanzhan gieghaku zhiguitu oronde beisei ta chanlane. (Onshichen kunla, ene kielienni isii dunjirekuni wo.)
MAT 24:16 Ingiekude Yudayade sousan kunla, ulade piile echi.
MAT 24:17 Gie jieredula, giederase dunxi agile bu bouzhe.
MAT 24:18 Ghazha jieredula, khareizhi jienne agile bu echi.
MAT 24:19 Hhe udude kewosi laisan, gogoghasanlade gou widawo.
MAT 24:20 Ta holukude uncha, hhamuraku udui bu kuzhegha giezhi onxian gie.
MAT 24:21 Ingiekushi hhezighan udude zeinan zui fugie wo. Duya kaishi giesanse eli kutula imutu zeinan uwo, khuinashiye uwo.
MAT 24:22 Hhezighan zeinantu udui ese choghonshighazhoshi nieda jiui danema, sunghusan kunladene oluzhi choghonshighane.
MAT 24:23 Hhe udude kunla tande uzhe, Mexiha enende wo, hhende wo giese ta xianxin bu gie.
MAT 24:24 Jia Mexiha, jia xienzhila khizhezhi fugie ghudureqi, fugie shiqinlai giekushi sunghusanlaiye kenen miine.
