MAT 24:25 Uzhe, bi shiqinlai tande eqie kieliewo.
MAT 24:26 Ingiese kunla tande uzhe, 'Mexiha hontande wo.' giezhi kieliese ta khizhi bu echi. Pse, 'Uzhe, hhe giedera wo.' giezhi kieliese ta xianxin bu gie.
MAT 24:27 Shanjien dunmiense khizhezhi ximiende zhouiku mutun Kunnikewon irekudeye ingiene.
MAT 24:28 Fugusan dunxi khalashi inye khala wo."
MAT 24:29 "Hhezighan zeinanni udu jian daose naran kharalane. Sara gon ulie faine. Hodunla asiman jierese anda bouzhene. Asimanyi lilianla gojiolune.
MAT 24:30 Ingiekude Kunnikewonyi zunji asiman jiere khizhene. Zemin jieredu minzula man wilane. Hhela Kunnikewon nenli, famanude olien jiere irekui chanlane.
MAT 24:31 Laba fugiede tunguliese Kunnikewon qienxienlane peizhi asiman enemanse hhemande kutula sunghusan kunlane simiense uruzhi hhantulaghane."
MAT 24:32 "Ta uhuago mutunyi bilasei suru. Mutun niazi faizhi lachen keise khaluncha orokui ta mejiene.
MAT 24:33 Taye niekielien wo. Ta ene shiqinla fashen giesei man chanlase hhe shihou chadashizhi shida kuzhesei mejiene.
MAT 24:34 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene idaini kunla fugutula ene shiqinla man gholune.
MAT 24:35 Asiman, zemin widaliuzhe mii kielien kenjin ulie widane."
MAT 24:36 "Hhe udu, hhe shihouni kiema ulie mejiene. Asiman jieredu qienxienlaye ulie mejiene. Kewonye ulie mejiene. Zinie Ada mejiene.
MAT 24:37 Nuhhani xienzide matugiezhoshi Kunnikewon irekudeye qingiene.
MAT 24:38 Hunshuise melieshidaku hhe xienzide kunla ijiezho, ochizho, bierei agizho, dafalazhi izhi Nuhha chon sudoro oroku hhe udude kuruwo.
MAT 24:39 Yamai mejie dakude hunshui iredene kunlai man tou yolawo. Kunnikewon irekudeye ingiene.
MAT 24:40 Hhe shihoude ghua kun ghazha jiereshi niei uduru echine, niei jiene.
MAT 24:41 Ghua bierei qieman sidase niei uduru echine, niei jiene.
MAT 24:42 Ingiese ta jinxin gie. Tai Ezhan yan xienzide irekui ulie mejiene.
MAT 24:43 Ta enei mejie, giei ezhan ghughei yan xienzide irekui mejiese jinxin giezhi giedene ulie oroghane.
MAT 24:44 Ingiese ta goude zhunbei giendu, ta mejie dakude Kunnikewon irene."
MAT 24:45 "Qinse kienshi kekaotu jienzha hoji wo? Zhanguijini hhende giededu hojilai, ijiekulani man gonjighasan pushonu?
MAT 24:46 Zhanguiji irekude hoji ingiezhi giesei chanlase hhe hojide fuqi wine.
MAT 24:47 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, zhanguiji hhende caichanlane man gonjighane.
MAT 24:48 Hhe doghun hoji zhughedene sumulazhi mini zhanguiji deigo ulie irene gie,
MAT 24:49 psedu hojilai eghizhi sudosan kunlare ochizhi ijiese,
MAT 24:50 hhe sumula daku udu, mejie daku shihoude zhanguijini iredene
MAT 24:51 hhei sidasunyi qiuizhi jiazhon giesan kunlare hhantu faise hhende shidunne zhouzhi wilane."
MAT 25:1 "Hhe shihoude asiman gojia hoxian hharan shini bierei zhula bareidene shini khughonyi jienliekui xianli.
MAT 25:2 Hhelai dunda tawun benni, tawun jienzhani wo.
MAT 25:3 Tawun bennila zhula bareidene tosun ese bareizho.
MAT 25:4 Tawun jienzhanila zhula bareidene hulude tosun bareizho.
MAT 25:5 Shini khughon udazhi da ese irese hhela man nokuzhi kijie hhunturawo.
MAT 25:6 Banyedei kunla waradazho, 'Bosizhendu! Shini khughon irewo! Ghujighan jienliele khizhendu!'
MAT 25:7 Shini biereila man bosizhedene zhulalane zhendunlawo.
MAT 25:8 Bennila jienzhanilade kieliewo, 'Tosunsene gouji ogi, zhulabijienyi xiniene giezho.'
MAT 25:9 Jienzhanila kieliewo, 'Ulie olune. Manlade injizhi ulie kurune. Ta huisan kunlase agile echi.'
MAT 25:10 Hhela agile echikude shini khughon irewo. Zhunbei gie goudaghasanla shini khughonre hhantu ghurunde echise wijienyi khawo.
MAT 25:11 Khuinashi psedu shini biereila iredene kieliewo, 'Ezhan, Ezhan, bijiende wijienyi nieya!'
MAT 25:12 Shini khughon kieliewo, 'Bi tande shuhua kielieye, bi tai tani dane.'
MAT 25:13 Ingiese ta jinxin gie, hhe udu, hhe zhuntouni ta ulie mejiene."
MAT 25:14 "Asiman gojia hoxian nie kun gholode echine giezhi hojilane uruzhi ire baerne hhelade jiuizhi gonjighakui xianli.
MAT 25:15 Zhao hhelai benshizhe niede 500 antan, niede 200 antan, niede 100 antan ogidene gholode echiwo.
MAT 25:16 500 linlasan deigo echidene meimei giezhi 500 zhenjiwo.
MAT 25:17 200 linlasanye 200 zhenjiwo.
MAT 25:18 100 linlasan echidene zeminde oko wai ezhanne baerni niuighawo.
MAT 25:19 Hende oloncha beidene ezhanni ire hhelase zhan sanazho.
MAT 25:20 500 linlasan ezhanne shida ire zhenjisan 500 ne bareizhi kieliewo, 'Ezhan, chi made 500 ogiwo. Uzhe, bi pse 500 zhenjiwo.'
MAT 25:21 Ezhanni kieliewo, 'Giesan gou wo. Chishi gou, kekaotu hoji wo. Ga shiqinde shixinji giezho, bi chii olon shiqinlai gonjighane. Ezhanghalane hhantu bayasu.'
MAT 25:22 200 linlasan ire kieliewo, 'Ezhan, chi made 200 ogiwo. Uzhe, bi pse 200 zhenjiwo.'
MAT 25:23 Ezhanni kieliewo, 'Giesan gou wo. Chishi gou, kekaotu hoji wo. Ga shiqinde shixinji giezho. Bi chii olon shiqinlai gonjighane. Ezhanghalane hhantu bayasu.'
MAT 25:24 100 linlasan ire kieliewo, 'Ezhan, chishi jiafatu kun bikui bi mejiene. Ese tareisan oronse ghurane, ese shizhisan oronse hhantulaghane.
MAT 25:25 Bi ayizhi echidene chii 100 ni zeminde niuighawo. Uzhe, chii miengu enende wo.'
MAT 25:26 Ezhanni hhende kieliewo, 'Chi ene doghun, langantu hoji, bi ese tareisan oronse ghurane, ese shizhisan oronse hhantulaghakui chi mejiese
MAT 25:27 mii baerni inhande jiekuni wo, bi irekude benqien lixiji agi khizhene.
MAT 25:28 Ta hhei baerlani agi echidene hhe 1000 bisande ogi.
MAT 25:29 Bichen kunlade pse olon ogizhi feilieghane, wichen kunlase bisanlainiye agi echine.
MAT 25:30 Ene yama zoin witu hojini ghadanedu kharanide benda. Hhende shidunne zhouzhi wila gie!'"
MAT 25:31 "Kunnikewon qienxienlare man hhantu goya fama dunda irekude hhe famatu baozo jierene soune.
MAT 25:32 Duyani soyuji minzulai hhei melie hhantulaghazhi hhe hhelai fenji keighane. Hoxian ghoni adulachen ghoni, imanyi fenji keighakui xianli.
MAT 25:33 Ghonilai borun miendene teine, imanlai soghei miendene teine.
MAT 25:34 Ingie honshan borun mienne kunlade kieliene, 'Adami fuqi ogisan kunla, irendu. Duyai zhayaghazhi iresanse tande zhunbei giesan gojiani jienliendu.
MAT 25:35 Bi oliesukude ta made ijieghazho, undasukudei made ochighazho. Bi chumen giekude ta mii soughazho.
MAT 25:36 Bi hulan muchughun bikude ta made musighazho. Bi giemerekude ta mii ushilazho. Bi bafanzideshi ta mii uzhele irezho.'
MAT 25:37 Gou kunla kieliene, 'Ezhan, bijien yan xienzide chi oliesusei chanladene chade ijieghazhi undasusei chanladene chade ochighawo?
MAT 25:38 Yan xienzide chumen giesei chanladene chii soughazhi hulan muchughun bikude chade jien musighawo?
MAT 25:39 Pse chi yan xienzide giemeresei chanladene ushilazhi bafanzideshi chii uzhele irewo?'
MAT 25:40 Honshan kieliewo, 'Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ta enezighan mii gaijiu dunda zui ganide oluzhi giese made oluzhi giezho.'"
MAT 25:41 "Ingie honshan soghei mienne kunlade kieliene, 'Ta ene kharasan kunla, yola. Ibilisi, Ibilisii hojilade zhunbei giesan ulie xinieku khande oro!
MAT 25:42 Bi oliesukude ta made ese ijieghazhi undasukude made ese ochighawo.
MAT 25:43 Bi chumen giekude ta mii ese soughawo. Bi hulan muchughun bikude made ese musighawo. Bi giemerekude ta mii ese ushilazhi bafanzideshi ta mii uzhele ese irewo.'
MAT 25:44 Hhelaye kieliene, 'Ezhan, bijien yan xienzide chi oliesusei, undasusei, chumen giesei, hulan muchughun bikui, giemeresei, bafanzide bikui chanlazhi ese banman giewo?'
MAT 25:45 Honshan kieliene, 'Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ta enezighan kun dunda zui ganide ese oluzhi giese made oluzhi ese giezho.'
MAT 25:46 Enezighan kunla chanqi faikude orone, gou kunla chanqi amitukude orone."
MAT 26:1 Ersa enezighan kielienlai man kielie baragha tujiladene kieliewo,
MAT 26:2 "Pse ghuarudushi Jiulidaosan Jiei ta mejiene. Kunnikewonyi kunlade jiuidene shizijia jiere ghadazhi fugughane."
MAT 26:3 Qingiekude fugie buwa, bexinlani zhanlaola Gaiyafa giezhi urusan zui fugie buwai ghoronde hhantulazho.
MAT 26:4 Hhela piendaku banfaghala Ersai bareidene alane giezhi shanlian giezho,
MAT 26:5 "Jieqii udude ulie olune, bexinla londane."
MAT 26:6 ErsaBodanide pifugientu Ximunyi giede bikude
MAT 26:7 nie bierei ishighala giesan huapinde guizhuntu xianshuini hhei shida agizhi ire Ersa ijiezhi soukude qiorun jiereni kiewo.
MAT 26:8 Tujila chanladene hokuzhi kieliewo, "Ingiezhi lanfei giezhi yangiene?
MAT 26:9 Ene xianshuini olon baer huidene nanxin kunlade ogikui wo."
MAT 26:10 Ersa hhelai isii mejiedene kieliewo, "Ene biereide chijia teizhi yangiene? Hhe made nie gou shiqin giewo.
MAT 26:11 Nanxin kunla tanre chan hhantu woma, bi chan hhantu uwo.
MAT 26:12 Ene bierei xianshuini mii jiere kiekushi mii bulakude zhunbei giezho.
MAT 26:13 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene gouxioxini chonjizhi qienxiade kutula ene bierei gieseiye kieliezhi jilane."
MAT 26:14 Ingiedene 12 gie tuji dundadu Jialie kun Yuda giesan tuji fugie buwalai hhende echi kieliewo,
MAT 26:15 "Bi hhei tande bareighase ta made yan ogine?" Hhela 30 gie miengu ogiwo.
MAT 26:16 Hhe shihouse YudaErsai ghudanduku jihui ereizho.
MAT 26:17 Tanmien Jieni tou 1 qiende tujila Ersai shida ire asawo, "Bijien Jiulidaosan Jieni xini chade khala zhunbei giene?"
MAT 26:18 Hhe kieliewo, "Ta chenshini nie kunyi hhende echidene kielie, 'Loushi kieliezho, "Mii shihou ghujinlazho. Bi tujilarene chii giede Jiulidaosan Jieni daoghane."'"
MAT 26:19 Tujila Ersa kieliesan mutun echidene Jiulidaosan Jieni zhunbei giewo.
MAT 26:20 Khara oluse Ersa 12 gie tujirene hhantu xi souzho.
MAT 26:21 Hhela ijiekude Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, tai dunda nie kun mii ghudandune."
MAT 26:22 Hhela hende munan giedene Ezhan, bi pushoba giezhi nienieji asa qiiwo.
MAT 26:23 Ersa kieliewo, "Mare hhantu jiezise zhanjizhi ijiesan kun mii ghudandune.
MAT 26:24 Kunnikewon jinwun jiere huaisan mutun fugunema, hhei ghudandusan kunde gou widawo! Hhe kunyi ese oluzhoshida gou wo."
MAT 26:25 Ersai ghudandusan Yuda hhende asawo, "Loushi, bi pushoba?" Ersa kieliewo, "Chi enbene, goyane kieliewo."
MAT 26:26 Hhela ijiekude Ersa ginanyi barei onxian giedene ghulu, tujilade ogi kieliewo, "Ta bareidene ijie. Eneshi mii beye wo."
MAT 26:27 Pse beizii barei mafan kieliedene hhelade ogi kieliewo, "Ta man enei ochi.
MAT 26:28 Eneshi olon kunlai zuini mienliene giezhi usurusan bi yenjisan chusun wo.
MAT 26:29 Bi tande kielieye, bi pse ene putoujiuni ulie ochizhi adaimi gojiade tanre hhantu shinii ochiku hhe udu kune."
MAT 26:30 Hhela douladene khizhe Ganlanshande echiwo.
MAT 26:31 Ingiedene Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Ene xii ta man mii bendane. Jinwun jiere kieliezho, 'Bi yanbashii eghi unaghase ghonila sandane.'
MAT 26:32 Ingieliuzhe bi aminne oludene tanse melie Jialilide echine."
MAT 26:33 Ingiese Beduru kieliewo, "Kunla man chii bendaliuzhe bi jiedui ulie bendane!"
MAT 26:34 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Bi chade shuhua kielieye, ene xii tigha kheilatula chi mii 3 hui ulie renjine."
MAT 26:35 Beduru kieliewo, "Bi chare hhantu fuguliuzhe chii tani dane giezhi ulie kieliene!" Tujilaye man qingiezhi kieliezho.
MAT 26:36 Ersa tujilare nie Keximani giesan oronde ire tujilade kieliewo, "Ta enende sou, bi hhemiende onxian giele echine."
MAT 26:37 ErsaBeduru, Xibitaini ghua kewonni uduruzhi echiwo. Ingie yuchou giezhi nango gie qii
MAT 26:38 hhelade kieliewo, "Mii zhughede nango giezhi fugukui xianli. Ta enende sagheizhi mare hhantu jinxin gie."
MAT 26:39 Hhe goujinie melie yodene zemin jiere papala onxian giezhi kieliewo, "Mii ada, olu shidase ene shouku giekui made bu iregha! Ingieliuzhe mii duranghala bu gie, chii duranghala gie."
MAT 26:40 Ersa tujilai hhende irese hhela hhunturasei chanladene Bedurude kieliewo, "Ta mare nie zhuntouye jinxin gie danu?
MAT 26:41 Jinxin giezhi onxian gie, pse miine. Tai zhughede duran winema, beyetai zholien wo."
MAT 26:42 Ingie pse erchan likai giedene onxian giezhi kieliewo, "Mii ada, ene kuni bi ulie shouizhi ulie oluse, chi duranghalane gie."
MAT 26:43 Pse irese hhela hhunturasei chanlawo. Hhela nokuzhi nudunne nie dazho.
MAT 26:44 Ersa pse hhelase likai gie ji 3 hui onxian giele echiwo. Kieliesan kielien melieshidakughala niekielien wo.
MAT 26:45 Ingie tujilai hhende ire hhelade kieliewo, "Ta dou hhunturazhi hhamuranu? Uzhe, shihou kuzhewo. Kunnikewonyi zuirenlai khade ghudanduwo.
MAT 26:46 Bosizhe, matan yoye. Uzhe, mii ghudandusan kun irewo."
MAT 26:47 Ersa zhen kieliekude 12 gie tuji dundadu Yuda fugie buwa, bexinlai zhanlaola peisan idaban banban, khudogho bareisan kunlare hhantu irewo.
MAT 26:48 Ersai ghudandusan kun hhelade nie jihao kieliezho, "Bi kiende orese kien enbene. Ta hhei barei."
MAT 26:49 Yuda dei Ersai shida echi loushi, salan giedene orewo.
MAT 26:50 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Zhanlien, chi giele iresan shiqinne gie." Ingiese hhela melie ire Ersai bareiwo.
MAT 26:51 Ingiekude Ersare hhantuku nie kun khudoghoi lai khizhe zui fugie buwai hojii nie chighinyi chizhi agiwo.
MAT 26:52 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Khudoghone xiuzide orogha. Kien khudogho gojiolughase khudogho doura fugune.
MAT 26:53 Bi Adane xiahua giese hhe made deigo 12 gie buduitonse da olon qienxienyi ireghakui chi mejie dazhou?
MAT 26:54 Qingiese bixi fashen giene giezhi kieliesan jinwunlani matugie gholughane?"
MAT 26:55 Hhe shihoude Ersa kunlade kieliewo, "Ta khudogho, banbanlai bareidene mii qiandao mutun bareile irewu? Niudunie bi mechide soudene sughase ulie bareine.
MAT 26:56 Enela man fashen giekushi xienzhini shu jieredu kielienyi gholughane giezho." Ingiekude tujila man Ersase likai gie holu widawo.
MAT 26:57 Ersai bareisan kunla Ersai zui fugie buwa Gaiyafai hhende lai echiwo. Hhende jinwun hanjia, zhanlaola hhantulazho.
MAT 26:58 Beduru gholose daghazhi zui fugie buwai ghoronde orodene wijien sagheisan kunlare hhantu souzhi ene shiqin matui gholukui uzhezho.
MAT 26:59 Fugie buwa, zui fugie fayenni soyuji kunla man jia ganzhen ereizhi Ersai alane giezho.
MAT 26:60 Olon kunla khizhezhi jia ganzhen beizhoma, zhenji erei dazho. Zuihoude ghua kun ire kieliewo,
MAT 26:61 "Ene kun orun mechii cheidene ghurudude gie khigha shidane giezhi kieliezho."
MAT 26:62 Zui fugie buwa bosizhedene Ersade kieliewo, "Ene kunla ganzhen beizhi zhasande chi yama huida ulie gienu?"
MAT 26:63 Ersa shenqi ese khizhezho. Zui fugie buwa kieliewo, "Chanqiku Hudade bi chii fayen gieghaye. Chishi Mexiha, Hudai kewon enbese bijiende kielie."
MAT 26:64 Ersa hhende kieliezho, "Chi goyane kieliezho. Ingiezhoma bi tande kielieye, Ta enedu khuinashi Kunnikewon Nenlitu Hudai borun miende sousei, pse asimanni olien jierese irekui chanlane."
MAT 26:65 Zui fugie buwa jienne sida keigha kieliewo, "Hhe kufurei fanjiwo! Matan pse yan ganzhen beiku kun kerene? Hhe kufurei fanjisei ta jian chenliewo.
MAT 26:66 Ta kieliese matugiene?" Hhela kieliese sixin panjikuni wo giezho.
MAT 26:67 Hhela ungie jiereni nunpuzhi chuidazho. Niezhanla hhaghadazhi kieliezho,
MAT 26:68 "Mexiha, chii kien eghisei bijiende nie kielie."
MAT 26:69 Ingiekude Beduru ghadanedu ghoronde souzho. Nie hoji oqin hhei melie iredene kieliewo, "Chiye Jialilini Ersare hhantuku wo."
MAT 26:70 Beduru dajialai melie ese renjizhi kieliewo, "Chi yan kieliesei bi ulie mejiene."
MAT 26:71 Hhe wijien shida echise da nie hoji oqin chanladene hhendedu kunlade kieliewo, "Ene kunshi Nasale kun Ersare hhantuku wo."
MAT 26:72 Beduru pse ese renjidene fayen giezhi kieliewo, "Bi hhe kunyi tani dane."
MAT 26:73 Goujicha beidene shidani beisan kunla Bedurui melie ire kieliewo, "Chi kenjinshi hhelare hhantuku kun wo. Chii kouin chii mejieghawo."
MAT 26:74 Beduru fayen giezhi khara qiiwo, "Hhe kunyi bi tani dane!" Deigo tigha kheilawo.
MAT 26:75 BeduruErsa kieliesan tigha kheilatula chi mii 3 hui ulie renjine giesei sumula ire, khizhi echidene nango giezhi hende wilawo.
MAT 27:1 Eqiemagha oluse fugie buwa, bexinlani zhanlaola man shanlian giezhi Ersai alane giezho.
MAT 27:2 Hhela Ersai banladene laizhi Bilado shenzhande jiuiwo.
MAT 27:3 Ersani ghudandusan YudaErsade zui jinjisei chanladene houhui giezho. Hhe 30 gie mienguni fugie buwa, zhanlaolade khareizhi ogidene kieliewo,
MAT 27:4 "Bi hanhanji kunyi ghudanduse made zui wo." Hhela kieliewo, "Eneshi chii shiqin wo. Bijienre yan gonxi wo?"
MAT 27:5 Yuda miengui mechide benda jiedene khizhi echi jiuzhilie fuguwo.
MAT 27:6 Fugie buwala miengui qiangudene kieliezho, "Eneshi chusun qien wo. Mechini kufande teizhi ulie olune."
MAT 27:7 Hhela shanlian giedene hhe baerghala gan giesan kunyi ghazhai agizhi niman kunyi meza giewo.
MAT 27:8 Ingiese eli kutula hhe ghazhai chusun ghazha giezho.
MAT 27:9 Ingiese Ezhan Yelimi xienzhii tungo giezhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholuwo, "Hhela Isilie kun hhei aminde jinjisan 30 gie miengughala
MAT 27:10 gan giesan kunyi ghazhai agiwo. Eneshi Huda made fenfulasan wo."
MAT 27:11 ErsaBilado shenzhanni melie beizho. Shenzhan hhende asawo, "Chishi Yutai kunni honshan onu?" Ersa kieliewo, "Chi kieliezho."
MAT 27:12 Fugie buwa, zhanlaola hhei zhase hhe yama ulie kieliene.
MAT 27:13 Ingie Bilado asawo, "Hhela chii imegheni zhase chi ese sonosuzhou?"
MAT 27:14 Ersa nie amanda huida ese giese shenzhan hende ghanirazho.
MAT 27:15 Niefanie ene jieqide shenzhan bexinla keresan mutun nie fanren andaghaku xigon wine.
MAT 27:16 Hhe shihoude nie chumin giesan fanrenni Balaba giene.
MAT 27:17 Kunla hhantulakude Bilado hhelade kieliewo, "Bi tande aliniei andagha? Balaba onu, Mexiha giesan Ersa wo?"
MAT 27:18 Hhela Ersai dubiliezhi hhende jiuizhi ogisei hhe mejiedene ingiezhi asazho.
MAT 27:19 Hhe shenpantai jiere soukude biereini kun peizhi iregha kieliewo, "Chi ene gou kunni shiqinyi goujida bu gonji. Ene xii mii zhoujinde hhei yenyin jiere bi hende munan giezho."
MAT 27:20 Fugie buwa, zhanlaola bexinlai shanjizhi Balabai andagha, Ersai ala giezho.
MAT 27:21 Shenzhan hhelade kieliewo, "Bi ene ghualase tande aliniei andagha?" Hhela kieliewo, "Balaba wo!"
MAT 27:22 Bilado kieliewo, "Qinse Mexiha wo giesan Ersai bi matugiene?" Hhela man kieliewo, "Hhei shizijia jiere ghada!"
MAT 27:23 Bilado kieliewo, "Yangiezhi? Hhe yan doghun shiqin giewo?" Hhela pse hende waradazhi kieliewo, "Hhei shizijia jiere ghada!"
MAT 27:24 Bilado uzhese goya kieliesan yama oronde uwo, kharei londakui xianli. Ingie bexinlai melie usu agizhe, khane wagha kieliewo, "Ene kunni chusun usurusan zui mii jiere uwo. Ta goyalane danji."
MAT 27:25 Bexinla man hhantu kieliezho, "Hhei chusun bijien, bijienyi houdeini jiere ire gie!"
MAT 27:26 Ingiese BiladoBalabai andaghawo. Ersai mabienzighala eghidene kunlade jiuizhi shizijia jiere ghada giezho.
MAT 27:27 Shenzhanni buduila Ersai laizhi shenzhan sousan oronde echi, nie tonni buduilai man hhei shida hhantulaghawo.
MAT 27:28 Hhela Ersai jienyi teighadene dahun fudu jienyi musighawo.
MAT 27:29 Eghesunyi honshan zhoku maghalai onjidene qiorun jierei zhoghasenu borun khadei ghulusunyi bareighadene meliei xiutuliezhi Yutai kunni honshan, onsui giezhi xilun giezho.
MAT 27:30 Hhei jiere nunpuzhi qiorun jierei ghulusunghala eghizho.
MAT 27:31 Xilun gie balu, fudu jienyi teigha, jienyini musighadene lai shizijia jiere ghadale echiwo.
MAT 27:32 Hhela khikude Gulinaini nie Ximun giesan kunyi penjidene ninkounin Ersai shizijiai beilieghawo.
MAT 27:33 Gegeta giesan nie oronde kuruwo. Gegetani isishi qiorun yasun oron wo.
MAT 27:34 Buduila kudanni jiude huigha Ersade ochighase goujinie ochi ese ochiwo.
MAT 27:35 Hhela Ersai shizijia jiere ghadadene fendan qianguzhi jienyini ghughasenu
MAT 27:36 hhende souzhi uzhezho.
MAT 27:37 Peizi jiere eneshi Yutai kunni honshan Ersa wo giezhi zuinini huaidene qiorun qiendei guaiwo.
MAT 27:38 Ingiedene hhere hhantu ghua qiandaoi shizijia jiere niei borun miende niei soghei miende ghadawo.
MAT 27:39 Hhense yozhi daosan kunla sugiezhi qiorunne shuiqizhi kieliezho,
MAT 27:40 "Chi mechii cheise ghurudude gie khighane giesan, chi Hudai kewon enbese goyane jiuizhi shizijia jierese bouzhesha!"
MAT 27:41 Fugie buwa, jinwun hanjia, zhanlaolaye ingiezhi uzhezhi xiniezhi kielienduzho,
MAT 27:42 "Hhe kunlai jiuiwo, goyane jiui dane. Hheshi Isilieni honshan wo. Ede shizijia jierese bouzhe giema, bijien xianxin gieye.
MAT 27:43 Hhe Hudai kouizho, dou orunshi Hudai kewon wo giezho. Qinse Huda duran bise ede hhei jiui gie!"
MAT 27:44 Hhantu ghadasan qiandaolaye ingiezhi sugiezho.
MAT 27:45 Zhunwuse xiawu 3 jien olutula zemin man kharalazho.
MAT 27:46 Chabudu 3 jien oluse Ersa fugiede, "Ili, Ili, lamasabagedani?" giezhi waradazho. Isishi, "Mii Huda, mii Huda, chi mii yangiezhi ulie gonjine?" giezho.
MAT 27:47 Hhende beisan niezhan kunla chenliedene kieliezho, "Ene kun Iliyani waradazho."
MAT 27:48 Hhelai dundadu nie kun deigo holu echi, haimiende cui zhanji ghulusun jiere banla hhende ughawo.
MAT 27:49 Psedu kunla kieliezho, "Gouji saghei, matan Iliya hhei jiuile irenu ulie irekui uzheye."
MAT 27:50 Ersa pse fugiede nie warada, ho sirawo.
MAT 27:51 Zhen ingiekude dajienni sudorodu menlienzi jierese doura kei echidene ghua gholuwo. Zemin gojioluzhi tashila ghaluwo.
MAT 27:52 Mezala keizhi olon duya ijiesan shentulai beyela aminne oluwo.
MAT 27:53 Ersa aminne oludene hhela mezase khizhezhi zhiguitu chenshi Yelusalende oro, olon kunlade chujiegheghawo.
MAT 27:54 Baifuzhan, pse hhere hhantu Ersai sagheisan kunla zemin gojiolusan, psedu shiqinlai chanladene hende ayizhi, "Ene kunshi zhenzhenji Hudai Kewon enbene." giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 27:55 Hhende Jialilise Ersai daghazhi ushilasan olon biereila gholose uzhezho.
MAT 27:56 Hhelai dunda Modalani Mereiyen, YagebuYusufu ghualai anani Mereiyen, Xibitaini kewonlai anani wo.
MAT 27:57 Khara oluse Yalimataini Yusufu giesan nie bayan kun irewo. Hheshiye Ersai tuji wo.
MAT 27:58 Ene kun Biladoi hhende echidene Ersai beyeni xiahua giezhi kerewo. Ingie Bilado ogi giezhi fenfulawo.
MAT 27:59 Yusufu beyeni agi bouzhe, ganjin boside boui goudaghawo.
MAT 27:60 Tashide waisan goya shini mezadene teiwo. Pse fugie tashii ghoghoreighazhi meza kouzii duighadene likai giewo.
MAT 27:61 Hhende Modalani Mereiyen, da nie Mereiyenghala mezai duimiende souzho.
MAT 27:62 Khuichudushi hhamuraku udu wo. Fugie buwa, Falisai kunla Biladoi hhende hhantuladene kieliewo,
MAT 27:63 "Noyen, bijien jilase kunlai piendasan hhe kun ese fugukudei ghurudushi aminne olune giezhi kieliezho.
MAT 27:64 Chi ghurudu olutula mezai uzhezhi goudagha giezhi fenfula. Pse tujilani ghula echizhi bexinlade, 'Hhe fugudene aminne oluwo.' giezhi kieliene. Ingiese kun piendaku melieshikuse pse hendane."
MAT 27:65 Bilado kieliewo, "Ta buduilai uduru echi. Jinlianji uzhezhi goudagha."
MAT 27:66 Hhela echi meza kouzini tashii fenjidene buduilade goude uzheghawo.
MAT 28:1 Hhamuraku udu daozhi xinqini ogheikude Modalani Mereiyen da nie Mereiyenghala mezai uzhele irewo.
MAT 28:2 Menzhali zemin hende gojiolukushi Ezhanyi qienxien asiman jierese bouzhe tashii ghoghorei daogha jierei souzho.
MAT 28:3 Hhei yanzini gieghande gon faisei xianli, jienni chighande zhansunyi xianli.
MAT 28:4 Mezai sagheisan kunla ayizhi pugharadene fugusan kun mutun gholuwo.
MAT 28:5 Qienxien biereilade kieliewo, "Bu ayi! Ta shizijia jiere ghadasan Ersai ereisei bi mejiene.
MAT 28:6 Hhe enende uwo. Hhe kieliesan mutun aminne oluwo. Hhe kijiesan oronni ta uzhele ire.
MAT 28:7 Ta ghujighan echidene tujiladeni hhe fugusan kun dundase aminne oluwo. Tanse melie Jialilide echine. Ta hhende hhei chanlane giezhi kielie. Uzhe, bi tande kieliesei jila."
MAT 28:8 Biereila jindazhi mezase khizhe, hende bayasuzhi ayidene holuzhi tujiladeni kieliele echiwo.
MAT 28:9 Menzhali Ersa hhelai penji, "Ta gou onu?" giezhi kieliezho. Hhela shidani echi konsei qioru hhei beiizho.
MAT 28:10 Ersa hhelade kieliezho, "Bu ayi! Ta echidene mii gaijiulade Jialilide echi giezhi kielie. Hhela hhende mii ochirane."
MAT 28:11 Biereila echikude giedun uzhesan buduila chenshide echi, fashen giesan shiqinlai fugie buwalade man kieliewo.
MAT 28:12 Fugie buwa zhanlaola hhantulazhi shanlian giedene buduilade olon baer ogizhi kieliezho,
MAT 28:13 "Ta 'Bijien xieni kijiekude tujilani ire hhei beyeni ghula echiwo.' giezhi kielie.
MAT 28:14 Ene kielien shenzhanyi chighinde echise bijien hhende kieliezhi tai yama bu gieghaye."
MAT 28:15 Buduila baerni jienliedene hhela fenfulasan mutun giewo. Ene kielien Yutai kunyi dunda chonjizhi eli kuzho.
MAT 28:16 11 gie tujila Jialilide echizhi Ersa jinjisan ulade khireiwo.
MAT 28:17 Hhela Ersai chujieghedene beiizho, niezhan kunla inxin giezho.
MAT 28:18 Ersa melie ire hhelade kieliewo, "Asiman, zemin jieredu qienlilani man made ogiwo.
MAT 28:19 Ingiese ta echidene soyuji minzuni kunlai Ada, Kewon, Shenlinni niereghala xili gieghazhi tuji gholugha.
MAT 28:20 Bi tande fenfulasan soyujilai hhelade sughazhi zunjigha. Uzhe, bi duya baratula tanre chanqi hhantu wo."
MAR 1:1 Hudai kewon Ersa Mexihani gouxioxi ingiezhi kaishi giezho.
MAR 1:2 Isaiya xienzhini shu jiere huaizho, "Uzhe, bi qinsi kunne chii melie peizhi chii moni zhunbei gieghane.
MAR 1:3 Hontande nie kun waradazho, 'Ezhanni moni zhunbei gie! Hhei moni zhidagha!'"
MAR 1:4 Zhao ene kielien mutun xili gieghasan Yaheiya hontande irezhi kunlade xili gieghazhi, "Ta geizhen giendu, Huda tai zuini rouliene." giezhi chonjizhi kieliezho.
MAR 1:5 Yudayani go orondedu kun, Yelusalenyi kunla man Yaheiyai hhende echidene zuine renjizhi Yedanhede Yaheiyase xili jienliezho.
MAR 1:6 Yaheiya loto noghosunghala giesan jienyi musizhi arasunni pixie pixieliezho. Machazi, shimei ijiezho.
MAR 1:7 Hhe chonjizhi kieliewo, "Mase khuina irechen kun mase nenli fugie wo. Bi ghodeizhi hhende mahei deizi andaghaseye pei dane.
MAR 1:8 Bi usughala tai xili gieghazhoma, hhe Shenlinghala tai xili gieghane."
MAR 1:9 Hhe shihoude ErsaJialilini Nasalese Yedanhede ire Yaheiyase xilii jienliewo.
MAR 1:10 Ersa dei ususe khizhese asiman keizhi Shenlin ghoghochen mutun goyai jiere bouzhesei chanlawo.
MAR 1:11 Ingiedene asiman jierese shenqi irezhi kieliewo, "Chishi bi oresan kewon wo. Bi chade xiqi wo."
MAR 1:12 Deigo Shenlin Ersai biizhi hontande echighawo.
MAR 1:13 Hhe hontande souzhi Ibilisi 40 qien shiizho. Yewolase hhantu wo. Qienxienla ushilazho.
MAR 1:14 Yaheiyai barei echise ErsaJialilide ire, Hudai gouxioxini chonjizhi kieliewo,
MAR 1:15 "Udu kuruwo. Hudai gojia chadashiwo. Ta geizhen giezhi gouxioxini xianxin gie."
MAR 1:16 ErsaJialilihai bienzide yozhi daokude Ximun, Ximunni jiu Andelie haide on xiaisei chanlawo. Hhelashi zhaghasun bareisan kun wo.
MAR 1:17 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta iredene mii dagha. Bi tai zhaghasun bareiku mutun kun bareichen gholughane."
MAR 1:18 Hhela onni deigo jiedene hhei daghawo.
MAR 1:19 Ersa melie gouji yodene pse Xibitaini kewon Yagebu, Yagebui jiuni Yaheiyani chanlawo. Hhela chon jiere on huduzho.
MAR 1:20 Ersa deigo hhelai uruse hhela Xibitai adane, pse guisan kunlai chon jiere jiedene Ersani daghawo.
MAR 1:21 Hhela Jiabainunde kudene Ersa hhamuraku udude deigo huitande orozhi kunlade sughazhi kieliezho.
MAR 1:22 Chenliesan kunla hhe sughasande ghanirazho. Ersa hhelade sughadan jinwun hanjialai buxian wo, nie qienlitu kunni xianli.
MAR 1:23 Ingiekude hhelai huitande nie kunni zannan ruhher heizho. Waradazhi kieliewo,
MAR 1:24 "Nasale kun Ersa, chi bijienyi jiohoro bu gie. Chi bijienyi widaghale irewu? Chishi kien bikui bi mejiene. Chishi Hudase iresan hhe zhiguitu wo!"
MAR 1:25 Ersa hhei sugiezhi kieliewo, "Amanne menji. Ene kunni jierese khizhe!"
MAR 1:26 Zannan ruhher hhe kunni nie tigharagha, fugiede waradadene hhe kunni jierese khizhewo.
MAR 1:27 Kunla man ghanirazhi nieniedene asazhi kieliezho, "Eneshi yan shiqin wo? Eneshi nie nenlitu, shini daoli wo. Hhe zannan ruhherde minlin xiaise hhei kielienyi chenliene!"
MAR 1:28 Ingie Ersai minshen Jialili oronde man chonji keiwo.
MAR 1:29 Hhela huitanse dei khizhe Yagebu, Yaheiyare hhantu Ximun, Andelietai giede echiwo.
MAR 1:30 Ximunyi ghadunmekieni fashao gie kijiezho. Kunla deigo Ersade kieliewo.
MAR 1:31 Ersa hhei shida ire khasei feizhi bosighase fashao giesan daowo. Ingiedene ghadunmekieni hhelai ushilazho.
MAR 1:32 Khara oluse kunla yanyanji giemeresan kun, sheitan heisan kunlai man Ersai shida uduru irewo.
MAR 1:33 Chenshini kunla man wijien konde hhantulazho.
MAR 1:34 Ersa olon gientulai goudaghawo. Olon sheitanlai tou khighawo. Hhe sheitanlai kielien ese kielieghazho, sheitanla hhei tanine.
MAR 1:35 Khuichuduni eqiemagha ese ogheikude Ersa bosizhedene hontande echi onxian giezho.
MAR 1:36 Ximun hhantuku kunlarene ereile echiwo.
MAR 1:37 Ereizhi oludene hhende kieliewo, "Kunla man chii ereizho."
MAR 1:38 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Matan psedulade yozhi shidadu aghinlade jiomun chonjiye. Bishi ene shiqinde iresan wo."
MAR 1:39 Ingie Jialilini gochude man yozhi hhelai huitanlade chonjizhi sheitan touzho.
MAR 1:40 Nie pifugientu Ersai melie ire xiutuliedene xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Chi duran bise mini ganjinragha shidane."
MAR 1:41 Ersai zhugheni zholierese khane zhighazhi hhei maqizhi kieliewo, "Bi duran wine. Chi ganjinra!"
MAR 1:42 Pifugien deigo likai giese hhe ganjinrawo.
MAR 1:43 Ersa hhei echighakude hende fenfulazhi kieliewo,
MAR 1:44 "Chi kiemade yama bu kieliedene echizhi beyene buwade uzhegha. Musai shu jiere fenfulasan mutun beyechii ganjinrasande oluzhi Hudade mure ogizhi kunlade ganzhen bei."
MAR 1:45 Hhe kun khireidene olon kielien kieliezhi ene shiqinyi gochude kieliese Ersa khuinashi mindaminji chenshide echi dazhi zinie hontande wo. Go oronse kunla hhei ereizhi echizho.
MAR 2:1 Giedudu daose Ersa pse Jiabainunde echiwo. Ersa giedoura bikui kunla sonosudene
MAR 2:2 olon kunla hhantulazhi wijien konde oron goujida uwo. Ersa hhelade Hudai kielienyi chonjizho.
MAR 2:3 Nie tanhon giesan gientui jieran kun qienliedene Ersai hhende irewo.
MAR 2:4 Kun olonshi Ersai shida qienliezhi echi dazho. Ingie hhe bisan oronni giei nouzii cheizhi chouraghadene ruzi lienqien boughawo.
MAR 2:5 Ersa hhelai xianxin giekui uzhedene tanhon giesan gientude kieliewo, "Gaijiu, chii zuini mienliewo."
MAR 2:6 Giedun jinwun hanjiala hhende sousenu zhughedene sumulazhi kieliezho,
MAR 2:7 "Ene kun yangiezhi imutui kieliezho? Hhe kufurei fanjizho! Hudase chugo zuini kien mienliene?"
MAR 2:8 Ersa hhelai zhughenughunyi mejiedene kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi zhughedene imutui sumulane?
MAR 2:9 Tanhon giesan gientude chii zuini mienliewo giese sunfan onu, ruzine agisenu yo giese sunfan wo?
MAR 2:10 Kunnikewon duyade zuini mienlieku qienli bikui tande mejieghane giezho." Ingie tanhon giesan gientude kieliewo,
MAR 2:11 "Bi chade kielieye, bosidene ruzine agisenu giedene echi!"
MAR 2:12 Hhe kun bosidene deigo ruzine agi kunlai melieghun khireiwo. Kunla man ghaniradene Hudai kuaizhi kieliezho, "Bijien imutu shiqin uzhezhi ese daozho!"
MAR 2:13 Ersa pse haibienzide echiwo. Kunla man hhei shida irese hhelade sughazho.
MAR 2:14 Ersa melie yose Yalefeini kewon Liwi shui shanjisan oronde sousei chanlawo. Hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii dagha." Ingie hhe bosizhedene Ersai daghawo.
MAR 2:15 ErsaLiwini giede ijiekude olon shui shanjisan kun, zuirenla Ersa, Ersai tujilare man hhantu soudene ijienduzho. Imutu kunla olon Ersai daghazho.
MAR 2:16 Falisai kunni jinwun hanjiala Ersa shui shanjisan kun, zuirenlare hhantu ijiesei chanladene hhe yangiezhi shui shanjisan kun, zuirenlare hhantu ijiezho giezhi tujiladeni kieliezho.
MAR 2:17 Ersa sonosudene hhelade kieliezho, "Gien witu kunla deifu ulie kerene. Gientula deifu kerene. Bi gou kunlai ereile ese irezho, zuirenlai ereile irezho."
MAR 2:18 Hhe xienzide Yaheiyani tujila, Falisai kunla orozo bareizho. Kunla iredene Ersade kieliezho, "Yaheiyani tujila, Falisai kunni tujila orozo bareizho. Chii tujila yale orozo ulie bareine?"
MAR 2:19 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ghurunde iresan zhochenla shini khughon bikude matugie orozo bareine? Shini khughon hhelase hhantushi hhela orozo barei danema,
MAR 2:20 shini khughonni kunla lai echiku udu kuzhene. Hhe udude hhela orozo bareine."
MAR 2:21 "Shini popui khuichen jien jiere huduchen kun uwo. Qingiese hudusan shini popu khuichen jienni tanturaghasan pse fugiedane.
MAR 2:22 Shini jiuni khuichen tulunde zhonlochen kun uwo. Qingie zhonlose shini jiu tulunni ghalughazhi, jiu usuru khizhezhi tulunye qida olune. Shini jiuni shini tulunde zhonlone."
MAR 2:23 Nie hhamuraku udude Ersa boudei ghazhaghun yozhi daokude tujilani boudei qiorun sidazho.
MAR 2:24 Falisai kunla Ersade kieliezho, "Uzhe, hhela yangiezhi hhamuraku udude ulie giekui giezho?"
MAR 2:25 Ersa hhelade kieliezho, "Dawude, hhantuku kunlarene oliesukude giesan shiqinyi ta onshizhi ese daowu?
MAR 2:26 Yabiyata zui fugie buwa danlakude hhe Hudai giede orodene Hudade ogiku ginanyi ijiewo. Pse hhantuku kunladene ogiwo. Ene ginanyi buwase andase kiema ijiezhi ulie olune."
MAR 2:27 Pse hhelade kieliewo, "Hhamuraku udushi kunde giesan wo. Kunshi hhamuraku udude giesan pusho.
MAR 2:28 Kunnikewonshi hhamuraku uduni Ezhan wo."
MAR 3:1 Ersa pse huitande orowo. Hhende nie khani ghosan kun wine.
MAR 3:2 Kunla Ersa hhamuraku udude goudaghase zhane giezhi xianxide uzhezho.
MAR 3:3 Ersa khani ghosan kunde kieliezho, "Bosizhedene dunda bei."
MAR 3:4 Ersa kunlade kieliezho, "Hhamuraku udude gouni giese gou onu, huaini giese gou wo? Aminni jiuinu, heine? Alinie oluzho?" Hhela yama shenqi ese khizhewo.
MAR 3:5 Ersa hokuzhi zhouwine kunlai uzhezho. Hhelai zhughe khidunshi nango giezhi hhe kunde, "Khane khizhegha." giezhi kieliese hhe khane khizheghase khani goudawo.
MAR 3:6 Falisai kunla khizhi echidene deigo Hherodepai kunlare shanlian giezhi Ersai matui widaghane giezho.
MAR 3:7 Ersa tujilarene likai gie haibienzide echise tebieji olon kunla hhei daghazho. Olon kunla hhe giesan shiqinni sonosudene Jialili, Yudaya, Yelusalen, Itumai, Yedanheni dunmien, Tuilo, Xidun zhouwini oronse man hhei shida irezho.
MAR 3:9 Kun olonshi jigheidane. Ersa tujiladene chon nie zhunbei gie giezhi kieliewo.
MAR 3:10 Ingiekushi Ersa olon kunyi goudaghawo. Gientula man jigheidazhi hhei maqine giezho.
MAR 3:11 Zannan ruhherla hhei chanlase chishi Hudai Kewon wo giezhi niefanie papaladene waradazhi kieliene.
MAR 3:12 Ingiese Ersa hhelade hheshi kien bikui bu kielie giezhi hende minlin xiaizho.
MAR 3:13 Ersa ulade khirei, goya zhughe jieredu kunlane uruse hhela hhei shida irewo.
MAR 3:14 Hhe 12 gie kun sunghudene shitu danlaghawo. Hhelai goyarene chan hhantu beighazhi peidene jiomun chonjighazhi
MAR 3:15 sheitan touku qienli ogine giezho.
MAR 3:16 Hhe sunghusan 12 gie kunshi ErsaBeduru giezhi niere ogisan Ximun wo,
MAR 3:17 Xibitaini kewon Yagebu, Yagebuni jiuni Yaheiya wo. Ene ghualade ErsaBanniqi giezhi niere ogiwo. Isishi xinbinni olien tungulieku niekielien wo.
MAR 3:18 Pse Andelie, Feili, Badolomai, Matai, Doma, Yalefeini kewon Yagebu, Datai, Rexinpaini Ximun,
MAR 3:19 pse Ersai ghudandusan Jialie kun Yuda wo.
MAR 3:20 Ersa nie giedoura orowo. Kunla olon hhantulazho. Hhelade ijieku gunfuye uwo.
MAR 3:21 Ersai gieini kunla Ersa fenjiulizho giezhi kieliesei sonosudene khizhesenu hhei laizhi echine giezho.
MAR 3:22 Yelusalense bouzhesan jinwun hanjiala kieliezho, "Hhei jiere Biexibu wine. Hhe sheitanni touzii kouizhi sheitan touzho."
MAR 3:23 Ersa hhelai uruzhi ire bilazhi kieliewo, "Ibilisi matugie Ibilisini toune?
MAR 3:24 Nie gojia goyalane eghinduse hhe gojia bei dane.
MAR 3:25 Nie giede goyalane eghinduse hhe gie bei dane.
MAR 3:26 Ibilisi goyalane eghinduse hhela bei dazhi widane.
MAR 3:27 Kun liliantu kunyi giede orozhi dunxilai qianlane giese xien liliantu kunyi ulie banlase qianla dane.
MAR 3:28 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kunla fanjisan soyuji zui, hu kieliesanlai man roulienema,
MAR 3:29 Shenlinni hu kieliese chanqi ulie rouliene. Zui chanqi wine."
MAR 3:30 Ene kielienyi kieliekushi hhela, "Hhei jiere zannan ruhher wine." giezhi kieliezho.
MAR 3:31 Hhe shihoude Ersai anani, gaijiulani iredene ghadane beizhi kunlai Ersai urughale echiwo.
MAR 3:32 Olon kunla Ersai izhonde souzho. Ingie Ersade kieliewo, "Uzhe, anachii, gaijiulachii, eghechijiulachii ghadane chii ereizho."
MAR 3:33 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Kienshi mii ana wo? Kienshi mii gaijiula wo?"
MAR 3:34 Zhouwidene sousan kunlai uzhezhi kieliewo, "Uzhe, mii ana, mii gaijiula wo!
MAR 3:35 Hudai isii zunjizhi giesan kunlashi mii gaijiu, eghechijiu, ana wo."
MAR 4:1 Ersa pse haibienzide sughazhi qiiwo. Tebieji olon kunla hhei shida hhantulase hhe haini chon jiere khirei souwo. Kunla man haibienzide wo.
MAR 4:2 Ersa hhelade bilazhi olon sughazho. Sughakudeni hhelade kieliewo,
MAR 4:3 "Ta chenliendu, nie kun shizhile echiwo.
MAR 4:4 Shizhikudeni niezhanla mo jiere luise bunzhula ire ijie agiwo.
MAR 4:5 Niezhanla tura olon witu tashitu oronde luise tura ninkienshi niazi faizhi ghujin woma,
MAR 4:6 genzi uwoshi naran khizhe nie xiese ghowo.
MAR 4:7 Pse niezhanla eghesun dunda luise eghesun khizhezhi jigheidase bolu dawo.
MAR 4:8 Da niezhanla gou ghazhade luise osizhi fugiedadene 30 pei, 60 pei, 100 pei zhonjia souwo."
MAR 4:9 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"
MAR 4:10 Ersa niezheghanne bikude daghasan kunla, 12 gie shitu bilasan isii asazho.
MAR 4:11 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Hudai gojiai mimii tande mejieghawoma, ghadanedu kunlade bilazhi kieliekushi,
MAR 4:12 'Hhela uzhese minbai olu dane, chenliese dunjire dane. Pse kharei daorese Huda hhelai zuini mienliekuse ayizho.'"
MAR 4:13 Pse hhelade kieliewo, "Ta ene bilasei mejie danu? Qinse ta soyuji bilasei matugie mejiene?
MAR 4:14 Fure shizhisan kun shizhisanshi Hudai kielien wo.
MAR 4:15 Mo bienzide luisanshi kun Hudai kielienyi chenliedene Ibilisi deigo ire sudoro shizhisan kielienyi agi echiwo.
MAR 4:16 Tashitu oronde luisanshi kun kielienyi chenliedene bayasuzhi deigo jienliewoma,
MAR 4:17 zhughedeni genzi wise niechaku wo. Kielienyi yenyinghala zeinan onu heiku kuzhese deigo furawo.
MAR 4:18 Eghesun dunda luisanshi kun kielienyi chenliewoma,
MAR 4:19 duyai munan gieku, baer miiku, pse duyai yanyanji onxian giekughala kielienyi jigheidazhi yama sou dawo.
MAR 4:20 Gou ghazhade luisanshi kun kielienyi chenliezhi jienliedene 30 pei, 60 pei, 100 pei zhonjia souwo."
MAR 4:21 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Kun zhulai agi irese ighaghala komoronu? Chonban doura jienu? Zhula teiku teizi jiere jiene.
MAR 4:22 Niuighasanlai ulie khizheghakui uwo. Ghulazhi giesan shiqinlai ulie khizheghakui uwo.
MAR 4:23 Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"
MAR 4:24 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Ta goude chenliendu, ta kunlade yanghala nanjizhi ogise tandeye yanghala nanjizhi ogine, da olon ogine.
MAR 4:25 Bichen kunde pse olon ogine. Wichen kunse bisanlainiye agi echine."
MAR 4:26 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Hudai gojia kun fureni ghazhade shizhisei xianli.
MAR 4:27 Xieni kijiene, udu bosine, ene fure matui niazi faizhi osisei hhe kun ulie mejiene.
MAR 4:28 Ghazhase zhonjia goya osine. Xien niazi faine, khuinashi fugiedazhi qiorun khidene chuduzho.
MAR 4:29 Zhonjia boluse liendaoghala ghadune. Ghuraku shihou oluwo."
MAR 4:30 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Hudai gojia yanni xianli? Matan yanghala bilane?
MAR 4:31 Nie caizi furei xianli. Zemin jiere shizhisan furese zui gaji woma,
MAR 4:32 shizhidene khizhese yan caiseliuzhe fugie wo. Chalani fugiedazhi asiman jieredu bunzhula holiene."
MAR 4:33 Ersa zhao hhela dunjire shidaku mutun bilazhi olon kieliezho.
MAR 4:34 Bilazhi ulie kieliese hhelade ulie kieliene. Kun widakude tujiladene isii kieliezhi man mejieghazho.
MAR 4:35 Hhe xii Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Matan hai duimiende daoye."
MAR 4:36 Tujilani olon kunlase likai gie Ersa sousan chon jiere khireidene hhantu echiwo. Psedu chonlaye hhantu yozho.
MAR 4:37 Menzhali honfen kei bosidene lan chonni eghizhi chonde usu durune giezho.
MAR 4:38 Ersa chonni khuina zhentouni zhentoula kijie hhunturazho. Tujilani hhei xiereigha kieliewo, "Loushi, bijienyi amin widane giezho! Chi ulie gonjinu?"
MAR 4:39 Ersa xiereidene keini nie sugiezhi haide kieliewo, "Bei! Nanranshi!" Ingiese kei beiwo, fugiede nanranshiwo.
MAR 4:40 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi ayizho? Tande xianxin giekui uwonu?"
MAR 4:41 Hhela fugiede ayizhi nieniedene kieliezho, "Eneshi yan kun wo? Kei, haiye kielienyini chenliene."
MAR 5:1 Hhela hai duimienni Gelasen kunyi oronde irewo.
MAR 5:2 Ersa chon jierese bouzhese nie zannan ruhher heisan kun mezase khizhe Ersai shida irewo.
MAR 5:3 Hhe kun chan meza sudoro souzho. Hhei kunla banla dazhi qieshenghalaye han wo.
MAR 5:4 Kunla niefanie qieshen, jielioghala sozilase qieshenyi denji siraghazhi jielioni zhazhazi gholughane. Kiemada hhei hanshilie dane.
MAR 5:5 Hhe xieni uduji meza konde, ulade onghonozhi da tashighala goyane zaizho.
MAR 5:6 Hhe gholose Ersai chanladene holu ire hhei melie xiutuliedene
MAR 5:7 fugiede waradazhi kieliewo, "Zui Undu Hudai kewon Ersa, chi mii jiohoro bu gie. Bi Hudai zhiizhi chii xiahua gieye, mii bu zayala!"
MAR 5:8 Ingiekushi Ersa zannan ruhherde ene kunyi jierese khizhe giezhi fenfulazhi daozho.
MAR 5:9 Ersa hhende asawo, "Chii nierei yan giene?" Hhe kieliewo, "Bijien olonshi Iban giezhi uruzho."
MAR 5:10 Hhe Ersade oruntanyi hhe oronse bu yolagha giezhi hende xiahua giezho.
MAR 5:11 Hhe popo jiere idaban khighei ijiezhi souzho.
MAR 5:12 Zannan ruhher Ersade, "Bijienyi khigheilai dunda echighazhi hhelai jiere khigha!" giezhi xiahua giewo.
MAR 5:13 Ersa dain giese zannan ruhher khizhedene khigheilai jiere khiwo. Khigheila egheide chunji bou, haide yenji alawo. Khighei chabudu 2000 wo.
MAR 5:14 Khighei adulasan kunla holu echidene chenshi, aghinlade kieliese kunla yan shiqin fashen giewo giezhi uzhele irewo.
MAR 5:15 Hhela Ersai shida ire uzhese eqighandei "Iban" sheitan heisan hhe kun jien musizhi jinshen goudazhi souzho. Ingiese hhela ayizho.
MAR 5:16 Sheitan heisan kunde fashen giesan shiqin, khigheini shiqinyi chanlasan kunla kunlade kieliezho.
MAR 5:17 Ingiese kunla Ersai, "Enense likai gie!" giezhi xiahua giezho.
MAR 5:18 Ersa chon jiere khireikude eqighandei sheitan heisan kun Ersai xiahua giezhi hhere hhantulane giese,
MAR 5:19 Ersa dain ese giezhi hhende kieliewo, "Chi giedene echizhi jiawune kunlade Ezhan chade giesan fugie shiqin, pse matugiezhi ubali xiisei man kielie."
MAR 5:20 Hhe kun echidene Jijiapolide Ersa hhende giesan fugie shiqinyi chonji qiise kunla man ghanirazho.
MAR 5:21 Ersa pse chon souzhi hai duimiende daose olon kunla hhei shida hhantulazho. Hhe zhen haibienzide wo.
MAR 5:22 Nie huitan gonjisan kunyi niereni Yalu giene. Ire Ersai chanladene kon kondei papala
MAR 5:23 hende xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Mii ga oqin ede duya ijiene giezho. Chi yodene hhei jiere khane teizhi onxian giese hhe goudazhi aminne olune."
MAR 5:24 Ingiese Ersa hhere hhantu echiwo. Tebieji olon kunla hhei daghazhi jigheidazho.
MAR 5:25 Nie biereii chusun usurusan gien 12 nien olune.
MAR 5:26 Deifulai khade olon shouku giezhi bisan baerlane man huai widaghazho. Goujida ese goudadene kharei gundudazho.
MAR 5:27 Hhe Ersai shiqinyi sonosudene kunlai dunda jiaidene Ersai khuinase jienni nie maqiwo.
MAR 5:28 Hhe, "Ersai jienni nie maqise gienni goudane." giezhi sumulazho.
MAR 5:29 Ingiese usurusan chusunni deigo beizhi goyane uzhese goudawo.
MAR 5:30 Ersa jieresene nenli khisei deigo mejiedene ochira daozhe kieliewo, "Mii jienni kien maqiwo?"
MAR 5:31 Tujilani Ersade kieliewo, "Imegheni kun jigheidazho. Chi da, 'Kien maqiwo.' giezhi asane."
MAR 5:32 Ersa zhouwidene ene shiqinni giesan biereii uzhene giezho.
MAR 5:33 Ene bierei jiereni gholusan shiqinyi mejie, ayi pugharazhi Ersai melie ire papaladene shuhuane man kieliewo.
MAR 5:34 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Funi, chii xianxin gieku chii jiuiwo. Pinnande echi, chii gien goudawo."
MAR 5:35 Ersa zhen kieliekude huitan gonjisan kunni giese kunla kieliele irewo, "Oqinchii duya ijiewo. Loushii pse mafan bu giegha."
MAR 5:36 Ersa hhela kieliesei ese gonjidene huitan gonjisan kunde kieliewo, "Bu ayi, zi xianxin gie."
MAR 5:37 Ingie Ersa kunlai ese daghaghadene Beduru, Yagebu, Yagebui jiuni Yaheiya enela hhantu echiwo.
MAR 5:38 Hhela huitan gonjisan kunyi giede irese kunla fugiede wilazhi onghonozhi lon chouisei Ersa chujieghewo.
MAR 5:39 Sudoro orodene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi lon chouizhi wilazho? Oqin ese duya ijiezho, hhunturazho."
MAR 5:40 Ingiese hhela Ersai uzhezhi xiniezho. Ersa hhelai man tou khighadene ada, anaini, daghasan kunlai uduru oqinyi giedera orowo.
MAR 5:41 Ingie oqinni khai bareidene kieliewo, "Talita kumu!" Isishi oqin, bosizhe giezho.
MAR 5:42 Oqin deigo bosizhe yowo. Oqin 12 olune. Kunla hende ghanirazho.
MAR 5:43 Ersa ene shiqinyi kiemade bu mejiegha giezhi kunlade hende fenfuladene oqinde ijiuni ogi giezhi kieliewo.
MAR 6:1 Ersa hhense likai giedene goya orondene irewo. Tujilani hhei daghazho.
MAR 6:2 Hhamuraku udude Ersa huitande kunlade sughase kunla chenliedene ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Ene kunde khalase imutu benshi irezho? Hhende ogisanshi yan agheli wo? Hhe matugie imutu nenlitu shiqin giezho?
MAR 6:3 Eneshi hhe mujian pushonu? Mereiyenni kewon pushonu? Gaijiulani Yagebu, Yusei, Yuda, Ximun, oqinjiulani mai enende uwonu?" Hhela Ersade hokuzho.
MAR 6:4 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Xienzhini goya oron, goya minzu, goya giese chugo khalaliuzhe zunjine."
MAR 6:5 Hhela Ersai xianxin ese giese Ersa hhende nenlitu shiqinyi olon ese giewo. Zinie giedun gientulai jiere khane teizhi onxian giedene goudaghawo.
MAR 6:6 Hhela xianxin ese giese Ersa ghanirawo. Ersa go aghinlai yo baraghazhi sughazho.
MAR 6:7 Ersa 12 gie tujini uru ire ghua ghuaji peizhi echighakude hhelade zannan ruhher touku qienli ogiwo.
MAR 6:8 Ersa hhelade fenfulawo, "Mo yose zhugunse andase ijiuni, kuabao bu barei. Kakade maqie bu barei.
MAR 6:9 Maheine musidene jien ghua bu barei."
MAR 6:10 Pse hhelade kieliewo, "Ta alinie giede orose hhe oronse likai gietula hhe giede sou.
MAR 6:11 Alinie oronyi kunla tai ulie jienliezhi ulie chenliese hhense likai giekude kon jieredu turane kui boughazhi fandui giezhi zhenmin gie."
MAR 6:12 Shitula khizhi echidene kunlade, "Geizhen gie!" giezhi chonjizho.
MAR 6:13 Olon sheitanlai tou khighazhi olon gientulai jiere tosun fureizhi goudaghazho.
MAR 6:14 Ersai minshenyi chonji khireise Hherode honshan sonosuwo. Niezhan kunla kieliezho, "Xili gieghasan Yaheiya fugudene aminne oluwo. Ingiese ene nenlitu shiqinla hhei jierese khizhezho."
MAR 6:15 Psedu kunla kieliese hheshi Iliya wo giezho. Da kunla kieliese hheshi melieshiku nie xienzhi wo giezho.
MAR 6:16 Hherode enei sonosudene kieliewo, "Bi qiorunyini pienjisan Yaheiya aminne oluwo."
MAR 6:17 Eqighandei ene Hherode honshan jiuni Feilini bierei Xilojini yenyinghala kun peizhi Yaheiyai bareidene banlasenu bafanzide khawo. Ingiekushi Hherode hhe biereii agizho.
MAR 6:18 YaheiyaHherodede, "Chi jiune biereii agise ese oluzho." giezhi kieliezho.
MAR 6:19 Ingiese Xiloji hhei henjizhi alane giezhoma, ala dakushi
MAR 6:20 HherodeYaheiyase ayizho, hhei huizho. Ingiekushi Yaheiyashi nie gou kun, zhiguitu kun wo. Hherode hhei kielienyi chenliedene munan giezhoma kielienyini chenliekude xiqi wo.
MAR 6:21 Niudude gou jihui irewo. Hherodeni olusan udu kuzhese xi beilazhi fugie noyen, buduini lindao, pse Jialilini lindaolai xinlazhi irewo.
MAR 6:22 Xilojini oqin orozhedene wu jiuliwo. Hherode, xi sousan kunla man bayasuwo. Honshan oqinde kieliewo, "Chi mase yan kerese yan ogiye."
MAR 6:23 Pse fayen giezhi kieliewo, "Chi mase yan kerezhi xiahua giese mii gojiani olieliuzhe ogine!"
MAR 6:24 Hhe khizhi echidene anadene asawo, "Bi yan kerene?" Anani kieliewo, "Xili gieghasan Yaheiyani qiorunyi kere."
MAR 6:25 Hhe jindazhi orodene honshande kieliewo. "Bi xili gieghasan Yaheiyani qiorunyi kerene. Ede hhamusade donjidene made ogi."
MAR 6:26 Honshan hhantu sousan kunlai melie fayen giese hende munan giezhi fura dazho.
MAR 6:27 Honshan deigo nie binni peidene Yaheiyai qiorunyi agizhe giezho. Bin echidene bafanzide Yaheiyai qiorunyi chizhisenu
MAR 6:28 hhamusade donji ire oqinde ogise oqin anadene ogiwo.
MAR 6:29 Yaheiyai tujila enei sonosudene ire beyeini linlasenu mezade teiwo.
MAR 6:30 Shitula Ersai shida iredene giesan shiqin, chonjisanlane man hhende kieliewo.
MAR 6:31 Irewo echiwoji kun olonshi hhelade ijieku gunfuda uwo. Ingiese Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta ire, matan konkonji hontande yodene niecha hhamuraye."
MAR 6:32 Hhela chonni soudene konkonji hontande echiwo.
MAR 6:33 Olon kunla hhela yolasei chanladene hhelai tanidene go chenshise holuzhi hhelase melieshida kuruwo.
MAR 6:34 Ersa chon jierese bouzhese tebieji olon kunlai chanladene ubali xiiwo. Hhela adulachen witu ghonilai xianli. Ingie hhelade olon sughazhi qiiwo.
MAR 6:35 Khara olune gie tujilani hhei shida ire kieliewo, "Eneshi hontan wo. Shihou udazho.
MAR 6:36 Kunlai sandaghazhi hhela goyalane zhouwini go oron, aghinlade echidene agizhi ijiele echigieba."
MAR 6:37 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta hhelade ogizhi ijiegha." Tujila kieliewo, "Bijien 200 gie miengughala hhelade ginan agizhi ijieghanu?"
MAR 6:38 Ersa kieliewo, "Tande ginan giedughon wo? Nie uzhele echi." Hhela uzhedene kieliewo, "Tawun ginanji ghua zhaghasun wo."
MAR 6:39 Ersa hhelade fenfulazhi kunlai iban ibanji osuntu oronde sougha giezho.
MAR 6:40 Kunla iban ibanji souzho. Ibande 100 gie, 50 gie souzho.
MAR 6:41 Ersa tawun ginan, ghua zhaghasunyi barei, asimanyi uzhe Hudade mafan kieliedene ginanyi ghulu keigha, tujiladene ogise tujila kunlai melie teiwo. Ghua zhaghasunyiye kunlade ghughazhi ogiwo.
MAR 6:42 Dajiala man ijiedene chuduwo.
MAR 6:43 Hhela feiliesan ginan, zhaghasun zhazhai hhantulaghase 12 gie lanzi zhonlowo.
MAR 6:44 Ginan ijiesan ere kun 5000 wo.
MAR 6:45 Ersa deigo tujilai biizhi chon jiere khighadene xien hai duimienni Bosaidade echigha goyane olon kunlai sandaghazho.
MAR 6:46 Hhe hhelai khozhi yolaghadene goyane ula jiere khisenu onxian giele echiwo.
MAR 6:47 Khara oluse chon hai dunda wo. Ersa niezheghanne zemin jiere wo.
MAR 6:48 Ersa tujilai uzhese kei shun uwoshi chonni huaizhi chijia no wo. Xieni 3 jiense 6 jienni shihoude hhe haini usu jiere yozhi hhelai hhense daone giezho.
MAR 6:49 Tujila hai jiere hhe yosei chanladene perei wo gie waradazho.
MAR 6:50 Hhela hhei chanladene ayizho. Ersa deigo hhelade kieliewo, "Ta zhughelane tei. Bi wo. Bu ayi!"
MAR 6:51 Ersa hhelare hhantu chon jiere khireise kei beiwo. Hhela hende ghanirazho.
MAR 6:52 Ingiekushi hhela ginan ijieghasan shiqinyi minbai olu dazho. Zhughelani khidun wo.
MAR 6:53 Hhela haini daodene Genisaleni haibienzide chonni beighawo.
MAR 6:54 Chon jierese bouzhese kunla deigo Ersai taniwo.
MAR 6:55 Ingie kunla hhe oronne holu onjighadene Ersa khala bikui mejiese gientulai ruzide qienlie hhei shida irewo.
MAR 6:56 Ersa ali aghin, chenshi, xiande echise kunla gientulai qienliedene geidoude jiene. Ersai xiahua giezhi lien jien ghizhane nie maqigha giezho. Maqisan kunla man goudawo.
MAR 7:1 Falisai kun, giedun jinwun hanjiala Yelusalense ire Ersai hhende hhantulazho.
MAR 7:2 Ersai niezhan tujila khane ese wagha ijiesei hhela chanlawo.
MAR 7:3 Falisai kun, soyuji Yutai kunla man xienrenla sughasan xigonyi zunjizho. Khane ulie waghatula ulie ijiene.
MAR 7:4 Jise irese ulie waghatula ulie ijiene. Hhela da zunjisan xigon olon wo. Beizi, huhu, aduma enelai waghane.
MAR 7:5 Falisai kun, jinwun hanjiala Ersade asawo, "Chii tujila yangiezhi xienrenla sughasan xigonni ulie zunjidene khane ulie wagha ijiene?"
MAR 7:6 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Isaiya ta jiazhon giesan kunlai zhiizhi melieshida kieliesan ese codazho. Jinwun jiere kieliezho, 'Ene bexinla amanghalane mii zunjine, zhugheni mase gholo wo.
MAR 7:7 Hhela kunni guijinyi zhenzhenji daoli mutun kunlade sughazho, ingiese mii beiise yama oronde uwo.'
MAR 7:8 Ta Hudai minlinyi jiezhi kunni xigonyi zunjine."
MAR 7:9 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Ta goya xigonne zunjine giezhi Hudai minlinyi gou banfaghala bendawo.
MAR 7:10 Musa, 'Ada anane zunji, ada anane sugiesan kunni ala.' giezhi kieliezho.
MAR 7:11 Ingieliuzhe ta, 'Kun ada anadene bi tande ogi shidakui gurubani giewo.' giezhi kieliese
MAR 7:12 hhe kun ada anadene yama ulie giese olune giezho. (Gurubani isishi Hudade ogikui kieliezho.)
MAR 7:13 Ingiezhi ta goya xigonghalane Hudai kielienyi widaghazho. Ta dou intu shiqin olon giezho."
MAR 7:14 Ersa pse kunlai uruzhi ire hhelade kieliewo, "Ta man mii kielienyi chenliezhi minbai olu,
MAR 7:15 ghadanese orosan kunyi ulie zannanshighanema, sudorose khizhesan kunyi zannanshighane."
MAR 7:17 Ersa kunlase likai gie giedoura orose tujilani bilasan isini asazho.
MAR 7:18 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Taye minbai olu danu? Ghadanese orosan kunyi ulie zannanshighakui ta ulie mejienu?
MAR 7:19 Ghadanese orosan kunyi zhughede oro dazhi kielighun mekiende echizho." Ingiezhi kieliezhi ijiekulashi man ganjinni wo giezho.
MAR 7:20 Ersa kieliewo, "Kunyi sudorose khizhesan kunni zannanshighane.
MAR 7:21 Doghunni sumulakulashi kunyi zhughese khizhezho. Lon kijieku, ghulaku, alaku,
MAR 7:22 piofen gieku, tanxin, doghunni, piendaku, hu gieku, dubilieku, sugieku, kondaku, benni wo.
MAR 7:23 Ene doghun shiqinlashi man kunyi sudorose khizhezhi kunni zannanshighane."
MAR 7:24 Ersa hhense likai giedene Tuilo oronde echi nie giede orowo. Kunlade mejieghaku duran uwoma, ingieliuzhe kunla mejiezho.
MAR 7:25 Nie biereini oqinyi zannan ruhher heizho. Ersai shiqinyi sonosudene ire Ersai kon melieni papalawo.
MAR 7:26 Ene biereishi niman kun wo. Xiliyani-Feiniji minzu wo. Hhe Ersai xiahua giezhi oqinyini jierese sheitanyi tou khigha giezho.
MAR 7:27 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Kesilade xien ijiezhi chudughakuni wo, kesilai ginanyi ga nogheide bendazhi ogise ese oluzho."
MAR 7:28 Bierei kieliewo, "Ezhan, kesila ijiezhi feiliesan zhazhai nogheiye shire doura ijiene."
MAR 7:29 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Ene nie aman kielienghala chi khareizhi echi. Sheitan chii oqinse likai giewo."
MAR 7:30 Hhe khareizhi echi uzhese sheitan khizhi echizhi oqin chonban jiere kijiezho.
MAR 7:31 ErsaTuilose likai gie Xidunse daozhi Jijiapoli orondedu Jialilihaide echiwo.
MAR 7:32 Hhe oronyi kunla dulei yaba gholusan nie kunyi uduruzhi Ersai ochirale irewo. Ersai xiahua giezhi khane beye jiereni tei giezho.
MAR 7:33 Ersa hhei uduruzhi olon kunse likai giezhi nimande echiwo. Kha ghurunne ghua chighindei teiwo. Ingie nunpudene kielien jiereni moiwo.
MAR 7:34 Asimanyi uzhezhi nie shanholo hhende kieliewo, "Ifada!" Isishi keii giezho.
MAR 7:35 Hhei chighinni deigo keiwo. Kielienni goudazhi kielien kielieseye qinchu wo.
MAR 7:36 Ersa kunlade bu kielie giezhi hhelade fenfulazhoma, ye fenfulase ye chonji keighawo.
MAR 7:37 Olon kun hende ghuduredene kieliezho, "Hhe giesan shiqinla man gou wo. Duleii sonosughawo. Yabaiye kielien kielieghawo."
MAR 8:1 Hhe shihoude pse olon kun hhantulase ijiekui uwo. Ersa tujilane uruzhi ire kieliewo,
MAR 8:2 "Ene kunla mare hhantu ghurudu oluzho, hhelade ijiekui widazho. Bi hhelade ubali xiizho.
MAR 8:3 Bi hhelai oliesuzhi giedei echighase hhela mo jiere injirene. Gholose iresanye wine."
MAR 8:4 Tujilani hhende kieliewo, "Ene hontande imeghei kunlade matugie ginanyi ijiezhi chudughane?"
MAR 8:5 Ersa hhelade asawo, "Tande ginan giedughon wo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Dolon wo."
MAR 8:6 Ersa olon kunlai fenfulazhi zemin jiere soughadene dolon ginanyi barei mafan kieliedene ghulu tujilade ogise tujila olon kunlai melie beilawo.
MAR 8:7 Pse hhelade giedun zhaghasun wo. Ersa mafan kieliedene fenfulazhi kunlai melie beilaghawo.
MAR 8:8 Hhela ijiezhi chududene feiliesei dolon lanzi zhonlowo.
MAR 8:9 Hhende chabudu 4000 kun wo. Ersa hhelani dafalazhi echighawo.
MAR 8:10 Deigo tujilarene hhantu chon jiere khirei Damanuta oronde echiwo.
MAR 8:11 Falisai kunla Ersai shida ire jianjindu qiiwo. Hhela Ersai shiizhi, "Asiman jierese iresan ghudureqi xienjigha." giezhi xiahua giezho.
MAR 8:12 Ersa zhughedene hende nie shanholo kieliewo, "Ene idai kunla yangiezhi ghudureqii kerene? Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene idai kunlade xienjighaku ghudureqi uwo."
MAR 8:13 Ingiedene hhelase likai gie, chon jiere khirei hai duimiende daowo.
MAR 8:14 Tujila ginan bareikui matazho. Chon jiere khireise zinie ginan wo. Pse ijiuni uwo.
MAR 8:15 Ersa hhelade fenfulazhi kieliezho, "Ta Falisai kunni kunieghe, Hherode kunni kunieghei jinxin giezhi fangula."
MAR 8:16 Tujila nieniedene kielienduzho, "Matande ginan wise ingiezhi kieliezhoba."
MAR 8:17 Ersa mejiedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi ginan wikui kielienduzho? Ta dou mejie dazhi minbai olu danu? Ta dou intu men onu?
MAR 8:18 Tande nudun wine, uzhe danu? Chighin wine, chenlie danu? Ta jila dazhou?
MAR 8:19 Tawun ginanyi ghuludene 5000 kunde ogikude zhazhai giedun lanzi zhonlowo?" Hhela kieliewo, "12 gie wo."
MAR 8:20 "Pse dolon ginanyi ghuludene 4000 kunde ogikude zhazhai giedun lanzi zhonlowo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Dolon wo."
MAR 8:21 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta dou minbai olu danu?"
MAR 8:22 Hhela Bosaidade irewo. Kunla nie sughoi uduruzhi ire Ersai xiahua giezhi hhei nie maqi giezho.
MAR 8:23 Ersa sughoi khase laidene aghin ghadane echiwo. Nudun jierei nunpudene ghua khane hhei jiere teizhi, "Chi yan chanlawo." giezhi asazho.
MAR 8:24 Hhe qiorunne qila nie uzhe kieliewo, "Bi kunlai chanlawo. Hhela mutunyi xianli, da yozho."
MAR 8:25 Ersa pse khane nudun jierei teizho. Sugho xianxide uzhese goudadene yanyanjilai qinchude chanlawo.
MAR 8:26 Ersa hhei giedei echighakude, "Aghinde bu echi." giezhi kieliewo.
MAR 8:27 Ersa tujilarene khidene Kaisaliya-Feilibini aghinlade echiwo. Mo jiere tujiladene asazho, "Kunla kieliese bishi kien wo giezho?"
MAR 8:28 Hhela kieliewo, "Kunla kieliese xili gieghasan Yaheiya wo giezho. Niezhan kunla kieliese Iliya wo giezho. Pse niezhan kunla kieliese xienzhi dundadu nie wo giezho."
MAR 8:29 Ersa hhelade asawo, "Ta kieliese bishi kien wo?" Beduru kieliewo, "Chishi Mexiha wo."
MAR 8:30 Ersa orunyi kiemade bu kielie giezhi hhelade hende fenfulawo.
MAR 8:31 Ingiedene Ersa hhelade sughazhi qiiwo, "Kunnikewon matugieseda hende shouku giezhi zhanlao, fugie buwa, jinwun hanjiala mii fandui giezhi alane. Ghurudu oludene aminne olune."
MAR 8:32 Ersa ene kielienyi mindamin kieliese Beduru hhei laidene kheila qiiwo.
MAR 8:33 Ersa ochira daore tujilai uzhedene Bedurui kheilazhi kieliewo, "Ibilisi, mii khuina dao! Chi Hudai isii ulie sumulazhi kunni isii sumulane!"
MAR 8:34 Ersa olon kun, tujilane uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Kien mii daghane giese goyane sheidene shizijiane beiliezhi mii daghakuni wo.
MAR 8:35 Kien aminne jiuine giese aminne widaghane. Made, gouxioxide oluzhi aminne widaghase aminne jiuine.
MAR 8:36 Kun duyani man zhenjidene goya aminne widaghase yande gou wo?
MAR 8:37 Kun pse yanghala aminne arunzhane?
MAR 8:38 Kien ene piofen giezhi zui fanjisan duyade bi, kieliensemi jiuren giese Kunnikewon Adane fama dunda zhiguitu qienxienlare hhantu irekude hhenseye jiuren giene."
MAR 9:1 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, enende beisan kun dunda niezhanla Hudai gojia nenli dunda irekui ulie chanlatula ulie fugune."
MAR 9:2 Zhighudu daose ErsaBeduru, Yagebu, Yaheiyai danxin uduru undu ulade khireidene hhelai melie bienjiwo.
MAR 9:3 Jienni gon faidene chighande duya jiere popu waghachen kun dunda kiema qingiezhi waghazhi chighashigha dane.
MAR 9:4 Iliya, MusaErsare kielien kieliesei hhela chujieghewo.
MAR 9:5 BeduruErsade kieliewo, "Loushi, matan enende gou wo. Enende ghuran zhanfan daiye. Niei chade, niei Musade, niei Iliyade."
MAR 9:6 Ingiekushi hhela hende ayidene Beduru yan kieliekune ulie mejiene.
MAR 9:7 Niegieda olien iredene hhelai khawo. Oliense shenqi irezhi kieliewo, "Eneshi bi oresan mii kewon wo. Ta hhei kielienyi chenlie!"
MAR 9:8 Menzhali tujila zhouwidene nie uzhese kiemai ese chanlawo. Zi Ersa hhelare hhantuwo.
MAR 9:9 Ulase boukude Ersa, "Kunnikewon fugusan kun dundase aminne ulie olutula chanlasei kiemade bu kielie!" giezhi hhelade fenfulawo.
MAR 9:10 Tujila ene kielienyi zhughedene jilasenu, "Fugusanse aminne olune giese yan isi wo." giezhi kielienduzho.
MAR 9:11 Hhela Ersade asawo, "Jinwun hanjiala yangiezhi Iliya ijinyo xien irene giezhi kieliezho?"
MAR 9:12 Ersa kieliewo, "Iliya xien iredene man erchan gie goudaghakuni woma, jinwun jiere yangiezhi, 'Kunnikewon olon shouku giezhi kunla hhei uzhe dane?' giezhi huaizho?
MAR 9:13 Bi tande kielieye, Iliya shuhuajia irezhoma, jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun kunla hhei shimatu giezho."
MAR 9:14 Hhela psedu tujilai hhende khareizhi irese olon kunla wiqizhi jinwun hanjiala tujilare jianjindusei chanlawo.
MAR 9:15 Kunla man Ersai chanladene ghudurezho. Ingie holu echi kielien asazho.
MAR 9:16 Ersa hhelade asawo, "Ta hhelare yan jianjinduzho?"
MAR 9:17 Kunlai dundase nie kun kieliewo, "Loushi, bi kewonne uduruzhi chii enende irewo. Hhei yaba sheitan heizho.
MAR 9:18 Khalaliuzhe sheitan hhei barei agise hhei banjighazhi amansei momozi moine. Shidunne zhouzhi beyeni khiduzhezho. Bi chii tujilade kieliezhi sheitanyi tou khigha giese hhela han wo."
MAR 9:19 Ersa kieliewo, "Ai, ta ene xianxin ulie giechen idaini kunla! Bi tanse rennai giezhi giedoghoncha beine? Kewonni uduruzhi mii enende ire!"
MAR 9:20 Hhela kewonni uduru irewo. Sheitan Ersai chanlasenu kewonni hende nie tigharaghawo. Kewon zemin jiere unadene ghoghoreizhi amansei momozi moizho.
MAR 9:21 Ersa adadei asawo, "Hhe giemerezhi giedoghoncha oluzho?" Adani kieliewo, "Ga xienzise ingiezho.
MAR 9:22 Sheitan hhei niefanie khande, usude bendazhi fugughane giezho. Chi gie shidase bijiende ubali xiizhi banman nie gie."
MAR 9:23 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Gie shidaseshi yan kielien wo? Xianxin giesan kunde yanniliuzhe giene."
MAR 9:24 Ingie adani deigo fugiede kieliewo, "Bi xianxin giene, bi xianxin gie dasei chi made banman gie!"
MAR 9:25 Ersa olon kunla holu iresei chanlasenu zannan ruhheryi sugiezhi kieliewo, "Chi ene dulei yaba sheitan, bi minlin xiaiye, ene kunyi jierese khizhedene pse bu oro!"
MAR 9:26 Sheitan fugiede nie warada kewonni nie tigharaghadene khizhewo. Kewon fugusan niekielien wo. Olon kunla kieliese hhe fuguwo giezho.
MAR 9:27 Ersa hhei khase laidene feizhi bosighase hhe bosizhewo.
MAR 9:28 Ersa giedera orose tujilani konkonji asawo, "Bijien yangiezhi ene sheitanyi khigha dane?"
MAR 9:29 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Onxian ulie giese ene izhun sheitanni khigha dane."
MAR 9:30 Hhela hhe oronse likai giezhi Jialiliyi daowo. Ersa kunlade mejieghaku duran uwo.
MAR 9:31 Ingiekushi Kunnikewonyi kunlai khade jiuidene hhela alase ghurudude aminne olune giezhi Ersa tujiladene sughazho.
MAR 9:32 Tujila ene kielienyi dunjire dazho, ayizhi asaye dazho.
MAR 9:33 Hhela Jiabainunde irese Ersa giedoura tujilade asawo, "Ta mo jiere yan zhenjinduzho?"
MAR 9:34 Tujila shenqi ese khizhezho. Hhela mo jiere kien zui fugie wo giezhi zhenjinduzho.
MAR 9:35 Ersa sousenu 12 gie tujii uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Kien laoda danlane giese kunlase gajishizhi ushilachen kun danlakuni wo."
MAR 9:36 Ingie Ersa nie kewosii uduru ire hhelai dunda beighadene qioru hhelade kieliewo,
MAR 9:37 "Kien mii niereghala intu kewosii jienliese mii jienliezho. Kien mii jienliese mii ese jienliezho, mii peizhi ireghasan hhei jienliezho."
MAR 9:38 YaheiyaErsade kieliewo, "Loushi, bijien nie kunyi uzhese chii niereghala sheitan touzho. Bijien danlazhi ese toughawo. Hhe matanyi ese daghazho."
MAR 9:39 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bu danla. Mii niereghala fugie shiqin giedene deigo mii sugiechen kun uwo.
MAR 9:40 Matanyi fandui ulie giese matande oluzhi giezho.
MAR 9:41 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kien tande tashi Mexihanughun wo giezhi nie beizi usu ogiliuzhe hhende jianli kenjin ogine."
MAR 9:42 "Kien mii xianxin giesan enezighan ga kun dundadu niei zui fanjighase ghuzhundeni qiemanshai banladene haide bendase da gou wo.
MAR 9:43 Chii nie kha chii zui fanjighase chizhidene agi! Beyechii canfei gholuzhi chanqi amitukude echiku ghua kha bidene dozode, ulie xinieku khande orokuse gou wo.
MAR 9:45 Chii nie kon chii zui fanjighase chizhidene agi! Beyechii canfei gholuzhi chanqi amitukude echiku ghua kon bidene dozode bendakuse gou wo.
MAR 9:47 Chii nie nudun chii zui fanjighase waidene agi! Chade nie nudun chaizhi Hudai gojiade oroku ghua nudun bidene dozode bendakuse gou wo.
MAR 9:48 Hhende ghughei ulie fugune, khan ulie xiniene.
MAR 9:49 Khan dansun wo giezhi jien kunyi yenliene.
MAR 9:50 Dansunshi gouni wo. Widaoni widase matugie koudaghane? Tai dunda dansun bizhi nieniedene heqishi."
MAR 10:1 Ersa hhense likai giezhi Yudaya oronde, Yedanhe duimiende irewo. Kunla pse hhei hhende hhantulase Ersa chanqiku mutun kunlade sughazho.
MAR 10:2 Falisai kunla ire Ersai shiizhi asazho, "Ere kun biereine lihun gieghase olunulie?"
MAR 10:3 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Musa tande matugie fenfulazho?"
MAR 10:4 Hhela kieliewo, "Musa kieliese lihun qiuzi huaidene lihun giese olune giezho."
MAR 10:5 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Tai zhughe khidunshi Musa ene minlinyi huaizho.
MAR 10:6 Duyai zhayaghakude Huda ere kun, eme kunyi zhayaghawo.
MAR 10:7 Ingiese kun ada anasene likai giedene biereighalane hhantulazhi
MAR 10:8 ghuala nie beye gholune. Hhela ghua pusho, nie wo.
MAR 10:9 Ingiese Huda hhantulaghasei kun fenkai gieghase ulie olune."
MAR 10:10 Giedoura orose tujila Ersade ene shiqinyi pse asazho.
MAR 10:11 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Kien biereighalane lihun giedene pse agise piofen giezho. Biereine kuighazho.
MAR 10:12 Bierei zhanguijighalane lihun giedene pse loujide khiseye piofen giezho."
MAR 10:13 Kunla kesilane uduruzhi Ersai melie ire maqighane giese tujila hhelai sugiezho.
MAR 10:14 Ersa chanladene hokuzhi tujilade kieliewo, "Kesilai bu dui, mii shida ire gie. Hudai gojiashi imutu kunlanughun wo.
MAR 10:15 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kien kewosi mutun Hudai gojiai ulie jienliese hhende oro dane."
MAR 10:16 Ingie kesilai qiorudene hhelai jiere khane teizhi gouni kieliezho.
MAR 10:17 Ersa yozhi qiikude nie kun holuzhi iredene hhei melie xiutuliezhi asawo, "Gou loushi, bi matui giese chanqiku aminni jienliene?"
MAR 10:18 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii yangiezhi gou wo giezho? Hudase chugo gouni uwo.
MAR 10:19 Minlinyi chi mejiene, kun bu ala, piofen bu gie, bu ghula, jia ganzhen bu bei, bu pienda, ada anane zunji giezho."
MAR 10:20 Hhe kun kieliewo, "Loushi, enelai bi ga xienzise man zunjizho."
MAR 10:21 Ersa hhei uzhedene orezhi kieliewo, "Chade da nie chaizho. Echidene bisanlane man huizhi nanxin kunlade ogi. Ingiese chii boubei asiman jiere wo. Ingiedene irezhi mii dagha."
MAR 10:22 Hhende caichan olonshi ene kielienyi chenliedene ungieni bouzhi yuchourazhi yolawo.
MAR 10:23 Ersa zhouwidene uzhe tujiladene kieliewo, "Baertu kun Hudai gojiade oroku chijia no wo."
MAR 10:24 Tujila ene kieliende ghudurezho. Ingiese Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Kesila, Hudai gojiade oroku chijia no wo.
MAR 10:25 Loto zhun boghose daoku bayan kun Hudai gojiade orokuse da sunfan wo."
MAR 10:26 Tujila hende ghanirazhi nieniedene asazho, "Ingiese kienyi jiui shidane?"
MAR 10:27 Ersa hhelai uzhedene kieliewo, "Kun gie danema, Huda buxian wo. Huda yanniliuzhe giene."
MAR 10:28 BeduruErsade kieliewo, "Uzhe, bijien man bendadene chii daghazho!"
MAR 10:29 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kun made, gouxioxide oluzhi gie, gaijiu, eghechijiu, ada, ana, kesila, ghazhane bendase
MAR 10:30 ene duyade gie, gaijiu, eghechijiu, ana, kesila, ghazha 100 pei ogine. Ogikude heikuiye hhantu ogine. Houshide chanqiku amin ogine.
MAR 10:31 Ingiese olon melieshikula khuinashilane, khuinashikula melieshilane."
MAR 10:32 Hhela Yelusalende khireiku mo jiere Ersa melie yozho. Tujilani ghanirazho, daghasan kunla ayizho. Ersa pse 12 gie tujii uruzhi ire goyade kuzheku shiqinyi kielie qiiwo,
MAR 10:33 "Uzhe, matan Yelusalende khireine. Kunnikewonyi fugie buwa, jinwun hanjialade jiuise hhela hhei sixin panjidene niman kunlade jiuine.
MAR 10:34 Hhela hhei xilun giene, ungie jiere nunpune, mabienzighala eghine, da alane. Ingie ghurudu daose aminne olune."
MAR 10:35 Xibitaini ghua kewon Yagebu, YaheiyaErsai melie ire kieliewo, "Loushi, bijien yan xiahua giese chi bijiende yan ogiba."
MAR 10:36 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta mii yan gieghane?"
MAR 10:37 Hhela kieliewo, "Chi famatu baozo jiere soukude bijienyi niei borun miende niei soghei miende sougha."
MAR 10:38 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta yan keresanne ulie mejiene. Bi shouiku kuni ta shoui shidanu? Bi jienlieku xilini ta jienlienu?"
MAR 10:39 Hhela kieliewo, "Jienliene." Ersa kieliewo, "Bi shouiku kuni ta shoui, bi jienlieku xilini ta jienlienema,
MAR 10:40 mii lianmien kanzide soughakui bi ogiku pusho. Kiende zhunbei giezhoshi kiende ogine."
MAR 10:41 Psedu hharan tujini sonosudene Yagebu, Yaheiyaghalade hokuzho.
MAR 10:42 Ersa hhelai uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Niman kunlai dunda lindao, noyen giezhi urusanla qienli bareizhi kunlai gonjisei ta mejiene.
MAR 10:43 Ta niekielien pusho, tai dunda kien fugieni danlane giese tande ushilachen kun danlakuni wo.
MAR 10:44 Tai dunda kien laoda danlane giese dajialade hoji danlakuni wo.
MAR 10:45 Kunnikewon irekushi kunlai ushilaghale ese irezho. Kharei kunlai ushilazhi aminne sheidene olon kunlade shuiku Jiage danlale irezho."
MAR 10:46 Hhela Yeligede irewo. Ersa tuji, tebieji olon kunlare Yeligese likai giekude nie ghuichen sugho Jimaini kewon Bajimai mo bienzide souzho.
MAR 10:47 Hhe chenliese Nasaleni Ersa wo giese warada qiiwo, "Dawudeni houdei Ersa, made ubali nie xii!"
MAR 10:48 Olon kunla hhei jiebalazhi shenqi bu khizhe giese hhe genjia fugiede waradazhi kieliezho, "Dawudeni houdei, made ubali nie xii!"
MAR 10:49 Ersa beidene kieliewo, "Hhei uru daozhe." Hhela sughoi uruzhi kieliewo, "Zhughene teidene bosizhe. Hhe chii uruzho."
MAR 10:50 Sugho jienne jiezhi jiuli bosizhedene Ersai hhende yozhi irewo.
MAR 10:51 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chade yan giene?" Sugho kieliewo, "Loushi, bi chanlaku duran wo!"
MAR 10:52 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi echi. Chii xianxin gieku chii jiuiwo." Sugho deigo chanladene mo jiere Ersai daghawo.
MAR 11:1 Hhela Yelusalense chadashizhi Ganlanshanni Bofaqi, Bodanide kuzhekude Ersa ghua tujine peizhi
MAR 11:2 hhelade kieliewo, "Ta duimienni aghinde echi. Dei orose nie huiyasan ga enzheghei chanlane. Kieme unuzhi ese daozho. Ta andaghadene lai ire.
MAR 11:3 Kunla tande enei, 'Yangiezhi giezho?' giese ta 'Ezhan injine. Ingie deigo enende khugho ireghane.' giezhi kielie."
MAR 11:4 Hhela echise nie ga enzheghei wijien konni mo jiere huiya jiesei chanlawo. Hhela hhei andaghase
MAR 11:5 hhende beisan giedun kunla asawo, "Ta ga enzhegheni andaghazhi yan giene?"
MAR 11:6 Tujila Ersa kieliesan mutun kieliese hhela laighawo.
MAR 11:7 Hhela ga enzheghei lai Ersai shida ire goya jienlane enzheghe jiere daidene Ersai unughawo.
MAR 11:8 Olon kunla jienlane mo jiere peizho. Psedu kunla ghazhase chizhisan mutun chalai mo jiere peizho.
MAR 11:9 Melie khuinadu kunla waradazhi kieliezho, "Hesanna! Ezhanyi niereghala iresan hhei doulandu!
MAR 11:10 Mai xienren Dawudeni gojia iresande doulandu! Zui Undudedu Hudade doulandu! Hesanna!"
MAR 11:11 ErsaYelusalende kuru mechide orozhi zhouwini man nie uzhewo. Khara oluse Ersa 12 gie shiturene chenshise khirei Bodanide echiwo.
MAR 11:12 Khuichudu hhela Bodanise khizhese Ersa oliesuzho.
MAR 11:13 Gholose nie lachen winetu nie uhuago mutunyi chanlawo. Hhende echizhi mutun jierese alima ereizhi olune giezho. Hhe mutun doura echise yama uwo, zinie lachen bikushi alima souku shihou pusho.
MAR 11:14 Ersa mutunde kieliewo, "Enedu khuinase chii jiere pse ibeizi alima ulie soune!" Tujilani kielienyini sonosuzho.
MAR 11:15 Hhela Yelusalende irewo. Ersa mechide orodene meimei giesan kunlai tou khighawo. Baer arunzhasan kunlai shire, ghoghochen huisan kunlai bandoulai tungu unaghawo.
MAR 11:16 Kunlai mechise dunxilai agizhi ese daoghazho.
MAR 11:17 Hhelade sughazhi kieliezho, "'Mii giei go minzula onxian gieku gie giezhi urune.' giezhi jinwun jiere ese huaizhou? Ta hhei ghughei ho gholughazho!"
MAR 11:18 Fugie buwa, jinwun hanjiala ene kielienyi chenliedene banfa xianjizhi Ersai widaghane giezho. Olon kunla man hhe sughasan tebie gou wo giese hhense ayizho.
MAR 11:19 Khara olukude hhela chenshi ghadane khireizho.
MAR 11:20 Eqiemagha hhela hhense yozhi daokude uhuago mutun lien genzi ghosei chanlawo.
MAR 11:21 BeduruErsai kielienyi sumula ire hhende kieliewo, "Loushi, uzhe! Chi kharasan uhuago mutun ghozho."
MAR 11:22 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta Hudai xianxin gie.
MAR 11:23 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kien zhughedene inxin ulie giezhi ene ulade oronsene noidene haide bou giese jiu qingiezhi gholune.
MAR 11:24 Ingiese bi tande kielieye, ta onxian giezhi xiahua giekude tande ogiwo giezhi xianxin giema, tande qingiezhi gholune.
MAR 11:25 Ta beidene onxian giekude kunla chii hokughasei sumula irese roulie. Asiman jieredu adataiye tai codasei rouliene."
MAR 11:27 Hhela pse Yelusalende irewo. Ersa mechide yokude fugie buwa, jinwun hanjia, zhanlaola Ersai shida iredene
MAR 11:28 hhende kieliezho, "Chi yan qienlighala ene shiqinlai giezho? Kien chade ene qienlii ogizhi ene shiqinyi gieghazho?"
MAR 11:29 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Biye tande nie unqi asaye. Ta made huida giese bi yan qienlighala ene shiqinlai giesei tande kieliene.
MAR 11:30 Yaheiyai xili gieghaku qienli asimanse onu, kunlase wo? Ta made huida gie."
MAR 11:31 Hhela goyalane shanlian giezhi kieliewo, "Matan asimanse wo giese ta yale hhei xianxin ulie giene giezhi hhe kieliene.
MAR 11:32 Kunlase wo giese?" Jien kunla man Yaheiyashi zhenzhenji xienzhi wo giese hhela bexinlase ayizho.
MAR 11:33 Ingie Ersade kieliewo, "Bijien ulie mejiene." Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Biye tande yan qienlighala ene shiqinlai giesei ulie kieliene."
MAR 12:1 Ersa hhelade bilazhi kielie qiiwo, "Nie kun nie yenzi putou zeiladene izhonyini qienjiwo. Jiu daruku chizi waizhi yenzi uzheku teizi giedene kunlade bouizhi ogi, gholode echiwo.
MAR 12:2 Shihou kuzhese nie hojine peizhi bouisan kunlase nexianne ghuraghale echiwo.
MAR 12:3 Bouisan kunla hhei bareidene idun eghi khosun khareighawo.
MAR 12:4 Pse nie hoji peizhi echighase hhela qiorunyini eghi ghalughazhi shizheghazho.
MAR 12:5 Pse nie hoji peizhi echighase hhela hhei alawo. Khuinashida olon hojilai peizhi echighase niezhanlai eghizho, niezhanlai alazho.
MAR 12:6 Yenzii ezhande oresan niekozi kewon wo. Zuihoude hhei peizhi echighazhi kieliezho, 'Hhela kewonyimi zunjineba.'
MAR 12:7 Ingie bouisan kunla nieniedene kieliewo, 'Eneshi jiachanni jienliechen wo. Matan enei alayema, jiachanni manughun gholune!'
MAR 12:8 Ingie hhei bareidene alazhi putou yenzise benda khighawo.
MAR 12:9 Ingiese putou yenzii ezhan matugiene? Hhe iredene bouisan kunlai alazhi putou yenzii psedu kunlade ogine.
MAR 12:10 Ta ene idon jinwunni onshizhi ese daowu? 'Gie giesan kunla bendasan tashi giei zhunyo tashi gholuwo.
MAR 12:11 Eneshi Ezhan giesan wo. Matan uzhese xihan giezho.'"
MAR 12:12 Ersa hhelai zhiizhi bilazhi kieliesei hhela uzhe khizhedene bareine giezhoma, olon kunlase ayidene Ersase likai gie yolawo.
MAR 12:13 Hhela giedun Falisai kun, Hherodepai kunni peizhi Ersai hhende echighadene hhei kielienghala heine giezho.
MAR 12:14 Hhela iredene hhende kieliewo, "Loushi, chi shuhua kieliekui bijien mejiene. Chi yan kunyiliuzhe niekielien uzhezhi kunni mienzii ulie uzhene. Hudai daolini shixinde sughazho. Matan Kaisa Honshande shui jiuise oluzhou ese oluzho?
MAR 12:15 Matan jiuiku onu, ulie jiuiku wo?" Ersa hhelai jiazhon giesei mejiedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta mii shiizhi yan giene? Made miengui agizhedene nie uzhegha."
MAR 12:16 Hhela agizhese Ersa kieliewo, "Ene qiorun, haoshi kiennughun wo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Kaisanughun wo."
MAR 12:17 Ersa kieliewo, "Kaisanughunshi Kaisade ogi, Hudanughunshi Hudade ogi." Ingiese hhela Ersade hende ghanirazho.
MAR 12:18 Fuho gieku shiqin uwo giesan Sadugai kunla ire Ersade asazho,
MAR 12:19 "Loushi, Musa guijin jiere huaizho, nie kun bierei agidene kewosi wi duya ijiese jiuni zhoui gaidene houdei liuikuni wo giezho.
MAR 12:20 Gaijiu dololie, laoda bierei agidene kewosi wi duya ijiewo.
MAR 12:21 Laoer hhei zhouidene kewosi wi duya ijiewo. Laosanye ingiezho.
MAR 12:22 Hhe dololiede kewosi nieda uye feiliezho. Zuihou biereiye duya ijiewo.
MAR 12:23 Ingiese fuho giekude hheshi kienyi bierei wo? Gaijiu dololie man hhei agiwo."
MAR 12:24 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Tanughun codazho. Ta jinwunni mejie dazho, Hudai nenliniye mejie dazho. Eneshi tai codasan yenyin wo.
MAR 12:25 Kun aminne olukude ulie agine, ulie dafalane, asiman jieredu qienxien niekielien wo.
MAR 12:26 Duya ijiesan kun aminne olukui kieliese ta eghesun khan siderasan jinwunni Musai shu jiere onshizhi ese daowu? Huda Musade, 'Bishi Iburaheimuni Huda wo, Isagheini Huda wo, Yagebuni Huda wo.' giezhi kieliezho.
MAR 12:27 Hudashi duya ijiesan kunyi Huda pusho, amitu kunyi Huda wo. Tanughun fugiede codazho."
MAR 12:28 Nie jinwun hanjia ire hhela jianjindusei sonosuwo. Ersa kieliesan gou bikui mejiedene Ersade asazho, "Minlin dunda alinie zui zhunyo wo?"
MAR 12:29 Ersa kieliewo, "Ji 1 gieshi ene wo, Isilieya, chenliendu! Ezhan mai Hudashi zi niekozi wo.
MAR 12:30 Chi qienbuji zhughe, qienbuji jinshen, qienbuji sumulaku, qienbuji lilianghalane Ezhan Hudadene ore giezho.
MAR 12:31 Jie 2 gieshi ene wo, goyadene mutun giebeidene ore giezho. Ene ghua minlinse fugieni uwo."
MAR 12:32 Jinwun hanjia Ersade kieliewo, "Loushi, chi kieliesan oluzho. Hudashi nie wo. Hhense chugo pse Huda uwo.
MAR 12:33 Qienbuji zhughe, qienbuji sumulaku, qienbuji lilianghalane Ezhan Hudadene oreku, pse goyadene mutun giebeidene oreku yanyanji sideraghaku sidagha, ogiku murelase zhunyo wo."
MAR 12:34 Ersa uzhese hhe huida giesande agheli wine. Ingie hhende kieliewo, "Chi Hudai gojiase gholo uwo." Enense khuinashi kunla hhende yama asa dazho.
MAR 12:35 Ersa mechide sughakude kieliezho, "Jinwun hanjiala matugie Mexihashi Dawudeni houdei wo giezhi kieliezho?
MAR 12:36 Dawude goya Shenlinni tungo giezhi kieliewo, 'Ezhan mii Ezhande kieliewo, "Bi duitoulaichii kon dourachii teitula chi mini borun miende sou."'
MAR 12:37 Dawude goyane Mexihai Ezhan giezhi uruse Mexiha matugie Dawudeni houdei wo?" Ingiese tebieji olon kunla hhenughunyi chenliekude xiqi wo.
MAR 12:38 Ersa kunlade sughakude kieliewo, "Ta jinwun hanjialai fangula. Hhela fudu jien musidene geidoude toreizhi kunla hhelade kielien asakude xiqi wo.
MAR 12:39 Huitanni undu wizi, xini shanxide soukude xiqi wo.
MAR 12:40 Hhela guafui gieni chigheine. Jiazhon giezhi oloncha onxian giene. Enezighan kunlai pse gundude faine."
MAR 12:41 Ersa mechii baer teiku xianzii duimiende soudene kunla matui baer teisanyi uzhezho. Olon bayan kunla xianzide baer olon teizho.
MAR 12:42 Nie nanxin guafu iredene ghua fenfenzi baer teizho.
MAR 12:43 Ersa tujilane uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene nanxin guafu xianzide teisan soyuji kunlase olon wo.
MAR 12:44 Kunla olonsene teiwo, guafude yama uwoma, udu daoku baerlane man teiwo."
MAR 13:1 Ersa mechise khizhekude nie tujini hhende kieliewo, "Loushi, uzhe! Ene tashi, loula matu fama wo!"
MAR 13:2 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi ene fugie gielai chanlawu? Jianlai man cheizhi tashi jiere tashi nieda ulie jiene."
MAR 13:3 Ersa mechini duimienni Ganlanshande soukude Beduru, Yagebu, Yaheiya, Andelie konkonji ire asazho,
MAR 13:4 "Yan xienzide ene shiqinla fashen giene? Enela man chenjikude yan zunji bikui bijiende nie kielie."
MAR 13:5 Ersa hhelade kielie qiiwo, "Ta xioxin giezhi kunlai bu miigha.
MAR 13:6 Olon kunla mii niereghala iredene bishi hhe enbene giezhi olon kunlai miine.
MAR 13:7 Ta eghindusan, eghindune giesan xioxini sonosuse bu jinda. Ene shiqin kenjin fashen gienema, duya baraku shihou dou ese kuzhezho.
MAR 13:8 Minzu minzula eghindune, gojia gojiala eghindune. Gochude zemin gojioluzhi oliesune. Eneshi tendunni keitou wo."
MAR 13:9 "Ingiese ta goyane xioxin gie. Kunla tai zui fugie fayende jiuine. Huitanlade eghine. Mii yenyinghala ta shenzhan, honshanlai melie beizhi ganzhen beine.
MAR 13:10 Pse gouxioxini go minzulade matugieseda xien chonjizhi ogine.
MAR 13:11 Kunla tai bareizhi fayende jiuikude ta yan kieliekui melieshighan munan bu gie. Hhe shihoude tande yan kielieghase yan kielie. Kieliesanshi ta pusho, Shenlin wo.
MAR 13:12 Gaijiu gaijiune, ada kewosine ghudanduzhi fugughakude kune. Kesila ada, anane zodui giezhi fugughakude jiuine.
MAR 13:13 Mii yenyinghala soyuji kunla man tai henjine. Ingieliuzhe rennai giezhi zuihou kusanlai jiuine."
MAR 13:14 "Hhe pohai giezhi hanzhan gieghaku ulie beiku oronde beisei ta chanlane. (Onshichen kunla, ene kielienni isii dunjirekuni wo.) Ingiekude Yudayade sousan kunla, ulade piile echi.
MAR 13:15 Gie jieredula, bu bouzhezhi giederase dunxi agile bu oro.
MAR 13:16 Ghazha jieredula, jienne agile khareizhi bu echi.
MAR 13:17 Hhe udude kewosi laisan, gogoghasanlade gou widawo.
MAR 13:18 Enei unchade bu kuzhegha giezhi onxian gie.
MAR 13:19 Ingiekushi hhezighan udude zeinan fugie wo. Huda duyai zhayaghazhi eli kutula imutu zeinan uwo, khuinashiye uwo.
MAR 13:20 Ezhan hhezighan zeinantu udui ese choghonshighazhoshi nieda jiui danema, hhe sunghusan kunladene oluzhi choghonshighawo.
MAR 13:21 Hhe udude kunla tande uzhe, Mexiha enende wo, uzhe, hhende wo giese ta xianxin bu gie.
