LUK 11:51 Jiushi Hhabini alasanse qiizhi izhi sidagha gieku teiziji dajien dunda Sajialiyai alasan zuini guini man ene idai kunlai jiere teine. Enbene, bi tande kielieye, ene guini ene idai kunlai jiere teine.
LUK 11:52 Ta jinwun loushilade gou widawo! Ta Hudai taniku yeshii agizhi echidene goyalane ese orowo, orone giechen kunlaiye ese oroghawo."
LUK 11:53 Ersa enense ghadane khireise jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunla Ersai hende fandui giedene unqi olon asazhi
LUK 11:54 kieliensei babin ereine giezho.
LUK 12:1 Ingiekude jiqien jiwon kun hhantulazhi nieniene taikui xianli. Ersa xien tujiladene kieliewo, "Ta Falisai kunni kunieghei xioxin gie. Hhelashi jiazhon giesan kun wo.
LUK 12:2 Jizide giesan shiqinlai ulie khizheghakui uwo. Niuighasanlai ulie mejieghakui uwo.
LUK 12:3 Ta beichazide kieliesan kielienlai kunla ghadane mindamin chenliene. Ta giedera chighinde kieliesei kunla gie jiere fugiede kieliene."
LUK 12:4 "Mini zhanlienla, bi tande kielieye, beyeni aladene pse yama gie dachen hhelase bu ayi.
LUK 12:5 Bi tande kiense ayikui mejieghaye, beyeni aladene dozoheide echighaku qienli bichen hhense ayi."
LUK 12:6 "Tawun bunzhui 2 mao baer huinela? Ingieliuzhe Huda hhelai nieda ulie matane.
LUK 12:7 Tai qiorun jieredu usunniliuzhe toulazhi agizho. Ta bu ayi, ta olon bunzhulase zhunyo wo."
LUK 12:8 "Bi pse tande kielieye, kien kunlai melie mini renjise Kunnikewonye Hudai qienxien melie hhei renjine.
LUK 12:9 Kien kunlai melie mini ulie renjise bi Hudai qienxien melie hhei ulie renjine.
LUK 12:10 Kunnikewonni fandui giezhi kieliese roulienema, Shenlinni hu kieliese ulie rouliene.
LUK 12:11 Kunla tai laizhi huitan, noyen, qienli bareichen kun shida echise ta matugie huida giekui, yan kieliekui munan bu gie.
LUK 12:12 Hhe shihou kuse ta yan kieliekuni Shenlin mejieghane."
LUK 12:13 Ingiedene olon kunla dundase nie kun Ersade kieliewo, "Loushi, chi gaidemi kieliezhi jiachanyi made ghughazhi ogi gie."
LUK 12:14 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi ene kun, mini tande kien noyen danlaghazhi gieni ghughaghane?"
LUK 12:15 Ingie pse kieliewo, "Ta xioxin giezhi yanyanji tanxin giekulase gholodo. Kunni amin olon baerghala gonxi uwo."
LUK 12:16 Pse bilazhi kieliewo, "Nie bayan kunyi ghazhadeni osisan zhonjia gansan no wo.
LUK 12:17 Hhe sumulawo, 'Bi ene zhonjiani khala teine? Teiku oron uwo.'
LUK 12:18 Pse bi ene cankune cheidene pse fugiede nie gie, taran dunxilane teiye giezho.
LUK 12:19 Ingie goyadene made ijin sunjisan olon no wo. Jinien ijieliuzhe bara dane. Ede suibien ijiezhi ochizhi udu daose olune giezho.
LUK 12:20 Ingiese Huda hhende kieliewo, 'Chi ene ulie mejiechen kun! Ene xii chi fugu widase dunxilachii kiende feiliene?'"
LUK 12:21 Ersa kieliewo. "Jin goyadene boubeini sunjizhi Hudai miende bayan wichen kunshi man intui wo."
LUK 12:22 Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Ingiese bi tande kielieye, ta amindene oluzhi yan ijiene, musine giezhi munan bu gie.
LUK 12:23 Amin ijiekuse zhunyo wo, beye musikuse zhunyo wo.
LUK 12:24 Ta louwalani uzhe, hhela yama ese tareizho, ese ghurazho, ghuraku canku ye uwoma, Huda qiezhezho. Ta bunzhulase zhunyo uwonu?
LUK 12:25 Tani dunda kien zhughe chilakughala aminne niecha fududagha shidane?
LUK 12:26 Ta intughani ga shiqinyi gie dane, pseshiku shiqinde munan giezhi yangiene?
LUK 12:27 Ta baihe chizhe matugie osisei nie uzhe, hhela ulie khishilane, bosiye ulie giene. Bi tande kielieye, Sulumane honshan zui henni xienzide musisanla ene nie chizhede ulie kurune.
LUK 12:28 Ta goude xianxin ulie giechen kunla, banche jieredu osun enedu wine, maghashijie luzide teiliuzhe Huda dou ingiezhi dabalaghazho. Tai qingie ulie gienu?
LUK 12:29 Ta ijiezhi ochikude xiahua bu giezhi munan bu gie,
LUK 12:30 enelashi man duyani kunla xiahua giekuni wo. Tande enezighan chaisanlai Adatai mejiene.
LUK 12:31 Ta Hudai gojiai xiahua gie, ingiese enelai man tande ogine."
LUK 12:32 "Ta kun choghontu kunla, bu ayi. Tai Ada bayasuzhi asiman gojiani tande ogine.
LUK 12:33 Ta giededu dunxilane huizhi nanxin kunlade ghughazhi ogi. Goyadene oluzhi ulie qida oluku qienbaoni zhunbei giedene boubeini asiman jiere sunji. Hhende boubeila ulie widane, ghughei ghula dane, ghughei ijie dane.
LUK 12:34 Tai boubei khalashi zhughetaiye khala wo."
LUK 12:35 "Ta pixiene pixiliezhi zhulane jienjidene goude zhunbei gie.
LUK 12:36 Eneshi nie ezhan ghurunse irekuni sagheisan hojila niekielien wo. Ezhan iredene wijienyi eghikure hhantu niewo.
LUK 12:37 Ezhan irekude zeixin giesan hojilade fuqi wine. Bi tande shuhua kielieye, Ezhan goya wilie gieku jienne musidene hojilani shire jiere soughazhi ushilane.
LUK 12:38 Hhe banyede iremu, giegherekude irekude hojila ingiezhi giesei uzhese hhe hojilade fuqi wine.
LUK 12:39 Ta enei mejie, giei ezhan ghughei yan xienzide irekui mejiese giedene ulie oroghane.
LUK 12:40 Taye goude zhunbei giendu, ta mejie dakude Kunnikewon irene."
LUK 12:41 Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, ene bilasan kielienni bijiende kieliewu, dajialade kieliewo?"
LUK 12:42 Ezhan kieliewo, "Qinse kienshi kekaotu jienzha giechen gonjia wo? Zhanguijini hhende giededu hojilai, ijiekulani man gonjighasan pushonu?
LUK 12:43 Zhanguiji irekude hoji ingiezhi giesei chanlase hhe hojide fuqi wine.
LUK 12:44 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, zhanguiji hhende caichanlane man gonjighane.
LUK 12:45 Hhe hoji zhughedene sumulazhi mini zhanguiji deigo ulie irene gie, kewon, oqin hojilai eghizhi ijiezhi jiu ochizhi sudose
LUK 12:46 hhe sumula daku udu, mejie daku shihoude zhanguijini iredene hhei sidasunyi qiuizhi kielien ese chenliesan kunlare hhantu faine.
LUK 12:47 Ene hoji ezhanni isini mejiewoma, zhunbei ese giewo. Zhanguijini kielien mutun ye ese giewo. Ingiese hheni gundude faikuni wo.
LUK 12:48 Zinie zhanguijini isini mejie dazhi gou ese giesan kunlai gongiende faine. Olon ogisan kunlase olon kerene, choghon ogisan kunlase choghon kerene."
LUK 12:49 "Bi zemin jiere khan teile irewo. Bi sumulase khan ghujighan sidera qiisejiu.
LUK 12:50 Made da nie chijia xili giekuni wine. Hhei onchen gietula made yali fugie no wo.
LUK 12:51 Ta sumulase bi zemin jiere pinnan deilazhi irewo giezhou? Uye, bi tande kielieye, bi tani fandui gieghale irewo.
LUK 12:52 Enedu khuinase nie giede tawun kun bise ghuran kun ghua kunghala fandui giene, ghua kun ghuran kunghala fandui giene.
LUK 12:53 Ada kewonghalane fandui giene, kewon adaghalane fandui giene, ana oqinghalane fandui giene, oqin anaghalane fandui giene, ghadunmekie konbiereighalane fandui giene, konbierei ghadunmekieghalane fandui giene."
LUK 12:54 Ersa pse olon kunlade kieliewo, "Ta xibangiede olien nie chanlase 'Ghura boune.' giezhi kieliene. Kieliese boune.
LUK 12:55 Nanbangiese kei bosise, 'Khalundane.' giezhi kieliese khalundane.
LUK 12:56 Ta ene jiazhon giesan kun, ta qienqi bienjikuni mejiene, ene shihouni fenji dane?"
LUK 12:57 "Ta yale alinie olusei fenji dane?
LUK 12:58 Chi noyenyi shida echikude mo jiere duitoughalane gouda. Pse hhe chii panjiku noyen shida lai echise panjiku noyen gunnande jiuise gunnan chii bafanzide khane.
LUK 12:59 Bi chade kielieye, chi 1 fen baerniliuzhe honjizhi ulie qindaghase bafanzise khizhe dane."
LUK 13:1 Ene shihoude danchan kunla BiladoJialili kunlai alasan chusunni hhelai sidagha giesan dunxi dunda huighasan shiqinni Ersade kieliewo.

LUK 13:3 Uye. Bi tande kielieye, ta geizhen ulie giese hhela mutun fugune.

LUK 13:5 Uwo. Bi tande kielieye, ta geizhen ulie giese hhela mutun fugune."
LUK 13:6 Ingiedene Ersa pse bilazhi kieliewo, "Nie kun putou yenzide nie uhuago mutun zeilawo. Hhe mutunsene alima ereile irese nieda ereizhi olu dawo.
LUK 13:7 Ezhanni yenzi sagheisan kunde kieliewo, 'Uzhe, bi ene 3 niende uhuago mutun jierese alima nieda chujieghe dawo. Eneni chizhi daogha, belien oron ezheliezho.'

LUK 13:9 Khuinashi alima souse sougie, ulie souse chizhi widaghaye.'"

LUK 13:11 Hhende sheitan heizhi 18 nien nurunne zhidagha dasan nie bierei wine.
LUK 13:12 Ersa chanla uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Funi, ede chi giensene andawo."

LUK 13:14 Huitan gonjisan kun Ersa hhamuraku udude gien goudaghase hokuzhi kunlade kieliewo, "Hhe tawun zhighudu winema, yangiezhi hhamuraku udude goudaghane?"

LUK 13:17 Ingiesenu fandui giesan kunla nanchan duruzho. Ersa giesan famatu shiqinlai uzhedene kunla man bayasuzho.
LUK 13:18 Ersa pse kieliezho, "Hudai gojia yanni xianli? Yanghala bilane?
LUK 13:19 Hoxian nie caizi furei xianli. Kun agizhi echi yenzidene tareise fugiedazhi mutun gholuse chala jiere bunzhula holiene."
LUK 13:20 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Hudai gojiai yanghala bilane?
LUK 13:21 Hoxian kunieghei xianli. Nie bierei agizhi echidene nie deizi ghurunde teizhi man faighazho."
LUK 13:22 ErsaYelusalenni mo jiere echikude kunlai chenshi aghinlade sughazho.
LUK 13:23 Nie kun asazho, "Ezhan, jiuisan kun choghon woba?" Ersa kunlade kieliewo,
LUK 13:24 "Witan wijiense orokuni xiacha gie. Bi tande kielieye, orone giechen kun olon wo, oro dane.
LUK 13:25 Giei ezhan wijienni khase ta ghadanese wijienni eghizhi 'Ezhan, bijiende wijienni nieya.' giese hhe 'Bi tai tani dane. Ta khalase iresei bi ulie mejiene.' giezhi kieliene.
LUK 13:26 Hhe shihoude ta kieliene, 'Hhe xienzide matan hhantu ochizhi ijienduzho. Pse chi bijienyi geidoude sughazho.'
LUK 13:27 Ingiese hhe kieliene, 'Bi tande kielieye, ta khalase iresei bi ulie mejiene. Ta ene huaishi giesan kunla, mase likai gie.'"
LUK 13:28 "Ta Hudai gojiade Iburaheimu, Isaghei, Yagebu, pse hhe xienzhilani man chanlaku shihoude tani toudene ghadane khighase ta shidunne zhouzhi wilane.
LUK 13:29 Dunnanxibeise kunla irezhi Hudai gojiade xi soune.
LUK 13:30 Chenlie, khuinashikula melieshilane, melieshikula khuinashilane."

LUK 13:32 "Ta echidene hhe funieghede kielie, 'Enedu maghashijie bi sheitanlani touzhi gien goudaghane, chinaer mini shiqin barawo.'
LUK 13:33 Enedu, maghashi, chinaer bi bixi mone yone, Hudai xienzhini Yelusalense chugo ala dane.
LUK 13:34 Yelusalen, Yelusalen, peizhi ireghasan xienzhilai tashidazhi alasan chenshiya. Bi chii kesilani gieduifa muji tigha zhunzhughalane siban doura hhantulaghaku mutun hhantulaghane giese ta duran uwo.
LUK 13:35 Uzhe, chii gie hontan gholuzhi chade feiliene. Bi chade kielieye, chi 'Ezhanni niereghala iresan kunni doulandu.' giezhi kielietula mii pse chanla dane."
LUK 14:1 Hhamuraku udude Ersa nie Falisai kunni lindaoni giede ijiele echikude kunla ghulazhi uzhezho.
LUK 14:2 Zhen hheni melie shighara beghelieni khaitusan kun wine.
LUK 14:3 Ersa jinwun loushi, Falisai kunlade asazho, "Hhamuraku udude gien uzhese olunu ulie olune?"
LUK 14:4 Hhelade shenqi uwo. Ersa hhei jiere khane tei, uzhe goudaghadene echighawo.
LUK 14:5 Ingie hhelade kieliewo, "Tai dunda hhamuraku udude enzheghe, fughe nokiende anda bouse laizhi ulie khizhenu?"
LUK 14:6 Hhela ene kieliende yama kielie dawo.
LUK 14:7 Xinlazhi iresan zhochenla goyalane shanxide echi souwo. Ersa hhelai chanla bilazhi kieliewo,
LUK 14:8 "Ta ghurunde echise shanxide bu sou, tanse fugie zhochen bise tani daoghane.
LUK 14:9 Giei kun iredene kieliese chi ene oronyi zhochende nie ranji giese chi shizhezhi daone.
LUK 14:10 Xinlazhi irekude ta zui bixinni oronde souse xinlasan kun chini uruzhi kieliene, 'Zhanlien, chi ene shanxide sou.' Ingiese kunla uzhese giedughon gou wo.
LUK 14:11 Kien goyane undudaghase boghonidaghane. Goyane boghonidaghase undudaghane."
LUK 14:12 Ersa xinlasan kunde kieliewo, "Chi udukun, heifande zhanlienlane, gaijiulane, qingulane, giebei bayankunlai bu xinla, pse hhelaye chii xinlane.
LUK 14:13 Chi ghurun ijiekude nanxin kunla, canfei, dogholon, sugho, enelani xinla, ingiese chade fuqi wine.
LUK 14:14 Hhela chini khareizhi xinla danema, gou kunla fuho giekude Huda chade gouni ogine."
LUK 14:15 Hhantu sousan kun dunda nie kun enei chenliedene Ersade kieliewo, "Hudai gojiade xi ijiesan kunde fuqi wine."
LUK 14:16 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Nie kun fugiede xi beilazhi zhochen olon xinlawo.
LUK 14:17 Xi souku shihoude hojine peizhi xinlasan kunlai urughale echiwo, 'Irendu, man zhunbei gie goudaghawo.'
LUK 14:18 Kunla nienieji man tui qiiwo. Tou 1 gie kun kieliewo, 'Bi nie ghazha agizho. Uzhele echine. Ire dane. Bu hoku.'
LUK 14:19 Da nie kun kieliewo, 'Bi 5 dui fughe agiwo. Shiile echine. Bu hoku.'
LUK 14:20 Pse nie kun kieliewo, 'Bi bierei agiwo, ingiese echi dane.'"
LUK 14:21 "Hhe hoji kharei iredene ezhandene ene shiqinni man kieliewo. Ezhan hokuzhi hojidene kieliewo, 'Ghujighan echidene chenshini fugie geidou, ga geidoudedu nanxin kun, canfei, sugho, dogholonlai urude ire.'
LUK 14:22 Hoji ezhandene kieliewo, 'Chi kieliesanlai man banji goudaghawo, da kun oron wine.'
LUK 14:23 Hojidene kieliewo, 'Chi echidene dalu mo jieredu, ga mo jierededu kunlai ninkounin uruzhi iredene mini oronni souzhi durugha.'
LUK 14:24 Bi tande kielieye. Touchan xinlasan dunda mini ghurunse ijiechen kun nieda uwo."
LUK 14:25 Tebieji olon kun Ersare hhantu yozho. Hhe ochiradene hhelade kieliewo,
LUK 14:26 "Kun mini enende irese goyane ada, ana, bierei, kesila, eghechijiu, gaijiulasene, pse goya aminsene made olon ulie orese mini tuji danla dane.
LUK 14:27 Kien goya shizijiane beiliezhi mii ulie daghase mini tuji danla dane."
LUK 14:28 "Ta kien lou giekude giezhi gholughanu gholugha dane giezhi baerni ulie sananu?
LUK 14:29 Kunpa ta jichune jiedene pse giedase kunla uzhezhi xiniene,
LUK 14:30 'Ene nie kun loune giedene giezhi khigha dawo.'"
LUK 14:31 "Pse nie honshan hhe nie gojiani honshanghala eghindune giese xien soudene kun giedughon bikuni ulie sananu? Bi 10000 kunghala kunlai 20000 kunni eghi shidanu?
LUK 14:32 Eghi dase hhela gholo bikude kun nie peisenu matugiezhi heqishighakui shanlian giene.
LUK 14:33 Kienliuzhe shihenine ulie jiese mini tuji danla dane."
LUK 14:34 "Dansunshi gouni wo. Widaoni widase pse matugie koudaghane?
LUK 14:35 Widao widasan dansunni ghazha, hhaghade teise yama zoin uwo. Zinie ghadane bendane. Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!"

LUK 15:5 Ereizhi oludene bayasuzhi dalou jierene danladene giedene echiwo.
LUK 15:6 Zhanlien, giebeiladene widasan ghoni ereizhi oluwo. Matan hhantu hunnerei daghaye giezho.

LUK 15:16 Hende oliesuse khighei ijieku noshui ijiene gieliuzhe kiema ulie ogine."

LUK 15:19 Enedu khuinase bi chade kewon danla dane. Mini nie wiliechi danlagha." giezhi kielieye.'"
LUK 15:20 "Ingiedene bosizhe adane hhende echiwo. Adani gholose chanladene zhugheni zholierese holu echi qioru agi orewo.
LUK 15:21 Kewonni adadene kieliewo, 'Ada, bi Hudai melie, chii melie giesan ese oluzho. Enedu khuinase bi chade kewon danla dane.'"
LUK 15:22 "Adani hojidene kieliewo, 'Ghujighan gou jienni agizhe musigha. Kha jiereni geizhi zhogha. Mahei musigha.
LUK 15:23 Hhe taghun fughe tughuchai lai khizhe zharu. Matan ochizhi ijiezhi hunnerei daghaye.
LUK 15:24 Mini fugusan kewon aminne oluwo, widasan kewon kharei irewo!' Ingiese hhela hunnerei daghazho."

LUK 15:27 Hoji kieliewo, 'Jiuchii giede irewo. Hhe pinnan khareizhi irese adachii bayasuzhi taghun fughe tughuchai zharughawo.'"
LUK 15:28 "Fugie kewonni hokuzhi ese orose adani khizhe kewondene sughazhi kieliezho.

LUK 15:30 Chii ene kewon biozilare hhantu jiachanchii ijie widaghadene irese hhende taghun tughuchai zharune!'"
LUK 15:31 "Adani kieliewo, 'Kewon, chi mare hhantu chan souzho. Minughunshi man chinughun wo.
LUK 15:32 Jiuchini fugudene aminne oluwo, widadene khareizhi irewo. Matan indan bayasuzhi hunnerei daghakuni wo.'"
LUK 16:1 Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Nie bayan kunni gonjiai kunla baerni hu huaizho giezhi zhazho.
LUK 16:2 Ezhanni hhei uruzhi iredene kieliewo, 'Mii chighinde iresanshi yan shiqin wo? Chi zhanlai made nie jiui. Chii gonjia pse ulie danlaghane.'"
LUK 16:3 "Hhe gonjia zhughedene kieliezho, 'Mii gonjia ulie danlaghase bi jianlai yan giene? Ghazha waise lilian uwo, ghuile echise shizhene.
LUK 16:4 Bi matui giekui mejiewo. Ingiezhi giese bi gonjia danla dakude kunla mini jienliene.'"
LUK 16:5 "Ingiedene hhe ezhande baer chaisan kunlai nienieji uru irewo. Touchankude asawo, 'Chi ezhandemi giedughon chaine?'
LUK 16:6 '100 gie tunzi tosun chaine.' 'Chi zhanne agizhedene ghujighan souzhi 50 gie tunzi huai.'
LUK 16:7 Da nie kunde asazho, 'Chi giedughon chaine?' '100 gie deizi boudei chaine.' 'Chi zhanne agizhedene 80 gie deizi huai.'
LUK 16:8 Ezhanni gou witu gonjiai jienzhaini kuaiwo. Ene duyani kunla goyadene shiqin banjise gonni kunlase jienzha wo."
LUK 16:9 "Bi tande kielieye, duyai baerghala goyadene oluzhi zhanlien tani. Ingiese baer widakude qientande tai jienliene.
LUK 16:10 Ta ga shiqinde zhunshi ulie giese fugie shiqindeye zhunshi ulie giene. Ga shiqinde undan wise fugie shiqindeye undan uwo.
LUK 16:11 Ta duyani baerni zhunshi ulie giese tande kien asiman jieredu zhen baerni gonjighane?
LUK 16:12 Ta kunlai dunxilai zhunshi ulie giese tande kien dunxilane ogine?"
LUK 16:13 "Alinie hojiliuzhe ghua ezhanni shunji dane. Ene niede henjise hhe niede orene. Ene niede gundushi hhe niede gongien wo. Ta Huda baer ghualai hhantu shunji dane."
LUK 16:14 Falisai kun jin baerrezhe, ene kielienyi sonosudene uzhezhi xiniezho.
LUK 16:15 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta kunyi melie gou kun danlazho. Tai zhughede yan sumulasanyi Huda mejiene. Kunlai melie kuaisanshi Hudai melie henjikuni wo.
LUK 16:16 Musani guijin, xienzhishu Yaheiyase jieshu oluwo. Enense khuinashi Hudai gojiai gouxioxii chonji keiwo, kunla man xiacha giezhi hhende orone giezho.
LUK 16:17 Ingieliuzhe asiman zemin widaliuzhe guijin jieredu nie jienjienda ulie widane.
LUK 16:18 Kien biereighalane lihun giedene pse agise piofen giezho. Lihun giesan biereini agisan kunye piofen giezho."
LUK 16:19 "Nie bayan kun zishei gou jien musizhi niudunie gofende xianfu giezho.
LUK 16:20 Nie Lasalu giesan ghuichenyi hunshende man yara wo. Chan bayan kunyi wijien konde soughazho.
LUK 16:21 Sumulase bayan kunyi shire jierese ijiezhi feiliesan ginan zhazha anda bou irese ijiezhi chudune giezho. Lien noghei irezhi yaraini doluzho.
LUK 16:22 Khuinashi ghuichen duya ijiewo. Qienxienla qienliedene Iburaheimui shida echighawo. Hhe bayan kun ye duya ijiedene bulawo."
LUK 16:23 "Bayan kun dozoheide lolien giezho. Qiorunne qila gholose marazhi Iburaheimui chanlawo. Lasalu hhei shida wo.
LUK 16:24 Waradazhi kieliewo, 'Iburaheimu mii xienren, made ubali nie xii! Lasalui dafalazhi kha ghurundene usu nie zhanjidene kielienyimi nie liandagha gie. Bi khan dunda siderazhi tendun shouizho!'"
LUK 16:25 "Iburaheimu kieliewo, 'Kewon, chi melieshida xianfu giesanne nie sumula. Lasalu lolien giezho. Ede Lasalude futanshiwo, chi lolien giene.
LUK 16:26 Pse nieshi matanyi dunda ghon geizho. Bi chii hhende daorene giese daore dane. Chi mii enende daorene gieliuzheye daore dane.'"
LUK 16:27 "Bayan kun kieliewo, 'Mii xienren, qinse bi chii xiahua gieye. Lasalui mii giede peizhi echigha.
LUK 16:28 Made tawun gaijiu wo. Hhe echidene nie jingao gie gie. Pse hhela ene oronde lolien giele irene.'"
LUK 16:29 "Iburaheimu kieliewo, 'Hhelade Musai shu, xienzhilai shu wine. Chenlie gie.'
LUK 16:30 Hhe kieliewo, 'Ulie olune, mii xienren Iburaheimu, fugusan kun aminne oludene echise hhela geizhen giene.'
LUK 16:31 Iburaheimu kieliewo, 'Musai shu, xienzhilai shui ulie chenliese fugusan kun aminne oluseye ulie chenliene.'"
LUK 17:1 Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Zui fanjiku shiqin chan winema, kunlai zui fanjighasan hhe kunde gou widawo!
LUK 17:2 Enezighan ga kun dundadu niei zui fanjighase ghuzhundeni qiemanshai banladene haide boughase da gou wo.
LUK 17:3 Ta xioxin giendu, gaijiutai chii hokughase kheila. Hhe geizhen giese roulie.
LUK 17:4 Nie kun niudude doleifa zui fanjidene doleifa khareizhi 'Bi ese oluzho.' giezhi kieliese roulie."
LUK 17:5 Shitula Ezhande kieliewo, "Bijiende xianxin giekui olodogha."
LUK 17:6 Ezhan kieliewo, "Tande caizi fure chigei xianxin gieku bise ta ene sunshu mutunde chi genzilada khizhe haide echi osi gieseye kielienyichii chenliene."
LUK 17:7 "Tai dunda kienyi hoji ghazha qighalazhi irenu, ghoni adulazhi irese 'Chi ghujighan soudene ijie.' giezhi kielienu?
LUK 17:8 Kenjin ulie kieliene. Khareidene 'Chi made budan giezhi mii ushilazhi ijieghadene chi ochizhi ijie.' giezhi kieliene.
LUK 17:9 Hoji ezhan kieliesan mutun giese ezhan mafan giezho giezhi kielienu? Ulie kieliene.
LUK 17:10 Taye niekielien wo. Ta ezhan kieliesan mutun giezhi baraghadene ingiezhi kieliene, 'Bijienshi yama gie daku hoji wo. Eneshi bijien indan giekuni wo.'"
LUK 17:11 ErsaYelusalende echikude Samaliya, Jialilini dundadu oronde echizho.
LUK 17:12 Nie aghinde orone giese hharan pifugientu gholode ire beidene
LUK 17:13 fugiede waradazho, "Ezhan Ersa bijiende ubali nie xii!"

LUK 17:15 Hhelai dundase nie kun goyane goudasanyi mejiedene kharei ire Hudai fugiede kuaizho.
LUK 17:16 Ersai kon konde xiutulie papaladene mafan kieliewo. Eneshi Samaliya kun wo.
LUK 17:17 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta goudasanshi hharolie wola? Da yesun kun khala wo?
LUK 17:18 Ene niman kunse chugo pse nieda Hudai kuaile ese irewu?"
LUK 17:19 Ingie hhe kunde kieliewo, "Chi bosizhedene echi. Chii xianxin gieku chii jiuiwo."
LUK 17:20 Niudude Falisai kunla Ersade asazho, "Hudai gojia yan shihoude irene?" Ersa kieliewo, "Hudai gojia irese chanlakui pusho.
LUK 17:21 Kunla uzhe, Hudai gojia enende wo, hhende wo giezhi ulie kieliene. Hudai gojia tani dunda wo."
LUK 17:22 Pse tujiladene kieliewo, "Ta Kunnikewonni niudui uzhene gieku shihou kuzhenema, uzhe dane.
LUK 17:23 Kunla 'Uzhe, kunnikewon enende wo.' 'Uzhe, hhende wo.' giezhi kieliese ta bu echi. Hhelai bu dagha.
LUK 17:24 Shanjien asiman enemiense khizhezhi hhemiende zhouiku mutun Kunnikewonni ududeye ingiene.
LUK 17:25 Kunnikewon irese ijinyo xien shouku giezhi ene idai kunla hhei fandui giene."
LUK 17:26 "Nuhhani xienzide matugiezhoshi Kunnikewonyi xienzideye qingiene.
LUK 17:27 Hhe shihoudedu kunla ijiezho, ochizho, bierei agizho, dafalazhi izhi Nuhha chon sudoro oroku hhe udude hunshui iredene man yenji alawo."
LUK 17:28 "Kunnikewonni udu Luteii hhe shihoudedu niekielien wo. Hhe kunla ijiezho, ochizho, agizho, huizho, ghazha tareizho, gie giezho.
LUK 17:29 LuteiSodomase yolaku hhe niudude khan funi asiman jierese bouredene man sidera widawo."
LUK 17:30 "Kunnikewon xienjiku ududeye ingiene.
LUK 17:31 Hhe udude gie jieredu kunla giederase dunxilai agile bu bouzhe. Ghazha jieredulaye giedene khareizhi bu echi.
LUK 17:32 Ta Luteii bierei matui gholusanni nie sumula.
LUK 17:33 Kien aminne baohu giene giese aminne widaghane. Aminne widaghase jiuine.
LUK 17:34 Bi tande kielieye, hhe nie xii ghuala nie chon jiere kijiese niei uduru echine, niei jiene.
LUK 17:35 Ghua bierei qieman sidase niei uduru echine, niei jiene."
LUK 17:37 Hhela asawo, "Ezhan, imutu shiqin khala fashen giene?" Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Fugusan dunxi khalashi inye khala wo."
LUK 18:1 Ersa tujiladene izhi ulie beidene onxian giezhi zhughe ulie widakui bilazhi kieliewo.
LUK 18:2 "Nie chenshide nie noyen Hudase ulie ayine, kunlaiye ulie zunjine.
LUK 18:3 Hhe chenshide nie guafu wo. Ibeizi noyenyi hhende echizhi kieliezho, 'Made nie duitou wo. Chi made gundande chuli gie.'
LUK 18:4 Ene noyen izhi ese gonjizho. Oloncha oludene sudorone sumulazho, 'Bi Hudase ulie ayine, bexinlaiye ulie zunjinema,
LUK 18:5 ene bierei ibeizi mii souine. Enei bi goudaghaye pse mini jindaghazhi alane.'"
LUK 18:6 Ezhan kieliewo, "Ene gou witu noyen kieliesanyi ta chenlie.
LUK 18:7 Huda sunghuzhi irezhi xieni udu hhei waradasan kunlade Huda gundanni ulie ogidene udazhi banman gienu?
LUK 18:8 Bi tande kielieye, Huda hhelade ghujighan gundanni ogine. Ingieliuzhe Kunnikewon irekude duyade goude xianxin giechen kun giedun ereizhi olune?"
LUK 18:9 Goyaneshi gou kun wo giezhi kunlai meilade uzhesan kunlade Ersa bilazhi kieliewo.
LUK 18:10 "Nie Falisai kun shui shanjisan kunghala huitande onxian giele echiwo.
LUK 18:11 Falisai kun niezheghan beidene onxian giezho, 'Huda, bi chade mafan kielieye. Bi kunlai buxian wo. Ese qianlazho, gou wini ese giezho, piofen ese giezho. Ene shui shanjisan kunyiye genben buxian wo.
LUK 18:12 Bi nie xinqide lianhui orozo bareizho. Shourusene 10 fenzhi 1 ni chade ogizho.'
LUK 18:13 Shui shanjisan kun gholode beidene asimanyi ayizhi uzhe da echanne chuidazhi kieliezho, 'Huda, bishi zuiren wo. Made ubali nie xii!'
LUK 18:14 Bi tande kielieye, giedene echikude Huda gounide sanasanshi hhe kun pusho, ene kun wo. Kien goyane undudaghase boghonidaghane. Goyane boghonidaghase undudaghane."
LUK 18:15 Kunla jiujiulane qioruzhi Ersai melie ire maqighane giezho. Tujila chanladene hhelai sugiezho.
LUK 18:16 Ersa hhelai uruzhi ire tujilade kieliewo, "Kesilai bu dui, mii shida ire gie. Hudai gojiashi imutu kunlanughun wo.
LUK 18:17 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kien kewosi mutun Hudai gojiai ulie jienliese hhende oro dane."
LUK 18:18 Nie noyen Ersade asawo, "Gou loushi, bi matui giese chanqiku aminni jienliene?"
LUK 18:19 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii yangiezhi gou wo giezho? Hudase chugo gouni uwo.
LUK 18:20 Minlinyi chi mejiene, Piofen bu gie, kun bu ala, bu ghula, jia ganzhen bu bei, ada anane zunji giezho."
LUK 18:21 Hhe kieliewo, "Enelai bi ga xienzise man zunjizho."
LUK 18:22 Ersa chenliedene kieliewo, "Chade da nie chaizho. Chi bisanlane man huizhi nanxin kunlade ogi. Ingiese chii boubei asiman jiere wo. Ingiedene irezhi mii dagha."
LUK 18:23 Hheshi nie fugie bayan kun wo. Ene kielienyi chenliedene hende yuchourazho.
LUK 18:24 Ersa hhei uzhedene kieliewo, "Baertu kun Hudai gojiade oroku chijia no wo.
LUK 18:25 Loto zhun boghose daoku bayan kun Hudai gojiade orokuse da sunfan wo."
LUK 18:26 Chenliesan kunla kieliewo, "Ingiese kienyi jiui shidane?"
LUK 18:27 Ersa kieliewo, "Kun gie dakui Huda giene."
LUK 18:28 Beduru kieliewo, "Uzhe, bijien goyanughunne bendadene chii daghazho."
LUK 18:29 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, kun Hudai gojiade oluzhi gie, bierei, gaijiu, ada, ana, kesilane bendase
LUK 18:30 ene duyade pse olon ogine, houshide chanqiku amin ogine."

LUK 18:32 Hhela hhei niman kunlade jiuise kunla xilun, shizheghane, ungie jiere nunpune.
LUK 18:33 Mabienzighala eghine, da alane. Ingie ghurudude aminne olune."
LUK 18:34 Ene shiqinyi tujila dunjire dawo. Isii niuighazho, hhela hhe kieliesan isii mejie dawo.
LUK 18:35 ErsaYeligede chadashikude nie sugho mo bienzide soudene ghuizho.

LUK 18:38 Deigo waradawo, "Dawudeni houdei Ersa, made ubali nie xii!"
LUK 18:39 Melie yosan kunla shenqi bu khizhe giezhi jiebalase hhe genjia fugiede waradazhi kieliezho, "Dawudeni houdei, made ubali nie xii!"

LUK 19:1 ErsaYeligede orodene yozhi daokude
LUK 19:2 nie kunyi niereini Sagai giene. Shui shanjisan kun dunda qienli fugie wo, bayan no wo.

LUK 19:4 Ingie holu melieshidadene nie mutun jiere khirei Ersai uzhene giezho. Ersa hhense yozhi daone.
LUK 19:5 Ersa mutun konde echidene qiorunne qila kieliewo, "Sagai, ghujighan bouzhe. Enedu bi chii giede ijinyo soune."
LUK 19:6 Hhe jindazhi bouzhedene hende bayasuzhi Ersai jienliewo.
LUK 19:7 Uzhesan kunla ene matugie zuirenyi giede souwo giezhi nieniedene kieliezho.

LUK 19:14 Hhei gojiani kunla ene noyenyi henjizhi daibioni khuina dafalazhi echigha 'Ene kunyi matande honshan danlaghaku duran uwo.' giezhi kieliewo."

LUK 19:16 Ji 1 gie hojini kieliewo, 'Ezhan, bi nie antan jierese 10 pei zhenjiwo.'
LUK 19:17 Noyen hhende kieliewo, 'Giesan gou wo. Chishi gou hoji wo. Chi ga shiqinde shixinji giezho, ingiese bi chade hharan chenshi gonjighaye.'"
LUK 19:18 "Da nie hojini kieliewo, 'Ezhan, bi nie antan jierese 5 pei zhenjiwo.'
LUK 19:19 Noyen ene niedeye kieliewo, 'Bi chade tawun chenshi gonjighaye.'"
LUK 19:20 "Pse nie hojini kieliewo, 'Ezhan, uzhe. Bi chii ene nie antanyi shoujinde boui ghurazho.
LUK 19:21 Chi lihaishi bi chase ayizho. Chi ese jiesan oronse agine, ese tareisan oronse ghurane.'"
LUK 19:22 "Noyen hhende kieliewo, 'Chi ene doghun hoji! Bi chii kielienghala chii kheilane. Bi ese jiesan oronse agizhi ese tareisan oronse ghurachen lihaitu kun bikui chi mejienu?
LUK 19:23 Qinse mini baerni yale inhande ese teiwo? Bi irekude benqien lixiji agi khizhene.'
LUK 19:24 Ingie hhe shida beisan kunlade kieliewo, 'Ene kunse nie antanni agi echidene hharan antantu kunde ogi.'"
LUK 19:25 "Ingie kunla hhende kieliewo, 'Ezhan, hhende hharan antan wine.'
LUK 19:26 Noyen kieliewo. 'Bi tande kielieye, bichen kunde pse olon ogine. Wichen kunse bisanlainiye agi echine.
LUK 19:27 Mini honshan ulie danlaghachen hhe duitoulai mini melie lai iredene ala.'"
LUK 19:28 Ersa enei kielie baludene melie yozhi Yelusalende khireine giezho.
LUK 19:29 Ganlanshan giezhi urusan ula shida Bofaqi, Bodanide kuzhekude Ersa ghua tujine peizhi
LUK 19:30 kieliewo, "Ta duimienni aghinde echi. Orose nie huiyasan ga enzheghei chanlane. Kieme unuzhi ese daozho. Ta andaghadene lai ire.
LUK 19:31 Kunla tande 'Yangiezhi andaghane?' giezhi asase 'Ezhan injine.' giezhi kielie."

LUK 19:36 Ersa yokude kunla man jienlane mo jiere peiwo.

LUK 19:38 "Ezhanyi niereghala iresan honshande doulandu! Asiman jiere pinnan wo, Zui Undudedu Hudai kuai!"

LUK 19:42 "Bi sumulase enedu chi pinnan olukuni mejiese gou woma, ede chi mejie dane, mejiekui niuighazho.

LUK 20:3 Ersa kieliewo, "Biye tande nie unqi asaye. Ta made kielie,
LUK 20:4 Yaheiyai xili gieghaku qienli asimanse onu, kunlase wo?"

LUK 20:6 Kunlase wo giese bexinla man matai tashighala eghi alane, hhela Yaheiyashi xienzhi wo giezhi xianxin giezho."
LUK 20:7 Ingie khalase iresei ulie mejiene giezhi hhela kieliewo.

LUK 20:11 Da nie hojine pse ghuraghale echiwo. Eghizhi shizheghadene khosun echighawo.
LUK 20:12 Pse nie hojine echighawo. Eghizhi shan dailaghadene tungu khizheghawo.
LUK 20:13 Putou yenzii ezhan kieliezho, 'Bi matugiene? Bi oresan kewonne echighayema, hhela zunjineba.'
LUK 20:14 Bouisan kunla hhei chanladene nieniene shanlian giezhi kieliewo, 'Eneshi jiachanni jienliechen wo. Matan enei alayema, jiachanni manughun gholune!'
LUK 20:15 Ingie putou yenzise tungu khigha alawo. Ta sumulase putou yenzii ezhan ene kunlai matugiene?
LUK 20:16 Ezhan iredene bouisan kunlai man alazhi psedu kunlade bouizhi ogine." Chenliesan kunla kieliewo, "Imutu shiqin jiedui uwo!"

LUK 20:18 Jien hhe tashi jiere anda bousan kunla zhazhazi gholune. Ene tashi kienyi jiere anda bouse zai miendaghane."
LUK 20:19 Jinwun hanjia, fugie buwala Ersa hhelai bilazhi kieliesei uzhe khizhedene deigo bareine giezhoma, bexinlase ayizho.
LUK 20:20 Hhela kunlai jizide jiazhon gieghazhi Ersani uzheghale echiwo. Hhe kielie codaghase shenzhande zhazhi bareighane giezho.
LUK 20:21 Jiazhon giesan kunla Ersade asazho, "Loushi, chi kieliesan, jianjisan man oluzho. Enei bijien mejiezho. Chi kunni niekielien uzhezhi Hudai daolini shixinde sughazho.
LUK 20:22 Matan Kaisa honshande shui jiuise oluzhou ese oluzho?"
LUK 20:23 Ersa piendasanyini mejiedene hhelade kieliewo,
LUK 20:24 "Made miengui nie uzhegha. Ene qiorun, haoshi kiennughun wo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Kaisanughun wo."
LUK 20:25 "Qinse Kaisanughunshi Kaisade ogi, Hudanughunshi Hudade ogi."
LUK 20:26 Hhela kunlai melie Ersa kieliesande yama codasei erei dazho. Ersa huida giesande ghaniradene amanlane menjiwo.
LUK 20:27 Fuho gieku shiqin uwo giesan niezhan Sadugai kunla Ersai shida ire asawo,
LUK 20:28 "Loushi, Musa guijin jiere huaizho, nie kun bierei agidene kewosi wi duya ijiese jiuni zhoui gaidene houdei liuikuni wo giezho.
LUK 20:29 Ingiese gaijiu dololie laoda bierei agidene kewosi wi duya ijiewo.
LUK 20:30 Laoer, laosan man hhei zhouiwo.
LUK 20:31 Dololie man zhouidene kewosi wi duya ijiewo.
LUK 20:32 Zuihoude biereiye duya ijiewo.
LUK 20:33 Ingiese fuho giekude hheshi kienyi bierei wo? Gaijiu dololie man hhei agiwo."
LUK 20:34 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ene duyani kunla agizhi dafalane.
LUK 20:35 Duya ijiesan kun dundase aminne oluzhi houshide zige bichen kunla ulie agizhi ulie dafalane.
LUK 20:36 Hhela pse ulie duya ijiene, qienxien niekielien wo. Hhelashi fuho giechen wo, Hudai kesila wo.
LUK 20:37 Duya ijiesan kun aminne olukui Musaye eghesun khan sideraku jinwun jiere zhenmin giezho. Musa Ezhanni urukude Iburaheimuni Huda, Isagheini Huda, Yagebuni Huda giezho.
LUK 20:38 Ingiese Hudashi duya ijiesan kunyi Huda pusho, amitu kunyi Huda wo. Huda uzhese kunla man amitu wo."
LUK 20:39 Giedun jinwun hanjia kieliewo, "Loushi, chi kieliesan oluzho."
LUK 20:40 Hhela ayizhi pse hhende yama asa dazho.
LUK 20:41 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Kunla matugie Mexihashi Dawudeni houdei wo giezho?
LUK 20:42 Dawude goyane Zeburei jiere kieliezho, 'Ezhan mii Ezhande kieliewo, "Bi duitoulaichii kon dourachii teitula chi mini borun miende sou."'
LUK 20:44 Qingiese Dawude Mexihai Ezhan giezhi uruse Mexiha matugie Dawudeni houdei wo?"
LUK 20:45 Bexinla chenliekude Ersa tujiladene kieliewo,
LUK 20:46 "Ta jinwun hanjialai fangula. Hhela fudu jienni musidene geidoude toreizhi kunla hhelade kielien asakude xiqi wo. Huitanni undu wizi, xini shanxide soukude xiqi wo.
LUK 20:47 Hhela guafui gieni chigheine. Jiazhon giezhi oloncha onxian giene. Enezighan kunlai pse gundude faine."
LUK 21:1 Ersa qiorunne qila bayan kunla mechii baer teiku xianzide baer teikuni uzhezho.
LUK 21:2 Pse nie nanxin guafu hhende ghua fenfenzi baer teisei uzhewo.
LUK 21:3 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene nanxin guafu soyuji kunlase olon teiwo.
LUK 21:4 Kunla olonsene teiwo. Guafude yama uwoma, udu daoku baerlane man teiwo."
LUK 21:5 Niezhan kunla mechini seighan tashi, Hudade ogisan mureghala zhonhon giesei kielienduzho. Ingiese Ersa kieliewo.
LUK 21:6 "Ta chanlasan enelai hhe shihou kuzhese cheizhi tashi jiere tashi nieda ulie jiene."
LUK 21:7 Hhela Ersade asazho, "Loushi, yan xienzide ene shiqinla fashen giene? Enela fashen giekude yan zunji wine?"
LUK 21:8 Hhe kieliezho, "Ta xioxin giezhi kunlai bu piendagha. Olon kunla mii niereghala iredene bishi hhe enbene, ede shihou kuzhewo giese ta bu dagha.
LUK 21:9 Ta eghinduzhi londasan xioxini sonosuse bu ayi. Ene shiqin xien fashen gienema, duya baraku deigo ulie kuzhene."
LUK 21:10 Pse hhelade kieliewo, "Minzu minzula eghindune, gojia gojiala eghindune.
LUK 21:11 Zemin fugiede gojiolune, gochude oliesuku inzhanku gien wine, asiman jierese fugie ghudureqi irezhi ayighane."
LUK 21:12 "Ene shiqin iretula kunla tai heizhi bareidene huitan, bafanzide jiuine. Mii yenyinghala tai honshan, shenzhanlai melie lai echine.
LUK 21:13 Hheshi made ganzhen beiku jihui wo.
LUK 21:14 Panjichen kunde matugie huida giekui melieshi zhunbei bu gie.
LUK 21:15 Bi tande duitoulatai tai kieliezhi dao daku kielien, agheli ogine.
LUK 21:16 Lien ada, ana, gaijiu, qingu, zhanlienlaye tai ghudanduzhi niezhanlani alane.
LUK 21:17 Mii yenyinghala kunla man tai henjine.
LUK 21:18 Ingieliuzhe tai niekozi usunye ulie widane.
LUK 21:19 Ta izhigie rennai giese goyane jiuine."
LUK 21:20 "Budui iredene Yelusalenyi wiqikui ta chanlase hhe widaghaku udu ghujinlasei mejiene.
LUK 21:21 Ingiekude Yudayade sousan kunla, ulade piile echi. Chenshini kunla ghadane khirei. Xianni kunla chenshide bu oro.
LUK 21:22 Enezighan udushi faiku udu wo. Jinwun jiere huaisan kielienyi gholughane.
LUK 21:23 Hhe udude kewosi laisan, gogoghasanlade gou widawo! Zemin jiere zeinan wo, Hudai hokuku ene bexinlai jiere irezho.
LUK 21:24 Hhela khudogho doura fugune, pse bareidene go gojiade lai echine. Niman kunni udu kurutula niman kun iredene Yelusalenni tai pindaghane."
LUK 21:25 "Hhe shihou kuzhese naran, sara, hodunla bienjizhi zunji uzheghane. Haide lan jiulizhi onghonose zemin jieredu gojiala man jindazhi matugiekui mejie dazho.
LUK 21:26 Asimanyi lilianla gojioluse duya matui gholune gie kunla ayidene injirene.
LUK 21:27 Ingiekude Kunnikewon nenli, famanude olien jierese irekui kunla chanlane.
LUK 21:28 Ene shiqin kaishi giese bosizhedene qiorunne qila. Tai shuiku udu chadashiwo."
LUK 21:29 Ersa hhelade bilazhi kieliewo, "Ta uhuago mutun, psedu mutunlai uzhe.
LUK 21:30 Mutun lachen keikui ta uzhese khaluncha orokui mejiene.
LUK 21:31 Taye niekielien wo. Ta ene shiqinla fashen giesei chanlase Hudai gojia chadashisei mejiene.
LUK 21:32 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, ene idaini kunla fugutula ene shiqinla man gholune.
LUK 21:33 Asiman zemin widaliuzhe mii kielien kenjin ulie widane."
LUK 21:34 "Ta jinxin giendu. Pse ta hunnerei daghazhi ochizhi ijiekude, duyani shiqinghala munan giezhi zhugheitai kunzhi giekude hhe udu irene. Hhe shihou irese onghala zhaghasun bareiku niekielien wo, mejie dakude irene.
LUK 21:35 Hhe udu irekude zemin jiereshiku kunlade man irene.
LUK 21:36 Ta chan onxian giezhi jinxin giendu. Qingiese ene shiqin irekude holuzhi andadene Kunnikewonni melie bei shidane."
LUK 21:37 Ersa niudunie mechide kunlade surughazho. Niexiinie Ganlanshande echizhi souzho.
LUK 21:38 Bexinla man eqiemagha eqie mechide Ersa jianjisei chenliele irezho.
LUK 22:1 Jiulidaosan Jie giezhi urusan Tanmien Jie kuzhewo.
LUK 22:2 Fugie buwa, jinwun hanjiala bexinlase ayise yan banfaghala Ersai alase gou wo giezhi sumulazho.
LUK 22:3 Ingiekude Jialie kun Yudani sudoro Ibilisi orowo. Hheshi 12 gie tuji dundadu nie wo.
LUK 22:4 Yuda fugie buwa, mechi sagheisan kunlare Ersai matugie ghudandukui shanlian giele echiwo.
LUK 22:5 Hhela bayasuzhi Yudade baer ogikui dain giewo.
LUK 22:6 Yuda tunyi oludene bexinla wikude Ersai ghudanduku jihui ereizho.
LUK 22:7 Tanmien Jie kuzhezhi Jiulidaosan Jieni ghoni zharuku udude
LUK 22:8 ErsaBeduruYaheiya ghualani peizhi kieliewo, "Ta matande Jiulidaosan Jieni ijiuni zhunbei giele echi. Matan ijienduye."

LUK 22:12 Hhe tande lou jiere man qiendaghasan nie fugie gieni uzheghane. Ta hhende zhunbei gie."
LUK 22:13 Hhela echidene chanlasan Ersa kieliesanghala niekielien wo. Ingie hhela hhende Jiulidaosan Jieni zhunbei giewo.
LUK 22:14 Shihou kuzhese Ersa shitularene hhantu xi souwo.

LUK 22:17 Ersa beizii agi daore Hudade mafan kieliedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta enei man ghughazhi ochindu.
LUK 22:18 Bi tande kielieye, enedu khuinase bi pse putoujiuni ulie ochizhi Hudai gojia ireku shihou kune."
LUK 22:19 Ingie ginanyi barei mafan kieliedene ghulu hhelade ogi kieliewo, "Eneshi tande oluzhi ogisan mii beye wo. Ta mii jilazhi enei gie."

LUK 22:21 Ingieliuzhe, uzhe, mini ghudandune giesan kun mii shida souzhi mare hhantu ijiezho.
LUK 22:22 Huda jiejin giesan mutun Kunnikewon duya ijienema, hhei ghudandusan kunde gou widawo!"
LUK 22:23 Hhela nieniedene asazho, "Imutu shiqini kien giene?"
LUK 22:24 Hhelai dunda kien zui fugie wo giezhiye nienieji zhenjinduzho.
LUK 22:25 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Niman kunlai dunda honshan noyenla qienli bareizhi kunlai gonjiliuzhe hhelai gouni ogisan kun giezhi uruzho.
LUK 22:26 Ta niekielien pusho, tai dunda zui fugieni zui meilashi, lindao danlane giesan kun ushilachen kun mutun gie.
LUK 22:27 Kien fugie wo? Xi sousan kun fugie onu ushilachen kun fugie wo? Xi sousan kun fugie woba. Ingieliuzhe bishi tai dunda ushilachen kun wo.
LUK 22:28 Kunla mini fandui giezhi alane giese ta izhi mare hhantu wo.
LUK 22:29 Huda made gonjiku qienlini ogiku mutun bi ye tande qienlini ogiye.
LUK 22:30 Ta marezhe hhantu mini gojiade ijiezhi ochine. Ta baozo jiere souzhi Isilieni 12 gie paini gonjine."
LUK 22:31 "Ximun, Ximun! Ibilisi tai boudei shierlaku mutun shierlane giezhi Hudade xiahua giewo.
LUK 22:32 Ingiese bi chade oluzhi chii xianxin gieku bu fura giezhi onxian giewo. Chi geizhen giedene gaijiulane khiduzhegha."
LUK 22:33 Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi chimare hhantu bafanzide orozhi fuguseye zhunbei gie goudazho!"
LUK 22:34 Ersa kieliewo, "Beduru, bi chade kielieye, enedu tigha kheilatula chi mii 3 hui ulie renjine."
LUK 22:35 Ingie pse kieliewo, "Bi tai echighakude baer, qibao, maheiye uwo. Tande yama chaizhoye?" Hhela kieliewo, "Uye."
LUK 22:36 Ersa kieliewo, "Ede baer, qibao bichenla barei, khudogho wise jienne huizhi agi.
LUK 22:37 Bi tande kielieye hhei zuirende sanawo giezhi jinwun jiere mii zhiizhi kieliesanla kenjin gholune. Enbene, mii zhiizhi kieliesan ene zhen gholuzho."
LUK 22:38 Hhela kieliewo, "Ezhan, enende ghua khudogho wo." Ersa kieliewo, "Kuruwo."

LUK 22:42 "Ada, chi duran bise ene shouku giekui made bu iregha! Ingieliuzhe mii duranghala bu gie, chii duranghala gie."
LUK 22:43 Ingiekude nie qienxien asiman jierese iredene hhende nenli ogiwo.

LUK 22:45 Onxian gie balu bosizhedene tujilai hhende echiwo. Hhela hende munan giedene hhunturazho.
LUK 22:46 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yangiezhi hhunturazho? Bosizhedene onxian gie, pse miine."

LUK 22:53 Niudunie bi mechide tanre hhantu wo, ulie bareine. Ede tai shihou wo, kharani qienlii bareizho."
LUK 22:54 Hhela Ersai bareidene zui fugie buwai giede lai echiwo. Beduru gholose daghazho.

LUK 23:1 Kunla man hhantu Ersai Biladoi melie echighawo.

LUK 23:6 Bilado chenliedene asawo, "Eneshi Jialili kun onu?"

LUK 23:15 Hherodeye yama zuini ereizhi olu dadene enende kharei ireghawo. Ene kunde fugughaku zui uwo.

LUK 23:30 Hhe shihoude kunla fugie ulade kieliezhi bijienni jiere una! Ga ulade kieliezhi bijienni kha giene.
LUK 23:31 Hhela noghon mutunde ingiezhi giese ghosan mutunde matugie giene?"
LUK 23:32 Da ghua fanrenlai Ersare hhantu alane giezho.
LUK 23:33 Hhela qiorun yasun oron giesan oronde kudene Ersai shizijia jiere ghadawo. Ghua fanrenniye Ersai lianmiende ghadawo.
LUK 23:34 Ersa kieliewo, "Adaya, hhelai mienlie. Hhela yan giesanne ulie mejiene." Buduila fendan qianguzhi Ersai jienni ghughazho.
LUK 23:35 Bexinla beidene uzhezho. Noyenlaye uzhezhi xiniezhi kieliezho, "Hhe kunlai jiuiwo, goyashi Huda sunghusan Hudai Mexiha enbese goyane jiui gie."
LUK 23:36 Buduila Ersai shida khirei cu ogidene xilun giezhi
LUK 23:37 chi Yutai kunni honshan enbese goyane jiuisha giezho.
LUK 23:38 Ersai qiorun qinde nie peizii gie eneshi Yutai kunni honshan wo giezho.
LUK 23:39 Hhantu ghadasan nie fanren Ersai sugiezhi kieliewo, "Chishi Mexiha pushonu? Goyane jiuidene bijienyiye jiuisha!"
LUK 23:40 Da nie fanren hhei sugiezhi kieliewo, "Chii xianxianji fugughaku zui panjidene Hudase da ulie ayinu?
LUK 23:41 Matan giesan wilie mutunshi ghadase oluzho, ene kun nie huaishi ese giezho."
LUK 23:42 Ingie kieliewo, "Ersa, chi goya gojiadene qienli bareikude mini jila."
LUK 23:43 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chade shuhua kielieye, enedu matan ghuala qientande hhantulane."
LUK 23:44 Chabudu zhunwuse xiawu 3 jien olutula zemin man kharalazho.
LUK 23:45 Naran nudun kharalawo. Dajienni sudorodu menlienzi dundase kei echidene ghua gholuwo.
LUK 23:46 Ersa fugiede waradazhi kieliewo, "Ada, bi chade ruhherne jiuiye!" Ene kielienyi kieliedene ho sirawo.
LUK 23:47 Baifuzhan ene shiqinni chanladene Hudai kuaizhi kieliewo, "Eneshi zhenzhen gou kun enbene!"
LUK 23:48 Fashen giesan shiqinni uzhesan kunla man echanne chuidazhi khareiwo.
LUK 23:49 Niezhan Ersai tanisan kunla, Jialilise daghazhi iresan biereila gholode beidene uzhezho.
LUK 23:50 Fugie fayenni nie noyenyi nierei Yusufu giene. Hheshi nie gou kun wo, gundan kun wo.
LUK 23:51 Fayende kunla hui keizhi Ersai widaghane giese ene kun tunyi ese oluwo. Hheshi Yudayani Yalimatai chenshini kun wo, izhi Hudai gojia irekui sagheizho.
LUK 23:52 Biladoi hhende echidene Ersai beyeni xiahua giezhi kerewo.
LUK 23:53 Agi bouzhe boside boui tashide waisan fugie mezade teiwo. Hhe mezade kun nieda teizhi ese daozho.
LUK 23:54 Enedushi zhunbei gieku udu wo. Hhamuraku udu ede kuzhene.
LUK 23:55 Jialilise Ersai daghazhi iresan biereila khuina daghadene mezade Ersai beyeni matui teisei uzhewo.
LUK 23:56 Ingie hhela khareizhi echidene xianlio, xianshui zhunbei giezho. Hhamuraku udu oluwo. Hhela jiomunni minlinni zunjizhi hhe niudude hhamurawo.
LUK 24:1 Xinqini ogheikude giedun biereila zhunbei giesan xianlioni bareidene mezade irewo.
LUK 24:2 Hhela uzhese mezai duighasan tashi ghoghorei daozho.
LUK 24:3 Oro echi uzhese Ezhan Ersai beye wida khizho.
LUK 24:4 Hhela zhen jindakude menzhali ghua kun shidani beizho, jienseni gon faine.
LUK 24:5 Niende ayidene melie papalazho. Hhe ghua kun biereilade kieliezho, "Ta yangiezhi fugusan kun dundase amitu kun ereine?
LUK 24:6 Hhe enende uwo, aminne oluwo. Hhe Jialilide kieliesan kielienyi ta jila danu?
LUK 24:7 Hhe kieliezhi Kunnikewonyi matugieseda zuirende jiuizhi ogidene shizijia jiere ghadane. Ghurudu udude aminne olune giewo."
LUK 24:8 Hhe biereila Ersa kieliesanyi sumula irewo.
LUK 24:9 Hhela mezase khareizhi echidene ene shiqinlai 11 gie tujilade pseshiku kunlade man kieliezho.
LUK 24:10 Ene shiqinyi shitulade kieliesan biereilashi Modalani Mereiyen, Yeyana, Yagebuni anani Mereiyenji pse giedun biereila wo.
LUK 24:11 Shitula ene kielienyi xianxin ese giezho. Hu kieliezho giezho.
LUK 24:12 Ingieliuzhe Beduru bosi ire mezade holuzhi echidene ghodei nie uzhese nie bosi wo, pse yama uwo. Khareikude matui imutui gholuwo giezhi sumulazho.
LUK 24:13 Hhe niudude Ersai daghasan ghua tujilani Imawusi giesan aghinde echine giezho, Yelusalense 22 li mo wo.
LUK 24:14 Hhela mo jiere yokude fashen giesan shiqinlai kielienduzho.
LUK 24:15 Zhen kieliendukude Ersa qinsi shidani kuzhezhi hhelare hhantu yozhoma,
LUK 24:16 hhelai nudun madadene kien bikuni tani dazho.
LUK 24:17 Ersa hhelade asazho, "Ta yon yon yan kielienduzhou?" Hhela beidene nango giezhi uxinne boughazho.
LUK 24:18 Nie kunni niereini Geliuba giene. Ersade kieliewo, "Chi Yelusalende toreizhi ene giedudu fashen giesan shiqinlai chi niezheghanne ulie mejienu?"
LUK 24:19 Ersa asawo, "Yan shiqin wo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Nasaleni Ersai shiqin wo. Hheshi nie xienzhi wo. Hudai melie bexinlai melie kielien kieliekude, giekude nenli wine.
LUK 24:20 Mai fugie buwa, noyenla hhei jiuidene fugughaku zui panjisenu shizijia jiere ghadawo.
LUK 24:21 Bijien panjise hheshi Isilieni jiuile iresan enbene giezho. Ene shiqin fashen giezhi ghurudu oluwo.
LUK 24:22 Ingiedene bijienyi dundase giedun bierei bijienyi ghaniraghawo. Hhela eqiemagha eqie meza konde echise
LUK 24:23 Ersai beye wida khizho. Ingie kharei iredene bijiende kieliese qienxienlai chanlawo giezho. Qienxienla kieliese hhe aminne oluwo giene.
LUK 24:24 Ingie bijien giedun kun dagha mezadei uzhele echise biereila kieliesan mutun wo. Ersai chanla dawo."
LUK 24:25 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta ene yama ulie mejiesan kunla, ta xienzhila kieliesan kielienyi gou xianxin ese giezho.
LUK 24:26 Mexiha Hudaghala hhantu undu wizide soutula ingiezhi shouku giedene goyane famashighaku pushonu?"
LUK 24:27 Ingiedene Musa, xienzhilani shu kaishi giezhi jinwun jiere goya fanmiende huaisan kielienni hhelade kieliezhi man minbai olughawo.
LUK 24:28 Hhela echiku hhe aghinde kuzhese Ersa melie yosanyi xianli.
LUK 24:29 Hhela ninkounin Ersai feilieghazhi kieliewo, "Ede nanran pudawo, khara oluwo. Matan enende hhantu souye." Ingiese Ersa hhelare hhantu echi souwo.
LUK 24:30 Ijiekude Ersa ginanyi barei Hudade mafan kieliedene ghulu hhelade ogiwo.
LUK 24:31 Ingiekude hhelai nudun gieghere Ersai tanise Ersa menzhali hhelai meliese wida khiwo.
LUK 24:32 Hhela kieliewo, "Mo jiere hhe matande jinwun jianjikude matanyi zhughe khalundazhola?"
LUK 24:33 Ingie deigo bosizhe Yelusalende echidene 11 gie tuji, psedu kunla hhantulakui chanlawo.
LUK 24:34 Kunla kieliezho, "Ezhan shuhuane aminne oludene Ximunde chujiegheghazho."
LUK 24:35 Hhe ghuala mo jiere Ersai penjisan shiqinyi, pse ginan ghuluzhi ogikude matugie tanisanyi hhelade man kieliewo.
LUK 24:36 Zhen ene kielienyi kieliekude Ersa qinsi hhelai dunda ire beizhi kieliewo, "Ta pinnan onu?"
LUK 24:37 Hhela hende ayizhi sumulase ruhher chanlawo giezho.
LUK 24:38 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yale ingiezhi jindazhi xianxin ulie giene?
LUK 24:39 Ta kon khaimini nie moizhi uzhema, bi enbekui mejiene. Ruhherde yasun migha uwo. Ta uzhe, made wine."
LUK 24:40 Ene kielienyi kieliedene kha, konne hhelade uzheghawo.
LUK 24:41 Hhela bayasuzhoma, xianxin gie dazhi ghudurezho. Ersa kieliewo, "Tai enende yama ijiekui winu uwo?"
LUK 24:42 Ingie hhela shirasan zhaghasunse gouji ogiwo.
LUK 24:43 Hhe jienliedei hhelai melie ijie agiwo.
LUK 24:44 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Eneshi bi melieshida tanre hhantu bikude kieliesan wo. Musani guijinshu, xienzhishu, zeburei jiere mii zhiizhi huaisanlai man ijinyo gholughakuni wo."
LUK 24:45 Ingiedene Ersa hhelai sumuladanyi minbai olughazhi jinwunni dunjireghadene
LUK 24:46 hhelade kieliewo, "Jinwun jiere ingiezhi huaizho, Mexiha irese ijinyo shouku giezhi duya ijiedene ghurudushi aminne olune.
LUK 24:47 Pse hhei niereghala geizhen giese roulieku gouxioxini Yelusalense soyuji minzulade chonji keine.
LUK 24:48 Ta ene shiqinde ganzhen bei.
LUK 24:49 Adami dain giesan hhei bi tai jiere peizhi ireghane. Asiman jierese Hudai nenli tande olon iretula ta ene chenshide saghei."
LUK 24:50 Ersa hhelai uduruzhi Bodanide echidene khane zhadeighazhi hhelade oluzhi onxian giewo.
LUK 24:51 Zhen onxian giekude hhelase likai gie asiman jiere khireiwo.
LUK 24:52 Hhela Ersai beiidene hende bayasuzhi Yelusalende khareiwo.
LUK 24:53 Hhela Hudade doulazhi chan mechide wo.
JOH 1:1 Zui melieshida Kielien wine. Ene Kielien Hudaghala hhantu wo. Ene Kielienshi Huda wo.
JOH 1:2 Hhe zui melieshida Hudaghala hhantu wo.
JOH 1:3 Duya jiereshikulai man hhe zhayaghawo. Hhe uye zhayaghasei nieda uwo.
JOH 1:4 Hhei sudoro amin wine. Ene aminshi kunlai gon wo.
JOH 1:5 Gon kharanide zhouise kharani gonni gieru dane.
JOH 1:6 Yaheiya giezhi nie kunyi Hudai hhense peizhi ireghawo.
JOH 1:7 Hhei peizhi ireghase hhe gonde ganzhen beizhi kunlai man xianxin gieghane giezho.
JOH 1:8 Ene kunshi gon pusho, gonde ganzhen beile irezho.
JOH 1:9 Kunlai giegheraghaku zhenzhenji hhe gon duyade irezho.
JOH 1:10 Hhe duyade wo, hhei tungo giezhi duyai zhayaghawoma, duya hhei tani dane.
JOH 1:11 Hhe goya orondene irese goyai kunla hhei ese jienliewoma,
JOH 1:12 jien hhei jienliezhi niereini xianxin giesan kunlade Hudai kewosi danlaku qienli ogiwo.
JOH 1:13 Ene kesilashi kun jierese iresan pusho. Kunni duranghala jihua giedene olusanye pusho, Hudase iresan wo.
JOH 1:14 Ene Kielien kun gholudene mai dunda souzho. Matan hhei famani uzhese zhen Adani niekozi Kewonni famani wo. Hhei sudoro nenjien, zhendao olon wo.
JOH 1:15 Yaheiya hhende ganzhen beizhi fugiede kieliewo, "Eneshi hhe mase khuina irenema, mase hen wo. Hhe zui melieshidasejiu wine giezhi bi kieliezhi daosan hhe wo."
JOH 1:16 Matan man hhei fugie nenjien jierese nenjien olon jienliezho.
JOH 1:17 Guijinshi Musase irezho. Nenjien, zhennishi Ersa Mexihase irezho.
JOH 1:18 Kiemada Hudai chujieghezhi ese daozhoma, Hudai zhughe jieredu niekozi kewon Hudai mejieghawo. Hhe benshenshi Huda wo.
JOH 1:19 Yelusalense Yutai kunla buwa, Liwi kunlai peizhi Yaheiyashi kien bikuni asaghale echise Yaheiya ingiezhi ganzhen beizho.
JOH 1:20 Hhe ghudan ese kieliezhi zhijie kieliewo, "Bishi Mexiha pusho."
JOH 1:21 Hhela pse asawo, "Qinse chishi kien wo? Iliya onu?" "Pusho." "Qinse chishi hhe nie xienzhi onu?" "Pusho."
JOH 1:22 Ingiese hhela kieliewo, "Chi daojishi kien wo? Bijien khareizhi echise peizhi ireghasan kunlade jiodai giene. Chi goyane nie kielie. Chishi kien wo?"
JOH 1:23 Hhe kieliewo, "Bishi Isaiya xienzhi kieliesan mutun Ezhanni moni zhidagha giezhi hontande waradasan hhe shenqi wo."
JOH 1:24 Hhelashi Falisai kun peizhi ireghasan wo.
JOH 1:25 Ingiese asazho, "Chi Mexiha pusho, Iliya pusho, hhe nie xienzhiye pusho. Chi yangiezhi kunlade xili gieghazho?"
JOH 1:26 Yaheiya kieliewo, "Bi usughala xili gieghazhoma, ta tani dasan daniezhan tai dunda beizho.
JOH 1:27 Hhe mase khuina irenema, bi hhende mahei deizi andaghaseye pei dane."
JOH 1:28 Ene shiqinlashi Yedanheni hhemandedu Bodanide fashen giesan wo, zhen Yaheiya xili gieghasan oron wo.
JOH 1:29 Khuichuduni Ersa hhelai hhende iresei Yaheiya chanladene kieliewo, "Uzhe, duyai kunlai zuini widaghaku Hudai ghoni ghughan wo!
JOH 1:30 Eneshi hhe mase khuina irenema, mase hen wo. Hhe zui melieshidasejiu wine giezhi bi kieliezhi daosan hhe wo.
JOH 1:31 Bi melieshidase hheni tani dane. Bi ede usughala xili gieghase hhei Isilie kunlade mejieghane giezho."
JOH 1:32 Yaheiya pse ganzhen beizhi kieliewo, "Bi melieshi chanlase Shenlin ghoghochen mutun asiman jierese bouzhezhi hhei jiere luiwo.
JOH 1:33 Bi melieshise hhei tani dane. Mii peizhi usughala xili gieghasan Huda made kieliewo, 'Shenlin kienyi jiere bouzhesei chi chanlase hhe Shenlinghala xili gieghane.'
JOH 1:34 Enei bi chanlawo. Eneshi Hudai kewon enbene giezhi bi ganzhen beine."
JOH 1:35 Khuichuduni Yaheiya ghua tujilaghalane hhantu hhende beizho.
JOH 1:36 YaheiyaErsai yosei chanladene kieliewo, "Uzhe, Hudai ghoni ghughan wo."
JOH 1:37 Ghua tujilani ene kielienyi sonosudene Ersai daghawo.
JOH 1:38 Ersa ochirasenu hhela daghasei chanladene asawo, "Ta yan kerene?" Hhela kieliewo, "Labi, chi khala souzho?" Labishi loushii isi wo.
JOH 1:39 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta uzhele irendu." Hhela daghazhi echidene sousan oronyini uzhewo. Hhe xienzide chabudu xiawu 4 jien oluzho. Hhe udu hhela Ersare hhantu souwo.
JOH 1:40 Yaheiyai kielienyi chenliedene Ersai daghasan ghua kun dundadu nieshi Ximun-Bedurui jiuni Andelie wo.
JOH 1:41 Hhe xien Ximun gaine ereizhi oludene kieliewo, "Bijien Mexihai penjiwo!" Mexihai fanyi giese Jidu wo.
JOH 1:42 Ingiedene hhe Ximunni uduruzhi Ersai shida echiwo. Ersa hhei uzhedene kieliewo, "Chishi Yaheiyai kewon Ximun wo. Ede chii Jifa giezhi urune." Jifai fanyi giese Beduru wo.
JOH 1:43 Khuichuduni Ersa jiejin giezhi Jialilide echine giezho. Ingiekude Feilii penjidene hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii dagha."
JOH 1:44 Feilishi Bosaida kun wo. Andelie, Beduru enelashi nie oronnughun wo.
JOH 1:45 FeiliNadanyei ereizhi oludene kieliewo, "Musai guijin jiere huaisan, xienzhila jilasan hhe kunyi bijien chanlawo. Hheshi Nasale kun, Yusufui kewon Ersa wo."
JOH 1:46 Ingie Nadanye kieliewo, "Nasalese pse yama khizheneba." Feili kieliewo, "Chi iredene uzhe."
JOH 1:47 ErsaNadanye shidani iresei chanladene kieliewo, "Uzhe, eneshi nie zhenzhenji Isilie kun wo. Hhei zhughede yama huaini uwo."
JOH 1:48 Nadanye asawo, "Chi mii matugie taniwo?" Ersa kieliewo, "Feili chii da ese urukude chi uhuago mutun doura bikui bi chanlawo."
JOH 1:49 Nadanye kieliewo, "Loushi, chishi Hudai Kewon, Isilie kunni honshan wo."
JOH 1:50 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chii uhuago mutun doura bikui chanlawo giezhi kieliese chi mii xianxin giewu? Chi enense da fugie shiqin uzhene."
JOH 1:51 Pse hhelade kieliewo, "Bi shuhuajia tande kielieye, asiman keizhi Hudai qienxienla Kunnikewonyi jiere bouzhi khikui ta chanlane."
JOH 2:1 Ghurudude Jialilini Jianade kunla ghurun ijiezho. Ersai anani ye hhende wo.
JOH 2:2 Ersa, tujilaini man hhantu xinlazhi echizho.
JOH 2:3 Jiuni ochizhi baraghawo. Ersai anani Ersade kieliewo, "Hhelade jiu widazho."
JOH 2:4 Ersa kieliewo, "Ana, hhe made yan xiangan wo? Mii shihou da ese kuruzho."
JOH 2:5 Hhei anani hojilade kieliewo, "Hhe tai yan gieghase ta yan giendu."
JOH 2:6 Hhende usu zhonloku zhighon gan wine. Nie gande ghua ghuran tunzi usu zhonlone. Zhonmun libai giekude injiku usui hhende teizho.
JOH 2:7 Ersa hojilade kieliewo, "Gande usui durugha." Ingiese hojila usui zhonlozhi gan kouzide khizheghawo.
JOH 2:8 Ersa pse hojilade kieliewo, "Ede yuzhi xi gonjisan kunde khughozhi echigha." Ingiese hhela echighawo.
JOH 2:9 Xi gonjisan kun usu jiu bienjisei nie ochise ene jiu khalase iresei ulie mejiene. Zi usu yusan hojila mejiene. Xi gonjisan kun shini khughonyi uru ire kieliewo,
JOH 2:10 "Kunla gou jiuni melieshi ireghane. Zhochenla ochizhi sudosenu bixin jiuni ireghane. Chi matui gou jiuni feilieghazhi eli kuzho."
JOH 2:11 Eneshi Ersa xienjighasan tou 1 gie ghudureqi wo. Jialilini Jianade xienjighawo. Ene ghudureqighala kunlade famane mejieghawo. Ingiese tujilani hhei xianxin giewo.
JOH 2:12 Enense khuinashi Ersa, anani, jiulani, tujila man Jiabainunde bouzhi echidene giedudu souwo.
JOH 2:13 Yutai kunni Jiulidaosan Jie ghujinlase ErsaYelusalende echiwo.
JOH 2:14 Echise kunla mechide orodene meimei giesei chujieghewo. Kunla fughe, ghoni, ghoghochen huizho. Dazeghan kunla souzhi baer arunzhazho.
JOH 2:15 Ingiese Ersa jiesunyi mushigheidene fughe ghonilai mechise tou khighawo. Baer arunzhasan kunlai baerlani kie khizhegha, shirelani tungu unaghawo.
JOH 2:16 Pse ghoghochen huisan kunlade kieliewo, "Dunxilane man banji khirei! Adaimi giei meimei gieku oron bu gholugha!"
JOH 2:17 Ingiekude tujilani jinwun jiere huaisan kielienyi sumula irewo, "Bi Adane giede oluzhi zhughedemi khan siderazho."
JOH 2:18 Ingiese Yutai kunla Ersade kieliewo, "Chade ingiezhi gieku qienli winu? Chi bijiende yan ghudureqi xienjighane?"
JOH 2:19 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta ene mechini chei. Bi ghurudude gie khizheghane."
JOH 2:20 Hhela kieliewo, "Ene mechishi 46 niende giezhi khireighasan wo. Chi ghurudude giezhi khizheghanu?"
JOH 2:21 Ersa kieliesan mechishi goya beyene kieliezho.
JOH 2:22 Ersa aminne oludene tujilani Ersai ene nie aman kielienyi sumula irewo. Ingiese hhela jinwunyi xianxin giewo. Ersa kieliesan kielienlai ye xianxin giewo.
JOH 2:23 ErsaYelusalende Jiulidaosan Jie daoghakude ghudureqi xienjighase olon kunla uzhedene Ersai xianxin giewo.
JOH 2:24 Ingieliuzhe Ersa hhelai xianxin ese giezho. Ersa kunlai man mejiene.
JOH 2:25 Hhe kunni zhughede yan bikuni mejiene. Ingiese hhende kunshi matunie bikui kielieku biyo uwo.
JOH 3:1 Falisaini nie kunyi niereni Nigedemu giene. Yutai kunlani nie lindao wo.
JOH 3:2 Ene kun xienidei Ersai ochirale ire hhende kieliewo, "Labi, chi Hudai hhense iresan loushi bikui bijien mejiene. Huda chighala hhantu wise chi giesan ghudureqini kiemada gie dane."
JOH 3:3 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Bi chade shuhuajia kielieye, kunyi erchan ulie oluse Hudai gojiai chanla dane."
JOH 3:4 Nigedemu kieliewo, "Kun fugiedadene pse matugie olune? Anane kielide orosenu pse olunu?"
JOH 3:5 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chade shuhuajia kielieye, kunyi usu, Shenlinse ulie oluse Hudai gojiade oro dane.
JOH 3:6 Beyese olusanshi beye wo, ruhherse olusanshi ruhher wo.
JOH 3:7 Bi kieliese ta erchan olukuni wo giese ta bu ghudure.
JOH 3:8 Kei suibien feiliekui ta sonosu shidanema, khalase iresanyi, khala echikui ulie mejiene. Ruhherse olusan kun keighala niekielien wo."
JOH 3:9 Nigedemu asazho. "Matugie imutu shiqin wine?"
JOH 3:10 Ersa kieliewo, "Chishi Isilieni fugie loushi wo. Ene shiqinyi ulie mejienu?
JOH 3:11 Bi shuhuajia kielieye, bijien mejiesanne tande kieliezho, chujieghesanne ganzhen beizhoma, ta bijienyi kielienyi xianxin ulie giene.
JOH 3:12 Bi zemin jieredu shiqinyi kieliese ta xianxin ulie giene, asiman jieredu shiqinyi kieliese matugie xianxin giene?
JOH 3:13 Asiman jierese bouzhesan Kunnikewonse chugo kiemada asiman jiere khizhi ese daozho.
JOH 3:14 Musa hontande mogheini qila qiighaku mutun Kunnikewonniye qingiezhi qila qiighane.
JOH 3:15 Ingiese jien hhei xianxin giesan kunlade chanqiku amin ogine giezho.
JOH 3:16 Huda duyani kunlade olon orezhi lien niekozi kewonneliuzhe ogiwo. Ingiese jien hhei xianxin giesan kunlai ulie widaghazhi chanqiku amin ogine giezho.
JOH 3:17 Hhe kewonne peizhi duyade ireghase zui jinjile ese irezho, kunlai jiuighale irezho.
JOH 3:18 Hhei xianxin giesan kunlade zui ulie jinjine. Xianxin ulie giesan kunlade zui ijin jinjiwo. Hhela Hudai niekozi kewonni xianxin ese giezho.
JOH 3:19 Hhela giesan doghunnishi gon duyade irese gonde xiqi uwo, kharanide xiqi wo. Hhelai zuini jiu ingiezhi soughawo.
JOH 3:20 Doghunni giesanla gonni henjine, gon shida ulie irene. Giesanlaini khizheghakuse ayizho.
JOH 3:21 Zhendaode giesan kunla gon shida irene. Hudai isighala giesan shiqinlai man mejieghane giezho."
JOH 3:22 Enense khuinashi Ersa tujilarene Yudayani oronde echidene nietan souzhi kunlai xili gieghazho.
JOH 3:23 Salenni kouisan Ainende usu olonshi Yaheiyaye hhende xili gieghazho. Kunla hhende xili gieghakui jienliele irezho.
JOH 3:24 Hhe shihoude Yaheiyani da bafanzide bareizhi ese echizho.
JOH 3:25 Yaheiyai tujila nie Yutai kunghala waghaku banfa jiere jianjindu qiiwo.
JOH 3:26 Hhela Yaheiya shida iredene kieliewo, "Loushi, melieshida Yedanhe hhemiende chighala hhantulasan hhe kun ede kunlade xili gieghazho. Chi hhende ganzhen beizho. Kunla man hhei shida echizho."
JOH 3:27 Yaheiya kieliewo, "Huda ulie ogise kun yama jienlie dane.
JOH 3:28 Bishi Mexiha pusho. Mii hhense melie peizhi ireghawo giezhi bi kieliezhi daosei ta mejiene.
JOH 3:29 Shini bierei agikushi shini khughon wo. Peikieni hhei kanzide beizhi shenqiini nie sonosuse hende bayasune. Biye qingiezhi hende bayasuzho.
JOH 3:30 Hhe hendakuni wo, bi bixindakuni wo."
JOH 3:31 "Jierese iresan hhe yanseliuzhe fugie wo. Zemin jierese iresanshi zemin jieredu wo. Kieliesan kielienla yeshi zemin jieredu wo. Asiman jierese iresan hheshi yanseliuzhe fugie wo.
JOH 3:32 Hhe chujieghesanne, chenliesanne ganzhen beizhoma, hhei ganzhenyi kiema ulie jienliene.
JOH 3:33 Hhei ganzhenyi xianxin giesan kunla Hudashi zhenni enbene giezho.
JOH 3:34 Huda peizhi ireghasan hhe Hudai kielienyi kieliene. Huda hhende Shenlinni shuzi witui ogizho.
JOH 3:35 Adani kewondene orezhi man hhei khade jiuiwo.
JOH 3:36 Kewonyini xianxin giesan kunde chanqiku amin wine. Hhei ulie shunjichen kunde amin uwo. Hudai hokuku chan hhei jiere wo."
JOH 4:1 Falisai kun chenliese ErsaYaheiyase tuji olon ghurazhi xili gieghazho. Shiji jiere Ersa goyane xili ese gieghazho, tujilani gieghazho. Ersa ene shiqinlai mejiedene Yudayase likai gie Jialilide khareine giezho.
JOH 4:4 Echikudeni Samaliya moni daone.
JOH 4:5 Samaliyai nie chenshide kuruwo. Niereini Xijia giene. Ene chenshishi YagebuYusufu kewondene ogisan oron konde wo.
JOH 4:6 Yagebuni jin hhende wo. Ersa yozhi hhechese jin konde souwo. Chabudu zhunwu xienzi wo.
JOH 4:7 Samaliyai nie bierei usu daile irese Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Made ususene gouji ogi."
JOH 4:8 Ene shihoude tujilani chenshise ijiuni agile echizho.
JOH 4:9 Samaliyai bierei kieliewo, "Chishi Yutai kun wo. Matugie Samaliyai nie biereise usu kerene?" Yenlai Yutai kun Samaliya kunghala laiwon ese giezho.
JOH 4:10 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi Hudai nenjienni mejiese, pse chase usu keresanshi kien bikui mejiese chi hhei xiahua giene, hhe amitu usui chade ogine."
JOH 4:11 Bierei kieliewo, "Gujiu, chade usu daiku tunzida uwo. Jin imutu gun wo. Chi khalase amitu usu daine?
JOH 4:12 Bijienyi xienren Yagebu ene jinni bijiende jiewo. Hhe goyane, kesilani, asunla man enense ijiezho. Chi hhense da fugie onu?"
JOH 4:13 Ersa kieliewo, "Ene usui usan kunla pse undasune.
JOH 4:14 Bi ogisan usui use chanqi ulie undasune. Bi ogisan usu hhei sudoro bula gholuzhi izhi usuruzhi khizhezhi hhende chanqiku amin ogine."
JOH 4:15 Bierei kieliewo, "Gujiu, made ene usui nie ogi. Ingiese bi ulie undasune. Bi pse enense usu daile ulie irene."
JOH 4:16 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi echidene zhanguijine uruzhi ire."
JOH 4:17 Bierei kieliewo, "Made zhanguiji uwo." Ersa kieliewo, "Chade zhanguiji uwo giezhi kieliesan oluzho.
JOH 4:18 Melieshida chade tawun zhanguiji wine. Edekushi chii zhanguiji pusho. Chi kieliesan oluzho."
JOH 4:19 Bierei kieliewo, "Gujiu, bi uzhese chishi nie xienzhi wo.
JOH 4:20 Bijien Samaliya kunyi xienrenla ene ulade beii giezhoma, ta Yutai kunla kieliese Yelusalenshi beiiku oron wo giezho."
JOH 4:21 Ersa kieliewo, "Funi, mii xianxin gie. Shihou kuzhese Adai beiiku ene ulade uwo, Yelusalende ye uwo.
JOH 4:22 Ta Samaliya kun kienyi beiisanne ulie mejiene. Bijien Yutai kun kienyi beiisanne mejiene. Jiuikushi Yutai kunni tungo giezhi irene.
JOH 4:23 Shihou kuzhese Adai shixinji beiisan kun zhughesene shixinji beiine. Shihou ede enbene. Ada ingiezhi goude beiisan kunyi ereine.
JOH 4:24 Hudashi ruhher wo. Hhei beiisan kun indan zhughesene shixinji beiikuni wo."
JOH 4:25 Bierei kieliewo, "Hhe Jidu giezhi urusan Mexihai irekui bi mejiene. Hhe irese bijiende man mejieghane."
JOH 4:26 Ersa kieliewo, "Chimare kielien kieliesanshi enbene."
JOH 4:27 Ingiekude tujilani kharei ire Ersa nie biereire kielien kieliesei uzhedene ghanirazho. Chi yan kerene? Chi yangiezhi biereighala kielien kieliezho giezhi kiema asa dawo.
JOH 4:28 Hhe bierei usu tunzine jie, chenshide echisenu olon kunlade kieliewo,
JOH 4:29 "Ta uzhele irendu, nie kun bi giesan shiqinlai man kielie khizheghawo! Ene kunshi Mexiha enbeneba?"
JOH 4:30 Ingiese kunla aghinse khizhe Ersai hhende echiwo.
JOH 4:31 Ingiekude tujilani kieliewo, "Loushi, ijie."
JOH 4:32 Ersa kieliewo, "Made ta mejie daku ijiuni wine."
JOH 4:33 Ingiese tujilani nieniedene asazho, "Kunla ogizhi ijieghazhoba?"
JOH 4:34 Ersa kieliewo, "Mii ijiunishi mii peizhi ireghasan hhei isini gieku wo. Hhei wilielai chengun olughane.
JOH 4:35 Ta kieliese pse jieran sarashi boudei ghuraku shihou olune giezho. Bi tande kielieye, ta qiorunne qila hhe ghazhade nie uzhe, ede ghuraku oluwo.
JOH 4:36 Ghurasan kun gunzi bareizhi chanqiku aminde ugu cunjizho. Ingiese tareisan kun ghurasan kunghala hhantu bayasune.
JOH 4:37 Kienni kieliedanma, 'Nie kun tareine, da nie kun ghurane.' Ene kielien oluzho.
JOH 4:38 Bi tai peizhi ghuraghale echise ta ese khishulasan ghazhade echighawo. Ta kunla khishulasei xianshou giezho."
JOH 4:39 Hhe bierei ganzhen beizhi, "Bi giesan shiqinlai hhe kun man kielie khizheghawo!" giezhi kieliese hhe chenshidedu olon Samaliya kunla Ersai xianxin giewo.
JOH 4:40 Samaliya kunla Ersai ochirale irewo. Hhei xiahua giezhi hhelai hhende sou giese, Ersa ghuarudu souwo.
JOH 4:41 Ersai kielienyi chenliedene xianxin giesan kun pse olodowo.
JOH 4:42 Hhela biereide kieliewo, "Bijien ede xianxin giese chi kieliesan pusho. Bijien goyane hhei kielienyini chenliedene hheshi zhenzhenji duyani jiuichen enbekui mejiewo."
JOH 4:43 Ghuarudu daosenu Ersa hhe oronse likai gie Jialilide echiwo.
JOH 4:44 Ersa goyane kieliezhi daozho, "Xienzhini goya aghindene ulie zunjine."
JOH 4:45 ErsaJialilide kuse hhe oronyi kunla jienliezho. Hhela Yelusalende jieqi daoghale echisande Ersa giesan shiqinlai man uzhewo.
JOH 4:46 Ersa pse Jialilini Jianade khareizhi irewo. Yen melieshida usui jiu gholughasan hhe oronde wo. Hhende nie fugie noyen wine, kewonni Jiabainunde giemerezho.
JOH 4:47 ErsaYudayase Jialilide iresanyi hhe sonosudene ochirale ire, "Mii kewon duya ijiene giezho. Goudaghale yo!" giezhi xiahua giewo.
JOH 4:48 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta ghudureqi, fugie shiqinlai ulie chanlatula xianxin ulie giene."
JOH 4:49 Noyen kieliewo, "Gujiu, kewonmi ese duya ijietula nie bouzhi yo."
JOH 4:50 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi kharei, kewonchii goudawo." Hhe kun Ersai kielienyi xianxin giedene khareiwo.
JOH 4:51 Giedene boukudeni mo jiere hojilani hhei jienliele ire, "Kewonchii goudawo." giezhi kieliewo.
JOH 4:52 Ingiese hhe asawo, "Kewon yan shihoude goudawo?" Hojila kieliewo, "Uchughudu xiawu 1 jiende tuishao giezhi qiiwo."
JOH 4:53 Ingiese adani Ersa kewonchii goudawo giesan hhe shihoui mejiewo. Ingiese hhe nie giechilie man Ersai xianxin giewo.
JOH 4:54 Eneshi ErsaYudayase Jialilide khareidene giesan ji 2 gie ghudureqi wo.
JOH 5:1 Enense khuinashi Yutai kunyi nie jieqi kuzhewo. ErsaYelusalende khizhi echiwo.
JOH 5:2 Yelusalenyi Ghoni wijien shida nie bula wine. Xibolai kielienghala kieliese Bishida giene. Bula zhouwide tawun zoulan wine.
JOH 5:3 Zoulande giemeresan kun olon kijiezho. Sugho, dogholon, beye fugusan kun olon wo.
JOH 5:5 Hhende nie kun giemerezhi 38 nien olune.
JOH 5:6 Ersa hhe kijiesei chujieghewo. Oloncha giemeresei mejiesenu asawo, "Chi gienne goudaghaku duran winu?"
JOH 5:7 Giemeresan kun kieliewo, "Gujiu, usu gojiolukudei mii usude boughachen kun uwo. Bi goya boukudei kunla mase melieshida qianla boune."
JOH 5:8 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bosizhedene ruzine agidei echi."
JOH 5:9 Hhe kun deigo gouda ruzine agisenu yozhi echiwo. Hhe nie udushi hhamuraku udu wo.
JOH 5:10 Ingiese Yutai kunla hhe goudasan kunde kieliewo, "Enedushi hhamuraku udu wo. Chi ruzii bareizhi yose ese oluzho."
JOH 5:11 Hhe kun kieliewo, "Mii goudaghasan kun ruzine bareizhi yo giezhi made kieliewo."
JOH 5:12 Hhela asazho, "Chade ruzine agidene yo giesanshi kien wine?"
JOH 5:13 Goudasan kun kien hhei goudaghasei ulie mejiene. Hhende kun olonshi Ersa niui widazho.
JOH 5:14 Khuinashi Ersa mechide hhe kunyi chujieghedene kieliewo, "Chi ede goudawoma, pse zui bu fanji. Pse enense yenzhunshine."
JOH 5:15 Hhe kun echidene Yutai kunlade kieliewo, "Mii goudaghasanshi Ersa wo."
JOH 5:16 Ingiese Yutai kunla Ersa chan hhamuraku udude enezighan shiqinlai giese hhei heizhi qiiwo.
JOH 5:17 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Adami izhi eli kutula wilie giezho, biye giezho."
JOH 5:18 Ingiese Yutai kunla hhei alane giezhi hendawo. Hhe hhamuraku udui guijinyi ese zunjizho, da Hudashi goyai Ada wo giezho. Pse goyane Hudaghala pin wo giezho.
JOH 5:19 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye. Kewon goyane kouizhi yama gie dane. Zinie Ada giesanyi uzhedene giezho. Ada giesan wilielai Kewon ye giene.
JOH 5:20 Ada Kewondene orezhi goya giesanlane hhende man uzheghazho. Da enense fugie shiqinlai hhende uzheghane. Ingiese tai ghaniraghane.
JOH 5:21 Ada fugusan kunlai bosi ireghazhi amin ogiku mutun Kewonniye goya duranghalane kunlade amin ogine.
JOH 5:22 Ada yan kunyiliuzhe ulie panjinema, panjiku qienlini Kewondene jiuizhi ogiwo.
JOH 5:23 Ingiese kunla Adai zunjiku mutun Kewonne zunjighane giezho. Kewonni ulie zunjise hhei peizhi ireghasan Adainiye uye zunjizho.
JOH 5:24 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, kien mii kielienyi chenliezhi mii peizhi ireghasan hhei xianxin giese chanqiku amin wine. Zui ulie soughane, fugukuse amitude ijin ireghawo."
JOH 5:25 "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, shihou kuzhese fugusan kunla Kunnikewonni shenqii sonosune. Sonosusan kunla aminne olune. Ede hhe shihou enbene.
JOH 5:26 Ada benshenshi aminni genzi wo. Kewonneye aminni genzi gholughawo.
JOH 5:27 Hheshi Kunnikewon wo. Ingiese Ada hhende kunlai panjiku qienlii ogiwo.
JOH 5:28 Ta ene shiqinde bu ghanira, shihou kuzhese mezai kunla man Kewonni shenqii sonosuse,
JOH 5:29 fuho giedene khizhene. Gouni giesanla chanqi amiturane, huaishi giesanlade zui jinjine."
JOH 5:30 "Bi goyane kouizhi yama gie dane. Bi matui sonosuse matui panjine. Bi panjisanshi gundanni wo. Bi panjise goya isighalane ese giezho. Mii peizhi ireghasan hhei isighala giezho."
JOH 5:31 "Bi goyadene ganzhen beise zoin ulie qiine.
JOH 5:32 Da niekozi made ganzhen beizho. Hhe beisanshi zhenni bikui bi mejiene.
JOH 5:33 Ta melieshidase Yaheiyai hhende kun peizhi echighase Yaheiya zhendaode ganzhen beizho.
JOH 5:34 Bi kunse ganzhen ulie kerenema, bi ene kielienyi kieliekushi tai jiuine giezho.
JOH 5:35 Yaheiyashi siderazhi gon faisan zhula niekielien wo. Ta zhanshi jiere hhei gonde xiqi woma,
JOH 5:36 made Yaheiyase da fugie ganzhen wine. Hheshi Adami mii onchengie giesan wilie wo. Ede bi giesan wilie enbene. Ene wiliela Adami mii peizhi ireghasande ganzhen beizho.
JOH 5:37 Pse mii peizhi ireghasan Adami made ganzhen beizho. Ta hhei shenqiini chenliezhi uye daozho. Yanziini ye uzhezhi uye daozho.
JOH 5:38 Ada peizhi ireghasei ta xianxin ese giezho, ingiese hhei kielienyi ta zhughedene ese teizho."
JOH 5:39 "Ta sumulase jinwunyi uzhezhi suruse hhe jierese chanqiku aminyi ereine giezhoma, jinwun zhen made ganzhen beizho.
JOH 5:40 Ingieliuzhe ta aminni mii enense ereile ulie irene."
JOH 5:41 "Kun mii kuaikui bi ulie jienliene.
JOH 5:42 Bi tai mejiene. Tande Hudade oreku zhughe uwo.
JOH 5:43 Bi Adane niereghala irese ta ulie jienliene. Kunla goya niereghalane irese ta jienliene.
JOH 5:44 Ta nieniene kuaikui jienlienduzhoma, niekozi Hudase iresan kuaikui ulie ereine. Ingiese ta mii matui xianxin giene?
JOH 5:45 Bi Adai melie tai zhane giezhi bu sumula. Tai zhakui da nie wine. Ta kouizhi xianxin giesan Musa tai zhane.
JOH 5:46 Ta Musai xianxin giese miiye xianxin giekui wo. Hhe huaisanshi mii zhiizhi kieliezho.
JOH 5:47 Hhe huaisanyi ta xianxin ulie giese mii kielienyi matugie xianxin giene?"
JOH 6:1 Enense khuinashi ErsaJialilihaini daowo. Hhei Qibiliyahai giezhi ye uruzho.
JOH 6:2 Tebieji olon kunla hhe gientulai goudaghasan ghudureqii uzhedene hhei daghazho.
JOH 6:3 Ersa ulade khirei tujilarene hhantu souwo.
JOH 6:4 Hhe shihoude Yutai kunni Jiulidaosan Jie chadashizho.
JOH 6:5 Ersa qiorunne qila uzhese tebieji olon kunla hhei melie iresei chanladene Feilide kieliewo, "Matan khalase imegheni ginan agizhi irezhi ene kunlade ijieghane?"
JOH 6:6 Hhe ingiezhi kieliese Feilii shiizho. Goyane matui giekui eqie mejiene.
JOH 6:7 Feili kieliewo, "200 gie miengughala ginan agise nie kunde goujinie ijiezhiye ulie kurune."
JOH 6:8 Nie tujishi Ximun-Bedurui jiuni Andelie wo. Ersade kieliewo,
JOH 6:9 "Enende nie ga kewon dunmaighala giesan tawun ginanji ghua zhaghasun bareizho. Imegheni kunlade yan gholune?"
JOH 6:10 Ersa "Dajialai sougha." giezhi kieliewo. Hhe oronde osun henshi kunla souwo. Gon ere kun sanase chabudu 5000 wine.
JOH 6:11 Ersa ginanyi barei Hudade mafan kieliedene sousan kunlade ghughazhi ogiwo. Zhaghasunyiye ingiezhi giedene kunlade ogiwo. Dajiala giedughonni ijiese giedughonni ogiwo.
JOH 6:12 Hhela ijie chuduse Ersa tujiladene kieliewo, "Feiliesei zaota bu giedene man shidolozhi agi."
JOH 6:13 Ingiese kunla ijiedene feiliesan tawun ginanni zhazhai shidolose 12 gie lanzi zhonlowo.
JOH 6:14 Ersa giesan ghudureqini uzhedene kunla kieliezho, "Eneshi zhen duyade ireku hhe nie xienzhi enbene."
JOH 6:15 Kunla iredene Ersai bareizhi biizhi honshan danlaghakui mejiedene Ersa niezheghanne pse ulade khireiwo.
JOH 6:16 Khara oluse tujilani haibienzide bouwo.
JOH 6:17 Chon jiere khireidene hai hhemienni Jiabainunde yozhi qiiwo. Khara oluzhoma, Ersa hhelai hhende dou ese irezho.
JOH 6:18 Nie fugie kei feiliese hai jiere lan yebeiseye fugiedawo.
JOH 6:19 Tujila chonni huaizhi 10 jili yozho. Ingiekude hhela Ersa hai jiere yozhi chon shida iresei chujieghedene ayizho.
JOH 6:20 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bi wo, bu ayi."
JOH 6:21 Ingiese hhela hende bayasudene Ersai jienliezhi chon jiere khise echiku orondene deigo kuruwo.
JOH 6:22 Khuichudu hai duimiende beisan kunla hhende zi niekozi chon bikui mejiene, pse chon uwo. Ersa tujilarene chon jiere hhantu uye khiseiye mejiene. Tujilani goyane echizho.
JOH 6:23 Pse giedun chon Qibiliyase Ezhan mafan kieliedene kunlade ginan ijieghasan hhe oron shida irewo.
JOH 6:24 Kunla Ersa, tujilai chanla dase chon souzhi Jiabainunde Ersai ereile echiwo.
JOH 6:25 Hhela hai duimiense Ersai ereizhi oludene kieliewo, "Loushi, chi yan xienzide enende irewo?"
JOH 6:26 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, ta mii ereile irese bi xienjighasan ghudureqide ese oluzho, ginanni ijiezhi chudusande oluzho.
JOH 6:27 Ta widaku ijiunide oluzhi wilie bu gie. Chanqiku amin wineku ijiunide oluzhi gie. Enei Kunnikewon tande ogine. Kunnikewonshi Huda Ada renjisan wo."
JOH 6:28 Ingiese hhela asawo, "Bijien yan wilie giese Hudai wilie sanane?"
JOH 6:29 Ersa kieliewo, "Huda peizhi ireghasan hhei xianxin giese, hheshi Hudai wilie wo."
JOH 6:30 Hhela pse kieliewo, "Chi yan ghudureqi xienjighazhi bijienyi xianxin gieghane? Chi yan giene?
JOH 6:31 Jinwun jiere, 'Asiman jierese hhe hhelade ginanyi ogizho.' giezhi huaisan mutun mai xienrenla hontande mana ijiewoma."
JOH 6:32 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, asiman jierese tande ginanyi ogisanshi Musa pusho. Asiman jierese tande zhenzhenji ginan ogisanshi Adami wo.
JOH 6:33 Hudai ginanshi asiman jierese bouzhesan hhe nie wo. Hhe duyani kunlade amin ogine."
JOH 6:34 Ingiese hhela kieliewo, "Gujiu, chi imutu ginanyi bijiende chanqi ogi."
JOH 6:35 Ersa kieliewo, "Bishi aminni ginan enbene. Mii enende iresan kunla ulie oliesune. Mii xianxin giese ibeizi ulie undasune.
JOH 6:36 Ingieliuzhe, bi kieliezhi daozhoma, ta mii chujiegheseye, xianxin ulie giene.
JOH 6:37 Adami made ogisan kunla mii enende irene. Mii enende iresanlai bi jiedui ulie danlane.
JOH 6:38 Bi asiman jierese bouzhese goya isighalane ulie giene. Mii peizhi ireghasan hhei isighala giene.
JOH 6:39 Mii peizhi ireghasan hhei isishi made ogisan kunlai bi nieda ulie widaghazhi duya barakudeni aminne olughane giezho.
JOH 6:40 Adaimi isishi Kewonyini uzhedene xianxin giesan kunlade man chanqiku aminyi ogine. Duya barakudeni bi hhelai aminne olughane."
JOH 6:41 Yutai kunla Ersa orunshi asiman jierese bouzhesan ginan wo giese hhei kieliendu qiiwo.
JOH 6:42 Hhela kieliewo, "Eneshi Yusufui kewon Ersa pushonu? Ana adaini matan tanine. Hhe matugie imutui kielien kieliene? Orunshi asiman jierese bouzhesan wo giezho?"
JOH 6:43 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta qingiezhi bu kieliendu.
JOH 6:44 Mii peizhi ireghasan Adami ulie ireghase mii enende kiemada ire dane. Mii enende iresanlai duya barakudeni bi hhei aminne olughane.
JOH 6:45 Xienzhii shu jiere, 'Hhela man Hudase suruzho.' giezhi huaizho. Adase chenliezhi surusan kunla man mii enende irene.
JOH 6:46 Ene kielienshi kiema Adai chanlazhi daosan hhe isi pusho. Hudai hhense iresan hhense chugo kiemada Adai uzhezhi ese daozho.
JOH 6:47 Bi shuhuajia kielieye, xianxin giesan kunde chanqiku amin wine.
JOH 6:48 Bishi aminni ginan wo.
JOH 6:49 Tai xienren hontande manai ijieliuzhe fuguwo.
JOH 6:50 Eneshi asiman jierese bouzhesan ginan wo. Kun ijiese ulie fugune.
JOH 6:51 Bishi asiman jierese bouzhesan amin ogiku ginan wo. Kun ijiese chanqi amitu wo. Ene ginanshi mii migha wo, duyai kunlai aminde oluzhi ogizho."
JOH 6:52 Yutai kunla nieniedene jianjinduzho, "Ene kun matugie mighane ogizhi ijieghane?"
JOH 6:53 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi shuhuajia kielieye, ta Kunnikewonyi mighai ulie ijiezhi chusunyi ulie ochise tai sudoro amin uwo.
JOH 6:54 Mii mighai ijiezhi chusunyi ochisan kunde chanqiku amin wine. Duya barakudeni bi hhei aminne olughane.
JOH 6:55 Mighamishi zhenzhenji ijiuni wo, chusunmishi zhenzhenji ochikui wo.
JOH 6:56 Mighaimi ijiezhi chusunyimi ochisan kun mii sudoro beizho. Biye hhei sudoro beizho.
JOH 6:57 Mii peizhi ireghasan ulie fuguku Adai kouizhi bi amituku mutun mighaimi ijiesan kunla mii kouizhi amiturane.
JOH 6:58 Eneshi asiman jierese bouzhesan ginan wo. Enei ijiesan kun chanqi amitu wo. Tai xienrenghala buxian wo, manai ijieliuzhe fuguwo."
JOH 6:59 Enezighan kielienshi ErsaJiabainunni huitande kunlade sughazhi kieliesan wo.
JOH 6:60 Tujilani hhei kielienyi sonosudene kieliewo, "Ene kielien chijia wo. Kien dunjirene?"
JOH 6:61 Ersa tujilani kieliendusei mejiedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ene kielien tai zhughei gojiolughawu?
JOH 6:62 Qingiese Kunnikewon yenlaiku orondene khikui chanlase ta matugie sumulane?
JOH 6:63 Kunde amin ogikushi Shenlin wo, beye yama oronde uwo. Bi tande kieliesan kielienshi ruhher wo, aminye enbene.
JOH 6:64 Ingieseye tai dunda mii xianxin ese giesan kun wine." Ersa kaishi giekude kien hhei ghudandukuni mejiene.
JOH 6:65 Ersa pse kieliewo, "Ene yenyin jiere bi tande kieliezhi daozho. Ada ulie ireghase kiemada mii enende ire dane."
JOH 6:66 Enense khuinashi Ersai daghasan olon kunla yolazhi pse hhei ese daghawo.
JOH 6:67 Ingiese Ersa 12 gie tujidene kieliewo, "Taye yolanu?"
JOH 6:68 Ximun-Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, chade chanqiku amin ogiku kielien wine. Bijien pse kienyi daghane?
JOH 6:69 Bijien chishi Hudase iresan hhe zhiguitu bikui xianxin giezhi mejiezho."
JOH 6:70 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tai 12 giei sunghuwola? Tai dunda niekozishi Ibilisi wo."
JOH 6:71 Ersai ene kielienshi Jialie kun Ximunyi kewon Yudai kieliezho. Hheshi 12 gie tuji dundadu nie wo, khuinashi Ersai ghudandune.
JOH 7:1 Enense khuinashi ErsaJialilide toreizho. Hhe Yudayade echiku duran uwo. Yutai kunla hhei alane giezho.
JOH 7:2 Hhe shihoude Yutai kunlani Zhanfan Jie kuzhele qiiwo.
JOH 7:3 Ersai gaijiula hhende kieliewo, "Chi enense likai giezhi Yudayade echi. Chi giesan wilielane tujiladene uzhegha.
JOH 7:4 Kun minshende khiku duran bise niuise ulie olune. Chi ene shiqinlai giene giese duyai kunlade man uzhegha."
JOH 7:5 Yenlai gaijiulaniye hhei xianxin ese giezho.
JOH 7:6 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Ta giezhe echiliuzhe olune, mini shihou da uye kuzhezho.
JOH 7:7 Duyani kunla tai ulie henjine, mii henjine. Duyai kunla giesanlashi doghun wo giezhi bi kieliese mii henjine.
JOH 7:8 Ta jieqi daoghale echi. Bi ede da ulie echine. Mini shihou da uye kuzhezho."
JOH 7:9 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliesenu Jialilide souzho.
JOH 7:10 Hhei gaijiulani jieqi daoghale echikude Ersaye echiwo. Minminji ese echizho, ghulazhi echizho.
JOH 7:11 Zhen jieqi daoghakudeni Yutai kunla Ersai ereizhi asazho, "Hhe khala wine?"
JOH 7:12 Hhe xienzide kunla man Ersai kielienduzho. Ezighan kunla kieliese hheshi nie gou kun wo pse ezighan kunla kieliese hheshi nie pienzi wo giezho.
JOH 7:13 Ingieliuzhe Yutai kunse ayizhi Ersai minminji kiema kielie dane.
JOH 7:14 Jieqi daoghazhi zhen dundani echikude Ersa mechide khizhi echidene kunlade sughazhi qiiwo.
JOH 7:15 Yutai kunla chenliesenu ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Ene kun olon uye onshizho, matui imeghei mejiene?"
JOH 7:16 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo. "Bi sughasanshi minughun pusho. Mii peizhi ireghasan hhenughun wo.
JOH 7:17 Hudai isii zunjizhi giesan kunshi bi sughasanshi Hudanughun onu minughun bikuni mejiene.
JOH 7:18 Goya sumulasanne kieliechen kunshi goyane kuaichen kun wo. Peizhi ireghasan hheni kuaichen kunshi olusan kun wo, sudoroni yama gou wini uwo.
