JOH 7:19 Musa tande guijinni ogiwola? Kiema uye zunjizho. Ta yangiezhi mii alane giezho?"
JOH 7:20 Kunla kieliewo. "Chii jiere sheitan wine. Chii kien alane giezho?"
JOH 7:21 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi niekozi wilie giese ta man ghanirazho.
JOH 7:22 Musa chonjisan hetoune gieku guijinni ta hhamuraku udude ye giezho. Shijishan eneshi Musase kaishi giesan pusho, mai famatu xienrenlase kaishi giesan wo.
JOH 7:23 Ta Musai guijinyi ulie fanjine giezhi hhamuraku udude hetoune giene. Bi hhamuraku udude nie kunyi hunshenyi man goudaghase ta yangiezhi made hokune?
JOH 7:24 Ta kunni kieliese mienzini bu uzhe, gundande gie."
JOH 7:25 Yelusalenyi niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Eneshi hhela alane giesan kun pushonu?
JOH 7:26 Chi uzhe, hhe mindaminji jianjizho, hhela hhei yama ulie kieliene. Noyenla hheshi Mexiha bikui mejienu?
JOH 7:27 Ene kun khalase iresei matan mejiene. Mexiha irekude hhe khalase irekui kiema ulie mejiene."
JOH 7:28 Ingiekude Ersa mechide kunlade sughazhi fugiede kieliewo, "Ta mii tanine. Bi khalase ireseiye mejiene. Shijishan bi goyane ese irezho. Mii peizhi ireghasanshi zhoni wo, ta hhei tani dane.
JOH 7:29 Bi hhei tanine. Bishi hhense iresan wo. Hhe mii peizhi ireghazho."
JOH 7:30 Ingiese hhela Ersai bareine giezho. Shihouni ese kuse kiema kha tei dazho.
JOH 7:31 Olon kunla hhei xianxin giedene kieliewo, "Mexiha irese ene kunse ghudureqi olon xienjigha shidanu?"
JOH 7:32 Falisai kunla chenliese kunla Ersai kielienduzho. Ingiese fugie buwa, Falisai kunla mechini sagheisan kunlai peizhi Ersai bareighale echiwo.
JOH 7:33 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tanrezhe hhantuku udu choghonshiwo. Bi ede mii peizhi ireghasan hhende echine.
JOH 7:34 Ta mii ereise ereizhi olu dane. Bi biku oronde ta ire dane."
JOH 7:35 Yutai kunla nieniedene asazhi kieliewo, "Ene kun khala echinu? Matan ereizhi olu dane giene? Hhe niman gojiade sousan maikun dunda echinu, pse Xila kunlade surughale echinu?
JOH 7:36 Ta mii ereise ereizhi olu dane. Bi biku oronde ta ire dane giesan ene kielienshi yan isi wo?"
JOH 7:37 Jieqini zuihouku udu, zui zhunyoni udude Ersa beidene fugiede kieliewo, "Kun undasuse mii enende ule ire.
JOH 7:38 Mii xianxin giesan kunde jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun 'Sudoroseni amitu usu moron mutun holune.'"
JOH 7:39 Ersai ene kielienshi hhei xianxin giesan kunlade Shenlin ireghakui kieliezho. Hhe xienzide Ersade kuaikui ese ogizho. Ingiese kunlade Shenlin da ese irezho.
JOH 7:40 Ene kielienyi chenliedene niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Eneshi zhen hhe xienzhi wo."
JOH 7:41 Pse niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Ene kunshi Mexiha wo." Pseshiku kunla kieliewo, "Mexiha matugie Jialilise khizhene?
JOH 7:42 Mexihashi Dawudei houdeise hhei aghin Bolihense khizhene giezhi jinwun jiere ese kieliewu?"
JOH 7:43 Ingiese kunla Ersai ene shiqinde ghugha keiwo.
JOH 7:44 Hhelai dundadu kunla Ersai bareine giezhoma, kiema kha tei dazho.
JOH 7:45 Mechini sagheisan kunla khareizhi fugie buwa, Falisai kun shida irewo. Fugie buwa, Falisai kunla hhelade asawo, "Ta yale hhei bareizhi ese irewo?"
JOH 7:46 Mechini sagheisan kunla kieliewo, "Hhe kun mutun kielien kieliesan kun uwo!"
JOH 7:47 Falisai kunla kieliewo, "Taye dan jiere khireiwu?
JOH 7:48 Noyen, Falisai kun dunda hhei xianxin giesan kun nieda uwola?
JOH 7:49 Enezighan Musai guijinni yama dunjire dasan kunlade gou widawo."
JOH 7:50 Hhela dundadu nie kunshi Nigedemu wo. Melieshidase Ersai ochirale echizho. Hhelade kieliewo,
JOH 7:51 "Xien hhe goyane kieliesan kielienyi ulie chenliezhi hhe giesanlai chaizhi qinchu ulie olutula mai guijinghala matugie hhende zui jinjine?"
JOH 7:52 Hhela kieliewo, "Chiye Jialili kun onu? Chi echidene nie chaima, Jialilise xienzhi khizhenu ulie khizhene."
JOH 7:53 Ingiedene kunla man gieladene khareiwo.
JOH 8:1 ErsaGanlanshande echiwo.
JOH 8:2 Eqiemagha eqie mechide irewo. Olon kunla hhei shida irese hhe soudene sughazho.
JOH 8:3 Jinwun hanjia, Falisai kunla nie bierei zhen kunlare kijiekude barei ire kunlai dunda beigha
JOH 8:4 Ersade kieliewo, "Loushi, ene bierei zhen kunlare kijiekude barei irewo.
JOH 8:5 Musani guijin jiere imutu biereii tashighala eghi ala giezhi fenfulazho. Chi kieliese matugiene?"
JOH 8:6 Hhela ene kielienyi kieliese Ersai shiizho. Ersade nie zui jinjidene zhane giezho. Ersa ghodeidene kha ghurunghalane zemin jiere urou huaizho.
JOH 8:7 Hhela ulie beidene izhi asazho. Ersa bosizhedene kieliewo, "Tai dunda kiende zui uwoshi xien tashii bareidene eghi."
JOH 8:8 Ingie pse ghodeidene zemin jiere urou huaizho.
JOH 8:9 Hhela ene kielienyi chenliedene xien nasun fugienise nienieji yolawo. Zuihoude Ersa hhe biereighala feiliewo.
JOH 8:10 Ersa bosizhedene biereide kieliewo, "Funi, hhela khala echiwo? Chade kiema zui ese jinjiwu?"
JOH 8:11 Bierei kieliewo, "Gujiu, uye." Ersa kieliewo, "Biye chade zui ulie jinjine. Chi echidene pse zui bu fanji."
JOH 8:12 Ersa pse kunlade kieliewo, "Bishi duyani gon wo. Mii daghasan kunlade aminni gon wine, kharanide ulie yone."
JOH 8:13 Falisai kunla kieliewo, "Chi goyadene ganzhen beizho, chii ganzhen yama oronde uwo."
JOH 8:14 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi goyane ganzhen beiliuzhe mii ganzhen oronde wine. Bi goyane khalase iresanne mejiene, khala echikuneye mejiene. Bi khalase iresanyi ta ulie mejiene, khala echikuiye ulie mejiene.
JOH 8:15 Ta kunni uzhedanghala panjinema, bi kiemai ulie panjine.
JOH 8:16 Bi kunyi panjiliuzhe mii panjiku oronde wine. Bi niezheghanne pusho. Mii peizhi ireghasan Adaghalane hhantu wo.
JOH 8:17 Tai guijin jiere, 'Ghua kun ganzhen beise zhenni wo.' giezhi huaizho.
JOH 8:18 Bi goyadene ganzhen beizho, pse mii peizhi ireghasan adamiye made ganzhen beizho."
JOH 8:19 Ingiese hhela asazho, "Adachii khala wo?" Ersa kieliewo, "Ta mii tani dane, adaimiye tani dane. Mii tanise adaimiye tanine."
JOH 8:20 Ene kielienshi Ersa mechini baer teiku kufan konde kunlade sughazhi kieliesan woma, hhei shihouni uye kuzhese kiemada hhei uye bareizho.
JOH 8:21 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Bi echine. Ta mii ereinema, ta zui dunda fugune. Bi echiku oronde ta echi dane."
JOH 8:22 Ingiese Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Hhe kieliese hhe echiku oronde matan echi dane giene. Hhe goyane fugune giezhou?"
JOH 8:23 Ersa hhelade pse kieliewo, "Tashi zemin jierese iresan wo, bishi asiman jierese iresan wo. Tashi duyadedu wo, bishi duyadedu pusho.
JOH 8:24 Ingiese ta zui dundane fugune giezhi bi kieliewo. Ta bishi hhe enbekui xianxin ulie giese zui dundane fugune."
JOH 8:25 Ingiese hhela asazho, "Chishi kien wo?" Ersa kieliewo, "Bishi dei irekude tande kieliesan hhe nie wo.
JOH 8:26 Bi tande kieliekui olon wo, zui jinjikuiye olon wo. Ingieliuzhe mii peizhi ireghasanshi zhenni wo, ingiese bi hhense chenliesanlai duyai kunlade kieliene."
JOH 8:27 Ersa Adane zhiizhi kieliesei hhela mejie dazho.
JOH 8:28 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Ta Kunnikewonyi qila qiighakude bishi hhe enbekui mejiene. Bi goya isighalane uye giezho, Adami sughasan mutun kieliesei ta mejiene.
JOH 8:29 Mii peizhi ireghasan hhe mare hhantu wo. Hhe mii niezheghan ese jiezho. Bi chan hhei bayasughakui giezho."
JOH 8:30 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliedene olon kunla hhei xianxin giewo.
JOH 8:31 Ingiese Ersa hhei xianxin giesan Yutai kunlade kieliewo, "Ta mii kielienyi chan zunjizhi giese mii zhenzhenji tuji wo.
JOH 8:32 Ta zhendaoni mejiene, zhendao tai ziyushighane."
JOH 8:33 Hhela kieliewo, "Bijienshi Iburaheimui houdei wo. Bijien kiemade hoji danlazhi ese daozho. Chi matui 'Bijienyi ziyushighane.' giezhi kieliene?"
JOH 8:34 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Bi shuhuajia kielieye, zui fanjisan kunshi zuini hoji wo.
JOH 8:35 Hoji chanqi giede sou dane, kewon chanqi giede soune.
JOH 8:36 Ingiese Kewon tai ziyushighase ta zhenzhenji ziyushine.
JOH 8:37 Tashi Iburaheimui houdei bikui bi mejiene. Mii kielien tai zhughede oro dase ta mii alane giezho.
JOH 8:38 Bi Adane hhense chujieghesei kieliezho. Ta adane hhense chenliesei giezho."
JOH 8:39 Hhela kieliewo, "Bijienyi adashi Iburaheimu wo." Ersa kieliewo, "Pusho, ta Iburaheimui houdeishi taye Iburaheimu giesan wilie mutun giene.
JOH 8:40 Bi Hudai hhense chenliesan zhendaoi tande kieliese, ta mii alane giezho. Eneshi Iburaheimu gieku wilie pusho.
JOH 8:41 Ta giesan wilieshi zhen adatai giesan wilie wo." Ingiese hhela Ersade kieliewo, "Bijienshi zagieda pusho. Bijiende niekozi ada wo, hheshi Huda wo."
JOH 8:42 Ersa kieliewo, "Huda tai ada enbese ta made orene. Bishi Hudase tai enende iresan wo. Bi goyane iresan pusho, hhe mii peizhi ireghazho.
JOH 8:43 Bi kieliesanlai ta yangiezhi minbai olu dane? Bi sughakui ta jieshou ulie giene.
JOH 8:44 Tashi tai ada Ibilisise iresan wo. Adatai yan duralase ta yan giene. Hheshi dei qiisanse kun alachen wo. Ibeizi zhennide ulie beine. Zhughedeni zhenni uwo. Hheshi ghudanchi wo, ghudanchini touzi wo. Ingiese hhe ghudan kieliese hhei xinbin wo.
JOH 8:45 Ingiese bi zhendaoni kieliese ta mii xianxin ulie giene.
JOH 8:46 Tai dunda kien made zui jinjine? Bi tande zhendaoni kieliese, ta yale mii xianxin ulie giene?
JOH 8:47 Hudase khizhesan kunla Hudai kielienyi chenliene. Ta ulie chenliese Hudase khizhesei pusho."
JOH 8:48 Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Bijien kieliese chishi Samaliya kun wo, chii jiere sheitan wo giesan ene kielien ese oluzhou?"
JOH 8:49 Ersa kieliewo, "Mii jiere sheitan uwo. Bi adane zunzhun giezho, ta mii zunzhun uye giezho.
JOH 8:50 Bi goyane kuaikui ulie sumulanema, da niezhan mii kuaine. Hheshijiu panjichen wo.
JOH 8:51 Bi shuhuajia kielieye, kien mii kielienyi chenliese hhe chanqi ulie fugune."
JOH 8:52 Ingiese Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Ede bijien zhenzhen mejiewo! Chii jiere sheitan wine. Iburaheimu duya ijiewo, xienzhilaye duya ijiewo. Chi kieliese chii kielienyi chenliese chanqi ulie fugune giezho.
JOH 8:53 Qinse chi bijienyi xienren Iburaheimuse pse fugie onu? Hhe duya ijiewo, xienzhilaye duya ijiewo. Chi goyane yan kun wo giezho?"
JOH 8:54 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi goyane kuaise hhe yama zoin uwo. Mii kuaisanshi Adami wo. Hheshijiu ta kieliesan mai huda wo giesan hhe wo.
JOH 8:55 Ta hhei tani dane, bi hhei tanine. Bi hhei tani dane giezhi kieliese ta mutun ghudanchi gholune. Ingiese bi hhei tanine, kielienyini ye chenliene.
JOH 8:56 Tai xienren Iburaheimu mii udui uzhene giezhi bayasuzhi sagheizho. Udui chanladene hende bayasuzho."
JOH 8:57 Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Chii nasun 50 da ulie olune, matugie Iburaheimui uzhezhi daowo giezhi kieliene?"
JOH 8:58 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, Iburaheimui ese olukudeni bi wine."
JOH 8:59 Ingiese hhela tashii bareisenu Ersai eghine giezho. Ersa piidene mechise khizhi echiwo.
JOH 9:1 Ersa mo yozhi daokudeni olusanse nie sughoi chanlawo.
JOH 9:2 Tujilani Ersade asazho, "Loushi, ene kun goya zui fanjizhi sugho gholuwu, ada anani zui fanjizhi sugho gholuwo?"
JOH 9:3 Ersa kieliewo, "Hhe zui fanjizhi gholusan pusho, ada anani zui fanjizhi gholusanye pusho. Eneshi hhei jierese Huda nenline kunlade mejieghane giezho.
JOH 9:4 Udu bikude matan mii peizhi ireghasan hhei wiliei giekuni wo. Khara oluse kiemada wilie gie dane.
JOH 9:5 Bi duyade bikude bishi duyani gon wo."
JOH 9:6 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliesenu zemin jiere nunpuwo. Nunpusunghala shuwa zhuwadene sughoni nudun jiere moiwo.
JOH 9:7 Ingie hhende kieliewo, "Chi Xiloya loubade echidene nie wagha." Xiloyani isishi peizhi ireghasan wo. Hhe echi nie wagha kharei irese chujieghewo.
JOH 9:8 Hhei giebeilane, hhe ghuisei chujieghesan kunla kieliewo, "Eneshi melieshida soudene ghuisan hhe kun pushonu?"
JOH 9:9 Ezighan kunla hhe enbene giezho. Psezighan kunla pusho, hhei xianli giezho. Hhe goyane bi enbene giezho.
JOH 9:10 Hhela asazho, "Chii nudun matui goudawo?"
JOH 9:11 Hhe kieliewo, "Ersa giechen nie kun shuwa giedene mii nudun jiere moi made kieliewo, 'Chi Xiloya loubade echi nie wagha.' Bi echi nie waghase chujieghewo."
JOH 9:12 Hhela asawo, "Hhe kun khala wine?" Hhe kieliewo, "Bi ulie mejiene."
JOH 9:13 Kunla melieshidaku sughoni udurusenu Falisai kunlai hhende echiwo.
JOH 9:14 Ersa shuwa zhuwazhi nudunyi goudaghasan hhe niudushi hhamuraku udu wo.
JOH 9:15 Ingiese Falisai kunla hhe kunde asazho, "Chii nudun matui goudawo?" Hhe kieliewo, "Hhe shuwani mii nudun jiere moiwo. Bi nie waghase chujieghewo."
JOH 9:16 Falisai kun dunda niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Hheshi Hudase iresan kun pusho. Hhe hhamuraku uduiye uye zunjizho." Da niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Nie zui winetu kun imutu ghudureqi gie shidanu?" Ingie kunla ghugha keiwo.
JOH 9:17 Ingiese hhela pse sughode kieliewo, "Hhe chii nudunyi goudaghazho. Chi nie kielie, hheshi nie matunie kun wo?" Hhe kieliewo, "Hheshi nie xienzhi wo."
JOH 9:18 Ingiese Yutai kunla hheshi melieshida sugho wo, ede goudasei xianxin ese giedene nudun goudasan kunyi ada anaini uruzhi ire asazho,
JOH 9:19 "Eneshi olusanse sugho wo giesan tai kewon enbenu pusho? Ede matui chujieghewo?"
JOH 9:20 Ada anani kieliewo, "Eneshi bijienyi kewon enbene. Hhe olusanse sugho bikui bijien mejiene.
JOH 9:21 Ede matui chujieghewoshi bijien ulie mejiene. Nudunyini kien goudaghawoshi bijienye ulie mejiene. Ta hhende asa, hhe ede fugiedazho. Goyane kielie shidane."
JOH 9:22 Ada anani ingiezhi kieliekushi Yutai kunlase ayizho. Yutai kunla jiejin giezhi kien Ersashi Mexiha wo giezhi renjise huitanse tou khighane giezho.
JOH 9:23 Ingiese ada anani ta hhende asa, "Hhe ede fugiedazho." giezhi kieliewo.
JOH 9:24 Ingiese hhela hhe sughoi erchan uruzhi iredene asazho, "Chi indan Hudai kuaikui wo. Ene kunshi zuiren bikui bijien mejiene."
JOH 9:25 Ingiese hhe kun kieliewo, "Hhende zui winu uwokui bi ulie mejienema, melieshi bi sugho wo, ede chujieghekune mejiene."
JOH 9:26 Ingiese hhela asazho, "Hhe chade yan giewo? Hhe chii nudunyi matugie goudaghawo?"
JOH 9:27 Hhe kieliewo, "Bi munigie tande kieliewo, ta ulie chenliene. Ta yangiezhi pse chenliene giezho? Taye hhei tuji danlane giezhou?"
JOH 9:28 Hhela sugiezhi kieliewo, "Chishi hhei tuji wo, bijienshi Musai tuji wo.
JOH 9:29 Huda Musade kieliesanyi bijien mejiene. Hhe kun khalase iresanyi bijien ulie mejiene."
JOH 9:30 Hhe kun kieliewo, "Hhe mii nudunyi goudaghawo. Hhe khalase iresanyi ta ulie mejienu? Ta zhenzhen hunnerei wo.
JOH 9:31 Huda zuirenni kielienyi ulie chenliene. Zinie hhei zunjizhi kielienyini chenliesan kunnughunyi chenliene. Enei matan man mejiene.
JOH 9:32 Duyai zhayaghasanse sughoi nudunyi goudaghasei chenliezhi uye daozho.
JOH 9:33 Hhe kun Hudai hhense uye irezhoshi imutu wilie gie dane."
JOH 9:34 Hhela kieliewo, "Chii olusanse qienbu zui dunda wo, chi da bijiende sughanu!" Ingiedene hhei tou khighawo.
JOH 9:35 Ersa hhe kunyi tou khighasanyi chenliedene hhei ereizhi oluwo. Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi Kunnikewonni xianxin giezhou?"
JOH 9:36 Hhe kun kieliewo, "Gujiu, hheshi kien wine? Bi xianxin gieye."
JOH 9:37 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi hhei chujieghezho. Chare kielien kieliesanshi enbene."
JOH 9:38 Hhe kieliewo, "Gujiu, bi xianxin giene!" Ingiesenu Ersade xiutuliewo.
JOH 9:39 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi duyade panjile irewo. Chujieghe dachen kunlai chujiegheghane, chujieghechen kunlai sugho gholughane."
JOH 9:40 Hhei shida ene kielienyi chenliesan ezighan Falisai kunla kieliewo, "Qinse bijienye sugho onu?"
JOH 9:41 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Tashi sughoshi tande zui uwo. Ta, 'Chujieghe shidane.' giezhi kieliese tande zui wine."
JOH 10:1 "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, kien ghoni khudonde orokude wijiense ulie orozhi pse khalamase orose hheshi ghughei, qiandao wo.
JOH 10:2 Wijiense orosan kunshi zhen ghoni adulachen kun wo.
JOH 10:3 Ghoni adulachen kun irese wijienyi sagheisan kun wijienyi niene, ghonilaye hhei shenqii tanine. Hhe ghonine nierese uruzhi khizheghane.
JOH 10:4 Man uruzhi khizhesenu goyane melie yone. Ghonila hhei shenqii tanise hhei daghane.
JOH 10:5 Ghonila tani daku kunyi ulie daghane. Hhei shenqii ulie mejiese holu widane."
JOH 10:6 Ersa enezighan kielienyi hhelade bilazhi kieliezho. Hhela yan isi bikui dunjire dane.
JOH 10:7 Ingiese Ersa hhelade pse kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, bishi ghoni yoku wijien enbene.
JOH 10:8 Mase melie iresanshi man ghughei, qiandao wo. Ghonila hhelai ese chenliewo.
JOH 10:9 Bishi wijien wo. Mase tungo giezhi orosanlai jiui shidane, orozhi ire khizhi echise osun ijie shidane.
JOH 10:10 Ghughei irese ghulane, alane, qida olughane. Bi irese ghonilade amin ogine, da fugiede ogine.
JOH 10:11 Bishi nie gou ghoni adulachen kun wo. Gou ghoni adulachen kun ghonide oluzhi aminne sheine.
JOH 10:12 Guisan kunshi zhenzhenji ghoni adulachen pusho. Ghonishi hhenughun pusho. Zhanghei irekui chanlase ghonilai benda jie holu widane. Zhanghei ghonise nie bareise ghonila man sanda widane.
JOH 10:13 Guisan kun ghonilade zhughe ulie chilane. Ingiese holu widane.
JOH 10:14 Bishi gou ghoni adulachen wo. Bi ghonine tanine, mii ghonilaye mii tanine.
JOH 10:15 Eneshi Adami mini taniku, bi Adane tanikughala niekielien wo. Bi ghonidene oluzhi aminne sheine.
JOH 10:16 Made ene khudonde wiku ghoni da wine. Hhelaiye bi uduruzhi irene. Hhela mii shenqii sonosudene man hhantulazhi nie adulachen kun gonjine."
JOH 10:17 "Bi aminne widaghadene pse agizhi irene. Ingiese Adami made orezho.
JOH 10:18 Mii aminyi kiema agizhi echi dane. Bi goyane ogisan wo. Bi aminne bendaku qienli wine. Pse agizhi ireku qienliye wine. Eneshi Adami made ogisan minlin wo."
JOH 10:19 Yutai kunla ene kieliende pse ghugha keiwo.
JOH 10:20 Olon kunla kieliezho, "Hhei jiere sheitan khizho, hhe fenjiulizho. Ta dou kielienyini chenliezhou?"
JOH 10:21 Pse iban kunla kieliewo, "Hhei jiere sheitan khise imutu kielien kielie dane. Sheitan sughoi goudagha shidanu?"
JOH 10:22 Yelusalende mechii giesan jieqi kuzhewo. Eneshi unchade wo.
JOH 10:23 Ersa mechini Sulumane doudoughun yozho.
JOH 10:24 Yutai kunla hhei wiqidene kieliewo, "Chi bijienyi giedoghoncha inxin gieghane? Chi Mexiha enbese mindamin kielie."
JOH 10:25 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi tande ijin kieliewoma, ta mii xianxin ulie giene. Bi adane niereghala giesan shiqinla made ganzhen beine.
JOH 10:26 Ta mii ghoni pusho, ingiese mii xianxin ulie giene.
JOH 10:27 Mii ghoni mii shenqii chenliene, bi hhelai tanine, hhela mii daghane.
JOH 10:28 Bi hhelade chanqiku amin ogine. Hhela ibeizi ulie widane, kiemada mii khase agizhi echi dane.
JOH 10:29 Hhelai made ogisan Adami yanseliuzhe fugie wo. Adaimi khase hhelai kiemada qianlazhi echi dane.
JOH 10:30 Bi Adaghalaneshi nie wo."
JOH 10:31 Yutai kunla pse tashii bareidene Ersai eghine giezho.
JOH 10:32 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Bi Adane hhendedu gou wiliei giezhi tande uzheghazho. Ta alinie shiqinde mii eghine giezho?"
JOH 10:33 Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Gouni giewo giezhi eghine giesan pusho. Chi kufurei fanjizho. Chishi nie kun wo, goyane Huda giezhi kieliene."
JOH 10:34 Ersa kieliewo, "Tai guijinshu jiere tashi huda wo giezhi bi kieliewo giezhi ese huaizhou?
JOH 10:35 Jinwun jieredu kielien nieda ulie widane. Hudai kielienyi jienliesan kunlade huda giezhi kieliewoma,
JOH 10:36 Adami mii zhiguishighadene duyade peizhi ireghase bi kieliezhi 'Bishi Hudai Kewon wo.' giese ta mii kufurei fanjiwo giezhi kielienu?
JOH 10:37 Bi Adane wiliei ulie giese ta mii xianxin bu gie.
JOH 10:38 Bi giese ta mii xianxin ulie gieliuzhe bi giesan shiqinlai xianxin gie. Ingiese Adami mii sudoro wo, bi Adane sudoro bikui ta qinchude mejiene."
JOH 10:39 Ingiese hhela Ersai pse bareine giese Ersa hhelai khase anda yolasenu
JOH 10:40 Yedanheni pse daozhi Yaheiya melieshida kunlade xili gieghasan hhe oronde echizhi souwo.
JOH 10:41 Olon kunla hhei shida iredene kieliewo, "Yaheiya yama ghudureqi uye giezhoma, hhe ene kunyi zhiizhi kieliesanshi man zhenni wo."
JOH 10:42 Ingiedene hhende olon kunla Ersai xianxin giewo.
JOH 11:1 Nie giemeresan kunyi nierei Lasalu giene. Mereiyen, Mada ghua eghechijiularene Bodani aghinde souzho.
JOH 11:2 Ene Mereiyenshi Ezhanni jiere xianshui kiedene usunghalane konyini saisan hhe wo. Giemeresan Lasalushi hhei jiu wo.
JOH 11:3 Ghua eghechijiuni kun peizhi Ersade kielieghale echiwo, "Ezhan, chi oresan kun giemerezho."
JOH 11:4 Ersa chenliedene kieliewo, "Eneshi fuguku gien pusho. Hudai kuaiku shiqin wo. Ingiedene eneghala Hudai Kewonni kuaine."
JOH 11:5 Ingiese ErsaMada, hhei eghechijiu, pse Lasalude orezhoma,
JOH 11:6 Lasalu giemeresanyi sonosudene sousan orondene pse ghuarudu souwo.
JOH 11:7 Ingie tujiladene kieliewo, "Matan pse Yudayade khareiye."
JOH 11:8 Tujilani kieliewo, "Loushi, ene ghuarudu Yutai kunla chii tashighala eghine giezho. Chi da hhende echinu?"
JOH 11:9 Ersa kieliewo, "Udu 12 gie xioshi pushonu? Kun ene duyani gonni chanlase udu mo yose ulie banjine.
JOH 11:10 Xieni yose hhe kunde gon uwoshi banjine."
JOH 11:11 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliedene pse kieliewo, "Mai zhanlien Lasalu hhunturazho. Bi echidene uruzhi xiereighane."
JOH 11:12 Ingiese tujilani kieliewo, "Ezhan, hhe hhunturazhoshi goudane."
JOH 11:13 Ersai ene kielienshi hhe fugusei kieliezho. Hhela sumulase Ersai ene kielienshi hhe kijie hhunturazho giezho.
JOH 11:14 Ersa hhelade minminji kieliewo, "Lasalu duya ijiezho.
JOH 11:15 Bi hhende wise bi tande oluzhi bayasuzho. Ene jihui jiere ta mini xianxin giene. Ede matan hhende yoye."
JOH 11:16 Shongo giezhi urusan Doma psedu tujilade kieliewo, "Matanye yo, Ersare hhantu duya ijieye."
JOH 11:17 Ersa kuzhedene Lasalui mezade teizhi ijin jierudu olusanyi mejiewo.
JOH 11:18 BodaniYelusalense gholo uwo, chabudu 6 li mo wo.
JOH 11:19 Olon Yutai kunla Mada, Mereiyenyi uzhele irewo. Jiunini shiqinde sidaghazhi kieliele irewo.
JOH 11:20 MadaErsa iresei mejiedene jienliele echiwo. Mereiyen yen giedene souzho.
JOH 11:21 MadaErsade kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi enende wineshi jiumi ulie duya ijienema,
JOH 11:22 edeliuzhe chi Hudase yan kerese Huda chade ogikui bi mejiene."
JOH 11:23 Ersa kieliewo, "Jiuchii aminne olune."
JOH 11:24 Mada kieliewo, "Duya barazhi kunla fuho giekude hheye aminne olukui bi mejiene."
JOH 11:25 Ersa kieliewo, "Bishi fuho wo, amin wo. Mini xianxin giesan kun fuguliuzhe aminne olune.
JOH 11:26 Kun amitu bikude mii xianxin giese chanqi ulie fugune. Chi eneni xianxin gienu?"
JOH 11:27 Mada kieliewo, "Ezhan, oluzho. Chishi Mexiha wo, duyade irene giesan Hudai Kewon enbekui bi xianxin giene."
JOH 11:28 Mada ene kielienyi kieliedene khareizhi echi eghechijiu Mereiyende konkonji kieliewo, "Loushi irewo. Chii uruzho."
JOH 11:29 Mereiyen chenliedene jindazhi bosizhe Ersai hhende echiwo.
JOH 11:30 Ersa aghinde orozhi ese echidene Mada hhei jienliesan hhe oronde wo.
JOH 11:31 Hhezighan Mereiyenyi giede sidaghazhi kieliesan Yutai kunla Mereiyen bosizhedene jindazhi ghadane echisei chanlasenu daghazhi echiwo. Hhela sumulase Mereiyen mezade wilale echine giezho.
JOH 11:32 MereiyenErsai hhende kuzhi ire hhei chanladene kon shidai papala kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi enende wineshi jiumi ulie duya ijiene."
JOH 11:33 Ersa hhe wilasei, pse hhei daghazhi iresan Yutai kunla wilasei chanladene zhughedene zhoqi giezhi nango giezho.
JOH 11:34 Hhe asawo, "Ta hhei khala teiwo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Ezhan, uzhele ire."
JOH 11:35 Ersa wilawo.
JOH 11:36 Ingiese Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Ta uzhe, ene kun Lasalude matugiezhi orezho."
JOH 11:37 Niezhan kunla kieliewo, "Hhe sughoni nudunyi goudaghawoma, ene kunyi matugie ese goudaghazhi fugughawo?"
JOH 11:38 Ersa pse sudorone zhoqi giezhi meza konde irewo. Hhe mezashi nie alima wo. Niekozi tashighala kouzii duighazho.
JOH 11:39 Ersa kieliewo, "Tashii daogha." Ingiese duya ijiesan kunyi ajieni Mada hhende kieliewo, "Ezhan, hhe duya ijiezhi jierudu olune. Ede fumugheishizho."
JOH 11:40 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi xianxin giese Hudai famai chanlakuni bi chade kieliezhi ese daowu?"
JOH 11:41 Ingiese hhela tashii daoghawo. Ersa qiorunne qila asimanni uzhedene kieliewo, "Ada, chii mafan gieghawo. Chi minughunyi chenliewo.
JOH 11:42 Chi chan minughunyi chenliekui bi mejiene. Bi ene kielienyi kieliese zhouwini beisan kunlade oluzho. Chi mii peizhi ireghasanyi hhelade xianxin gieghane giezho."
JOH 11:43 Ene kielienyi kieliedene fugiede waradawo, "Lasalu, khizhe!"
JOH 11:44 Ingiese fugusan kun khizhewo. Khakonyini bosighala horozho, ungienyini ye shoujinghala bouizho. Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Hhei andaghadene yogha."
JOH 11:45 Ingiese Mereiyenyi hhende iresan olon Yutai kunla Ersa giesan shiqinyi uzhedene hhei xianxin giewoma,
JOH 11:46 hhelai dunda niezhan kunla Falisai kunyi shida echidene Ersa giesan shiqinyi kieliewo.
JOH 11:47 Fugie buwa, Falisai kunla goyane zui fugie fayenni kunlai hhantulagha kieliewo, "Ene kun ghudureqi olon xienjighazho. Matan matugiene?
JOH 11:48 Enei izhi ingiezhi gieghase kunla man hhei xianxin giene. Pse Loma kunla irese mai mechii, mai minzui widaghane."
JOH 11:49 Hhelai dunda nie kunyi nierei Gaiyafa giene. Hhe niehonde zui fugie buwa danlazho. Hhelade kieliewo, "Ta yama ulie mejiene!
JOH 11:50 Hhe niezheghanne bexinlade oluzhi fuguse nie gojia man widakuse gou wo. Ene tande haochu bikui ta ulie mejienu?"
JOH 11:51 Ene kielienshi goyane kieliesan pusho. Ene honku zui fugie buwa danlase ErsaYutai kunlade oluzhi fugukuni melie kieliezho.
JOH 11:52 Zinie Yutai kunlade pusho, gochude sousan Hudai kesilai hhantulaghazhi nie gholughane giezhi fugukui kieliezho.
JOH 11:53 Hhe uduse hhela shanlian giezhi Ersai alane giezho.
JOH 11:54 Ingiese Ersa pse Yutai kun dunda mindaminji uye ochirazho. Hhense likai giedene hontan shida Ifalien giezhi nie oronde echisenu tujighalane hhantu souwo.
JOH 11:55 Yutai kunni Jiulidaosan Jie kuzhene giezho. Olon kunla xianlase Yelusalende eqie khizhi iresenu goyalane waghane giezho.
JOH 11:56 Hhela Ersai ereizhi mechide beisenu nieniedene kieliewo, "Ta uzhese matugiezho? Hhe jieqi daoghale ulie ireneba."
JOH 11:57 Hhe shihoude fugie buwa, Falisai kunla eqie fenfula goudaghazho. "Kien Ersa khala bikui mejiese mejiegha. Hhei bareine."
JOH 12:1 Jiulidaosan Jieni melieshi zhighudude ErsaBodanide kuzhi irewo. Hheshi ErsaLasalui aminne olughasan oron wo.
JOH 12:2 Kunla Ersade oluzhi heifan zhunbei giezho. Mada ushilazho. LasaluErsaghala kunlare hhantu souzho.
JOH 12:3 Mereiyen 1 jin zhen nadaghala giesan guizhuntu xianshuini agizhedene Ersai kon jiere kiesenu usunghalane saiwo. Giedera xianshui widao penjizho.
JOH 12:4 Ersai ghudandune giesan tuji Jialie kun Yuda kieliewo,
JOH 12:5 "Ene xianshuini 300 gie miengu huidene nanxin kunlade oginema!"
JOH 12:6 Hhe ene kielienyi kieliekushi nanxin kunlade sumulasan pusho. Goyaneshi nie ghughei wo. Baer qibaoni hhe bareizho. Hhense baerni chan agizho.
JOH 12:7 Ingiese Ersa kieliewo, "Bu danla, hhe ene xianshuii mii bulaku udude zhunbei giezho.
JOH 12:8 Nanxin kunla tanre chan hhantu woma, bi tanre chan hhantu uwo."
JOH 12:9 Olon Yutai kunla Ersa hhende bikui mejiedene uzhele irewo. Zinie Ersai uzhekui pusho. Fuguzhi aminne olusan Lasaluiye uzhene giezho.
JOH 12:10 Ingiese fugie buwala Lasaluiye alane giezhi shanlian giezho.
JOH 12:11 Ingiekushi Lasalui ene shiqin jiere olon Yutai kunla hhelai bendadene Ersai xianxin giezho.
JOH 12:12 Khuichudu olon kunla jieqi daoghale iredene ErsaYelusalende irekui mejiewo.
JOH 12:13 Ingie zunshu mutun chalalai bareidene hhei jienliele echi fugiede waradazhi kieliewo, "Hesanna! Ezhanni niereghala iresan Isilieni honshande doulandu!"
JOH 12:14 Ersa nie ga enzheghei ereizhi olu unuwo. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun,
JOH 12:15 "Xiwunni kunla bu ayi. Uzhe, tai honshan ga enzheghe unuzhi irewo."
JOH 12:16 Hhe xienzide tujilani ene shiqinyi minbai olu dazho. Ersa kuaikui jienliedene hhela ene kielienshi Ersai zhiizhi kieliesei, pse kunla hhende qingiezhi giesei sumula irewo.
JOH 12:17 ErsaLasalui mezase waradazhi khizhedene aminne olughakude shidani beisan kunla hhe giesan shiqinyi kunlade izhi kieliezho.
JOH 12:18 Ingiese olon kunla Ersa xienjighasan ghudureqii mejiedene hhei jienliele echiwo.
JOH 12:19 Ingiese Falisai kunla nieniedene kieliewo, "Matande yama banfa widawo. Duyai kunla man hhei dagha echiwo."
JOH 12:20 Jieqide libai giele iresan kun dunda giedun Xila kun wo.
JOH 12:21 Hhela Jialilini Bosaida kunni Feilini ochiradene xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Gujiu, bijien Ersai ochirale irewo."
JOH 12:22 Feili echidene Andeliede kieliewo. AndelieFeili ghuala hhantu Ersade echi kieliewo.
JOH 12:23 Ingie Ersa kieliewo, "Kunnikewonni kuaiku shihou kuzhewo.
JOH 12:24 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, niekozi boudei fure ghazha jiere luidene ulie fuguse dou niekozi fure wo. Fuguse olon boudei osizhi khizhene.
JOH 12:25 Goya amindene oresan kun aminne widaghane. Ene duyade aminne henjisan kun aminne chanqi bouine.
JOH 12:26 Mii ushilasan kun indan mii daghakuni wo. Bi khalashi mii ushilasan kun ye khala wo. Mii ushilasan kunyi Adami danren giene.
JOH 12:27 Ede mii zhughede nango giezho. Bi yan kieliese gou wo? 'Ada, mii ene shiqinse daogha.' giezhi kielienu? Ulie, bi zhen ene shiqinde irezho.
JOH 12:28 Ada, chi nierene famashigha!" Hhe xienzide asiman jierese shenqi irezhi kieliewo, "Bi ijin nierene famashighawo, pse famashighane."
JOH 12:29 Shida beisan kunla sonosusenu kieliewo, "Olien tunguliezho." Psedu kunla kieliewo, "Qienxien hhende kielien kieliezho."
JOH 12:30 Ersa kieliewo, "Ene shenqishi made oluzhi iresan pusho. Tande oluzhi iresan wo.
JOH 12:31 Ede duyani panjiku shihou kuzhewo. Ene duyani touzii tou khighane, jiushi Ibilisi wo.
JOH 12:32 Mii zemin jierese qila qiighakude bi kunlai man xiidene shidane irene."
JOH 12:33 Ersai ene kielienshi goyane matugie fugukui zhiizhi kieliezho.
JOH 12:34 Ingiese kunla kieliewo, "Bijien chenliese jinwunde kieliesanshi Mexiha ibeizi amitu wo giezho. Chi matugie 'Kunnikewonni qila qiighane.' giezhi kieliene? Chi kieliesan Kunnikewonshi kien wo?"
JOH 12:35 Ersa kieliewo, "Gon tai dunda oloncha widazho. Gon bikude ta gon dunda yodu. Pse kharani kuzhese tai khane. Kharanide yochen kun khala echikune ulie mejiene.
JOH 12:36 Gon bikude ta gonni xianxin giezhi gonni kewosi danla." Ersa ene kielienyi kielie baragha likai giedene hhelase pii widawo.
JOH 12:37 Hhelai melie Ersa ghudureqi olon xienjighazhoma, hhela hhei xianxin ulie giene.
JOH 12:38 Ingiese Isaiya xienzhi kieliesan kielien mutun gholuwo, "Ezhan, bijienyi chonjisanyi kien xianxin giewo? Chii nenlii kiende xienjighane?"
JOH 12:39 Hhela xianxin ulie giekushi Isaiya pse kieliezho,
JOH 12:40 "Ezhan hhelai nudunyini sugho gholughazhi zhugheini khiduzheghakushi Hhela nudundene chanlazhi zhughedene minbai olusenu kharei daorese Bi hhelai goudaghakuse ayizho."
JOH 12:41 IsaiyaErsai famani chanladene hhei zhiizhi ene kielienyi kieliesan wo.
JOH 12:42 Ingieliuzhe Yutai kunni noyen dundaye hhei xianxin giesan kun olon wo, Falisai kunla huitanse tou khighakuse ayizhi chenren gie dazho.
JOH 12:43 Hhela kunni kuaikui Hudai kuaikuse xiqi wo.
JOH 12:44 Ersa fugiede kieliewo, "Kunla mii xianxin giese zinie mii xianxin giesan pusho, mii peizhi ireghasan hhei xianxin giezho.
JOH 12:45 Kunla mii chujieghese mii peizhi ireghasanyi chujieghezho.
JOH 12:46 Bi duyade irese duyani gon wo. Mii xianxin giesan kunlai bi kharanide ulie soughane.
JOH 12:47 Mii kielienyi sonosudene ulie giechen kunyi bi ulie panjine. Bi duyade irese duyai panjile ese irezho, jiuile irezho.
JOH 12:48 Mii ulie kerechen, kielienyimi ulie jienliechen kunni panjiku wine. Bi kieliesan kielien duya barakude hhei panjine.
JOH 12:49 Bi kieliesanshi goyane sumulazhi kieliesan pusho. Mii peizhi ireghasan Adami made minlin ogizhi mii yan kielieghase bi yan kieliezho.
JOH 12:50 Adaimi minlinshi chanqiku amin bikui bi mejiene. Ingiese bi zinie Adami made kielieghakuni kieliene."
JOH 13:1 Jiulidaosan Jieni melieshida Ersa duyase likai giezhi Adane hhende echiku shihou kurukui mejiewo. Hhe ene duyani goya kunladene orezhi zuihou kurutula izhi orezho.
JOH 13:2 Heifan ijiekude Ibilisi Jialie kun Ximunyi kewon Yudai zhughede Ersai ghudandukui melieshise gie goudaghazho.
JOH 13:3 Ersa Adani duyani qienlii hhei khade jiuisanyi, goyaneshi Hudai hhense iresanyi, pse Hudai hhende echikui mejiene.
JOH 13:4 Ingie Ersa shire konse bosi ire jienne tei, kanzidene nie shoujinyi banla,
JOH 13:5 nie nienpen usui kiezhi ire, tujilane konyi waghasenu kanzidene banlasan shoujinghala caizhi ghoghawo.
JOH 13:6 Waghazhi Ximun-Bedurude kuzhese BeduruErsade kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi mini konni waghanu?"
JOH 13:7 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi giesanyi ede chi ulie mejienema, khuinashi mejiene."
JOH 13:8 Beduru kieliewo, "Chi mini konni jiedui waghazhi ulie olune." Ersa kieliewo, "Bi chii ulie waghase bi jienliesan guzide chi bei dane."
JOH 13:9 Ximun-Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, qinse gon konyimi bu wagha. Kha, qiorunyimi man wagha."
JOH 13:10 Ersa kieliewo, "Xizao giezhi daosan kun zinie konne waghase hunshenni man ganjin wo. Tashi ganjinni woma, manshi ganjinni pusho."
JOH 13:11 Ersa kien hhei ghudandukui melieshise mejiene. Ingiese "Tashi man ganjinni pusho." giezhi kieliewo.
JOH 13:12 Ersa hhelai konni waghazhi balu, jienne musidene pse souwo. Ingie hhelade kieliewo, "Bi tande giesanyi ta dunjirewoye?
JOH 13:13 Ta mini loushi, ezhan giezhi uruzho. Ta urusan oluzho. Bi enbene.
JOH 13:14 Bishi tai ezhan, loushi woma, tai konni waghawo. Taye nieniene konyi wagha.
JOH 13:15 Bi tande nie yanzi uzheghawo. Ta ye zhao bi tande giesan mutun giendu.
JOH 13:16 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, hoji ezhanse fugie uwo. Peizhi ireghasan kun peisan kunse fugie uwo.
JOH 13:17 Enei ta mejienema, ta ingiezhi giese tande fuqi wine.
JOH 13:18 Mini ene kielienshi ta manlai zhiizhi kieliesan pusho. Bi goyane kienyi sunghusei mejiene. Ingieliuzhe jinwun jieredu kielien bixi gholune, 'Mare hhantu ginan ijiesan kun konghalane mii qiuine.'
JOH 13:19 Ede shiqin da uye chenjikude bi tande xien kieliekushi shihou kuruse bishi hhe enbekui tai xianxin gieghane giezho.
JOH 13:20 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, kun bi peisan kunlai jienliese mii jienliezho. Mii jienliese mii peizhi ireghasan hhei jienliezho."
JOH 13:21 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliesenu zhughedene nango giezhi minminji kieliewo, "Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, tai dunda nie kun mii ghudandune."
JOH 13:22 Tujilani nieniene uzhezhi hhe kienyi kieliesei mejie dazho.
JOH 13:23 Tujilani dunda niekozishi Ersa oresan wo. Hhe Ersai kanzide souzho.
JOH 13:24 Ximun-Beduru hhe nie tujide qiorun jienjizhi, "Ezhan kienyi kieliezho?" giezhi asaghawo.
JOH 13:25 Hhe nie tuji Ersai kanzii shighadene asazho, "Ezhan, kien wine?"
JOH 13:26 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi goujinie ginanyi zhanjizhi kiende ogise hhe enbene." Ingiedene Ersa goujinie ginanyi zhanjisenu Jialie kun Ximunni kewon Yudade ogiwo.
JOH 13:27 Hhe jienliese Ibilisi hhei sudoro orowo. Ingiese Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Chi giekune ghujighan gie."
JOH 13:28 Shire konde hhantu sousan kunla hhende kieliesan ene kielienyi kiemada dunjire dawo.
JOH 13:29 Kunla sumulase Yuda baerni bareizho, Ersa hhende kieliesanshi hhe matande jieqi daoghaku dunxi agile echi giezho. Pse jiahui kunlade yama khugho giezho.
JOH 13:30 Yuda hhe ginanyi jienliedene deigo ghadane khizhi echiwo. Hhe xienzishi xieni wo.
JOH 13:31 Yuda khizhi echisenu Ersa kieliewo, "Ede Kunnikewonni kuaiku kuzhewo. Kunnikewonni tungo giezhi Hudaiye kuaiwo.
JOH 13:32 Huda Kunnikewonni tungo giezhi goyane kuaikui jienliese hheye goyai tungo giezhi Kunnikewonni kuaine. Ede kuaiku ghujinlazho.
JOH 13:33 Kesila, bi tanre hhantu biku shihou oloncha widazho. Khuinashi ta mii ereinema, bi echiku oronde ta echi dane. Ene kielienyi bi melieshi Yutai kunlade kieliezhi daozho. Ede tandeye ingiezhi kielieye.
JOH 13:34 Bi tande nie shini minlin ogiye, ta nieniedene orendu. Bi tande oresan mutun taye qingiezhi nieniedene orendu.
JOH 13:35 Ta nieniedene orese tashi mini tuji bikui kunla mejiene."
JOH 13:36 Ximun-BeduruErsade asawo, "Ezhan, chi khala echine?" Ersa kieliewo, "Bi echiku oronde chi ede echi dane. Khuinashi chi mii daghazhi echine."
JOH 13:37 Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi ede yale echizhi ulie olune? Bi chade aminne sheine."
JOH 13:38 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi made aminne sheinu? Bi chade shuhuajia kielieye, tigha kheilatula chi mii 3 hui ulie renjine."
JOH 14:1 "Ta zhughedene nango bu gie. Ta Hudai xianxin gie, miiye xianxin gie.
JOH 14:2 Adaimi giede souku oron olon wo. Uwoshi bi tande eqie kieliene. Bi echise tande oron zhunbei giele echine.
JOH 14:3 Bi echi tande oron zhunbei giedene pse ire tai hhende jienlie echine. Ingiese bi khalashi taye khala wo.
JOH 14:4 Bi echiku hhe moni ta mejiene."
JOH 14:5 DomaErsade kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi khala echikui bijien ulie mejiene. Hhe moni bijien matui mejiene?"
JOH 14:6 Ersa kieliewo, "Bishijiu mo wo, zhendao wo, amin wo. Mase tungo ulie giese kiemada Adai hhende echi dane.
JOH 14:7 Ta mii tanise Adaimiye taniwo. Enedu khuinashi ta hhei taniwo, ye chujieghewo."
JOH 14:8 FeiliErsade kieliewo, "Ezhan, bijiende Adai nie uzheghama, bijiende kuruwo."
JOH 14:9 Ersa kieliewo, "Feili, bi tanre hhantu imeghenicha oluzho. Chi da mii tani dazhou? Kun mii chujieghese Adaimi chujieghezho. Chi matugie 'Adai bijiende uzhegha.' giezhi kieliene?
JOH 14:10 Bi Adai sudoro wo, Ada mii sudoro bikui chi xianxin ulie gienu? Bi tande kieliesan kielienshi bi goyane kieliesan pusho. Mii sudoro sousan Adami goya wiliene giezho.
JOH 14:11 Bi Adai sudoro wo, Ada mini sudoro wo giesan ene kielienyi ta xianxin gie. Xianxin gie dase bi giesan wilielani uzhedene xianxin gie.
JOH 14:12 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, ede bi Adai hhende echine. Ingiese mii xianxin giesan kunla bi giesan wilielaiye gie shidane. Da enense fugie wiliei giene.
JOH 14:13 Ta mini niereghala yan xiahua giese bi tande yan gholughane. Ingiese Ada Kewonne jierese kuaikui jienliene.
JOH 14:14 Ta mini niereghala mase yan xiahua giese bi yan gholughane."
JOH 14:15 "Ta made orese mini minlinni zunji.
JOH 14:16 Bi Adasene xiahua giezhi tande da nie banjichen ireghaye. Hhe tanre chan hhantula gie.
JOH 14:17 Eneshi zhendaoni ruhher wo. Duyani kunla hhei chujieghe dane, taniye dane. Ingiese hhei jienlie dane. Ta hhei tani shidane. Hhe tanre hhantu souzho, tai sudoro wine.
JOH 14:18 Bi tai oliechen mutun bendazhi ulie jiene. Bi da tai shida irene.
JOH 14:19 Pse goujicha beise duyani kunla mini chujieghe danema, ta mini chujieghene. Bi amitu wo, taye amitu wo.
JOH 14:20 Hhe niudu kuse bi Adai sudoro wo, ta mii sudoro wo, biye tai sudoro bikui ta mejiene.
JOH 14:21 Kien mini minlinyi jienliezhi zunjise made orezho. Made orese Adamiye hhende orene. Biye hhende orezhi goyane xienjighane."
JOH 14:22 YudaErsade asazho (Ene Yudashi Jialie kun Yuda pusho), "Ezhan, chi bijiende xienjighane, duyani kunlade yale ulie xienjighane?"
JOH 14:23 Ersa kieliewo, "Kun made orese mini kielienyi zunjine. Adamiye hhende orene. Bi Adaghalane hhei hhende echidene hhantu soune.
JOH 14:24 Made ulie orechen kun mini kielienyi ulie zunjine. Ta sonosusan kielienshi minughun pusho, mini peizhi ireghasan Adaimi kielien wo."
JOH 14:25 "Ene kielienlai bi tanre hhantu bikude tande kieliewo.
JOH 14:26 Banjichen giezhi urusan Shenlin irese shiqinlai man tande surughane, bi tande kieliesan kielienlai man sumula ireghane. Hheshi Ada mini niereghala peizhi ireghasan wo.
JOH 14:27 Bi tande pinnan ogiye. Goya pinnanne tande ogiye. Bi ogisan pinnanshi duyani kunla ogisan pinnanyi buxian wo. Ta zhughedene munan bu gie, ye bu ayi.
JOH 14:28 Bi yolane, pse tai enende irene giesan ene kielienyi ta chenliezhi daozho. Ta made orese bi Adai hhende echise ta bayasune. Ada mase fugie wo.
JOH 14:29 Ede shiqinla da uye gholukude bi xien tande kieliewo. Ingiezhi giese shiqin gholukudeni tai xianxin gieghane giezho."
JOH 14:30 "Ene duyani touzi ede irewo. Ingiese bi tanre kielien kielieku shihou oloncha widazho. Hhe mini yama gie danema,
JOH 14:31 ingieliuzhe bi Adadene oresei, pse Adami made matugiezhi fenfulase bi qingiezhi giesei duyani kunlade mejieghane. Bosizhe! Matan yoye."
JOH 15:1 "Bishi zhen putou mutun wo. Adamishi zeilasan kun wo.
JOH 15:2 Hhe mii jiere alima ulie sousan chalai man ghigha widaghane. Alima souku chalai ulou giezhi goudaghase hhei jiere alima pse olon soughane.
JOH 15:3 Ta bi jianjisan kielienghala ijin ganjinshiwo.
JOH 15:4 Ta mii sudoro bei. Biye tai sudoro beine. Chala mutun jiere uwoshi goyane alima sou dane. Ta mii sudoro ulie beiseye niekielien wo.
JOH 15:5 Bishi putou mutun wo. Tashi chala wo. Kien mii sudoro beizhi bi hhei sudoro beise hhe alima olon soune. Mase likai giese ta yama gie dane.
JOH 15:6 Kun mini sudoro ulie beise bendadene ghosan chala niekielien wo. Kunla hhei qianguzhi echise khande tulie widaghane.
JOH 15:7 Ta mini sudoro beizhi mini kielien tai sudoro beise ta yan xiahua giezhi kerese tande man gholughane.
JOH 15:8 Ta alima olon souzhi mini tuji gholuse Adademi kuaiku irene.
JOH 15:9 Adami made oreku mutun biye tande orezho. Ta mini oreku sudoro bei.
JOH 15:10 Ta mii minlinyi zunjise mii oreku sudoro beizho. Eneshi bi Adane minlinyi zunjizhi hhei oreku sudoro beikughala niekielien wo."
JOH 15:11 "Bi enezighan kielienyi tande kieliese mii bayasukughala tai bayasughane. Tai fugiede bayasughane.
JOH 15:12 Bi tande oreku mutun ta nieniedene orendu. Eneshi mini minlin wo.
JOH 15:13 Kun zhanliendene aminne sheise, ene orekuse fugieni uwo.
JOH 15:14 Bi fenfulasan minlinyi ta zunjise tashi mini zhanlien wo.
JOH 15:15 Bi tai pse hoji giezhi ulie urune. Ezhanyi wiliei hojila ulie mejiene. Bi tai zhanlien danlaghazho. Bi Adane hhense chenliezhi iresanlai tande man mejieghawo.
JOH 15:16 Ta mini sunghusan pusho, bi tai sunghusan wo. Bi tai peizhi chanqiku alimai soughale echiwo. Ingiese ta mini niereghala yan xiahua giese Adami tande ogine.
JOH 15:17 Ta nieniedene orendu. Eneshi mini minlin wo."
JOH 15:18 "Duyai kunla tai henjise ta mejiendu. Mii tanse melieshi henjizho.
JOH 15:19 Ta duyaghunshi duyani kunla tande orenema, ta duyaghun pusho. Bi tai duyase sunghuwo. Ingiese duya tai henjine.
JOH 15:20 Hoji ezhanse fugie uwo giezhi bi tande kieliesan ene kielienyi jila. Hhela mini heise taiye heine. Hhela mii kielienyi zunjizhi giese tai kielienyiye zunjizhi giene.
JOH 15:21 Hhela mini yenyinghala tande ingiezhi giezho. Hhela mini peizhi ireghasan Hhei tani dazho.
JOH 15:22 Bi irezhi hhelade uye kieliezhoshi hhelade zui uwo. Ede hhelade zui uwo giezhi kielie dane.
JOH 15:23 Mini henjise Adaimiye henjizho.
JOH 15:24 Bi hhelai dunda kiema gie dasei ese giezhoshi hhelade zui uwoma, ede hhela bi adamighalai chanladene henjizho.
JOH 15:25 Ene hhelai jinwun jiere huaisan kielien mutun gholuwo, 'Hhela mii uyenwuguji henjizho.'"
JOH 15:26 "Bi Adane hhense banjichenyi peizhi ireghane. Hheshi Adai hhense iresan zhendaoni ruhher wo. Hhe irese made ganzhen beine.
JOH 15:27 Taye made ganzhen beine. Ta kaishi giesanse izhi bighala hhantu wo."
JOH 16:1 "Bi tande enezighan shiqinyi kieliese tai zhughei ulie gojiolughane giezho.
JOH 16:2 Kunla tai huitanse tou khighane. Shihou kuzhese tai alachen kunla ingiezhi giese Hudai shunjizho giezhi sumulane.
JOH 16:3 Hhela ingiezhi giekushi Adai tani dane, miiye tani dane.
JOH 16:4 Bi enezighan shiqinyi tande kieliekushi shihou kuzhese bi tande kieliezhi daosanyi sumulazhi ireghane giezho. Melieshi bi tanre hhantushi ene shiqinyi tande ese kieliezho."
JOH 16:5 "Ede bi mini peizhi ireghasan Adai hhende echinema, tai dunda chi khala echine giezhi made asachen kun nieda uwo.
JOH 16:6 Kharei bi enezighan shiqinyi tande kieliese ta zhughedene hende nango giezho.
JOH 16:7 Bi tande shuhua kielieye, bi echise tande kharei gou wo. Bi ulie echise banjichen tai enende ulie irene. Bi echise hhei tande peizhi ireghane.
JOH 16:8 Hhe irese zui fanmiende, gundanni fanmiende, panjiku fanmiende duyani codasei kheilane.
JOH 16:9 Zuini fanmiende kieliekushi hhela mini xianxin ese giewo.
JOH 16:10 Gundanni fanmiende kieliekushi bi Adai hhende echise ta mini chanla dane.
JOH 16:11 Panjikuni fanmiende kieliekushi ene duyani touzini ijin panjiwo."
JOH 16:12 "Bi tande kielieku shiqin da olon woma, ta ede jienlie dane.
JOH 16:13 Zhendaoni ruhher irese tai uduruzhi soyuji zhendaode echighane. Hhe kieliesanshi goyane sumulasan pusho. Hhe chenliesanlane tande kieliene. Khuinashiku shiqinlaiye tande mejieghane.
JOH 16:14 Hhe mase chenliesanlane man tande kieliezhi ogine. Ingiese made kuaiku irene.
JOH 16:15 Adaghunshi man minughun wo. Ingiese hhe mase chenliesanlane man tande kieliezhi ogine giezhi bi kieliewo."
JOH 16:16 "Goujicha beise ta mini chujieghe dane. Pse goujicha beise ta mini chujieghene."
JOH 16:17 Ingiese giedun tujila nieniedene kieliezho, "Hhe matande yan kieliezho? 'Goujicha beise matan hhei chujieghe dane. Pse goujicha beise matan hhei chujieghene.' Da bi Adai hhende echine giesan eneshi yan isi wo?"
JOH 16:18 Pse kieliezho, "Hhe kieliesan goujichashi yan isi wo? Matan hhe kieliesan kielienyi dunjire dawo."
JOH 16:19 Ersa hhela asane giesei mejiedene kieliewo, "Bi kieliesan goujicha beise ta mini pse chujieghe dane, pse goujicha beise ta mini chujieghene giesan ene kielienghala ta nieniedene asaduzhou?
JOH 16:20 Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, ta nango giezhi hende wilane, duyani kunla bayasune. Ta nango gienema, tai nango bayasukui gholune.
JOH 16:21 Biereila oluku shihou kuzhese munan giene. Hhe kewosini oluse otusanlai mata widaghane. Hhe duyade nie kewosi oluse hende bayasune.
JOH 16:22 Ta ede munan giezhoma, bi tai pse chujieghene. Qingiese ta bayasune. Ene bayasukui kiemada agizhi echi dane.
JOH 16:23 Hhe niudu kuse ta made yama ulie asane. Bi tande shuhuajia kielieye, ta mini niereghala yan xiahua giese Adami tande ogine.
JOH 16:24 Eli kutula ta mini niereghala yama xiahua uye giewo. Ta xiahua gie, tande ogine. Ta hende bayasune."
JOH 16:25 "Ene kielienlai bi tande bilazhi kieliewo. Shihou kuzhese bi pse tande bilazhi ulie kieliene. Adai shiqinyi tande mindaminji kieliezhi ogine.
JOH 16:26 Hhe niudude ta mini niereghala xiahua giene. Eneshi bi tande oluzhi Adade xiahua gieku isi pusho.
JOH 16:27 Ta made orezho, pse bishi Adai hhense ireseiye xianxin giezho. Ingiese Ada goyane tande orezho.
JOH 16:28 Bi Adai hhense khizhezhi duyade irewo. Pse duyase likai giezhi Adai hhende echine."
JOH 16:29 Tujila kieliewo, "Ede chi mindaminji kieliezho, bilazhi uye kieliezho.
JOH 16:30 Chi yanniliuzhe mejiekui bijien ede mejiene. Kunla chade asaku biyoye uwo. Eneghala bijien chishi Hudai hhense iresei xianxin giezho."
JOH 16:31 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta ede xianxin giezhou?
JOH 16:32 Uzhe, ta sandazhi goya oronladene echiku shihou kuzhene, shijishan ede kuzhewo. Ta mini niezheghan benda jiene. Bi niezheghanne pusho, Adaghalane hhantu wo.
JOH 16:33 Bi ene kielienyi kieliekushi ta mii tungo giezhi pinnanyi jienlieghane giezho. Ta duyade shouku gienema, zhughene khidunde gie! Bi duyani injiwo!"
JOH 17:1 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliedene qiorunne qila asiman jiere uzhe kieliewo, "Ada, shihou kuruwo. Chi Kewone kuai, ingiese Kewonye chii kuaine.
JOH 17:2 Chi Kewondene ogisan kunlade chanqiku aminni ogine giezhi soyuji kunlai man gonjiku qienlii hhende ogizho.
JOH 17:3 Niekozi zhen Hudai tanizhi hhe peizhi ireghasan Ersa Mexihani tanise chanqiku amin enbene.
JOH 17:4 Chi made fenfulasan wiliei bi onchen giezhi ene zemin jierese chade kuaikui ireghawo.
JOH 17:5 Ada, ede chii melie made famani ogi. Duyase melie matan hhantu xianshou giesan famani made ogi."
JOH 17:6 "Chi duya jierese made ogisan kunlade bi chii nierei mejieghawo. Hhela benshenshi chinughun wo. Chi hhelai made ogiwo. Hhelaye chini kielienyi zunjiwo.
JOH 17:7 Ede hhela chi made ogisanshi man chii hhense iresanyi mejiewo.
JOH 17:8 Chi made ogisan kielienyi bi hhelade ogise hhela jienliewo. Hhela bishi chii hhense iresanyi mejiewo. Chi mini peizhi ireghasanyiye xianxin giewo."
JOH 17:9 "Bi hhelade oluzhi onxian giezho. Duyani kunlade oluzhi onxian ese giezho. Hhelashi chinughun wo. Ingiese chi made ogisan kunlade bi onxian giezho.
JOH 17:10 Minughunshi man chinughun wo. Chinughunshi minughun wo. Hhelai jierese made kuaikui irezho.
JOH 17:11 Enense khuinashi bi duyade uwo. Hhela duyade wine. Bi chii hhende echine. Zhiguitu Ada, chi made ogisan niereghalane hhelai baohu giezhi matan mutun hhelai niekozi gholugha.
JOH 17:12 Bi hhelare hhantu bikude chi made ogisan niereghalane bi hhelai baohu giezhi ezheliezho. Chugo hhe widaku kunse andase pse nieda ulie widane. Ene jinwun jieredu kielien mutun gholuwo."
JOH 17:13 "Ede bi chii hhende echine. Bi duyade bikudeni mii bayasukughala hhelai bayasughane giezhi enezighan kielienlai kieliewo.
JOH 17:14 Bi chii kielienyi hhelade ogidene duya hhelai henjiwo. Ene yenyinshi bi duyanughun pusho mutun hhelashiye duyanughun pusho.
JOH 17:15 Hhelai, 'Duyase khizhegha!' giezhi bi chii xiahua ulie giene, 'Hhe doghunnise baohu!' gie giezhi xiahua giene.
JOH 17:16 Bi duyanughun pusho mutun hhelaye duyanughun pusho.
JOH 17:17 Zhendaoghala zuise hhelai zhiguishigha. Chii kielienshijiu zhendao wo.
JOH 17:18 Chi mii duyade peizhi ireghasan mutun bi hhelaiye qingiezhi duyade peizhi echighane.
JOH 17:19 Bi hhelade oluzhi goyane zhiguishighawo. Ingiese hhelaiye zhendaoi tungo giezhi zhiguishighane."
JOH 17:20 "Bi zinie enelade oluzhi onxian gieku pusho. Hhelai kielienyi chenliedene mii xianxin giesan kunladeye onxian giezho.
JOH 17:21 Bi onxian giese Ada mii sudoro wo, bi chii sudoro biku mutun, hhelaye matanyi sudoro nie gholu gie. Ingiese duyai kunlai chi mii peizhi ireghasanyi xianxin giegha."
JOH 17:22 "Chi made ogisan famani bi hhelade ogiwo. Ingiese hhelai matan mutun nie gholughane.
JOH 17:23 Bi hhelai sudoro wo, Chi mii sudoro wo, hhelai man nie gholughane. Ingiese duyai kunlai chi mii peizhi ireghasanyi, pse chi made oresan mutun hhelade oresanyi mejieghane.
JOH 17:24 Ada, chi made ogisan hhela bi khalashi khala bizhi mii famani hhelade uzhegha. Ene mienzishi duyai zhayaghaku melie chi made orezhi ogisan wo."
JOH 17:25 "Gundantu Ada, duyai kunla chii tani dane. Bi chii tanine. Enezighan tujila chi mii peizhi ireghasanyi mejiene.
JOH 17:26 Bi hhelade chii mejieghawo, izhi mejieghane. Ingiese chi made oresan hhelai sudoro wo, biye hhelai sudoro wo."
JOH 18:1 Ersa enezighan kielienyi kieliedene tujilarene hhantu khizhi echiwo. Hhela Jilun ghonni daodene nie yenzide orowo.
JOH 18:2 Ersa tujilarene chan hhe nie oronde hhantulazho. Ersai ghudandusan Yudaye hhe oronyi mejiene.
JOH 18:3 Yuda idaban Loma buduilai uduruzhi hhende irewo. Fugie buwa, Falisai kunla peisan mechini sagheisan kunlaye hhantu irezho. Hhela denlun, hoba, uqilai bareizho.
JOH 18:4 Ersa goyadene yan wilie kuzhekui man mejiene. Ingie khizhedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta kienyi ereizho?"
JOH 18:5 Hhela kieliewo, "Nasale kun Ersai ereizho." Ersa kieliewo, "Bi enbene." Ersai ghudandusan Yudaye hhelare hhantu beizho.
JOH 18:6 Ersa "Bi enbene." giezhi kieliekude hhela khuina tuidene zemin jiere unawo.
JOH 18:7 Ersa pse hhelade asawo, "Ta kienyi ereizho?" Hhela kieliewo, "Nasale kun Ersai ereizho."
JOH 18:8 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi enbene giezhi tande kieliewo. Ta mini ereizhoshi enelai yolagha."
JOH 18:9 Eneshi chi made ogisan kunlai bi nieda ese widaghawo giesan Ersa melieshi kieliesan kielien mutun gholuwo.
JOH 18:10 Ingiekude Ximun-Beduru nie khudogho bareizho. Lai khizhe zui fugie buwai hojii borun chighinyi chizhi agiwo. Hhe hojini nierei Malegu giene.
JOH 18:11 ErsaBedurude kieliewo, "Khudoghone xiuzide orogha. Adami made ogisan ene kuni bi ulie shouise olunu?"
JOH 18:12 Ingiese budui, qienfuzhan, Yutai kunni mechini sagheisan kunla Ersai barei banladene
JOH 18:13 Yanasii melie xien lai echighawo. Yanasishi hhe niehonyi zui fugie buwa danlasan Gaiyafani ghadun wo.
JOH 18:14 Ene Gaiyafashi melieshi Yutai kunlade ijien qilazhi "Nie kun bexinlade oluzhi fuguse haochu wine." giezhi kieliesan hhe kun wo.
JOH 18:15 Ximun-Beduru da nie tujighala Ersai daghazho. Hhe tuji zui fugie buwai tanine. Ingiese daghazhi zui fugie buwai ghoronde orowo.
JOH 18:16 Beduru damen ghadane beizho. Zui fugie buwai taniku hhe tuji khizhe damen sagheisan oqinde nie kieliese Bedurui oroghawo.
JOH 18:17 Wijien sagheisan hoji oqin Bedurude kieliewo, "Chiye hhei tuji pushonu?" Beduru kieliewo, "Pusho."
JOH 18:18 Hhe xienzide qienqi kuiqienshi hoji, mechini sagheisan kunla hhantu khan teidene beizhi kouizho. Beduruye hhelare hhantu beidene kouizho.
JOH 18:19 Ingiese zui fugie buwa Ersade tujilaini, sughasanlaini shenwun giezho.
JOH 18:20 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi kunlade mindaminji kieliezho. Bi chan huitande, mechide kunlade surughazho. Bi ghulazhi yama ese kieliezho.
JOH 18:21 Chi made yangiezhi asane? Asase chenliesan kunlade asale echi. Bi yan kieliesanyi hhela man mejiene."
JOH 18:22 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliese shidani beisan nie mechini sagheisan kun khaghalane Ersai eghizhi kieliewo, "Chi zui fugie buwade imutu kielien kielienu?"
JOH 18:23 Ersa kieliewo, "Bi kieliesan ese oluse chi kieliezhi mejiegha. Bi kieliesan oluzhoshi chi mini yangiezhi eghizho?"
JOH 18:24 Ingiese YanasiErsai banlaghadene zui fugie buwa Gaiyafai hhende echighawo.
JOH 18:25 Ximun-Beduru zhen beizhi khan xiekude nie kun hhende kieliewo, "Chiye hhei tuji pushonu?" Beduru bi pusho giezhi ese renjiwo.
JOH 18:26 Da nie zui fugie buwai hojishi Beduru chighinyini chizhi bouzheghasan hhei qingu wo. Hhe kieliewo, "Bi chii Ersare hhantu yenzide bisei ese chanlawu?"
JOH 18:27 Beduru pse ese renjiwo. Deigo tigha kheilawo.
JOH 18:28 Eqiemagha eqie Ersai Gaiyafai hhense Loma kunyi shenzhanfude echighawo. Hhela goyane shenzhanfude ese orowo. Orose zannantukuse ayizho. Jiulidaosan Jieni xini ijie dane.
JOH 18:29 Bilado khizhedene hhelade kieliewo, "Ta ene kunyi yan shiqinde zhazho?"
JOH 18:30 Hhela kieliewo, "Ene kun zui ulie fanjise bijien chade ulie ireghane."
JOH 18:31 Bilado kieliewo, "Ta hhei uduru echi. Zhao goyane guijinghala panji." Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Bijiende kun alaku qienli uwo."
JOH 18:32 Eneshi Ersa melieshida goyane matui fugukune kieliesan kielien mutun gholuwo.
JOH 18:33 Bilado pse shenzhanfude orodene Ersai uru ire hhende asawo, "Chishi Yutai kunni honshan onu?"
JOH 18:34 Ersa kieliewo, "Ene kielienshi chi goyane kieliesan onu, kunla mii kieliesan wo?"
JOH 18:35 Bilado kieliewo, "Chi sumulase bishi Yutai kun wo giezhou? Tai gojiai kunla, fugie buwala chii made jiuizhi ogizho. Chi yan giewo?"
JOH 18:36 Ersa kieliewo, "Mini gojiashi ene duyaghun pusho. Mini gojia ene duyaghunshi mini hojila made oluzhi zhan eghizhi mii Yutai kunlade jiuizhi ulie ogine. Mini gojiashi ene duyaghun pusho."
JOH 18:37 Bilado hhende kieliewo, "Ingiese chishi honshan onu?" Ersa kieliewo, "Bishi honshan wo giezhi chi kieliezho. Mii oluzhi duyade iresanshi zhendaode ganzhen beine giezho. Zhendaode beisan kunla mini kielienyi chenliene."
JOH 18:38 Bilado kieliewo, "Zhendaoshi yan wo?" Ene kielienyi kieliedene pse khizhesenu Yutai kunlai hhende echi kieliewo, "Bi hhei zuini chaizhi khizhe dawo.
JOH 18:39 Tai nie xigonshi Jiulidaosan Jiede bi nie kun andaghane. Tande Yutai kunni honshanyi tei giezhou?"
JOH 18:40 Ingiese hhela pse waradazhi kieliewo, "Bijien ene kunyi ulie kerene! Balabai kerene!" Balabashi nie panlon giesan kun wo.
JOH 19:1 Ingiedene Bilado mabienzighala Ersai eghighawo.
JOH 19:2 Buduila eghesunyi maghala onjidene qiorun jierei zhoghazhi zishei fudu jienyi musighawo.
JOH 19:3 Ingie shidani echi kieliewo, "Yutai kunni honshan, onsui!" Ingiedene khaghalane eghizho.
JOH 19:4 Bilado pse khizhedene bexinlade kieliewo, "Uzhe, bi hhei uduruzhi tai melie khizheghaye. Bi hhense yama zui chaizhi khizhe dasei ta mejiendu."
JOH 19:5 Ingiese Ersa khizhewo. Eghesun maghala zhozho. Zishei fudu jien musizho. Bilado hhelade kieliewo, "Uzhe, ene kun wo."
JOH 19:6 Fugie buwa, mechini sagheisan kunla hhei chanlasenu waradazhi kieliewo, "Hhei shizijia jiere ghada! Shizijia jiere ghada!" Ingiese Bilado kieliewo, "Ta goyalane hhei shizijia jiere ghadale echi. Bi hhei zuiini chaizhi khizhe dawo."
JOH 19:7 Ingiese Yutai kunla kieliewo, "Bijiende guijin wine. Zhao guijin mutunshi hhe fugukuni wo. Hhe goyane Hudai kewon wo giezho."
JOH 19:8 Bilado ene kielienyi sonosudene genjia ayizho.
JOH 19:9 Ingie shenzhanfude orosenu Ersade asawo, "Chishi khalase iresan wo?" Ersa yama huida ese giewo.
JOH 19:10 Bilado kieliewo, "Chi made kielien ulie kielienu? Made chii andaghaku, shizijia jiere ghadaku qienli bikui chi ulie mejienu?"
JOH 19:11 Ersa kieliewo, "Asiman jierese chade qienli ese ogizhoshi chi mii yama gie dane. Ingiese mii chade jiuisan hhe kunde zui pse gundu wo."
JOH 19:12 Enense khuinashi BiladoErsai andaghane giezho. Yutai kunla waradazhi kieliewo, "Chi ene kunyi andaghase Kaisa honshanni goude ese zunjizho. Kien goyane honshan giezhi kieliese Kaisa honshanyi ghudanduwo giezho."
JOH 19:13 Bilado ene kielienyi sonosudene Ersai laizhi khizhesenu shenpantai jiere souwo. Sousan hhe oronyi Puisan Tashi giene. Xibolai kielienghala Jiabada giene.
JOH 19:14 Hhe niudushi Jiulidaosan Jieni zhunbei giesan uduni udukun xienzi wo. BiladoYutai kunlade kieliewo. "Uzhe, eneshi tai honshan wo."
JOH 19:15 Hhela waradazhi kieliewo, "Hhei widagha! Hhei widagha! Shizijia jiere ghada!" Bilado kieliewo, "Bi tai honshanyi shizijia jiere ghadase olunu?" Fugie buwala kieliewo, "Kaisa honshanse andase bijiende honshan uwo."
JOH 19:16 Ingiese BiladoErsai hhelade jiuizhi shizijia jiere ghada giewo. Hhela Ersai laidene echiwo.
JOH 19:17 Ersa goyane shizijiai beiliezhi khizhedene qiorun yasun oron giezhi urusan nie oronde echiwo. Xibolai kielienghala kieliese Gegeta giene.
JOH 19:18 Hhende Ersai shizijia jiere ghadawo. Da ghua kunyi niemiendei nie ghadawo. Ersa dunda wo.
JOH 19:19 Bilado nie peizi huaidene shizijia jiere guaighawo. Huaisanshi Nasale kun ErsaYutai kunni honshan giezho.
JOH 19:20 Ersai ghadasan oron chenshise gholo uwo. Peizi jiere huaisanshi Xibolai, Loma, Xilani uroughala huaizho. Ingiese olon Yutai kunla peizi jiere huaisei onshizho.
JOH 19:21 Yutai kunni fugie buwala Biladode kieliewo, "'Yutai kunni honshan' giezhi bu huai. Huaise, 'Ene kun goya bishi Yutai kunni honshan wo giezho.' giezhi huai."
JOH 19:22 Ingiese Bilado kieliewo, "Bi huaikune huai baraghawo."
JOH 19:23 Buduila Ersai shizijia jiere ghadasenu jienyini agi bouzhe jieran gholughadene nie kunde nie ghughawo. Pse sudorodu jienyini agise hhe jiendeni hudusan oron uwo. Jiere dourashi hulun giesan wo.
JOH 19:24 Hhela nieniedene kieliewo, "Matan sidazhi bu keighaye. Kiende irekui matan fendan qianguye." Ingiedene jinwun jieredu kielien mutun gholuwo, "Hhela mini jienni ghughane. Mii sudorodu jienni fendan qiangune." Buduila zhenzhenji ingiezhi giewo.
JOH 19:25 Ersai shizijia shida beisan kun dunda Ersai anani, inianni, Gelobani bierei Mereiyen, Modalani Mereiyen wine.
JOH 19:26 Ersa anani, oresan tujini kanzide beisanyi chanladene anadene kieliewo, "Ana, eneshi chii kewon wo."
JOH 19:27 Pse hhe tujidene kieliewo, "Uzhe, eneshi chii ana wo!" Enense khuinashi hhe tuji anaini jienliezhi giedene echiwo.
JOH 19:28 Enense khuinashi Ersa shiqinlane gie baraghasanyi mejiedene jinwun jieredu kielienyi gholughane giezhi kieliewo, "Bi undasuzho."
JOH 19:29 Cui zhonlozhi durughasan tantanyi hhende jiezho. Hhela haimienni cude zhanjidene osun gangan jiere banla, amandeni echighawo.
JOH 19:30 Ingiese Ersa cui ochidene kieliewo, "Chenjiwo!" Ingiedene qiorunne ghodeise ho sirawo.
JOH 19:31 Ene udushi Yutai kunla hhamuraku udude zhunbei gieku udu wo. Pse ene faku hhamuraku udushi nie fugie udu wo. Ingiese Yutai kunla Biladoi xiahua giezhi hhelai shigharai eghizhi ghuraghadene agi widagha giezho. Hhamuraku udude fugusan kunyi shizijia jiere jiese gou uwo giezho.
JOH 19:32 Ingiese buduila iredene Ersare hhantu ghadasan hhe ghua kunyi shigharai eghizhi ghuraghawo.
JOH 19:33 Ingie Ersai shida ire nie uzhese hhe duya ijiezho. Hhei shigharaini eghizhi uye ghuraghawo.
JOH 19:34 Ingiese niekozi budui zhidaghala leibadeni nie chujise chusun, usu usuru khizhewo.
JOH 19:35 Ene shiqinyi qinsi uzhesan kun ganzhen beizhi tai xianxin gieghane giezho. Hhe beisan ganzhenshi zhenni wo. Goyane kieliesanshi zhenni bikui mejiene.
JOH 19:36 Ene shiqinla fashen giekushi jinwun jieredu kielienyi gholughane giezho, "Hhei yasun nieda ulie ghurane."
JOH 19:37 Dou nie jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Hhela goya chujisan kunne uzhene."
JOH 19:38 Enense khuinashi Ersani nie tuji Yalimatai kun Yusufu giene. Hhe Yutai kunlase ayise ghulazhi tuji danlazho. Hhe Biladoi xiahua giezhi Ersai beyei kerezho. Bilado tunyi oluse Ersai beyeni agi echiwo.
JOH 19:39 Melieshi xienidei Ersai ochirale iresan Nigedemuye huighasan guizhuntu caoye, luhuini 65 jin bareizhi irewo.
JOH 19:40 Hhela zhao Yutai kunni bulaku xigonghala Ersai beyeni bosi xianshuighala boui goudaghawo.
JOH 19:41 Ersai shizijia jiere ghadasan oronde nie yenzi wine. Yenzide nie shini alimatu meza wine. Kun teizhi uye daozho.
JOH 19:42 Hhe niudushi Yutai kunlai zhunbei gieku udu wo. Pse hhe meza chadashi hhela Ersai hhende bulawo.
JOH 20:1 Xinqini eqiemagha udu da khara bikude Modalani Mereiyen mezade irewo. Nie uzhese tashi meza kouzise noi daozho.
JOH 20:2 Ingie holuzhi echidene Ximun-Beduru, Ersa oresan tujide kieliewo, "Kunla mezase Ezhanni agi echizho. Khala jiesanyi ulie mejiene."
JOH 20:3 Ingiese Beduru hhe tujighala khizhe mezai hhende echiwo.
JOH 20:4 Hhe ghuala hhantu holuzho. Hhe tuji Beduruse holuzhi ghujinshi xien mezade kuruwo.
JOH 20:5 Ghodeidene sudoro nie uzhese bosii hhende jiesanyi chanlawoma, orozhi ese echiwo.
JOH 20:6 Ingie Ximun-Beduru khuinasei kuzhi ire mezade orowo. Bosini hhende jiesanyi chanlawo.
JOH 20:7 Pse Ersai qiorunni huisan toujin bosighala hhantu ese jiezhi niemiende horo jiesei chanlawo.
JOH 20:8 Ingiedene melieshi kuzhi iresan hhe tujiye mezade orozhi echi uzhedene xianxin giewo.
JOH 20:9 Hhela Ersa fugusan kun dundase aminne olune giesan jinwun jieredu ene kielienyini dunjire dazho.
JOH 20:10 Ingiedene ghua tujila sousan orondene echiwo.
JOH 20:11 Mereiyen meza ghadane beizhi wilazho. Wilakudeni ghodei mezade nie uzhese
JOH 20:12 ghua chighan jien musisan qienxienyi chanlawo. Ersai teisan oronde souzho. Nie qiorun konde wo, nie kon konde wo.
JOH 20:13 Hhela Mereiyende asawo, "Funi, chi yangiezhi wilazho?" Hhe kieliewo, "Kunla mii Ezhanyi agi echizho, khala jiesei ulie mejiene."
JOH 20:14 Ene kielienyi kieliesenu ochira daozhese Ersa hhende beisei chanlawoma, Ersa bikui ulie mejiene.
JOH 20:15 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Funi, chi yangiezhi wilazho? Kienyi ereizho?" MereiyenErsai yenzi sagheisan kun wo giezhi asawo, "Gujiu, chi hhei noighazhi khala jiezhoshi made kielie. Bi agile echiye."
JOH 20:16 Ersa kieliewo, "Mereiyen!" Mereiyen ochiradene Xibolai kielienghala hhende kieliewo, "Laboni!" Labonii isishi 'loushi' wo.
JOH 20:17 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi mii bu barei. Bi da adane hhende ese khireizho. Chi echidene mii gaijiulade bi adane hhende khireine giezhi kielie. Hheshi tai adaye enbene, mii Huda wo, tai Hudaye enbene."
JOH 20:18 Modalani Mereiyen echidene tujilade kieliewo, "Bi Ezhanyi chujieghewo!" Pse Ezhan hhende kieliesan kielienlai hhelade kieliewo.
JOH 20:19 Xinqini yen hhe uduni xienidei tujila hhantulasan oronde Yutai kunlase ayise wijienlane khazho. Ersa hhelai dunda ire beizhi kieliewo, "Ta pinnan onu?"
JOH 20:20 Ene kielienyi kieliesenu hhelade kha, leibane uzheghawo. Tujila Ezhanyi chanladene bayasuzho.
JOH 20:21 Ingie Ersa pse hhelade kieliewo, "Ta pinnan onu? Adami mii peisan mutun biye tai peine."
JOH 20:22 Ene kielienyi kieliedene hhelade nie feiliesenu kieliewo, "Ta Shenlinyi jienliendu.
JOH 20:23 Ta kienyi zuini mienliese kienyi zui widane, kienyi zuini ulie mienliese kienyi zui ulie widane."
JOH 20:24 12 gie tuji dundadu Shongo giezhi urusan DomaErsa irekudeni hhelare hhantu uwo.
JOH 20:25 Psedu tujila hhende kieliewo, "Bijien Ezhanyi chujieghewo!" Doma kieliewo, "Bi hhei kha jieredu ghadasan oronyini, leibade chujisan oronyini ulie uzhetula xianxin ulie giene."
JOH 20:26 Neimudu daodene hhei tujilani pse giedera hhantulazho. Domaye hhelare hhantu wo. Wijienlai man khazhoma, Ersa iredene hhelai dunda beizhi kieliewo, "Ta pinnan onu?"
JOH 20:27 Ingie Domade kieliewo, "Khaghurunne enende teizhi mii khai uzhe. Khane khizheghazhi mii leibai moizhi uzhe. Inxin bu gie, xianxin gie."
JOH 20:28 Doma kieliewo, "Mii Ezhan, mii Huda!"
JOH 20:29 Ersa kieliewo, "Chi mii uzhedene xianxin gienu? Ese uzhedene xianxin giesan kunlade fuqi wine."
JOH 20:30 Ersa tujilai melie ene shu jiere uye jilasan ghudureqi da olon xienjighawoma,
JOH 20:31 enende jilasanlashi Ersashi Hudai Kewon Mexiha bikui tai xianxin gieghane giezhi pse xianxin giedene hhei niereghala tande amin ireghane giezhi huaizho.
JOH 21:1 Ene shiqinse khuinashi ErsaQibiliyahai bienzide tujiladene pse chujiegheghawo. Hhe matugie chujiegheghasei doura huaizho.
JOH 21:2 Ximun-Beduru, Shongo giezhi urusan Doma, Jialilini Jiana kun Nadanye, Xibitaini kewonla, pse ghua tuji enela man hhantu wo.
JOH 21:3 Ximun-Beduru hhelade kieliewo, "Bi zhaghasun bareile echine." Hhela kieliewo. "Bijienye chare hhantu yoye." Hhela khizhi echisenu chon jiere khiwo. Hhe xii hhela yama barei dazho.
JOH 21:4 Ogheine giekude Ersa haibienzide beizho. Tujila hheshi Ersa bikui ulie mejiene.
JOH 21:5 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Zhanlienla, ta zhaghasun bareiwoye?" Hhela kieliewo, "Uye."
JOH 21:6 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta onni chonni borun miende teima, zhaghasun barei shidane." Ingiese hhela onni chonyi borun miende teiwo. Zhaghasun texien olon, laizhi khizhe dazho.
JOH 21:7 Ersa oresan hhe nie tuji Bedurude kieliewo, "Hheshi Ezhan wo!" Hhe shihoude Beduru jien ese musizho. Ezhan wo giezhi nie sonosuse jienne pixilie hude jiuli bouwo.
JOH 21:8 Psedu tujila haibienzise gholo uwo, chabudu 100 mi wine. Chon jiere soudene nie on zhaghasunyi laizhi daozhewo.
JOH 21:9 Hhela bienzide khisenu nie duizi mutan khan chujieghewo. Khan jiere zhaghasun teizho, ginanye wine.
JOH 21:10 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ta jian bareisan zhaghasunsene giedun agi daozhe."
JOH 21:11 Ximun-Beduru chon shida echidene onni laizhi bienzide khizheghawo. Onde fugie zhaghasun duruzho, 153 gie wine. Ingieliuzhe on ese tanturazho.
JOH 21:12 Ersa kieliewo, "Ta yushe ijiele irendu." Tujila hheshi Ezhan bikui mejiedene chishi kien wo giezhi kiema asa dazho.
JOH 21:13 Ersa ginanyi bareizhi hhelade ogiwo. Zhaghasunyiye ingiezhi hhelade ogiwo.
JOH 21:14 Eneshi Ersa fugusan kun dundase aminne olusenu tujiladene 3 hui chujiegheghasan wo.
JOH 21:15 Hhela yushe ijiedene ErsaXimun-Bedurude asawo, "Yaheiyani kewon Ximun, chi made oresan enelase hen onu?" Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi chade oresei chi mejiene." Ersa kieliewo, "Chi mii ga ghonilai chezhe."
JOH 21:16 Ersa 2 hui hhende asawo, "Yaheiyani kewon Ximun, chi made orezhoye?" Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi chade oresei chi mejiene." Ersa kieliewo, "Chi mii ghonilai adula."
JOH 21:17 Ersa hhende 3 hui asawo, "Yaheiyani kewon Ximun, chi made orezhoye?" ErsaBedurude 3 hui orezhoye giezhi asase Beduru nango giezhi Ersade kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi yanniliuzhe mejiene. Bi chade oresei chi mejiene." Ersa kieliewo, "Chi mii ghonilai chezhe.
JOH 21:18 Bi chade shuhuajia kielieye, chi nasuchighan bikude yodaine banlazhi khalabi khala echinema, oqioluse kunla chii khai banlazhi chi duran wiku oronde deila echine."
JOH 21:19 Ersa ene kielienyi kieliekushi Beduru matugie fuguzhi Hudai kuaikui kieliezho. Ene kielienyi kieliesenu hhende kieliewo, "Chi mii dagha."
JOH 21:20 Beduru ochira daozhese Ersa oresan hhe tuji daghasei chujieghewo. Ene tujishi heifan ijiekude Ersai kanzii shighazhi, "Ezhan, chii ghudandukushi kien wo?" giezhi asasan hhe wo.
JOH 21:21 Beduru hhei chujieghedene Ersade asawo, "Ezhan, ene kun jianlai matui gholune?"
JOH 21:22 Ersa hhende kieliewo, "Bi hhei ulie fugughazhi bi pse ireku shihou oluliuzhe chare yan xiangan wo? Chi mini dagha."
JOH 21:23 Ene kielien gaijiulai chighinde echizhi "Hhe tuji ulie fugune." giezhi kieliezho. Shijishan Ersa "Hhe ulie fugune." giezhi ese kieliezho. "Bi hhei ulie fugughazhi bi pse ireku shihou oluliuzhe chare yan xiangan wo." giezhi kieliezho.
JOH 21:24 Ene kunshi ene shiqinlade ganzhen beizhi jilasan hhe tuji wo. Hhe beisan ganzhenshi zhenni bikui bijien mejiene.
JOH 21:25 Ersa giesan shiqinla da olon hen wo. Bi sumulase nienieji jilane giese huaisan shu olonde, duyadeliuzhe teizhi pudagha dane.
ACT 1:1 Qiafeilo noyen, bi melieshiku shu jiere Ersa wilie giezhi qiisanse sunghusan shitulade Shenlinghala fenfulasenu asiman jiere khireiku hhe udu kurutula hhe giesan, surughasanlai man huaiwo.
ACT 1:3 Ersa ku shouidene olon zhenjighala goya aminne oluwo giezhi shitulade uzheghawo. 40 qien dunda shitulade xienjighazhi Hudai gojiai shiqinyi jianjizho.
ACT 1:4 Ersa hhelare hhantulakude fenfulazhi kieliewo, "Ta Yelusalense likai bu giezhi bi tande kieliesan mutun Ada dain giesei saghei.
ACT 1:5 Yaheiya usughala xili gieghawoma, giedudu ulie beizhi tai Shenlinghala xili gieghane."
ACT 1:6 Hhela man hhantu bikude Ersade asawo, "Ezhan, chi ene shihoude Isilie gojiani yen goudaghanu?"
ACT 1:7 Ersa hhelade kieliewo, "Ada qienlighalane jinjisan shihou, uduni ta mejiekuni pushoma,
ACT 1:8 Shenlin tai jiere bouzhese tande nenli irezhi ta Yelusalen, Yudaya, Samaliya, pse duyai uzhude kutula made ganzhen beine."
ACT 1:9 Ene kielienyi kielie baraghadene hhela uzheku shihoude asiman jiere khireiwo. Niegieda olien hhei jienlie echise chanla dawo.
ACT 1:10 Hhe khireikude hhela asiman jiere xianxide uzhese menzhali ghua chighan jien musisan kun hhelai kanzide beizhi kieliewo,
ACT 1:11 "Jialili kunla, ta yale beizhi asimanyi uzhene? Tanse likai giezhi asiman jiere khireisan Ersa, ta matugie uzhezhi khireighazhoshi yen qingiezhi irene."
ACT 1:12 Ingiedene hhela Ganlanshanse Yelusalende khareiwo. GanlanshanYelusalense chada wo, hhamuraku udude yose olune.
ACT 1:13 Hhela chenshide orodene sousan lou jierene khireiwo. Hhende Beduru, Yaheiya, Yagebu, Andelie, Feili, Doma, Badolomai, Matai, Yalefeini kewon Yagebu, Rexinpaini Ximun, Yagebuni kewon Yuda enela wine.
ACT 1:14 Enezighan kunla, giedun bierei, Ersani anani Mereiyen, gaijiulareni hhantu hende onxian giezho.
ACT 1:15 Hhe oloncha chabudu 120 gie gaijiula hhantulakude Beduru bosizhedene kieliewo,
ACT 1:16 "Gaijiula, jinwun jiere Shenlin Dawudei amanghala melieshi kieliesan mutun Yuda kunlai uduruzhi Ersai bareiku shiqin zhao hhe mutun gholuse indanji wo.
ACT 1:17 Hhe yenlaishi matanyi dundashiku nie wo. Shitula gieku wiliese ibufen zhanjizho.
ACT 1:18 Ene nie kun gou wiku baerghala nie ghazha agiwo. Ingie ghazhadene fura bou, kielini gha oluzhi khizhesunlani usuru khizhezho.
ACT 1:19 Yelusalende sousan kunla ene shiqinni man mejiewo. Ingie goyalane kielienghala ghazhaini Yagedama giewo. Isishi chusun ghazha wo.
ACT 1:20 Enei Zeburei jiere ingiezhi kieliezho, 'Hhei sousan oronni honji gholuzhi kiemai ulie soughasejiu.' Pse kieliezho, 'Danie kunyi hhei oronde jinjighasejiu.'
ACT 1:21 Ingiese Ezhan Ersa matanyi dunda giekude Yaheiya xili gieghasanse Ezhan matanse likai giezhi asiman jiere khitula matanre chan hhantu bisan kun dundase nie sunghuzhi Ersa fuho giesande ganzhen beighakui wo."
ACT 1:23 Ingiedene hhela sunghune giezhi ghua kunyi khizheghawo. Nieshi Yusufu wo. Hhei Basabaye giene, Yushidu giezhiye uruzho. Da nieshi Maqiya wo.
ACT 1:24 Hhela onxian giezhi kieliewo, "Ezhan, chi kunlai zhughei man mejiene. Chi ene ghua kunse kienyi sunghuzhi ene shituni wiliei giekui bijiende mejiegha. Yuda ene wiliei bendadene goya orondene echiwo."
ACT 1:26 Ingie hhela fendan qiangudene Maqiyani choui khizhewo. Hhei 11 gie shitulare hhantulaghawo.
ACT 2:1 50 qienni jieqi kuzhese hhela man nie oronde hhantulazho.
ACT 2:2 Menzhali asiman jierese fugie kei feiliesan mutun nie xianshen bouzhezhi hhela sousan giedera duruwo.
ACT 2:3 Pse khanni hoyen mutun khizhedene jien kunyi jiere luiwo.
ACT 2:4 Ingie hhelai jiere Shenlin durudene Shenlin ogisan nenlighala psedu kielienghala kielie qiiwo.
ACT 2:5 Hhe xienzide xienliantu Yutai kunla shijieni go gojiase irezhi Yelusalende souzho.
ACT 2:6 Ene shenqi khizhese olon kunla man hhantuladene goya oronyi kielienyi sonosuse ghudure wo giezho.
ACT 2:7 Hhela hende ghanirazhi kieliewo, "Uzhe, ene kielien kieliesanlashi Jialili kun pushonu?
ACT 2:8 Matan chenliese hhela matugie mai olusan oronyi kielienghala kieliezho?
ACT 2:9 Mai dunda Paqiya, Madai, Ilan kun wine. Pse Meisobudamiya, Yudaya, Jiapadojia, Bendu, Yaxiya,
ACT 2:10 Fulijia, Panfeiliya, Aijidedu kun, Gulinaini kouisan Libiyai idou oronni kunlaye wine. Da Lomase irezhi toreisan kun dunda
ACT 2:11 Yutai kun, Yutaijioni suisan kun wine. Pse Kelite, Alabo kunye wine. Matan sonosuse hhela mai kielienghala Hudai fugie shiqinyi kieliezho."
ACT 2:12 Kunla man ghanirazhi mejie dazhi nieniedene, "Eneshi yan isi wo?" giezhi asazho.
ACT 2:13 Niezhan kunla hhelai xiniezhi hhela jiu ochi sudowo giezho.
ACT 2:14 Beduru 11 gie shitulare bosi ire kunlade fugiede kieliewo, "Yutai kun, Yelusalende sousan kunla, bi kieliesei goude chenliezhi mejiendu.
ACT 2:15 Ta sumulase enezighan kunla sudowo giezhou? Uye sudozho, eneshi eqiemaghaku 9 jien wo.
ACT 2:16 Eneshi zhen xienzhi Yeer kieliezhi daosan wo,
ACT 2:17 'Huda kieliewo, Duya baraku xienzide bi Shenlinne jien kunlai jiere kiene. Tai kewon, oqinla mini kielienyi kieliene. Tai nasuchighan kunla zhoujin mutun chanlane. Tai oqio kunla zhoujin zhoujiliene.
ACT 2:18 Hhe xienzi kuzhese bi Shenlinne ere kun, bierei hojilane jiere kiese hhela mini kielienyi kunlade kieliene.
ACT 2:19 Asiman jiere bi fugie shiqin xienjighane. Zemin jiere chusun, khan, funighala ghudureqi xienjighane.
ACT 2:20 Ezhanni fugie famatu udu kuzhetula naran kharalane, sara chusun mutun hularane.
ACT 2:21 Ingiese Ezhanyi xiahua giesan kunlai man jiuine.'"
ACT 2:22 "Isilie kunla, ene kielienyi chenliendu. Huda Nasale kun Ersai tungo giezhi tai dunda nenlitu shiqin, fugie shiqin, ghudureqi xienjighadene Ersade ganzhen beizho. Enei ta goyalane mejiene.
ACT 2:23 Huda zhao goyane isighala melieshi jihua giesan mutun Ersai jiuizhi ogiwo. Ta niman doghun kunlai tungo giezhi hhei shizijia jiere ghada alawo.
ACT 2:24 Ingieliuzhe Huda hhei fuguku nangoni widaghazhi aminne olughawo. Fuguku hhei hanshilie dazho.
ACT 2:25 Dawude hhei zhiizhi kieliewo, 'Bi chanlase Ezhan chan mii shida wo. Hhe mii borun miende beise bi ulie gojiolune.
ACT 2:26 Ingiese zhughedemi bayasuzhi amandemi doulakui wine. Made xiwon wine, bi hhamura shidane.
ACT 2:27 Chi mii ruhherni dozode ulie bendane. Zhiguitu kunne ulie fughane.
ACT 2:28 Chi aminni moni made uzheghawo. Chighala hhantushi bi hende bayasuzho.'"
ACT 2:29 "Gaijiula, famatu xienren Dawudeni shiqinyi bi tande minminji kielieye. Hhe duya ijiezhi bulawo. Hhei meza edeliuzhe mai enende wine.
ACT 2:30 Hheshi nie xienzhi wo. Huda hhende dadu giezhi hhei houdeise nie kun sunghudene hhei baozo jiere soughane giezhi kieliesei mejiewo.
ACT 2:31 Hhe melieshidase ene shiqinyi mejiezhi Mexiha fuho giekui kieliewo, 'Hhei dozode ese bendawo, beyeini ese fughawo.'
ACT 2:32 Ene nie Ersai Huda aminne olughawo. Bijien man ene shiqinde ganzhen beine.
ACT 2:33 Huda hhei undudaghazhi borun miendene soughawo. Ada dain giesan Shenlinni hhe jienliedene kie bouzheghawo. Eneshi ta chujieghezhi sonosusan wo.
ACT 2:34 Dawude asiman jiere ese khireiwoma, goyane kieliezho, 'Ezhan mii Ezhande kieliewo, "Bi duitoulaichii kon dourachii teitula chi mini borun miende sou."'
ACT 2:36 Ingiese Isilie kunla, man mejiendu. Ta shizijia jiere ghadasan ene Ersani Huda Ezhan, yeshijiu Mexiha gholughawo."
ACT 2:37 Kunla ene kielienyi chenliedene zhughedeni hende jindazhi Bedurude, psedu shitulade asazho, "Gaijiula, bijien matugiene?"
ACT 2:38 Beduru kieliewo, "Ta man geizhen giendu. Ersa Mexihai niereghala xilii jienliedene tai zuini mienlie gie. Ingiese Huda ogine giesan Shenlinni ta jienliene.
ACT 2:39 Ene dainshi tande, tai kesilade, pse Ezhan mai Huda gholodose uruzhi iresan kunlade man olusan wo."
ACT 2:40 Beduru pse olon kielienghala, "Ta ene idai doghun kunlai dundase goyalane jiuizhi khizhe!" giezhi ganzhen beizhi hhelade hende surughazhi kieliewo.
ACT 2:41 Hhei kielienyi xianxin giesan kunla xili jienliewo. Hhe niudude xianxin giesan kun chabudu 3000 olodowo.
ACT 2:42 Hhela zhomen shitula sughasanyi chenliezhi laiwon giezhi ginan ghuluzhi onxian gienduzho.
ACT 2:43 Shitula olon fugie shiqin, ghudureqi xienjighase kunla man ayizho.
ACT 2:44 Xianxin giesan kunla hhantulazhi yan dunxiiliuzhe hhantu injizho.
ACT 2:45 Hhela giene dunxi, jiachanlane huidene baer injine giesan kunlade ghughazhi ogizho.
ACT 2:46 Niudunie mechide hhantulazho. Pse gieladene ginan ghuluzhi bayasuzhi heqide ijienduzho.
ACT 2:47 Hudade doulazho. Olon kunla hhelai kuaizho. Ezhan yebeiseye kun olon jiuizho.
ACT 3:1 Niudude xiawu 3 jienni onxian gieku shihoude BeduruYaheiyaghala mechide echiwo.
ACT 3:2 Niekozi kun olusanse dogholon wo. Niudunie kunla qienliezhi mechii wijien konde teizhi wijiense orochen kunlase xiahua giezhi baer ghuizho. Hhe wijienyi nierei Seighan wijien giene.
ACT 3:3 Hhe kun Beduru, Yaheiyaghala orokui chanladene xiahua giezhi baer kerezho.
ACT 3:4 Beduru, Yaheiyaghala hhei xianxide uzhedene Beduru kieliewo, "Chi bijienyi uzhe."
ACT 3:5 Hhe kun hhelai xianxide uzhezhi sumulase yama kerene giezho.
ACT 3:6 Beduru kieliewo, "Made antan, miengu uwoma, bikune chade ogiye. Bi Nasale kun Ersa Mexihai niereghala kielieye, 'Chi bosidene yo!'"
ACT 3:7 Ingiedene hhei borun khase feizhi bosizheghawo. Hhei gugieni, konni deigo goudazhi lilian orowo.
ACT 3:8 Jiuli bosi ire, beidene yo qiiwo. Hhelare hhantu mechide orokude yozho, jiulizho, Hudade doulazho.
ACT 3:9 Kunla hhe yozhi Hudade doulasanyi chanlawo.
ACT 3:10 Hheshi mechini Seighan wijien konde sousan ghuichen bikuni mejiedene hhe goudasan shiqinde ghaniradei uzhe beizho.
ACT 3:11 Hhe kun Beduru, Yaheiyaghalai barei beikude olon kunla holuzhi hhende ire ghanirawo. Hheshi zhen Sulumaneni zoulan doura wo.
ACT 3:12 Beduru chanladene bexinlade kieliewo, "Isilie kunla, ta yale ene shiqinde ghanirazho? Ta bijienyi yangiezhi uzhezho? Ta sumulase bijien goya nenli, xienliantu zhugheghalane ene kunyi yoghawo giezhou?
ACT 3:13 Iburaheimu, Isaghei, Yagebui Huda, mai xienrenlai Huda goya hoji Ersai kuaizho. Ene Ersashi ta Biladode jiuizhi ogidene Bilado jiejin giezhi hhei andaghane giese ta fandui giesan hhe wo.
ACT 3:14 Ta zhiguitu, gou kunyi ulie keredene kun alasan kunyi andagha giezhi xiahua giewo.
ACT 3:15 Ta alasanshi aminni Ezhan wo. Huda hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughawo. Bijien ene shiqinde ganzhen beine.
ACT 3:16 Ta tanizhi chanlasan ene kunde Ersai niere lilian oroghawo. Ersai xianxin gieku xinyanghala ene kunyi tai melie qienbu goudaghawo.
ACT 3:17 Gaijiula, ta noyenlane mutun mejie dazhi qingiezhi giesei bi mejiene.
ACT 3:18 Huda eqighanse jien xienzhilani tungo giezhi Mexiha shouku giekui kieliewo. Ede qimutui gholuwo.
ACT 3:19 Ingiese ta geizhen giezhi Hudai miende khareizhi irendu. Tai zuini widaghane.
ACT 3:20 Ingiese futanni shihou Ezhanyi hhense irene. Huda eqighanse jinjisan Mexihai tande oluzhi ireghane. Hheshijiu Ersa wo.
ACT 3:21 Zhen Huda eqighandei zhiguitu xienzhilane tungo giezhi kieliesan mutun duyani cunxin goudaghaku shihou olutula Ersa Mexiha bixi asiman jiere feiliene.
ACT 3:22 Musa kieliezhi Ezhan Huda tai dundase bi mutun nie xienzhi khizheghane. Hhe yan kieliese ta man chenliendu.
ACT 3:23 Kien ene xienzhii kielienyi ulie chenliese Huda bexinlane dundase widaghane giezho.
ACT 3:24 Samuerse kaishi giezhi hhei khuinadedu alinie xienzhiliuzhe ene udulani shiqinyi kieliezhi daowo.
ACT 3:25 Tashi hhe xienzhilai houdei wo. Huda tai xienrenlade yenjisan kielienni taye jienliewo. Huda Iburaheimude ingie kielie goudaghazho, 'Zemin jieredu soyuji minzulade chii houdeini yenyinzhe fuqi irene.'
ACT 3:26 Huda hojine bosizheghadene peizhi xien tande iregha, tai alinie kunniliuzhe doghunnilase likai gieghazhi tande fuqi ogiwo."
ACT 4:1 BeduruYaheiyaghala kunlade kielien kieliekude buwala, mechii sagheisan duizhan, Sadugai kunla iredene
ACT 4:2 hhela bexinlade Ersai tungo giezhi fugusan kun fuho giesei surughazhi chonjise hende hokuzho.
ACT 4:3 Ingie hhelai barei agi, khara oluse khadene khuichudu kuwo.
ACT 4:4 Ingieliuzhe hhela jianjisan kielienni chenliedene xianxin giesan kun olon wo. Xianxin giesan ere kun 5000 gholuwo.
ACT 4:5 Khuichudu Yutai kunni noyen, zhanlao, jinwun hanjiala man Yelusalende hhantulawo.
ACT 4:6 Zui fugie buwa Yanasi, Gaiyafa, Yaheiya, Yalishanda, pse zui fugie buwani jiawuni kunla man hhende wine.
ACT 4:7 Hhela Beduru, Yaheiyaghalai dunda beighadene asawo, "Ta kienyi nenli, niereghala ene shiqinyi giezho?"
ACT 4:8 Qingiekude Bedurude Shenlin duruzhi hhelade kieliewo, "Bexinlai noyen, zhanlaolaya,
ACT 4:9 ta enedu ene dogholonyi jiere bijien giesan gou shiqin, pse hhe matugie goudasei bijiende asazhoshi
ACT 4:10 ta ashighala, Isilieni bexinla man mejiendu. Tai melie beizhi goudasan ene kunshi ta shizijia jiere ghadadene Huda fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Nasale kun Ersa Mexihani niereghala goudaghasan wo.
ACT 4:11 Ene Ersashi jinwunde ingiezhi kieliesan hhe wo, 'Ta jianrenla bendasan tashi ede giei zhunyo tashi gholuwo.'
