ACT 4:12 Ersase chugo pse jiuichen uwo. Qienxiade matanyi jiuiku psedu nierei ese ogizho."
ACT 4:13 Hhela Beduru, Yaheiya ghuala fugie danzighala kieliesei uzhewo. Hhelade yama unhua wikui mejiedene ghanirawo. Pse ene ghua kunshi Ersare hhantuku wo giezho.
ACT 4:14 Hhe goudasan kun hhelare hhantu beisanyi chanladene hhelade yama kielieku kielien widawo.
ACT 4:15 Ingie BeduruYaheiyai zui fugie fayense khireigha giezhi fenfuladene goyalane shanlian giezhi kieliewo.
ACT 4:16 "Matan ene ghua kunyi matugiene? Hhela nie ghudureqi xienjighawo, jien Yelusalende sousan kunla man mejiene. Matan uwo giezhi kielie danema,
ACT 4:17 ene shiqin bexinlai dunda fugiedakuse ayizhi matan hhelai nie ayighaye. Ene kunyi niereghala pse bu chonji gie."
ACT 4:18 Ingie hhe ghualai uruzhi ire, Ersani niereghala kunlade pse bu jianji, ye bu surugha giewo.
ACT 4:19 BeduruYaheiyaghala kieliewo, "Tai kieliei chenlie, Hudai kieliei ulie chenliese, Hudai melie heshi winu uwo? Ta goyalane sumula.
ACT 4:20 Bijien chujieghezhi sonosusanne ulie kieliezhi ulie olune."
ACT 4:21 Noyenla hhelade yama faikui jiekou ereizhi khizhe dawo. Pse bexinla ene fashen giesan shiqin jiere Hudai kuaise hhe ghualai hende nie ayigha andaghawo.
ACT 4:22 Yenlai ene ghudureqighala goudaghasan kun 40 ji olune.
ACT 4:23 BeduruYaheiyaghalai andaghadene hhela goya kunlane hhende echiwo. Fugie buwa, zhanlaolai kieliesan kielienyi goya kunladene kieliewo.
ACT 4:24 Hhela chenliedene Hudade nie zhugheghala fugiede kieliewo, "Asiman, zemin, hai, pse hhei sudorodu shihenilai man zhayaghazhi gonjisan Ezhan,
ACT 4:25 chi Shenlinyi tungo giezhi goya hojine, bijienyi xienren Dawudeni amanghala ingiezhi kieliewo, 'Go gojiala yale nouine? Go minzula yale oronde wikui jihua giene?
ACT 4:26 Duyai honshanla bosizhewo. Noyenla hhantulazho. Ezhanse, Ezhanni Mexihase fandui giene giezho.'
ACT 4:27 Hherode, Benjiu-Bilado ghuala ene chenshide niman kun, Isilie kunlare hhantuladene chi sunghu goudaghasan zhiguitu hoji Ersai qingiezhi fandui giezho.
ACT 4:28 Hhela giesanlashi man chii nenli, isighala eqighan jiejin giesan shiqin wo.
ACT 4:29 Ezhan, hhela ede bijienyi ayighasei chi nie uzhe. Hojiladene fugie danzi ogizhi chii kielienni kieliegha.
ACT 4:30 Chi nenline xienjighazhi gienlai goudagha. Chii zhiguitu hoji Ersai niereghala ghudureqi, fugie shiqin xienjigha."
ACT 4:31 Hhela onxian gie baluse hhantulasan oron gojiolu qii, hhelade man Shenlin duruzhi danzine fugiedagha, Hudai kielienni kielie qiiwo.
ACT 4:32 Xianxin giesan kunla zhughede, sumulasanla man nie wo. Kienliuzhe eneshi goyanughun wo ulie giene, man hhantu injizho.
ACT 4:33 Shitula fugie nenlighala Ezhan Ersa fuho giesande ganzhen beizho. Ingiese kunlade Hudai fugie nenjien irewo.
ACT 4:34 Hhelai dunda kiemade yama ese chaizho. Hhela ghazha, gielane huisan baerni agizhi iredene
ACT 4:35 shitulani melie jiese shitula zhao kunla injiku mutun ghughazhi ogiwo.
ACT 4:36 Nie Liwi kunyi nierei Yusufu giene. Saipuluside oluzho. Shitula hhei Banaba giezhi uruzho, isishi kunlade goude sughazhi kieliechen wo.
ACT 4:37 Hhe ghazhalane huidene baerni agizhi ire shitulai melie jiewo.
ACT 5:1 Da nie kunyi nierei Yananiya giene. Biereiini Safeila giene. Ghuala ghazhane huidene
ACT 5:2 baerse ghulazhi goyadene gouji feiliegha, psedulai shitulai melie jiewo. Enei biereiniye mejiene.
ACT 5:3 Beduru kieliewo, "Yananiya, yale chii zhughede Ibilisi duruzhi Shenlinyi piendane? Ghazhane huisan baerni yale goujinie feilieghawo?
ACT 5:4 Ghazhane uye huikude ghazhashi chinughun pushonu? Ede huise baerne chi zozhu giezhola? Chi yale intui giezho? Chi kunni ese piendazho. Hudai piendazho."
ACT 5:5 Yananiya ene kielienyi chenliedene fura bou, ho sirawo. Chenliesan kunla man hende ayizho.
ACT 5:6 Giedun nasuchighan kunla bosi ire, hhei boui goudaghadene qienlie khirei bulawo.
ACT 5:7 Ghuran zhuntou daose biereini irewo. Ene shiqinni dou ulie mejiene.
ACT 5:8 Beduru hhende asawo, "Chi made kielie, ta ghazha huisan baershi enezighan onu?" "Jiu enezighan wo."
ACT 5:9 Beduru kieliewo, "Ta ghuala yale hhantulazhi Ezhanni ruhherni shiine? Zhanguijii chii bulasan kunla ede wijien konde irewo, chiiye qienlie khighane."
ACT 5:10 Ingie hhe bierei deigo Bedurui kon konde fura bou, ho sirawo. Hhe nasuchighan kunla oro ire fuguseini chanladene, qienlie echi zhanguijiini kanzide bulawo.
ACT 5:11 Jien jiohuini kunla, pse ene shiqinyi chenliesan kunla man hende ayizho.
ACT 5:12 Ezhan shitulai tungo giezhi bexinlai dunda ghudureqi, fugie shiqin olon giewo. Xianxin giesan kunla Sulumane zoulande heqide man hhantulazho.
ACT 5:13 Bexinla man hhelai zanchen giezhoma, kunlase ayizhi hhelare hhantula dazho.
ACT 5:14 Ezhanyi xianxin giesan ere kun, biereila yebeiseye olodozho.
ACT 5:15 Niezhan kunla da gientulai qienliezhi geidoude khirei chon, ruzi jiere jiezho. Sumulase Beduru yozhi daokude xiujieniliuzhe hhelai jiere kuse giezho.
ACT 5:16 Pse Yelusalen zhouwini xianlase olon kunla gientu, zannan ruhher heisanlai uduru ire man goudaghawo.
ACT 5:17 Zui fugie buwa, hhei lienshoulani Sadugai kunla hende dubiliedene
ACT 5:18 shitulai barei agi bafanzide khawo.
ACT 5:19 Xienidei Ezhanyi qienxien bafanzi wijienyi niezhi hhelai uduru khizhegha kieliewo,
ACT 5:20 "Ta mechide echidene ene amin ogiku daolii bexinlade man kielie."
ACT 5:21 Ingiese shitula ene kielienyi chenliedene ogheikude mechide echizhi kunlade sughazho. Zui fugie buwa, lienshoularene kuzhedene zui fugie fayenni kun, Isilieni zhanlaolai uruzhi irewo. Kun peizhi bafanzise shitulai lai iregha giezho.
ACT 5:22 Mechini sagheisan kunla bafanzide echise kun nieda uwo. Ingie khareizhi ire kieliewo,
ACT 5:23 "Bijien echise bafanzi wijien yama ese giezho. Sagheisan kun wijien ghadane wo. Wijienyi niese sudoro kun nieda uwo."
ACT 5:24 Mechini sagheisan duizhan, fugie buwa ene kielienyi chenliedene ghanirazhi matugie imutui gholuwo giezho.
ACT 5:25 Nie kun iredene kieliewo, "Ta bafanzide bareisan kunla ede mechide beidene bexinlade sughazho."
ACT 5:26 Ingie duizhan mechini sagheisan kunlai uduruzhi shitulai barei irewo. Bexinla hhelai tashighala eghikuse ayizhi khidunde ese giezho.
ACT 5:27 Hhela shitulai barei ire zui fugie fayen sudoro beigha zui fugie buwa hhelade asazho,
ACT 5:28 "Bijien tande hende jingao giezhi ene kunyi niereghala kunlai bu surugha giezhi kieliewo. Ta daoline nie Yelusalende kielie kurughadene dou alasan ene kunni chusunni zhanni bijienyi jiere beilieghane."
ACT 5:29 Beduru, pse shitula kieliewo, "Hudai shunjizhi kunyi ulie shunjise indanji wo.
ACT 5:30 Mai xienrenni Huda ta mutun jiere guaidene alasan Ersai aminne olughawo.
ACT 5:31 Huda hhei undudaghazhi borun miendene khighawo. Hhei honshan, jiuichen danlaghazhi Isilie kunni geizhen gieghazhi zuini mienliene giezho.
ACT 5:32 Bijien ene shiqinlade ganzhen beine. Hudai shunjisan kunlade ogisan Shenlinye ganzhen beine."
ACT 5:33 Zui fugie fayenni kunla enei chenliedene hende hokuzhi hhelai alane giezho.
ACT 5:34 Nie Falisai kunyi niereini Jiamalie giene. Hheshi nie jinwun loushi wo, kunla man hhei zunjine. Zui fugie fayende bosi ire kunlade fenfulazhi shitulai ghadane niecha khireigha giewo.
ACT 5:35 Ingie kunlade kieliewo, "Isilie kunla, ta ene kunlai xioxin giezhi chuli gie.
ACT 5:36 Eqighandei Duda bosi ire goyane fugie wo giezho. Hhei daghasan kun 400 wine. Hhei alasenu daghasan kunlai man sanda widazhi yama widawo.
ACT 5:37 Hhense khuinashi hukou denji giekude Jialilini Yuda bexinlai yela giezhi goyane daghaghawoma, hhe fuguse daghasan kunla man sanda widawo.
ACT 5:38 Ede bi tande kielieye, ta ene kunlase gholodo. Hhelai bu gonji. Hhelai jihua, giesanlashi kunse irese widane.
ACT 5:39 Hudase iresan enbese ta hhelai widagha dane. Ta kenen Hudare duitou gholune." Zui fugie fayenni kunla hhei kieliei shunjidene
ACT 5:40 shitulai uru ire idun eghidene Ersai niereghala bu kielie gie andaghawo.
ACT 5:41 Shitula Ersai nierede oluzhi jiuren giese pei shidane giezhi hende bayasudene zui fugie fayense likai giewo.
ACT 5:42 Hhela niudunie mechide, go gielade ese beidene Ersashi Mexiha wo giezhi kunlade sughazhi gouxioxini chonjizho.
ACT 6:1 Hhe oloncha tuji niudunie olodozho. Niudunieku shenhofei ogiku shiqin jiere Xila kielien kieliechen Yutaii guafulai jiezho. Ingiese hhela Xibolai kielien kieliechen Yutai kunlade boxin kieliezho.
ACT 6:2 Ingie 12 gie shitu olon tujilai uru ire kieliewo, "Matan Hudai kielienyi chonjikui bendazhi jiedene ijiekui gonjise heshi uwo.
ACT 6:3 Gaijiula, tai dundase gou minshentu, Shenlin duruzhi agheli olontu dolon ere kunyi sunghuzhi ene shiqinlai gonjighaye.
ACT 6:4 Ingiese matan zhomen onxian giezhi pse Hudai kieliende giene."
ACT 6:5 Kunla man ene kielienyi zanchen giedene Siqifan, Feili, Bologelo, Nijiano, Qimun, Bamina, pse Yutaijiode suisan Anqiya kun Nigelai sunghuwo. Siqifan xianxin giesan gou wo, Shenlinye duruzho.
ACT 6:6 Enelai shitulai melie beighase shitula onxian giezhi hhelai jiere khane teiwo.
ACT 6:7 Hudai kielien ondazhi Yelusalende tujila zhenzhen olodozho. Tebie olon buwalaye ene xinyanni shunjizho.
ACT 6:8 Siqifande Hudai nenjien, nenli olonshi kunlai dunda fugie shiqin, ghudureqi giezho.
ACT 6:9 Ingiese Ziyutu kunla giezhi urusan huitanni giedun kun bosi ire Siqifanghala jianjinduwo. Enelashi Gulinai, Yalishanda, Jilijia, Yaxiya gochuse irezho.
ACT 6:10 Siqifan agheli, Shenlinyi kouizhi kielien kieliese hhela dui dane.
ACT 6:11 Ingie kunlai baerghala agidene kielieghawo, "Bijien chenliese SiqifanMusa, Hudaghalai sugiezho."
ACT 6:12 Hhela bexin, zhanlao, jinwun hanjialai shanjizhi Siqifanyi hhende echighase barei zui fugie fayende irewo.
ACT 6:13 Hhela pse jia ganzhen beisan kunlai uru ire kielieghawo, "Ene kun zhiguitu oronji Musani guijinni sugiezhi ese beizho.
ACT 6:14 Bijien chenliese hhe kieliezhi Nasale kun Ersa mechii furaghane, pse Musa matande ogisan guijinni geighane giezho."
ACT 6:15 Zui fugie fayende sousan kunla man Siqifanni xianxide uzhese ungieni qienxienni ungiei xianli.
ACT 7:1 Zui fugie buwa Siqifande asawo, "Intu shiqin winu?"
ACT 7:2 Siqifan kieliewo, "Oqio kun, gaijiula, ta chenliendu. Matai xienren IburaheimuHalande soutula Meisobudamiyade bikude famatu Huda hhende xienjighadene kieliewo,
ACT 7:3 'Chi goya oron, jiawusene likai giezhi bi chade uzheghaku oronde echi.'"
ACT 7:4 "Ingie hhe Jialeji kunlai oronse likai giedene Halande souwo. Hhei adani fugudene Huda hhei banjighazhi ta ede sousan ene oronde ireghawo.
ACT 7:5 Ene oronde Huda hhende yama jiachan, lien beiku oronye uye ogiwoma, Huda kielien yenjizhi ene oronyi hhende, hhei houdeide ogizhi caichan gie giewo. Hhe shihoude hhende kewosi uwo.
ACT 7:6 Ingiese Huda kieliewo, 'Houdeichii kunlai oronde souzhi hoji danlazhi 400 nien zayalane.'
ACT 7:7 Pse kieliewo, 'Hhelai hoji danlaghasan gojiani bi panjine. Khuinashi hhela khizhedene ene oronde mii shunjine.'
ACT 7:8 Ingiedene Huda Iburaheimude hetoune giekughala kielien yenjiwo. Iburaheimude Isagheini oluzhi neimudude hetoune giewo. Isagheide Yagebuni oluwo, Yagebude mai 12 gie famatu xienrenlai oluwo."
ACT 7:9 "Ene famatu xienrenla Yusufu jiuni dubiliedene Aijide huiwo. Ingieliuzhe Huda hheghala hhantushi
ACT 7:10 hhei yan kunnanseliuzhe khizheghawo. Huda hhende nenjien, agheli ogise Aijini Falao honshan hhei uzhedan gou wo. Falao hhei Aijide zui fugie noyen danlaghazhi giene man gonjighawo."
ACT 7:11 "Ingiedene Aiji, Jianande honnien kuzhezhi zeinan irewo. Mai xienrenlade taran sirawo.
ACT 7:12 Yagebu sonosuse Aijide taran wine. Ingie mai xienrenlani peizhi tou 1 hui hhende echighawo.
ACT 7:13 2 huide echise Yusufu gaijiuladene tanighawo. Ingiese Falao hhei gieni qinkonyi mejiewo.
ACT 7:14 Yusufu kun peizhi adane nie gie kunyi jienlieghale echiwo. Man 75 gie kun wo.
ACT 7:15 Ingie YagebuAijide bouzhewo. Khuinashi Yagebu, mai xienrenla man hhende duya ijiewo.
ACT 7:16 Hhelai laizhi Shijiende echi IburaheimuHamoni houdeilase miengughala agisan mezade bulawo."
ACT 7:17 "Huda Iburaheimude yenjisan kielien kuzhekude Aijide Isilie kunla hende olodowo.
ACT 7:18 Khuinashi Yusufui tani dachen nie shini honshan khizhezhi Aijini gonjizho.
ACT 7:19 Hhe mai kunlai heizhi xienrenlai mai zayalazho. Hhelai biizhi yeliwalai bendaghazhi aminne ese olughazho."
ACT 7:20 "Hhe shihoude Musani oluwo. Hudai melie hhe uzhezhi seighan wo. Hhei adaini giede ghuran sara qiezhedene
ACT 7:21 bendase Falaoi oqin kewonni giedene qiezhe fugiedaghawo.
ACT 7:22 MusaAiji kunlai unhuani man suruwo. Kielien kielie, shiqin giese nenli wine."
ACT 7:23 "Musa 40 olukude goya Isilie kunlane uzhele echine giezhi jiejin giewo.
ACT 7:24 Niefade hhe echikude nie Aiji kun nie Isilie kunyi qifulasanyi chanlasenu hhe Aiji kunyi alazhi hhe kunde bouchou giewo.
ACT 7:25 Hhe sumulase Huda hhei tungo giezhi goya kunlai jiuikui mejiemu giezhoma, hhela mejie dazho.
ACT 7:26 Khuichudu Musa chanlase Isilie kunla eghinduzho. Hhelai sidaghazhi kieliewo, 'Gujiu, tashi gaijiula wo, yale nieniene qifulane?'"
ACT 7:27 "Giebeine qifulasan kun Musai tungu daogha kieliewo, 'Kien chii bijiende lindao, panjichen kun danlaghawo?
ACT 7:28 Chi uchughudu hhe Aiji kunyi alaku mutun mii alanu?'
ACT 7:29 Musa ene kielienyi chenliedene Aijise ghula holu Mijiende toreisan mutun souwo. Hhe oronde hhende ghua kewon oluwo."
ACT 7:30 "40 nien daose Xinaishan hontande nie qienxien siderasan eghesun dunda Musade chanlaghawo.
ACT 7:31 Musa zhoujin mutunyi chanladene ghanirazhi melie daozhi uzhene giekude Ezhanyi shenqii sonosuwo,
ACT 7:32 'Bishi chii xienrenlai Huda wo. Iburaheimu, Isaghei, Yagebuni Huda wo.' Musa chenliesenu pugharadene ayizhi uzhe dazho.
ACT 7:33 Ezhan hhende kieliewo, 'Chi kon jieredu maheine tei. Chi beisan oronshi zhiguitu oron wo.
ACT 7:34 Mii bexinlai Aijide zayalasanyi bi qinchude chanlawo. Hhela shonholosan shenqiiye sonosuwo. Bi hhelai jiuile bouzhewo. Ede ire, bi chii peizhi Aijide echighane.'"
ACT 7:35 "Eneshi bexinla kien chii bijiende lindao, panjichen kun danlaghawo giezhi fandui giesan Musa wo. Ingieliuzhe Huda siderasan eghesun dunda qienxienyi tungo giezhi hhei peidene bexinlade noyen, jiuichen danlaghawo.
ACT 7:36 MusaAiji, Hunhai, hontande 40 nien olon fugie shiqin, ghudureqi giezhi bexinlai Aijise uduru khizhewo."
ACT 7:37 "Eneshijiu Isilie kunlade 'Huda tai dundase bi mutun nie xienzhi khizheghane.' giezhi kieliesan hhe Musa wo.
ACT 7:38 Ene Musa hontandedu Isilie kunlare hhantu wo. Mai xienrenghala hhantu Xinaishan jiere hhende kielien kieliesan qienxienyi tungo giezhi amin ogiku kielienyi jienliedene matande chonjizhi ogiwo."
ACT 7:39 "Mai xienrenla hhei kielienyi ese chenliedene hhei tungu daoghazhi Aijide khareiku duralazho.
ACT 7:40 Hhela Hharunede kieliewo, 'Bijiende mo uduruku nigiedalani gie. Bijienyi Aijise uduru khizhesan Musa yan shiqin penji woshi bijien ulie mejiene.'
ACT 7:41 Ingie hhe shihoude hhela nie fughe giedene hhe nigiedade mure khughozhi goya khaghalane giesanlade beiizhi bayasunduzho.
ACT 7:42 Ingiese Huda hhelase likai giedene hhela asiman jieredu naran, sara, hodunlai beiise uye gonjizho. Zhen xienzhii shu jiere huaisan mutun, 'Isilie kunla, ta hontande 40 nien dunda zharusan ghoni fugheji pse ogisan mureshi made giesan pusho.
ACT 7:43 Ta qienliesanshi Molo nigiedani zhanfan wo, Lifan nigiedani hodun wo. Enelashi ta goyala beiine giezhi giesan nigiedala wo. Ingiese bi tai touzhi Babilun ghadane khighane.'"
ACT 7:44 "Mai xienrenla hontande bikude ganzhen beiku zhanfan wine. Hheshi Huda Musade fenfuladene uzheghasan yanzi mutun gieghasan wo.
ACT 7:45 Mai xienrenla ene zhanfanyi jienliewo. Huda hhelai melie niman kunlai tou khighasan oronde hhela Yeshuyare hhantu zhanfanyi agi echizhi Dawude honshanni shihou kuruwo.
ACT 7:46 Huda Dawudede orezho. Ingiese hhe Hudai xiahua giezhi Yagebui houdeilade Huda souku oron zhunbei giene giezhoma,
ACT 7:47 Hudade giei beighasanshi Sulumane wo."
ACT 7:48 "Ingiezhoma, Zui Unduni Huda kun khaghalane giesan giede ulie soune. Xienzhi kieliesan kielien mutun wo,
ACT 7:49 Ezhan kieliewo, 'Asimanshi mii zowi wo. Zeminshi mii bandou wo. Ta made matui gie giene? Khalashi bi hhamuraku oron wo?
ACT 7:50 Enelashi man bi khaghalane giesan pushonu?'"
ACT 7:51 "Ta ene jianbanjin kunla, zhughe, chighindene hetoune ese giesan kunla. Ta xienrenlane mutun ibeizi Shenlinni fandui giezho.
ACT 7:52 Alinie xienzhilai tai xienrenla ese heiwo? Hhela nie gou kun irene giezhi melie kieliesan xienzhilai alawo. Ede ta hhe gou kunni ghudanduzhi alawo.
ACT 7:53 Ta qienxienla chonjizhi ogisan guijinni jienliedene ese zunjiwo."
ACT 7:54 Hhela ene kielienyi chenliedene Siqifande hende hokuzhi shidunne zhouzho.
ACT 7:55 Siqifande Shenlin duruzhi asimanyi xianxide uzhezhi Hudai fama, pse Ersa Hudai borun miende beisei chanladene kieliewo,
ACT 7:56 "Asiman keizhi Kunnikewon Hudai borun miende beisei bi chanlawo."
ACT 7:57 Ingiese kunla chighinne duigha fugiede onghonozhi hhei melie chunji echidene
ACT 7:58 hhei chenshi ghadane tungu khigha tashighala eghi qiiwo. Ganzhen beisan kunla jienne teidene nie Saolo giezhi urusan nasuchighan kunyi kon konde jiewo.
ACT 7:59 Hhela tashighala eghikude Siqifan onxian giezhi kieliewo, "Ezhan Ersa, mii ruhherni jienlie!"
ACT 7:60 Pse xiutuliezhi fugiede kieliewo, "Ezhan, ene zuini hhelade bu sougha!" Ene kielienyi kieliedene fuguwo.
ACT 8:1 Siqifanyi alasande Saolo tunyi giewo. Ene uduse Yelusalenni jiohuii hende heizho. Shitulase chugo psedu tujila sandazhi Yudaya, Samaliyani go oronde echiwo.
ACT 8:2 Niezhan xienliantu kunla Siqifanyi buladene hhende oluzhi fugiede wilazho.
ACT 8:3 Saolo jiohuini heizhi jien kunlai giede orodene ere kun, biereilai bafanzide lai echi khawo.
ACT 8:4 Hhe sandasan kunla gochude echizhi Hudai kielienyi chonjizho.
ACT 8:5 FeiliSamaliyai chenshide echizhi kunlade Mexihai chonjizho.
ACT 8:6 Olon kunla Feili kieliesan kielienyi chenliezhi giesan ghudureqii uzhedene man hhei kielienyi goude chenliezho.
ACT 8:7 Olon kunlai jierese zannan ruhherla fugiede nie onghonodene likai giewo. Pse olon tanhon giesan, dogholonlai goudaghawo.
ACT 8:8 Ingiese hhe chenshii kunla hende bayasuzho.
ACT 8:9 Hhe chenshide nie kunyi nierei Ximun giene. Eqighanse baxi shuaizhi bi hen wo giezho. Samaliyai bexinlai ghaniraghazho.
ACT 8:10 Bugon fugiei ganii man hhei daghazhi ene kunshi fugie nenlitu giezhi urusan Hudai nenli wo giezho.
ACT 8:11 Hhela hhei chenliekushi hhe oloncha baxi shuaizhi hhelai ghaniraghazho.
ACT 8:12 Ingiekude Feili hhelade Hudai gojiai gouxioxi, Ersa Mexihai nierei chonjise hhela xianxin giezhi ere kun, biereila xili jienliewo.
ACT 8:13 Lien Ximunye xianxin giedene xili jienliewo. Hhe Feilighala chan hhantulazhi Feili giesan ghudureqi, fugie nenlitu shiqinlai uzhedene ghanirazho.
ACT 8:14 Shitula Yelusalende bikude chenliese Samaliya kunla Hudai kielienyi jienliewo giese BeduruYaheiyaghalai hhelai hhende echighawo.
ACT 8:15 Hheghala boudene hhelade Shenlinyi jienlieghane giezhi onxian giezho.
ACT 8:16 Shenlin kiemai jiere ese bouzhezho. Hhela zinie Ezhan Ersai niereghala xili jienliezho.
ACT 8:17 BeduruYaheiyaghala hhelai jiere khane teise hhela Shenlinyi jienliewo.
ACT 8:18 Shitula khane teise Shenlin bouzhesei Ximun chanladene baerne hhelade ogizhi
ACT 8:19 kieliewo, "Ene nenlii madeye ogi. Bi kienyi jiere khane teizhi onxian giese kienye Shenlinyi jienliene."
ACT 8:20 Ingiese Beduru kieliewo, "Chi baerghalane hhantu fugule echi. Chi sumulase Huda ogiku nenjienni baerghala aginu?
ACT 8:21 Ene wiliede chade guzi uwo. Hudai melie chii zhughe donzhen uwo.
ACT 8:22 Chi ene doghunnii geizhi Ezhanni xiahua gie. Kenen chi zhughedene sumulasei mienliene.
ACT 8:23 Bi uzhese chii zhughede dubilieku olon wo, gou wini chii banlazho."
ACT 8:24 Ingiese Ximun kieliewo, "Ta made oluzhi Ezhanni xiahua gie. Ingiese ta kieliesanla mii jiere nieda ulie irene."
ACT 8:25 BeduruYaheiyaghala Ezhanyi kielienni kieliezhi ganzhen beidene Yelusalende khareiwo. Idou mo jiere Samaliyani go aghinlade gouxioxii chonjizho.
ACT 8:26 Ingiekude Ezhanni qienxien Feilide kieliewo, "Chi bosidene nanbangiede yo. Yelusalense Jiasade bouku mo jiere echi." Hhe mo hontande wo.
ACT 8:27 Feili bosizhedene echise mo jiere nie Aisaiebiya kunyi chanlawo. Ene kunshi Aisaiebiya bierei honshan Gandajini kha douradu taijien wo. Hheshi bierei honshanni baerlai man gonjisan fugie noyen wo. Yelusalende libai giezhi irezho.
ACT 8:28 Khareiku mo jiere mache souzhi xienzhi Isaiyai shuni onshizho.
ACT 8:29 Shenlin Feilide kieliewo, "Chi gierudene chezii shigha."
ACT 8:30 Feili holuzhi echise xienzhi Isaiyai shuni onshisei sonosuwo. Ingie hhende asawo, "Chi onshisanne dunjirenu?"
ACT 8:31 Hhe kieliewo, "Mii kiema ese uduruzho, bi matugie dunjirene?" Ingie Feilii chezi jierene uru khirei hhantu souwo.
ACT 8:32 Hhe onshisan jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Hhei ghoni zharuchen kun shida echiku ghoni mutun lai echiwo. Usun ghighachen kunni kha douradu qioqioji ghoni mutun hhe amanne ese angheiwo.
ACT 8:33 Kunla hhei uru giezho, gundande ese panjiwo. Hhei aminni duyase agi echiwo. Kunlade kielieku houdeiye uwo."
ACT 8:34 Taijien Feilide kieliewo, "Bi nie asaye, xienzhi kieliesan ene kielienshi kienyi kieliezho? Goyane kieliezhou? Pse nie kunyi kieliezho?"
ACT 8:35 Feili ene jinwunse kaishi giezhi hhende Ersai gouxioxii jianji qiiwo.
ACT 8:36 Hhela mo jiere yokude usu winetu oronde kuruwo. Taijien kieliewo, "Uzhe, enende usu wine. Bi enende xili jienliese ulie olunu?"
ACT 8:38 Ingie fenfulazhi chezii beighadene Feili taijienghala usude bouzhi Feili hhende xili gieghawo.
ACT 8:39 Ususe khizhese Ezhanyi Shenlin Feilii uduru yolawo. Taijien hhei chanla dawo. Ingiedene bayasuzhi mone yowo.
ACT 8:40 Ingie Feilii Yasodude chanlawo. Hhe yozhi go chenshilade gouxioxii chonjizhi izhi Kaisaliyade kuruwo.
ACT 9:1 Saolo izhigie Ezhanyi tujilai alane giezhi ayighazho. Ingie zui fugie buwai hhende echidene
ACT 9:2 Damashigeni go huitande echiku xinni kerewo. Ene daolini daghasan kunyi faxien giese bugon bierei ere kun barei Yelusalende lai echine giezho.
ACT 9:3 Saolo mo jiere yozhi Damashigede kurukude menzhali asiman jierese gonqi faizhi hhei simiende zhouizho.
ACT 9:4 Ingie hhe zemin jiere fura bouwo. Sonususe nie shenqi hhende kieliewo, "Saolo! Saolo! Chi mii yale heine?"
ACT 9:5 Hhe kieliewo, "Ezhan, chishi kien wo?" "Bishi chi heisan Ersa wo.
ACT 9:6 Chi bosizhedene chenshide echi. Hhende matui giekui chade kieliene."
ACT 9:7 Hhantu yosan kunla shenqii sonosuzhoma kunni chanla dase beidene kielien kielie dazho.
ACT 9:8 Saolo zemin jierese bosise nudunne niewoma, yama chanla dane. Kunla hhei khase lai Damashigede echiwo.
ACT 9:9 Ghurudu chanla dadene yama ese ijiezhi ese ochiwo.
ACT 9:10 Damashigede nie tuji wine. Niereini Yananiya giene. Ezhan zhoujin mutun xienjighazhi hhende kieliewo, "Yananiya." Hhe kieliewo, "Ezhan, matugiewo?"
ACT 9:11 Ezhan hhende kieliewo, "Chi bosizhedene Dondonji giezhi urusan geidoude echizhi Yudai giede nie Dashu kunyi erei. Niereini Saolo giene. Hhe zhen onxian giezho.
ACT 9:12 Hhe zhoujin mutun chanlase Yananiya giesan nie kun oro iredene hhei jiere khane teise goudawo."
ACT 9:13 Ingiese Yananiya kieliewo, "Ezhan, bi sonosuse ene kun Yelusalende chii shentulade olon doghun shiqin giezho giezhi olon kunla kieliezho.
ACT 9:14 Hhe pse fugie buwalase chii beiisan jien kunlai bareiku qienlii kere enende irezho."
ACT 9:15 Ingiese Ezhan hhende kieliewo, "Chi echi. Hheshi niman kun, honshan, Isilie kunlade bi nierene chonjighane giezhi sunghusan rencai wo.
ACT 9:16 Hhe mii nierede bixi olon ku shoukui bi hhende mejieghane."
ACT 9:17 Ingiese Yananiya echidene hhei giede orowo. Khane Saoloi jiere teizhi kieliewo, "Saolo gaijiu, chi ireku mo jiere chade chujiegheghasan Ezhan Ersa mii ireghakushi chii pse chanlaghazhi chade Shenlin durughane giezho."
ACT 9:18 Ingiese Saoloi nudun jierese deigo zhaghasun arasun mutun nie dunxi bou irese hhe chanlawo. Ingiedene bosi ire xili jienliewo.
ACT 9:19 Ijiewuni ijiedene lilian orowo. SaoloDamashigeni tujilare hhantu giedudu souzhi
ACT 9:20 deigo Ersashi Hudai kewon wo giezhi go huitanlade chonjizho.
ACT 9:21 Jien ene kielienyi chenliesan kunla man ghaniradene kieliewo, "Ene kunshi Yelusalende Ersai beiisan kunlai heisan hhe kun pushonu? Hhe enende irezhi hhelai bareidene fugie buwalade ogine ese giezhou?"
ACT 9:22 Saolode yebeiseye nenli olodozhi Ersashi Mexiha bikui zhenmin giese Damashigeni Yutai kunlai kielie beighawo.
ACT 9:23 Ezighancha daose Yutai kunla Saoloi alane giezhi shanlian giezho.
ACT 9:24 Hhela alane gieku jihuai kunla Saolode mejieghawo. Hhela xieni udu chenshi wijiende sagheizhi hhei alane giezho.
ACT 9:25 Nie xiidei hhei tujila nie lanlande hhei orogha chenqian jierese jiuzhilie bouzheghawo.
ACT 9:26 SaoloYelusalende kuzhedene psedu tujilare hhantulane giezhoma, hhe tuji gholusei xianxin gie dase hhela man ayizho.
ACT 9:27 Ingiese Banaba hhei jienliedene uduruzhi shitulai shida echiwo. Hhe mo jiere matugiezhi Ezhanyi chanlasei, Ezhan hhende kielien kieliesei, hhe Damashigede danzine fugiedaghazhi Ersai niereghala jianjisei man kieliewo.
ACT 9:28 Ingiedene SaoloYelusalende tujilare hhantulazhi ziyude yozho. Ezhanyi niereghala danzine fugiedagha kieliezho.
ACT 9:29 Hhe pse Xila kielien kieliechen Yutai kunlare kieliezhi jianjinduzho. Ingiese hhela Saoloi alane giezho.
ACT 9:30 Gaijiula enei mejiedene hhei Kaisaliyade khughozhi boughadene Dashude echighawo.
ACT 9:31 Ingiekude Yudaya, Jialili, Samaliyai gochudedu jiohui man pinnanshizhi hendawo. Hhela Ezhanyi zunjizhi giezho. Shenlin hhelai bayasughazho. Ingiese xianxin giesan kunla yebeiseye olodozho.
ACT 9:32 Beduru gochude yokude Lida oronde sousan shentulai hhende echiwo.
ACT 9:33 Hhende Iniya giesan nie kunni chanlawo. Tanhon giezhi ruzi jiere 8 nien kijiezho.
ACT 9:34 Beduru hhende kieliewo, "Iniya, Ersa Mexiha chii goudaghawo. Bosizhedene ruzine shidolo agi!" Ingiese hhe deigo bosi irewo.
ACT 9:35 Jien Lida, Shalunde sousan kunla hhei chanladene man Ezhanyi shunjiwo.
ACT 9:36 Yepade nie oqitu tuji wo. Niereini Dabida giene, Xila kielienghala kieliese Dojia giene, isishi lugo wo. Hhe chanqi gounii giezhi nanxin kunlade banman giezho.
ACT 9:37 Hhe shihoude hhe giemere fuguse kunla beyeini waghadene lou jiere teiwo.
ACT 9:38 LidaYepaghala chada wo. BeduruLidade bikui tujila sonosusenu ghua kunyi peizhi echighadene xiahua giezhi danwu bu giezhi bijienyi hhende ghujighan yo giezho.
ACT 9:39 Beduru qiizhi hhelare hhantu kuruse kunla uduru lou jiere khireiwo. Olon guafu biereila Bedurui kanzide beidene wilazhi Dojia hhelare hhantu bikude giesan lizii jien, mienzii jienlai uzheghawo.
ACT 9:40 Beduru kunlai man kieliezhi ghadane khighadene xiutuliezhi onxian giewo. Ingie fugusan kunyi miende ochiradene kieliewo, "Dabida, bosizhe!" Ingiese hhe nudunne nie Bedurui chanla bosi ire souwo.
ACT 9:41 Beduru khaghalane hhei fui bosighawo. Ingie shentulai, guafulai uru orozhe, Dojiai amitu hhelade jiuizhi ogiwo.
ACT 9:42 Ene shiqin Yepade man chonji kurudene olon kunla Ezhanyi xianxin giewo.
ACT 9:43 Khuinashi BeduruYepani nie arasun giesan Ximunyi giede ezighancha souwo.
ACT 10:1 Kaisaliyade nie kunyi niereini Geniliu giene. Hheshi Idali buduitonni baifuzhan wo.
ACT 10:2 Hheshi nie xienliantu kun wo. Nie gie kunlai man Hudai zunjizho. Da nanxin kunlade olon banman giezhi Hudase chan onxian giezho.
ACT 10:3 Niudude xiawu 3 jien olukude hhe zhoujin mutun qinchude chanlase Hudai nie qienxien oro ire Geniliu giezhi uruwo.
ACT 10:4 Geniliu xianxide nie uzhe ayizhi kieliewo, "Ezhan, yan shiqin wo?" Qienxien kieliewo, "Chi onxian giesan, nanxin kunlade banman giesanla Hudai melie echizhi jilawo.
ACT 10:5 Ede chi kun peizhi Yepase Beduru giesan Ximunni xinlazhi ire.
ACT 10:6 Hhe nie arasun jiagun giesan Ximunyi giede souzho. Gieni haibienzide wo."
ACT 10:7 Hhende kielien kieliesan qienxien yoladene Geniliu giene ghua hojini, pse hhei chan ushilasan nie xienliantu buduini uru ire
ACT 10:8 ene shiqinyi man kieliezhi ogidene peizhi Yepade echighawo.
ACT 10:9 Khuichudu hhela yozhi hhe chenshide kurukude Beduru zhunwude gie jiere onxian giele khireiwo.
ACT 10:10 Hhe oliesuzhi ijiene giezho. Kunla ijiuni zhunbei giekude Beduru zhoujin mutun nie ghudureqi chanlase
ACT 10:11 asiman keizhi hoxian nie fugie popu mutun dunxi bouzhewo. Jieran gozii banladene zemin jiere bou irewo.
ACT 10:12 Hhe sudoro zemin jieredu yanyanji jieran zhuazhuatu chushen, ghughei, pse asiman jiere musisanla wine.
ACT 10:13 Nie shenyin irezhi hhende kieliewo, "Beduru, bosizhedene ala ijie."
ACT 10:14 Ingiese Beduru kieliewo, "Ezhan, ulie olune. Ganjin wini, zannannilai bi ijiezhi ese daozho."
ACT 10:15 2 hui shenyin pse hhende kieliewo, "Huda ganjin wo giesanni chi ganjin uwo giezhi bu kielie."
ACT 10:16 Ingiezhi ghureifashi hhe dunxilai deigo asiman jiere agi khireiwo.
ACT 10:17 Beduru zhoujin mutun chanlasanshi yan isi wo giezhi zhughedene zhen sumulakude Geniliu peisan kunla asazhi Ximunyi gieni wijien konde beizho.
ACT 10:18 Hhela waradazhi, "Beduru giesan Ximun enende souzhoye?" giezhi asazho.
ACT 10:19 Beduru dou zhoujin mutun chanlasei sumulakude Shenlin hhende kieliewo, "Ghuran kun chii ereizho.
ACT 10:20 Bosi, boudene yama bu sumulazhi hhelare hhantu echi. Hhelashi bi ireghasan wo."
ACT 10:21 Ingiese Beduru boudene hhelade kieliewo, "Bishi ta ereisan kun wo. Ta yangiezhi irezho?"
ACT 10:22 Hhela kieliewo, "Baifuzhan Geniliushi Hudai zunjisan nie gou kun wo. Yutai kunla man hhei zunzhun giene. Nie zhiguitu qienxien hhende kieliezhi chii xinlazhi giedene iredene chi jianjisei chenlie giezho."
ACT 10:23 Beduru hhelai uruzhi oro nie xii soughawo. Khuichudu zhunbei gie hhelare hhantu echiwo. Yepani giedun gaijiulaye hhantu echiwo.
ACT 10:24 Pse niudude hhela Kaisaliyade kuruwo. Geniliu qingu, gou zhanlienlane uruzhi ire hhelai sagheizho.
ACT 10:25 Beduru orone giekude Geniliu hhei jienliedene kon kondeni papalazhi beiiwo.
ACT 10:26 Beduru hhei fei bosigha kieliewo, "Bosizhe. Bishiye nie kun wo."
ACT 10:27 Beduru hheghala kielienduzhi orose olon kunla hhantulasei chanlawo.
ACT 10:28 Ingie hhelade kieliewo, "Bijien Yutai kun niman kunghala laiwon giezhi hhantulase ese olusei ta goyane mejienema, yan kunyiliuzhe ganjin uwo, zannan wo giezhi kieliese ese olusei Huda made uzheghawo.
ACT 10:29 Ingiese ta mii xinlakude bi tuichi ese giezhi irewo. Ede bi tande asaye, ta mii yan shiqinde xinlazho?"
ACT 10:30 Geniliu kieliewo, "Jierudu melie ene shihoude bi giedene onxian giezho. Xiawu 3 jiende wo. Menzhali nie rouiku jien musisan kun mii melie beidene
ACT 10:31 kieliezho, 'Geniliu, chi onxian giesan, nanxin kunlade banman giesanlai Huda chenliezhi jilawo.
ACT 10:32 Ingiese chi kun peizhi Yepase Beduru giesan Ximunyi xinlazhi ire. Hhe haibienzini nie arasun jiagun giesan Ximunyi giede souzho.'
ACT 10:33 Ingiese bi deigo kun peizhi chii xinlaghale echiwo. Chi irese gou wo. Ede bijien Ezhan chade fenfulasan kielienlai man chenliene giezhi Hudai melie hhantulazho."
ACT 10:34 Ingiese Beduru kielie qiiwo, "Huda kunlade pienxin ulie giekui bi shuhua mejiewo.
ACT 10:35 Alinie gojiai kunlaliuzhe Hudai zunjizhi olusei giese Huda jienliene.
ACT 10:36 Taye mejieku mutun Huda yanyanjini Ezhan Ersa Mexihani tungo giezhi pinnantu gouxioxi daolini Isilie kunlade chonjizhi ogiwo.
ACT 10:37 Yaheiya xili giekui jianjizhi daodene ene daolii Jialilise kaishi giezhi Yudaya go oronlade chonji kuruwo.
ACT 10:38 Nasale kun Ersade Huda Shenlin, nenlini olon ogiwo. Huda hheghala hhantushi hhe gochude yozhi gouni giezho. Ibilisi heisanlai man uzhezhi goudaghawo.
ACT 10:39 Bijien hhe kun Yutai kunni oronde, Yelusalende giesan shiqinlade ganzhen beine. Kunla hhei mutun jiere guaidene alawo.
ACT 10:40 Ghurudude Huda hhei aminne olughazhi kunlade chanlaghawo.
ACT 10:41 Soyuji kunlade ese chanlaghazhi zinie Huda sunghuzhi hhende ganzhen beighane giesan bijiende chanlaghawo. Bijienshi hhe fugusan kun dundase aminne oludene hhere hhantu ijiezhi ochisan kun wo.
ACT 10:42 Hhe bijiende fenfulazhi kunlade ene daolii chonji giewo. "Hheshijiu Huda sunghuzhi amitu kun, fugusan kunyi panjichen wo." giezhi ganzhen bei giezho.
ACT 10:43 Xienzhila man hhende ganzhen beizhi kieliewo, 'Hhei xianxin giesan kunla hhei niereghala zuini mienliene.'"
ACT 10:44 Beduru kielien kieliekude daoli chenliesan jien kunlai jiere Shenlin bouzhewo.
ACT 10:45 Bedurughala hhantu iresan Yutaini Mexihai xianxin giesan kunla Shenlinni nenjien niman kunlai jiere kie bouzhese ghanirakushi
ACT 10:46 hhela pseshiku kielienyi kieliezhi Hudashi fugie wo giezhi doulasei sonosuzho. Ingiese Beduru kieliewo,
ACT 10:47 "Enezighan kunla bijien mutun Shenlinyi jienliewo. Ede usughala hhelade xili gieghase kien danla shidane?"
ACT 10:48 Ingie fenfulazhi Ersa Mexihai niereghala hhelade xili gieghawo. Hhela pse Bedurui danlazhi giedudu soughawo.
ACT 11:1 Niman kunla Hudai kielienyi jienliesei shitula, Yudayani gaijiula sonosuwo.
ACT 11:2 BeduruYelusalende echise Yutaini Mexihai xianxin giesan kunla hhei sugiezhi kieliewo,
ACT 11:3 "Chi hetoune ese giesan kunlai giede echizhi dou hhelare hhantu ijiene?"
ACT 11:4 Ingiese Beduru ene shiqinni hhelade qiqiji kieliewo,
ACT 11:5 "Bi Yepa chenshide onxian giekude zhoujin mutun nie ghudureqi chanlase hoxian nie fugie popu mutun dunxi bouzhezhi jieran gozii banlazho. Asiman jierese bouzhe mii melie irewo.
ACT 11:6 Bi xianxide uzhese sudoro zemin jieredu jieran zhuazhuatu chushen, yewo, ghughei, pse asiman jiere musisanla wine.
ACT 11:7 Bi sonosuse nie shenyin made kieliewo, 'Beduru, bosizhedene ala ijie.'
ACT 11:8 Ingie bi kieliewo, 'Ezhan, ulie olune. Ganjin wini, zannannila mii amande orozhi ese daozho.'
ACT 11:9 2 hui shenyin asiman jierese kieliewo, 'Huda ganjin wo giesanni chi ganjin uwo giezhi bu kielie.'
ACT 11:10 Ingiezhi ghureifashi man asiman jiere agi khireiwo.
ACT 11:11 Zhen qingiekude Kaisaliyase mii xinlaghale iresan ghuran kun bijien sousan gie konde beizho.
ACT 11:12 Shenlin made fenfulazhi yama bu sumuladene hhelare hhantu echi giewo. Ingiese ene zhighon gaijiu mare hhantu echizhi bijien Geniliui giede orowo. Hhe bijiende kieliewo.
ACT 11:13 Geniliu matugiezhi nie qienxienyi chanladene hhei giede beizhi chi kun peizhi Yepase Beduru giesan Ximunyi xinlazhi ire.
ACT 11:14 Hhe chii nie gie kunlai jiuiku daolii chade kieliene giesan kielienyi bijiende kieliewo.
ACT 11:15 Bi dei jianji qiise Shenlin hhelai jiere bouzhewo. Eqighandei matanyi jiere bouzhesan niekielien wo.
ACT 11:16 Ingiese Yaheiya usughala xili gieghawoma, tai Shenlinghala xili gieghane giesan Ezhanyi kielienyi bi sumula irewo.
ACT 11:17 Huda hhelade ogisan nenjien matan Ezhan Ersa Mexihai xianxin giekude matande ogisan nenjienghala niekielien wo. Bishi kien wo? Hudai duii shidanu?"
ACT 11:18 Hhela ene kielienyi chenliedene yama ese kieliezhi qinse Huda niman kunladeye geizhen giezhi amin ireku jihui ogiwo giezhi Hudai kuaizho.
ACT 11:19 Ene shihoude Siqifanni shiqin jiere biisan kunla sandazhi Feiniji, Saipulusi, Anqiyade echidene zinie Yutai kunlade Hudai kielienyi jianjizhoma,
ACT 11:20 Saipulusi, Gulinaise iresan niezhan kunla Anqiyade kurudene Xila kunladeye Ezhan Ersai gouxioxii jianjizho.
ACT 11:21 Ezhanni nenli hhelare hhantushi Ezhanyi xianxin giezhi shunjisan kun olonnudazho.
ACT 11:22 Ene xioxi Yelusalenni jiohuii kunlai chighinde echiwo. Ingie hhela Banabai peizhi Anqiyade echighawo.
ACT 11:23 Hhe kurudene Hudai nenjienyi chanla bayasuzhi kunlade khidunde beidene izhi Ezhanni koui giezhi sughazhi kieliezho.
ACT 11:24 Banabashi nie gou kun wo. Hhende Shenlin duruzhi Hudade kouiku xianxin gieku fugie wo. Ingiese olon kunla Ezhande shunjiwo.
ACT 11:25 Hhe Dashuse Saoloi ereile echi,
ACT 11:26 ereizhi oludene uduru Anqiyade echiwo. Hhe ghuala duduji niehon hhe oronni jiohuini kunlaghala hhantulazhi olon kunlade surughazho. Tujilai Anqiyase tou 1 hui Mexihani tuji giezhi uruzhi qiizho.
ACT 11:27 Hhe xienzide giedun xienzhila Yelusalense Anqiyade bouzhi irewo.
ACT 11:28 Hhelai dundadu nie kunyi niereini Yajiabu giene. Bosi iredene duya jiere honnien kuzhene giezhi Shenlinyi tungo giezhi melie kieliewo. Ene shiqin Kelaoji gonjiku shihoude fashen giewo.
ACT 11:29 Ingiese tujila zhao goyane nenlighala Yudayade sousan gaijiulade baer khughozhi echighane giezhi jiejin giewo.
ACT 11:30 Hhela baerni ghuradene BanabaSaolo ghualai peizhi zhanlaolai hhende khughozhi echighawo.
ACT 12:1 Hhe shihoude Hherode honshan jiohuini niezhan kunlai heiwo.
ACT 12:2 Khudoghoghala Yaheiyani gaii Yagebui alawo.
ACT 12:3 Hhe uzhese Yutai kunla ene shiqinde xiqishi Beduruiye bareighale echiwo. Hheshi zhen Tanmien Jieni udu wo.
ACT 12:4 Bedurui barei agi bafanzide khadene jieran duini buduilade uzheghazho. Nie duide jieran kun wo. Jiulidaosan Jie daose bexinlai melie hhei panjine giezho.
ACT 12:5 Bedurui bafanzide khase jiohuini kunla hhende oluzhi Hudase hende onxian giezho.
ACT 12:6 HherodeBedurui panjiku meliedu xii, Bedurui ghua qieshenghala sozilazhi ghua buduini dunda kijieghazho. Sagheisan kunla bafanzi wijien ghadane sagheizho.
ACT 12:7 Menzhali Ezhanyi qienxien xienjighazhi bafanzi sudoro gon zhouizho. Qienxien Bedurui lebadei peizhi xiereigha kieliewo, "Ghujighan bosizhe." Ingie qieshen hhei kha jierese anda bouwo.
ACT 12:8 Yodaine banlazhi maheine musi giezhi qienxien hhende kieliese hhe qingiezhi giewo. Qienxien pse kieliewo, "Jienne musidene mii dagha."
ACT 12:9 Beduru khizhedene hhei daghawo. Qienxien giesanshi zhenni bikui mejie dazho, zhoujin wo giezho.
ACT 12:10 Bafanzii ji 1 gon ji 2 gonyi daodene chenshide khireiku qieman shida irese hhe wijien goyane niewo. Hhela khizhedene nie moni yozhi daose qienxien deigo hhense likai giewo.
ACT 12:11 Beduru minbairedene kieliewo, "Ede bi zhenzhenji mejiewo. Ezhan qienxienne peizhi mii Hherodei khase, Yutai kunlai xiwon giesanse jiuizhi khizhewo."
ACT 12:12 Beduru nie sumuladene Mereiyeni giede echiwo. Hheshi Make giesan Yaheiyai anani wo. Hhende olon kunla hhantulazhi onxian giezho.
ACT 12:13 Beduru wijienyi nie eghise Loda giesan nie hoji oqin wijien niele irewo.
ACT 12:14 Hhe Bedurui shenqii mejiedene bayasuzhi wijienyi ese nie, holuzhi echi kunlade kieliewo, "Beduru wijien ghadane beizho!"
ACT 12:15 Hhela kieliewo, "Chi fenjiulizho!" Hoji oqin izhigie kieliezho, "Hhe enbene!" Hhela kieliezho, "Hheshi Bedurui qienxien wo."
ACT 12:16 Beduru ese beidene wijienyi eghizho. Hhela wijienyi niedene chanlase ghanirazho.
ACT 12:17 Beduru khane zhadeighazhi hhelai shenqi bu khizhe giezho. Ingie hhelade Ezhan matugiezhi hhei bafanzise uduruzhi khizheghasei kieliewo. Pse ene shiqinni Yagebu psedu gaijiulade kielie giedene khizhe, psedu oronde echiwo.
ACT 12:18 Ogheidene buduila londundunde Beduru khala echisei mejie dazho.
ACT 12:19 Hherode hhei ereizhi olu dase sagheisan kunlade asadene hhelai ala giezhi fenfulawo. Khuinashi HherodeYudayase likai gie Kaisaliyade bouzhi hhende souwo.
ACT 12:20 Hherode honshan Tuilo kun, Xidun kunlade hokuzho. Ene ghua oronni kunla honshanni oronse taran ijiezho. Ingie honshanni giei gonjisan Bolasidui kielie shundaghadene hhantu Hherodei ochirale echi goudane giezhi xiahua giezho.
ACT 12:21 Jinjisan udude Hherode honshan jienne musi wizi jierene souzhi kunlade jianjizho.
ACT 12:22 Ingiese bexinla waradazhi kieliezho, "Eneshi kunni shenqi pusho, hudai shenqi wo!"
ACT 12:23 Hherode kunla kuaikui Hudade ese ogise Ezhanyi qienxien deigo faizhi ghugheighala zhou alaghawo.
ACT 12:24 Hudai kielien yebeiseye ondazhi xianxin giesan kunla olodozho.
ACT 12:25 BanabaSaologhala renwune onchen giedene Make giesan Yaheiyai uduru Yelusalende khareiwo.
ACT 13:1 Anqiyani jiohuide giedun xienzhi, loushi wine. Banaba, heiren giesan Ximien, Gulinai kun Luqiu, Hherode onghala hhantu fugiedasan Manien, pse Saolo wo.
ACT 13:2 Hhela Ezhanyi beiizhi orozo bareikude Shenlin kieliewo, "Ta BanabaSaoloi sunghudene made jie. Bi hhelai uruzhi wiliene gieghane."
ACT 13:3 Ingie hhela orozo bareizhi onxian giedene hhelai jiere khane teizhi peizhi echighawo.
ACT 13:4 Hhelai Shenlin peizhi Xiliujide boughadene hhense chon souzhi Saipulusi daode kuruwo.
ACT 13:5 Hhende Salami geidoude echi Yutai kunlai huitanlade Hudai kielienyi jianjizho. Yaheiya hhelade banman giezho.
ACT 13:6 Hhela Saipulusi nie daoni yozhi zuihoude Pafude irewo. Hhende nie fashu shuaisan kunyi penjiwo. Hheshi nie xienzhii maochun giesan Yutai kun wo. Niereini Bayesu giene.
ACT 13:7 Hhe kun Shiqiu-Baolo giesan zunlighala jiodao daizho. Shiqiu-Baoloshi nie aghelitu kun wo, hhe BanabaSaologhalai xinlazhi ire Hudai kielienyi chenliene giezho.
ACT 13:8 IlimaBanabaSaologhalai jiohorozhi zunlii ene xinyanni ulie xianxin gieghane giezho. Ilimai isishi fashu shuaisan kun wo.
ACT 13:9 Baolo giesan Saolode Shenlin durudene hhei aralazhi kieliewo,
ACT 13:10 "Chishi Ibilisini kewon wo. Chi yanyanji gounii fandui giezho. Chade yanyanji piendakui doghunni duruzho. Chi Ezhanni zhendaoni wirulaghakui da ulie beinu?
ACT 13:11 Ede Ezhan chii faise chi sugho gholuzhi zhanshi jiere naranyi chanla dane!" Ingiese nudunni deigo borolozhi kharaladene simiendene moqioluzhi mo uduruku kun ereizho.
ACT 13:12 Zunli ene fashen giesan shiqinyi chanladene Ezhanyi daoli ghudure wo giezhi xianxin giewo.
ACT 13:13 Baolotan Pafuse chon souzhi Panfeiliyani Biejiade irewo. Yaheiya hhelase likai gie Yelusalende echiwo.
ACT 13:14 Baolotan Biejiase likai giedene yozhi Bixijini Anqiyade irewo. Hhamuraku udude huitande orozhi souwo.
ACT 13:15 Guijinshu, xienzhishui onshi baraghadene huitan gonjisan kunla kun peizhi hhelade kielieghawo, "Gaijiula, kunlade yan surughaku kielien bise kielie."
ACT 13:16 Ingie Baolo bosizhe khane nie zhadeigha kieliewo, "Isilie kunla, pse Hudai zunjisan niman kunla, chenliendu!
ACT 13:17 Ene Isilieni Huda mai xienrenlai sunghuzho. Hhela Aijide soukude Huda hhelai hendaghazhi fugie nenlighalane Aijise uduruzhi khizhewo.
ACT 13:18 Hontande hhelai 40 nien rennai giezho.
ACT 13:19 Jianan oronni dolon minzui widaghazhi hhe oronyi hhelade ogiwo.
ACT 13:20 Enezighan shiqinla chabudu 450 nien olune. Khuinashi Huda hhelade panjiku noyen ogizhi izhi Samuer xienzhii shihou kuruwo.
ACT 13:21 Ene shihoude hhela Hudase nie honshan kerewo. Ingie Huda Bienyamin pai dundadedu Jishini kewon Saoloi hhelade 40 nien honshan danlaghawo.
ACT 13:22 Ingie Saoloi widaghadene Dawudeni hhelade honshan danlagha, hhende oluzhi kieliewo, 'Bi ereisan Yexini kewon Dawude made talazho. Hhe mii jihuai chengun olughane.'"
ACT 13:23 "Huda dain giesan mutun Dawudeni houdeise Isilie kunlade nie jiuichen Ersai khizheghawo.
ACT 13:24 Hhe iretula Yaheiya jien Isilie kunlade, "Geizhen giedene xilini jienlie." giezhi chonjizho.
ACT 13:25 Yaheiya renwune onchen giekude kieliewo, 'Ta sumulase bishi kien wo? Bishi hhe pusho. Hhe mii khuinase irene. Bi hhende mahei deizi andaghaseye pei dane.'"
ACT 13:26 "Gaijiula, Iburaheimuni houdeila, pse Hudai zunjisan niman kunla, ene jiuiku daolishijiu matande ogisanwo.
ACT 13:27 Yelusalende sousan kun, hhelai lindaola Ersai tani dazho. Hhela niefanie hhamuraku udude onshisan xienzhii kielienyi dunjire dazhi Ersade zui jinjise xienzhila kieliesan mutun gholuwo.
ACT 13:28 Hhende yama fuguku zui ereizhi oludawoma, hhela Biladoi xiahua giezhi hhei ala giewo.
ACT 13:29 Ingiezhi jinwun jiere hhei zhiizhi kieliesanla man gholuwo. Ingiedene hhei mutun jierese agi bouzhe mezade teiwo.
ACT 13:30 Ingieliuzhe Huda hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughawo.
ACT 13:31 Ersaghala hhantu Jialilise Yelusalende khisan kunlade Ersa ezighancha xienjighawo. Hhela ede bexinlai dunda Ersade ganzhen beizho.
ACT 13:32 Bijienye ene gouxioxini tande chonjizhi ogine. Eneshi Huda matanyi xienrenlade dain giesanwo.
ACT 13:33 Ersai aminne olughazhi matan houdei danlasan kunde chenjighawo. Zeburei ji 2 piende jilasan mutun, 'Chishi mii kewon wo. Enedu bi chade ada danlawo.'
ACT 13:34 Pse fugusan kun dundase Ersai aminne olughazhi ulie fughaku shiqinde Huda ingiezhi kieliezhi daowo, 'Bi Dawudede ogisan zhigui, kekaotu nenjienni tande ogiye.'
ACT 13:35 Da nie Zeburei jiereye kieliewo, 'Chi zhiguitu kunne ulie fughane.'"
ACT 13:36 "Dawude duyade bikude Hudai isii zunjizhoma, duya ijiedene xienrenlareni hhantu bulase fuwo.
ACT 13:37 Zinie Huda aminne olughasan hhe ese fuwo."
ACT 13:38 "Ingiese gaijiula, ta mejiendu. Ene kunyi tungo giezhi zuini mienlieku daolii tande chonjizhi ogiwo.
ACT 13:39 Musai guijinghala giese gounide sana danema, Ersai xianxin giesan kunlai man yanseliuzhe gounide sanane.
ACT 13:40 Ingiese ta xioxin gie, pse xienzhila kieliesan tai jiere gholune.
ACT 13:41 'Uzhe, ta uzhezhi xiniesan kunla, jindazhi fugune. Bi tai xienzide kunla tande kielieliuzhe ta xianxin gie daku fugie shiqin giene. Ingiese ta ayidene fugune.'"
ACT 13:42 BaoloBanabaghala huitanse khizhekude kunla hhelai xinlazhi pse nie hhamuraku udude enezighan kielienyi hhelade pse jianji giezho.
ACT 13:43 Sanhui giedene olon Yutai kun, Yutaijioni suisan niman kunla Baolo, Banabaghalai daghazho. Hheghala hhelade Hudai nenjiende chan kouizhi gie giezhi jianjizhi goude kieliewo.
ACT 13:44 Pse nie hhamuraku udude nie chenshini kunla man hhantulazhi ire Ezhanyi kielienyi chenliene giezho.
ACT 13:45 Yutai kunla imeghei kun iresei chanladene dubiliezhi Baolo kieliesan kielienyi fandui giezhi sugiezho.
ACT 13:46 Ingiese BaoloBanabaghala danzine fugiedaghazhi kieliewo, "Hudai kielienyi xien tande kieliese indanji woma, ta ene daolii ulie jienliene. Ta goyane ene chanqiku aminni pei dane giezhi jiejin giezho. Ingiese bijien niman kunlai hhende echine.
ACT 13:47 Ezhan bijiende ingiezhi fenfulawo, 'Bi chii niman kunlade gon gholughadene jiuiku nenjienni deilazhi duyani uzhude echigha giezhi jinjiwo.'"
ACT 13:48 Niman kunla ene kielienyi chenliesenu bayasuzhi Ezhanyi kielien gou wo giezho. Chanqiku aminni ogine giezhi jinjisan kunla man xianxin giewo.
ACT 13:49 Ingiese Hudai kielienyi hhe oronde chonji kurughawo.
ACT 13:50 Yutai kunla Hudai beiisan minshentu biereilai, pse hhe chenshii zhanlaolai shanjizhi Baolo, Banabaghalai heizhi oronsene tou khighawo.
ACT 13:51 Hheghala kunlai fandui giezhi kon jieredu turane kui boughadene Igeniende echiwo.
ACT 13:52 Tujilade bayasuku, Shenlin duruzho.
ACT 14:1 Xianxianji shiqin Igeniendeye gholuwo. BaoloBanabaghala Yutai kunlai huitande orozhi daolii goude jianjise olon Yutai kun, Xila kunla xianxin giewo.
ACT 14:2 Ulie shunjisan Yutai kunla niman kunlai shanjizhi gaijiulade doghunni sumulaghazho.
ACT 14:3 Ingiese hheghala hhende oloncha souzhi Ezhande oluzhi danzine fugiedagha giezhi kieliezho. Ezhan hhelade nenli ogizhi ghudureqi, fugie shiqin giedene hhela jianjisan Hudai nenjientu daolide ganzhen beizho.
ACT 14:4 Ingiese chenshini kunla lianbanzi gholudene ibanlie Yutai kunyi daghazho, pse ibanlie shitulai daghazho.
ACT 14:5 Niezhan niman kunla, Yutai kunla, noyenlarene hhantuladene ghua shitulai zayalazhi tashighala eghine giezhi jiejin giewo.
ACT 14:6 Shitula ene shiqinni mejiedene holuzhi Ligaonini Luside, Tebi ghua chenshide, pse zhouwini oronlade echiwo.
ACT 14:7 Hhela hhe oronlade gouxioxini chonjizho.
ACT 14:8 Lusidede ghua konde lilian witu nie canfei souzho. Zhayaghasanse mo yozhi ese daozho.
ACT 14:9 Baolo jianjisanyi hhe kun chenliezho. Baolo hhei goude uzhese hhende goudaku xianxin gieku zhughe wine.
ACT 14:10 Ingie fugiede kieliewo, "Chi ghua konne zhidaghazhi bosizhe!" Ingiese hhe kun jiuli bosi ire yo qiiwo.
ACT 14:11 Olon kunla Baolo giesan shiqinyi chanladene Ligaonii kielienghala fugiede kieliewo, "Nigiedala kun gholudene mai dunda irewo!"
ACT 14:12 Ingie Banabai Zhousi giezhi uruzho. Baolo zhomen jianjise Xiermi giezhi uruzho.
ACT 14:13 Chenshi ghadaneshiku Zhousi mioni buwa giedun fughe laizhi chizhe bareidene chenshi wijien melie irewo. Olon kunlare hhantu shitulade khughozhi beiine giezho.
ACT 14:14 BanabaBaologhala sonosudene jienne sidakeigha, olon kunlai dunda holu oro fugiede kieliewo,
ACT 14:15 "Dajiala, ta yale intu shiqin giene? Bijienshiye kun wo, tanre niekielien wo. Bijien enende irezhi gouxioxii chonjikushi tai gou witu dunxilase likai gieghazhi asiman, zemin, hai, pse hhei sudorodu shihenilai man zhayaghasan zhenzhenji chanqiku Hudade shunjighane giezho.
ACT 14:16 Eqighanku gonyinde Huda go minzulani durare teizhi yan giese gie giezho.
ACT 14:17 Ingieliuzhe Huda gou shiqin giezhi goyane chan zhenmin giezho. Asiman jierese ghura bouzheghazhi, nanshihoude yanyanji osighazhi, tai chudughadene zhughede bayasughazho."
ACT 14:18 Shitula ene kielienyi kieliedene olon kunlai danlazhi beigha dazhi ingiezhi goyane seigie ese beiighawo.
ACT 14:19 Niezhan Yutai kunla Anqiyase Igeniense ire olon kunlai kielie shundagha Baoloi tashighala eghi, hhe fuguwo giedene chenshi ghadane lai khighawo.
ACT 14:20 Tujila Baoloi kanzide wiqi beise hhe bosi ire chenshide orowo. Khuichudu hhe Banabaghala hhantu Tebide echiwo.
ACT 14:21 Hhela Tebide gouxioxii chonjidene olon kunlai tuji gholughawo. Ingiedene hhela Luside, Igenienni jingo giezhi Anqiyade khareiwo.
ACT 14:22 Hhela tujilai zhugheini khiduzheghazhi izhi xianxin gie giezhi sughazhi kieliezho. "Matan Hudai gojiade orone giese bixi olon ku shouine."
ACT 14:23 Hhela go jiohuide zhanlaolai sunghudene ese ijiezhi onxian gie, hhelai xianxin giesan Ezhandei jiuizhi ogiwo.
ACT 14:24 Ingie ghuala Bixijini jingo giezhi Panfeiliyade echiwo.
ACT 14:25 Pse Biejiade Hudai kielienyi jianjidene Yadalide bouwo.
ACT 14:26 Hhense chon souzhi Anqiyade khareiwo. Anqiyashi chonjiku wiliede oluzhi ghua shitulai Hudai nenjiende jiuizhi ogisan oron wo. Ede onchen giedene khareizhi irewo.
ACT 14:27 Anqiyade kurudene jiohuini kunlai man uru ire Huda hhelai tungo giezhi matugie giesan shiqinlai, pse Huda niman kunlai xianxin gie qiighasei kieliezho.
ACT 14:28 Hhela hhende tujilare hhantu oloncha souwo.
ACT 15:1 Yudayase bouzhesan giedun kunla gaijiulade Musani guijinghala hetoune ulie giese jiui dane giezhi sughazho.
ACT 15:2 BaoloBanabaghala hhelare hende jianjiduzhi zhenjinduse jiohuini kunla Baolo, Banaba, pse giedun kunlai ene shiqinde Yelusalenni shitu, zhanlaolade asaghale echine giezhi jiejin giewo.
ACT 15:3 Ingiese jiohuini kunla hhelai khughowo. Hhela Feiniji, Samaliyani daokude niman kunla Ersai xianxin giesei kieliese hhendedu gaijiula man hende bayasuzho.
ACT 15:4 Yelusalende kuruse shitu, zhanlao, jiohuini kunla hhelai jienliewo. Huda hhelare hhantu giesan shiqinlai man jiohuini kunlade kieliewo.
ACT 15:5 Giedun Falisai paini Ersai xianxin giesan kunla bosizhedene kieliewo, "Niman kunlai bixi hetoune gieghadene fenfulazhi Musani guijinni zunjighakuni wo."
ACT 15:6 Shitu, zhanlaola hhantulazhi ene shiqinni shanlian giewo.
ACT 15:7 Dajiala ene shiqinni oloncha jianjidudene Beduru bosizhe kieliewo, "Gaijiula, Huda melieshida tani dundase mii sunghuzhi niman kunla mase gouxioxini chenliedene xianxin giesei ta mejiene.
ACT 15:8 Kunyi zhugheni mejiechen Huda matande ogisan mutun niman kunladeye Shenlinni ogizhi hhelai jienliewo.
ACT 15:9 Dou xianxin giekughala hhelani zhughei ganjinraghawo. Hhelai uzheku matanre niekielien wo.
ACT 15:10 Ede ta yale Hudai shiizhi matan, matanyi xienrenla lai daku jiabanni tujilai ghuzhun jiere zhoghane?
ACT 15:11 Ulie olune, matanyi jiuikushi Ezhan Ersai nenjienghala wo. Hhelaye niekielien wo. Bijien ingiezhi xianxin giezho."
ACT 15:12 Olon kunla man yama shenqi uye khizhezhi Huda BanabaBaologhalai tungo giezhi niman kunlai dunda giesan ghudureqi, fugie shiqinlai chenliezho.
ACT 15:13 Hhela kielie baludene Yagebu kieliewo, "Gaijiula, mii kielienyi chenliendu.
ACT 15:14 Huda matugiezhi niman kunlai zhaogu giezhi tou 1 hui hhelani dundase bexinlai sunghudene goyanughun gholughasei Ximien kieliewo.
ACT 15:15 Eneshi xienzhila kieliesan kielienghala niekielien wo. Jinwun jiere huaizho,
ACT 15:16 'Enense khuinashi bi khareizhi iredene Dawudeni furasan gieni erchan bosizheghane. Tairesanni gie goudaghazhi erchan bosizheghane.
ACT 15:17 Ingiese feiliesan kunlai man Ezhanyi ereighane. Bi sunghuzhi goyanughun gholughasan niman kunlai man Ezhanyi ereighane.
ACT 15:18 Eneshi dei qiikude ene shiqinlai mejieghasan Ezhan kieliesan wo.'
ACT 15:19 Ingiese bi uzhese Hudade shunjisan niman kunlade chijia bu teidene
ACT 15:20 hhelade xin huaizhi nigiedade ogidene zannanshisan, lon kijieku, lei alasan, chusun, enelase gholodo giezhi fenfulase oluzho.
ACT 15:21 Ingiekushi eqighanse izhi go chenshide Musani guijinni jianjichen kun wine. Niefanie hhamuraku udude huitande onshizho."
ACT 15:22 Ingiedene shitu, zhanlao, jiohuini kunla hhelai dundase kun sunghuzhi Baolo, Banabare hhantu Anqiyade echighane giezhi jiejin giewo. Sunghusan kunshi Basaba giesan Yuda, pse Seila wo. Ene ghualashi jiohuini zhanlao wo.
ACT 15:23 Ingie hhelade bareighasan xin jiere kieliezho, "Ersai sudoro gaijiu danlasan shitu, zhanlaola Anqiya, Xiliya, Jilijiadedu xianxin giesan niman gaijiulade kielien asazho."
ACT 15:24 "Bijien sonosuse bijienni enense giedun kun khizhi echi kielienghala tai jiohoro giezhi tande nanran ese ogizho. Shijishan bijien hhelade yama ese fenfulazho.
ACT 15:25 Ingie dajiala tunyigie giedun kun sunghu peizhi bijien oresan Banaba, Baolore hhantu tai hhende echighawo.
ACT 15:26 Ene ghualashi mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihade oluzhi aminne ulie kerechen kun wo.
ACT 15:27 Ingiese bijien Yuda, Seilaghalai peizhi tande qinsi ene shiqinlai kielieghane.
ACT 15:28 Shenlin bijienre hhantu tunyi giezhi ene giedun zhunyoni shiqinse chugo psedu achanni tai jiere ulie teise gou wo giezho.
ACT 15:29 Ta nigiedade teisan, chusun, lei alasan, lon kijieku enelase gholoduse jiu oluwo. Tande salan gieye."
ACT 15:30 Hhelani peizhi Anqiyade bou, xianxin giesan kunlai uruzhi hhantulagha xinni jiuizhi ogiwo.
ACT 15:31 Xinni onshidene zhichi giesan goushi hhela bayasuzho.
ACT 15:32 Yuda, Seilaghalashiye xienzhi wo. Olon kielienghala gaijiulade surughazhi hhelai xianxin giekuni khiduzheghawo.
ACT 15:33 Hhela hhende nietan soudene gaijiula hhelai dafalazhi hhelai peizhi ireghasan Yelusalenni jiohuide pinnande echighawo.
ACT 15:35 Baolo, Banabaghala Anqiyade zhanshi souzhi olon kunlare hhantu kunlade sughazhi Ezhanyi kielienyi chonjizho.
ACT 15:36 Giedudu daodene BaoloBanabade kieliewo, "Matan khareizhi eqighandei Ezhanni kielienyi chonjisan go chenshide gaijiulani qinkonyi uzhele yoye."
ACT 15:37 BanabaMake giesan Yaheiyani uduruzhi echine giese
ACT 15:38 Make eqighandei Panfeiliyase likai giezhi hhelare hhantu wilie ese giewo giezhi Baolo hhei jiedui ulie udurune giezho.
ACT 15:39 Ingie ghuala hende jianjindu ghaghachawo. BanabaMakei uduru chon soudene Saipuluside echiwo.
ACT 15:40 BaoloSeilai sunghusenu gaijiula hhelai Ezhanni nenjiende jiuizhi ogise yo qiiwo.
ACT 15:41 BaoloXiliyani, Jilijiani yozhi go jiohuilani khiduzheghawo.
ACT 16:1 BaoloTebide echi, pse Lusidede kuruse hhende nie tuji wine. Niereini Qimotai giene. Ananishi Yutai kun wo, Ezhanyi xianxin giezho. Adanishi Xila kun wo.
ACT 16:2 Luside, Igenienni gaijiula man Qimotaini kuaizho.
ACT 16:3 Baolo hhei uduruzhi echine giezho. Hhe oronni Yutai kunla adanishi Xila kun bikui man mejiene. Ingie hhende hetoune giewo.
ACT 16:4 Hhela go chenshilai yozhi daokude Yelusalenni shitu, zhanlaola jinjisan guijinni xianxin giesan kunlade ogizhi zunjighazho.
ACT 16:5 Ingiese jiohuilani kunlai xianxin gieku khiduzhezhi kun niudunie olodowo.
ACT 16:6 Shenlin hhelai danlazhi Yaxiyade Hudai kielienyi ese jianjighase hhela Fulijia, Jialatai oronlade echiwo.
ACT 16:7 Meixiyani bienzide kurudene Bituinide echine giese Ersai ruhher ese echighawo.
ACT 16:8 Ingiese hhela Meixiyani jingo giezhi Teloyade bouwo.
ACT 16:9 Xienidei Baolo zhoujin mutun chanlawo. Niekozi Maqidun kun beidene hhei xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Maqidunde daozhedene bijiende banman gie."
ACT 16:10 Baolo zhoujin mutun chanlase bijien deigo Maqidunde echine giezho. Bijien jiejin giese Huda bijienyi uruzhi hhe oronni kunlade gouxioxini chonjighane giezho.
ACT 16:11 Ingiese bijien Teloyase chon souzhi zhijie Samotelade echidene khuichudu Niyapolide kuruwo.
ACT 16:12 Hhense Feilibide kuruwo. Feilibishi Maqidun orondedu nie zhunyo chenshi wo, Loma gonjizho. Bijien ene chenshide giedudu souwo.
ACT 16:13 Hhamuraku udude bijien chenshini wijiense khirei nie moron bienzide echiwo. Sumulase hhende nie onxian gieku oron wine giezho. Bijien soudene hhantulasan biereilade daoli jianjiwo.
ACT 16:14 Chenliesan kun dunda Tuiyatuila chenshini nie zihun bosi huisan bierei wo. Niereini Lijiya giene. Hhe Hudai beiizho. Baolo jianjikude Ezhan hheni zhugheni keighase hhe goude chenliezho.
ACT 16:15 Hhe bierei, pse nie gie kunladeni man xili gieghawo. Ingie bijienyi xiahua giezhi kieliewo, "Ta bishi Ezhanni zhenzhenji xianxin giesan wo giese mii giede yodene sou." Ingie bijienyi ninguru danlawo.
ACT 16:16 Niefade bijien onxian gieku oronde echikude nie sheitan heisan hoji oqin irewo. Hhe fashu shuaizhi loubanladene baer olon ireghazho.
ACT 16:17 Ene oqin Baolo, pse bijienyi daghadene onghonozhi kieliewo, "Enezighan kunlashi Zui Undu Hudai hojila wo. Hhela tande jiuiku daolini chonjine!"
ACT 16:18 Hhe ingiezhi ezighancha onghonose Baolo pofensadene ochira daozhe sheitande kieliewo, "Bi Ersa Mexihani niereghala chii fenfulaye, hhei jierese khizhe!" Hhe sheitan danshi khizhewo.
ACT 16:19 Hoji oqinni loubanla uzhese baer ireku xiwon widase BaoloSeilaghalai bareidene geidoude khirei noyenyi shida lai echighawo.
ACT 16:20 Hhelai laidene noyenlai shida ire kieliewo, "Enezighan kunlashi Yutai kun wo, mai chenshini daolon giezho.
ACT 16:21 Hhela matan Loma kunla jienlie dazhi gie daku jiomun chonjizho."
ACT 16:22 Olon kunlaye hhantuladene hhelai fandui giezho. Panjiku noyenla fenfulazhi hhelai jienni teighadene banbanghala eghi giezho.
ACT 16:23 Hhelai hende eghidene bafanzide khawo. Sagheisan kunde goude uzhe giezhi fenfulawo.
ACT 16:24 Sagheisan kun ene minlinni jienliedene hhelani zui jizii bafanzide khazhi ghua kon jierei jieliu zhoghawo.
ACT 16:25 Banye olukudeni BaoloSeilaghala onxian giezhi Hudade doulazho. Fanrenlaye chenliezho.
ACT 16:26 Menzhali zemin hende gojiolu bafanzi jiziye gojioluwo. Ingie bafanzi wijienla man kei echi soyuji fanrenlani jieliu man andawo.
ACT 16:27 Sagheisan kun xiereise bafanzi wijienla man keise fanrenla man holuwo giedene khudoghone choui khizhe goyane fugune giezho.
ACT 16:28 Ingiekude Baolo fugiede waradazhi kieliewo, "Goyane bu shanji! Bijien man enende wo!"
ACT 16:29 Sagheisan kun zhulai kerezhi ire, jiuli bou, pugharazhi BaoloSeilani melie papalawo.
ACT 16:30 Ingie hhelani uduru khizhe kieliewo, "Gujiula, bi matugiese jiuine?"
ACT 16:31 Hhela kieliewo, "Ezhan Ersani xianxin gie. Ingiese chi, chii nie giechiliei man jiuine."
ACT 16:32 Ingie Ezhanni kielienyi hhei nie giechiliede jianjizhi chenlieghawo.
ACT 16:33 Yen hhe xii hhe shihoude sagheisan kun hhelani uduruzhi echi shankoulaini waghazhi ogiwo. Ingiedene hhe nie giechiliede man xili gieghawo.
ACT 16:34 Ingie sagheisan kun hhelai uduruzhi giedene echi budan ijieghawo. Hhe nie giechilie Hudai xianxin giese hende bayasuzho.
ACT 16:35 Khuichudu ogheise noyenla gunnanjilai peizhi iregha "Hhe ghua kunyi andagha." giezhi kieliewo.
ACT 16:36 Ingiese sagheisan kun Baolode kieliewo, "Panjiku noyenla tai andagha giezhi minlin xiaiwo. Ede ta khidene pinnande echi."
ACT 16:37 Baolo kieliewo, "Bijienshi Loma kun wo. Bijiende zui ese jinjidene olon kunlai melie bijienni eghizhi dou bafanzide khawo. Ede bijienni zhonmenji andaghanu? Ene ulie olune. Hhela goyalane irezhi bijienni uduzhi khireigha gie."
ACT 16:38 Gunnanjila ene kielienyi noyenlade kieliese noyenla hhelashi Loma kun wo giese ayizho.
ACT 16:39 Ingiedene ire hhelai sidaghazhi kielie, uduruzhi khizhedene, "Hhe chenshise likai gie!" giezhi xiahua giewo.
ACT 16:40 Ghuala bafanzise khizhedene Lijiyani giede echi gaijiulai ochira, zhichi giedene yolawo.
ACT 17:1 BaoloSeilaghala Anfeipoli, Yaboloniyani daodene Qiesalonijiade irewo. Hhende Yutai kunni nie huitan wine.
ACT 17:2 Baolo suchanku xigonghala hhende orozhi lienji ghuran hhamuraku udude kunlare jinwun kielienduzho.
ACT 17:3 Mexiha bixi shouku giedene fugusan kun dundase aminne olukui hhelade jianjizhi zhenmin giezho. Pse kieliewo, "Bi tande chonjizhi ogisan ene Ersashijiu Mexiha wo."
ACT 17:4 Hhelai dunda ezighan kunlai kielie shundaghase BaoloSeilai daghazho. Pse Hudai beiisan olon Xila kun, minshentu biereilaye olon daghazho.
ACT 17:5 Xianxin ulie giechen Yutai kunla dubiliezhi geidouse ezighan liumanlai uruzhi hhantulagha nie chenshii kunlai shanjidene Yasoni giede chunji oro, BaoloSeila ghualai ereizhi bexinlade jiuine giezho.
ACT 17:6 Ereizhi olu dadene Yaso, giedun gaijiulai laisenu hhe oronni noyenyi shida echi waradazhi kieliewo, "Qienxiani daolon giesan ene iban kunla enende irezho.
ACT 17:7 Yaso giedene hhelai jienliewo. Enezighan kunla man Ersa giechen da nie honshan wine giezhi Kaisai minlinyi fanjizho."
ACT 17:8 Olon kunla hhe oronni noyenla ene kielienyi chenliedene jindazho.
ACT 17:9 Ingiedene Yaso, psedu kunlai baer faidene andaghawo.
ACT 17:10 Xienidei gaijiula BaoloSeilaghalai deigo Biliyade echighawo. Ghuala kudene Yutai kunlai huitande echiwo.
ACT 17:11 Biliyani kunla Qiesalonijia kunlase sixian keifan giezho. Daolini rexinde jienliezhi niudunie xianxide jinwunni chaizhi ene daoli oluzhou ese oluzho giezho.
ACT 17:12 Ingie hhelai dunda olon kun xianxin giewo. Xilani minshentu bierei, ere kunlaye choghon uwo.
ACT 17:13 Qiesalonijiani Yutai kunla BaoloBiliyade Hudai kielienyi chonjisei mejiedene hhende echizhi kunlai shanjizhi londaghazho.
ACT 17:14 Ingiese gaijiula deigo Baoloi haibienzide echighawo. SeilaQimotaighala yen Biliyade feiliewo.
ACT 17:15 Baoloi khughosan kunla hhei khughozhi Yajiende echighawo. Hhela khareikude SeilaQimotaighala ghujighande mii enende ire giezhi Baolo fenfulasei deila echiwo.
ACT 17:16 BaoloYajiende hhelai sagheikude nie chenshide man nigiedashi hende nango giezho.
ACT 17:17 Hhe huitan sudoro Yutai kun, Hudai beiisan niman kunlare jianjinduzho. Pse niudunie geidoude penjisan kunlare jianjiduzho.
ACT 17:18 Da niezhan Ibijiulu, Sidoya ghua paini loushilaye Baolore jianjinduzhi kieliezho, "Ene hulihuduji yan kieliezho?" Pse niezhanla kieliezho, "Hhe hoxianshi niman kunlai nigiedani chonjizho." Ingiezhi kieliekushi Baolo hhelade Ersa fuho giesan daolii jianjizho.
ACT 17:19 Ingiese hhela Baoloi uduru Yaliebagu fayende echidene kieliewo, "Chi jianjisan ene nie shini daolini bijiende mejieghase olulie?
ACT 17:20 Chi kieliesan niezhan shiqinlai bijien chenliese ghudure no wo. Eneshi yan isi bikui bijien mejieku duran wine."
ACT 17:21 Yajien kun, hhende zhanshi jiere sousan waiji kunla man yama ulie gonjidene zui shini shiqinyi chenliezhi kieliekude xiqi wo.
ACT 17:22 BaoloYaliebagu fayende beidene kieliewo, "Yajien kunla, bi uzhese ta yan gieliuzhe zunjio xinyan jiere chighara wo.
ACT 17:23 Bi gochude yokude ta beiisanlai xianxide uzhese nie sidagha gieku teizi jiere, 'Tani Daku Hudade' giezhi huaizho. Ingiese ta tani dazhi beiisei bi kielieye."
ACT 17:24 "Hheshi duya, duya jieredu yanyanjilai man zhayaghasan Huda wo. Asiman zeminni Ezhan wo. Kun giesan huitande ulie soune.
ACT 17:25 Hhende chaiku mutun kunni khaghala ushilaku biyo uwo. Huda kunlade amin, ho, yanyanjilai man ogizho.
ACT 17:26 Niekozi kunse jien minzulani zhayaghadene zeminyi gochude soughawo. Hhelade nienjien, souku oronni jinjizhi ogiwo.
ACT 17:27 Ingiezhi giekushi Huda goyane kunlai ereighane giezho. Kenen moqioluzhi hhei ereizhi olune. Shijishan Huda matan alinie kunseliuzhe gholo uwo.
ACT 17:28 'Matan amituraku, gojioluku, bikushi man hhei kouizho.' Tai dunda shu huaisan kunla kieliesan mutun, 'Matanshi Hudase iresan wo.'"
ACT 17:29 "Matan Hudase iresanshi Hudai antan, miengu, tashighala, kunni jishu, sumulakughala giesan yanzi mutun uzhese ulie olune.
ACT 17:30 Melieshida kunla mejie dazhi giesei ese gonjiwoma, ede Huda gochui kunlade fenfulazhi geizhen gie giezho.
ACT 17:31 Huda sunghusan hhe kunghalane duyai gundande panjiku udui ijin jinji goudaghawo. Hhe kunyi fugusan kun dundase aminne olughazhi soyuji kunlade xianxin gieku zhenmin ogiwo."
ACT 17:32 Fugusanse fuho giesan ene kielienyi chenliedene niezhanla hhei uzhezhi xiniezho, niezhanla "Bijien pse chenlieku duran wine." giezhi kieliezho.
ACT 17:33 Ingie Baolo hhelai dundase khizhi echiwo.
ACT 17:34 Niezhan kunla Baolore hhantulazhi Ezhanni xianxin giewo. Hhelai dunda Yaliebagu fayendedu nie kun Jiunixiu, Damali giesan nie bierei, da ezighan kunye wine.
ACT 18:1 Ene shiqinse khuinashi BaoloYajiense likai giedene Gelindode echiwo.
ACT 18:2 Hhende Bendude olusan nie Yutai kunyi penjiwo. Niereini Yajila giene. Kelaoji honshan Yutai kunlade Loma gojiase likai gie giezhi minlin xiaise Baijila giesan biereighalane ene oloncha Lomani Idalise irewo. Baolo hhelai ochirale echiwo.
ACT 18:3 Hhelaye Baolo mutun zhanfan giezhi udu daoghazho. Ingiese Baolo hhelare hhantu souzhi wilie giezho.
ACT 18:4 Niefanie hhamuraku udude Baolo huitande kunlare jianjinduzhi Yutai kun, Xila kunlai kielie shundaghane giezho.
ACT 18:5 Seila, Qimotaighala Maqidunse iredene Baolo zhomen Hudai kielienyi chonjizhi Yutai kunlade, "Ersashi Mexiha wo." giezhi ganzhen beizho.
ACT 18:6 Hhela fandui giezhi zannan kielienghala hhei sugiese Baolo jien jieredu turane kuizhi kieliewo, "Ta goya zuine goya danji! Made yama ghadaghan uwo. Enedu khuinashi bi niman kunlai hhende echine."
ACT 18:7 Ingiedene huitanse likai giezhi Qido-Yushidu giesan nie kunyi giede echiwo. Ene kun Hudai beiizho. Hhei gieni huitan konde wo.
ACT 18:8 Huitan gonjisan Jilisibu nie giechiliene Ezhanyi xianxin giewo. Pse olon Gelindo kunlaye chenliedene xianxin giezhi xili jienliewo.
ACT 18:9 Xienidei Ezhan zhoujin mutun Baolode kieliewo, "Bu ayi, amanne bu menjidene kielie.
ACT 18:10 Bi chighala hhantu wo. Kieme chii hei dane. Ene chenshide mii bexin olon wo."
ACT 18:11 Baolo hhende nienban souzhi Hudai kielienyi hhelade sughazho.
ACT 18:12 JialiuYagaiyade zunli danlakude Yutai kunla hhantuladene Baoloi fandui giezhi lai shenpantai melie echi kieliewo,
ACT 18:13 "Ene kun guijinni ulie zunjidene Hudai beiise olune giezhi kunlai kielie shundaghazho."
ACT 18:14 Baolo jian kieliene giese JialiuYutai kunlade kieliewo, "Yutai kunla, fanfa giezhi yenzhunde zui fanjisan shiqinde zhazhoshi bi tanughunyi chenliese oluzhoma,
ACT 18:15 ta jianjindusanshi kielien, niere, tai guijinni shiqinshi ta goyalane banjile echi. Ene shiqinlani bi panjiku duran uwo."
ACT 18:16 Ingiedene hhelai fayense tou khighawo.
ACT 18:17 Ingiese kunla man huitan gonjisan Soqinii barei agidene shenpantai melie idun eghiwo. Ingieliuzhe Jialiu ese gonjizho.
ACT 18:18 BaoloGelindode pse ezighancha soudene gaijiulase ghaghachadene chon souzhi Xiliyade echiwo. Baijila, Yajila hhere hhantu echiwo. Hhe Jiengelide usunne ghigha widaghawo. Enei hhe eqighanse fayen giezhi daozho.
ACT 18:19 Ifusode kurudene Baolo hhelai hhende feiliegha goyane huitande orozhi Yutai kunlare daoli jianjinduzho.
ACT 18:20 Kunla hhei pse giedudu sou giese hhe dain ese giedene
ACT 18:21 hhelase likai giekude kieliewo, "Huda duran bise bi pse tai enede irene." Ingie chon souzhi Ifusose likai giewo.
ACT 18:22 Kaisaliyade chon jierese bouzhe, Yelusalende khireidene jiohuini kunlai nie asa, Anqiyade bouwo.
ACT 18:23 Giedudu soudene pse likai gie, Jialatai, Fulijia oronlai yozhi olon tujilai khiduzheghawo.
ACT 18:24 Yabolo giesan nie Yutai kun Ifusode irewo. Hhei Yalishandade oluzho. Koucai wine, jinwunde hen wo.
ACT 18:25 Ene kun Ezhanni daolini olon suruzho. Zhughe chilazhi Ersai shiqinni kunlade xianxide sughazhoma, zinie Yaheiyani xilini mejiene.
ACT 18:26 Hhe huitande danzine fugiedaghazhi jianjizho. Baijila, Yajilaghala jianjiseini chenliedene hhei danlin uruzhi Hudai daolini hhende pse xianxide jianjizhi mejieghawo.
ACT 18:27 YaboloYagaiyade echine giese Ifusoni gaijiula hhende zhichi giedene Yagaiyani tujila Yaboloi goude jienlie giezhi xin huaizho. Hhe hhende kuruse Ezhanni nenjienghala xianxin giesan kunlade banman fugie wo.
ACT 18:28 Hhe olon kunlai melie jinwunghala Ersashi Mexiha wo giezhi hende zhenmin giese Yutai kunlai kielie beighawo.
ACT 19:1 YaboloGelindode bikude Baolo beimienghun yozhi Ifusode echiwo. Hhende giedun tujilai penjidene asawo,
ACT 19:2 "Ta xianxin giekude Shenlinyi jienliewoye?" Hhela kieliewo, "Uye, lien Shenlin winekuida chenliezhi ese daowo."
ACT 19:3 Ingiese Baolo kieliewo, "Qinse ta yan xilini jienliewo?" Hhela kieliewo, "Yaheiya gieghasan xilini jienliewo."
ACT 19:4 Baolo kieliewo, "Yaheiya gieghasanshi geizhen gieku xili wo. Hhe bexinlade kieliezhi mii khuinase ireku hhei xianxin gie giezho. Hheshijiu Ersa wo."
ACT 19:5 Hhela ene kielienyi chenliedene Ezhan Ersai niereghala xili jienliewo.
ACT 19:6 Baolo hhelai jiere khane teise Shenlin hhelai jiere bouzhewo. Ingiese hhela shiheni kielienghala kieliezhi Hudai kielienyi kielie qiiwo.
ACT 19:7 Hhende chabudu 12 gie kun wo.
ACT 19:8 Baolo huitande orozhi danzine fugiedagha ghuran sara kunlare Hudai gojiai shiqinni jianjinduzhi kielie shundaghawo.
ACT 19:9 Ingieliuzhe niezhan kunla zhughene khiduzheghazhi ulie shunjidene olon kunlai melie ene daolini sugiene. Ingiese Baolo tujilarene hhantu hhelase likai giedene Tuilanuni suruku oronde niudunie jianjizhi kielienduzho.
ACT 19:10 Ingiezhi ghua honshi Yaxiyade sousan Yutai kun, Xila kunla man Ezhanni kielienyi chenliewo.
ACT 19:11 Huda Baoloi tungo giezhi tebieji nenlitu shiqinlai gieghazho.
ACT 19:12 Niezhan kunla da hhe injizhi daosan shoujin, wiqinyini agi ire gientulai jiere teise gienla goudazhi sheitanla khizhi echiwo.
ACT 19:13 Gochude toreizhi sheitan tousan giedun Yutai kunla Ezhan Ersai niereghala sheitanyi tou khighane giezhi sheitan heisan kunlade bi Baolo chonjisan Ersai niereghala tande minlin xiaiye giezhi shiizho.
ACT 19:14 Shijiwa giesan nie Yutai kunni fugie buwai dolon kewonla ene shiqinyi giezho.
ACT 19:15 Ingiese sheitan hhelade kieliewo, "Ersai bi mejiene. Baoloiye tanine. Tashi kien wo?"
ACT 19:16 Ingiedene sheitan heisan hhe kun hhelai jiere jiuli khirei, eghizhi hanshiliese hhela shan deilazhi hulan muchughun hhe giederase holu khireiwo.
ACT 19:17 Ifusode sousan Yutai kun, Xila kunla man ene shiqinyi mejiedene ayizho. Ingiese Ezhan Ersai minshen fugiedawo.
ACT 19:18 Pse olon xianxin giesan kunla iredene goya giesanlane man chenren giezhi kielie khizheghawo.
ACT 19:19 Olon fashu shuaisan kunla shulai agizhi ire dajialai melie sideraghawo. Shuni jiageni sanase 50000 miengu wine.
ACT 19:20 Ingiezhi Ezhanyi kielien yebeiseye ondazhi gochude echizho.
ACT 19:21 Ene shiqin daodene BaoloMaqidun, Yagaiya oronse daozhi Yelusalende echine giezhi zhughedene jiejin gie kieliewo, "Bi hhende kuruse bixi Lomade nie uzhele echine."
ACT 19:22 Ingie hhende banman giesan kun dundase Qimotai, Iladughalai Maqidunde echighawo. Goyane zhanshi jiere Yaxiyade feiliewo.
ACT 19:23 Hhe shihoude ene daolini yenyin jiere Ifusode hende londawo.
ACT 19:24 Nie miengu jianrenyi niereiini Jimijiu giene. Miengughala Yajimini yanzii giezhi jishugunlade baer olon zhenjighazho.
ACT 19:25 Hhe jishugun, hanjialane uruzhi hhantulaghadene kieliewo, "Dajiala, matan ene meimeighala facai giesei ta mejiene.
ACT 19:26 Ene Baolo zinie Ifusode pusho, Yaxiya go oronlade olon kunlai miizhi kun khaghala giesanlashi Huda pusho giesei ta chujieghezhi sonosuwo.
ACT 19:27 Ingiese zinie matanyi ene meimeini minshen bixindaku pusho. Yajimi famatu bierei nigiedani mioniye kunla meilade uzhene. Yaxiya kun, qienxiani kunla beiisan Yajimini wifen widane."
ACT 19:28 Kunla chenliedene hende hokuzhi Ifuso kunlai Yajimi hen wo giezhi onghonozho.
ACT 19:29 Nie chenshi man londa qiiwo. Kunla Baolore hhantu yosan Maqidunni Gaiyu, Yalidagui laidene xi yenjisan chanchande hhantu chunji orowo.
ACT 19:30 Baoloye bexinlai dunda orone giese tujila ese oroghawo.
ACT 19:31 Yaxiyani giedun noyenlashi Baoloi zhanlien wo. Kun peizhi iregha Baoloi wixiennide bu echi giezhi danlawo.
ACT 19:32 Hhantulasan kunla londundunji wo. Ingiezhi onghonone, qingiezhi onghonone. Fugie olie kunla yangiezhi hhantulasanne ulie mejiene.
ACT 19:33 Yutai kunla Yalishandai tungu melie khighase niezhan kunla hhende matugie giekui kieliezho. Yalishanda nie kha zhadeigha bexinlade jieshi giene giese
ACT 19:34 kunla hheshi Yutai kun bikui mejiedene man hhantu Ifuso kunlai Yajimi hen wo giezhi ghua zhuntou onghonozho.
ACT 19:35 Ingie hhe chenshini noyen ire olon kunla onghonosei beigha kieliewo, "Ifuso kunlaya, Ifusoshi hen Yajimi mioi sagheisan, pse asiman jierese bouzhesan tashii sagheisan chenshi bikui kien ulie mejiene?
ACT 19:36 Ene shiqinde yama kieliekui uwoshi ta qioqioji lon bu ire.
ACT 19:37 Ta laizhi iresan enezighan kunla mioni dunxilai ese ghulazho. Pse mai bierei nigiedaniye ese sugiezho.
ACT 19:38 Ingiese Jimijiu, hhantuku jishugunlarene yan zhakui bise fayende nieniene zhale echi gie. Ede fayenni niezho, zunlilaye wine.
ACT 19:39 Tande psedu shiqin wineshi zhao guijinghala hui keizhi chuli gie.
ACT 19:40 Eneduku londasan shiqinde matanyi zhaku wixien wine. Ene saorao giesande matande jieshi gieku kielien uwo."
ACT 19:41 Ene kielienyi kieliedene qinzhunlai sandaghawo.
ACT 20:1 Ene londasan shiqin bouzhi echisenu Baolo tujilai uruzhi ire, hhelade sughazhi kielie, pse chujiegheye giedene Maqidunde echiwo.
ACT 20:2 Baolo hhe oronlai jingo giekude olon kielienghala tujilade sughazhi kieliedene Xilade echiwo.
ACT 20:3 Hhende ghuran sara soudene chon souzhi Xiliyade zhen echine giekude Yutai kunla jihua giezhi hhei heine giekui mejie, Maqidunghun echine giezhi jiejin giewo.
ACT 20:4 Hhere hhantu Yaxiyade echisanshi Biliya kun Bilosini kewon Sobate wo, Qiesalonijia kun Yalidagu, Xigundu ghuala wo, Qimotai pse Tebi kun Gaiyu ghuala wo, da Yaxiya kun Tuijigu, Telofeimo ghuala wo.
ACT 20:5 Enezighan kunla xien Teloyade echi bijienyi sagheizho.
ACT 20:6 Bijien Tanmien Jie daodene Feilibise chon souzhi tawudushi Teloya hhelai hhende kuru, doludu souwo.
ACT 20:7 Xinqide bijien hhantuladene ginan ghuluzhi ijiekude Baolo khuichudu yolane giese hhelade banye olutula jianjiwo.
ACT 20:8 Bijien hhantulasan hhe lou jiere zhula olon wo.
ACT 20:9 Baolo jianjikude Yutuigu giesan nie nasuchighan kun chongun jiere souzho. Oloncha jianjise hhe kun funtura fugudene 3 lou jierese anda bouwo. Kunla fei bosizheghase fuguzho.
ACT 20:10 Baolo bou echi ghodeidene hhei qioru agi kieliewo, "Ta bu jinda, hhe dou amitu wo".
ACT 20:11 Baolo pse khizhi echi ginan ghuluzhi ijie, oloncha jianjizhi ogheidene yolawo.
ACT 20:12 Kunla nasuchighan kunyi amitu khugho echighase man hende bayasuzho.
ACT 20:13 Bijien xien chon souzhi Yashode echi hhende Baoloi jienliene giezho. Hhe goyane yozhi echine giezho. Eneshi hhe nanpei giesan wo.
ACT 20:14 BaoloYashode bijienre hhantulase bijien hhei chon jiere jienlie khirei Mituilinide irewo.
ACT 20:15 Hhense chon souzhi khuichudu Jiyani duimiende kurudene da niudude Samode daowo. Ingie pse niudude Milidude irewo.
ACT 20:16 BaoloYaxiyade danwu giekuse ayizhi Ifusoni onji daone giezhi eqighanse jiejin giewo. Hhe ghujighan yozhi jinlianji 50 qienni jieqi melie Yelusalende kune giezho.
ACT 20:17 BaoloMiliduse kun peizhi Ifuso jiohuini zhanlaolai xinlaghale echiwo.
ACT 20:18 Hhela irese Baolo hhelade kieliewo, "Bi Yaxiyase iresan hhe niuduse izhi tai dunda matugiezhi giesei ta mejiene.
ACT 20:19 Yutai kunla mii heizhi shouku gieghakude bi rennai giezhi goyane meilade uzhezhi nughusunghalane Ezhanyi zunjizhi giezho.
ACT 20:20 Tande oluzhi gounii bi nieda ese jiezhi olon kunlai melie pse kienyi giedeliuzhe tande sughazhi jianjiwo.
ACT 20:21 Pse Yutai kun, Xila kunlade ganzhen beizhi Hudai melie geizhen giedene mai Ezhan Ersai xianxin gie giewo."
ACT 20:22 "Ede Shenlin mii biizhi bi Yelusalende echine. Hhende yan shiqin penjikui ulie mejienema,
ACT 20:23 bi mejiekushi Shenlin go chenshide made ganzhen beizhi bareiku pse kunnan kuzhene giezho.
ACT 20:24 Ingieliuzhe bi Hudai nenjienni kielieku gouxioxide ganzhen beine giezhi Ezhan Ersase jienliesan renwune onchen ulie gietula aminne ulie kerene."
ACT 20:25 "Bi tai dunda irezhi Hudai gojiai daolii chonjizhoma, ihou ta mii pse chanla dakui ede bi mejiene.
ACT 20:26 Ingiese bi enedu tande ganzhen beiye. Tai dunda kien dozode echise made zui uwo.
ACT 20:27 Hudai isii bi goujida uye feilieghazhi man tande chonjizhi ogiwo.
ACT 20:28 Ta goyalane xioxin giezhi zhaogu gie pse Hudai bexinlani xioxin giezhi zhaogu gie. Ta ghoni adulachen kun mutun hhelai zhaogu gie. Shenlin tai hhelade lindao danlaghazho. Hhelashi Huda Kewonne chusunghala agizhi iresan Hudani jiohui wo.
ACT 20:29 Bi yolase mouxien zhanghei tai dunda orezhezhi ghonilai shanjikui bi mejiene.
ACT 20:30 Tai dundaseye niezhan kunla khizhedene zhendaoni wirulaghazhi tujilai miidene goyalane daghaghane.
ACT 20:31 Ingiese xioxin giendu. Bi ene 3 niende xieni uduiji nughusun usuruzhi soyuji kunlade sughazhi kieliesei ta jila.
ACT 20:32 Ede bi tai Hudade, hhei nenjientu daolide jiuizhi ogiye. Ene daoli tai hendagha shidane, pse taiji soyuji zhiguishisan kunlare hhantu Hudai jiachanni jienliegha shidane.
ACT 20:33 Bi kiemai antan, miengu, jienni nienhei giezhi ese daozho.
ACT 20:34 Bi ghua khaghalane goyadene hhantuku kunladene injiku dunxi gunjisei ta goyalane mejiene.
ACT 20:35 Bi yandeliuzhe yanzi uzheghazhi khishulazhi wilie giedene zholien kunlade banman giezho. Pse ogiku jienliekuse fuqi fugiewo giesan Ezhan Ersai kielienyi jila giezho."
ACT 20:36 Baolo ene kielienyi kielie baraghadene xiutulie dajialare hhantu onxian giewo.
ACT 20:37 Kunla man fugiede wilazhi Baoloi qiorudene orezho.
ACT 20:38 Ihou ta mii pse chanla dane giesan Baoloi ene kielien hhelai zhughei hende otughazho. Ingie hhela Baoloi chon jiere khugho echighawo.
ACT 21:1 Bijien hhelase likai giedene chon souzhi zhijie Geshide kuruwo. Khuichudu Lojide kurudene hhense Padalade echiwo.
ACT 21:2 Hhende nie Feiniji echiku chonyi penjidene chon jiere khirei yozhi qiiwo.
ACT 21:3 Ingie Saipulusiyi chanla soghei miende jiedene Xiliya fanxiande yozhi Tuilode kuruwo. Chon hhende ho xiine giezho.
ACT 21:4 Bijien hhende ezighan tujilai ereizhi oludene doludu souwo. Hhela Shenlinyi kouizhi Baolode Yelusalende bu khirei giezhi kieliewo.
ACT 21:5 Doludu daodene bijien yozhi qiiwo. Hhela bierei, kesilarene man bijienyi khughozhi chenshi ghadane ireghawo. Bijien haibienzide xiutulie onxian giedene
ACT 21:6 nieniedene feixin kieliewo. Bijien chon jiere khireise hhela gieladene khareiwo.
ACT 21:7 Bijien izhi chon souzhi Tuilose Dolimaide kuruwo. Hhendedu gaijiulade kielien asazhi hhelare niudu souwo.
ACT 21:8 Khuichudu bijien hhense likai gie Kaisaliyade iredene gouxioxi chonjisan Feilii giede oro hhere hhantu souwo. Hheshi dolon kun dundadu nie wo.
ACT 21:9 Hhende uye dafalasan jieran oqin wine. Hhelade Hudai kielien kielieku nenli wine.
ACT 21:10 Bijien hhende ezighancha souse Yudayase nie xienzhi bouzhewo. Niereini Yajiabu giene.
ACT 21:11 Bijienyi enende iredene Baoloi pixiei bareizhi goya kha, konne banladene kieliewo, "Shenlin ingiezhi kieliezho, 'Yutai kunla Yelusalende ene pixieni ezhanyi ingiezhi banladene niman kunlade jiuizhi ogine.'"
ACT 21:12 Bijien ene kielienyi chenliedene hhe oronyi kunlare Baoloi Yelusalende bu khirei giezhi hende danlazho.
ACT 21:13 Ingie Baolo kieliewo, "Ta yale ingiezhi wilazhi mii zhughei ghalughane? Bi Ezhan Ersade oluzhi kunla mii banlazhi pse Yelusalende fugughaliuzhe bi zhunbei gie goudazho."
ACT 21:14 Bijien Baoloi kieliezhi dao dase yama ese giedene zinie "Ezhanyi isi mutun gholu gie." giezhi kieliewo.
ACT 21:15 Giedudu daodene bijien zhunbei gie Yelusalende khireiwo.
ACT 21:16 Kaisaliyani giedun tujilaye bijienre hhantu echiwo. Hhela bijienyi uduruzhi Nasun giesan nie Saipulusi kunyi giede echiwo. Hhe tuji danlazhi oloncha olune.
ACT 21:17 Yelusalende kuruse gaijiula bijienyi bayasuzhi jienliewo.
ACT 21:18 Khuichudu Baolo bijienre hhantu Yagebui uzhele echiwo. Zhanlaolaye man hhende wine.
ACT 21:19 Baolo hhelade kielien asadene Huda hhei niman kunlai dunda gieghasan wilielai nienieji kieliezhi ogiwo.
ACT 21:20 Hhela chenliedene Hudai kuaizhi Baolode kieliewo, "Gaijiu, chi mejiene. Ezhanyi xianxin giesan Yutai kun hao jiwon wine. Hhela Musani guijinde chighara no wo.
ACT 21:21 Hhela chenliese chi sughazhi niman kunlai dundadedu soyuji Yutai kunlai Musai guijinni bu zunjizhi ga kewosilade hetoune bu giegha giezho. Pse hhelai xigonni bu dagha giezho.
ACT 21:22 Ede matugiene? Kunla chi enende iresei mejiene.
ACT 21:23 Chi zhao bijienyi kielien mutun giele echi. Bijienyi enende jieran kunla kielien yenji jiezho.
ACT 21:24 Chi hhelare hhantu echizhi waghaku xigonghala hhantu wagha. Hhelai qiorun duliku baerni chi ogi. Ingiese hhela chenliesanshi zhenni pusho bikui, pse chi Musai guijinni zunjisei dajiala mejiene.
