ACT 21:25 Bijien Ezhanni xianxin giesan niman kunlade nigiedade teisan, chusun, lei alasan, lon kijieku enelase gholodo giezhi jiejin giedene xin huaiwo."
ACT 21:26 Ingiese Baolo hhe jieran kunyi uduruzhi khuichudu waghaku xigonghala hhelare hhantu waghawo. Ingie mechide orodene hhela waghazhi baluku udui, pse jien kun Hudade mure ogiku uduni tunzhi giewo.
ACT 21:27 Hhe doludu barane giekude Yaxiyase iresan Yutai kunla Baolo mechide bikui chanladene olon kunlai man shanjizhi Baoloi barei agiwo.
ACT 21:28 Ingie waradazhi kieliewo, "Isilie kunla, bijiende ishula! Ene kun gochude toreizhi jien kunlade mai kun, guijin, mechii fandui giezhi sughazho. Hhe da niman kunlai uduruzhi mechide oro ene zhiguitu oronyi zannanshighawo."
ACT 21:29 Hhela ingiezhi kieliekushi Ifuso kun, TelofeimoBaologhala chenshide bisei chanlasenu Baolo hhei mechide uduru orowo giezho.
ACT 21:30 Nie chenshi man londazhi bexinla holu ire, Baoloi barei agidene mechise lai khireighawo. Ingie mechini wijienyi deigo kha jiewo.
ACT 21:31 Kunla zhen Baoloi alane giekude buduilani qienfuzhande Yelusalen nie chenshi man londawo giezhi huibao giewo.
ACT 21:32 Ingie qienfuzhan deigo budui, giedun baifuzhanlai uduru holuzhi hhelai hhende bouwo. Hhela qienfuzhan, buduilai chanladene Baoloi eghiku beiwo.
ACT 21:33 Ingie qienfuzhan melie echi Baoloi barei agidene fenfulazhi ghua qieshenghala sozila giezho. Ingiedene, "Hheshi kien wine, yan shiqin giezho?" giezhi asazho.
ACT 21:34 Niezhan kunla ingiezhi onghonone, niezhan kunla qingiezhi onghonone. Ingiezhi noise qienfuzhan yan shiqin bikui mejie da, Baoloi laidene buduila sousan loude echi giezhi fenfulawo.
ACT 21:35 Louqi konde irese olon kunla hende jigheidazhi eghine giese buduila zinie Baoloi qienlie daowo.
ACT 21:36 Kunla khuina daghazhi, "Hhei ala!" giezhi waradazho.
ACT 21:37 Baoloi buduila sousan lou sudoro lai orone giekude Baolo qienfuzhande asawo, "Bi chade nie aman kielien kieliese olunulie?" Hhe kieliewo, "Chi Xila kielien kielie mejienu?
ACT 21:38 Chishi hhe oloncha daolon giedene 4000 shashoui uduruzhi hontande echisan hhe Aiji kun pushoba?"
ACT 21:39 Baolo kieliewo, "Bishi Yutai kun wo. Jilijiani nie minshentu chenshi Dashuni hukouni bareizho. Bi chii xiahua gieye, mii bexinlade nie kielien kieliegha."
ACT 21:40 Qienfuzhan tunyi oluse Baolo louqi jiere beidene bexinlade nie kha zhadeighase shenqi widawo. Ingiese BaoloXibolai kielienghala kieliewo.
ACT 22:1 "Oqio kunla, gaijiula, bi goyane huizhi kieliesan kielienyi ta chenliendu."
ACT 22:2 BaoloXibolai kielienghala kieliese hhela chenliedene genjia nanranshiwo. Ingie Baolo kieliewo,
ACT 22:3 "Bishi Yutai kun wo. Jilijiani Dashude oludene ene Yelusalen chenshide fugiedazhi Jiamalieni kha doura suruzho. Matanyi xienrenlani guijinyi chigharade suruzhi Hudade rexin wo. Edeku tanre niekielien wo.
ACT 22:4 Bi eqighanse ene daolini daghasan kunlai heizhi fugughakude kuruwo. Ere kun, biereilai banlazhi bafanzide khawo.
ACT 22:5 Ene shiqinde hhe nie zui fugie buwa, soyuji zui fugie fayenni zhanlaola man ganzhen bei shidane. Bi hhelai hhense xinni keredene Damashigeni gaijiulai hhende echi, hhendedu xianxin giesan kunlai barei Yelusalende lai echi faine giezho."
ACT 22:6 "Bi Damashigede yozhi kurukude zhen zhunwu shihou wo. Menzhali asiman jierese fugie gonqi faizhi mii simiende zhouizho.
ACT 22:7 Bi zemin jiere fura bouse nie shenqi made kieliewo, 'Saolo! Saolo! Chi mii yangiezhi heine?'
ACT 22:8 Bi asawo, 'Ezhan, chishi kien wo?' Hhe kieliewo, 'Bishi chi heisan Nasale kun Ersa wo.'
ACT 22:9 Mare hhantu yosan kunla hhe gonqii chanlawoma, made kieliesan shenqini sonosu dazho.
ACT 22:10 Bi kieliewo, 'Ezhan, bi matugiene?' Ezhan kieliewo, 'Bosidene Damashigede echi. Hhende nie kun chi yan gieku shiqinni man kieliene.'
ACT 22:11 Hhe gonqini gieghanghala bi sugho gholuwo. Hhantu yosan kunla mii khase laizhi Damashigede orowo."
ACT 22:12 "Hhende nie kunyi niereiini Yananiya giene. Hheshi nie xienliantu kun wo, guijin jiere chighara wo. Hhende sousan Yutai kunla man hhei zunzhun giezho.
ACT 22:13 Hhe mii uzhele ire kanzidemi beidene Saolo gaijiu, chi chanla giezhi made kieliewo. Ingiekude bi nie uzhese hhei chanlawo."
ACT 22:14 "Ingie hhe kun kieliewo, 'Mai xienrenni Huda chii sunghudene goyane isii mejieghazhi hhe gou kunni chanlaghazhi shenqiini chenlieghawo.
ACT 22:15 Chi chanlasan, chenliesanne soyuji kunlai melie hhe kunde ganzhen beine.
ACT 22:16 Chi ede yan sagheizho? Bosidene Ezhanyi xiahua giezhi xilii jienliedene goya zuine waghazhi widagha.'"
ACT 22:17 "Khuinashi bi Yelusalende khareidene mechide zhen onxian giekude zhoujin mutun nie ghudureqi chanlase
ACT 22:18 Ezhan made kieliewo, 'Chi ghujighan Yelusalense likai gie. Chi made beisan ganzhenni hhela ulie jienliene.'
ACT 22:19 Ingie bi kieliewo, 'Ezhan, eqighandei bi chii xianxin giesan kunlai bafanzide khazhi pse go huitanlade hhelai eghisei hhela goyane mejiene.
ACT 22:20 Pse chade ganzhen beisan Siqifanyi heizhi chusun usurukude biye kanzide beizhi tunyi giezhi hhei alasan kunlade oluzhi jienlaini uzhezhi ogizho.'"
ACT 22:21 "Ingieliuzhe Ezhan made kieliewo, 'Chi echi, bi chii peizhi gholododu niman kunlai hhende echighane.'"
ACT 22:22 Bexinla ene nie aman kielienyi chenliedene fugiede kieliewo, "Intu kunyi duya jierese widagha! Hheshi fugukuni wo!"
ACT 22:23 Hhela izhi onghonozhi jienlane bendazhi turai asiman jiere khisigheise
ACT 22:24 qienfuzhan fenfulazhi Baoloi buduila sousan lou sudoro orogha, mabienzighala eghizhi kunla yangiezhi onghonosei asa giezho.
ACT 22:25 Eghine giezhi banlakude Baolo kanzide beisan baifuzhande kieliewo, "Bishi Loma kun wo. Zui ese jinjidene eghise falighala kieliese tande oluzhoye?"
ACT 22:26 Ene kielienni chenliedene baifuzhan qienfuzhande echidene kieliewo, "Ene kunshi Loma kun wo. Chi matugiene giezho?"
ACT 22:27 Qienfuzhan ire Baolode asawo, "Chi made kielie, chishi Loma kun onu?" Baolo kieliewo, "Enbene."
ACT 22:28 Qienfuzhan kieliewo, "Bi olon baer huaizhi Loma gojiani hukoude orowo." Baolo kieliewo, "Bi olusanse enbene."
ACT 22:29 Ingiese Baoloi eghizhi asane giesan kunla hhense deigo likai giewo. Qienfuzhan banlasan Baoloshi Loma kun bikui mejiedene ayizho.
ACT 22:30 Khuichudu qienfuzhan Yutai kun Baoloi zhasan shiqinni mejiene giezhi hhei andaghadene fenfulazhi fugie buwa, zui fugie fayenni kunlai man hhantulaghasenu Baoloi uduru ire hhelai melie beighawo.
ACT 23:1 Baolo zui fugie fayenni kunlai nudunne ese agi uzhezhi kieliewo, "Gaijiula, bi Hudai melie giekude lianxin ese ghudanduzhi izhi eli kuruwo."
ACT 23:2 Ingie zui fugie buwa YananiyaBaoloi kanzide beisan kunlade hhei aman jiere eghi giezhi fenfulawo.
ACT 23:3 Ingiese Baolo hhende kieliewo, "Chi ene mienzide khireisan kun, ghadane seighan wo, sudoro zannan wo. Huda chii eghine! Chi hhende souzhi guijinghala mii panjine giedene da guijinni fanjizhi mii eghi giezhi fenfulanu?"
ACT 23:4 Kanzide beisan kunla kieliewo, "Chi lien Hudai zui fugie buwai sugienu?"
ACT 23:5 Ingie Baolo kieliewo, "Gaijiula, hheshi zui fugie buwa bikui bi mejie dawo. Bexinni gonjisan noyenne bu sugie giezhi jinwun jiere kieliezho."
ACT 23:6 Baolo hhelai dundadu olieshi Sadugai kun, olieshi Falisai kun bikui uzhe khizhedene zui fugie fayenni kunlade fugiede kieliewo, "Gaijiula, bishi Falisai kun wo, Falisai kunni houdei wo. Bi fugusan kun fuho giekui xianxin giese made shenwun giezho."
ACT 23:7 Ene kielienyi kieliese Falisai kun, Sadugai kunghala jianjidu qii kunla ghugha keiwo.
ACT 23:8 Yenlai Sadugai kunla kieliese qienxien, ruhher uwo, fuho gieku shiqinye uwo giezho. Falisai kun kieliese enela man wine giezho.
ACT 23:9 Kunla fugiede onghono qiiwo. Giedun Falisai paini jinwun hanjiala bosi ire hende jianjiduzho, "Ene kun yan codasei bijien ereizhi khizhe dawo. Kenen ruhher, qienxienla hhende kielien kieliezhoba."
ACT 23:10 Ingie jianjiduzhi hendawo. Qienfuzhan Baoloi sida zhazhazi gholughakuse ayizhi buduilai fenfula boughadene hhei qianla khizhe buduila sousan loude echigha giewo.
ACT 23:11 Hhe xii Ezhan Baoloi kanzide beizhi kieliewo, "Chi danzine fugiedagha. Chi Yelusalende matugie made ganzhen beizhoshi Lomadeye qingiezhi ganzhen beikuni wo."
ACT 23:12 Ogheidene Yutai kunla qioqioji shanlian giedene fayen giezhi kieliewo, "Baoloi ulie alatula matan ulie ijiene, ulie ochine."
ACT 23:13 Ingiezhi hhantu fayen giesan kun 40 gie daozho.
ACT 23:14 Hhela fugie buwa, zhanlaolai shida echidene kieliewo, "Bijien Baoloi ulie alatula yama ulie ijiene giezhi fayen gie goudaghazho.
ACT 23:15 Ta ede zui fugie fayenni kunlare hhantu qienfuzhande kieliezhi Baoloi tai enende uduru iregha. Jiazhon giezhi pse xianxide hhei shiqinni asane giezhi kielie. Bijien zhunbei gie goudazho. Hhe kuzhetula ala widaghane."
ACT 23:16 Ingie Baoloi wishen hhela ghulazhi giesan jihuai sonosudene buduila sousan loude echi Baolode kieliewo.
ACT 23:17 Ingie Baolo nie baifuzhanyi uruzhi ire kieliewo, "Chi ene nasuchighan kunyi udurudene qienfuzhanyi shida echi. Hhe hhende nie shiqin huibao giene."
ACT 23:18 Ingiese baifuzhan hhei uduruzhi qienfuzhanyi shida echi "Bareisan Baolo mii uruzhi echi xiahua giezhi ene nie nasuchighan kunyi udurudene chade nie shiqin kielieghane." giezhi kieliese
ACT 23:19 Qienfuzhan hhei khase laizhi niemiende echi asawo, "Chi made yan shiqin kieliene?"
ACT 23:20 Hhe kieliewo, "Yutai kunla Baoloi shiqinde xianxide asane giezhi jiazhon giedene maghashijie hhei zui fugie fayende uduru iregha giezhi chii xiahua giekui shanlian gie goudawo.
ACT 23:21 Ingiese chi hhelanughunyi bu chenlie. Baoloi ulie alatula ulie ijiezhi ulie ochine giezhi fayen giesan 40 dogie kunla ede alane giezhi niuizho. Ede zhunbei gie goudazhi chii dain giekui sagheizho."
ACT 23:22 Ingiese qienfuzhan nasuchighan kunde ene shiqinyi chi made kieliewo giezhi kiemade bu kielie giezhi fenfuladene hhei echighawo.
ACT 23:23 Qienfuzhan ghua baifuzhanyi uru ire kieliewo, "200 gie yosan budui, 70 gie morei unusan budui, 200 gie zhida bareisan buduilai zhunbei gie. Ene xii 9 jiende Kaisaliyade echine.
ACT 23:24 Pse morei zhunbei giezhi Baoloi unughadene baohu giezhi Feilisi shenzhanni hhende khughozhi echigha."
ACT 23:25 Hhe xin huaizhi kieliewo,
ACT 23:26 "Kelaoji-LixiyaFeilisi shenzhande kielien asazho.
ACT 23:27 Ene kunyi Yutai kunla bareizhi alane giekude hheshi Loma kun bikui bi mejiedene buduilai uduru echi hhei jiui khizhewo.
ACT 23:28 Hhela hhei yangiezhi zhasan shiqinyi bi mejiene giezhi hhei uduru hhelai zui fugie fayende echiwo.
ACT 23:29 Hhei zhasanshi zi hhelai jiomunni guijin jieredu shiqin bikui bi mejiewo. Yama fugughaku, banlaku zui uwo.
ACT 23:30 Khuinashi Yutai kunla hhei alane giesan jihuai nie kun made kieliese bi hhei deigo chii hhende ireghawo. Pse minlin xiaizhi hhei zhasan kun chii melie iredene zha giewo."
ACT 23:31 Ingiese buduila zhao fenfulasan mutun xienidei Baoloi uduru Anqipajide echighadene
ACT 23:32 khuichudu morei unusan buduila Baoloni khughozhi echigha, yosan buduila sousan loudene khareiwo.
ACT 23:33 Morei unusan buduila Kaisaliyade ire xinni shenzhande ogisenu Baoloni hhende jiuizhi ogiwo.''
ACT 23:34 Shenzhan xinni uzhe, "Baoloshi alinie shenni kun wo?" giezhi asadene Jilijiani kun bikui mejie kieliewo,
ACT 23:35 "Chii zhasan kunla irese panjiye." Ingie kunlade fenfulazhi Baoloi Hherode hongunde khawo.
ACT 24:1 Tawudu daodene zui fugie buwa Yananiya giedun zhanlao, pse nie Qietulo giezhi lishire hhantu iredene shenzhande Baoloi zhazho.
ACT 24:2 Baoloi uduru irese Qietulo hhei zhazhi kieliewo, "Feilisi fugie noyen, bijien chii yenyinghala chanqi nanrande udu daozhi chini melie uzheku aghelighala ene gojia fazhan giezhi goudazho.
ACT 24:3 Bijien suishisui chade hende mafan kieliezho.
ACT 24:4 Bijien chii olon mafan ulie gieghane. Chii xiahua gieye, zhughene aghuidaghazhi bijienyi giedun aman kielienyi nie chenlie.
ACT 24:5 Bijien ene kunyi uzhese inzhaku gien niekielien wo. Qienxiani Yutai kunlai shanjizhi londaghazho. Hheshi Nasale jiomunni nie touzi wo.
ACT 24:6 Mechini zannanshighane giese bijien hhei bareiwo.
ACT 24:8 Chi goyane ene kunyi shenwun giese bijien hhei zhasan shiqinlai man mejiene."
ACT 24:9 Yutai kunla daghadene shiqin intui enbene giezhi hhei zhazhi kieliewo.
ACT 24:10 Shenzhan qiorun jienjizhi Baoloi kielie giese Baolo kieliewo, "Chi ene gojiade fayenni yenzhan haojinien danlasei bi mejiene. Ingiese bi bayasuzhi goyane huizho.
ACT 24:11 Bi libai giele Yelusalende khizhezhi 12 qienda ese olusei chi nie chaima mejiene.
ACT 24:12 Bi mechide kunlare jianjindusei, huitande, chenshini go oronlade kunlai shanjisei hhela chanlazhi ese daozho.
ACT 24:13 Hhela ede mii zhasan shiqinde chade yama zhenji ogi dane.
ACT 24:14 Ingiese bi chade nie shiqinni chenren gieye. Hhela xiejio wo giesan ene daolini bi daghazhi bijienyi xienrenyi Hudai beiizho. Guijinshu, xienzhini shu jiere jilasanyi man xianxin giezho.
ACT 24:15 Pse ene kunla xianxin giesan mutun gou kun, gou witu kunla man fuho giekui bi Hudase panjizho.
ACT 24:16 Ingiese bi Hudai melie, kunlai melie chan lianxin ulie ghudandune giezhi xiacha giezho.
ACT 24:17 Jinien daodene bi goya minzune nanxin kunlade baer khughozhi Hudade mure ogine giezhi Yelusalende irewo.
ACT 24:18 Bi mechide ogine giezhi waghazhi ganjinrasei hhela chujieghewoma, olon kunlare hhantu uwo, daolonye ese giezho.
ACT 24:19 Zinie Yaxiyase iresan giedun Yutai kunla hhende wo. Hhelade mii zhaku shiqin bise chii shida irezhi zhane.
ACT 24:20 Pse enezighan kunla bi zui fugie fayen melie bidene mii yan codasei mejiewoshi goyalane nie kielie gie.
ACT 24:21 Bi zinie hhelai dunda beizhi ene nie aman kielienyi fugiede kieliewo, 'Enedu tai melie made shenwun giekushi fugusan kun fuho giesan shiqin wo.'"
ACT 24:22 Feilisi ene daolini xiandan qinchu wo. Ingie shenpanhuini danlazhi beighadene kieliewo, "Lixiya qienfuzhan bouzhese bi tai shiqinni panjiye."
ACT 24:23 Ingiese baifuzhande fenfulazhi Baolode ezighan ziyu ogizhi hhei uzhe giewo. Pse zhanlienlani hhende injiku dunxi ogise bu danla giezho.
ACT 24:24 Giedudu daodene Feilisi biereighalane Baoloi ochirale irewo. Hhei biereishi Yutai kun wo. Niereini Tuxila giene. Baoloi uruzhi iresenu Ersa Mexihani xianxin gieku daolii kielieghazhi chenliene giezho.
ACT 24:25 Baolo gundande gieku, goyane kunzhi gieku, jianlai ireku shenpanni kieliese Feilisi hende ayidene kieliewo, "Chi xian echi, made fanbien winekude chii uruzhi ireye."
ACT 24:26 FeilisiBaolo hhende baer ogimu giezhi onxian giezhi hhei olonfa uruzhi ire kielien kielienduzho.
ACT 24:27 Ghua hon gierudene Boqiu-FeisiduFeilisini oronde noyen danlawo. FeilisiYutai kunlai bayasughane giezhi Baoloi bafanzide kha jiezho.
ACT 25:1 FeisiduKaisaliyade noyen danlazhi ghurudu oludene Yelusalende khireiwo.
ACT 25:2 Hhende fugie buwa, Yutai kunni noyenla Feisidude Baoloi zhazho.
ACT 25:3 Feisidui xiahua giezhi banman kerezhi Baoloi Yelusalende iregha giezho. Hhela mo jiere Baoloi alane giezhi jihua giezho.
ACT 25:4 Feisidu kieliewo, "Baoloi ede Kaisaliyade khazho. Bi deigo hhende echine giezho.
ACT 25:5 Tai dunda qienlitu kun mare hhantu bousenu hhe kunde yan zui wineshi hhei zha."
ACT 25:6 Feisidu hhelai hhende neimudu, hharudu soudene Kaisaliyade bouwo. Khuichudu hui keine giezhi shenpantai jiere soudene fenfulazhi Baoloi uduru ire giewo.
ACT 25:7 Baolo irese hhezighan Yelusalense bouzhesan Yutai kunla zhouwideni beizhi olon, gundu zuighala hhei zhazhoma, yama zhenji ogi dazho.
ACT 25:8 Baolo goyane huizhi kieliewo, "Bugon Yutai kunyi guijin, mechi, pse Kaisa honshande bi zui fanjizhi ese daozho."
ACT 25:9 FeisiduYutai kunlai bayasughane gie Baolode asawo, "Chi Yelusalende khireidene bi ene shiqinyi shenwun giese duran winu uwo?"
ACT 25:10 Ingiese Baolo kieliewo, "Bi ede Kaisa honshanni shenpantai melie beizho. Enende made shenwun giese indanji wo. Bi Yutai kunlade yama codasan shiqin giezhi ese daosei chiye qinchu wo.
ACT 25:11 Bi codasan shiqin giezhi fuguku zui wineshi fuguliuzhe made yama kieliekui uwo. Hhela mii zhasan shiqinshi zhenni pushoshi kiemada mii hhelade jiuizhi ogi dane. Bi Kaisa honshande zhane."
ACT 25:12 Feisidu goya kunlarene shanlian giedene kieliewo, "Chi Kaisa honshande zhase Kaisa honshanyi hhende echikuni wo."
ACT 25:13 Giedudu daodene Yajipa honshan Beinisighala Kaisaliyade irezhi Feisidude kielien asawo.
ACT 25:14 Hhende ezighancha soukude FeisiduBaoloni shiqinyi Yajipa honshande kieliewo, "Enende nie fanren wine. Feilisi feilieghasan wo.
ACT 25:15 Bi Yelusalende bikude Yutai kunni fugie buwa, zhanlaola hhei shiqinyi made zhazhi, "Hhende zui jinji!" giezhi xiahua giewo.
ACT 25:16 Bi hhelade Loma kunni falishi zhasan kun duifanghala ulie hhantulazhi duifande goyane huiku jihui ulie ogidene zui jinjise ulie olune giezhi kieliewo.
ACT 25:17 Ingiese hhela enende irese bi danwu ese giezhi khuichudu shenpantai jiere soudene fenfulazhi hhe kunyi uduru ire giewo.
ACT 25:18 Zhasan kunla beidene hhei zhase bi sumulasan qintu doghun shiqin pusho.
ACT 25:19 Hhela zinie goyai jiomunni shiqin jiere, pse fugusan Ersa giesan nie kunyi shiqin jiere jianjinduzho. Baolo kieliese hhe kun amitu wo giezho.
ACT 25:20 Bi enei matugie chaikui mejie da, "Baolode ene shiqinyi Yelusalende khireidene shenwun giese duran winuwo?" giezhi asawo.
ACT 25:21 Ingiese Baolo mii xiahua giezhi goyane feilieghadene Kaisa honshan jiejin gie giezho. Ingie bi hhei Kaisa honshanyi hhende khughozhi echighatula feiliegha giezhi fenfulawo."
ACT 25:22 YajipaFeisidude kieliewo, "Bi goyane ene kun kieliekui chenlieku duran wine." Feisidu kieliewo, "Maghashijie chi chenlie."
ACT 25:23 Khuichudu YajipaBeinisighala yoqi yoqi daqinde irewo. Qienfuzhan, hhe chenshini minshen fugietu kunlaiye deilazhi orowo. Feisidu nie fenfulase Baoloi uduru irewo.
ACT 25:24 Feisidu kieliewo, "Yajipa honshan, pse enende bisan dajiala, ta uzhesan ene kunshijiu Yelusalenni, pse enendedu Yutai kunla man made fugiede waradazhi yoqiu giezhi hhei amitu feilieghase ulie olune giesan hhe kun wo.
ACT 25:25 Bi chaise hhende yama fuguku zui uwo. Pse hhe goyane Kaisa honshande zhane giese bi hhei khughozhi hhende echighane giezhi jiejin giewoma,
ACT 25:26 ene kunyi xianxi shiqinyi Kaisa honshande huaikui uwo. Ingie yama huaiku dunxi enende chaizhi olu shidanu gie, tai melie, yuqishi chi Yajipa honshanyi melie hhei uduru irewo.
ACT 25:27 Bi sumulase zhaku shiqinyi kieliezhi qinchu ulie olughadene fanrenni khughokude heshi uwo giezho."
ACT 26:1 YajipaBaolode kieliewo, "Chi goyadene oluzhi kielie." Ingiese Baolo khane zhadeigha goyane huizhi kieliewo,
ACT 26:2 "Yajipa honshan, Yutai kunla mii zhasan shiqinde enedu chii melie bi goyane huise mii inqi gou wo.
ACT 26:3 Tebieshi chi Yutai kunlai xigon, jianjindukulai man shuxi wo. Ingiese bi chii xiahua gieye, chi rennai giezhi bi kieliesanyi chenlie."
ACT 26:4 "Bi meila shihouse izhi goya kun dundane Yelusalende matugie giesei Yutai kunla man mejiene.
ACT 26:5 Bishi mai jiomun dundadu zui chigharadu Falisai paini nie goude giesan kun bikui hhela eqighanse mejiene. Enei hhela duran bise ganzhen bei shidane.
ACT 26:6 Ede mii enende beigha shenwun giekushi Huda mai xienrenlade dain giesei bi panjiwo giezho.
ACT 26:7 Ene panjikushi mai 12 gie paini kunla xieni udu Hudai goude beiizhi ene dain giesei gholuse giesan hhe wo. Honshanya, ene nie panjiku yenyin jiere Yutai kunla mii zhazho.
ACT 26:8 Ta yale Huda fugusan kunlai aminne olughase xianxin giekui pusho giezho?"
ACT 26:9 "Shijishan bi goyane Nasale kun Ersai jinlianji fandui giese indanji wo giezhi sumuladene
ACT 26:10 Yelusalende ingiezhi giewo. Fugie buwalase qienli keredene shentulai bafanzide khazhi, da hhelai sixin panjikude beizhi bi tunyi oluwo.
ACT 26:11 Bi pse go huitanlade olonfa hhelai faizhi biidene Ersani sugieghazho. Bi hhelade hende hokuzhi da niman kunlai chenshilade echizhi heizho."
ACT 26:12 "Ene mujighala bi fugie buwalase qienli, minlinni bareidene Damashigede echine giezho.
ACT 26:13 Honshanya, zhunwude bi mo jiere yokude chanlase asimanse gon faizhi naranse da gieghan wo. Simiende bi, bighala hhantu yosan kunlai zhouizho.
ACT 26:14 Bijien man zemin jiere fura bouse nie shenqi Xibolai kielienghala made kieliewo, 'Saolo! Saolo! Yale mii heine? Chi fugherei mutun ezhanni eghesuntu teiyai qiuise goyane shanjine.'"
ACT 26:15 "Ingiese bi kieliewo, 'Ezhan, chishi kien wo?' Ezhan kieliewo, 'Bishi chi heisan Ersa wo.
ACT 26:16 Chi bosizhedene bei. Bi goyane chade xienjighakushi chii goyadene hoji danlaghazhi chi mii chanlasan shiqinde, pse bi chade jianlai xienjighaku shiqinde ganzhen beighane giezho.
ACT 26:17 Bi chii Yutai kunlai, niman kunlai dundase jiuizhi khizhene. Bi chii peizhi hhelai hhende echighadene
ACT 26:18 nudunlaini keighazhi kharanise gon dunda ireghane. Ibilisii nenlise likai gieghazhi Hudade shunjighane. Ingiese mii xianxin giezhi zuini mienliedene zhiguitu gholusan kunlare hhantu guzide beighane.'"
ACT 26:19 "Yajipa honshanya, bi asimanse iresan zhoujin mutunyi shunjizhi
ACT 26:20 xien Damashigede, pse Yelusalende, Yudayani go oronlade, niman kunlade chonjizhi geizhen giedene Hudade shunjizhi geizhen giesan shiqinne giezhi uzhegha giewo.
ACT 26:21 Ene yenyin jiere Yutai kunla mechide mii barei agidene alane giezho.
ACT 26:22 Ingieliuzhe enedu kurutula Huda made banman giese bi enende beizhi undu kun boghoni kunliuzhe hhelade man ganzhen beizho. Xienzhila, Musa kieliezhi jianlai fashen giene giesan shiqinse chugo bi yama ese kieliezho.
ACT 26:23 Hheshijiu Mexiha bixi shouku giedene fugusan kun dundase xien aminne oludene Yutai kun, niman kunlade gonni mejieghane giesan wo."
ACT 26:24 Baolo ingiezhi huise Feisidu fugiede kieliewo, "Baolo, chi fenjiulizho. Chii unhua texien undudase chii fenjiulighazho!"
ACT 26:25 Baolo kieliewo, "Feisidu fugie noyen, bi uye fenjiulizho. Bi qinchude sumulasan daolini kieliezho.
ACT 26:26 Honshanye ene shiqinlai mejiene. Ingiese bi uye ayizhi hhende kieliezho. Ene shiqinni beimiende ese giezho, ingiese enelai noyende nieda mii dakui bi mejiene.
ACT 26:27 Yajipa honshanya, chi xienzhini xianxin gienu? Chi xianxin giekui bi mejiene."
ACT 26:28 Ingiese YajipaBaolode kieliewo, "Chi intughanighala mii kieliezhi Mexihani tuji gholughanu?"
ACT 26:29 Baolo kieliewo, "Intughaniye olune, olonye olune. Chi, pse enedu enende chenliesan kunla man bi mutun gholuse giezhi bi Hudase onxian giezho, zinie bi mutun jieliu bu zho giezho."
ACT 26:30 Ingiese honshan, shenzhan, Beinisi, pse sousan kunlare bosizhedene
ACT 26:31 khuina dao echi nieniedene kieliezho, "Ene kun fuguku, khaku zui ese fanjizho."
ACT 26:32 Ingiedene YajipaFeisidude kieliewo, "Ene kun Kaisa honshande ese zhazhoshi eqighan andaghawo."
ACT 27:1 Bijienni chon soughazhi Idalide echighane giezhi jiejin giese hhela Baolo, psedu fanrenlai hongun buduilani nie baifuzhande jiuizhi ogiwo. Niereini Yuliu giene.
ACT 27:2 Niekozi Yadamiqiense iresan chon Yaxiya oronni haibienzighun yone giezho. Bijien hhe chon jiere khirei yowo. Bijienre hhantu yosanshi Maqidunni Qiesalonijia kun Yalidagu wo.
ACT 27:3 Khuichudu Xidunde kuruwo. YuliuBaoloi danren giezhi zhanlienlaini uzheghale echise zhanlienlani Baoloi zhaogu giezho.
ACT 27:4 Hhense chonni keizhi qiise kei shun uwoshi bijien keini piizhi Saipulusiyi beimienghun yozho.
ACT 27:5 Bijien Jilijia, Panfeiliyani meliedu haini daodene Lijiani Meilade kuzhewo.
ACT 27:6 Hhende niekozi Idalide echine giesan Yalishandani chonni penjise baifuzhan bijienyi hhe chon jiere khireighawo.
ACT 27:7 Lienjizhi giedudu chon yozhi tanshi kuzhe dazhi ingiezhi cai Genitu bienzide kuzhewo. Kei bijienyi jiohoro giese Samonini bienzise keini piizhi Kelitedao douraghun yozho.
ACT 27:8 Bijien bienzighun yose chon yozhi chijia no wo. Ingie cai Laxiya chenshini kouisan Seighan Haibienzi giezhi nie oronde irewo.
ACT 27:9 Oloncha shijien danwu giezhi orozo bareiku shihou ijin daose pse chon keizhi wixiennudawo. Ingie Baolo kunlade sughazhi kieliewo,
ACT 27:10 "Dajiala, bi uzhese enefa chon keizhi wixien no wo. Zinie ho, chonni qida olughaku pusho, matan aminne da gui dane."
ACT 27:11 Baifuzhan Baoloi kielienni ese chenliezhi chon keisan kun, chonni ezhanyi kielienyi chenliezho.
ACT 27:12 Ene haibienzide uncha daoghaku chijia wo. Ingiese dabufen kunla hhense likai giezhi Feinikede echidene uncha daoghaye giezhi jiejin giewo. Feinikeshi Kelitedaoni nie haibienzi wo. Niemienni xinan miende wo, niemienni xibei miende wo.
ACT 27:13 Ene shihoude nanbangiese ga kei bosiwo. Hhela sumulase zhao jihuaghala yose olune giezhi chon beighaku gougoui khizheghadene Kelitedaoi kouizhi yozho.
ACT 27:14 Oloncha ese beidene nie honfenkei Kelitedao bienzise feilie irewo. Hhe honfenkeini nierei Dunbeifen giene.
ACT 27:15 Chonni kei wiqi agise pse melie yo da, keini dagha yozho.
ACT 27:16 Nie ga daoni nierei Gaoda giene. Bijien ene daoni kanzighun keini piizhi yozho. Khuina laisan ga chonni beigha dazhi ingiezhi beighawo.
ACT 27:17 Ga chonni laizhi khizhedene zhashighala fugie chonni zhouwini banla goudaghawo. Saierjini usu douradu shazide guai feilieghakuse ayizhi chon jieredu fugie popui bouzhegha chonni durare yoghawo.
ACT 27:18 Bijienyi kei, lan izhi biidene jindaghase khuichudu hhela holai haide bendawo.
ACT 27:19 Pse niudu daosenu hhela chonde injisan dunxilai qinsi bendawo.
ACT 27:20 Hao giedudu naran, hodunyi chanla dawo. Honfenkei bijienyi biise bijienyi jiuiku xiwon widawo.
ACT 27:21 Kunla giedudu yama ese ijiezho. Baolo hhelai dunda beidene kieliewo, "Dajiala, ta mini kielienyi indan chenliekui wo. Kelitedaose likai ese giewoshi imeghei sunshiji qida olukui uwo.
ACT 27:22 Ede bi tande kielieye, ta zhughene tei. Tai kiemai amin nieda ulie widane, zinie chon widane.
ACT 27:23 Mii gonjisan, bi beiisan Hudai qienxien uzhughu xii mii kanzide beizhi kieliewo,
ACT 27:24 'Baolo, bu ayi. Chi kenjin Kaisa honshanyi melie beine. Huda chighala hhantu chon sousan kunlade pinnan ogine.'
ACT 27:25 Ingiese dajiala, zhughene tei. Huda made matugiezhi kieliese qintui gholukui bi xianxin giene.
ACT 27:26 Matanyi nie haini dao jiere guai feilieghane."
ACT 27:27 14 qien kurudene xienidei chon Yadeliyahai jiere hheliezhi eneman hheman giezho. Chabudu banyedei chon jieredu wiliechila zemin jiere chadashiwo gie,
ACT 27:28 jiochighala nie nanjise gunde 12 zhan wo. Melie gouji yodene pse nie nanjise 9 zhan wo.
ACT 27:29 Hhela chon tashi jiere mughukuse ayizhi chon boghose jieran chon beighaku gougoui boughadene ogheikui panjizho.
ACT 27:30 Wiliechila chon beighaku gougoui chon qiorunse boughazho giezhi yanzi gie, ga chonni usude bougha, holuku muji daizho.
ACT 27:31 Baolo baifuzhan, buduilade kieliewo, "Enezighan kunla chon jiere ulie feiliese ta aminne gui dane."
ACT 27:32 Ingiese buduila ga chonni zhashii chizhi siragha anda boughawo.
ACT 27:33 Ogheikude Baolo ashighalade ijiuni ijie giezhi sughazhi kieliezho, "Ta izhi yama ese ijiezhi enedushi 14 qien oluwo.
ACT 27:34 Ingiese bi tande sughazhi kielieye, ta gouji ijie. Ene tai aminni jiuine. Tai kiemadai nieganzi usunye ulie widane."
ACT 27:35 Ingie Baolo ene kielienyi kieliedene ginanyi barei ashighalai melie Hudade mafan kieliedene ghulu ijiewo.
ACT 27:36 Ingie hhela man zhughene teizhi ijiewo.
ACT 27:37 Bijien chon jiere 276 gie kun wo.
ACT 27:38 Hhela ijie chududene chonni gongiereghane giezhi boudeilai haide bendawo.
ACT 27:39 Ogheisenu hhela hhe oronyi tani dawoma, nie haibienzii chanlawo. Ingie chonni jinlianji bienzide echighane giezho.
ACT 27:40 Ingie jiesunyi chizhi siragha chon beighaku gougoui haide boughawo. Fanxian kunzhi gieku doni sularaghazhi popui lai khireighase zhao keizhe bienzide echiwo.
ACT 27:41 Lianmienni usu hhantulasan shazitu oronde chonni qiorunyi jiai beighawo. Lan chon boghoi eghi qida olughawo.
ACT 27:42 Ingiekude fanrenla unba holu widakuse ayizhi buduila hhelai alane giezho.
ACT 27:43 Baifuzhan Baoloi jiuine giezhi hhelai ingiezhi ese gieghawo. Ingie fenfulazhi unba mejiechen kunla usude jioli bou, xien bienzide khirei giewo.
ACT 27:44 Psedu kunla banba, chon jieredu dunxighala bienzide khirei gie wo. Ingiezhi dajialai jiuizhi usu bienzide khireiwo.
ACT 28:1 Bijien pinnande bienzi jiere khirei, ene daoni Maerta giekui mejiewo.
ACT 28:2 Hhe oronyi kunla bijiende gou no wo. Hhende ghura bouzhi qienqi kuiqienshi khan sideraghazhi bijienyi zhaogu giewo.
ACT 28:3 Baolo ezighan muzhai qiangu ire khande teise nie mogheii tulie bazilie da, holu khizhe Baoloi khaini jinji beizho.
ACT 28:4 Hhe oronyi kunla moghei hhei kha jiere horo beisanyi chanladene nieniedene kieliezho, "Ene kunshi kenjin nie sharenfan wo. Haise jiui khizhewoma, asiman hhei aminne ulie olughane."
ACT 28:5 Baolo mogheini khande benda oroghawoma, shan ese deilazho.
ACT 28:6 Hhela sumulase hhe khaitumu, pse zemin jiere fura boudene fugumu giezho. Oloncha sagheise yama uye giesei chanladene kharei hheshi nie huda wo giezho.
ACT 28:7 Hhe shida nie ghazha wine, dao jieredu zui fugie noyen Bubailiunughun wo. Hhe bijienyi jienliezhi shixinji ghurudu zhaodai giewo.
ACT 28:8 Ingiekude Bubailiuni adani fashao giezhi xieli kudene kijiezho. Baolo orozhi echi onxian giezhi hhei jiere khane teiwo.
ACT 28:9 Ingiese dao jieredu gientulaye irezhi man goudaghawo.
ACT 28:10 Hhela bijienyi hende danren giezhi bijien yokude mo jiere injiku dunxilai chon jiere khughozhi ogiwo.
ACT 28:11 Dao jiere ghuran sara beidene bijien nie Yalishandase iresan chon jiere khirei yo qiiwo. Ene chonshi haini dao jiere uncha daoghasan wo, qiorun jiereni Shongo giesan hao teizho.
ACT 28:12 Bijien Xilagude kurudene ghurudu beiwo.
ACT 28:13 Pse hhense raoizhi Lijiwunde echiwo. Niudu daose nanbangieni kei bosise khuichudu Bujiulide kuruwo.
ACT 28:14 Hhende ezighan gaijiulai ochiradene bijienyi xinlazhi echi hhelare hhantu doludu souwo. Bijien ingiezhi Lomade kuzhewo.
ACT 28:15 Hhendedu gaijiula bijienyi xioxini sonosudene Lomase Yabiwu geidoude, pse Ghuran Lishe giesan ime gholo oronde bijienyi jienliele irewo. Baolo hhelai chanladene Hudade mafan kieliezhi danzi fugiedawo.
ACT 28:16 Bijien Lomade kuruse Baoloi uzhesan nie buduighala danxin soukui tunyi oluwo.
ACT 28:17 Ghurudu daodene BaoloYutai kunni lindaolai uruzhi irewo. Hhela irese Baolo kieliewo, "Gaijiula, bi goya kunlane, xienrenlai guijinni fandui gieku shiqin uye giezhoma, mii Yelusalende bareizhi Loma kunde jiuizhi ogiwo.
ACT 28:18 Hhela mii shenwun giezhi yama fuguku zui ereizhi olu dadene mii andaghane giese
ACT 28:19 Yutai kunla fandui giezhi made banfa widadene Kaisa honshande zhawo. Bi goya kunlane zhane ese giezho.
ACT 28:20 Ingiese bi tai xinlazhi ire danmien kielieye giezho. Bi Isilie kunla panjisan hhe kunyi yenyin jiere ene qieshenyi zhozho."
ACT 28:21 Ingiese hhela kieliewo, "Bijien Yudayase chii kieliesan xinni jienliezhi ese daozho. Gaijiula dundaye kiema chii zhazhi yama huaini kieliezhi ese daozho.
ACT 28:22 Ingieliuzhe bijien chii ijien matugiezho giezhi chenlieku duran wine. Ene jiomunni kunla gochude fandui giekui bijien mejiene."
ACT 28:23 Ingiese hhela udu jinjidene olon kunla Baolo sousan oronde irewo. Baolo eqiemaghase khara olutula hhelade Hudai gojiai daolii jianjizhi ganzhen beizho. Musani shu, xienzhilai shughala Ersani shiqinyi kieliezhi shundaghawo.
ACT 28:24 Baolo kieliesan kielienyi chenliedene niezhanla xianxin giewo, niezhanla xianxin ese giewo.
ACT 28:25 Hhelai ijien kiemai ijien buxianshi sandane giekude Baolo nie aman kielien kieliewo, "Shenlin Isaiya xienzhii tungo giezhi tai xienrenlade kieliesan kielien ese codazho,
ACT 28:26 'Chi echidene ene bexinlade kielie, 'Ta izhi chenliezhoma, dunjire dane. Ta izhi uzhezhoma, minbai olu dane.
ACT 28:27 Ene bexinlai zhughe khiduzhezhi chighin beidazhi nudunne hameizho. Pse nudunni chanlazhi chighinni sonosuzhi zhughedeni minbai oludene kharei daorese Bi hhelai goudaghakuse ayizho.
ACT 28:28 Ingiese ta mejiendu. Huda ene jiuiku daolini niman kunlade chonjizhi ogiwo. Hhelaye chenliene."
ACT 28:30 Baolo goya bouisan giedene ghua hon souzhi hhei ochirale iresan kunlai man jienliewo.
ACT 28:31 Hhe zui fugie danzighala Hudai gojiai daolii jianjizhi Ezhan Ersa Mexihani shiqinyi kunlade sughase danlachen kun uwo.
ROM 1:1 Bishi Ersa Mexihani hoji Baolo wo. Hudai gouxioxini zhomen chonjighane giezhi mii uruzhi iredene shitu danlaghawo.
ROM 1:2 Ene gouxioxishi eqighanse Huda xienzhilai tungo giezhi zhiguitu jinwun jiere dain giesan wo.
ROM 1:3 Gouxioxishi Hudai kewon, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai kieliezho. Hhei kunni fanmiende kieliese Dawudeni houdei wo. Zhiguitu ruhherni fanmiende kieliese fugie nenlighala fugusan kun dundase aminne oluzhi Hudai kewon bikui mejieghawo.
ROM 1:5 Huda Mexihai tungo giezhi bijiende shitu danlaku nenjien ogidene soyuji minzulade hhei nierei xianxin gieghazhi shunjighazho.
ROM 1:6 Ene dunda taye wine. Huda tai uruzhi iredene Ersa Mexihanughun danlaghawo.
ROM 1:7 Huda orezhi uruzhi iredene shentu danlaghasan Loma kunlade bi xin huaizho. Mai ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
ROM 1:8 Bi xien ta dajialade oluzhi Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi bi zunjisan Hudade mafan kieliekushi ta xianxin giesei qienxiani kunla man mejiezho.
ROM 1:9 Bi onxian giekude ese beidene tai jilazho. Bi hhei kewonni gouxioxi jiere zhughesene shunjisan Huda enende ganzhen beine.
ROM 1:10 Bi chan xiahua giese Hudai isi enbese bi zuihoude tai hhende echine.
ROM 1:11 Bi tai hende chujiegheku duranshi Hudai nenjienni tande deilazhi tai khiduzheghane giezho.
ROM 1:12 Isishi matan nieniene xianxin giekughala nieniedene zhichi gieye giezho.
ROM 1:13 Gaijiula, psedu minzula dundashiku mutun tai dundase jiego khizheghane giezhi bi tai hhende haojihui echine giesan jihuai tande mejieghaku duran wine. Daliuzhe jiohoro giezhi echi dazho.
ROM 1:14 Bugon Xila kun, wigokun, unhuatu kun, unhua witu kunlade bi yama chaisan mutun giezho.
ROM 1:15 Ingiese bi ta Lomade sousanladeye gouxioxini chonjine giezhi hende duralazho.
ROM 1:16 Bi gouxioxise ulie shizhene. Gouxioxishi soyuji xianxin giesan kunlai jiuiku Hudai nenli wo, xien Yutai kun, pse Xila kun.
ROM 1:17 Gouxioxi jiere Hudai gundanni khizhezho. Ene gundanni kaishi giezhi baratula xianxin giekughala giene. Jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun, "Gou kun xianxin giekughala amiturane."
ROM 1:18 Hudai hokuku doghunnighala zhendaoi duisan kunlai soyuji xienlian witu, gou wituni kunlai jiere asiman jierese bouzhezho.
ROM 1:19 Ingiekushi kunla Hudai shiqinni mejiekui man mejiene. Hhelade Huda qinchude uzheghawo.
ROM 1:20 Duyai zhayaghasanse Hudai tejien, hhei chanqiku nenlini chanla danema, zhayaghasanlai uzhezhi qinchude mejiene. Ingiese kunlade yama kieliekui uwo.
ROM 1:21 Hhela Hudai mejienema, Huda wo giezhi ulie kuaizhi mafan ulie kieliene. Hhelai sumulaku yama oronde wiku gholuwo, zhugheni benni gholuzhi kharanide wo.
ROM 1:22 Hhela goyane jienzha wo giezhoma, ben wo.
ROM 1:23 Hhela chanqiku Hudai famani fuguku kun, bunzhu, yewo, ghugheilai yanzi gholughawo.
ROM 1:24 Ingiese Huda hhelai ese gonjidene hhela nefuxinne daghazhi zannannide echizhi nieniene beyede shizhekuni giezho.
ROM 1:25 Hhela Hudai zhendaoi jianighala daiqi giedene zhayaghachenni ese beiidene zhayaghasanlai shunjizhi beiine. Hudashi indan chanqi kuaikuni wo. Amine.
ROM 1:26 Ingiese Huda hhelai ese gonjidene hhela shizheku nefuxin giezho. Hhelai biereila zhenchande giekui ulie giedene zhenchan wini giene.
ROM 1:27 Ere kunlaye biereighalane zhenchande giekuni ulie giedene nienieni nefuxin bazilie dase ere kun ere kunghala shizhekuni giene. Ingiezhi hhelai codasande indan chenfa giekui goya jierene ireghazho.
ROM 1:28 Hhela Hudai tanise guazi wo giese Huda hhelai ese gonjidene guazitu sumuladande fanqi giewo. Ingiese hhela ulie giekuni giezho.
ROM 1:29 Hhelade yanyanji gou wini, doghunni, tanxin, mouxienni duruzho. Dubilieku, alaku, eghinduku, piendaku, tuguni duruzho. Xienhua kieliene,
ROM 1:30 beihoude kunni sugiene, Hudai henjine, kunni yamacha ulie teine, goyane fugiede uzhezhi kuaine, doghun shiqinyi khizheghane, ada anadene ulie shunjine.
ROM 1:31 Yama ulie mejiene, kieliendene ulie kurune, oreku, ubali xiiku zhughe uwo.
ROM 1:32 Hudai guijin mutunshi jien ene shiqinni giesan kun indan fugukuni hhela mejiene. Ingieliuzhe goyalane giene, da kunla giese gou wo giezho.
ROM 2:1 Ingiese chi ene kunlai kieliechen kun, chi kienliuzhe yama jiekou erei dane. Chi kunlai kieliekude goyaneye niekielienji giese goyadene zui jinjizho.
ROM 2:2 Huda intui giechen kunlai gundande panjikui matan mejiene.
ROM 2:3 Chi ene kunlai kieliedene niekielienji giesan kun, chi sumulase Hudai panjikuse andane giezhou?
ROM 2:4 Huda tebieji goude giezhi, ranjizhi, rennai giese chi meilade uzhenu? Huda chade goude giekushi chii geizhen gieghane giekuni ulie mejienu?
ROM 2:5 Chii zhughe khidunde geizhen ulie giedene Huda gundande panjiku hhe udu kuzhetula goyadene Hudai hokukui izhi olodoghazho.
ROM 2:6 Huda kunla giekughala kunlade kharulune.
ROM 2:7 Gou wilieni izhi giezhi kuaiku, gou minshen, chanqi ulie qida olukuni giesan kunlade Huda chanqiku aminni ogine.
ROM 2:8 Zi goyane guizhi zhendaoni ulie shunjidene gou winii shunjichen kunlade hokuku, faikughala kharulune.
ROM 2:9 Jien doghunnii giesan kunlade zeinan, tunkuni ogine. Xien Yutai kun, pse Xila kun.
ROM 2:10 Jien gounii giesan kunlade kuaiku, gou minshen, pinnanni ogine. Xien Yutai kun, pse Xila kun.
ROM 2:11 Huda kunlai pienxin ulie giene.
ROM 2:12 Jien guijinni chenliezhi uye daodene zui fanjisan kunla guijinghala gonxi widene widane. Jien guijinni chenliedene zui fanjisan kunlai guijinghala panjine.
ROM 2:13 Guijinni chenliese Hudai melie gounide ulie sanane, guijinni zunjise gounide sanane.
ROM 2:14 Guijin ese ogisan niman kunla olusanse goyane guijin mutun giese, hhelade guijin uwoma, ene hhelai guijin gholuwo.
ROM 2:15 Giesanlaini uzhese guijinni yoqiu hhelai zhughede teisei mejiene. Lianxinniye enende ganzhen beine. Hhelai zhughede maodun giezhi goyane kheilane, baohu giene.
ROM 2:16 Eneshi, bi chonjisan gouxioxi mutun, Huda Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi kunla niuighasan shiqin man panjiku hhe udude fashen giene.
ROM 2:17 Chi ene goyane Yutai kun wo giesan, guijinni kouizhi Hudai mejiene giezhi goyane kuaizho.
ROM 2:18 Chi Hudai isii mejiene, guijinse suruzhi gounii fenji shidane,
ROM 2:19 goyane sughoni udurusan wo, kharani dundadu gon wo giezho.
ROM 2:20 Chi guijinghala erlin, zhendaoi zhanwo giezhi ben kun, kesilade sughachen loushi danlane giezhi goyane xianxin giezho.
ROM 2:21 Qinse chi kunlade sughase goyadene yan giezhi ese sughazho? Kunlade bu ghula giezhi sughadene goyane ghulanu?
ROM 2:22 Chi kunlade piofen bu gie giezhi kieliedene goyane piofen gienu? Chi nigiedalai uzhe dadene, goyane mioni dunxii ghulanu?
ROM 2:23 Chi guijinni kuaidene guijinni fanjizhi Hudai shizheghanu?
ROM 2:24 Jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun, "Tai yenyinghala niman kunlai dunda Hudai nierei sugiezho."
ROM 2:25 Chi guijinni zunjise giesan hetoune haochu wine. Hetoune giedene guijinni fanjise hetoune ese giesanghala niekielien wo.
ROM 2:26 Ingiese hetoune ese giesanla guijinni zunjise hetoune ese giezhoma hetoude ulie sananu?
ROM 2:27 Hetoune ese giedene guijinni zunjisan kunla hetoune giezhi huaisan guijinni bidene guijinni fanjisan kunni zui jinjine.
ROM 2:28 Biomien jiere Yutai kunshi Yutai kun pusho. Beye, mienzide giesan hetouneshi zhen hetoune pusho.
ROM 2:29 Zinie sudoro Yutai kun danlasan kunshi Yutai kun wo. Zhen hetouneshi zhughenughun wo. Huaisande ulie kouine. Shenlinde kouine. Ene kunyi kuaikushi kunse iresan pusho, Hudase wo.
ROM 3:1 Ingiese Yutai kun danlase yan haochu wo? Hetoune giese yande gou wo?
ROM 3:2 Go fanmiende wine. Xien Hudai kielienyi hhelade ogiwo.
ROM 3:3 Niezhanla xianxin ulie giese matugiene? Hhela kekao wise Hudaye kekao uwonu?
ROM 3:4 Kenjin pusho! Kunla man ghudan kieliese Huda ghudan ulie kieliene. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Chi kielien kieliekude gundan wo giene. Shenwun giekude chi injine."
ROM 3:5 Matanyi gou wiku Hudai gounii khizheghase matan matui kieliene? Huda matanyi faise gundan uwonu? Bi kunni jiodughala kieliezho.
ROM 3:6 Kenjin pusho! Qinse Huda matugie duyani panjine?
ROM 3:7 Bi ghudan kieliedene Hudai zhennii qinchushighazhi hhei kuaise mii yangiezhi zuiren mutun panjine?
ROM 3:8 Qinse matan huaini gieyema, gouni irene giezhi yale ulie kieliene? Niezhanla bijien ingiezhi kieliezho giezhi zhazho. Ene kunlai indan panjikuni wo.
ROM 3:9 Ingiese bijien Yutai kun niman kunlase hen onu? Kenjin pusho! Kunla man zui dunda wo, Yutai kun niman kun man niekielien wo giezhi bijien kieliezhi daozho.
ROM 3:10 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Gou kun uwo, nieliuzhe uwo.
ROM 3:11 Minbai oluchen kun uwo, Hudai ereichen kun uwo.
ROM 3:12 Kunla man xiemachalazhi yama oronde uwo. Gounii giechen kun uwo, nieliuzhe uwo."
ROM 3:13 "Hhelai gholei keisan meza niekielien wo. Hhelai kielienshi kun piendakui wo." "Hhelai aman furedeni mogheii du wine."
ROM 3:14 "Hhelai amande okho sugiekui duruzho."
ROM 3:15 "Kun alane giese ghujin no wo.
ROM 3:16 Kurusan orondeni pohai nangoi jiezho.
ROM 3:17 Pinnanni moni ulie mejiene."
ROM 3:18 "Hudase goujida ulie ayine."
ROM 3:19 Guijinshi guijintu kunlade kieliesei matan mejiene. Ingiedene soyuji kunlai amanni menjighazhi qienxiani kunlai man Hudai panjikude ireghane.
ROM 3:20 Guijinni zunjizhi giedene Hudai melie gounide sanasan kun nieda uwo. Guijinni tungo giezhi zuini mejiene.
ROM 3:21 Ede guijinse chugo Hudai gundanni khizhezho. Enende guijinshu, xienzhishu jiere ganzhen beizho.
ROM 3:22 Hheshijiu Ersa Mexihai xianxin giesan jien kunlade olusan Hudai gundanni wo. Yan kunliuzhe niekielien wo.
ROM 3:23 Jien kunla zui fanjidene Hudai famade dai dazhoma,
ROM 3:24 Ersa Mexihai shuikui tungo giezhi Hudai nenjienghala belien gouni wo giezho.
ROM 3:25 Huda Ersai kunni oronde fugughazhi shuiku gholughawo. Hhei xianxin giesan kunlai zuini mienliene. Ingiezhi Huda gundanne uzheghawo. Eqighandei Huda kunla fanjisan zuini rennai giezhi ese gonjizho.
ROM 3:26 Edeku shihoude ingiezhi Huda goyaneshi gundan bikui, pse Ersai xianxin giesan kunlai gounii uzheghazho.
ROM 3:27 Ingiese matan yanni kuaine? Yama kuaikui uwo. Yan banfaghala wo? Gieku banfaghala onu? Pusho! Xianxin gieku banfaghala wo.
ROM 3:28 Bijien uzhese kunni gounide sanakushi guijinni zunjizhi giekughala pusho, xianxin giekughala wo.
ROM 3:29 Hudashi zinie Yutai kunlai Huda onu? Niman kunlai Huda pushonu? Enbene, hheshi niman kunlai Hudaye enbene.
ROM 3:30 Hudashi nie wo. Hetoune giesanlai xianxin giekughala gounide sanane, hetoune uye giesanlaiye xianxin giekughala gounide sanane.
ROM 3:31 Ingiese matan xianxin giekughala guijinni bendazhou? Kenjin uye! Khareidene guijinni khiduzheghazho.
ROM 4:1 Ingiese bijienyi minzui xienren Iburaheimui matui kieliene? Hhe yan mejiewo?
ROM 4:2 Iburaheimu giekughala gounide sanazhoshi kuai shidanema, Hudai melie kuaikui uwo.
ROM 4:3 Jinwun jiere matui kieliezho? Iburaheimu Hudai xianxin giedene Huda hhei gounide sanazho giezho.
ROM 4:4 Wilie giezhi gunzi bareise indanji wo, nenjiende ulie sanane.
ROM 4:5 Kun yama wilie ulie giedene xienlian witu kunlai gouni wo giesan Hudai xianxin giese hhei xianxin giekuni gounide sanane.
ROM 4:6 Wilie giekughala gonxi wi Huda gounide sanasan kunlade fuqi winekui Dawudeye kieliezho,
ROM 4:7 "Codasanyi rouliezhi zuini khasan kunlade fuqi wine.
ROM 4:8 Huda zui uwo giesan kunlade fuqi wine."
ROM 4:9 Ingiese ene fuqii zinie hetoune giesan kunlade ogizhou? Hetoune ese giesan kunlade uye ogizhou? Iburaheimu xianxin giekughala gounide sanasanyi matan kieliezho.
ROM 4:10 Hhei yan xienzide gounide sanazho? Hetoune gietula onu, hetoune giedene wo? Hetoune giedene pusho, gietula wo.
ROM 4:11 Hhe giesan hetouneshi hetoune ese giekude xianxin giekughala gouni wo giesande zhanzi taisan hao wo. Ingiedene hhezighan hetoune ese gie xianxin giekughala gounide sanasan kunlade xienren danlawo.
ROM 4:12 Iburaheimushi hetoune giesan kunlai xienrenye enbene. Zinie hetoune gieku pusho. Mai xienren Iburaheimu hetoune ese giekude xianxin giesan yanziini daghasan kunlai xienren wo.
ROM 4:13 Huda Iburaheimuji houdeiladeni duyani ogine giezhi dain giesanshi guijinghala pusho, xianxin giedene iresan gounighala wo.
ROM 4:14 Zinie guijintu kunlade ogizhoshi xianxin giesan yama oronde uwo, dain giesanyiye ulie sanane.
ROM 4:15 Guijin Hudai hokukuni ireghazho. Guijin wise guijinyi fanjiku shiqinye uwo.
ROM 4:16 Ingiese dain giesanshi xianxin giekughala ogizho. Hheshi Iburaheimuni houdeilade belien ogisan nenjien wo. Zinie guijintu kunlade ogisan pusho, Iburaheimu mutun xianxin giesan kunladeye bouisan wo. Hudai melie Iburaheimushi matan dajialai xienren wo.
ROM 4:17 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Bi chii olon minzulai xienren gholughane." Fugusan kunni aminne olughachen, uwokuse wineku gholughachen Hudai Iburaheimu xianxin giewo.
ROM 4:18 Hhe xiwon wikude xiwon giezhi olon minzulai xienren danlakui xianxin giewo. Huda hhende kieliesan mutun, "Chii houdeila ingiezhi olodone."
ROM 4:19 Hhe 100 oluzhi beyeni fuguku mutun, biereini olu dakui mejieliuzhe xianxin giekuni ese zholierezho.
ROM 4:20 Huda dain giesanyi xianxin giezhi uye inxin giedene kharei xianxin giekuni khiduzhezhi Hudai kuaizho.
ROM 4:21 Huda dain giesei chenjighakui hhe hende xianxin giezho.
ROM 4:22 Ingiese hhei gounide sanazho.
ROM 4:23 Gounide sanazho giesan ene kielienyi zinie hhende ese huaizho,
ROM 4:24 matandeye huaizho. Mai Ezhan Ersai fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Hudai xianxin giesan maiye gounide sanane.
ROM 4:25 Ersai kunlade jiuizhi mai zuide oluzhi duya ijiewo, matanyi gounide sanane giezhi aminne oluwo.
ROM 5:1 Ingiese matan xianxin giekughala gounide sanase matan mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi Hudare goudazho.
ROM 5:2 Matan Ersai tungo giezhi xianxin giekughala ede xianshou giesan nenjiende irezho. Da bayasuzhi Hudai famani panjizho.
ROM 5:3 Zinie ene pusho. Chijia dundaye bayasune. Chijiase rennai surune,
ROM 5:4 rennaise undan surune, undanse xiwon surukuni matan mejiene.
ROM 5:5 Xiwon matai ulie kushidaghakushi Huda matande ogisan Shenlinni tungo giezhi orekune matai zhughede kie durughawo.
ROM 5:6 Matande banfa widakude shihou kuruse Mexiha matan xienlian witu kunlade oluzhi duya ijiewo.
ROM 5:7 Gundan kunde oluzhi fuguchen kun choghon wo, gou kunde oluzhi fuguchen kun kenen winema,
ROM 5:8 matan dou zuiren bikude Mexiha matande oluzhi fugudene Huda matande oresanne qinchude uzheghazho.
ROM 5:9 Ede Mexihai chusunyi tungo giezhi matai gounide sanawo, hhe Hudai hokusanse matai genjia jiuine.
ROM 5:10 Matan Hudai duitou bikude hhe kewonne fugughazhi matanre goudazho, Mexihai aminghala matai genjia jiuine.
ROM 5:11 Zinie ene pusho. Matan Ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi Hudare goudadene Hudai yenyin jiere bayasuzho.
ROM 5:12 Ingiese zui nie kunse duyade irezhi fuguku zuise iresan mutun kunla man zui fanjidene fuguku kunlai jiere irezho.
ROM 5:13 Guijin witula zui duyade winema, guijin uwoshi zuide ulie sanane.
ROM 5:14 Ingieliuzhe Adanse Musade kurutula fuguku qienli bareizho. Lien Adan fanjisan zuini ese fanjisan kunlaye man fuguzho. Adanshi khuina ireku hhe kunyi yanzi wo.
ROM 5:15 Ingiese nenjien zuighala buxian wo. Nie kun zui fanjise olon kunla fuguzhoma, Hudai nenjien, Ersa Mexiha niezheghanyi nenjienghala belien ogisan mure olon kunlade genjia olon ogizho.
ROM 5:16 Huda ogisan mure nie kun fanjisan zuighala buxian wo. Panjikushi nie kun zui fanjisande zui jinjizho, nenjienshi olon kunla zui fanjisande gounide sanasan wo giezho.
ROM 5:17 Nie kun zui fanjise fuguku nie kunni tungo giezhi qienli bareizho, nenjien olon jienliezhi belien gouni wo giesan hhezighan kunla Ersa Mexiha niezheghanyi tungo giezhi amin dunda qienli genjia bareine.
ROM 5:18 Ingiese nie zui fanjidene soyuji kunlade zui jinjiku mutun, nie gounii giedene soyuji kunlai gounide sanazhi amin ogiwo.
ROM 5:19 Nie kun ulie shunjidene olon kunlai zuiren gholughaku mutun, nie kun shunjidene olon kunlai gounide sananne.
ROM 5:20 Guijin iredene zui olodozhoma, zui olodosan oronde nenjien genjia fugiedazho.
ROM 5:21 Ingiedene zui qienli bareizhi fugukui ogisan mutun, nenjien qienli bareizhi kunlai gounide sanadene mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani tungo giezhi chanqiku amin ogizho.
ROM 6:1 Ingiese matan matui kieliene? Matan nenjienni olodoghane giezhi zui dunda izhi beinu?
ROM 6:2 Kenjin ulie olune! Matan zui miende fugudene matugie zui dunda udu daone?
ROM 6:3 Matan xilii jienliezhi Mexiha Ersare hhantulasan kun hhere hhantu fugusei ta ulie mejienu?
ROM 6:4 Matan xilii tungo giezhi hhere hhantu fuguzhi hhantu bulawo. Ingiekushi Adai famaghala Mexihai fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan mutun mataiye shini amin dunda udu daoghane giezho.
ROM 6:5 Matan hhe fugukude hhere hhantulase hhe aminne olukudeye hhere hhantulane.
ROM 6:6 Matan khuichen kunne hhere hhantu shizijia jiere ghadazhi zuitu beyene widaghasei mejiene. Ingiese matan pse zuide hoji ulie danlane.
ROM 6:7 Fugusan kun zuise andazho.
ROM 6:8 Matan Mexihare hhantu fuguse hhereye hhantu amiturakui xianxin giene.
ROM 6:9 Mexiha fugusan kun dundase aminne oluzhi pse ulie fugune. Fuguku hhei kunzhi gie dakui matan mejiene.
ROM 6:10 Hhe fuguse zui miende 1 huide fuguwo. Amiturase Hudai miende amiturazho.
ROM 6:11 Taye zui miende goyane fugusan sanazhi Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi Hudai miende amitu sana.
ROM 6:12 Ingiese zuini tai fuguku beye jiere qienli bu bareighazhi zui gieku nefuxinyi bu dagha.
ROM 6:13 Ta beye jieredu yama iyanzii zuide ogizhi gou winide jiaji bu danlagha. Khareidene fugusan kun dundase aminne olusan kun wo giezhi goyane Hudade ogi. Beye jieredulane man Hudade ogizhi gou jiaji danlagha.
ROM 6:14 Zui tai gonji dakushi ta guijin doura uwo, nenjien doura wo.
ROM 6:15 Qinse matugiene? Matan guijin doura uwo, nenjien dourashi zui fanjise olunu? Kenjin ulie olune!
ROM 6:16 Ta goyane kiende ogizhi kienyi shunjise kiende hoji danlakui ta ulie mejienu? Zuini hoji danlase fugune, Hudai shunjichen hoji danlase gouni gholune.
ROM 6:17 Hudade mafan kielieye, ta melieshida zuini hoji woma, ede tande chonjisan daolini ta zhughesene shunjiwo.
ROM 6:18 Ingiedene zuise tai andaghazhi gounide hoji danlawo.
ROM 6:19 Ta dunjire dakuse ayizhi bi ibanji kielienghala kielieye. Ta melieshida beyene ganjin winide, uhunnide ogizhi hoji danladene uhunni gholughasan mutun ede ta beyene gounide ogizhi hoji danladene zhiguitu gholugha.
ROM 6:20 Ta zuide hoji danlakude gouni gieku biyo uwo.
ROM 6:21 Ingiese ta ede sumulase shizheku shiqinyi hhe xienzide giedene tande yan haochu wo? Hhei jiegoshi fuguku wo.
ROM 6:22 Ede tai zuise andaghazhi Hudai hoji danlaghawo. Tai haochushi zhigui wo. Jiegoshi chanqiku amin wo.
ROM 6:23 Zuini daijiashi fugukuni wo. Hudai nenjienshi mai Ezhan Mexiha Ersai sudoro bisan chanqiku amin wo.
ROM 7:1 Gaijiula, ta guijinni mejiechen kunlade bi kielieye. Guijinshi kun zinie amitu bikude oronde bisei ta ulie mejienu?
ROM 7:2 Biereide zhanguiji bizhi amitushi guijinni yenyinghala zhanguijisene likai gie dane. Zhanguijini fuguse zhanguijine guijinse andawo.
ROM 7:3 Ingiese zhanguijini bidene pse nie kunde khise biozi giezhi urune. Zhanguijini fuguse hhe guijinse andawo. Pse nie kunde khise biozi pusho.
ROM 7:4 Mii gaijiula, taye niekielien wo. Ta Mexihani beyei tungo giezhi guijinse fuguwo. Ingiedene pse nienughun gholuzhi matan Hudade gou jiego ireghane. Hheshi fugusan kun dundase aminne olusan Mexiha wo.
ROM 7:5 Matan beyenughun bikude zui gieku nefuxin guijinni tungo giezhi mai jiere wilie giedene fugukui ireghawo.
ROM 7:6 Ede matanyi banlasan guijinse matan fuguzhi andawo. Ingiese matan Ezhanni shunjise uroughala giesan guijinni khuichen banfaghala ulie giene, Shenlinni shini banfaghala giene.
ROM 7:7 Ingiese matan matui kieliene? Guijinshi zui onu? Kenjin pusho! Guijin uwoshi bi yanshi zui bikui ulie mejiene. Guijin jiere tanxin bu gie giezhi ese kieliezhoshi bi tanxinshi yan bikui ulie mejiene.
ROM 7:8 Zui minlinghala jihui ereizhi mii zhughede yanyanji tanxin giekui khizheghazho. Guijin uwoshi zuishi fugusei wo.
ROM 7:9 Eqighan guijin uwokude bi amitu wo. Minlin irese zui aminne oluwo, bi fuguwo.
ROM 7:10 Hhe yenlai amin ireghaku minlin mii fugukui gholughawo.
ROM 7:11 Zui minlinni jihuighala mii piendadene hhei tungo giezhi mii fugughawo.
ROM 7:12 Ingiese guijinshi zhiguitu wo. Minlinshiye zhiguitu, gundan, gouni wo.
ROM 7:13 Qinse gouni khareidene mii fugughanu? Kenjin pusho! Mii fugughasanshi zui wo. Zuishi zui bikui mejieghane giezhi gounii tungo giezhi mii fugughawo. Minlinyi tungo giezhi zui zhenzhen doghunne khizheghazho.
ROM 7:14 Guijinshi ruhhernughun bikui matan mejienema, bishi beyenughun wo. Mii zuide huizhi hoji danlaghawo.
ROM 7:15 Bi giene giekune ulie giene, henjisanne kharei giene. Bi yan giesanne ulie mejiene.
ROM 7:16 Bi henjisanne giese guijinshi gouni bikui bi chenren giezho.
ROM 7:17 Ingiese giesanshi bi pusho, mii sudoro sousan zui giezho.
ROM 7:18 Mii sudoro, mii beye jiere gouni uwokui bi mejiene. Bi gounii gieku duran winema, gie dane.
ROM 7:19 Bi gounii gieku duran winema, ulie giene. Doghunnii gieku duran uwoma, khareidene giene.
ROM 7:20 Bi duran wikune giese giesanshi bi pusho. Mii sudoro sousan zui giezho.
ROM 7:21 Bi nie guijin mejiewo. Bi gounii giene giekude doghunniye hhantu wo.
ROM 7:22 Bi sudorone kun Hudai guijinde xiqi woma,
ROM 7:23 beye jieremi pse nie guijin mii zhugheni guijinghala maodun giezhi mii bareidene beye jiere bisan zuini guijinde hoji danlaghasei bi chanlazho.
ROM 7:24 Mii amin muchughun wo, kien mii ene fuguku beyese jiuizhi khizheghane?
ROM 7:25 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi Hudade mafan kielieye! Ingiese mii sumulaku Hudai guijinni shunjizho, mii beye zuini guijinni shunjizho.
ROM 8:1 Ingiese ede Mexiha Ersai miendedu kunlade zui jiedui ulie jinjine.
ROM 8:2 Amin ogiku Shenlinni guijin Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi zuiji fuguku guijinse chii andaghawo.
ROM 8:3 Kunde lilian wiku yenyinghala guijin gie dakui Huda giewo. Huda zuini widaghane giezhi Kewonne zuitu beyeni yanzighala peizhi ireghadene zuini kunlai ese gonjighawo.
ROM 8:4 Ingiedene beyeni ulie daghazhi Shenlinni daghasan mai jiere guijinyi yoqiui gholughawo.
ROM 8:5 Beyeni daghasan kunla beyeni shiqinyi gonxin giene. Shenlinni daghasan kunla Shenlinni shiqinyi gonxin giene.
ROM 8:6 Beyeni shiqinyi gonxin giese fugune. Shenlinni shiqinyi gonxin giese amin, pinnan irene.
ROM 8:7 Kun beyeni shiqinyi gonxin giese Hudaghala duitou gholune. Hudai guijinni ulie shunjine, shunjiye dane.
ROM 8:8 Beyenughunla Hudai bayasugha dane.
ROM 8:9 Hudai Ruhher tai sudoro souse tashi beyenughun pusho, Shenlinnughun wo. Kunde Mexihani ruhher uwoshi Mexihanughun pusho.
ROM 8:10 Mexiha tai sudoro bise beye zuini yenyinghala fuguzhoma, ruhher gounii yenyinghala amiturazho.
ROM 8:11 Ersai fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Hudai Ruhher tai sudoro souse Mexihai fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Huda tai sudoro sousan Shenlinne tungo giezhi tai fuguku beyeni aminne olughane.
ROM 8:12 Gaijiula, ingiese matan beyede zhan chaisan mutun hhei daghazhi gieku biyo uwo.
ROM 8:13 Ta beyeni daghazhi giese fugune. Shenlinde kouizhi beyeni doghun wiliei fugughase amiturane.
ROM 8:14 Jien Hudai Ruhher udurusanlashi Hudai kewosi wo.
ROM 8:15 Ta jienliesanshi hojini ruhher pusho. Pse ulie ayighane. Jienliesanshi kewosi danlaku ruhher wo. Ingiese matan Aba, ada giezhi urune.
ROM 8:16 Shenlin qinsi matanyi ruhherre hhantu matanshi Hudai kewosi wo giezhi ganzhen beizho.
ROM 8:17 Kewosi enbese jiachanyi jienliechen enbene. Matanshi Mexihare hhantu jiachanyi jienliechen Hudai kewosi wo. Matan hhere shouku giekude hhantulase famadeye hhantulane.
ROM 8:18 Bi uzhese edeku shouku gieku jianlai matande ireku famaghala bilazhi ulie olune.
ROM 8:19 Zhayaghasanla jirezhi Hudai kesila xienjizhi khizhekuni panjizho.
ROM 8:20 Zhayaghasanla yama oronde widawo. Hhela imutui gholukushi goya duranghalane pusho, Huda ingiezhi gieghawo.
ROM 8:21 Hhela qida olusande hoji danlakuse andadene Hudai kesilani famatu ziyuni jienliekui panjizho.
ROM 8:22 Zhayaghasanla man hhantu shonholozhi tendun shouizhi eli kusanyi matan mejiene.
ROM 8:23 Zinie zhayaghasanla pusho, Shenlinshi toushu alima wo giezhi jienliesan matanye zhughedene shonholozhi Hudai kewosi danlaku, pse mai beyei jiuizhi shuikui panjizho.
ROM 8:24 Onxianghala matanyi jiuiwo. Chujieghekui onxian giese onxian pusho. Chujieghekui kien onxian giene?
ROM 8:25 Matan chujieghe dakune onxian giese rennai giezhi panjikuni wo.
ROM 8:26 Niekielien wo, Shenlinye matan zholierekude banman giene. Matan indan matugie onxian giekui ulie mejienema, Shenlin hende nango giezhi qinsi matande xiahua giene.
ROM 8:27 Kunni zhughei uzhechen Huda Shenlinyi sumulakui mejiene. Shenlin zhao Hudai isighala shentulade oluzhi xiahua giezho.
ROM 8:28 Hudade oresan kun, jiushi Huda jihuaghalane uruzhi iresan kunlade shiqinla man hhantulazhi gouni gholukui matan mejiene.
ROM 8:29 Huda eqie mejiesan kunlai kewonne yanzi mutun gholughane giezhi pse eqie jinjiwo. Ingiezhi kewonne olon gaijiu dunda fugie kewon danlaghane giezho.
ROM 8:30 Hhe eqighan jinjisan kunlai pse uruzhi irewo. Uruzhi iresan kunlai pse gounide sanawo. Gounide sanasan kunlai famani gholughawo.
ROM 8:31 Ingiese matan enezighan shiqinde yan kieliene? Huda matande banman giese kien fandui giene?
ROM 8:32 Huda Kewonne sheizhi matande ogiwoma, hhere hhantu pseshikulai man matande ulie oginu?
ROM 8:33 Kien Huda sunghusan kunlai zha shidane? Hhelai gounide sanasanshi Huda wo.
ROM 8:34 Kien hhelade zui jinjine? Mexiha Ersa duya ijiezhi aminne oludene ede Hudai borun miende bizhi matande oluzhi xiahua giezho.
ROM 8:35 Kien Mexiha matande orekui siraghane? Kunnan onu? Khishun onu? Heiku onu? Oliesuku onu? Nanxin onu? Wixien onu? Khudogho onu?
ROM 8:36 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Chii yenyinghala bijienyi chanqi alazho. Kunla bijienyi alaku ghoni mutun uzhezho."
ROM 8:37 Ingieliuzhe matande oresan Ezhanni tungo giezhi ene soyuji shiqin jiere suibiende injine.
ROM 8:38 Bi hende xianxin giese bugon fuguku, amituku, qienxien, qienli bareichen, edeku shiqin, jianlaiku shiqin, lilian,
ROM 8:39 unduni, gunni, psedu zhayaghasanla man Huda mai ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi matande orekui siragha dane.
ROM 9:1 Bi Mexihani miende shuhuai kieliene, ghudan ulie kieliene. Mii lianxin Shenlinyi tungo giezhi made ganzhen beizho.
ROM 9:2 Bi hende munan giezhi zhughedemi izhi otuzho.
ROM 9:3 Bi gaijiuladene oluzhi mii kharazhi Mexihare danlinraghaseye duran wine. Hhelashi mare nie minzu wo,
ROM 9:4 yeshi Isilie kun wo. Kewonni nexian, fama, yenjisan kielien, guijin, libai gieku banfa, dain giesei man hhelade ogizho.
ROM 9:5 Hhe famatu xienrenlashi hhelanughun wo. Mexihaye kunni fanmiende kieliese hhelase khizhezho. Mexihashi manlai gonjisan Huda wo, chanqi doulakui wo. Amine!
ROM 9:6 Ingieseye bi Hudai kielienshi belienni wo giezhi ese kieliezho. Isiliese olusanlashi man Isilie kun pusho.
ROM 9:7 Iburaheimuni houdeilashi man hhei kewosi pusho. Zinie Isagheise olusei chii houdei giezhi urune giezho.
ROM 9:8 Isishi beyese olusan kesilashi man Hudai kewosi pusho. Zinie dain giesan mutun olusan kesilai houdeide sanane.
ROM 9:9 Eneshi Huda dain giesan kielien wo, "Gonien eli kuse bi irene. Sare nie kewon olune."
ROM 9:10 Zinie ene pusho. Mai xienren Isagheise Libaijia shongo laikudeye qingiezho.
ROM 9:11 Shongoni ese oluzhi gounii, doghunnii ese khizhekude Huda Libaijiade, "Jianlai fugieni ganinughunyi chenliene." giezhi kieliewo. Ingiezhi Huda kunni sunghuse goya mujighalane giezho. Kun giekughala ese giezho, kunni uruzhi iresan Huda jiejin giezho.
ROM 9:13 Jinwun jiere Huda kieliesan mutun, "Yagebude bi orezho, Isaode ese orezho."
ROM 9:14 Ingiese matan matui kieliene? Huda gundan uwonu? Kenjin pusho.
ROM 9:15 Huda Musade kieliewo, "Bi kiende ubali xiise kiende ubali xiine. Kiende nenjien ogise kiende nenjien ogine."
ROM 9:16 Ingie uzhese eneshi kunni duran, xiacha giekui kouisan pusho. Ubali xiisan Hudade kouizho.
ROM 9:17 Jinwun jiere Huda Falaode kieliezho, "Bi chii tungo giezhi nenline xienjighazhi qienxiade nierene chonji kurughane giezhi chii undudaghawo."
ROM 9:18 Ingie uzhese Huda kiende ubali xiise kiende ubali xiine. Kienyi khiduzheghase kienyi khiduzheghane.
ROM 9:19 Ingiese chi made kieliene, "Qinse Huda kunlade yangiezhi gui teine? Kien hhei isii fandui giene?"
ROM 9:20 Chishi kien wo? Zinie kun wo. Hudaghala jianjindunu? Gholusan dunxi matugie hhei gholughasande, "Chi mii yangiezhi intui giewo?" giezhi kieliene?
ROM 9:21 Ighachi shuwa dundase niegieda shuwai agidene niei guizhuntu, niei bixintu ighai gieku qienli uwonu?
ROM 9:22 Hudaye niekielien wo. Hhe hokukune, nenline mejieghaku duran woma, hokuzhi widaghane giesan kunlade hende rennai giewo.
ROM 9:23 Ingiedene Huda ubali xiisan kunlade hhei fama olon bikui mejieghazho. Enelashi famai ogine giezhi melie zhunbei giesan kunla wo,
ROM 9:24 yeshijiu Huda uruzhi iresan matan wo. Gon Yutai kun pusho, niman kunlaye enbene.
ROM 9:25 Zhen Huda Hexiyani Shu jiere kieliesan mutun, "Mii bexin pushotu kunlai bi mii bexin giezhi urune. Uye oresanlade bi oresan giezhi urune."
ROM 9:26 Pse kieliezho, "Ta mii bexin pusho giesan yen hhe oronde hhelai chanqiku Hudai kesila giezhi urune."
ROM 9:27 Isilie kunlai kieliese Isaiya fugiede kieliezho, "Isilie kunla olonde haibienni shazi niekielien woma, zinie feiliesanlai jiuine.
ROM 9:28 Ezhan zemin jiere panjikune ghujighande man gie baraghane."
ROM 9:29 Isaiya melieshi kieliezhi daosan mutun, "Qienwon buduini Ezhan matande houdei ese feilieghazhoshi matan zaojiu Sodoma, Emola gholuwo."
ROM 9:30 Ingiese matan matui kieliene? Hudare goudakui onxian ese giesan niman kunla xianxin giekughala Hudare goudawo.
ROM 9:31 Guijinghala Hudare goudane giesan Isilie kunla khareidene guijinni mujide dai dazho.
ROM 9:32 Eneshi yan yenyin wo? Eneshi hhela giekudene kouizho, xianxin giekude ese kouizho. Hhela banjighaku tashi jiere banjiwo.
ROM 9:33 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Bi Xiwunde nie banjighaku tashi teiwo. Kunni banjighaku tashi wo. Hhei xianxin giesan kunla jiuren ulie giene."
ROM 10:1 Gaijiula, bi zhughedene panjizhi Hudase onxian giesanshi Isilie kunlai jiuise giezho.
ROM 10:2 Hhela Hudade rexin bikui bi ganzhen beizhoma, zhao unhuaghala ese giezho.
ROM 10:3 Hudai gundanni ulie mejiene. Goya gundanine gholughane giezhi Hudai gundanni ulie shunjine.
ROM 10:4 Mexihashi guijinni uzhu wo. Jien xianxin giesan kunlai gounide sanane.
ROM 10:5 Guijinghala gounide sanakui ene shiqinyi giesan kunla amiturane giezhi Musa huaizhoma,
ROM 10:6 xianxin giekughala gounide sanaku daolii ingiezhi kieliezho, "Kien asiman jiere khireine giezhi chi zhughedene bu kielie." (Jiushi Mexihani jierese lai bouzheghane giezho.)
ROM 10:7 Pse "Kien dozoheide boune giezhi chi zhughedene bu kielie." (Jiushi Mexihani fugusan kun dundase lai khizheghane giezho.)
ROM 10:8 Hhe kieliesanshi ene wo, "Hudai kielien chase gholo uwo. Chii amande, zhughede wo." Jiushi bijien chonjisan xianxin gieku daoli wo.
ROM 10:9 Chi amandene Ersashi Ezhan wo giezhi chenren giezhi zhughedene Huda hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasei xianxin giese jiuine.
ROM 10:10 Kun zhughedene xianxin giese gounide sanane, amandene chenren giese jiuine.
ROM 10:11 Jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Jien hhei xianxin giesan kunla jiuren ulie giene."
ROM 10:12 Yutai kun, Xila kun yama chabie uwo. Soyuji kunlade niekozi Ezhan wo, hhei xiahua giesan soyuji kunlade dafande ogine.
ROM 10:13 "Jien Ezhanni nierei xiahua giesan kunlai jiuine."
ROM 10:14 Qinse kun hhei xianxin ulie giese matugie xiahua giene? Hhei chenliezhi ese daodene matugie xianxin giene? Kieme ulie chonjise matugie chenliene?
ROM 10:15 Kiemei ese peise matugie chonjine? Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Gouxioxii chonjisan kunlai koronlon zhengiejia seighan wo!"
ROM 10:16 Ingieliuzhe kunla man gouxioxini shunjisan pusho. Isaiya kieliezho, "Ezhan, bijien chonjisanyi kien xianxin giewo?"
ROM 10:17 Ingiese xianxin giekushi chenliesanse irezho. Chenliesanshi Mexihani kieliense irezho.
ROM 10:18 Bi nie asaye. Kunla ese chenliewu? Kenjin chenliezho. "Hhelai shenqi qienxiade kuruwo. Hhelai kielien duyani uzhude kuruwo."
ROM 10:19 Bi pse asaye. Isilie kun yama ulie mejienu? Mejiene! Xien Musa Hudai kielienyi ingiezhi kieliezho, "Bi minzude ulie sanaku minzuni tungo giezhi tai dubilieghane. Bi yama ulie mejiechen minzui tungo giezhi tai hokughane."
ROM 10:20 Pse Isaiya danzine fugiedaghazhi Hudai kielienyi ingiezhi kieliezho, "Mii ese ereisan kunlade bi chujiegheghane. Mii xiahua ese giesan kunlade bi xienjighane."
ROM 10:21 Isilie kunlade hhe kharei ingiezhi kieliezho, "Bi niudunie kielien ulie chenliezhi jianjinduku bexinlai jienliene giezhi khane rouizho."
ROM 11:1 Ingiese bi asaye, Huda goya bexinne bendawu? Kenjin uye! Bishiye Isilie kun, Iburaheimuni houdei, Bienyamin jiawuse khizhesan wo.
ROM 11:2 Huda melie mejiesan bexinlane ese bendazho. Jinwun jiere Iliyai matugie kieliesei ta ulie mejienu? Hhe Hudade Isilie kunlai zhazhi kieliezho,
ROM 11:3 "Ezhan, hhela chii xienzhilai alazhi sidagha gieku chii teizii cheiwo. Jianie bi feiliezhi hhela dou mii aminyi kerene."
ROM 11:4 Ingiese Huda matugie huida giewo? Bi goyadene oluzhi Balii ese beiisan 7000 kun feilieghawo giezho.
ROM 11:5 Edeku shihouye niekielien wo. Feiliesan kun wine. Hhelai nenjienghala sunghuzho.
ROM 11:6 Nenjienghala giese giekughala ese giezho. Qingiese nenjienshi nenjien pusho.
ROM 11:7 Ingiese matugie gholuwo? Isilie kunla goya ereisanne ereizhi olu dawo. Zinie Huda sunghusan kunla ereizhi oluwo. Psedu kunlai zhughe khiduzhewo.
ROM 11:8 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Huda hhelade sudoku zhughe ogizho nudunlani chanla dane, chighinlaiye sonosu dazhi eli kuwo."
ROM 11:9 Pse Dawude kieliewo, "Hhelai ijieku xini sa, on, banjighaku, bouin gieku gholusejiu.
ROM 11:10 Hhelai nudun borolozhi chujieghe dasejiu. Hhelai nurun ibeizi ghodeisejiu."
ROM 11:11 Ingiese bi asaye, hhela banjise bosizhe danu? Kenjin pusho! Hhela codadene jiuiku niman kunlade echise Isilie kunlai dubilieghazho.
ROM 11:12 Isilie kunlai codasan duyai kunlade haochu ireghazho, hhelai ese olusan niman kunlade gounii ireghazho. Qinse Isilie kunlai man jiuiku dunda oroghase ireku gounii genjia fugie uwonu?
ROM 11:13 Bi ta niman kunlade kielieye. Bishi niman kunlade peisan shitu wo. Ene wiliei bi fugiede uzhekushi
ROM 11:14 goya minzune dubilieghazhi ezighan jiuine giezho.
ROM 11:15 Huda hhelai bendadene duyai kunlare goudazho, hhelai jienliese zhengiejia gou uwonu? Fugusanse aminne olusan niekielien wo.
ROM 11:16 Hudade ogiku ghurun ganjinshi nieduizi ghurun man ganjin wo. Mutun genzi ganjinshi chalaye ganjin wo.
ROM 11:17 Bilase nie ganlan mutunyi giedun chalani ghigha bouzhedene yeganlan chalai chaiwo. Chishijiu chaisan chala wo. Chaisan chala mutun genzise gounii hhantu xiikude
ROM 11:18 ghighasan chalade kuai dane. Kuaine giese chi jila. Chi genzii ese qiezhezho, genzi chii qiezhezho.
ROM 11:19 Ingiese chi kieliene, 'Hhezighan chalai ghigha bouzhekushi mii chaine giezho.'
ROM 11:20 Oluzho! Hhela xianxin ulie giese ghigha bouzhezho, chi xianxin giese beizho. Ingiese ayizhi goyane undude bu uzhe.
ROM 11:21 Huda yenlaiku chalai sheise chiiye sheine.
ROM 11:22 Ingie uzhese Huda renyi, yenge wo. Hhezighan xinyan jiere banjisan kunlade yenge wo, tande renyi wo. Chi renyideni chanqi kouise beizhoma, pse chiiye ghigha widaghane.
ROM 11:23 Isilie kunla ulie guidene xianxin giese yen chaine. Hudade erchan chaiku nenli wine.
ROM 11:24 Chishi goya osisan ganlan mutun jierese ghighazhi bouzhedene zeilasan ganlan mutun jiere zhenchan wide chaisan wo. Qinse yenlaiku chalai yenlaiku mutun jiere chaise genjia zhenchan uwonu?
ROM 11:25 Gaijiula, bi ene mimii tande mejieghaku duran wo. Pse ta goyalane jienzha wo giene. Ene mimishi niman kunlai jiuiku shuzi kurutula niezhan Isilie kunlai zhughei khiduzheghazho.
ROM 11:26 Ingiedene Isilie kunlai man jiuine. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Xiwunse jiuichen khizhezhi Yagebuse xienlian wituni widaghane.
ROM 11:27 Hhe shihoude bi hhelai zuini widaghane. Eneshijiu bi hhelare yenjisan kielien wo."
ROM 11:28 Gouxioxighala kieliese Isilie kunla Hudare duitou gholudene tande haochu ireghawo. Hhelai xienrenni sunghusei uzhese hhelashi Huda oresan wo.
ROM 11:29 Hudai nenjien, uruku ulie bienjine.
ROM 11:30 Ta eqighandei Hudai ulie shunjiku mutun ede hhelai ulie shunjiku yenyinghala tande kharei ubali xiizho.
ROM 11:31 Niekielien wo. Hhela ede uye shunjizhoma, tande ubali xiisan yenyinghala ede hheladeye ubali xiine.
ROM 11:32 Huda soyuji kunlai ulie shunjiku dunda oroghazhi khakushi soyuji kunlade ubali xiine giezho.
ROM 11:33 Hudai bayan, agheli, erlin matui fugie wo! Hhe panjikui kiema mejie dane! Hhe giekui kiema dunjire dane!
ROM 11:34 "Kien Ezhanyi zhughei mejiene? Kien hhende sughachen danlane?"
ROM 11:35 "Kien Hudade xien ogidene khareizhi goyadene honjighane?"
ROM 11:36 Soyujila man hhense khizhezhi hhende kouizhi hhende oluzho. Kuaikui chanqi hhende ogi! Amine!
ROM 12:1 Ingiese gaijiula, bi Hudai ubali xiikughala tai goude fenfulaye. Ta beyene amitu mure danlaghazhi Hudade ogi. Intu mureshi Huda xiqi biku wo, zhiguitu wo. Eneshijiu zhenzhenji beiiku wo.
ROM 12:2 Ene duyani bu dagha. Sumulakune arunzhazhi shinishighadene Hudai gou, bayasuku, onqien isii shiizhi mejie.
ROM 12:3 Bi made ogisan nenjienghala ta jien kunlade kielieye, goyane texien undude bu uzhe. Goude sumulazhi Huda tande ghughazhi ogisan xianxin gieku fenlianghala goyane heshide uzhe.
ROM 12:4 Matanyi nie beye jiere iyanzi olon biliuzhe zoin buxian mutun
ROM 12:5 matanye olon woma, Mexihai miende nie beye wo. Nienieji beyede lienjizhi buxiantu iyanzi gholuwo.
ROM 12:6 Huda nenjienghalane matande buxiantu nenli ogizho. Hudai kielienyi kieliekushi xianxin gieku kamaghala kielie.
ROM 12:7 Ushilakushi ushila, surughakushi surugha.
ROM 12:8 Zhichi giezhi kieliechenla zhichi gie. Ogichenla dafande ogi. Gonjichenla xiacha giezhi gonji. Ubali xiichenla bayasuzhi gie.
ROM 12:9 Orekude jianii bu deila. Doghunnii henji, gounii barei.
ROM 12:10 Zhenzhenji orekughala nieniedene ore. Ranjizhi nieniene zunji.
ROM 12:11 Langan bu giedene zhughesene rexinde Ezhanni shunji.
ROM 12:12 Panjizhi bayasu, kunnan dunda rennai gie, izhi onxian gie.
ROM 12:13 Nanxintu shentulade ogi. Bayasuzhi kunlai jienlie.
ROM 12:14 Tai heisanlade oluzhi gouni kielie, bu kharadene gouni kielie.
ROM 12:15 Bayasuchen kunlare hhantu bayasu, wilachen kunlare hhantu wila.
ROM 12:16 Nieniedene heqitughan, goyane undude bu uzhezhi bixin kunlare laiwon gie. Goyane jienzha wo bu gie.
ROM 12:17 Kiemade doghunnide doghunnii bouchou bu gie, dajiala gou wo giesan shiqinni jinlianji gie.
ROM 12:18 Tande nengou bise jinlianji jien kunlare heqitu.
ROM 12:19 Mii orentula, goyane bouchou bu giedene Ezhan hhelai faikui saghei. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Ezhan kieliezho, 'Bouchoushi bi giekui wo, bi kharulune.'"
ROM 12:20 Khareidene chii duitou oliesuse ijiegha. Undasuse ochigha. Chi ingiezhi giese shitan khanni hhei qiorun jiere teizho.
ROM 12:21 Goyasene doghunnii bu injigha, gounighala doghunnise inji.
ROM 13:1 Jien kunla qienli bareisan noyenlai shunji. Qienlishi man Hudase irezho. Soyuji qienli bareichenlashi Huda jinjisan wo.
ROM 13:2 Ingiese qienli bareichenlai fandui giese Huda jinjisanyi fandui giezho. Fandui giesanla goyadene faikui ereizho.
ROM 13:3 Noyenlashi gouni giesanlai ayighachen pusho, doghunni giesanlai ayighachen wo. Chi qienli bareichenlase ulie ayine giezhou? Gouni giema, hhela chii kuaine.
ROM 13:4 Hhelashi tai haochude olusan Hudai hoji wo. Chi doghunni giese indan ayikui wo. Hhela khudoghoi belien bareisan pusho. Hhelashi doghunni giesan kunlai faichen Hudai hoji wo.
ROM 13:5 Ingiese ta bixi shunji, zinie Hudai hokuruku yenyinghala pusho, lianxinni yenyinghala wo.
ROM 13:6 Ta shui ogikuyeshi ene yenyin wo. Hhelashi zhomen ene shiqinyi gonjisan Hudai hoji wo.
ROM 13:7 Jien kunlade indan ogikui ogi. Shui ghurasande shui ogi, baer ghurasande baer ogi. Indan zunjichenlai zunji, danren giekulai danren gie.
ROM 13:8 Nieniedene orekuse chugo kiemade zhan bu chai. Kunlade orechenla guijinni chenjighawo.
ROM 13:9 Piofen bu gie, kun bu ala, bu ghula, tanxin bu gie giesan minlin, psedu guijinla man goyadene mutun giebeidene ore giesan ene minlinde bouizho.
ROM 13:10 Orechen kun giebeidene doghunni ulie giene. Ingiese oreku guijinni chenjighawo.
ROM 13:11 Ingiekushi edeshi yan shihou bikui ta mejiene. Ta hhunturazhi xiereiku shihou wo. Matanyi jiuiku matan dei xianxin gieku shihouse ede chadashizho.
ROM 13:12 Xieni daozhi ogheine giezho. Ingiese matan kharanide giesan shiqinlai jiedene gieghantu baohu gieku majiani musiye.
ROM 13:13 Matan udude gieku mutun yan gieliuzhe donzhende gieye. Lon naduzhi sudoku, lon kijiezhi hu gieku, jianjinduzhi dubilieku enelai bu gieye.
ROM 13:14 Khareidene Ezhan Ersa Mexihai musi. Zui gieku durande jihui bu ogizhi nefuxinni bu dagha.
ROM 14:1 Xianxin gieku zholientu kunlai ta jienlie. Ijien buxianshi bu jianjindu.
ROM 14:2 Niezhan kunla yanniliuzhe ijiese olune giezhi xianxin giezho. Xianxin gieku zholientu kunla zinie cai ijiene.
ROM 14:3 Migha ijiesan kunla migha ese ijiesan kunlai meilade bu uzhe, migha ese ijiesan kunla migha ijiesan kunlai bu kielie. Huda hhelai jienliewo.
ROM 14:4 Kunlai hojii kieliezhi chishi kien wo? Hhela olu, ulie olu ezhanyini shiqin wo. Ezhande olughaku nengou wine. Ingiese hhe olu shidane.
ROM 14:5 Niezhan kunla enenie udui psedu udulase zhunyo wo giezho. Niezhan kunla niuduniei uzhedan niekielien wo giezho. Alinie kunliuzhe zhughedene oluzhou ese olusei jiejin gie gie.
ROM 14:6 Udu jilasan kunla Ezhande oluzhi udu jilazho. Ijiesan kunla Hudade mafan giedene Ezhande oluzhi ijiezho. Ese ijiesan kunlaye Hudade mafan kieliedene Ezhande oluzhi ese ijiezho.
ROM 14:7 Matan alinie kunliuzhe goyadene oluzhi ese amiturazho. Goyadene oluzhiye ulie fugune.
ROM 14:8 Matan amitushi Ezhande oluzhi amiturazho. Fuguseye Ezhande oluzhi fugune. Ingiese matan amitura, fuguliuzhe Ezhannughun wo.
ROM 14:9 Mexiha fugusan kun, amitu kunde Ezhan danlane giezhi duya ijiedene aminne oluwo.
ROM 14:10 Matan man Hudai shenpantai melie beine. Chi yale gaijiune kieliene? Chi yale gaijiune meilade uzhene?
ROM 14:11 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Ezhan kieliewo, 'Bi goyane aminghala fayen gieye. Soyuji odoula made xiutuliene. Soyuji amanla bishi Huda wo giezhi chenren giene.'"
ROM 14:12 Ingiese matan alinie kunliuzhe Hudai melie goyane shiqinyi jiodai giene.
ROM 14:13 Ingiese matan nieniene bu kielieye. Jiexin xiaizhi gaijiulai melie boujia, banjighaku dunxii bu tei.
ROM 14:14 Bi Ezhan Ersai xianxin giezhi kenjin mejiene. Yandeliuzhe benshen ganjin wituni uwo. Zinie kun ganjin uwo giese hhende ganjin uwo.
ROM 14:15 Chi ijiunighala gaijiulane munan gieghase oreku daolighala ese giezho. Mexiha hhende oluzhi duya ijiewo, chi goyane ijiunighala hhei baxi bu olugha.
ROM 14:16 Ingiese ta goya gounine kunlai bu sugiegha.
ROM 14:17 Hudai gojiashi ijieku, ochiku pusho, Shenlin ogisan gundan, heqi, bayasuku wo.
ROM 14:18 Mexihani ingiezhi shunjisan kunde Huda bayasune, kunlaye kuaine.
ROM 14:19 Ingiese matan heqituzhi nieniene hendaghakui xiacha gieye.
ROM 14:20 Ijiunighala Hudai wiliei bu qida olugha. Manshi ganjinni woma, chi ijiedene kunlai zui fanjighase ese oluzho.
ROM 14:21 Migha ijie, jiu ochi, pse yan shiqindeliuzhe gaijiulani zui fanjighakui ulie giese gou wo.
ROM 14:22 Chi xianxin giesanne Hudai melie goude barei. Kun goyane gou wo giesan shiqinyi giedene gui ulie teise fuqi wine.
ROM 14:23 Inxin giezhi ijiese zui jinjine. Xianxin giekughala ese ijiezho. Xianxin giekughala giesanni pushoshi man zui wo.
ROM 15:1 Matan khidun kunla indan goyane bu bayasughazhi khidun witu kunlai zholiennii danjikuni wo.
ROM 15:2 Matan alinie kunliuzhe kunlai haochude oluzhi bayasughazhi hhelai hendaghakuni wo.
ROM 15:3 Mexihaye goyane ese bayasughazho. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Chii sugiesan kunlai sugieku man mii jiere irewo."
ROM 15:4 Eqighandei huaisan jinwunshi man matande oluzhi sughazhi huaisan wo. Hhe matai rennai gieghazhi sughazhi kieliedene matande xiwon ogizho.
ROM 15:5 Bi onxian giese rennai gieghazhi sughazhi kieliesan Huda tai sumuladanyi Mexiha Ersai daghazhi nie gholughadene
ROM 15:6 dajiala man hhantu mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani Ada Hudai kuai!
ROM 15:7 Ingiese Mexiha tai jienlieku mutun taye nieniene jienliezhi Hudai kuai.
ROM 15:8 Bi kieliese Mexiha Hudai zhendaode oluzhi Yutai kunlade hoji danlazhi xienrenlade dain giesei chenjighawo,
ROM 15:9 pse niman kunlai Huda hhelade ubali xiisande kuaighazho. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Ingiese bi niman kunlai dunda chii chenren giene. Bi donghala chii nierei doulane."
ROM 15:10 Pse kieliezho, "Niman kunla, ta Ezhanyi bexinlare hhantu bayasundu."
ROM 15:11 Pse, "Soyuji niman kunla, ta Ezhande doulandu. Soyuji minzula, hhende doulandu!"
ROM 15:12 Pse Isaiya kieliezho, "Jianlai Yexini houdei irene. Hhe khizhedene niman kunlai gonjine. Niman kunla hhei xiwon giene."
ROM 15:13 Xiwon ogisan Huda ta xianxin giekude yanyanji bayasukui, pinnanni tai zhughede durughazhi Shenlinni nenlighala xiwon olon ogi gie!
ROM 15:14 Mii gaijiula, tande gouni, yanyanji agheli duruzhi ta nieniedene surugha shidakui bi kenjin mejiene.
ROM 15:15 Ingieliuzhe bi niezhan shiqin jiere tai sumula ireghane giezhi danzine fugiedaghazhi tande xin huaikushi Huda made ogisan nenjienghala
ROM 15:16 bi niman kunlade oluzhi Mexiha Ersade wiliechi danlazho. Bi hhelade Hudai gouxioxii chonjise buwa niekielien wo. Shenlinyi tungo giezhi hhelai zhiguishighadene jienlieku mure mutun Hudade ogizho.
ROM 15:17 Ingiese Mexiha Ersai miende bi Hudade oluzhi giesan shiqinde kuaikui wine.
ROM 15:18 Niman kunlai shunjighane giezhi Mexiha mii tungo giezhi giesan wiliese chugo bi psedulai yama ulie kieliene. Hheshi kielienji, giekughala giesan wo.
ROM 15:19 Ghudureqi, fugie shiqinyi nenlighala, pse Hudai Ruhheryi nenlighala giesan wo. Bi Mexihai gouxioxii Yelusalense izhi Ililigude man chonji kurughawo.
ROM 15:20 Ingiezhi bi Mexihani nierei chenliezhi ese daosan oronlade chonjine giezhi hende duralakushi kunlai jigun jiere gie ulie beighane giezho.
ROM 15:21 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Hhei xioxii mejie dasanla chanlane. Chenliezhi ese daosanla dunjirene."
ROM 15:22 Ene yenyin jiere bi tai hhende haojihui echine giezhoma, echi dazho.
ROM 15:23 Ede ene oronlade chonjiku oron widazho, pse haojinien bi tai hhende echiku duralazho.
ROM 15:24 Ingiese bi Xibenyade echikude tai ochira, xien nietan laiwon giezhi xianshou giedene ta mii khughose giezhi xiwon giezho.
ROM 15:25 Ingiezhoma, ede bi Yelusalende echizhi shentulade banman giene giezho.
ROM 15:26 Maqidun, Yagaiyani kunla Yelusalenni nanxintu shentulade banman giene giezhi bayasuzhi baer khireighawo.
ROM 15:27 Hhela enei bayasuzhi giekushi shuhuajia shentulade chaizho. Niman kunla hhelase ruhher jieredu haochui ghughazhi echise hhela injikude banman giese indanji wo.
ROM 15:28 Ingiese bi kunla khireighasanni goude jiuizhi ogi ene shiqinyi onchen giedene tai hhense jingo giezhi Xibenyade echine.
ROM 15:29 Bi tai hhende irekude Mexihani olon nenjienni deilazhi irekui bi mejiene.
ROM 15:30 Gaijiula, bi matanyi Ezhan Ersa Mexiha, Shenlinni orekughala tande goude fenfulaye. Ta mare hhantu xiacha giezhi made oluzhi Hudase ingiezhi onxian gie,
ROM 15:31 "Mii Yudaya oronni xianxin ulie giechen kunlai khade bu oroghazhi bi Yelusalende banman giesan shiqinde shentulai bayasuzhi jienliegha gie.
ROM 15:32 Pse mii Hudai isighala tai hhende bayasuzhi iregha tanre hhantu hhamuragha gie."
ROM 15:33 Pinnan ogisan Huda ta dajialare hhantu bi gie. Amine!
ROM 16:1 Bi Jiengelini jiohuide gonjia danlasan mai eghechijiu Feibini tande jieshao gieye.
ROM 16:2 Ta Ezhanni miende hhei shentula indan gieku mutun heshide jienlie. Hhe yan shiqinde banman kerese banman gie. Hhe olon kunlade banman giezho, madeye banman giezho.
ROM 16:3 Baijila, Yajilade kielien asa. Hhela Mexiha Ersai miende mare hhantu wilie giezho.
ROM 16:4 Mii aminde oluzhi goya aminne ese kerewo. Zinie bi hhelade mafan kielieku pusho, niman kunlai jiohuila man hhelade mafan kieliezho.
ROM 16:5 Pse hhelai gieni jiohuii kunlade kielien asa. Bi oresan Ibainitude kielien asa. Hheshi Yaxiya oronyi ji 1 gie Mexihai xianxin giesan kun wo.
ROM 16:6 Mereiyende kielien asa. Hhe tande oluzhi hende khishulazho.
ROM 16:7 Mare hhantu bafanzi sousan mii qingu Andonigu, Yuniyade kielien asa. Hhela shitulai dunda minshen fugie wo, mase melie Mexihai xianxin giezho.
ROM 16:8 Ezhanyi miende bi oresan Anbolide kielien asa.
ROM 16:9 Mexihai miende matanre hhantu wilie giesan Erbanu, pse bi oresan Shidagude kielien asa.
ROM 16:10 Mexihai miende olune giesan Yabilide kielien asa. Yalidobui giei kunlade kielien asa.
