ROM 16:11 Mii qingu Xiloqiende kielien asa. Naqishu giei Ezhanyi miendedu kunlade kielien asa.
ROM 16:12 Ezhanyi miende khishulasan TufeinaTufusa ghualade kielien asa. Ezhanyi miende hende khishulasan oresan Bixide kielien asa.
ROM 16:13 Ezhanyi miende sunghusan Lufu, hhei anadeni kielien asa. Hhei ana made ana danlazho.
ROM 16:14 Yaxinqitu, Fulegan, Xiermi, Baloba, Heima, pse hhelare hhantuku gaijiulade kielien asa.
ROM 16:15 Feilologu, Yuliyaghala, Niliya, hhei eghechijiughala, Alinba, pse hhelare hhantuku shentulade man kielien asa.
ROM 16:16 Ta zhughesene nieniedene kielien asa. Mexihani jiohuila man tande kielien asazho.
ROM 16:17 Gaijiula, bi tai xiahua gieye, ta surusan daolini fandui giezhi tai khudoghozhi banjighachen hhezighan kunlase gholodo.
ROM 16:18 Imutu kunla mai Ezhan Mexihai ulie shunjizhi zinie goya shiqinne guizhi kuaiku seighan kielienghala loushi kunlai miine.
ROM 16:19 Tai shunjisan shiqinla gochude chonji kuruzho. Ingiese bi tande oluzhi bayasuzho. Mii duranshi ta gou shiqin jiere jienzhaghan, doghun shiqin jiere menghan.
ROM 16:20 Pinnan ogisan Huda Ibilisii kon douratai taizhi ireghaku ghujinlazho. Matanyi Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjien tanre hhantu bi gie!
ROM 16:21 Mare hhantu wilie giesan Qimotai, mii qingu Luqiu, Yaso, Soxibade enela tande kielien asazho.
ROM 16:22 Made xin deilazhi huaisan Deqi Ezhanyi miende tande kielien asazho.
ROM 16:23 Mii jienliezhi jiohuini kunlai man jienliesan Gaiyu tande kielien asazho. Chenshii baer gonjisan Iladu, mai gaijiu Kotughala tande kielien asazho.
ROM 16:25 Hudade kuaikui ogi. Bi chonjisan Ersa Mexihai gouxioxighala, eqighanku gonyinni niuighasan mimii mejieghakughala Huda tai khiduzhegha shidane.
ROM 16:26 Ene mimi ede xienjizhi khizhezho. Chanqiku Hudai minlin mutun xienzhilai shuni tungo giezhi soyuji minzulade mejieghadene hhelai xianxin gieghazhi shunjighawo.
ROM 16:27 Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi zi niekozi aghelitu Hudade chanqi kuaikui ogi. Amine!
1CO 1:1 Hudai isighala urudene Ersa Mexihade shitu danlasan BaoloSoqini gaijiughala
1CO 1:2 Gelindoni Hudai jiohuide xin huaizho. Tai Mexiha Ersai miende zhiguishighazho, gochude mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai nierei xiahua giesan kunlare hhantu man shentu giezhi uruzho. Mexihashi hhelai Ezhan wo, mai Ezhanye enbene.
1CO 1:3 Mai Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
1CO 1:4 Huda Mexiha Ersai miende tande nenjien ogise bi tande oluzhi bi zunjisan Hudade chan mafan kieliezho.
1CO 1:5 Ta hhei sudoro kielien kielieku, erlin, yanyanjilai jiere man hendazho.
1CO 1:6 Ingiezhi Mexihade beisan ganzhen tai dunda khiduzhezho.
1CO 1:7 Ta nenjien jiere yama ese chaizhi mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha xienjikui sagheizho.
1CO 1:8 Huda tai zuihou kutula khiduzheghazhi mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani udude ulie kheilaghane.
1CO 1:9 Hudashi kekaoni wo, hhe tai uruzhi goya kewonre, yeshijiu mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihare laiwon gieghazho.
1CO 1:10 Gaijiula, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani niereghala bi tai goude fenfulaye, ta man xianlitu kielien kielie. Tai dunda maodun bu khizhezhi nie zhughe nie sumuladanghala goude heqishi.
1CO 1:11 Mii gaijiula, tai dunda maodun wine giezhi Gelaini giededu kunla made kieliezho.
1CO 1:12 Mii isishi ta jien kunla, "Bishi Baolonughun wo," "Bishi Yabolonughun wo," "Bishi Jifanughun wo," "Bishi Mexihanughun wo." giezhi kieliezho.
1CO 1:13 Mexihashi fenkai giesanni onu? Baolo tande oluzhi shizijia jiere fuguwu? Ta Baoloni niereghala xili jienliewu?
1CO 1:14 Bi Jilisibu, Gaiyughalase chugo pse tai dunda kiemade xili ese gieghasande Hudade mafan kieliezho.
1CO 1:15 Pse ta mii niereghala xili jienliewo giezhi kunla kieliene.
1CO 1:16 Bi Siqifanai gieni kunladeye xili gieghazhi daozho, psedu kunlade xili gieghazhi daozhoyeshi bi matazho.
1CO 1:17 Mexiha mii peikushi xili gieghaku pusho, gouxioxii chonjighaku wo. Bi aghelitu kielienghala ese chonjizho, pse Mexihani shizijiai zoin widane.
1CO 1:18 Shizijiani daoli hhezighan widachen kunladeshi ben wo, matan enezighan ji0 uisan kunladeshi Hudai nenli wo.
1CO 1:19 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Bi aghelitu kunlai aghelini widaghane, jienzhatu kunlai jienzhani bendane."
1CO 1:20 Aghelitu kun khala wo? Hanjia khala wo? Ene duyani erlintu kun khala wo? Huda ene duyai aghelini benni ese gholughazhou?
1CO 1:21 Duya goya aghelighalane Hudai ese taniwo. Ingiese Huda kunla benni wo giesan bijien chonjisan daolighala xianxin giesan kunlai jiuine giezhi jiejin giewo. Eneshi Hudai agheli wo.
1CO 1:22 Yutai kun ghudureqi kerezho, Xila kun agheli ereizhoma,
1CO 1:23 bijien chonjisanshi shizijia jiere ghadasan Mexiha wo. Eneshi Yutai kunde banjiku tashi wo, niman kunde benni woma,
1CO 1:24 bugon Yutai kun niman kun, Huda urusan kunde Mexihashi Hudai nenli, Hudai agheli wo.
1CO 1:25 Hudai benni kunni aghelise fama wo. Hudai zholienni kunni khidunnise khidun wo.
1CO 1:26 Gaijiula, tai urusanni nie sumula. Kunni isighala kieliese tai dunda aghelitu, nenlitu, zhiguitu kun choghon wo.
1CO 1:27 Huda duya jieredu bennilai sunghuzhi aghelitulai shizheghazho. Huda duya jieredu zholiennilai sunghuzhi khidunnilai shizheghazho.
1CO 1:28 Huda duya jieredu kunla uzhezhi xiniesan, henjisan, yama witu kunlai sunghuzhi winetulai widaghazho.
1CO 1:29 Ingiese kun kiemada Hudai melie goyane kuai dane.
1CO 1:30 Ingiezhoma, Huda tai Mexiha Ersare hhantulaghazho. Hhe Hudase irezhi mai agheli, gundan, zhigui, shuiku gholuwo.
1CO 1:31 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Kien kuaise Ezhanyi kuai."
1CO 2:1 Gaijiula, eqighandei bi tai hhende echizhi Hudai mimii chonjikude seighan kielien, aghelighala ese giezho.
1CO 2:2 Bi tai dunda bikude zinie Ersa Mexiha, pse hhei shizijia jiere ghadasanse chugo psedulai ulie mejiene giezhi jiejin giewo.
1CO 2:3 Bi tai hhendeshi zholien, ayi, hende pugharazho.
1CO 2:4 Bi kieliezhi chonjikude seighan, aghelitu kielienghala ese giezhi Shenlinni nenlighala zhenmin giezho.
1CO 2:5 Ingiese tai xianxin gieku kunni aghelide ese kouizho, Hudai nenlide kouizho.
1CO 2:6 Ingiezhoma, xinyan jiere qiendasan kunlade bijien aghelini jianjizho. Eneshi duyai agheli pusho, duyai qienlini bareizhi widachen kunlai agheliye pusho.
1CO 2:7 Bijien jianjisanshi eqighandei niuighasan Hudai mimitu agheli wo. Eneshi Huda duyai zhayaghaku melie matande famai ogine giezhi jinjisan wo.
1CO 2:8 Ene aghelini duyani qienli bareichen kunla dunda mejiechen nieda uwo. Hhela mejiezhoshi famatu Ezhanyi shizijia jiere ulie ghadane.
1CO 2:9 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Hudade oresan kunlade Huda zhunbei giesanshi nudunghala uzhezhi ese daosan wo, chighinghala chenliezhi ese daosan wo, kunni zhugheye sumulazhi ese daosan wo."
1CO 2:10 Ingiezhoma, matande Huda Shenlinni tungo giezhi mejieghawo. Shenlin yanniliuzhe mejiene, lien Hudai chijia isiniye mejiene.
1CO 2:11 Kunni sudorodu ruhherse chugo kunni shiqinni kien mejiene? Niekielien wo, Hudai Ruhherse chugo Hudai shiqinni kiema mejie dane.
1CO 2:12 Matan jienliesanshi duya jieredu ruhher pusho, Hudase iresan ruhher wo, ingiese Huda matande ogisan nenjienlai matan mejiene.
1CO 2:13 Bijienye enelai jianjikude kunni agheli sughasan kielienghala ese giezho, Shenlin sughasanghala giezho. Ruhhertu shiqinlai ruhhertu kielienghala mejieghane.
1CO 2:14 Hudai Ruhher uwotu kunla Hudai ruhher ogisanlai jienlie dane. Hhela enei ben wo giezho, ye dunjire dane. Ene shiqinlai zinie ruhherghala uzhe khizhene.
1CO 2:15 Ruhhertu kunla yan shiqinniliuzhe uzhe khizhenema, kiema hhelai uzhezhi khizhe dane.
1CO 2:16 "Kien Ezhanyi zhughei mejiene? Kien hhende surughane?" Mai kieliese matande Mexihani zhughe wine.
1CO 3:1 Gaijiula, bi eqighandei tande kielien kieliekude tai ruhhernughun danlagha dazhi beyenughun danlaghazho. Mexihai miende tai yeliwa mutun uzhezho.
1CO 3:2 Bi tande budan ese qiezhezhi neizi qiezhekushi ta budanyi ijie dane, edeliuzhe ijie dane.
1CO 3:3 Tashi beyenughun wo. Tai sudoro dubilieku, jianjinduku wine. Eneshi beyenughun pushonu? Zhao duyani kunla giesan mutun ese giezhou?
1CO 3:4 Niezhan kunla kieliese bi Baoloni daghazho. Niezhan kunla kieliese bi Yaboloi daghazho giezho. Ingiezhi ta duyai kunlare niekielien pushonu?
1CO 3:5 Yaboloshi kien wo? Baoloshi kien wo? Manshi wiliechi wo, zhao Ezhan nieniede ogisan renwughala tai xianxin gieghasan wo.
1CO 3:6 Bi tareiwo, Yabolo usu teiwo, osighasanshi Huda wo.
1CO 3:7 Ingiese tareisan, usu kiesan yama pusho, zinie osighasan Huda hen wo.
1CO 3:8 Tareisan, usu kiesanghala niekielien wo, zhao nieniede wilie giesan mutun gunzi ogine.
1CO 3:9 Bijienshi hhantu wilie giesan Hudai wiliechi wo. Tashi Hudai ghazha, mechi wo.
1CO 3:10 Zhao Huda made ogisan nenjienghala bi nie hen guntou mutun jichui daizho, psedu kun jiereni gie giezhoma, jien kun matugie giekui xioxin gie.
1CO 3:11 Ene dai goudaghasan jichushi Ersa Mexiha wo, psedu jichui kiemada dai dane.
1CO 3:12 Ene jichu jiere kienliuzhe antan, miengu, boushi, mutun, osun, ghuyughala gie giese
1CO 3:13 panjiku udude jien kunla giesei xienjizhi khizheghane, khanghala khizheghane. Goya giesanla matugiezho giezhi ene khan shiine.
1CO 3:14 Gie giesan kun hhe jichu jiere giesan bei shidase hhende jianli ogine.
1CO 3:15 Giesanni sidera widase hhe kuiine. Hhei jiuinema, jiuiku hoxian khan dundase holu khizheku niekielien wo.
1CO 3:16 Tashi Hudai dajien bikui, pse Hudai ruhher tai sudoro sousanyi ta ulie mejienu?
1CO 3:17 Kien Hudai dajienyi qida olughase Huda hhe kunyi qida olughane. Hudai dajienshi zhiguitu wo, tashi ene dajien wo.
1CO 3:18 Kienliuzhe goyane bu pienda. Tai dunda kun goyane ene duyade agheli wine giezhi sumulase benni gholu. Ingiese aghelitu gholune.
1CO 3:19 Ene duyani aghelii Huda uzhese benni wo. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Ezhan aghelitu kunlai jienzhanii hhelai bareiku on gholughawo."
1CO 3:20 Pse huaizho, "Aghelitu kunlai sumulaku yama isi witui Ezhan mejiene."
1CO 3:21 Ingiese kienliuzhe kunni bu kuai, yanliuzhe manshi tanughun wo.
1CO 3:22 Baolo, Yabolo, Jifa, duya, amituku, fuguku, edeku shiqin, jianlaiku shiqin manshi tanughun wo.
1CO 3:23 Tashi Mexihanughun wo, Mexihashi Hudanughun wo.
1CO 4:1 Ingiese ta bijienyi Mexihani wiliechi, pse Hudai chijia daolini gonjia danlaghakui wo.
1CO 4:2 Gonjiade yoqiu giekushi shixinji giekui wo.
1CO 4:3 Ta mii kielie yehao kunla kielie yehao bi yamacha ulie teine. Bi goyane goya ulie kieliene.
1CO 4:4 Bi sumulase mii lianxinde yama ese chaizhoma, ingieliuzhe minughun man oluzho giezhi kielie dane. Mii kieliekushi Ezhan wo.
1CO 4:5 Ingiese shihou ese kuzhezhi Ezhan ese iretula ta kienyiliuzhe bu kielie. Hhe irese kharade niuighasanlai zhouizhi khizheghane, kunyi zhughei mujilai khizheghane. Hhe shihoude Huda jien kunlai kuaine.
1CO 4:6 Gaijiula, bi tande oluzhi ene shiqin jiere Yaboloji goyane bilazhi yanzi uzheghazho. Ingiekushi jinwun jiere jilasanse bu daogha giesan isii ta bijiense suru giezho, pse tai dunda kienliuzhe goyane bu kondazhi ene niei fugiede uzhe, hhe niei meilade uzhe bu gie giezho.
1CO 4:7 Kien chii kunlare niekielien pusho giezho? Chii alinieshi chade ogisan pusho? Ogisan enbese ogisan pusho giezhi yale goyane kuaine?
1CO 4:8 Ta ijin chuduzho, ijin bayazhewo. Bijiense chugo ta honshan danlawo. Mii xiwonshi ta zhenzhenji honshan danlama, bijienye tanre hhantu danlaye!
1CO 4:9 Bi sumulase Huda bijien shitu danlasanlai zhan eghisanse barei ire sixin panjisan kun mutun zui khuina teizhi kunlade uzheghasanyi xianli. Bijienyi xi mutun duyani kunlade, qienxienlade uzheghazho.
1CO 4:10 Bijien Mexihani yenyinghala benni gholuzho, ta Mexihai miende jienzhani gholuzho. Bijien zholien wo, ta khidun wo, kunla tai kuaizho, bijienyi meilade uzhezho.
1CO 4:11 Eli kuliuzhe bijien oliesuzhi undasuzho, hulan muchughun wo, kunlase neizhi souku oron uwo.
1CO 4:12 Khishulazhi goyane khaghala wilie giezho. Kunla kharase bijien gounii kieliezho, kunla heise rennai giezho.
1CO 4:13 Kunla bijienyi sugiese bijien gou kielienghala khareizhi kieliezho. Edeliuzhe bijien duya jieredu zannanni, yanyanjilai dundadu laji gholuzho.
1CO 4:14 Bi enei huaise tai shizheghane ese giezho, goya oresan kesilane mutun tande jingao giezho.
1CO 4:15 Mexihai miende tande loushi olon no woma, ada olon uwo. Bi gouxioxii chonjizhi Mexiha Ersai miende tande ada danlazho.
1CO 4:16 Ingiese bi tai goude fenfulaye, ta mii yanzii suru.
1CO 4:17 Ene yenyin jiere bi Qimotaini peizhi tai hhende echighawo. Hheshi Ezhanyi miende bi oresan shixinji kewon wo. Hhe tai qixin giezhi bi Mexiha Ersai sudoro matugie giesei, pse go oron, go jiohuilade matugie sughasei jilaghane.
1CO 4:18 Tai dunda niezhan kunla sumulase bi tai hhende ulie irene giezhi goyalane fugiede uzhezho.
1CO 4:19 Ingieliuzhe Ezhan duran bise bi tai hhende ghujighan echidene goyane fugiede uzhesanlai kielienni ulie uzhene, nenlii uzhene.
1CO 4:20 Hudai gojiashi kieliende uwo, nenlide wo.
1CO 4:21 Ta yan kerene? Bi banban bareizhi tai faile iremu, oreku, renyitu zhugheghala ire?
1CO 5:1 Bi chenliese shuhuajia tai dunda lon kijieku shiqin wine. Intu shiqin niman kunlai dundaliuzhe uwo. Nie kun goya khuitu anarene kijiezho.
1CO 5:2 Ta dou goyalane fugiede uzhene. Ta indan hende nango giekui wo. Ene shiqinni giesan kunni tai dundase tou khighakui wo!
1CO 5:3 Mii kun tanre hhantu uwoma, zhughemi tanre hhantu wo. Bi tai hhende bisan mutun intu shiqinyi giesan kunyi Ezhan Ersai niereghala ijin zui jinjiwo.
1CO 5:4 Ta hhantulazhi mii zhughe tanre hhantu bikude mai Ezhan Ersani qienlighala
1CO 5:5 intu kunni Ibiliside jiuizhi beyeni huailugha gie, ingiese ruhheryini Ezhanni udude jiuine.
1CO 5:6 Ta goyalane kuaise ese oluzho. Goujinie kunieghe nie duizi ghurunni man faighakui ta ulie mejienu?
1CO 5:7 Tashi tanmien woshi khuichen kunieghei widaghadene shini ghurun gholu. Matanyi Jiulidaosan Jieni ghoni ghughan yeshijiu Mexihai ijin zharuzhi sidagha giewo.
1CO 5:8 Ingiese matan jieqi daoghase doghun, mouxientu khuichen kuniegheghala bu daoghadene ganjin, shixintu tanmienghala daoghaye.
1CO 5:9 Bi eqighandei tande xin huaizhi ta lon kijiechen kunlare laiwon bu gie giezhi kieliewo.
1CO 5:10 Mii isishi ene duyadedu lon kijiechen, tanxin giechen, piendachen, nigiedai beiichen kunlare jiedui laiwon bu gie giekui pusho. Qingiese ta ene duyase likai giese da gou wo.
1CO 5:11 Ede bi ene xinni tande huaikushi goyaneshi xianxin giesan gaijiu wo giedene lon kijiesan, tanxin giesan, nigiedai beiisan, kun sugiesan, jiu ochisan, piendasan intui giesan kunlare ta laiwon bu giezhi budanye hhantu bu ijie giezho.
1CO 5:12 Ghadanedu kunyi bi kheilaku pushoma, sudorodu kunyi ta kheilaku pushonu?
1CO 5:13 Ghadanedu kunyi Huda panjine. "Ta dundasene mouxien kunlai tou khigha."
1CO 6:1 Tai dunda jianjinduku shiqin bidene matugie shentulade ese zhazhi gou witu kunlade zhale echizho?
1CO 6:2 Shentula duyai panjikui ta ulie mejienu? Ta duyai panjise ene ga shiqinlai panji danu?
1CO 6:3 Matan qienxienlai panjikui ta ulie mejienu? Ingiese duyai shiqinni yan sanane?
1CO 6:4 Ingiese jiohuide intu shiqin bise matugie jiohui zunzhun ese giesan kunlai panjighane?
1CO 6:5 Bi ingiezhi kieliekushi tai shizheghane giezho. Tai dunda gaijiulai shiqinyi chuli gieku aghelitu kun nieda uwonu?
1CO 6:6 Tai dunda gaijiula gaijiulai zhazhi dou xianxin ulie giechen kunlai melie zhale echiwo.
1CO 6:7 Ta nieniene zhase tanughun fugiede codazho. Ta yale bixinde ulie beizhi kui ulie ijiene?
1CO 6:8 Ta khareidene kunlai bixindaghazhi kuighazho, hhelashi goyai gaijiu wo.
1CO 6:9 Gou witu kunla Hudai gojiai jienlie dakui ta ulie mejienu? Goyane bu pienda, lon kijiechen, nigiedai beiichen, piofen giechen, ere kun biozi danlachen, tunxinlien giechen,
1CO 6:10 ghulachen, tanxin giechen, sudochen, kunni sugiechen, piendachen enela Hudai gojiani jienlie dane.
1CO 6:11 Tai dunda niezhan kunla eqighandei intui giezhi daozhoma, ede Ezhan Ersa Mexihani niere, pse mai Hudai ruhherni tungo giezhi tai ijin waghazho, zhiguishighazho, gounide sanazho.
1CO 6:12 Goyane yan shiqin gieliuzhe olune giezhi kunla kieliezhoma, man haochu bikui pusho. Bi yan shiqin gieliuzhe oluzhoma, alinie shiqinniliuzhe bi goyane kunzhi ulie gieghane.
1CO 6:13 Ijiuni kielide oluzho, kieli ijiunide oluzho giezhoma, Huda ene ghualai widaghane. Beyeshi lon kijiekude giesan pusho, Ezhande oluzhi giesan wo, Ezhan kunni beyede oluzho.
1CO 6:14 Huda Ezhanyi aminne olughazhi maiye goya nenlighalane aminne olughane.
1CO 6:15 Tai beyeshi Mexihani iyanzi bikui ta ulie mejienu? Bi Mexihani iyanzii biozini iyanzi gholughazhi olunu? Kenjin ulie olune!
1CO 6:16 Biozighala hhantulase hheghala nie beye gholukui ta ulie mejienu? Jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Ghuala nie beye gholune."
1CO 6:17 Ezhanghala hhantulasan kun Ezhanghala nie ruhher gholune.
1CO 6:18 Ta lon kijieku shiqinse pii. Kun yan zui fanjiliuzhe beye ghadane giezho, zinie lon kijiekushi goyai beye jiere giezho.
1CO 6:19 Tai beyeshi Huda tande ogisan Shenlin tai sudoro souku dajien bikui ta ulie mejienu? Tashi goyanughun pusho,
1CO 6:20 fugie jiageghala agizhi iresan wo. Ingiese ta beyeghalane Hudai kuai.
1CO 7:1 Xin jiere ta qiisan shiqinni kielieye. Ere kun eme kunni ulie shighase gou wo giezhoma,
1CO 7:2 lon kijieku shiqinlase ayizhi ere kunde bierei bise gou wo, eme kunde zhanguiji bise gou wo.
1CO 7:3 Zhanguiji biereidene zhanguiji danlaku zherenyi feii, biereiye zhanguijidene ingiezhi gie.
1CO 7:4 Bierei goya beyene gonjiku qienli uwo, qienli zhanguijide wo. Zhanguijiye goya beyene gonjiku qienli uwo, qienli biereide wo.
1CO 7:5 Ghuala nieniene bu kuigha. Zinie zhomen onxian giene giese ghuala tunyi bise zhanshi jiere danlin kijiese olune. Khuinashi ghuala hhantula, pse ta goyane kunzhi gie dakude Ibilisi miine.
1CO 7:6 Bi ingiezhi kieliese tande minlin ese xiaizho, ijien qilazho.
1CO 7:7 Mii xiwonshi kunla man bi mutun woshi giezhoma, jien kun Hudase jienliesan nenjien buxian wo. Niezhanla ingiezho, niezhanla qingiezho.
1CO 7:8 Jiehun ese giesan, pse guafulai kieliese hhela bi mutun jiehun ulie giese gou woma,
1CO 7:9 goyane kunzhi gie dase jiehun giekui wo. Zhughe tuliezhi bazilie datula jiehun giese gou wo.
1CO 7:10 Jiehun giesanlade bi fenfulaye. Eneshi bi fenfulasan pusho, Ezhan fenfulasan wo. Bierei zhanguijisene bu danxinra.
1CO 7:11 Danxinrase pse jiehun bu gie, yen zhanguijighalane gouda. Ere kunye biereine bu benda.
1CO 7:12 Psedu kunlade bi kielieye. Eneshi Ezhan kieliesan pusho, bi kieliesan wo. Xianxin giesan gaijiude xianxin ese giesan bierei bizhi hhe bierei hhere hhantu udu daoku duran bise hhei bu benda.
1CO 7:13 Biereide xianxin ese giesan zhanguiji bizhi hhe zhanguiji hhere hhantu udu daoku duran bise hhei bu benda.
1CO 7:14 Ese xianxin giesan zhanguiji biereini yenyinghala zhiguitu gholune. Ese xianxin giesan bierei zhanguijini yenyinghala zhiguitu gholune. Pse tai kesila ganjin uwoma, ede hhela zhiguitu wo.
1CO 7:15 Xianxin ese giesan kun danxinrane giese hhei danxinragha. Intu shiqinde xianxin giesan gaijiu eghechijiulade ziyu wine. Huda tai urukushi tai heqishighane giezho.
1CO 7:16 Bierei danlachen, chii tungo giezhi zhanguijiichii kenen jiui shidane. Zhanguiji danlachen, chii tungo giezhi biereinichii kenen jiui shidane.
1CO 7:17 Alinie kunliuzhe Ezhan nanpeilasan mutun, pse Huda hhei urusan mutun udu dao. Eneshi bi go jiohuilade jinjisan wo.
1CO 7:18 Niezhan kunlai hetoune giedene uruzhoshi jihaoni widaghaku biyo uwo. Niezhan kunlai hetoune ese giedene uruzhoshi hetoune gieku biyo uwo.
1CO 7:19 Hetoune gie, ulie gie zhunyo uwo. Zui zhunyonishi Hudai minlinyi goude zunji.
1CO 7:20 Jien kunyi urukude matui woshi qingiezhi bei.
1CO 7:21 Chii urukude chi hoji danlazhoshi munan bu gie. Ziyushiku jihui bise goude barei.
1CO 7:22 Hoji danlasei Ezhan uruse hheshi Ezhanni ziyutu kun wo. Ziyutu kunyi uruse hheshi Mexihani hoji wo.
1CO 7:23 Tashi fugie jiageghala agizhi iresan wo, kunde hoji bu danla.
1CO 7:24 Gaijiula, jien kunyi urukude matui woshi Hudai melie qingiezhi bei.
1CO 7:25 Jiehun ese giesan kunni kieliese made Ezhanni yama minlin uwoma, Ezhan made ubali xiizhi mii nie kekaotu kun gholughase bi ijienne kielieye.
1CO 7:26 Edeku kunnan mutunshi bi uzhese ta qinkonne ulie bienjighase gou wo.
1CO 7:27 Chade bierei bise hhense danxinrane bu gie. Chade bierei wise bierei agine bu gie.
1CO 7:28 Bierei agise zui ese fanjizho, oqin jiehun gieseye zui ese fanjizhoma, jiehun giesan kunla udu daokude ku shouine, bi tai intu ku shouighaku duran uwo.
1CO 7:29 Gaijiula, bi tande kielieye, shihou oloncha widawo. Enedu khuinashi bierei bichenla bierei wichen mutun giekui wo.
1CO 7:30 Wilachenla ese wilachen mutun gie. Bayasuchenla ese bayasuchen mutun gie. Dunxi agichenla yama uwoku mutun gie.
1CO 7:31 Duya jieredulai xianshou giesanla xianshou ese giesan mutun gie. Edeku duyai yanzi widane.
1CO 7:32 Mii duranshi ta yamade munan ulie giesejiu. Bierei ese agisanla Ezhanni shiqinde munan giezhi matugie Ezhanni bayasughakui sumulazho.
1CO 7:33 Bierei agisanla duya jieredu shiqinde munan giezhi matugie biereine bayasughakui sumulazhi
1CO 7:34 zhugheni nie jiere uwo. Guafu, oqinla Hudai shiqinde munan giezhi beye, ruhherlani man zhiguishighane giezho. Biereila duyani shiqinde munan giezhi zhanguijine matugie bayasughakui sumulazho.
1CO 7:35 Bi ene kielienyi kieliekushi tai gonjine ese giezho, tai gounide oluzho. Tai olusan shiqin gieghazhi psedu shiqinde zhughe bu chilazhi zhomen Ezhanni shunji giezho.
1CO 7:36 Nie kun goyade bolusan oqinyi kuighawo giese pse hhe oqinye jiehun gieku nasunse daose hhe kun sumulase indan jiehun giene giese zhao goyane isighala gie, eneshi zui pusho. Hhelai jiehun giegha.
1CO 7:37 Jiaru hhe kun zhughedene jiexin xiaizhi kunzhi gie shidazhi yama biiku shiqin uwoshi ulie jiehun gieseye gou wo.
1CO 7:38 Ingiese jiehun gieseye gou woma, ulie jiehun giese genjia gou wo.
1CO 7:39 Zhanguiji bikude biereini gonjizho, zhanguiji fuguse bierei ziyude kiende khiku duranshi khireima, Ezhanyi xianxin giesan kunde khikui wo.
1CO 7:40 Hhe bierei loujide ulie khise genjia gou wine. Eneshi mii ijien woma, bi sumulase Hudai Ruhher mii jiereye wine.
1CO 8:1 Nigiedade ogisan ijiunii kieliese matande man ene fanmienni erlin bikui matan mejienema, erlin kunni fugiede uzheghane, oreku kunni hendaghane.
1CO 8:2 Goyane mejiene giesan kun indan mejiekune dou ulie mejienema,
1CO 8:3 Hudade oresan kunni Huda tanine.
1CO 8:4 Nigiedade ogisan ijiuni ijiekui kieliese nigieda duyade yama pusho bikui matan mejiene. Huda niekozi wo, pse Huda wikui matan mejiene.
1CO 8:5 Asiman, zemin jiere Huda, Ezhan giezhi urusan olon woma,
1CO 8:6 matande niekozi Huda Ada wo. Yanyanjila man hhense irezho, matanshiye hhenughun wo. Pse matande niekozi Ezhan wo, hheshi Ersa Mexiha wo. Yanyanjila hhei tungo giezhi wine, matanye hhei tungo giezhi wine.
1CO 8:7 Ingieliuzhe intu erlinni jien kunde ese ogizho. Niezhan kunla edeliuzhe nigiedai beiizhi gon oluzho. Ingiese hhela ijiekude nigiedade ogizhi daosan wo giezho. Hhelai lianxin zholienshi zannanshiwo.
1CO 8:8 Shijishan ijieku matan Hudaghalai chadashigha dane. Ulie ijiese yama sunshi uwo, ijieseye yama haochu uwo.
1CO 8:9 Ingiese ta xioxin gie, pse tai ziyu xianxin gieku zholientu kunlai zui fanjighane.
1CO 8:10 Chi intu erlintu kun nigiedai miode ijiesei lianxin zholientu kunla chanlase hhe danzine fugiedaghazhi nigiedade ogisan ijiuni ulie ijienu?
1CO 8:11 Zholientu kun chii erlinni yenyinghala widane. Hheshi Mexiha hhende oluzhi duya ijiesan gaijiu wo.
1CO 8:12 Ta ingiezhi gaijiulai reizhi hhelai zholientu lianxinyi shanjise Mexihani reiwo.
1CO 8:13 Ingiese ijieku gaijiulai zui fanjighase bi chanqi migha ulie ijiene, pse bi gaijiulane zui fanjighane.
1CO 9:1 Bishi ziyutu kun pushonu? Shitu pushonu? Bi mai Ezhan Ersai chanlazhi ese daowu? Tashi bi Ezhanyi miende giesan wiliei jiego pushonu?
1CO 9:2 Bi kunlai shitu pusholiuzhe tai shitu enbene. Tashi bi Ezhanyi miende shitu danlasan zhenji wo.
1CO 9:3 Mii kieliesan kunlade bi goyane ingiezhi huine.
1CO 9:4 Bijiende ijiezhi ochiku qienli uwonu?
1CO 9:5 Bijiende psedu shitu, Ezhanni gaijiula, pse Jifa mutun xianxin giesan biereine uduruku qienli uwonu?
1CO 9:6 Zinie bi Banabaghalade wilie ulie gieku qienli uwonu?
1CO 9:7 Budui danlachen kun kien ijiunine bareizho? Kien putou tareidene yenzini putoui ulie ijiene? Kien iman chezhedene neizii ulie ochine?
1CO 9:8 Bi ingiezhi kieliekushi kunni kieliedanghala kieliezhou? Guijin jiereye ingiezhi ese kieliezhou?
1CO 9:9 Musani guijin jiere, 'Fughe tughon yanchikude zuilun bu zhogha.' giezhi huaizho. Huda fughereide zhughe chilazhou?
1CO 9:10 Enei man matande kieliesan pushonu? Kenjinshi matande oluzhi huaizho. Tareichen kun ghurane giezhi panjizhi tareizho, yanchichen kun ghughane giezhi panjizhi yanchizho.
1CO 9:11 Bijien tai dunda ruhher fanmienni fureni tareidene tanse beye fanmienni injikui ghurase gofen onu?
1CO 9:12 Psedu kunlade tai jierese intu xianshou gieku qienli bise bijiende genjia uwonu? Ingieliuzhe bijien ene qienlini ese injiwo. Khareidene Mexihani gouxioxii duikuse ayizhi soyujilai rennai giewo.
1CO 9:13 Mechide wilie giesan kun mechii dunxii ijiesei, pse sidagha gieku teizi konde ushilasan kun sidagha gieku teizi jieredu dunxii ghughasei ta ulie mejienu?
1CO 9:14 Qingiezhi Ezhanye fenfulazho. Gouxioxini chonjisan kunla gouxioxide kouizhi udu dao giezho.
1CO 9:15 Ingieliuzhe intu qienlini bi goujida injizhi ese daozho. Bi ede xin huaikushi made ingiezhi gie ese giezho. Bi fuguliuzhe bi kuaikune kunlade qianlazhi ulie echighane.
1CO 9:16 Bi gouxioxii chonjise yama kuaikui uwo. Bi ulie chonjise banfa uwo. Ulie chonjise made gou widawo!
1CO 9:17 Bi duralazhi enei giese made gunzi wine. Duran wiliuzhe ene zherenni made ogizho.
1CO 9:18 Ingiese mii gunzishi yan wo? Jiushi gouxioxii kunlade belien chonjizhi indan kereku baerni ese kerekui wo.
1CO 9:19 Made ziyu wine, kiema mii gonji danema, bi soyuji kunlade yenyizhe hoji danlakushi jinlianji olon kunyi jiuighane giezho.
1CO 9:20 Bi Yutai kunlade Yutai kun danlakushi Yutai kunlai jiuighane giezho. Bi guijin doura uwoliuzhe guijin douradu kunlade guijin douradu kun danlakushi guijin douradu kunlai jiuighane giezho.
1CO 9:21 Bi guijin witu kunlade guijin witu kun danlakushi guijin witu kunlai jiuighane giezho. Shijishan made Hudai guijin uwoku pusho, bi Mexihani guijin doura wo.
1CO 9:22 Bi zholien kunlade zholien kun danlakushi zholien kunlai jiuighane giezho. Bi yan kunde yan kun danlakushi matugieliuzhe ezighan kunyi jiuighane.
1CO 9:23 Bi gouxioxini yenyinghala man giekushi kunlare hhantu gouxioxii haochui xianshou giene giezho.
1CO 9:24 Bisai giekude kunla man holuliuzhe zi niekozi kun jianli linlakui ta ulie mejienu? Taye ingiezhi holuma, jianli linlane.
1CO 9:25 Bisai giechen kunla go fanmiende goyane gonjizho. Ingiezhi hhela widaku jianlini linlane giezhoma, matan ulie widaku jianlini linlane giezho.
1CO 9:26 Ingiese bi muji wizhi ese holuzho, chuidase ulie noughachen kun ulie gholune.
1CO 9:27 Bi beyene hende gonjizhi kunzhi giene, pse bi kunlade gouxioxii chonjizhi ogidene goyane baxi olune.
1CO 10:1 Gaijiula, matanyi xienrenla eqighandei olien dourase haise daosan ene shiqinyi bi tai goude jilaghane giezho.
1CO 10:2 Manla olien dourase haise xili jienliezhi Musai daghawo.
1CO 10:3 Manla niekielienji ruhhertu ijiunii ijiewo.
1CO 10:4 Manla niekielienji ruhhertu usui ochiwo. Ochisanshi hhelare yosan ruhhertu tashise khizhesan wo. Ene tashishi Mexiha wo.
1CO 10:5 Ingieliuzhe hhelai dundadu fugie olie kunlade Huda xiqi wise hhelai hontande alawo.
1CO 10:6 Fashen giesan ene shiqinla matande jingao giezhi hhela mutun doghun shiqinni bu neii giezho.
1CO 10:7 Ye hhelai dundadu kunla mutun nigiedalai bu beii giezho. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Bexinla sousenu ochizhi ijiene, bosizhese nadune."
1CO 10:8 Hhela kunlare lon kijiezhi niudude 23000 kun fuguwo. Matan hhela mutun bu gieye.
1CO 10:9 Hhelai dundadu kunla Ezhanni shiidene moghei zhou alawo. Matan hhela mutun Ezhanni bu shiiye.
1CO 10:10 Hhela boxin kieliedene azaraili qienxien hhelai aminni agiwo. Ta hhela mutun boxin bu kielie.
1CO 10:11 Enezighan shiqinla hhelai jiere fashen giezhi kunlade jingao giezho. Matan enezighan duya baraku kunlade surughane giezhi huaizho.
1CO 10:12 Ingiese goyane beizhi undanlawo giesanla indan xioxin gie, pse banjine.
1CO 10:13 Tande iresan shiiku kunlade man wine. Hudashi kekaoni wo, Hhe tande danji daku shiikui ulie ireghane. Shiikude tande nie piiku mo keighazhi tai danji shidaghane.
1CO 10:14 Ingiese mii orentula, ta nigiedalai beiikuse gholodo.
1CO 10:15 Bi minbaitu kunlade kieliezho, bi kieliesanlai ta goyalane uzhezhi gie.
1CO 10:16 Matan onxian giedene ochisan fuqitu beizishi Mexihani chusunde hhantulasan pushonu? Matan ginan ghuluzhi ijiekude Mexihani beyede hhantulasan pushonu?
1CO 10:17 Ginan niekozi wo, matan kun olon woma, nie beye wo. Matan man nie ginande hhantulazho.
1CO 10:18 Ta Isilie bexinlai sumula, sidagha gieku teizi jieredu dunxii ijiesanlashi sidagha gieku teizide hhantulasan pushonu?
1CO 10:19 Bi kieliesanshi yan isi wo? Nigieda, pse nigiedade ogisan ijiunishi yan wo? Yamada pusho!
1CO 10:20 Bi kieliesanshi niman kunla ogise Hudade ese ogizho, sheitande ogizho. Bi tai sheitanre hhantulaghaku duran uwo.
1CO 10:21 Ta Ezhanni beizii ochidene sheitanni beizii ochise jiedui ulie olune. Ezhanni xii soudene sheitanni xii souse jiedui ulie olune.
1CO 10:22 Matan Ezhanni reizhi hokughanu? Matan hhense fama onu?
1CO 10:23 Yanniliuzhe giese olune giezhi kunla kieliezhoma, man haochu wineku pusho. Yanniliuzhe giese olune giezhoma, man kunlai hendaghakui pusho.
1CO 10:24 Kienliuzhe goyane haochude bu olu, kunlai haochude olu.
1CO 10:25 Shichande huisan mighalai ta man ijie, lianxinni yenyinghala yama bu asadene ijie.
1CO 10:26 Zemin, zemin jiere durusanlashi man Ezhannughun wo.
1CO 10:27 Niezhan xianxin ulie giesan kunla tai xinlazhi ijieghase ta duran bizhi echise tai melie beilasanlai ijie, lianxinni yenyinghala yama bu asa.
1CO 10:28 Bifan "eneshi nigiedade xienji giesan ijiuni wo" giezhi kunla tande kieliese, hhe kunde oluzhi, lianxinni yenyinghala bu ijie.
1CO 10:29 Bi kieliesanshi tai lianxin pusho, hhe kunyi lianxin wo. Mii ziyuni yangiezhi kunlai lianxinghala kieliene?
1CO 10:30 Bi mafan kieliedene ijiese yangiezhi bi mafan kieliesan ijiunii yenyinghala mii sugiene?
1CO 10:31 Ingiese ta ijie, ochi yan gieliuzhe Hudai kuaine giezhi gie.
1CO 10:32 Bugon Yutai kun, Xila kun, Hudai jiohuiliuzhe ta hhelai bu banjigha.
1CO 10:33 Bi giesan mutun yan shiqindeliuzhe kunlai bayasugha. Goyane haochude bu oludene kunlai haochude oluzhi hhelai jiuigha.
1CO 11:1 Bi Mexihase surusan mutun ta mase suru.
1CO 11:2 Ta yandeliuzhe mii jilazhi da bi tande chonjizhi ogisei goude bareizho, ingiese bi tai kuaizho.
1CO 11:3 Jien ere kunlai qiorunshi Mexiha wo, biereilai qiorunshi ere kun wo, Mexihai qiorunshi Huda bikui bi tande mejieghaku duran wine.
1CO 11:4 Ere kun onxian giekude, Hudai kielienyi kieliekude qiorunne huighase qiorunne shizheghazho.
1CO 11:5 Biereila onxian giekude Hudai kielienyi kieliekude qiorunne ulie huighase qiorunne shizheghazho. Qingiese qiorunne dulisan niekielien wo.
1CO 11:6 Biereila qiorunne ulie huighase usunne ghigha. Usunne ghigha, dulidene shizhese qiorunne huigha.
1CO 11:7 Ere kun indan qiorunne ulie huighakuni wo, hheshi Hudai yanzi, kuaikui wo. Biereishi ere kunyi kuaiku wo.
1CO 11:8 Ere kunshi biereise khizhesan pusho, biereishi ere kunse khizhesan wo.
1CO 11:9 Da ere kunshi biereide oluzhi zhayaghasan pusho, biereishi ere kunde oluzhi zhayaghasan wo.
1CO 11:10 Ingiese biereila qienxienni yenyinghala qiorun jierene indan jihao giekuni wo. Ene jihaoshi qienli dourashiku isi wo.
1CO 11:11 Ingieliuzhe Ezhanni miende ere kun uwoshi ulie olune, bierei kun uwoshiye ulie olune.
1CO 11:12 Bierei ere kunse khizhesan mutun ere kunye biereii tungo giezhi khizhezho. Soyujila man Hudase khizhezho.
1CO 11:13 Ta goyalane sumula, biereila Hudase onxian giekude qiorunne ulie huighase heshi winu?
1CO 11:14 Ere kunla fudu usun liuise shizhekui ta yenlai ulie mejienu?
1CO 11:15 Biereila fudu usun liuise kuaine. Usunshi biereii qiorunni huighakude ogizho.
1CO 11:16 Niezhan kunla jianjindune giese bijiende intu xigon uwo, Hudai jiohuiladeye intu xigon uwo.
1CO 11:17 Ede bi tai fenfulane giesande tai ulie kuaine. Ta hhantulase haochu uwo, zinie huaichu wo.
1CO 11:18 Ji 1 gieshi bi chenliese ta nie jiohuinughunla libai giene giezhi hhantulakude tai dunda danlinraku shiqin wine. Ene kielienyi bi gouji xianxin giezho.
1CO 11:19 Tai dunda danlinraku shiqin kenjin khizhene, ingiekude caigie hhezighan shixinji giesan kunlai uzhezhi khizhene.
1CO 11:20 Ta hhantulakude ijiesanni Ezhanni heifande ulie sanane.
1CO 11:21 Ta ijiekude man qianlazhi xien ijiezho. Niezhan kunla ijiezhi chudu dazho, niezhan kunla ochi sudozho.
1CO 11:22 Tande ijiezhi ochiku gie uwonu? Pse ta Hudai jiohuii meilade uzhezhi yama witu kunlai shizheghanu? Bi tai matugie kieliene? Tai kuaimu? Intu shiqin jiere bi tai ulie kuaine!
1CO 11:23 Bi Ezhanse jienliesanni tande chonjizhi ogiwo. Ezhan Ersani ghudandusan hhe xii ginanni barei
1CO 11:24 mafan kieliedene ghulu kieliewo, "Eneshi tande oluzhi ogisan mii beye wo. Ta mii jilazhi enei gie."
1CO 11:25 Ijie baludene qingiezhi beizii barei kieliewo, "Ene beizishi mii chusunghala shini yenjisan kielien wo. Ta niefanie ochikude mii jilazhi enei gie."
1CO 11:26 Ta niefanie ene ginanyi ijiezhi ene beizii ochikude Ezhan iretula Ezhan duya ijiesan shiqinni kunlade man mejieghazho.
1CO 11:27 Ingiese yan kunliuzhe Ezhanni ginan, beizii lon ijiezhi ochise Ezhanni beye, chusunyi kuighazho.
1CO 11:28 Kun indan goyade zui winu uwo giezhi goyane goude sumuladene ene ginanyi ijie, ene beizii ochikuni wo.
1CO 11:29 Kun Ezhani beyeshi yan isi bikui ulie mejiedene ijiezhi ochise goyadene zui jinjizho.
1CO 11:30 Ene yenyin jiere tai dunda olon kunla zholierezhi gien kuwo, da fugusanye olon wo.
1CO 11:31 Matan goyalane goude jiencha giese ulie panjine.
1CO 11:32 Matanni panjikude Ezhan matanyi gonjizho, pse matanyi duyai kunlare hhantu zui jinjine.
1CO 11:33 Ingiese mii gaijiula, ta hhantulazhi ijiekude nieniene saghei.
1CO 11:34 Kien oliesuse xien giedene ijie, pse hhantulasanni man panjine. Psedu shiqinlani bi iredene nanpei gieye.
1CO 12:1 Gaijiula, Shenlin fanmienni shiqinni kieliese bi tande ulie mejieghaku duran uwo.
1CO 12:2 Taye mejiene, ta niman kun bikude tai miizhi kielien kielie daku nigiedalai hhende uduruzho.
1CO 12:3 Ingiese bi tande mejieghaye. Hudai Ruhher udurusan kunla Ersani kharakuni wo giezhi kiema ulie kieliene. Shenlin ulie uduruse Ersashi Ezhan wo giezhi kiema kielie dane.
1CO 12:4 Ogisan nenlila buxian woma, manshi nie Shenlin ogisan wo.
1CO 12:5 Ushilaku wiliela buxian woma, manshi nie Ezhande oluzhi giezho.
1CO 12:6 Zoinye buxian woma, manshi nie Huda soyuji kunlai tungo giezhi khizheghasan wo.
1CO 12:7 Shenlin jien kunlai jiere xienjighakushi dajialade haochu ireghane giezho.
1CO 12:8 Niezhan kunlade Shenlinyi tungo giezhi tebieji aghelitu kielienyi ogizho. Niezhan kunlade nie Shenlinyi tungo giezhi tebieji erlin kielieku nenli ogizho.
1CO 12:9 Niezhan kunlade nie Shenlinyi tungo giezhi xianxin gieku ogizho. Niezhan kunlade niekozi Shenlinyi tungo giezhi gien goudaghaku nenli ogizho.
1CO 12:10 Niezhan kunlade nenlitu shiqin gieku, niezhan kunlade Hudai kielienyi kielieku, niezhan kunlade ruhherlani fenjiku, niezhan kunlade psedu kielien kielieku, niezhan kunlade psedu kielienyi fanyi gieku nenli ogizho.
1CO 12:11 Enelashi man hhe niekozi Shenlin giesan wo, hhe goya isighalane buxiantu nenlini jien kunlade fenjizhi ogizho.
1CO 12:12 Niekozi beye jiere iyanzi olon wine, beyede iyanzi olonliuzhe beyeshi nie wo. Mexihaye niekielien wo.
1CO 12:13 Matan bugon Yutai kun, Xila kun, hoji danlasan, ziyutu kunliuzhe hhe niekozi Shenlinse xili jienliezhi nie beye gholudene niekozi Shenlinni xianshou giezho.
1CO 12:14 Beyeshi niekozi iyanzi pusho, olon iyanzi wo.
1CO 12:15 Kon kieliezhi bishi kha pusho, ingiese bi beyenughun pusho gieliuzhe beyenughun pusho bikui pusho.
1CO 12:16 Chighin kieliezhi bishi nudun pusho, ingiese bi beyenughun pusho gieliuzhe beyenughun pusho bikui pusho.
1CO 12:17 Beyede gon nudunshi matugie chenliene? Beyede gon chighinshi matugie funqiene?
1CO 12:18 Huda goya isighalane buxiantu iyanzii nienieji beye jiere teiwo.
1CO 12:19 Soyujila man niekozi iyanzishi matugie beye sanane?
1CO 12:20 Iyanzi olon woma, beye niekozi wo.
1CO 12:21 Nudun khade "Bi chii ulie kerene." giezhi kielie dane. Qiorunye konde "Bi chii ulie kerene." giezhi kielie dane.
1CO 12:22 Khareidene beye jieredu uzhese zholien wo giesan iyanzila chaizhi genjia ulie olune.
1CO 12:23 Matan sumulase beye jieredu zhunyo uwo giesan iyanzilai genjia zhunyoni gholughazhi uzhezhi bixinnilai genjia goude dabalaghazhoma,
1CO 12:24 hennilai qingiezhi gieku biyo uwo. Huda genjia fugie mienzii hhezighan bixin iyanzilade ogizhi beyeni nanpei giekushi
1CO 12:25 beyei iyanzilai ulie danlinraghazhi nieniei zhaogu gieghane giezho.
1CO 12:26 Nie iyanzi ku shouise man hhantu ku shouine. Nie iyanzide famani irese man hhantu bayasune.
1CO 12:27 Tashi Mexihani beye wo, jien kunshi beyeni iyanzi wo.
1CO 12:28 Huda jiohuide nanpei giesan ji 1 gieshi shitu, ji 2 gieshi xienzhi, ji 3 gieshi loushi wo, pse nenlitu shiqin gieku, gien goudaghaku nenli, banman gieku, gonjiku, yanyanji psedu kielien kielieku wo.
1CO 12:29 Manshi shitu onu? Manshi xienzhi onu? Manshi loushi onu? Man nenlitu shiqin gienu?
1CO 12:30 Jien kunlade gien goudaghaku nenli winu? Man psedu kielien kielie shidanu? Man psedu kielienyi fanyi gie shidanu?
1CO 12:31 Ta genjia fugie nenlii hende onxian gie. Bi zui gou moi tande uzheghaye.
1CO 13:1 Bi kunni buxiantu kielienyi kieliezhi qienxienyi kielienyi kielieliuzhe oreku wise tunguliesan laba, gu niekielien wo.
1CO 13:2 Made Hudai kielienyi kielieku nenli bizhi yanyanji chijia daoliji erlinni mejiezhi ulai noighaku fugie xianxin gieku biliuzhe oreku wise bi yama pusho.
1CO 13:3 Bi baerlane man nanxin kunde ogizhi beyene kunlade oluzhi tulieghaliuzhe oreku wise made yama haochu uwo.
1CO 13:4 Oreku izhi rennai giene, renyi wo, ulie dubiliene, goyane ulie kuaizhi zishi ulie shuaine,
1CO 13:5 limao witui ulie giene. Zi goyadene oluzhi ulie giene, suibiende ho ulie kuruzhi kunlai chouni ulie bareine.
1CO 13:6 Gou winide xiqi uwo, zhendaode xiqi wo.
1CO 13:7 Yandeliuzhe aghuide sumulane, soyujilai man xianxin giene, soyujilai man xiwon giene, soyujilai man rennai giene.
1CO 13:8 Hudai kielienyi kielieku, psedu kielienyi kielieku, erlin enela jianlai man baranema, oreku chanqi ulie barane.
1CO 13:9 Matan mejiesanshi ezighan wo, Hudai kielien kieliesanshi ezighan woma,
1CO 13:10 hulunni irese ezighanla man widane.
1CO 13:11 Bi ga shihoude kielieku, sumulaku, jiejin giekula man ga kunyi xianli, fugiedase ga kunnughunyi man widaghawo.
1CO 13:12 Matan ede belijide uzhesan mutun qinchude ese uzhezhoma, hhe xienzi kuse mienduimien uzhene. Bi ede mejiesanshi ezighan woma, hhe xienzi kuse Ezhan mii man mejiesan mutun bi man mejiene.
1CO 13:13 Xianxin gieku, xiwon gieku, oreku chan wine. Ene ghuron dundase orekushi zui fugieni wo.
1CO 14:1 Ta orekui dagha. Pse Shenlin ogisan nenli, tebieshi Hudai kielienyi kielieku nenlini hende onxian gie.
1CO 14:2 Psedu kielienyi kieliesanshi kunlade ese kieliezho, Hudade kieliezho. Kunla dunjire dane, hhe ruhherghalane yanyanji mimii kieliezho.
1CO 14:3 Hudai kielienyi kieliesanshi kunlade kieliezho. Kunlai hendaghazhi surughazhi sidaghazhi kieliezho.
1CO 14:4 Psedu kielienyi kieliesanshi goyane hendaghazho. Hudai kielienyi kieliesanshi jiohuini hendaghazho.
1CO 14:5 Ta man psedu kielienyi kieliekui bi xiwon giezhoma, Hudai kielienyi kieliekui genjia xiwon giezho. Psedu kielienyi kieliedene fanyi ulie giezhi jiohuini ese hendaghazhoshi Hudai kielienyi kieliesan kun hhense hen wo.
1CO 14:6 Gaijiula, bi tai hhende echidene zinie psedu kielienyi kieliezhi Huda mejieghasan, erlin, Hudai kielienyi kielieku, surughasanlai ulie injise tande yan haochu wo?
1CO 14:7 Shenqi khizhesan xiu, qin xianlitu dunxiliuzhe zhao hashuzhe ulie yose yan feiliezhi yan tanjisei kien mejiene?
1CO 14:8 Labai feilie londaghase kien eghindune giezhi zhunbei giene?
1CO 14:9 Taye niekielien wo. Amanghala dunjire daku kielienyi kieliese kieliesei kien mejiene? Enei goyadene kieliezho.
1CO 14:10 Duyade kielien kenjin olon woma, isi witui nieda uwo.
1CO 14:11 Kieliesan kielienyi isini bi dunjire dase hhe kieliechen kun uzhese bishi wigokun wo, bi uzhese hheshi wigokun wo.
1CO 14:12 Taye niekielien wo. Ta Shenlinni nenlii neiizhoma, jiohuini hendaghaku mutun jinlianji olon gie.
1CO 14:13 Ingiese psedu kielienyi kieliesanla indan fanyi gieku nenlini onxian gie.
1CO 14:14 Bi psedu kielienghala onxian giese mii ruhher onxian giezho, mii sumulaku yama zoin uwo.
1CO 14:15 Qingiese matugiene? Bi ruhherghala onxian giene, sumulakughalaye onxian giene. Bi ruhherghala doulane, sumulakughalaye doulane.
1CO 14:16 Ingiezhi ulie giese chi ruhherghala Hudade mafan kieliekude hhantulasan dunda mejie dasan kun chii kielienyi dunjire dase matugie amine giene?
1CO 14:17 Chi Hudade mafan kieliesan gou woma, kunlai hendagha dane.
1CO 14:18 Bi psedu kielienyi ta manlase olon kieliezho. Ingiese Hudade mafan kieliene.
1CO 14:19 Ingiezhoma, bi jiohuide psedu kielienyi 10000 aman kielietula tawun aman sumulakughala kunlade sughazhi kielieku duran wo.
1CO 14:20 Gaijiula, sumulaku jiere ga kun bu gholu. Doghun shiqin jiere yeliwa gholuzhi sumulaku jiere fugie kun gholu.
1CO 14:21 Jinwun jiere huaizho, Bi psedu kielienghala, niman kunlai amanghala ene bexinde kieliene, Ingieliuzhe hhela minughunyi ulie chenliene. Eneshi Ezhan kieliesan wo giezho.
1CO 14:22 Ingiese psedu kielienyi kieliese xianxin giesan kunlade hao ese giezho, xianxin ese giesan kunlade hao giezho. Hudai kielienyi kieliese xianxin giesan kunlade hao giezho, xianxin ese giesan kunlade hao ese giezho.
1CO 14:23 Ingiese jiohuide man hhantulakude dajiala man psedu kielienyi kieliese mejie dasan ibanji kun, xianxin ese giesan kunla iredene ta fenjiulizho giezhi ulie kielienu?
1CO 14:24 Dajiala Hudai kielienyi kieliese xianxin ese giesan kun, ibanji kunla orezhedene ene kielienghala goya zuine mejiezhi goyane kheilazhi
1CO 14:25 zhughedene niuighasanlai khizheghane. Ingie papala Hudai beiizhi Huda shuhuajia tai dunda wo giezhi chenren giene.
1CO 14:26 Gaijiula, qingiese matugiene? Ta hhantulakude jien kunde zeburei onshiku, surughaku, Huda uzheghasan, psedu kielien, fanyi gieku winema, enelai man kunlai hendaghaku mutun gie.
1CO 14:27 Psedu kielienghala kieliekude ghua kun, zui olon ghuran kun lunjizhi kielie. Niekozi kun fanyi gie.
1CO 14:28 Fanyi giechen kun uwoshi hhela jiohuide bu kielie. Goyadeneji Hudade kielie.
1CO 14:29 Hudai kielienyi deilazhi kieliekude ghua ghuran kun kielie. Psedu kunla chenliedene pandon gie.
1CO 14:30 Sousan kun dunda nie kunde Huda mejieghase Hudai kielienyi kieliesan kun xien bu kielie.
1CO 14:31 Ta man ingiezhi nienieji Hudai kielienyi kieliezhi dajialai surughazhi sidaghane.
1CO 14:32 Hudai kielienyi kieliechen kun goyane kunzhi giene.
1CO 14:33 Hudashi londaghachen pusho, heqishighachen wo. Shentulani jiohuilade man ingiezho.
1CO 14:34 Biereila jiohuide kielien bu kielie. Guijin jiere kieliesan mutun hhelai kielien ulie kielieghane, indan shunjikui wo.
1CO 14:35 Hhela yan surune giese giedene zhanguijidene asa, biereila jiohuide kielien kieliese shizheku shiqin wo.
1CO 14:36 Hudai kielien zinie tanse khizhesan onu? Jianie tande ogizhou?
1CO 14:37 Kien goyane xienzhi wo, Shenlinghala hhantu wo giese bi huaisanlashi Ezhanni minlin bikui mejiene.
1CO 14:38 Kien enei chenren ulie giese ta hhei chenren bu gie.
1CO 14:39 Ingiese mii gaijiula, ta Hudai kielienyi kieliekui neii. Psedu kielienyi kieliese bu danla.
1CO 14:40 Ta yan giese nanpeilasan mutun heshide gie.
1CO 15:1 Gaijiula, bi eqighandei tande chonjisan gouxioxii jila ireghaye. Enei ta jienliedene beizhi undanlazho.
1CO 15:2 Bi tande chonjisanni ta belien xianxin ese giedene goude bareizhoshi enei tungo giezhi tai jiuine.
1CO 15:3 Bi eqighandei jienliesan zui zhunyo daolini tande chonjizhi ogiwo. Jiushi jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun Mexiha mai zuide oluzhi duya ijiewo,
1CO 15:4 bulawo, pse jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun ghurudude aminne oluwo,
1CO 15:5 ingie Jifade, pse 12 gie shitulade chujiegheghawo.
1CO 15:6 Khuinashi 500 gie gaijiulade hhantu chujiegheghawo. Hhela dunda niezhanla fuguzho, dabufen ede wine.
1CO 15:7 Khuinashi Yagebude, pse soyuji shitulade chujiegheghawo.
1CO 15:8 Zuihou, shihoude ese olusan mutun zui bixintu madeye chujiegheghawo.
1CO 15:9 Bi shitu dundase zui gani wo. Eqighandei Hudai jiohuii heizho, mii shitu giezhi uruse pei dane.
1CO 15:10 Ingieliuzhe ede bi imutui gholuse Hudai nenjien wo. Hhe made ogisan nenjien zoin witui pusho, bi psedu shitulase olon xiacha giezhi wilie giezho. Eneshi bi pusho, Hudai nenjien bighala hhantu wo.
1CO 15:11 Ingiese biye hao, psedu shitulaye hao, bijien man ingiezhi chonjizho. Taye ingiezhi xianxin giezho.
1CO 15:12 "Mexiha fugusan kun dundase aminne oluwo." giezhi chonjizhoma, tai dunda matugie, "Intu shiqin uwo." giezho?
1CO 15:13 Fugusan kun aminne oluku shiqin uwoshi Mexihaye aminne ese oluzho.
1CO 15:14 Mexiha aminne ese oluzhoshi bijien chonjisan yama oronde uwo, ta xianxin giesanye yama oronde uwo.
1CO 15:15 Zinie ene pusho, bijien lien Hudade oluzhi jia ganzhen beichen danlazho. Ingiekushi bijien ganzhen beizhi Huda Mexihai aminne olughawo giezho. Fugusan kun aminne oluku shiqin uwoshi Hudaye Mexihai aminne ese olughazho.
1CO 15:16 Fugusan kun aminne ulie oluse Mexihaye aminne ese oluzho.
1CO 15:17 Mexiha aminne ese oluzhoshi ta xianxin giesan yama oronde uwo, dou zui dunda wo,
1CO 15:18 Mexihani xianxin giedene duya ijiesanlaye widawo.
1CO 15:19 Matan Mexihai miende jianie duyade xiwon giezhoshi soyuji kun dunda zui ubali wo.
1CO 15:20 Ingiezhoma, Mexiha zhenzhenji fugusan kun dundase aminne oluzhi fugusan kun dundadu toushu gholuwo.
1CO 15:21 Fuguku nie kunse irezho, fugusan kun aminne olukuye da nie kunse irezho.
1CO 15:22 Adanyi miende man fugusan mutun Mexihai miende man aminne olune.
1CO 15:23 Jien kun aminne olukui nanpeilasan mutun giene. Xien toushu Mexiha wo, pse hhe irekude hhenughunla wo.
1CO 15:24 Ingiedene duya barane. Hhe shihoude Mexiha duyade gonjisan, qienli bareisan, nenli bitulai man widaghasenu qienlini Adadene jiuine.
1CO 15:25 Huda Mexihare duitou danlasanlai man hhei kon doura teitula hhe bixi honshan danlane.
1CO 15:26 Zuihou widaghaku duitoushi fuguku wo.
1CO 15:27 Huda soyujilai hhei kon doura shunjighawo giezhi jinwun jiere kieliezhoma, man hhei shunjighazho giese manlai shunjighasan kenjin hhezighanlai sudoro uwo.
1CO 15:28 Man hhei shunjikude kewon goyaneye manlai shunjighasan hhende shunjine, ingiedene Huda manlai gonjizhi manlai jiere wo.
1CO 15:29 Aminne oluku shiqin uwoshi hhezighan kunla fugusan kunde oluzhi xili jienliezhi yan giezho? Fugusan kun zhenzhenji aminne ulie oluse kunla yangiezhi hhelade oluzhi xili jienliezho?
1CO 15:30 Pse yangiezhi bijien niechanie wixiennide echine?
1CO 15:31 Gaijiula, made niudunie fugukui penjizho. Eneshi shuhua wo, bi mai Ezhan Mexiha Ersai miende tai kuaiku mutun zhenni wo.
1CO 15:32 Bi kunni isighala yewore eghinduku mutun Ifuso kunlare eghinduse made yan zoin wo? Fugusan kun aminne ulie oluse, kunla kieliesan mutun "Matan ijie ochiye, maghashijie fugune." giene.
1CO 15:33 Ta shandan bu gie, "Doghun zhanlien gou kunni qida olughane."
1CO 15:34 Ta xiereizhi goude sumula, zui pse bu gie. Niezhan kunla Hudai tani dase bi tai shizheghane giezhi ingiezhi kieliewo.
1CO 15:35 Kunla, "Fugusan kun matugie aminne olune? Yan beyeghala irene." giezhi asane.
1CO 15:36 Yama ulie mejiechen kunlaya, tareisan ulie fuguse osizhi ulie khizhene.
1CO 15:37 Tareisanshi jianlaiku beye pusho, zinie boudei onu, pseshiku fure wo.
1CO 15:38 Huda goya isighalane furede beye ogine, buxiantu furede buxiantu beye ogine.
1CO 15:39 Beyelashi man buxiantu beye wo. Kunde 1 zhun beye wo, yewode 1 zhun beye wo, bunzhude 1 zhun beye wo, zhaghasunde 1 izhun beye wo.
1CO 15:40 Asiman jieredulade 1 zhun beye wo, zemin jieredulade 1 zhun beye wo. Asimanni beyeshi 1 zhun fama wo, zeminni beyeshi 1 zhun fama wo.
1CO 15:41 Naran narande 1 zhun fama wo, sara sarade 1 zhun fama wo, hodun hodunde 1 zhun fama wo, ene hodun hhe hodunghalai famai buxian wo.
1CO 15:42 Fugusan kun aminne oluseye ingiezho. Tareisanshi qida olukuni wo, aminne olusanshi ulie qida olukuni wo.
1CO 15:43 Tareisanshi bixinni wo, aminne olusanshi famani wo. Tareisanshi zholienni wo, aminne olusanshi liliantui wo.
1CO 15:44 Tareisanshi duyani beye wo, aminne olusanshi ruhhertu beye wo. Duyani beye bise ruhhertu beyeye wine.
1CO 15:45 Ji 1 gie kun Adan amitui gholuwo giezhi jinwun jiere huaizhoma, zuihouku Adan amin ogiku ruhher gholuwo.
1CO 15:46 Ingiezhoma, ruhhernughun melie uwo, duyanughun melie wo, khuinashi ruhhernughun wo.
1CO 15:47 Ji 1 gie kun zeminse irezho, turanughun wo, ji 2 gie kun asimanse irezho.
1CO 15:48 Turanughunlashi turase iresan hhei xianli. Asimanughunlashi asimanse iresan hhei xianli.
1CO 15:49 Matande turanughunyi yanzi wineku mutun jianlai asimannughunyi yanzi wine.
1CO 15:50 Gaijiula, bi tande kieliekushi beye Hudai gojiai jienlie dane. Qida oluku ulie qida olukui jienlie dane.
1CO 15:51 Chenliendu, bi tande nie chijia shiqin kielieye. Matan man fugukui pusho, man bienjine.
1CO 15:52 Menzhali nie nudun hameikude zuihouku laba tunguliese fugusan kunla aminne oluzhi ulie qida olune, matanye bienjine.
1CO 15:53 Ene qida oluku beye bixi ulie qida olukui gholune, fuguku beye bixi ulie fugukui gholune.
1CO 15:54 Ene qida oluku ulie qida olukui gholuzhi fuguku ulie fugukui gholukude fugukui injiku yenji boughawo giezhi jinwun jiere jilasan kielien mutun gholune.
1CO 15:55 "Fugukuya, chii injiku khala wo? Fugukuya, chii soyen khala wo?"
1CO 15:56 Fugukui soyenshi zui wo, zuini lilianshi guijin wo.
1CO 15:57 Hudade mafan kielieye, hhe mai ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi matanyi injighazho.
1CO 15:58 Ingiese mii gaijiula, ta khiduzhezhi bu gojiolu, chan xiacha giezhi Ezhanni wiliei olon gie. Ta khishulasanla Ezhanyi miende oronde wiku pusho bikui ta mejiene.
1CO 16:1 Shentulade baer khighakui kieliese bi Jialataini jiohuilade fenfulasan mutun taye qingiezhi gie.
1CO 16:2 Niefanie xinqide jien kunla goya hashughalane agizhi khizhedene ghura, pse bi irekude ta cai khireighane.
1CO 16:3 Bi irekudeni ta chenren giesan kunlade xinni deilazhi hhelai tai murei ughuzhi Yelusalende khughozhi echighaye.
1CO 16:4 Bi echise heshi bise hhela mare hhantu echise olune.
1CO 16:5 Bi Maqidunse daone giezho, daokudeni tai uzhele ireye.
1CO 16:6 Kenen bi tanre nietan soune, kenen unchai daoghane. Ingiedene bi khala echise ta mii khughose olune.
1CO 16:7 Bi ede zinie jingo giekude tai uzhedene echiku duran uwo. Ezhan duran bise bi tanre hhantu ezighancha souse giezho.
1CO 16:8 Bi izhi Ifusode souzhi 50 qienni jieqi kurune.
1CO 16:9 Fandui giechen kun olon woma, made yu aghui yu zointu wijien keizhi chonjiku jihui olon wo.
1CO 16:10 Qimotai irese ta hhende goude giezhi bu ayigha, hheye biwo giezhi Ezhanyi wilieni giezho.
1CO 16:11 Ingiese kienliuzhe hhei gade bu uzhe. Pinnande khughozhi echigha, mii enende ire gie. Gaijiulare hhantu hhe irekui bi sagheizho.
1CO 16:12 Gaijiu Yaboloi kieliese hhe gaijiulare hhantu tai hhende echi giezhi bi hhende haojihui goude fenfulawo, hhe ene shihoude echiku duran uwo, jihui irese echine.
1CO 16:13 Ta jinxin giezhi xinyan jiere beizhi undanla, ere kunyi yanzii khizheghazhi khidunde bei.
1CO 16:14 Ta yan giese oreku zhugheghala gie.
1CO 16:15 Siqifana nie gie kun Yagaiyade Ersai tou 1 giede xianxin giesei ta mejiene. Pse hhela zhomen shentulai ushilazho. Gaijiula, bi tai goude fenfulaye,
1CO 16:16 ta qimutu kunlai, pse hhelare hhantu khishulazhi wilie giesan kunlai man shunji.
1CO 16:17 Siqifana, Futunadu, Yagaigu irese bi bayasuzho. Ta enende uwoma, hhela banman giewo.
1CO 16:18 Hhela tai pse mii bayasughazho. Imutu kunlai ta danren gie.
1CO 16:19 Yaxiyani jiohuila tande kielien asazho. Yajila, Baijilaghala pse hhelai giede hhantulasan jiohui Ezhanni miende tande shixinji kielien asazho.
1CO 16:20 Gaijiula man tande kielien asazho. Ta zhughesene nieniedene kielien asa.
1CO 16:21 Bi Baolo qinsi huaizhi kielien asazho.
1CO 16:22 Kien Ezhande ulie orese hhei indan kharakui wo. Mai Ezhan, ire!
1CO 16:23 Ezhan Ersai nenjien tanre hhantu bi gie!
1CO 16:24 Mexiha Ersai miende mii oreku tanre man hhantu wo!
2CO 1:1 Hudai isighala Mexiha Ersade shitu danlasan BaoloQimotai gaijiughala Gelindoni Hudai jiohui, pse Yagaiyani shentulade man xin huaizho.
2CO 1:2 Mai ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
2CO 1:3 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani ada Hudade doula. Hheshi ubali xiichen ada wo, shiheni sidaghazhi kieliechen Huda wo.
2CO 1:4 Hhe olon kunnan dunda matai sidaghazhi kieliezhi hhe ogisan sidaghaku kieliesanghala matan psedu kunnan shouisan kunlai sidaghazhi kielie shidane.
2CO 1:5 Matan Mexihai kui olon shouisan mutun Mexihai tungo giezhi sidaghaku kielienye olon wo.
2CO 1:6 Bijien kunnan shouise tai sidaghazhi jiuikude oluzho. Bijienyi sidaghazhi kieliese tai sidaghazhi kieliekude oluzho. Ene sidaghazhi kielieku bijien shouisan xianlitu kunnanni ta shouikude tai rennai gieghane.
2CO 1:7 Ta bijien mutun ku shouise sidaghaku kielienyiye jienliekui bijien mejiene, ingiese bijien tande xiwon giesan goujida ulie bienjine.
2CO 1:8 Gaijiula, bijien Yaxiyade shouisan kunnanni tande ulie mejieghaku duran uwo. Hhe shihoude bijien danjisan achanshi bijien danji dakui wo, lien amituraku xiwon da widazho.
2CO 1:9 Bijien sumulase bijienyi ijin sixin panjiwo giezho. Ingiekushi bijienyi goyadene ese kouighazhi fugusan kunyi aminne olughasan Hudade kouighane giezho.
2CO 1:10 Huda bijienyi fuguku wixiense jiuiwo, da izhi jiuine. Taye onxian giezhi bijiende banman giema, hhe pse bijienyi jiuikui bijien hende xiwon giezho. Ingiezhi olon kunla bijiende onxian giedene Huda dain giese olon kunla bijienyi yenyin jiere Hudade mafan kieliene.
2CO 1:12 Bijien duyade giekude, tebieshi tanre laiwon giekude Huda ogisan zhijieji shixinji zhugheghala giezho. Kunni jienzhaghala ese giezhi Hudai nenjienghala giezho. Enende bijienyi lianxin ganzhen beine. Ingiezhi giesande bijien goyane kuaine.
2CO 1:13 Bijien ede tande huaisanshi zhao ta onshizhi dunjireku mutun huaizho. Ta ede bijienyi man dunjire dazhoma, bi xiwon giese man dunjire.
2CO 1:14 Ingiese Ezhan Ersai udude bijien tai kuaiku mutun taye bijienyi kuaine.
2CO 1:15 Made intu xinxin bise sumulazhi xien tai hhende echizhi tande ghuareifa nenjien ireghaye giezho.
2CO 1:16 Jiushi tai hhense jingo giezhi Maqidunde echine, ingie Maqidunse khareizhi tai dunda iredene ta mii Yudayade khughose giezho.
2CO 1:17 Bi ingiezhi jihua giese suibiende giezhou? Bi duyai banfaghala jihua giezhi enbene giekude pusho giezhi kielienu?
2CO 1:18 Bi kekaotu Hudai zhiizhi kielieye. Bijien tande kieliese yu enbene yu pusho giezhi ulie kieliene.
2CO 1:19 Bi, Seila, Qimotai ghuralie tai dunda chonjisan Hudai kewon, Ersa Mexihashi enbene giekude pusho giekui pusho. Hhende zinie enbekui wine.
2CO 1:20 Hudai dain giesanla giedughanliuzhe Mexihai sudoro man enbekui wo. Ingiese matan Mexihai tungo giezhi amine kieliezhi Hudai kuaine.
2CO 1:21 Mexihai miende bijienyi tanre hhantu khiduzheghazhi teshu wiliede oluzhi matanyi sunghusanshi Huda wo.
2CO 1:22 Hhe matai jiere zhanzi taizhi Shenlinni mai zhughede ogizhi yajin daruwo.
2CO 1:23 Bi Gelindode pse ese irekushi tande oluzho. Enende Huda made ganzhen bei giezhi bi kielie shidane.
2CO 1:24 Bijien tai xinyanni gonjine gieku pusho, tai bayasughane giezhi tanre hhantu wilie giezho. Ta xinyan jierene beizhi undanlazho.
2CO 2:1 Bi tai hhende echise pse nangoni deilazhi ulie echine giezhi jiejin giewo.
2CO 2:2 Bi tai nango gieghazhoshi bi nango gieghasan tanse chugo kien mii bayasughane?
2CO 2:3 Bi eqighandei xinni huaikushi bi irekude indan mii bayasughaku kunla khareidene mii nango gieghakuse ayizho. Bi bayasuse ta dajialaye bayasukui bi xianxin giezho.
2CO 2:4 Bi eqighandei zhughedemi otuzhi yuchou giezhi wilazhi tande xin huaikushi tai nango gieghane ese giezho, bi tande matugie oresei mejieghane giezho.
2CO 2:5 Kunni nango gieghasan hhe kun zinie mii nango gieghakui pusho, ta dajialaiye man ezighan nango gieghazho. Bi ingiezhi kieliese hende gofen uwo.
2CO 2:6 Intu kunyi ta olon kunla qingie faise kuruwo,
2CO 2:7 ede khareidene hhei rouliezhi sughazhi kielie, pse nango olon giese bazilie dane.
2CO 2:8 Ingiese bi tai xiahua gieye, ta hhe kunde oreku zhughene goude mejiegha.
2CO 2:9 Bi eqighandei xinni huaikushi ta yan shiqindeliuzhe shunjinu ulie shunjikui shiizhi mejiene giezho.
2CO 2:10 Ta kienyi mienliese bi kienyi mienliene. Bi kienyi mienliese Mexihai melie tande oluzhi mienliezho,
2CO 2:11 pse Ibilisi matanyi pienyi zhanjine. Matan hhei mujii ulie mejiekui pusho.
2CO 2:12 Bi Mexihani gouxioxide oluzhi Teloyade echise Ezhan made gouxioxi chonjiku wijienni niewoma,
2CO 2:13 bi oresan gaijiu Qidoi chanla dase zhughedemi nanran uwo. Ingie hhendedu kunlade salan gie Maqidunde echiwo.
2CO 2:14 Hudade mafan kielieye, hhe Mexihare hhantu matanyi chan uduruzhi zhan eghizhi injighazho. Pse matai tungo giezhi Mexihai taniku andatui gochude funqieghazho.
2CO 2:15 Bugon jiuisan kun, widachen kun dunda matanshi Hudade ogiku Mexihani andatu widao wo.
2CO 2:16 Ene widao widachen kunlade fugughaku fumughei wo, jiuisan kunlade aminni andatui wo. Kien intu renwuni gie shidane?
2CO 2:17 Bijien olon kunla mutun Hudai daolii baer huiku dunxi ese danlaghazho. Bijien jianjise Huda peisan mutun Hudai melie Mexihai kouizhi shixinji giezho.
2CO 3:1 Bijien pse goyane jieshao gie qiiwu? Bijien niezhan kunla wo giezhi bijienyi jieshao xinni tande oginu? Tanse jieshao xin keredene kunlade oginu?
2CO 3:2 Tashijiu bijienyi jieshao xin wo, bijienyi zhughede huaizhi kunla man tanizhi onshizho.
2CO 3:3 Ta minminjishi Mexihani xin wo, bijienyi tungo giezhi huaisan wo. Meshuighala huaisan pusho, chanqiku Hudai Ruhherghala huaisan wo. Tashi jiere ese huaizho, kunni zhughe jiere huaizho.
2CO 3:4 Bijien Mexihani tungo giezhi Hudai melie qingiezhi xianxin giezho.
2CO 3:5 Ingiezhi kieliese bijien goya nengandene kouizho giesan pusho. Bijienni nenganshi Hudase iresan wo.
2CO 3:6 Huda bijiende shini yenjisan kieliende gonjia danlaku nengou ogizho. Ene yenjisan kielienshi uroughala giesan pusho, ruhherghala giesan wo. Urou kunni fugughane, ruhher kunde amin ogine.
2CO 3:7 Tashi jiere uroughala huaisan fuguku wilie irekude fama bizhi Isilie kunla Musai khizha jieredu widaku gonni uzhe dazhoma,
2CO 3:8 Shenlinni wiliei famani genjia fugie uwonu?
2CO 3:9 Kunde zui jinjiku wiliede fama bise kunni gounide sanaku wiliede fama genjia fugie wo.
2CO 3:10 Ene tebieji fugie famani yenyinghala eqighanku fama widawo.
2CO 3:11 Hhe zhanshi jiere bidene widakude fama bise hhe chanqikude fama genjia olon wo.
2CO 3:12 Ingiese matande intu xiwon bise fugie danzighala kieliene.
2CO 3:13 Matan Musa wo giezhi shoujinghala khizhane huighazhi Isilie kunlai hhe niechaku famani widakui ulie chanlaghane gie ese giezho.
2CO 3:14 Ingieliuzhe hhelai zhughe khiduzhezhi eli kutula khuichen yenjisan kielienni onshikude ene shoujinni da ese agizho. Ene shoujinni Mexihare hhantulase agi widaghane.
2CO 3:15 Eli kutula niefanie Musai shuni onshikude shoujin hhelai zhughede wo.
2CO 3:16 Hhelani zhughe giezhe Ezhande shunjise shoujin giezhe widane.
2CO 3:17 Ezhanshi hhe ruhher wo, Ezhanni ruhher khalashi khala ziyu wine.
2CO 3:18 Matan man shoujin ese khaghasan khizhaghala Ezhanni famani uzhezhi, Ezhanyi yanzi mutun bienjizhi yebeiseye fugie famatu gholuzho. Ene Ezhanyi ruhherse irezho.
2CO 4:1 Ingiese Huda bijiende ubali xiizhi ene renwui ogise bijien zhughe ulie widane.
2CO 4:2 Khareidene niuighazhi giesan shizheku shiqinyi bendawo. Piendaku shiqin ulie giezhi Hudai daolii ulie wirulaghane. Zhendaoni qinchude kieliezhi Hudai melie jien lianxintu kunlade goyane jieshao giene.
2CO 4:3 Bijien chonjisan gouxioxii khaghazhoshi widachen kunlade khaghazho.
2CO 4:4 Ene duyai Ibilisi enezighan xianxin ulie giechen kunlai nudunyi sugho gholughazhi gouxioxii gonni ese chanlaghazho. Ene gouxioxide Mexihai famani kieliezho. Mexihashi Hudai yanzi wo.
2CO 4:5 Bijien chonjisanshi goyane pusho. Ersa Mexihashi Ezhan bikui, pse Ersade oluzhi tande hoji danlasanni chonjizho.
2CO 4:6 "Kharanise gon khizhe" giezhi kieliesan Huda Ersa Mexihai khizha jieredu goya famane mejieghaku gonni mai zhughede zhouighazho.
2CO 4:7 Bijiende ene boubei winema, bijienshi zinie boubei teiku wagangan wo. Ingiekushi tebieji fugie nenlishi bijiennughun pusho Hudanughun bikui mejieghane giezho.
2CO 4:8 Bijienyi simiense daruzhoma, daruzhi yama giegha dazho. Zhughede kunnan winema, xiwon ese widazho.
2CO 4:9 Heizhoma, Huda bijienyi ese bendazho. Eghi unaghazhoma, eghizhi ala dazho.
2CO 4:10 Bijien beye jierene Ersani duya ijiekui chan deilakushi Ersani aminni bijienyi jiereye xienjizhi khizheghane giezho.
2CO 4:11 Bijien amitukude Ersani yenyinghala chan fuguku wixien dunda wo. Ingiekushi Ersani aminyi bijienyi fuguku beye jiere xienjizhi khizheghane giezho.
2CO 4:12 Ingie uzhese fuguku bijienyi jiere ochirazho, amin tai jiere ochirazho.
2CO 4:13 Jinwun jiere, "Bi xianxin giezho, ingiese bi kieliezho." giezhi huaisan mutun bijiendeye xianxianji xianxin gieku wine, ingiese bijien xianxin giedene kieliezho.
2CO 4:14 Ezhan Ersai aminne olughasan hhe bijienyiye Ersare hhantu aminne olughazhi bijienyi tanre hhantu hhei melie beighakui bijien mejiene.
2CO 4:15 Enelashi man tande oluzhi giezho. Ingiese nenjien yebeiseye olon kunlade echizhi mafan gieku zhughe olodozhi kuaikui Hudade ogine.
2CO 4:16 Ingiese bijien zhughe ulie widane. Bijienyi beye goujijia qida olunema, zhughe niudunie shinishizho.
2CO 4:17 Bijienyi zhanshi jieredu gongien kunnan jianlai ireku hashu witu chanqiku fugie famani chenjighane.
2CO 4:18 Bijien gonxin giekushi chanlaku pusho, chanla daku wo. Chanlakushi niechaku wo, chanla dakushi chanqiku wo.
2CO 5:1 Mai zemin jieredu zhanfanyi chei widaghase Hudai hhense ireku gie matande winekui matan mejiene. Kunni khaghala giesan pusho, asiman jieredu chanqiku gie wo.
2CO 5:2 Matan ene zhanfande shonholozhi asimanse iresan gieghala jien musiku mutun arunzhakui panjizho.
2CO 5:3 Qingie musise hulan muchughun ulie gholune.
2CO 5:4 Matan ene zhanfande gunduni beiliezhi shonholokushi teine ese giezho, musine giezho. Ingiezhi ene fuguku beyei amin yenji boughane.
2CO 5:5 Ene mujide oluzhi matai nanpeilasanshi Huda wo. Hhe matande Shenlinni yajin danlaghazhi ogiwo.
2CO 5:6 Ingiese, matan beyede bikude Ezhanse gholo bikui mejienema, matande chan fugie danzi wine.
2CO 5:7 Matan yan giese chanlakughala ese giezho, xianxin giekughala giezho.
2CO 5:8 Matande fugie danzi wine. Beyese likai giezhi Ezhanghala hhantu souku genjia duran wine.
2CO 5:9 Ingiese matan beyedeye olune beyese likai gieye olune matanyi mujishi hhei bayasughane.
2CO 5:10 Matan man bixi Mexihani shenpantai melie xienjizhi khizheghadene zhao jien kun giesan gouni, doghunni mutun kharulune.
2CO 5:11 Ezhanshi indan zunjikui bijien mejiese kunlade sughazhi kieliene. Huda bijienyi mejiene, bi xiwon giese taye zhughedene bijienyi mejie.
2CO 5:12 Bijien pse tande goyalane jieshao ese giezho, bijienyi kuaiku jihuini tande ogine giezho. Ingiese hhezighan zhughei ulie uzhedene mienzii uzhezhi kuaisan kunlai melie kieliekui wine.
2CO 5:13 Bijien fenjiulise Hudade oluzho, zhenchanshi tande oluzho.
2CO 5:14 Ingiekushi Mexihani oreku bijienyi biizho. Nie kun soyuji kunlade oluzhi duya ijiese soyuji kunla duya ijiesanyi bijien mejiene.
2CO 5:15 Mexiha soyuji kunlade oluzhi duya ijiekushi amitu kunla pse goyadene oluzhi ulie amiturazhi hhelade oluzhi duya ijiedene aminne olusan Ezhande oluzhi amituraghane giezho.
2CO 5:16 Ingiese enedu khuinase matan kienniliuzhe kunni uzhedanghala ulie uzhene. Eqighandei Mexihaniye kunni uzhedanghala uzhewoma, ede pse qingiezhi ulie uzhene.
2CO 5:17 Kien Mexihai miende bise hheshi shini giesan kun wo, khuichennila daozhi man shinii gholuwo.
2CO 5:18 Enelashi man Hudase iresan wo. Hhe Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi matanyi goyarene goudaghazhi pse kun Hudaghala goudaghaku renwuni matande ogiwo.
2CO 5:19 Eneshijiu Huda duyai kunlai zuini ese asadene Mexihai tungo giezhi goyarene goudaghazho. Pse goudaghaku daolini matande jiuizhi ogiwo.
2CO 5:20 Ingiese matan Mexihai daibio giezho. Huda matai tungo giezhi kunlade sidaghazhi kieliezho. Matan Mexihai oronde ta Hudare gouda giezhi tai xiahua gieye.
2CO 5:21 Huda hhe zui wituni matande oluzhi zuitu gholughakushi matanyi hhei sudoro Hudai gouni gholughane giezho.
2CO 6:1 Hudare hhantu wilie giesan bijien tai xiahua gieye, Hudai nenjienni jienliezhi belienni bu gholugha.
2CO 6:2 Huda kieliezhi, "Heshitu shihoude bi chinughunyi chenliewo. Jiuiku udude bi chade banman giewo." giezho. Uzhe, ede zhen heshitu shihou wo, uzhe, ede zhen jiuiku udu wo!
2CO 6:3 Bijien giesan wiliene ulie sugieghane giezhi jinlianji kiendeliuzhe chijia ese teizho.
2CO 6:4 Khareidene goyaneshi Hudai hoji wo giezhi yanyanji shiqin jiere uzheghazho. Jiushi olon rennai gieku, kunnan, chijia shiqin, zeinan,
2CO 6:5 eghiku, khaku, nouiku, khishulaku, kijie daku, ijie daku dunda
2CO 6:6 bijien ganjinde giezhi erlin, rennai gieku, renyi, Shenlin, zhenzhenji oreku,
2CO 6:7 shuhua kielieku, Hudai nenlighala giezho. Borun soghei khade gundan uqi bareidene
2CO 6:8 bugon bijienyi zunjiye hao, shizheghaye hao, sugieye hao, kuaiye hao bijien ingiezhi giezho. Kunla kieliese piendachen wo giezhoma, bijien shuhua kieliezho.
2CO 6:9 Bijienyi kiema ulie mejiene giezhoma, niere fugie no wo. Fuguwo giezhoma, amitu wo. Bijienyi faizhoma, ese alazho.
2CO 6:10 Bijien yuchou giesanyi xianlima, chan bayasuzho. Nanxin wo giezhoma, olon kunlai bayazheghazho. Uzhese yama uwoma, yanliuzhe wine.
2CO 6:11 Gelindo kunlaya, bijien tande zhijie kieliezhi zhughene keighazho.
2CO 6:12 Bijien tai zhughei ese meilashighazho, ta goyalane meilashighazho.
2CO 6:13 Bi kewosidene kielieku mutun kielieye, bijien giesan mutun taye bijiende zhughene keigha.
2CO 6:14 Ta xianxin ulie giechen kunlare nie jiabanyi bu zho. Gouni mouxiennighala matugie hhantulane? Gon kharanighala matugie laiwon giene?
2CO 6:15 Mexiha Bilieghala matugie heqishine? Xianxin giesan, ulie xianxin giesanghala matugie hhantu giene?
2CO 6:16 Mechi nigiedaghala matugie hhantulane? Matanshi chanqiku mechi wo. Zhen Huda kieliesan mutun, "Bi hhelai dunda souzhi hhelare laiwon giene. Bi hhelade Huda danlane. Hhela made bexin danlane."
2CO 6:17 Ezhan kieliezho, "Ingiese ta hhelai dundase khizhezhi hhelase danxinra. Zannan dunxilai bu shighama, bi tai jienliene.
2CO 6:18 Bi tande ada danlane. Ta made kewon oqin danlane. Eneshi nenlitu Ezhan kieliesan wo."
2CO 7:1 Ingiese mii orentula, matande enezighan dain giesan bise beye, zhughe jieredu zannannilane waghazhi man widaghadene Hudai zunjiku zhugheghala onqienji zhiguishighaye.
2CO 7:2 Ta aghui zhugheghala bijienyi jienlie. Bijien kiemai ese kuighazho, kiemai ese heizhi pienyi ese zhanjizho.
2CO 7:3 Bi ingiezhi kieliekushi tai kheilane ese giezho. Bi eqighandei kieliezhi daosan mutun ta chan bijienyi zhughede bizhi bijien tanre amiturazhi fuguliuzhe hhantulaku duran wine.
2CO 7:4 Bi tande xinxin fugie wo, tai ologhonni kuaizhi zhughedemi futan no wo. Bijien shouisan olon kunnan dunda bi hende bayasuzho.
2CO 7:5 Bijien Maqidunde kurudeneye hhamura dazhi gochuse kunnan shouizho. Ghadane maodun wo, sudoro ayizho.
2CO 7:6 Ingieliuzhe xiwon widasan kunlai sidaghazhi kieliesan Huda Qidoi irekui tungo giezhi bijienyi sidaghazhi kieliewo.
2CO 7:7 Zinie hhei irekughala pusho, hhe tai hhense jienliesan sidaghazhi kieliekughala bijienyi sidaghazhi kieliewo. Ta mii sanasan, goya nango giesan, pse ta made rexinde giesei hhe made man kieliese bi genjia bayasuzho.
2CO 7:8 Bi tande hhe xinni huaizhi tai zhanshi jiere nango gieghasei mejiedene houhui giezhoma pse houhui ulie giene.
2CO 7:9 Ede bi bayasukushi tai nango gieghasande pusho, nango giedene geiikude echighasande wo. Ta Hudai isi mutun nango giedene bijien tai ese shanjizho.
2CO 7:10 Zhao Hudai isi mutun nango giese houhui ulie giezhi geidene jiuine. Duyai nango gieku kunyi fugughane.
2CO 7:11 Ta nie uzhe, ta zhao Hudai isi mutun nango giedene ede tai dunda imegheni rexinde gieku, goyane huiku, doghunnide hokuku, jinshen khizheku, mini sanaku, bayasuzhi gieku, codasanni faiku wine. Ene shiqin jiere go fanmiende ta goyalane gou bikui zhenmin giezho.
2CO 7:12 Ingiese bi tande hhe xinni huaise pienyi zhanjisan kunde ese huaizho, kuighasan kundeye ese huaizho. Khareidene ta bijiende rexin bisei Hudai melie tande zhenmin giene giezho.
2CO 7:13 Ingiese bijienyi sidaghazhi kieliewo. Ene sidaghasanse chugo ta olon kunla Qidoni zhughei futanshighazhi bayasughase bijien genjia bayasuzho.
2CO 7:14 Bi Qidode tai kuaizhi daozhoma, ta mii ese shizheghazho. Bijien tande kieliesan kielienshi man zhenni bikui mutun bijien Qidode tai kuaisanshi zhenni bikui zhenmin giewo.
2CO 7:15 Ta manla hhei shunjizhi ayi pugharazhi goude jienliesei hhe sumula irese tande oreku zhughe genjia hhereizho.
2CO 7:16 Bi tande onqienji zhughene teise bayasuzho.
2CO 8:1 Gaijiula, Huda Maqidun jiohuilade ogisan nenjienni bi tande mejieghaye.
2CO 8:2 Kunnan dunda hhelai fugiede shiikude hende bayasuzhi tebieji nanxin bikude kunlade tebieji dafande ogizho.
2CO 8:3 Hhela banman giekude zhao nenlighalane, pse nenlisene chaogo giezhi goyalane ogisei bi ganzhen bei shidane.
2CO 8:4 Hhela bijienyi haojihui hende xiahua giezhi shentulade banman gieku shiqin jiere jihui ogizhi guzi beigha giezho.
2CO 8:5 Hhela giesan bijien sumulasanse olon chaogo giezho. Hhela goyane xien Ezhande ogizhi pse Hudai isighala bijiende ogizho.
2CO 8:6 Ingiese bijien Qidode ene gou shiqinyi chi kaishi giese tai dunda giezhi chengun olugha giezhi sughazhi kieliewo.
2CO 8:7 Ta xianxin gieku, kielien kielieku, erlin, rexin, bijien tande oreku jiere man kunlase zui goude giesan mutun nanxin kunlade banman gieku shiqin jiereye zui goude giekui bijien xiwon giezho.
2CO 8:8 Bi ingiezhi kieliese tande ese fenfulazho, kunlai rexinghala tai oreku zhugheshi shixinji enbenu pusho bikui uzhene giezho.
2CO 8:9 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjienyi ta mejiene. Hhe yenlai bayan wo, tande oluzhi nanxinshikushi hhei nanxinnighala tai bayazheghane giezho.
2CO 8:10 Kunlade ogiku shiqin jiere bi tande sumulakune kielieye. Ta ingiezhi giese gou wo. Ta udai honse ene shiqinyi zui melie giezho, zui melie duralazhoma,
2CO 8:11 giezhi qiikude bisan rexin mutun ede ene shiqinyi giezhi chengun olugha. Zhao nengou biku mutun gie.
2CO 8:12 Ta duranghalane ogise Huda jienliene. Uwokulane ogi ese giezho, winekulane ogi giezho.
2CO 8:13 Bi kunlai gongienshighazhi tande kunnan ireghane ese giezho, manlai izhishighane giezho.
2CO 8:14 Edeku tai bayan hhelai chaisande banman gie shidaku mutun hhelai bayan jianlai tai chaisande banman giene, ingiese izhishiwo.
2CO 8:15 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Olon ghurasanlade feiliekui uwo, choghon ghurasanlade chaikui uwo."
2CO 8:16 Bi tande oluzhi rexintu zhughei Qidoi zhughede teisan Hudade mafan kielieye.
2CO 8:17 Qido bijien fenfulasei chenliezhoma, goyane genjia rexin bizhi yenyizhe tai hhende echiwo.
2CO 8:18 Bijien da nie gaijiui peizhi hhere hhantu echighawo. Ene kunyi gouxioxi chonjiku jiere olon jiohuila man kuaizho.
2CO 8:19 Zinie ene pusho, jiohuila hhei sunghudene peizhi bijienre hhantu echighazhi bijiende jiuizhi ogisan baerni khughoghazho. Bijien ene gou shiqinyi giese Ezhanni famade oluzho, bijien gou zhughene mejieghazho.
2CO 8:20 Bijien ingiezhi giekushi ene olon baerni gonjikude kunlai ulie sugieghane giezho.
2CO 8:21 Bijien gou shiqin giese zinie Ezhanni melie gieku pusho, kunlai melieye ingiezho.
2CO 8:22 Bijien pse nie gaijiui peizhi hhelare hhantu echighawo. Bijien olon shiqin jiere hhei kaoyen olon giedene hhende rexin bikui mejiewo. Ede hhe tai hende xianxin giedene genjia rexinshizho.
2CO 8:23 Qidoi kieliese hheshi mii nokie wo, tande oluzhi mare lienshou gholuzho. Pse hhe ghua gaijiushi jiohuila peisan wo, Mexihani fama wo.
2CO 8:24 Ingiese ta jiohuilai melie oreku zhughene, pse bijien tai kuaisei hhelade zhenmin gie.
2CO 9:1 Shentulade banman gieku shiqinyi kieliese bi tande xin huaiku biyo uwo.
2CO 9:2 Tande gou zhughe bikui bi mejiene. Bi Maqidun kunlade Yagaiya kunla udai honse zhunbei giezho giezhi tai kuaizho. Tai rexin olon kunlai zhughei gojiolughazho.
2CO 9:3 Ede bi hhe giedun gaijiulai peizhi echighakushi zhao mii kielienzhe tai zhunbei gie goudaghane giezho. Pse bijien ene shiqin jiere tai kuaisan belienni gholune.
2CO 9:4 Babuchu Maqidun kunla mare hhantu echizhi ta ese zhunbei giesei chanlase ta shizhekui pse bu kielieye, bijien tai xianxin giesan shizhekui gholune.
2CO 9:5 Ingiese bi sumulase hhe giedun gaijiui xien peizhi tai hhende echighazhi ta dain giesan olon mureni zhunbei gie goudagha giezhi goude kielieku biyo wine. Ingiezhi giese ta khireighasanshi biisan pusho, duranzhe giesan wo.
2CO 9:6 Eneshijiu choghon tareisan choghon ghurane, olon tareisan olon ghurane giesan wo.
2CO 9:7 Jien kun zhughedene jiejin giesan mutun ogikuni wo. Chijia bu tei, ye bu bii. Duranzhe khireighasan kunlade Huda xiqi wo.
2CO 9:8 Huda yanyanji nenjienlai tande olon ogizhi yandeliuzhe chan kurughazhi yanyanji gou shiqinni tai olon gieghane.
2CO 9:9 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Hhe dafande nanxin kunlade ogizho, hhei gundan chanqi wine."
2CO 9:10 Tareisan kunde fure ogisan, kunde ijiuni ogisan Huda tareiku fureni tande ogizhi olodoghane, ta giesan gundan wiliede jiego olon khizheghane.
2CO 9:11 Tai gofanmiende bayazheghazhi suishisui dafande kunlade ogighane. Ingiezhi bijien giesan wiliei tungo giezhi Hudade mafan kielieghane.
2CO 9:12 Ene banman gieku shiqinyi giezhi zinie shentulade chaisei buisan pusho, olon kunlai Hudade mafan kielieku tebie olodoghazho.
2CO 9:13 Ta Mexihai gouxioxii chenren giezhi shunjizhi hhelade, pse olon kunlade dafande ogiku wiliei hhela kaoyen giedene Hudai kuaizho.
2CO 9:14 Huda tande tebieji fugie nenjien ogizho. Ingiese hhela tande oluzhi onxian giezhi tai sanazho.
2CO 9:15 Nenjienyini kieliezhi baragha daku Hudade mafan kielieye!
2CO 10:1 Bi Baolo qinsi Mexihani renyi, gou zhugheghala tande goude kielieye. Kunla kieliese bi tai chujieghekude goyane meilade uzhezho, tai hhende uwokude wizha wo giezho.
2CO 10:2 Bi xiahua gieye, bijien duyani banfaghala giezho giezhi sumulasanlade bi wizhade gienema, bi tai hhende echikude mii biizhi wizhade bu giegha.
2CO 10:3 Bijien duyade udu daozhoma, duyani banfaghala zhan ese eghinduzho.
2CO 10:4 Bijien eghinduku uqishi duyanughun pusho, Hudai nenlitu wo, khidun chenqianni unaghane.
2CO 10:5 Bijien kun zhenjindusan, pse kunni danlazhi Hudai ulie tanighazhi goyane fugiede uzhesan yanyanjilai man widaghane. Yanyanji sumuladanlai man barei iredene Mexihade shunjighane.
2CO 10:6 Ta onqienji shunjikude soyuji ese shunjisan kunlai faikui bijien zhunbei gie goudaghazho.
2CO 10:7 Ta shiqin uzhese zinie mienzii uzhene. Niezhan kun goyaneshi Mexihanughun wo giese hhe goude sumulakui wo, hheshi Mexihanughun mutun bijienshiye Mexihanughun wo.
2CO 10:8 Ezhan bijiende qienli ogikushi tai qida olugha ese giezho, hendagha giezho. Bijienyi qienlii bi goujinie gofende kuaise shizhene ulie giene.
2CO 10:9 Bi ingiezhi kieliekushi bi xin huaizhi tai ayighane giezhi tai ulie sumulaghane giezho.
2CO 10:10 Niezhan kun kieliese hhei xin yenge wo, khidun wo, kunni chujieghese zholien wo. Hhe jianjisan yama jiazhi uwo giezho.
2CO 10:11 Intu kunla indan mejiekui wo. Bijien tai hhende uwokude xin jiere matugie kieliezhoshi chujieghese matugie giene.
2CO 10:12 Bijien hhezighan goyane jieshao giesan kunghala ulie bilane. Hhela goyane goya nanjizho, goyane goya bilazho, hhela men no wo.
2CO 10:13 Bijienyi kieliese bijien kuaise kamasene ulie daone. Zhao Huda bijiende nanjizhi ogisan kamaghala giene. Ene kama tai hhendeye kuruzho.
2CO 10:14 Bijien tai hhende echise kamasene daoku pusho. Shijishan bijien Mexihani gouxioxii lien tai hhendeye echizhi chonjizho.
2CO 10:15 Bijien kamasene ese daozhi kunlai khishulasanghala ese kuaizho. Bijien xiwon giese tai xianxin gieku fugiedakude tai dundadu bijienyi kamaye daghazhi hende fugiedase giezho.
2CO 10:16 Ingiese kunlai oronde kunla giesan wiliede ulie kuaizhi gouxioxini tanse chugo psedu oronlade chonjine giezho.
2CO 10:17 "Kien kuaise Ezhanyi kuai!"
2CO 10:18 Kaoyen giedene olusan kunshi goyane jieshao giesan pusho, Ezhan jieshao giesan wo.
2CO 11:1 Bi goujinie ben kun danlayema, ta rennai gie. Bi xiwon giese ta rennai gie.
2CO 11:2 Hudai dubilieku zhugheghala bi tande hende orezho. Bi tai nie zhanguijide boluwo. Ganjin oqin wo giezhi Mexihade ogiwo.
2CO 11:3 Moghei jienzhaghala Hhawai piendasan mutun ta Mexihade olusan zhenzhenji oreku zhughe widakuse bi ayizho.
2CO 11:4 Niezhan kunla irezhi bijien ese chonjisan da nie Ersai tande chonjise, pse ta jienliezhi ese daosan buxiantu ruhherni jienliezhi ta jieshou giezhi ese daosan buxiantu gouxioxii jieshou gieghase ta jienliezho!
2CO 11:5 Bi sumulase bi hhezighan famatu shitu wo giesanlase goujida bixin uwo.
2CO 11:6 Mii koucai hen uwoma, unhua boghoni uwo. Enei bijien gofanmiende olon banfaghala tande zhenmin giewo.
2CO 11:7 Bi tai undudaghane giezhi goyane boghonidaghazhi Hudai gouxioxii tande belien chonjise zui fanjizhou?
2CO 11:8 Bi psedu jiohuilase gunzi bareidene tande lilian khighase qianlakughala niekielien wo.
2CO 11:9 Bi tai hhende bikude made chaikude kiemade chijia ese teizho. Maqidunse iresan gaijiula made chaisei ogizhi kughazho. Bi gofanmiende goyane tande achan ese gholuzho, jianlaiye ulie gholune.
2CO 11:10 Yagaiya oronde bi ingiezhi kuaikui kiemada danla dane. Mii sudoro bisan Mexihai zhendaoi zhiizhi bi ingiezhi kielie shidane.
2CO 11:11 Yangiezhi? Bi tande ulie orenu? Bi orekui Huda mejiene.
2CO 11:12 Bi ede giesanne izhi giene. Ingiekushi goya kuaisan bijienre niekielien wo giesan hhezighan jihui ereisan kunlade jihuini siraghane giezho.
2CO 11:13 Hhe izhun kunlashi jia shitu wo, piendachen wiliechi wo, Mexihani shitu wo giezhi jiazhon giezho.
2CO 11:14 Ene hunerei uwo. Ibilisiye gieghantu qienxienni jiazhon giezho.
2CO 11:15 Ingiese Ibilisini hojilaye gundanni hoji jiazhon gieseye ghudure uwo. Hhelai jiego hhela giesan mutun gholune.
2CO 11:16 Bi pse kielieye, kiemada mii ben kun mutun bu uzhe. Ben kun mutun uzheliuzhe bi goyane goujinie kuaikui ta jienlie.
2CO 11:17 Bi ingiezhi kieliese Ezhanni qienlighala ese giezho, nie ben kun wo giezhi fugiede tunguliezho.
2CO 11:18 Olon kunla duyani biozhunghala kuaise biye kuaiye.
2CO 11:19 Ta zhenzhenji jienzha wo, bayasuzhi ben kunlai jienliezho!
2CO 11:20 Kien tai hoji danlaghazhi qianlazhi pienyi zhanjizhi meilade uzhezhi khizha jieretai eghise ta rennai giezho.
2CO 11:21 Bi ingiezhi kieliese shizhenema, bijien zholienshi qingiezhi gie dane. Ingieliuzhe kun yan shiqin jiere kuai shidase biye kuai shidane. Enei bi ben kun mutun kieliezho.
2CO 11:22 Hhelashi Xibolai kun onu? Biye enbene. Isilie kun onu? Biye enbene. Iburaheimuni houdei onu? Biye enbene.
2CO 11:23 Mexihani hoji onu? Bi ingie kieliese fenjiulizhoma, biye genjia enbene. Bi hhelase olon khishulazhi bafanzi olon souzhi olon mabienzi neizhi haojihui aminde wixien khizhezho.
2CO 11:24 Bi Yutai kunlase 39 gie mabienzi eghikui 5 hui neizho.
2CO 11:25 Mii banbanghala 3 hui eghizho, 1 hui tashidazho, hai jiere 3 hui zeinan penjizhi chon qida oluzho, 1 hui hai jiere niudu nie xii hheliezho.
2CO 11:26 Olonfa mo yokude moronni wixien, qiandaoni wixien, goya kunlai wixien, niman kunlai wixien, chenshii wixien, hontanni wixien, haini wixien, jia gaijiulani wixienyi penjizho.
2CO 11:27 Khishulazhi shouku giezho, olonfa hhuntura dazho, oliesuzhi undasuzho, olonfa ijiuni chaizho, gonjiezho, musiku jien uwo.
2CO 11:28 Psedulase chugo go jiohuilade zhughe chilazhi niudunie mii jiere achan daruzho.
2CO 11:29 Kien zholierese bi ulie zholierenu? Kien zui fanjise bi ulie jindanu?
2CO 11:30 Ijinyo kuaine giese bi zholiennine kuaine.
2CO 11:31 Ezhan Ersani ada Huda bi ghudan ese kieliesei mejiene. Hhei chanqi doulakui wo.
2CO 11:32 Bi Damashigede bikude Yalida honshanni kha douradu fugie noyen Damashige chenshini sagheighazhi mii bareine giezhoma,
2CO 11:33 kunla mii nie lanlande teidene chenqian jieredu chongunse jiuzhilie bouzheghase hhei khase andawo.
2CO 12:1 Kuaise yama haochu uwoma, bi ijinyo kuaine. Ede bi Ezhan made zhoujin mutun uzheghazhi mejieghasei kielieye.
