2CO 12:2 Bi Mexihai miende nie kunyi tanine. Hhei 14 nien qien ji 3 cen asiman jiere qila khireiwo. Beyere hhantu khireiwu beyese likai gie khireisei bi ulie mejiene, zinie Huda mejiene.
2CO 12:3 Bi intu kunyi tanine. Beyere hhantu khireiwu beyese likai gie khireisei bi ulie mejiene, zinie Huda mejiene.
2CO 12:4 Hhei qientande qila khireise kielie daku kielienyi sonosuwo. Enei kun kieliese ulie olukui wo.
2CO 12:5 Ene kunde oluzhi bi kuainema, goyadene oluzhi zholiennisene chugo yama ulie kuaine.
2CO 12:6 Bi kieliesanshi zhenni wo, ingiese bi kuaine gieliuzhe guazi pusho. Ingieliuzhe bi goyane ulie kuaine, pse kunla mase uzhezhi chenliesansene gofende mii uzhene.
2CO 12:7 Made uzheghasan tebie famashi bi goyane kondakuse ayizhi mii beye jiere nie eghesun teizho. Eneshi Ibilisi peisan wo, mii zayalazhi ese kondaghazho.
2CO 12:8 Ene shiqinde oluzhi bi Ezhande ene eghesunyi mii jierese widagha giezhi 3 hui xiahua giese
2CO 12:9 hhe made kieliewo, "Mii nenjien chade kuruzho. Mii nenli kunni zholienni jiere onqienshine." Ingiese bi goya zholiennine kuaikude hende xiqi bizhi Mexihani nenlii goya jierene huighane giezho.
2CO 12:10 Bi Mexihani yenyinde oluzhi zholien, shizheghaku, kunnan, heiku, chijia bikude bayasuzho. Bi yan shihoude zholienshi yan shihoude khidun wo.
2CO 12:11 Bi ene nie guazi kunshi ta biisan wo. Shijishan ta indan mii jieshao giekuni wo. Bi yama pushoma, hhezighan famatu shitu wo giesanlase goujida bixin uwo.
2CO 12:12 Bi tai dunda hende rennai giezhi ghudureqi, fugie shiqin, nenlitu shiqinni giezhi bishi shitu bikui zhenmin giewo.
2CO 12:13 Zinie bi tande achan ese danlasan ene shiqinse chugo bi tande psedu jiohuilase bixinde giezhou? Mii ene codasanyi ta rouliesha.
2CO 12:14 Ede bi zhunbei giezhi ji 3 hui tai hhende echine giezho. Tande yama achan ulie danlane, bi keresanshi tai dunxi pusho, tai zhughe wo. Kewosila ada anadene oluzhi baer cunjikui pusho, ada ana kesiladene oluzhi baer cunjikui wo.
2CO 12:15 Bi tande oluzhi bayasuzhi bisanlane ogizhi lien goyane man ogiku duran wine. Bi tande ye olon orese ta made ye choghon orenu?
2CO 12:16 Bi tande achan ese danlasei man mejiekui woma, niezhan kunla kieliese bishi nie jienzha kun wo, piendakughala tai bareizho giezho.
2CO 12:17 Bi tai hhende peizhi echighasan alinie kunyi tungo giezhi tai pienyi zhanjiwo?
2CO 12:18 Bi Qidoi tai hhende echighazhi hhere hhantu hhe nie gaijiui echighawo. Qido tai pienyi zhanjiwu? Bijien wilie giese nie zhugheghala ese giezhi nie korolonghala ese yozhou?
2CO 12:19 Ta sumulase bijien izhi tai melie goyane huizho giezhou? Bijien Mexihai miende Hudai melie kieliezho. Mii orentula, bijien giesanlashi man tai hendaghane giezho.
2CO 12:20 Bi echikude bi xiwon giesande ta ese daizhi ta xiwon giesande bi ese daisei mejiekuse ayizho. Zhenjinduku, dubilieku, piqi shuaiku, goyadene oluku, sugieku, xienhua kielieku, goyane undude uzheku, londaku shiqin winekuse ayizho.
2CO 12:21 Bi pse echikude bi zunjisan Huda tai melie mii shizheghakuse ayizho. Eqighandei olon kunla zui fanjizhi zannanni giezhi lon kijiezhi hu giedene ulie geisande bi nango giekuse ayizho.
2CO 13:1 Eneshi bi ji 3 hui tai hhende echine giezho. Ingiese "jien zhasan shiqinlai ghua, ghuran kunni ganzhenghala shidaghane".
2CO 13:2 Bi ji 2 hui tai hhende irekude hhezighan melieshida zui fanjisan kunji psedu soyuji kunlade jingao giezhi daosan mutun ede bi tai hhende uwokude pse jingao gieye, bi pse irese jiedui ulie rouliene.
2CO 13:3 Ingiekushi Mexiha mii tungo giezhi kieliesan zhenjini ta ereizho. Mexiha tande zholiende ulie giene, khidunde giene.
2CO 13:4 Hhei zholiennii yenyinzhe shizijia jiere ghada fugughawoma, Hudai nenlighala amitu wo. Bijien hhere hhantu zholien woma, tai hhende echikude Hudai nenlighala hhere hhantu amiturane.
2CO 13:5 Ta xinyan dunda udu daozhoye giezhi goyane jiencha gie. Goyane nie kaoyen gie. Ersa Mexiha tai sudoro bikui ta ulie mejienu? Enei mejie dase ta kaoyen giezhi dao dazho.
2CO 13:6 Bi xiwon giese bijien kaoyen giezhi daokui ta mejiene.
2CO 13:7 Bijien Hudase onxian giezhi tai yama codasei ulie gieghane. Bijien kaoyen giezhi daokui uzheghaku pusho. Kunla uzhese bijien shibai gieliuzhe tai gounii gieghane giezho.
2CO 13:8 Bijien yan shiqindeliuzhe zhendaoni duizhi gie dane, hhende oluzhi giene.
2CO 13:9 Bijien zholien bizhi ta khidun bikude bijien bayasuzho. Ta onqientu gholu giezhi bijien ingiezhi onxian giezho.
2CO 13:10 Ingiese bi tai hhende wikude ene kielienyi tande huaikushi bi tai chanlakudei zhao Ezhan made ogisan qienlighala tande gundude ulie giene giezho. Ene qienli kunni bixindaghaku pusho, hendaghaku wo.
2CO 13:11 Gaijiula, zuihoude kielieye, ta bayasundu. Onqientu kun gholuzhi bijien surughasei chenlie. Maodun bu khizhezhi heqishi. Ingiese oreku winetu, pinnantu Huda chan tanre hhantu wo.
2CO 13:12 Ta zhughesene nieniedene kielien asa. Shentula man tande kielien asazho.
2CO 13:13 Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjien, Hudai oreku, Shenlinni laiwon gieku chan tanre hhantu bi gie!
GAL 1:1 Shitu danlasan bi Baolo xin huaizho. Bi shitu danlakushi kun peisan pusho, kunni tungo giesanye pusho, Ersa Mexiha pse hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Ada Hudai tungo giezhi peisan wo.
GAL 1:2 Bi mare hhantulasan gaijiularene man Jialataini jiohuilade kielien asaye.
GAL 1:3 Mai Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
GAL 1:4 Huda mai Adai isighala Mexiha ene doghun duyase mai andaghane giezhi mai zuide oluzhi goyane sheiwo.
GAL 1:5 Kuaikui chanqi izhi Hudade ogi. Amine!
GAL 1:6 Mexihani nenjienyi tungo giezhi tai urusan Hudase ta deigo likai giedene psedu gouxioxini daghase bi ghanirazho.
GAL 1:7 Shijishan psedu gouxioxi uwo, niezhan kunla tai londaghazhi Mexihani gouxioxii geine giezho.
GAL 1:8 Bugon bijien, asiman jierese iresan qienxienliuzhe bijien tande chonjisan gouxioxii buxiantui chonjise hhei indan kharakui wo.
GAL 1:9 Bijien melieshida kieliezhi daozho, ede bi pse kielieye. Kienliuzhe ta jienliesan gouxioxii buxiantui tande chonjise hhei indan kharakui wo.
GAL 1:10 Ede bi kunlai kuaighanu, Hudai kuaighane? Bi kunlai bayasughane giezhou? Bi dou kunlai bayasughane giese bishi Mexihani hoji pusho.
GAL 1:11 Gaijiula, bi chonjisan gouxioxishi kunse iresan pusho bikui ta mejie.
GAL 1:12 Hheshi bi kunlase jienliesan pusho, kunla sughasanye pusho, Ersa Mexiha mejieghasan wo.
GAL 1:13 Bi melieshida Yutaijiode matugie udu daosanyi ta chenliezhi daozho. Bi Hudai jiohuini hende heizhi widaghane giezho.
GAL 1:14 Yutaijio fanmiende bi goya minzune nie nasuntu kunlase zui fama wo, mii xienrenla zunjisan xigonde zui rexin wo.
GAL 1:15 Ingiezhoma, Huda nenjienghalane mii oluku melie sunghuzhi urudene
GAL 1:16 niman kunlade Ersai chonjighane giezhi kewonne made bayasuzhi uzheghazho. Ingiekude bi kunlare shanlian ese gie,
GAL 1:17 mase melie shitu danlasan kunlade asane giezhi Yelusalende ese khirei, deigo Alabode echidene pse Damashigede khareiwo.
GAL 1:18 Ingie 3 nien daodene bi Yelusalende khirei, Jifai tani, hhere hhantu 15 qien souwo.
GAL 1:19 Zinie Ezhanyi jiuni Yagebuse chugo psedu shitulai nieda ese chanlawo.
GAL 1:20 Bi tande huaisanshi man shuhua wo. Bi Hudai melie ghudan ulie kieliene.
GAL 1:21 Khuinashi bi Xiliya, Jilijia oronde echiwo.
GAL 1:22 Hhe xienzide Mexihai xianxin giesan Yudayani jiohuila mii chanlazhi ese daozho.
GAL 1:23 Hhela zinie melieshida mai heisan kun ede hhe melieshida widaghane giesan xinyanni chonjizho giesei chenliedene
GAL 1:24 mii yenyin jiere Hudai kuaizho.
GAL 2:1 14 nien daodene bi Banabaghala Qidoi uduru pse Yelusalende khireiwo.
GAL 2:2 Bi khireikushi Huda made mejieghazho. Bi hhezighan lindaolai konkonji chujieghedene bi niman kunlade gouxioxi chonjisei kieliezhi minbai olughakushi bi melieshida, ede belien ese holuse giezho.
GAL 2:3 Mare hhantu echisan Qidoshi Xila kun woma, hhei biizhi hetoune ese gieghazho.
GAL 2:4 Enei kieliekushi niezhan jia gaijiula ghulazhi orozhedene konkonji Mexiha Ersai miendedu bijienyi ziyui uzhedene bijienyi hoji danlaghane giezho.
GAL 2:5 Bijien gouxioxini zhendaoi tai dunda beighane giezhi hhelade goujida ese ranjiwo.
GAL 2:6 Hhezighan lindao danlasanla bi chonjisan daolide yama ese jiaizho. Hhela eqighandei yan kun bikui made yama zoin uwo, Huda mienzighala ulie uzhene.
GAL 2:7 Khareidene Huda Bedurude hetoune giesan kunlade gouxioxini chonjiku renwuni ogiku mutun madeye hetoune ese giesan kunlade chonjiku renwui ogisei hhela uzhe khizhewo.
GAL 2:8 Bedurui sudoro wilie giezhi hhei hetoune giesan kunlade shitu danlaghasan hhe mii sudoroye wilie giezhi mii niman kunlade shitu danlaghawo.
GAL 2:9 Jiohuini tuhuade sanasan Yagebu, Jifa, Yaheiya enela Huda made ogisan nenjienyi chenren giedene bi Banabaghalade borun khane ogizhi lienshou gholu, bijien niman kunlai dunda echi, hhela hetoune giesan kunlai dunda echikui tunyi oluwo.
GAL 2:10 Hhela zinie bijienyi yoqiu giezhi nanxin kunlai jilazhi banman gie giezho. Ene shiqinyi yenlai bi xiacha giezhi giezho.
GAL 2:11 Khuinashi JifaAnqiyade irekude ulie giekui giese bi danmien hhei fandui giewo.
GAL 2:12 Yagebui hhense irechen kunla ese kuzhekude Jifa niman kunlare hhantu ijiezho. Hhela irese ijinyo hetoune gie giesan Yutaini Mexihai xianxin giesan kunlase ayidene tui gholodowo.
GAL 2:13 Psedu Yutai kunla hhei daghazhi jiazhon giezho, lien Banabaye shandan giedene hhelai daghazhi jiazhon giezho.
GAL 2:14 Bi chanlase hhelai giesan gouxioxini zhendaoghala buxianshi dajialai melie Jifade kieliewo, "Chishi nie Yutai kun bidene Yutai kunnughunyi ulie daghadene niman kunnughunyi daghase matugie niman kunlai biizhi Yutai kunnughunyi daghaghane?"
GAL 2:15 Matanshi nangha pusho, olusanse Yutai kun enbene.
GAL 2:16 Kunyi gounide sanakushi guijinni zunjikughala pusho, Ersa Mexihani xianxin giekughala bikui matan mejiene. Matanye Mexiha Ersai xianxin giekushi guijinni zunjikughala pusho, Mexihai xianxin giekughala gounide sanaghaku wo. Kiemada guijinni zunjizhi gounide sanasei uwo.
GAL 2:17 Matan Mexihai tungo giezhi gounide sanaghane giedene goyaneye zuiren gholuse Mexihashi mai zui fanjighachen onu? Kenjin pusho!
GAL 2:18 Bi cheisanne pse erchan giese goyaneshi zuiren bikui zhenmin giewo.
GAL 2:19 Bi guijinni tungo giezhi guijinse fugudene Hudade amiturawo.
GAL 2:20 Bi Mexihaghalai hhantu shizijia jiere ijin ghadawo. Ede amiturasanshi bi pusho, Mexiha mii sudoro amiturazho. Bi beye jiere amiturasanshi made orezhi made oluzhi goyane sheisan Hudai kewonni xianxin giesanghala amiturazho.
GAL 2:21 Bi Hudai nenjienyi ulie widaghane. Guijinni tungo giezhi gundanni irezhoshi Mexiha belien duya ijiewo.
GAL 3:1 Jialataini guazi kunlaya! Kien tai miiwo? Ersa Mexihani shizijia jiere ghadazhi qinchude tai melie beilawo.
GAL 3:2 Bi tande jianie shiqin asaye, ta Shenlinni jienliesanshi guijinni zunjikughala onu gouxioxini sonosudene xianxin giekughala wo?
GAL 3:3 Ta Shenlinghala kaishi giedene beyeghala jieshu olughanu? Tashi intu guazi onu?
GAL 3:4 Ta imeghei shouku giesanshi belienni onu? Bebelieghanji onu?
GAL 3:5 Huda tande Shenlinni ogizhi tai dunda nenlitu shiqin giesanshi ta guijinni zunjikughala onu gouxioxini sonosudene xianxin giekughala wo?
GAL 3:6 Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Iburaheimu Hudai xianxin giedene Huda hhei gounide sanazho."
GAL 3:7 Ingiese xianxin giesanlashi Iburaheimui houdei bikui ta mejie.
GAL 3:8 Niman kunlai xianxin giekughala Huda gounide sanakui jinwun jiere melie kieliezho. Ingie eqighanse Iburaheimude gouxioxini chonjizhi kieliezho, "Chii tungo giezhi soyuji minzulade fuqi irene."
GAL 3:9 Ingiese xianxin giesan kunla xianxin giesan Iburaheimure hhantu fuqi jienliene.
GAL 3:10 Guijinni zunjikude kouisan kunla man kharaku doura wo. Jinwun jiere jilasan mutun, "Guijinshu jiere jilasanlai man ulie zunjizhi ulie giesanlai man kharane."
GAL 3:11 Guijinni kouizhi kiemai Hudai melie gounide sana daku qinchu wo. Jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Gou kun xianxin giekughala amiturane."
GAL 3:12 Guijin xianxin giekughala buxian wo. Jinwun jiere kieliesan mutun, "Guijinni zunjisan kunla guijinni kouizhi amiturane."
GAL 3:13 Jien mutun jiere gualasanlai kharane giezhi jinwun jiere jilasan mutun Mexiha matande oluzhi kharakui shouizhi guijinni kharakuse matai shuiwo.
GAL 3:14 Ingiedene Iburaheimude ogisan fuqi Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi niman kunlade kuruwo, matan xianxin giekui tungo giezhi dain giesan Shenlinni jienliewo.
GAL 3:15 Gaijiula, bi nie pinchanku bifanyi kielieye. Kun kielien yenjise kiema widagha daji jiai dane.
GAL 3:16 Huda Iburaheimu, hhei houdeide dain giekude olon kunyi zhiizhi chii houdeila giezhi ese kieliedene niekozii zhiizhi chii houdei giezho. Hheshi Mexiha wo.
GAL 3:17 Mii isishi ingiezho. 430 nien daodene iresan guijin melieshida Huda yenjisei widagha dazhi dain giesei widagha dane.
GAL 3:18 Hudai jiachan guijinse irezhoshi dain giesanse ese irezho, ingieliuzhe Huda Iburaheimude dain giesei tungo giezhi ogizho.
GAL 3:19 Qinse guijinshi yan wo? Guijinshi Iburaheimude dain giesan houdei iretula zuini mejieghane giezhi jiaisan wo. Guijinshi qienxienlai tungo giezhi dundadu kunyi khai jingo giezhi jinjisan wo.
GAL 3:20 Dundadu kunshi shonfanmienyi daibio giezhoma, Hudashi nie wo.
GAL 3:21 Ingiese guijin Hudai dain giesanghala zodui giezhou? Kenjin uye! Amin ireghaku guijinni ogizhoshi kunla hhei tungo giezhi gounide sanawo.
GAL 3:22 Ingiezhoma, soyuji kunlai zuide qienji jiezho giezhi jinwun jiere kieliezho. Ingiedene Ersa Mexihai xianxin giezhi iresan dainni xianxin giesan kunlade ogizho.
GAL 3:23 Xianxin gieku iretula matai guijin doura khazhi xianxin gieku xienjizhi khizhetula uzhezho.
GAL 3:24 Ingiese guijinshi Mexiha iretula mai uduruku loushi wo. Ingiedene xianxin giekughala mai gounide sanaghazho.
GAL 3:25 Ede xianxin gieku irese matan hhe uduruku loushii doura uwo.
GAL 3:26 Ta man Mexiha Ersai xianxin giekughala Hudai kewosi gholuwo.
GAL 3:27 Xilii jienliezhi Mexihare hhantulasan ta man jierene Mexihai musizho.
GAL 3:28 Ta Mexiha Ersai miende man nie wo. Yutai kun, niman kun, ziyutu kun, hoji, ere kun, eme kunla yama chabie uwo.
GAL 3:29 Tashi Mexihanughunshi Iburaheimui houdei wo, dain giesanzhe caichanni jienliechen wo.
GAL 4:1 Bi kieliese jiachanshi man jienliechennughun woma, hhe kewosi xienzide hojilare yama chabie uwo.
GAL 4:2 Adani jinjisan shihou kuzhetula hhe izhi qiezhechen kun, gonjisan kunyi doura wo.
GAL 4:3 Matanye niekielien wo. Matan kewosi bikude ene duyani langan daoli matai gonjizhoma,
GAL 4:4 shihou onqienji kuzhese Huda kewonne peizhi eme kunyi tungo giezhi guijin doura ireghadene
GAL 4:5 guijin douradu kunlai shuizhi khizhe matande kewosi danlaku qienlii ogiwo.
GAL 4:6 Tashi kewosi wo, Huda Kewonne ruhherni peizhi mai zhughede teise matan Hudai Aba! Ada giezhi urune.
GAL 4:7 Ingiese chishi pse hoji pusho, kewon wo. Kewon enbese Huda renjisan jiachanyi jienliechen enbene.
GAL 4:8 Eqighandei ta Hudai tani dakude hhezighan yenlai Huda pushotulade hoji danlazhoma,
GAL 4:9 ede ta Hudai tanine, pse tashi Huda tanisan wo. Ta matugie pse hhezighan yama zoin witu bixin langan daolide hoji danlane giezhi daghazho?
GAL 4:10 Ta udu, sara, jieqi, nienjienni chigharade zunjizho.
GAL 4:11 Ingiese bi tande zhughe chilazhi khishulasan belien gholukuse ayizho.
GAL 4:12 Gaijiula, bi tai xiahua gieye, bi ta mutun gholusan mutun taye bi mutun gholu. Ta mii ese kuighazho.
GAL 4:13 Ta mejiene, bi giemerekuzhe caigie tande tou 1 hui gouxioxi chonjiwo.
GAL 4:14 Beyemi tande achan ogiwoma, ingieliuzhe ta mii gajide ese uzhezhi ese duisadene kharei Hudai qienxien mutun, Mexiha Ersa mutun jienliewo.
GAL 4:15 Hhe xienzide ta hende bayasusan ede khala echiwo? Hhe xienzide ta nudunne waidene made ogiku duran bikui bi tande ganzhen bei shidane.
GAL 4:16 Ede bi tande zhendaoi kieliese tai duitou gholuwu?
GAL 4:17 Hhezighan kunla tande rexinde giezhoma, zhughedeni gou muji uwo. Tai mase gholodoghazhi goyadene rexinde gieghane giezho.
GAL 4:18 Gou mujighala tande rexinde giese gou wo. Enei zinie bi tai hhende bikude gieku pusho, chanqi giese olune.
GAL 4:19 Mii kesilaya, Mexihai yanzi tai sudoro gholutula bi tande oluzhi pse kewosi oluku kui shouizho.
GAL 4:20 Bi ede tanre hhantulane giezhi kouqine bienjighadene goude kieliekui hende duralakushi tande oluzhi zhughedemi nanran uwo.
GAL 4:21 Ta enezighan guijinni shunjine giesan kunla, made nie kielie, guijinde matui kieliesei ta ulie mejienu?
GAL 4:22 Jinwun jiere huaizho, Iburaheimude ghua kewon wo. Nieshi hoji bierei olusan wo. Nieshi ziyu bierei olusan wo.
GAL 4:23 Hoji bierei olusanshi beyei kouizhi oluzho, ziyu bierei olusanshi dain giesei kouizhi oluzho.
GAL 4:24 Eneshi bifan wo. Ghua biereishi ghua yenjisan kielien wo. Nie biereishi Hhazhire wo, Xinaishanse irezhi olusan kesilashi hoji wo.
GAL 4:25 HhazhireAlaboni Xinaishanni daibio giezho, edeku Yelusalenghala niekielien wo. Hhe kesilarene manshi hoji wo.
GAL 4:26 Da nie biereishi asiman jieredu Yelusalenni daibio giezho. Hhe ziyu wo, matai ana wo.
GAL 4:27 Jinwun jiere huaizho, "Kewosi olu dachen, kewosi witu bierei, chi bayasu! Kewosi olusan tendunni ese shouisan bierei, chi bayasuzhi jiuli! Zhanguiji witu biereini kesila zhanguiji bisan biereini kesilase olon wo!"
GAL 4:28 Gaijiula, tashi Isaghei mutun Huda dain giedene iresan kewosi wo.
GAL 4:29 Hhe shihoude beyese olusan Shenlinse olusei heizho. Edeye niekielien wo.
GAL 4:30 Ingiezhoma jinwun jiere matugie kieliezho? Hoji biereiji hhei kewonni tou khireigha. Hoji biereini kewon ziyu biereini kewonghala hhantu jiachanni jienliese ulie olune giezho.
GAL 4:31 Gaijiula, ingiese matanshi hoji biereini kewosi pusho, ziyu biereini kewosi wo.
GAL 5:1 Mexiha matanyi ziyude oluzhi matanyi andaghawo. Ingiese ta beizhi undanla. Hojini jiaban tai pse kunzhi bu gie gie.
GAL 5:2 Ta chenliendu, bi Baolo tande goude kielieye. Ta hetoude kouise Mexiha tande yama haochu uwo.
GAL 5:3 Bi pse jien hetoune giesan kunlade jingao gieye. Tande guijinni man zunjiku zheren wine.
GAL 5:4 Ta enezighan guijinni kouizhi gounide sanane giesanla, Mexihaghala gonxi widazhi nenjiense likai giewo.
GAL 5:5 Bijien Shenlinde kouizhi xianxin giekughala gounide sanakui panjizhi sagheizho.
GAL 5:6 Mexiha Ersai miende hetoune gie, ulie gie yama zhunyo uwo. Zhunyonishi orekughala khizhesan xianxin gieku wo.
GAL 5:7 Ta izhi giesan gou woma, ede ta zhendaoni shunjikui kien duiwo?
GAL 5:8 Ingiezhi surughasanshi tai urusan hhe pusho.
GAL 5:9 Goujinie kunieghe nie duizi ghurunyi faighane.
GAL 5:10 Ta pseshikui ulie sumulakui bi Ezhanyi miende hende xianxin giezhoma, kien tai daolon giese hhei faine.
GAL 5:11 Gaijiula, bi izhigie hetoune giekui chonjizhoshi mii yangiezhi dou heine? Qingiezhoshi shizijia kunni hokurughaku widawo.
GAL 5:12 Bi xiwon giese tai daolon giesanla goyane atala gie!
GAL 5:13 Gaijiula, tai ziyude uruzhoma, ene ziyuni nefuxin gieku jihui bu gholughadene nieniene oreku zhugheghala ushila.
GAL 5:14 Soyuji guijin man goyadene mutun giebeidene ore giesan ene nie aman kieliende bouizho.
GAL 5:15 Ta xioxin giezhi nieniene bu zhouzhi bu yenji, pse man widane.
GAL 5:16 Bi kielieye, ta Shenlinni daghazhi gie, ingiese beyeni nefuxinni ulie giene.
GAL 5:17 Beyeni nefuxin Shenlinghala zodui giezho, Shenlinye beyeghala zodui giezho. Ene ghuala nieniene zodui giezhi ta duralasan shiqinni ulie gieghane.
GAL 5:18 Tai Shenlin uduruse guijin doura uwo.
GAL 5:19 Beye giekulai minminji mejiene, lon kijieku, zannanni, hu gieku,
GAL 5:20 nigiedai beiiku, fashu shuaiku, chou bareiku, zhenjinduku, henjiku, piqi shuaiku, zinie goyane guiku, danlinraku, danpai gholughaku,
GAL 5:21 dubilieku, jiu ochi sudoku, nouiku, pse intu shiqinla wo. Bi eqighanse tande jingao giesan mutun ede pse tande jingao gieye. Enezighan shiqinlani giesan kunla Hudai gojiai jienlie dane.
GAL 5:22 Shenlinni jiegoshi, oreku, bayasuku, pinnan, rennai, goude gieku, gou zhughe, kekaoni,
GAL 5:23 renyi, goyane kunzhi gieku wo. Intu shiqinlai guijin gonji dane.
GAL 5:24 Mexiha Ersani kunla beyeji nefuxin gieku duranne hhantu shizijia jiere ghadawo.
GAL 5:25 Matan Shenlinni kouizhi udu daose Shenlinni kouizhi giekuni wo.
GAL 5:26 Matan goyane undude bu uzhezhi nieniene bu hokughazhi nieniene bu dubilieye.
GAL 6:1 Gaijiula, nie kun zui fanjise ta Shenlini kouisan kunla renyitu zhugheghala hhei khareizhi daozhegha. Pse goyane miikui xioxin gie.
GAL 6:2 Ta nieniene achanyi banjizhi danjindu. Ingiezhi giese Mexihani guijinni chengun olughane.
GAL 6:3 Kun yama pushodene goyane hen wo giese goyane piendazho.
GAL 6:4 Jien kun goya giesan wilielane jiencha gie, ingiese bayasuku zinie goyade wo, kunlade uwo.
GAL 6:5 Jien kun goya zherenne goya danji.
GAL 6:6 Hudai kielienyi surusan kun surughasan kunde goude dunxilai man ogikuni wo.
GAL 6:7 Goyane bu pienda, Hudai meilade bu uzhe. Kun tareisanshi yan woshi ghurasanshi yan wo.
GAL 6:8 Zuitu beyene shunjizhi tareise zuitu beyese qida olukui ghurane, Shenlinni shunjizhi tareise Shenlinse chanqiku amin ghurane.
GAL 6:9 Matan gouni giekude fanqi bu giezhi zhazhen giema, heshitu shihou kuzhese ghurakui wine.
GAL 6:10 Ingiese matande jihui bikude dajialade gouni giekui wo, xianxin giesan nie gie kunlade genjia ingiezhi giekui wo.
GAL 6:11 Uzhe, bi qinsi tande huaisan uru matu fugie wo.
GAL 6:12 Hhezighan mienzii kuaichen kunla tai biizhi hetoune gieghakushi zinie Mexihani shizijiai yenyin jiere heikuse ayizho.
GAL 6:13 Hhezighan hetoune giesan kunla goyalane guijinni ulie zunjidene tai hetoune gieghakushi tai beyei tungo giezhi goyane kuaine giezho.
GAL 6:14 Bi zinie matai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani shizijiase chugo psedulai ulie kuaisejiu. Shizijiai tungo giezhi bi fugusan mutun duyare gonxi widazho. Duyaye fugusan mutun mare gonxi widazho.
GAL 6:15 Hetoune gie, ulie gie yama zhunyo uwo. Zhunyonishi shini kun wo.
GAL 6:16 Jien ene daoli mutun giesan kunlade, Hudai Isilie bexinlade Huda pinnan, ubali xiikui ogi gie!
GAL 6:17 Enedu khuinase kiemada mii jiohoro bu gie, mii jiere Ersani hou wine.
GAL 6:18 Gaijiula, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjien tai zhughede bisejiu. Amine!
EPH 1:1 Hudai isighala Mexiha Ersade shitu danlasan BaoloIfusoni Mexiha Ersai shixinji daghasan shentulade xin huaizho.
EPH 1:2 Mai ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien pinnan ogi gie!
EPH 1:3 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani ada Hudai kuaindu. Hhe Mexihai miende matande asiman jiereshiku yanyanji ruhhertu gounii ogizho.
EPH 1:4 Duyai zhayaghaku melie orekughala Mexihai miende matai sunghuzhi goyane melie zhiguishighazhi jienjien witui gholughane giezho.
EPH 1:5 Goya isighalane bayasuzhi Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi matai goyane kewosi danlaghakui eqie jinjiwo.
EPH 1:6 Oresan kewonne nenjienghalane matande belien ogiwo. Ingiese Hudai famatu nenjienni matai kuaighane giezho.
EPH 1:7 Mexihai miende fugie nenjienghalane Kewonne chusunyi jiageghala matai shuizhi codasanni mienliewo.
EPH 1:8 Ene nenjienyi soyuji agheli cunminghala hhantu matande pojiezhi olon ogiwo.
EPH 1:9 Matande jihuane mimii mejieghawo. Eneshi Hudai gou duran wo. Mexihai miende chenjighane giesan wo.
EPH 1:10 Ene jihuashi shihou kurukude asiman, zemin jieredu yanyanjilai man Mexihai miende hhantulaghane.
EPH 1:11 Pse matan Mexihai miende nexianyi jienliewo. Eneshi duranghalane yanniliuzhe giesan Huda goya jihuaghalane eqie jinjisan wo.
EPH 1:12 Ingiekushi bijien zui melieshida xiwonni Mexihai jiere teisan Yutai kunlai Hudai famani kuaighane giezho.
EPH 1:13 Taye zhenzhenji daoli, jiushi tai jiuiku gouxioxii chenliedene Mexihani xianxin giese Huda dain giesan Shenlinni tande ogizhi zhanzi taiwo.
EPH 1:14 Ene Shenlinshi matan jiachanni jienlieku yajin wo, matai shuizhi Hudai bexin gholughane, hhei famani kuaighane.
EPH 1:15 Ingiese ta Ezhan Ersai xianxin giezhi soyuji shentulade oresei bi chenliedene
EPH 1:16 onxian giekude tai jilazhi ese beidene tande oluzhi Hudade mafan kieliezho.
EPH 1:17 Bi tande mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai Huda, famatu Ada aghelitu ruhher pse mejieghaku ruhherni tande ogizhi ta hhei tani,
EPH 1:18 tai zhugheni nudunlai gieghereghazhi hhe tai uruzhi iresan xiwonshi yan bikui, pse shentulai dundadu hhei famatu jiachan matu olon bikui ta mejie,
EPH 1:19 pse Huda fugie lilianghalane matan xianxin giesan kunlade xienjighasan hhei nenli matu fugie bikui mejie giezhi onxian giezho. Ene nenlishi
EPH 1:20 Mexihai jiere giesan tebieji fugie lilian wo. Hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughazhi asiman jiere goya borun miendene soughazhi
EPH 1:21 yanyanji gonjisan, qienli bareisan, nenlitu, lindao danlasan, zinie edeku pusho, houshidedu yan nierelase da famashighawo.
EPH 1:22 Pse soyujilai Mexihai kon doura teizhi hhei jiohuini qiorun danlaghadene soyujilai gonjighazho.
EPH 1:23 Jiohuishi hhei beye wo. Soyujilai dunda soyujilai hulunshighasan Mexiha jiohuini hulunshighazho.
EPH 2:1 Eqighandei ta codasan dunda zui dundane fuguzho.
EPH 2:2 Hhe shihoude ta ene duyai xigonyi daghazhi asimanyi doghun lilianyi gonjisan hhei daghazhi zui dunda udu daozho. Hhe jiushi kielienyi ulie chenliechen kunlai sudoro wilie giesan ruhher wo.
EPH 2:3 Eqighandei matan man hhela mutun mai beyei nefuxinyi daghazhi udu daozho. Zui gieku duran, sumuladanni daghazhi giezho. Matan kunlare niekielien wo, olu bouzheghase Huda faichen kun wo.
EPH 2:4 Ingieliuzhe Hudade olon ubali xiiku wine, hhe matande oresan fugie orekughala
EPH 2:5 matan codasan dunda fugukudeni matanyi Mexihare hhantu aminne olughawo. Tai jiuikushi nenjienghala wo.
EPH 2:6 Mexiha Ersai miende matanyi Mexihare hhantu aminne olughadene asiman jiere hhere hhantu soughawo.
EPH 2:7 Ingiezhi giekushi Mexiha Ersai miende matande renyide ogisan hhei nenjien zhenzhen olon bikui jianlaiku kunlade man uzheghane giezho.
EPH 2:8 Tai jiuikushi nenjienghala wo, xianxin giedene jiuiwo. Eneshi goyase iresan pusho, Huda ogisan mure wo.
EPH 2:9 Giekughala pusho, pse goyane kuaine.
EPH 2:10 Matanshi Huda giesan wo, gou wilie gieghane giezhi Mexiha Ersai miende zhayaghasan wo. Eneshi Huda matande matugie udu dao giezhi eqighan jihua gie goudaghasan wo.
EPH 2:11 Ingiese ta jila, beyeghala kieliese eqighandei tashi niman kun wo. Hhezighan beye jiere kunni khaghala hetoune giesan kunla tai hetoune ese giesan kun giezhi uruzho.
EPH 2:12 Hhe shihoude tande Mexiha uwo, Isilie kun ese danlaghazho, Huda yenjisan kielienghala gonxi uwo, duyade yama xiwon uwo, Hudaye uwo.
EPH 2:13 Eqighandei Hudase gholodosan ta ede Mexiha Ersai miende hhei chusunde kouizhi Hudare chadashiwo.
EPH 2:14 Mexihashi matanyi heqishighachen wo. Hhe beyene fugughazhi Yutai kun niman kunyi dundadu danni unaghazhi chouni widaghawo.
EPH 2:15 Yutai kunni guijinni minlin, kuichenlai widaghadene goyane sudoro Yutai kun, niman kun ghualai nie shini kun gholughazhi heqishighawo.
EPH 2:16 Shizijiai tungo giezhi chouni widaghazhi ghualai nie beye gholughadene Hudare goudaghawo.
EPH 2:17 Da iredene heqishighaku gouxioxii ta gholodedu niman kunlade chonjizhi ogiwo, chadadedu Yutai kunladeye chonjizhi ogiwo.
EPH 2:18 Ingiedene Mexihai tungo giezhi matan man nie Shenlinghala Hudai shida echi shidane.
EPH 2:19 Ingiese ede tashi niman kun, wigo kun pusho, shentulare nie gojia kun gholuzhi mechini kun wo.
EPH 2:20 Tashi shitu, xienzhilani jichu jiere beighasan gie wo, Mexiha goyaneshi gieni jichu tashi wo.
EPH 2:21 Mexihai kouizhi nie gie man lienjidene fugiedazhi Ezhanni zhiguitu dajien gholuzho.
EPH 2:22 Mexihai kouizhi taiye hhantu beighazho. Ene gieshi Huda Shenlinyi tungo giezhi souku oron wo.
EPH 3:1 Ingiese Mexiha Ersai yenyinghala ta niman kunlade oluzhi bafanzi sousan bi Baolo tande oluzhi onxian giezho.
EPH 3:2 Huda tande oluzhi nenjienghalane made nie tebieji renwu ogisei ta kenjin chenliezhi daozho.
EPH 3:3 Huda mimii made qinsi mejieghawo. Enei bi eqighandei jiendanghan huaizhi daozho.
EPH 3:4 Ta onshise bi Mexihani mimii dunjiresanyi mejiene.
EPH 3:5 Ene mimii isii Huda ede Shenlinyi tungo giezhi zhiguitu shitu, xienzhiladene mejieghasan mutun eqighanku xienzidedu kunde ese mejieghazho.
EPH 3:6 Ene mimishi niman kunla gouxioxii tungo giezhi Mexiha Ersai miende hhantu caichanyi jienliechen danlazhi nie beyeni iyanzi gholuzhi hhantu Huda dain giesanyi jienliene.
EPH 3:7 Hudai nenjienghala bi gouxioxide hoji danlazho. Huda nenlighalane made ene nenlini ogizho.
EPH 3:8 Shentulai dundadu zui ganise da gajitu made Huda nenjien ogizhi Mexihani mejiezhi baragha daku olonnii niman kunlade chonji giezho.
EPH 3:9 Pse soyujilai zhayaghasan Hudai sudoro eqighanse izhi niuighasan mimitu jihuai olon kunlade man minbai olugha giezho.
EPH 3:10 Ingiekushi ede jiohuii tungo giezhi asiman jiere gonjisan, qienli bareisanlade Hudai yanyanji aghelilai mejieghane giezho.
EPH 3:11 Eneshi mai Ezhan Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi gholusan Hudai chanqiku jihua wo.
EPH 3:12 Matan Mexiha Ersai sudoro hhei xianxin giezhi danzine fugiedaghazhi ulie inxin giedene Hudai melie echine.
EPH 3:13 Ingiese bi tai xiahua gieye, bi tande oluzhi shouku giewo giezhi yuchou bu gie. Eneshi tai kuaikui wo.
EPH 3:14 Ingiese bi Adai melie xiutuliezhi onxian giezho.
EPH 3:15 Hheshi asiman, zemin jieredu soyuji jiawulade man niere ogisan wo.
EPH 3:16 Hhe zhao goya olon fama, Shenlinne tungo giezhi tai sudorodu xianxin gieku zhugheni lilianghala khiduzhegha gie.
EPH 3:17 Xianxin giekughala Mexiha tai zhughede souzhi tai oreku dunda genzi bareighazhi undanlagha gie.
EPH 3:18 Ingie tande nenli bizhi soyuji shentulare Mexihani oreku matu aghui, fudu, undu, gun bikui goude mejieghadene
EPH 3:19 hhei oreku kunni sumulakuse daosanyi tande mejieghazhi Hudai hulunshighakughala tai hulunshigha gie.
EPH 3:20 Nenlini matanyi dunda ochirazhi matan xiahua giezhi sumulasanse pse olon chenjighasan Hudade
EPH 3:21 jiohui, Mexiha Ersai tungo giezhi zuzubeibei chanqi izhi kuaikui ogi. Amine!
EPH 4:1 Ingiese Ezhande oluzhi bafanzi sousan bi tai sidaghaye, ta yan giese zhao Huda tai urusan mutun gie.
EPH 4:2 Yandeliuzhe goyane meilade uzhezhi renyide gie. Rennai giezhi oreku zhugheghala nieniedene ranji.
EPH 4:3 Heqighala nieniene lienjizhi Shenlin tonjie gieghasanni xiacha giezhi barei.
EPH 4:4 Tai urukude nie xiwonde urusan mutun nie beye, nie Shenlin,
EPH 4:5 nie Ezhan, nie xianxin gieku, nie xili gieku,
EPH 4:6 nie Huda wo. Hheshi soyujilai ada wo, soyujilai jiere soyujilai dunda soyujilai sudoro wo.
EPH 4:7 Matan jien kunde Mexiha ghughazhi ogisan nenli wine.
EPH 4:8 Ingiese jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Hhe undude khireikude olon duitoulane barei khireiwo, kunlade nenlilai ogiwo."
EPH 4:9 Hhe khireiwo giezhi ene kielienshi yan isi wo? Hhe xien doura, jiushi zemin jiere bouzhesan pushonu?
EPH 4:10 Bouzhesan hheshi zui undu asimande khireisan Hhe wo. Ingiezhi giekushi soyujilai hulunshighane giezho.
EPH 4:11 Kun dunda niezhanlade shitu, xienzhi, gouxioxi chonjichen, mushi, loushi danlaku nenlini ogisanshi Mexiha wo.
EPH 4:12 Ingiezhi giekushi Mexihani wiliede oluzhi shentulai goude zhunbei gieghadene Mexihani beyeni hendaghane giezho.
EPH 4:13 Izhi ingiezhi giezhi matan dajiala Hudai kewonyi xianxin giezhi taniku jiere nie gholudene fugiedazhi Mexihani hulunnide daine.
EPH 4:14 Ingiese matan pse kewosi ulie danlazhi kunlai doghun muji, piendaku guijijighala yanyanji xiejioni inxianyi shouizhi eneman, hheman ulie gojioludene
EPH 4:15 oreku zhugheghala shuhua kieliezhi go fanmiende touzi danlasan Mexiha mutun hendane.
EPH 4:16 Mexihai kouizhi nie beyei sidasunla man chigharade lienjizho. Go iyanzi zoinlane khizheghazhi nie beyeni oreku dunda fugiedazhi hendaghazho.
EPH 4:17 Ingiese bi enei Ezhanni miende tande khidunde kielieye. Pse niman kunla mutun qingiezhi udu bu dao. Hhelai sumuladan yama oronde uwo,
EPH 4:18 zhugheni kharalazho. Hhela yama ulie mejiezhi zhughene khiduzheghase Huda ogisan aminse danlinrazho.
EPH 4:19 Hhela shizhekui mejie dazhi hu giedene nefuxinghala yanyanji zannanni giene.
EPH 4:20 Ta Mexihase surusanshi intui pusho.
EPH 4:21 Zhendao Ersai sudoro wo. Ta Ersa Mexihani chenliezhi hhense suruse
EPH 4:22 khuichen kunni teizhi eqighanku xigonlai widagha. Eneshi nefuxin miidene qida olusan wo.
EPH 4:23 Ta zhughe, sumulakune shinishighazhi
EPH 4:24 Hudai yanzi mutun zhenzhenji gundan, ganjinde zhayaghasan shini kunni musi.
EPH 4:25 Ingiese ta pse ghudan bu kielie. Jien kun kunlade shuhua kielie. Matanshi nie beye jieredu iyanzi wo.
EPH 4:26 Hokuse zui bu fanji, hokuzhi naran bu puda.
EPH 4:27 Pse Ibiliside jihui ogine.
EPH 4:28 Ghulachenla pse bu ghula. Goyade iresei nanxin kunlade ghughazhi ogine giezhi qinsi zhendande wilie gie.
EPH 4:29 Zannan kielienni nie amanda bu khizheghazhi heshide kunlade banjiku kielien kielie. Ingiese chenliesan kunde haochu wine.
EPH 4:30 Hudai Shenlinni yuchou bu giegha. Hhe shuiku udude oluzhi tai jiere hhei zhanzii taizho.
EPH 4:31 Yanyanji henjiku, piqi shuaiku, hokuku, nouiku, kufurei fanjiku, pse mouxiennilai man tai dundase widagha.
EPH 4:32 Huda Mexihai miende tai rouliesan mutun taye renyitu zhugheghala ubali xiizhi nieniene roulie.
EPH 5:1 Ingiese ta Hudai daghazhi suru, tashi Huda oresan kewosi wo.
EPH 5:2 Mexiha matande orezhi matande goyane sheidene Hudade ogisan andatu dunxi, mure danlazhi Hudade ogisan mutun taye yan giese oreku zhugheghala gie.
EPH 5:3 Lon kijieku, yanyanji zannanni gieku, tanxin giekulai tai dunda qiizhi da ulie olune. Shentula ingiezhi giese heshi uwo.
EPH 5:4 Shizheku kielien, hu kielieku kielien, zannan kielienlai bu kieliedene mafan gieku kielien kielie.
EPH 5:5 Ta goude mejie, lon kijiechen, zannanni giechen, tanxin giechenla Mexiha Hudaghalai gojiai jiachanni jienlie dane. Tanxin gieku nigiedade beiikughala niekielien wo.
EPH 5:6 Enezighan shiqin jiere Hudai hokuruku hhezighan kielien ulie chenliechen kunlai jiere irene. Yama oronde witu kielienghala kiema tai bu piendagha.
EPH 5:7 Ingiese ta hhelare bu hhantula.
EPH 5:8 Ta eqighandeishi kharani woma, edeshi Ezhanyi miende gon wo. Ta yan giese gonni kewosi mutun gie.
EPH 5:9 Gonni jiegoshi yanyanji gouni, gundanni, zhenni wo.
EPH 5:10 Ezhan bayasuku shiqinshi yan wo giezhi kaoyen gie.
EPH 5:11 Yama haochu witu, khara shiqin giesan kunlare bu hhantula, khareidene hhezighan shiqin giesan kunlai kheila.
EPH 5:12 Hhela beimiende giesan shiqinlai qiise ungien hularane.
EPH 5:13 Manlai chujiegheghasanshi gon wo. Gon dunda khizheghasanlai man chujieghene. Ingiese kieliezho, "Unturasan kunya, xierei! Fugusanse bosizhe, Mexiha chii zhouine."
EPH 5:15 Ingiese ta xioxin giezhi gie. Aghelitu kun mutun gie, ben kun mutun bu gie.
EPH 5:16 Jihuini goude barei, edeku gonyin doghun wo.
EPH 5:17 Ingiese ben kun bu danlazhi Ezhanni isishi yan bikui mejie.
EPH 5:18 Jiu ochizhi bu sudo, jiu kunni hu gieghane. Khareidene Shenlinghala goyane durugha.
EPH 5:19 Shige, zanmeige, ganjin donghala nieniedene doula. Zhughesene don giezhi Ezhande doula.
EPH 5:20 Yan shiqindeliuzhe mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani niereghala chan ada Hudade mafan kielie.
EPH 5:21 Mexihai zunjiku zhugheghala nieniene shunji.
EPH 5:22 Biereila, Ezhande shunjiku mutun zhanguijidene shunji.
EPH 5:23 Mexihashi jiohuini qiorun biku mutun zhanguijishi biereini qiorun wo. Mexihashi ene beye, jiushi jiohuini jiuichen wo.
EPH 5:24 Jiohui Mexihade matugie shunjiku mutun biereiye yandeliuzhe zhanguijidene qingiezhi shunji.
EPH 5:25 Zhanguijila, Mexiha jiohuide orezhi goyane sheisan mutun biereidene ore.
EPH 5:26 Hhe ingiezhi giekushi Hudai kielienyi tungo giezhi usughala jiohuini waghazhi zhiguishighadene
EPH 5:27 famashighazhi goyadene khughoghane giezho, yama zannan jienjien chuchutu intui wizhi zhiguitu yama maobin witui gholughane giezho.
EPH 5:28 Niekielien wo, zhanguijiye beyedene oreku mutun biereidene orekuni wo. Biereidene orese goyadene orezho.
EPH 5:29 Kiemada goya beyene henjichen kun uwo, kharei guizhunde zhaogu giezhi Mexiha jiohuini zhaogu giekughala niekielien wo.
EPH 5:30 Matanshi hhei beye jieredu iyanzi wo.
EPH 5:31 "Ingiese kun ada anasene likai giedene biereighalane hhantulazhi ghuala nie beye gholune."
EPH 5:32 Eneshi fugie mimi wo. Bi Mexiha, jiohuighalai zhiizhi kieliezho.
EPH 5:33 Ingieliuzhe ta jien kunlaye goyadene oreku mutun biereidene ore. Biereiye zhanguijine zunji.
EPH 6:1 Kewosila, Ezhanyi miende ada ananughunne chenlie. Eneshi indanji wo.
EPH 6:2 "Ada anane zunji, ingiese chade gouni irezhi duyade oloncha agine." Eneshi dain giesanyi deilasan ji 1 gie minlin wo.
EPH 6:4 Adala, kesilane ho bu kughadene Ezhanni gonjiku banfa, pse sughakughala lai.
EPH 6:5 Hojila, Mexihanughunyi chenlieku mutun ayi pugharaku zhugheghala shixinji duyai ezhannughunne chenlie.
EPH 6:6 Zinie kunlai bayasughane giezhi kunlai melie bu gie. Khareidene Mexihade hoji danlazhi zhughesene Hudai isii zunji.
EPH 6:7 Kunni ushilaku mutun bu giedene Ezhanne ushilaku mutun bayasuzhi gie.
EPH 6:8 Bugon hoji danlasan, ziyutu kun, Ezhan jien kun giesan gou shiqinde jianli ogikui ta jila.
EPH 6:9 Ezhanla, hojiladeneye ingiezhi giezhi hhelai pse bu ayigha. Ta hhelade asiman jiere niekozi Ezhan bikui jila. Hhe kunlade pienxin ulie giene.
EPH 6:10 Zuihoude kielieye, ta Ezhanyi miende hhei fugie liliande kouizhi khiduzhe.
EPH 6:11 Zhan eghikude baohu gieku Hudai 1 tao jienni musi. Ingiese Ibilisini piendakui duii shidane.
EPH 6:12 Matan kunlare ese eghinduzho. Gonjisan, qienli bareisan, ene khara duyani lilian, asiman jieredu doghun ruhherlare eghinduzho.
EPH 6:13 Ingiese zhan eghikude baohu gieku Hudai 1 tao jienni musi. Ingiese ta ene doghun duyade duitoulai duizhi eghindu baludene bei shidane.
EPH 6:14 Bei undanlazhi nurundene zhendaoni pixilie, gundannii zhughei baohu gieku majia danlaghazhi musi,
EPH 6:15 heqishighaku gouxioxini heini chan zhunbei giedene kon jiere musi.
EPH 6:16 Enense chugo pse xianxin giekuni baohu gieku banba danlaghazhi barei. Ingiese Ibilisini khantu gunjienlai man xiniegha shidane.
EPH 6:17 Jiuikui toukui danlaghazhi zho. Shenlinni boujienyi barei, eneshi Hudai kielien wo.
EPH 6:18 Yan shihoudeliuzhe Shenlinde kouizhi olon onxian giezhi xiahua gie. Enende oluzhi jinxin giezhi chan zhazhen giezhi soyuji shentulade xiahua gie.
EPH 6:19 Madeye oluzhi onxian gie. Bi kieliekude Huda made heshini kielien ogizhi fugie danzighala gouxioxii mimii jianjizhi minbai olugha gie.
EPH 6:20 Ene gouxioxide oluzhi mii sozilawoma, bishi Hudai daibio enbene. Bi indan kieliekui danzine fugiedaghazhi jianjigha giezhi onxian gie.
EPH 6:21 Mii qinkon, bi yan giesanlai Tuijigu man tande mejieghane. Hheshi nie oresan gaijiu wo, Ezhande oluzhi shixinji giesan wiliechi wo.
EPH 6:22 Bi zhomen hhei tai hhende peizhi echighakushi bijienyi qinkonyi tande mejieghazhi tai zhughei nanranshighane giezho.
EPH 6:23 Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha pinnan, oreku, xianxin giekui gaijiulade ogi gie.
EPH 6:24 Ulie bienjiku zhugheghala mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihade oresan soyuji kunlade man nenjien ogi gie!
PHI 1:1 Mexiha Ersani hoji BaoloQimotaighala Feilibide sousan Mexiha Ersai miendedu soyuji shentu, lindao, gonjialade xin huaizho.
PHI 1:2 Mai ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
PHI 1:3 Bi niefanie tai sumulakude bi zunjisan Hudade mafan kieliezho.
PHI 1:4 Bayasuku zhugheghala ta dajialade oluzhi izhi onxian giezho.
PHI 1:5 Ingiekushi ta kaishi giesan hhe uduse eli kutula gouxioxii chonjizhi hhantu wilie giezho.
PHI 1:6 Tai dunda gou wilieni kaishi giesan hhe ene wilieni Ersa Mexihani udu kuzhese onchen giekui bi hende xianxin giezho.
PHI 1:7 Bi ingiezhi tai man sumulase indanji wo, ta mii zhughede wine. Bi bafanzi soukude, pse gouxioxide oluzhi huizhi ganzhen beikude Huda made ogisan nenjiende ta man hhantulazho.
PHI 1:8 Bi Mexiha Ersai zhugheghala tai matugie sanasanyi Huda made ganzhen beine.
PHI 1:9 Bi onxian giese tai oreku erlinji pandon gieku jiere yebeiye olodo,
PHI 1:10 yanshi zui gouni bikui fenjizhi Mexiha ireku udude ganjin, yama ulie sugieghachen kun danla,
PHI 1:11 Ersa Mexihani kouizhi gou wilielai olon giedene kuaiku, zanjikuni Hudade ogi giezho.
PHI 1:12 Gaijiula, made penjisan shiqin kharei gouxioxii ondaghasanyi bi tande mejieghaku duran wine.
PHI 1:13 Bi Mexihade oluzhi bafanzi sousei hongunni soyuji budui, psedu kunla man mejiewo.
PHI 1:14 Mii bareise dabufun gaijiula Ezhanyi goude xianxin giedene goujida ulie ayizhi danzine fugiedagha Hudai daolii chonjizho.
PHI 1:15 Niezhanla dubiliezhi zhenjinduzhi chonjizho, da niezhanla gou zhugheghala Mexihai chonjizho.
PHI 1:16 Enezighan kunla Huda mii nanpei giezhi gouxioxii huighasei mejiedene oreku zhugheghala giezho.
PHI 1:17 Hhezighan kunla Mexihai chonjise zinie goyadene oluzhi shixinji ese giezho. Mujishi bi bafanzi soukude olon shouku gieghane giezho.
PHI 1:18 Ingieseye yan xiangan wo? Huai mujiye oluzho, gou mujiye oluzho, yan gieliuzhe Mexihani chonji keighase bi bayasuzho. Bi pse bayasukushi
PHI 1:19 tai onxian gieku, pse Ersa Mexihani ruhherni banman giekui tungo giezhi mii andaghakui bi mejiene.
PHI 1:20 Bi hende panjizhi xiwon giesanshi mii yan shiqindeliuzhe ulie shizheghazhi eqighanku mutun edeye danzine fugiedaghazhi fugu amituliuzhe mii jiere Mexihani zhiguishighakui wo.
PHI 1:21 Mii kieliese bi amitushi Mexihade oluzho, fuguseye haochu wine.
PHI 1:22 Ingieliuzhe bi amiturazhi wilie giezhi jiego goushi bi alinie sunghukui ulie mejiene.
PHI 1:23 Ghuala mii jiai beizho. Bi duyase likai giezhi Mexihaghala hhantulaku duran wine. Enense pse gouni uwoma,
PHI 1:24 bi tande oluzhi duyade biku genjia biyo wine.
PHI 1:25 Bi ingiezhi hende xianxin giese duyade feiliezhi tanre man hhantu soukui mejiene. Ingiese tai xinyan jiere hendazhi bayasukui wine.
PHI 1:26 Ingie bi tai hhende pse echikude mii tungo giezhi Mexiha Ersa giesan shiqinde kuaikui genjia olodoghane.
PHI 1:27 Zhunyonishi tashi asiman gojiani kun wo giezhi tai giekula Mexihani gouxioxi mutun izhishi. Ingiese bi tai uzhele irenu, ulie ireliuzhe tande nie muji bizhi beizhi undanladene gouxioxini xinyan fanmiende hhantu xiacha giezhi
PHI 1:28 tai fandui giesan kunlase goujida ulie ayikui bi mejiene. Ta ulie ayise hhelai widaku, pse tai jiuikui hhelade zhenmin giezho. Enelashi man Huda giesan wo.
PHI 1:29 Tande ogisan nenjienshi zinie Mexihai xianxin gieku pusho, hhende oluzhi shouku giekuye enbene.
PHI 1:30 Ta eghindusan zhanshi bi eghindusanghala niekielien wo. Eqighandei ta mii jiere chujieghezhi daozho, ede bi eghindusei ta chenliezho.
PHI 2:1 Ingiese Mexihai miende tande sughaku kielien, orezhi sidaghaku, Shenlinghala laiwon gieku, pse renyi, ubali xiiku bise
PHI 2:2 tai sumuladan nie gholuzhi nieniedene orezhi nie zhughe gholu. Ingiese bi hende bayasune.
PHI 2:3 Yan shiqinniliuzhe zinie goyadene oluzhi bu gie, minshenni tanxin bu gie, goyane meilade uzhezhi kunlai goyasene fugiede uzhe.
PHI 2:4 Zinie goyane shiqinni bu gui, kunlai shiqinniye gui.
PHI 2:5 Ta zhughene Mexiha Ersai zhughe mutun gholugha.
PHI 2:6 Hhende Hudai yanzi winema, goyane Hudaghala pindane giezhi xiacha ese giedene
PHI 2:7 Kharei goyane yanyanjilai bendazhi hojini yanzi gholuzhi kun mutun oluwo. Kunni yanzi mutun irese
PHI 2:8 Goyane meilade uzhezhi fugutula shunjiwo, da shizijia jiere fuguwo.
PHI 2:9 Ingiese Huda hhei zui unduni gholughazhi hhende yanyanji nierese fugie nierei ogiwo.
PHI 2:10 Ingie asiman jieredu, zemin jieredu, zemin douradu yanyanjila man Ersani nierede xiutuliezhi
PHI 2:11 Jien kunlai amanla Ersa Mexihashi Ezhan wo giezhi chenren giedene Huda Adade kuaikui ireghawo.
PHI 2:12 Ingiese mii orentula, bi tanre hhantu bikude ta chan chenliesan mutun ede bi tai hhende uwokude genjia qingiezhi ayi pugharazhi tai jiuikui shiqinni xiacha giezhi chenjigha.
PHI 2:13 Tai sudoro wilie giezhi goya gou isine gieghane giezhi tande duranji gieku nenli ogisanshi Huda wo.
PHI 2:14 Ta yan shiqin gieliuzhe boxin bu kielie, bu jianjindu.
PHI 2:15 Tande yama kheilaku wizhi ganjintu kun gholu. Ta Hudade yama maobin witu kewosi danlazhi duyade doghun, wirulasan kunlai dunda gon fai.
PHI 2:16 Aminni daolii xienjizhi khizhegha. Ingiese bi Mexihani udude goyane belien ese holuzhi belien wilie ese giezho giezhi kuaine.
PHI 2:17 Bi tai xianxin giekude oluzhi goyane sidagha gieku teizi jiere mure danlaghazhi chusunne pojieliuzhe bayasuzhi da tanre hhantu bayasune.
PHI 2:18 Taye qingiezhi bayasu, da mare hhantu bayasu.
PHI 2:19 Bi Ezhan Ersai kouizhi Qimotaini tai hhende ghujighande peizhi echighaye giezho. Tai qinkonlai mejiezhi bi zhughene nanranshighane giezho.
PHI 2:20 Mare hhantu tande shixinji gonxin giesan kun hhense chugo nieda uwo.
PHI 2:21 Psedu kunla man zinie goyane shiqinyi guine, Ersa Mexihani shiqinyi ulie guine.
PHI 2:22 Ingieliuzhe Qimotaini kunyi ta mejiene. Hhe goya adane mutun mii uzhezhi mare hhantu gouxioxide oluzhi wilie giezho.
PHI 2:23 Ingiese bi goyane shiqinni jiegoi mejiese deigo hhei peizhi echighane giezho.
PHI 2:24 Ingie oloncha ulie beidene biye echikui Ezhanyi miende xianxin giezho.
PHI 2:25 Ingiezhoma, bi sumulase Ibafuqini tai hhende khareizhi echighaku biyo wine giezho. Hheshi mii gaijiu, lienshou, mare hhantu zhan eghindusan kun wo. Ta hhei peizhi bi xiyo bikude banman gieghale irezho.
PHI 2:26 Hhe ta dajialai hende sanazhi, da hhe giemeresei ta mejiese hhe hende nango giezho.
PHI 2:27 Shuhua hhe giemerezhi fugukude kuruwoma, ingieliuzhe Huda hhende ubali xiizhi madeye ubali xiizho. Pse bi genjia yuchou giene.
PHI 2:28 Ingiese bi genjia jindazhi hhei peizhi echighaye. Ta hhei chanlase bayasune, mii yuchou giekuye choghonshine.
PHI 2:29 Ta Ezhanyi miende hende bayasuzhi hhei jienlie. Imutu kunlai zunzhun gie.
PHI 2:30 Ta made banman gie dasande hhe banman giezhi Mexihai wiliede oluzhi chabudu aminni widawo.
PHI 3:1 Mini gaijiula, zuihoude kielieye, ta Ezhanni miende bayasu. Bi xianxianji kielienyi pse huaise chijia uwo, tande haochu wine.
PHI 3:2 Ta hhezighan doghunni giesan kunlai fangula. Hhela nogheini xianli, beyene otolusan kun wo.
PHI 3:3 Zhenzhenji hetoune giesanlashi matan enezighan Hudai Ruhherde kouizhi libai giesanla wo, Mexiha Ersai kuaizho, beyede ese kouizho.
PHI 3:4 Biye beyede koui shidane. Kunla sumulase beyede kouine giese bi genjia ingiezhi gie shidane.
PHI 3:5 Mii oluzhi neimudude hetoune giewo. Bishi Isilie minzu, Bienyamin painughun wo. Zhenzhenji Xibolai kun wo. Guijinghala kieliese bishi Falisai kun wo.
PHI 3:6 Rexinni kieliese bi jiohuini heizhi daozho. Guijinni yoqiughala kieliese made yama kheilakui uwo.
PHI 3:7 Ingieliuzhe eqighandei made gouni wo giesanlai ede bi Mexihani yenyinghala man gou wini danlaghazho.
PHI 3:8 Zinie ene pusho, bi soyujilai gou wini danlaghakushi bi zunjisan Ezhan Mexiha Ersani tanikui zui zhunyoni danlaghazho. Bi hhende oluzhi soyujilane bendazhi hhagha mutun uzhekushi Mexihani goyadene ireghazhi
PHI 3:9 hhere hhantulane giezho. Made bisan gounishi guijinse iresan pusho, bi Mexihani xianxin giekughala Huda ogisan wo.
PHI 3:10 Bi Mexihani tanizhi hhei aminne olusan nenlii mejieku duran wine. Pse hhere hhantu ku shouizhi hhei fugukui daghaku duran wine.
PHI 3:11 Ingie bi fugusanse aminne oluse giezho.
PHI 3:12 Eneshi bi ijin chengun oluwo, ijin onqienshiwo giesan pusho. Mexiha Ersa made agighasanyi bi agine giezhi izhi holuzho.
PHI 3:13 Gaijiula, bi goyane agiwo giezhi ulie sumulane. Bi zinie nie shiqin giezho, daosan shiqinyi matadene meliedekui agine giezhi
PHI 3:14 mubiode daine giezhi holuzho. Ingie Huda Mexiha Ersai miende mii urudene ogine giesan asiman jieredu jianlini linlane giezho.
PHI 3:15 Ingiese matanyi dundadu hen kunla man ingiezhi sumulakui wo. Tande buxiantu xianfa bise Huda eneiye tande mejieghane.
PHI 3:16 Matan yan chendude kuruse zhao ene chenduzhe gieye.
PHI 3:17 Gaijiula, ta man mii daghazhi suru. Pse bijien tande surughasan yanzii daghazhi giesan hhezighan kunlai ta goude uzhe.
PHI 3:18 Bi chan tande kieliezho, ede pse wilazhi kielieye, olon kunla Mexihani shizijiai duitou mutun giezho.
PHI 3:19 Hhelani jiegoshi widakuni wo. Hhelani hudashi goyani kieli wo. Hhela goya shizhekune ulie mejiedene kuaine, sumulasanlashi duyani shiqin wo.
PHI 3:20 Matanshi asiman gojiani kun wo, hhense nie jiuichen irekui sagheizho. Hheshijiu Ezhan Ersa Mexiha wo.
PHI 3:21 Hhe yanyanjii goyadene shunjighasan fugie nenlighala matanyi bixin beyeni goya famatu beyene mutun niekielien gholughane.
PHI 4:1 Ingiese bi orezhi sanasan gaijiula, tashi mii bayasuku wo, mii mienzi wo. Bi oresanla, ta Ezhanni kouizhi beizhi undanla.
PHI 4:2 Bi Yuyajiede xiahua gieye, pse Xindujide xiahua gieye, ta ghuala Ezhanni miende tonjie gie.
PHI 4:3 Mii zhenzhenji gou lienshou, bi chiiye xiahua gieye. Chi ene funilade banman gie. Hhela gouxioxini wiliede mare, pse Gelimien, psedu lienshoulare hhantu khishulazhi daozho. Hhelai nierei aminni jilasan benzi jiere huaizho.
PHI 4:4 Ta Ezhanni miende chan bayasu. Bi pse kielieye, ta bayasu.
PHI 4:5 Jien kunlade renyine mejiegha. Ezhan chadashiwo.
PHI 4:6 Yamade munan bu giezhi yan shiqindeliuzhe onxian gie, xiahua giezhi kere, mafan gieku zhugheghala ta keresanlane Hudade kielie.
PHI 4:7 Ingiese kun lijie gie daku Hudai pinnan Mexiha Ersai sudoro tai zhughe, sumulakui baohu giene.
PHI 4:8 Gaijiula, zuihoude kielieye, ta chan zui gouni, kunla kuaikui sumula. Jien zhenni, zunjiku, gundanni, ganjinni, oreku, gou minshen enelai sumula.
PHI 4:9 Ta mase surusan, jienliesan, chenliesan, chanlasanlai izhigie gie. Ingiese pinnantu Huda tanre hhantu wo.
PHI 4:10 Bi Ezhanni miende hende bayasukushi ta mii zhaogu giekui ede pse jila irewo. Shijishan ta izhi mii zhaogu giene giezhoma jihui ese irezho.
PHI 4:11 Bi ingiezhi kieliekushi made yama chaisan pusho. Bi yan qinkondeliuzhe zhigan giekui suruwo.
PHI 4:12 Bi nanxinde matugie giekui mejiene, bayande matugie giekuiye mejiene. Chuduku, oliesuku, bayanni, chaiku, yan shiqin yan qinkondeliuzhe matugie gieku banfai bi suruwo.
PHI 4:13 Made lilian ogisan hhende kouizhi bi yanniliuzhe gie shidane.
PHI 4:14 Ingiezhoma, bi kunnan bikude ta mare hhantu danjizho, ingiese gou wo.
PHI 4:15 Feilibi kunla, bi gouxioxi chonjizhi qiizhi Maqidunse likai giekude baer ogiku shiqin jiere tanse chugo psedu jiohuila mare hhantu ese danjisanyi taye mejiene.
PHI 4:16 Bi Qiesalonijiade bikude ta touchan erchanji bi injikulai ta khughozhi ireghawo.
PHI 4:17 Bi tanse mure kerene gie ese giezho. Zinie ta giesan wiliede haochu olodoghane giezho.
PHI 4:18 Made yanyanji wine, da feiliezho. Ta Ibafuqii tungo giezhi made khughosanlai bi jienliedene kuruzho. Eneshi Huda bayasuzhi jienlieku andatu mure wo.
PHI 4:19 Bi zunjisan Huda famatu bayansene Mexiha Ersai miende tai yanyanji injikulai ogizhi kurughane.
PHI 4:20 Matanyi ada Hudade chanqi izhi kuaikui ogi. Amine!
PHI 4:21 Mexiha Ersai miendedu jien shentulade kielien asa. Mare hhantuku gaijiula tande kielien asazho.
PHI 4:22 Shentula man, tebieshi Kaisa hongunni kunla tande kielien asazho.
PHI 4:23 Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjien tai zhughede bi gie!
COL 1:1 Hudai isighala Mexiha Ersade shitu danlasan Baolo, Qimotai gaijiughala
COL 1:2 Geloxidedu shentulade, Mexihani shixinji daghasan gaijiulade xin huaizho. Nenjien, pinnanni mai ada Hudase tande ogi gie!
COL 1:3 Bijien tande oluzhi onxian giekude mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani ada Hudade chan mafan kieliezho.
COL 1:4 Eneshi bijien chenliese ta Ersa Mexihai xianxin giezhi soyuji shentulade orezho.
COL 1:5 Xianxin gieku, orekushi tande asiman jiere sunjisan xiwonse irezho. Ene panjikushi ta melieshida zhenzhenji daoli, jiushi gouxioxise chenliesan wo.
COL 1:6 Tai hhende iresan ene gouxioxi qienxiade chonji kurudene olodozhi jiego khizhezho, zhen ta gouxioxini chenliedene Hudai nenjienni zhenzhenji dunjireku hhe uduse qiizhi tai dunda jiego khizhesanghala niekielien wo.
COL 1:7 Ene gouxioxini bijien oresan, hhantu hoji danlasan Ibafuse ta suruwo. Hhe tande oluzhi Mexihade shixinji wiliechi danlazho,
COL 1:8 pse Shenlin tande ogisan orekui bijiende kieliezho.
COL 1:9 Ingiese bijien tai xioxii chenliesan hhe uduse tande oluzhi ese beidene onxian giezho. Bi xiahua giese tai ruhher fanmienni shiqinni soyuji agheliji lijie giekui qiendaghazhi Hudai isii mejie.
COL 1:10 Ingiedene ta udu daokude Ezhanyi pei shidaku mutun giezhi yandeliuzhe hhei bayasugha, yanyanji gou wilie jiere olon jiego khizheghazhi Hudai olon tani.
COL 1:11 Zhao hhei famatu fugie nenlizhe tande olon nenli bizhi bayasuku zhugheghala yan shiqindeliuzhe zhazhen giezhi rennai gie,
COL 1:12 gieghantu gojiade shentulai caichanni xianshou gieku zigeni tande ogisan Adade mafan kielie giezho.
COL 1:13 Ada kharanii qienlise matai jiuizhi khizhedene goya oresan kewonne gojiade ireghawo.
COL 1:14 Hhei kewonni tungo giezhi matanyi shuizhi zuini mienliewo.
COL 1:15 Mexihashi chanla daku Hudai yanzi wo, soyuji zhayaghasanlase tou 1 giede olusan wo.
COL 1:16 Hhei kouizhi asiman, zemin jieredu soyujilai man zhayaghawo. Chanlaku, chanla daku, honshan danlasan, ezhan danlasan, gonjisan, qienli bareisanlai man hhei tungo giezhi, hhende oluzhi zhayaghawo.
COL 1:17 Hhe soyujilase melie wine. Soyujila hhei kouizhi beizho.
COL 1:18 Hheshi beyeni qiorun wo, ene beyeshi jiohui wo. Hheshi keitou wo, fugusan kun dundase xien aminne oluzhi soyujilai touzi gholuwo.
COL 1:19 Huda bayasuzhi hulunnine man hhei sudoro teizhi
COL 1:20 hhei tungo giezhi soyujilai goyarene goudaghawo. Mexiha shizijia jiere usurusan chusunghala zemin asiman jieredulai man heqishighawo.
COL 1:21 Eqighandei ta Hudare danxinrazhi sumulaku jiere Hudare duitou gholuzhi doghunni giezhoma,
COL 1:22 ede Huda Mexihai beyei fugukui tungo giezhi tai goyarene goudaghawo. Ingiekushi tai zhiguitu, jienjien witu, yama kieliekui witui gholughazhi hhei melie beilaghane giezho.
COL 1:23 Ta indan xinyanne izhi goude bareizhi undanlagha. Ta chenliesan gouxioxini panjikuse likai bu gie. Ene gouxioxini qienxiani soyuji zhayaghasanlade man chonji kurughawo. Bi Baoloye ene gouxioxide hoji danlazho.
COL 1:24 Ede bi tande oluzhi bayasuzhi ku shouizho. Mexiha beyedene, yejiushi jiohuide oluzhi ese shouizhi baraghasan kuini bi beye jierene shouizho.
COL 1:25 Huda tande oluzhi made ogisan renwughala bi jiohuide wiliechi danlakushi Hudai kielienyi man chonjizhi khizheghane giezho.
COL 1:26 Ene mimii melieshidaku olon shidaini kunlade niuighazhoma, ede shentuladene mejieghawo.
COL 1:27 Ene mimi niman kunlai dunda zhengiejia fama bikui Huda shentuladene mejieghane giezhi duralawo. Ene mimishi tai sudoro bisan Mexiha wo, jiushi famanide echighaku xiwon wo.
COL 1:28 Bijien hhei chonjizhi olon aghelighala jien kunyi jingao giezhi jien kunde surughakushi jien kunyi Mexihai miende hendaghazhi Hudai melie beilaghane giezho.
COL 1:29 Bi enende oluzhi mii sudoro fugiede wilie giesan nenlide kouizhi xiacha giezhi khishulazho.
COL 2:1 Bi tande, Laojijiani kunlade, pse soyuji mii chanlazhi ese daosan kunlade oluzhi matugie xiacha giesanyi tande mejieghaku duran wine.
COL 2:2 Hhelai sidaghazhi orekughala nieniedene lienji giezho. Qinchude liojie gieku nenlighala Hudai mimini goude mejie giezho. Hheshi Mexiha wo.
COL 2:3 Hhei sudoro soyuji agheli, erlinni boubeilai man ghurazho.
COL 2:4 Bi ene kielienlai kieliekushi kienyiliuzhe seighan kielienghala tai ulie miighane giezho.
COL 2:5 Bi tai hhende uwoma, zhughemi tanre hhantu wo. Ta goude giezhi Mexihai khidunde xianxin giekui uzhese bi bayasuzho.
COL 2:6 Ta Mexiha Ersani Ezhan wo giezhi jienliese hhende kouizhi gie.
COL 2:7 Ta surusan mutun hhei sudoro genzilazhi fugieda. Xianxin giekui undanlaghazhi mafan gieku zhughe olodogha.
COL 2:8 Ta xioxin giezhi kiema tai kunni erlinji piendaku seighan kielienghala bareizhi bu echigha. Eneshi Mexihai daghasan pusho, kunni xigon, duyai langan daolini daghazho.
COL 2:9 Hudai soyuji tejienla kunni beyeghala iresan Mexihani jiere man wine.
COL 2:10 Ta hhei sudoro hulunshizho. Hheshi soyuji gonjisan, qienli bareisanlai qiorun wo.
COL 2:11 Pse hhei sudoro ta kunni khaghala ese giesan hetoune giezho. Mexihani tungo giezhi hetoune giedene nefuxintu beyeni widaghawo.
COL 2:12 Ta xilii jienliezhi hhere hhantu bulazhi hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Hudai nenlii xianxin giezhi hhere hhantu aminne oluwo.
COL 2:13 Ta melieshida codasan dunda, pse hetoune ese giesan zui gieku beyei yenyinzhe fuguzhoma, Huda tai codasanlai man mienliezhi tai Mexihare hhantu aminne olughawo.
COL 2:14 Guijin jiere mai zhazhi kunzhi giezhi jilasanlai moizhi widaghawo. Shizijia jiere ghadazhi widaghawo.
COL 2:15 Gonjisan, qienli bareisanlai barei iredene uqilaini widagha shizheghazhi kunlai melie beilazhi shizijiai tungo giezhi injiwo.
COL 2:16 Ingiese ijieku, ochiku, jieqi, chuyi, hhamuraku udu jiere kunlai goyalane bu kieliegha.
COL 2:17 Enelashi jianlai irekuni xiujie wo, zhennishi Mexihanughun wo.
COL 2:18 Kunla nanxighan goyane meilade uzhezhi qienxienlani beiikughala tai jianlii bu qianlagha. Imutu kunla goya chanlawo giesande miizho. Nefuxinghalane hanhanji goyane fugiede uzhene,
COL 2:19 qiorunghala ese lienjizho. Hhense jinlian khizhezhi nie beyei go mouzi sidasunlai man lienjighazhi zhao Huda osighasan mutun osizho.
COL 2:20 Ta Mexihare hhantu fuguzhi duyai langan daolise andazhoma, yale dou duyanughunyi daghazhi giesan mutun bu barei, bu ijie, bu shigha giesan guijinlai shunjine?
COL 2:22 Enelai nie injise zoin man wida khine, zinie kun fenfulazhi surughasan wo.
COL 2:23 Uzhese enezighan guijinlashi suibiende beiiku, goyane guide meilade uzheku, goyane zayalaku jiere agheli winekui xianli, shijishan kunni nefuxinni daruku jiere yama zoin uwo.
COL 3:1 Ingiese ta Mexihare hhantu aminne oluse asiman jiereshiku shiqinni erei. Hhende Mexiha Hudai borun miende souzho.
COL 3:2 Ta zemin jiereshiku shiqinni bu sumuladene asiman jiereshiku shiqinni sumula.
COL 3:3 Ta ijin fuguzhi tai amin Mexihare hhantu Hudai sudoro niuizho.
COL 3:4 Mexihashi matai amin wo. Hhe xienjikudei ta hhere hhantu fama dunda xienjine.
COL 3:5 Ingiese tai sudoro bisan zemin jieredu zui gieku duranlai fugugha, jiushi lon kijieku, zannanni, nefuxin, doghunnii sumulaku, tanxin gieku wo. Tanxin giese nigiedai beiizho.
COL 3:6 Enelai yenyin jiere Hudai hokuku kielien ulie chenliechen kunlai jiere bouzhene.
COL 3:7 Taye eqighandei enelai dunda udu daokude ingiezhi giezhoma,
COL 3:8 ede ta hokuku, piqi shuaiku, doghunni, kufurei fanjiku, shizheku kielienlai man widagha.
COL 3:9 Ta nieniedene ghudan bu kielie. Ta khuichen kun, pse hhe giedanlai teidene
COL 3:10 shini kunni musizho. Ene shini kun hhei zhayaghasan Ezhanyi yanzizhe hhei tanizhi izhi shinishizho.
COL 3:11 Enende Xila kun Yutai kun, hetoune giesan kun ese giesan kun, yeren, unhua witu kun, hoji, ziyutu kun, enelai ulie fenjine. Mexihashi soyuji wo, soyujilai dunda wine.
COL 3:12 Tashi Huda sunghusan, zhiguitu, oresan kun wo. Ingiese ta ubali xiiku, gou zhughe, meilade uzheku, renyi, rennai giekui musi.
COL 3:13 Ene kun hhe kunde boxin kieliekui bise aghuide sumulazhi nieniene roulie. Ezhan tai matugie rouliezhoshi taye qingiezhi kunlai roulie.
COL 3:14 Enelase chugo orekui musi. Oreku manlai lienjighazhi hulunshighane.
COL 3:15 Mexihani pinnan tai zhughei gonji gie. Ene pinnande oluzhi tai uruzhi nie beye gholughawo. Taye chan mafan kielie.
COL 3:16 Ta Mexihani kielienyi zhughedene zhengiejia olonde teizhi soyuji aghelighala nieniedene surughazhi nieniene jingao gie. Mafan gieku zhugheghala shige, zanmeige, ganjin donghala Hudade doula.
COL 3:17 Ta yan kieliezhi yan gieliuzhe Ezhan Ersani niereghala gie. Hhei tungo giezhi ada Hudade mafan kielie.
COL 3:18 Biereila, zhanguijine shunji, ene Ezhanyi miende heshi wo.
COL 3:19 Zhanguijila biereidene ore, hhelai bu zayala.
COL 3:20 Kewosila, yandeliuzhe ana adanughunne chenlie, eneshi Ezhan bayasukui wo.
COL 3:21 Adala, kesilane bu hokugha, pse hhelade zhughe widane.
COL 3:22 Hojila, yandeliuzhe duyani ezhannughunne chenlie. Yan giese kunlai bayasughachen kun mutun zinie kunlai nudun melie bu giedene Ezhanni zunjizhi shixinji gie.
COL 3:23 Ta yan giese kunlade gieku mutun bu giedene Ezhande gieku mutun zhughesene gie.
COL 3:24 Ingiekushi ta Ezhanni hhense jianli wo giezhi jiachanni jienliekui mejiene. Ta shunjisanshi Ezhan Mexiha wo.
COL 3:25 Gou wini giesan kunde gou wini irene. Ezhan kunde pienxin ulie giene.
COL 4:1 Ezhanla, hojiladene gundande gie. Tandeye asiman jiere Ezhan bikui ta mejiene.
COL 4:2 Ta jinxin giezhi mafan giekughala izhi onxian gie.
COL 4:3 Pse bijiende oluzhiye onxian gie. Huda bijiende daoli chonjiku wijienyi keighazhi Mexihai mimini jianjigha gie. Bi ene yenyinde bafanzi souzho.
COL 4:4 Ingiezhi onxian giema, bi indan kielieku kielienghala daolini man kielie khizheghane.
COL 4:5 Ta jihuini goude bareizhi aghelighala xianxin ese giesan kunlare laiwon gie.
COL 4:6 Ta kielien kieliese dansunghala andatughaku mutun chan renyide kielie. Ingiese jien kunde matugie huida giekui mejiene.
COL 4:7 Mii qinkonlai Tuijigu man tande mejieghane. Hheshi nie oresan gaijiu wo, shixinji giesan wiliechi wo, mare hhantu Ezhande hoji danlazho.
COL 4:8 Bi zhomen hhei tai hhende peizhi echighakushi bijienyi qinkonyi tande mejieghazhi tai zhughei nanranshighane giezho.
COL 4:9 Hhere hhantu echiku dou nie oresan, shixinjitu gaijiu Aniximu wine. Hheshi tai hhendedu kun wo. Hhe ghuala enendedu shiqinlai man tande kieliene.
COL 4:10 Mare hhantu bafanzi sousan Yalidagu, Banabani gujiu Make, Yushidu giezhi urusan Ersa enela tande kielien asazho. Makeni kieliese, tande fenfulazhi daozho. Hhe tai hhende irese ta hhei jienlie. Yutaini Mexihai xianxin giesan kun dunda zinie enela mare hhantu Hudai gojiade oluzhi wilie giezhi mii zhughei nanranshighazho.
COL 4:12 Mexiha Ersade hoji danlasan tai hhendeduku kun Ibafu tande kielien asazho. Hhe chan tande oluzhi xiacha giezhi onxian giese ta Hudai isi jiere man hulunshizhi xianxin gieku duruzhi beizhi undanlase giezho.
COL 4:13 Hhe tande, pse Laojijia, Xilapolini gaijiulade oluzhi olon khishulazho, enei bi hhende ganzhen bei shidane.
COL 4:14 Oresan deifu Lujia, Jimaghala tande kielien asazho.
COL 4:15 Laojijiadedu gaijiulade, pse Ninfade, hhei giededuku jiohuide kielien asa.
COL 4:16 Ta ene xinni onshidene Laojijiani jiohuide ogizhi hhelade onshigha. Laojijiase iresan xinni taye onshi.
COL 4:17 Ezhanse jienliesan renwuni ijinyo onchen gie giezhi Yajibude kielie.
COL 4:18 Bi Baolo qinsi huaizhi kielien asazho. Bi bafanzi sousanyi ta jila. Nenjien tanre chan hhantu bi gie!
1TH 1:1 Baolo, Seila, Qimotai ghurelie Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexihai xianxin giesan Qiesalonijiai jiohuide xin huaizho. Tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
1TH 1:2 Bijien ta ashighalade oluzhi Hudade chan mafan kieliezho. Onxian giekude tai qiizhi kieliezho.
1TH 1:3 Bijien mai Ada Hudai melie tai izhigie jilazhi kieliezho. Ta xianxin giekughala giesan wilie, orezhi khishulasan, pse mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai panjizhi rennai giesei jilazhi onxian giezho.
1TH 1:4 Huda oresan gaijiula, tai sunghusei bijien mejiene.
1TH 1:5 Bijien tande gouxioxini chonjikude zinie kielienghala giesan pusho, nenli, Shenlin, hende xianxin gieku zhugheghala giesan wo. Bijien tanre hhantu bikude tande oluzhi matugie giesei ta goyalane qinchu wo.
1TH 1:6 Ta bijien, Ezhan mutun qingie giezhi heikui fugiede shouiliuzhe Shenlin banman giedene daolini bayasuzhi jienliewo.
1TH 1:7 Ingiese Maqidun, Yagaiyani orondedu xianxin giesan kunlade yanzi uzheghawo.
1TH 1:8 Ezhanyi kielien tai hhense chonji khizhezhi zinie Maqidun, Yagaiyade pusho, gochude man chonji kuruwo. Ta Hudai xianxin giesan xioxii gochui kunla man mejiese bijien yama kielieku biyo uwo.
1TH 1:9 Ta matugiezhi goude bijienyi jienliesei, pse nigiedalai bendadene amitu, zhen Hudai shunjisei hhela goyane kielienduzho.
1TH 1:10 Pse ta asiman jierese ireku Hudai Kewonni sagheizho giene. Hheshi Huda fugusan kun dundase aminne olughasan Ersa wo, jianlai ireku Hudai hokurukuse matanyi jiuine.
1TH 2:1 Gaijiula, bijien tai oronde irese zoin ulie qiikui pusho. Enei ta goyalane qinchu wo.
1TH 2:2 Ta mejiesan mutun bijien Feilibide bikude kunla bijienyi heizhi shizheghawoma, ingieliuzhe mai Huda ogisan danzighala kunla hende fandui gieliuzhe Hudai gouxioxii tande kieliezhi ogiwo.
1TH 2:3 Bijien tande surughazhi kieliekude codasei, ganjin witu zhughe, piendakughala ese giezho.
1TH 2:4 Khareidene bijien kieliekude Huda bijienyi chenren giezhi gouxioxini deilaghasan kun wo giezhi kunlai bayasughane ese giezho. Mai zhughei uzhesan Hudai bayasughane giezho.
1TH 2:5 Bijien seighan kielienghala ese kieliezho, tanxin gieku zhugheghalaye ese giezho. Enei ta mejiene, Hudaye ganzhen beine.
1TH 2:6 Bijien Mexihani shitu danlachenlade tai melie qienli winema, goyane taye hao, kunlaye hao kuaighane ese giezho. Bijien tai dunda renyi zhugheghala ana kesilane qiezheku mutun giezho.
1TH 2:8 Bijien tande hende orezhi zinie Hudai gouxioxini ogiku pusho, lien goya aminneye ogiku duran wo. Tashi bijien ingiezhi oresan wo.
1TH 2:9 Gaijiula, bijien khishulazhi shouku giesei ta mejiene. Bijien tande Hudai gouxioxini chonjikude ta kiemade achan ulie ogine giezhi xieni udu wilie giezho.
1TH 2:10 Ta xianxin giesan kunlade bijien giesanshi zhigui, gundanni wo, yama kieliekuni uwo. Enende ta ganzhen bei, Hudaye ganzhen beine.
1TH 2:11 Ada kesiladene giesan mutun
1TH 2:12 bijien tande sidaghazhi surughazhi goude fenfulasei ta mejiene. Ingiezhi giekushi goyane gojiade, famade urusan Huda tai heshide gieghane giezho.
1TH 2:13 Bijien pse Hudade chan mafan kielieku dounie yenyinshi ene wo. Ta bijiense Hudai kielienyi jienliekude kunni kielien wo uye giedene Hudai kielien wo giezho. Hhe shuhua Hudai kielien enbene. Ene kielien ta xianxin giesan kunlade zoin wine.
1TH 2:14 Gaijiulaya, Yudaya orondedu Mexiha Ersai xianxin giesan Hudai jiohuini kunlai Yutai kunlase heisanyi shouisan mutun taye goya kunlase heisanyi shouiwo.
1TH 2:15 Ene Yutai kunla Ezhan Ersai, xienzhilai alazhi bijienyi tou khireighawo. Hhela Hudai ese bayasughazhi jien kunlare duitou gholuwo.
1TH 2:16 Hhela bijienyi niman kunlade ulie chonjighazhi ulie jiuighane giezho. Hhelai zui izhi olodozhi duruse Hudai hokuku zuihoude hhelani jiere bouzhewo.
1TH 2:17 Gaijiula, bijien zhanshi jiere tanse danxinrase beye danxinrazhoma, zhughe ese danxinrazho. Bijien tai chujiegheku hende duralazho.
1TH 2:18 Ingiese bi Baolo 1 lianhui tai uzhele echine giese Ibilisi bijienyi duiwo.
1TH 2:19 Mai Ezhan Ersa pse irekude bijien hhei melie panjiku, bayasuku, kuaighaku jianlishi yan wo? Ta pushonu?
1TH 2:20 Tashijiu bijienyi kuaiku, bayasuku wo!
1TH 3:1 Ingiese bijien bazilie dadene goyane Yajiende feilieye giezhi jiejin gie,
1TH 3:2 Qimotaini tai hhende peizhi echighawo. Hheshi mai gaijiu wo. Bijienre hhantu Mexihani gouxioxii chonjizhi Hudade wilie giesan kun wo. Hhei echighakushi tai khiduzheghazhi xianxin gieku jiere zhichi gieghane giezho.
1TH 3:3 Ingiese enezighan heiku shiqin dundase tai nieda ulie gojiolughane giezho. Matande heiku shiqin jinjisei ta goyalane mejiene.
1TH 3:4 Bijien tanre hhantu bikude matande heiku shiqin irekui tande melieshi kieliezhi daowo. Ede qintui gholusei ta mejiene.
1TH 3:5 Ingiese bi pse bazilie dadene Qimotaini peizhi tai xianxin gieku matugiezho giezhi daqinlaghale echiwo. Hhe miichen tai miizhi bijien khishulasan wilielani belien gholughakuse ayizho.
1TH 3:6 Ingie Qimotai jian tai hhense iredene tai xianxin gieku, oreku gouxioxini bijiende kieliewo. Da kieliezhi ta chan bijienyi bayasuzhi jilazho. Bijien tai chujieghene gieku mutun taye bijienyi chujieghene giezho.
1TH 3:7 Ingiese gaijiula, bijiende kunnan, heiku olon biliuzhe ta xianxin giesan yenyin jiere bijien bayasuzho.
1TH 3:8 Ta Ezhanyi miende beizhi undanlase bijien ede amiturawo.
1TH 3:9 Bijien mai Hudai melie tai yenyin jiere hende bayasuzho. Eneni Hudade matugie mafan kieliene?
1TH 3:10 Bijien tai ochirazhi uye kurusan tai xianxin giekuni kurughane giezhi xieni udu Hudai hende xiahua giezho.
1TH 3:11 Mai Ada Huda, mai Ezhan Ersa moni keighadene bijienyi zhijie tai hhende echigha gie.
1TH 3:12 Pse bijien tande olon oreku mutun Ezhan tande oreku zhughei ologhan ogizhi durughadene tai nieniedene oregha gie, jien kunladeye oregha gie.
1TH 3:13 Ingiese zhughei tai khiduzheghazhi mai Ezhan Ersa soyuji shentularene hhantu irekude mai Ada Hudai melie zhiguitu yama kielieku witu gholugha gie.
1TH 4:1 Ingiese gaijiula, zuihoude kielieye, Ezhan Ersai miende bijien tai xiahua giezhi tande sughazhi kielieye. Ta bijiense surusan mutun Hudai bayasughazhi gie. Ta ijin giezhoma, pse ologhoni izhigie gie.
1TH 4:2 Bijien Ezhan Ersai qienlighala tande yan minlin ogisei ta mejiene.
1TH 4:3 Hudai isishi ene wo, tai zhiguini gholughane giezho. Lon kijieku, pse qimutu zuilase gholode beighazhi
1TH 4:4 jien kunde goya beyene hanshiliezhi ganjin, zhiguide giekuni mejieghane.
1TH 4:5 Hudai tani dasan niman kun mutun lon gieku nefuxinni daghazhi hu ulie gieghane.
1TH 4:6 Ene shiqin jiere xianxin giesan gaijiulade piendazhi pienyi bu zhanji. Bijien melieshi tande kieliezhi hende jingao giesan mutun Ezhan qimutu zui fanjisan kunlai faine.
1TH 4:7 Huda matanyi urukushi ganjin wini bu giezhi, zhiguide gie giezho.
1TH 4:8 Ingiese ene sughasei ulie chenliechen kunshi kunni ulie chenlieku pusho, tande goya Shenlinne ogisan Hudai uye chenliezho.
1TH 4:9 Gaijiulade oreku shiqinni kieliese tande xin huaiku biyo uwo. Nieniedene orekuni ta goyane Hudase suruzho.
1TH 4:10 Ta Maqidunni gaijiulade man shuhua ingiezhi giezho. Gaijiula, bijien tande xiahua gieye, ta pse ologhonni gie.
1TH 4:11 Bijien tande fenfulasan mutun ta xiacha giezhi udune nanrande daogha. Goya shiqinlane gonji. Khaghalane wilielai gie.
1TH 4:12 Qingiese ghadanedu kun ta giesanlai uzhese zunzhun giene, taye kiemade ulie kouine.
1TH 4:13 Gaijiula, bijienyi duranshi hhe fugusan kunlai shiqinni ta mejiese gou wo. Ingiese hhe xiwon wichen kun mutun zhughetai ulie otune.
1TH 4:14 Matan Ersa duya ijiedene aminne olusanyi xianxin giese Ersai xianxin giedene duya ijiesan kunlai Huda Ersaghala hhantu udurukuiye xianxin giene.
1TH 4:15 Bijien Ezhanyi kielienyi tande kielieye. Ezhan pse irekude matan amitu kun hhe fugusan kunlase melieshida dane.
1TH 4:16 Nie minlin xiaise fugie qienxien waradazhi Hudai labai shenqi dunda Ezhan asiman jierese qinsi irene. Ingiekude Mexihani xianxin giedene fugusan kun xien aminne olune.
1TH 4:17 Ingiedene bijien amitu kunyi hhelare hhantu olien jiere deila echi asiman jiere Ezhanyi ochirane. Ingiedene chanqi Ezhanre hhantu soune.
1TH 4:18 Ingiese ta enezighan kielienghala nieniedene surughazhi kielie.
1TH 5:1 Gaijiula, ene shiqin giezhe fashen giekui tande xin huaiku biyo uwo.
1TH 5:2 Ezhanni udushi ghughei xienidei ireku mutun mejie dakude irekui ta qinchu wo.
1TH 5:3 Kunla "Pinnan wo, yama shiqin uwo." giezhi kieliekude menzhali hhelade zeinan kuzhi irene. Biereila kewosi olukude otuku niekielien wo. Kiema anda dane.
1TH 5:4 Gaijiula, ingieseye ta kharanide uwo. Hhe ireku udu tande ghughei mutun ulie irene.
1TH 5:5 Ta manshi gonni kewosi, uduni kewosi wo. Matanshi xieninughun pusho, kharaninughunye pusho.
1TH 5:6 Ingiese matan kunla mutun bu hhunturadene goude jinxin gieye.
1TH 5:7 Hhunturachen kun xienidei hhunturane. Sudochen kun xienidei sudone.
1TH 5:8 Matanshi udunughun wo, indan jinxin gieye. Xianxin gieku, oreku kuijiani musizhi jiuiku xiwonni toukuini zhoye.
1TH 5:9 Huda mai sunghuse faine ese giezho. Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi jiuine giezho.
1TH 5:10 Ersa Mexiha matande oluzhi duya ijiese bugon matan amitu kun, fugusan kun man hheghala hhantu udu daoghane giezho.
1TH 5:11 Ingiese ta chan gieku mutun nieniedene surughazhi kieliezhi nieniene hendagha.
1TH 5:12 Gaijiula, bijien tai xiahua gieye, tande oluzhi khishulasan kunlai zunji. Hhela Ezhanyi miende tai gonjizhi sughazho.
1TH 5:13 Hhela giesan wilieni yenyinghala ta hhelade orezhi goude zunzhun gie. Ta nienierene heqishi.
1TH 5:14 Gaijiula, bijien pse tande sughazhi kielieye, hhe lansunlade jingao gie, danzi widasan kunlade hunlazhi kielie, zhoreliesan kunlai fei, soyuji kunlade rennai gie.
1TH 5:15 Ta kienliuzhe ijinyo doghunnide doghunni bu kharei. Nieniedene, ashighalade gouni giekude chan xiacha gie.
1TH 5:16 Ta chan bayasu,
1TH 5:17 bu beidene onxian gie,
1TH 5:18 yan shiqindeliuzhe mafan kielie. Eneshi Mexiha Ersai sudoro tande olusan Hudai isi wo.
1TH 5:19 Shenlinni wiliei bu danla.
1TH 5:20 Hudai kielienyi kieliese uzhezhi bu xinie.
1TH 5:21 Yandeliuzhe shiizhi uzhe, gounii barei,
1TH 5:22 shiheni doghunnise gholode bei.
1TH 5:23 Pinnan ogisan Huda qinsi tai zhengiejia zhiguitu gholugha gie. Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha irekude tai ruhher, jinshen, beyei man bouizhi yama kieliekui widagha gie.
1TH 5:24 Tai urusanshi kekaoni wo. Hhe ijinyo chenjighane.
1TH 5:25 Gaijiula, bijiende oluzhi onxian gie.
1TH 5:26 Zhughesene jien gaijiulade kielien asa.
1TH 5:27 Bi Ezhanyi niereghala tande minlin xiaiye. Ene xinni soyuji gaijiulade man onshizhi chenliegha.
1TH 5:28 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai nenjien tanre hhantu bi gie!
2TH 1:1 Baolo, Seila, Qimotai ghurulie mai Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexihai miendedu Qiesalonijiai jiohuide xin huaizho.
2TH 1:2 Mai Ada Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie!
2TH 1:3 Gaijiula, bijien tande oluzhi Hudade chan mafan kieliese indanji wo. Tai xianxin gieku zhughe fugiedazhi, nieniedene oreku zhugheye olodozho.
2TH 1:4 Bijien Hudai jiohuilade tai kuaizhi kieliezho. Ta olon heiku, kunnanni penjikude rennai giezho, xianxin giekuni goude bareizho.
2TH 1:5 Eneshi Huda gundande panjikui zhenmin giezho. Hudai gojiade oluzhi tai shouku gieghazhi Hudai gojiade peighane giezho.
2TH 1:6 Hudashi gundanni wo. Tai biisan kunlai Huda biikughala bouin giene.
2TH 1:7 Ta shouku giesan kunlai bijienre hhantu pinnanshighane. Ezhan Ersa nenlitu qienxienghalane asiman jierese khan dunda xienjikude
2TH 1:8 Hudai tani dasan kun, mai Ezhan Ersani gouxioxini ulie shunjichen kunlai faine.
2TH 1:9 Ezhan enelai faizhi meliesene, famatu nenlisene likai gieghadene chanqi widaghane.
2TH 1:10 Ezhan ireku hhe udude hhei shentula, jien xianxin giesan kunla man hhei ghudure wo giezhi kuaine. Taye hhelai dunda wine. Bijien ganzhen beisanyi ta xianxin giewo.
2TH 1:11 Enende oluzhi bijien tande chan onxian giezho. Mai Huda tai urusan mujide tai peigha gie. Huda nenlighalane tai gounide olusan duran, pse xianxin giekughala giesan wilielani man chengun olugha gie.
2TH 1:12 Ingiese mai Ezhan Ersai niere zhao mai Huda, Ezhan Ersa Mexihai nenjienghala tai jiere famashine, taye hhei jiere famashine.
2TH 2:1 Gaijiula, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha pse irekude, matan hhei melie hhantulakude oluzhi tai xiahua giezhi kielieye.
2TH 2:2 Ezhanni udu ijin kuzhewo giezhi kunla kieliese ta suibien bu gojioluzhi bu jinda. Hhelade kenen Shenlin mejieghazho, loushila jianjizho, pse shitulai xin wo giezhi maochun giene.
2TH 2:3 Hhela yan banfaghala piendaliuzhe goyane bu piendagha. Hhe uduse melie panjio gieku shiqin wine. Pse zuihoude widaku hhe fugie zuitu xienjizhi khizhene.
2TH 2:4 Hhe irese kunla huda wo giezhi urusanlase, kunla beiisan shihenilase duizhi goyane hhelase fugiede uzhene, da mechide souzhi goyane Huda wo giene.
2TH 2:5 Bi tanre hhantu bikude kieliesan ene shiqinlani ta jila danu?
2TH 2:6 Ede hhe fugie zuituni yan duisei ta mejiene. Shihouni kuzhese hhei xienjizhi khizheghane.
2TH 2:7 Hhe fugie zuitu ijin jizide wilie giezho. Duisan hhe widatula ingiezhi giene.
2TH 2:8 Ingiedene hhe fugie zuitu xienji khizhene. Ezhan Ersa amanne hoghala hhei widaghane, ireku gonqighala hhei fugughane.
2TH 2:9 Hhe fugie zuitu irese Ibilisini wiliei giezhi yanyanji nenlitu shiqin, ghudureqi, jia fugie shiqin giene.
2TH 2:10 Pse widaku kunlai jiere yanyanji gou wini piendaku shiqinlai giene. Enela jiuiku zhendaode xiqi wizhi ese jienliezho.
2TH 2:11 Ene yenyin jiere Huda hhelade codaku zhughe olon ogizhi jiani xianxin gieghawo.
2TH 2:12 Ingiedene zhendaoni xianxin uye giezhi gou winide xiqi bisan hhe kunlade man zui jinjine.
2TH 2:13 Ezhan oresan gaijiula, tande oluzhi bijien Hudade chan mafan kieliekuni wo. Huda eqighanse tai sunghuzhi Shenlinghala zhiguishighadene zhendaoni xianxin gieghazhi tai jiuiwo.
2TH 2:14 Bijien chonjisan gouxioxighala Huda tai uruzhi jiuiwo. Ingiese mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani famai tande ireghane giezho.
2TH 2:15 Ingiese gaijiula, ta beizhi undanla. Bijien kielien, xinghala tande sughasan daolini ta goude barei.
2TH 2:16 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha goyane, matande orezhi nenjienghalane mai chanqi sidaghazhi kieliesan, pse gou xiwon ogisan mai Ada Hudaghala
2TH 2:17 tai sidaghazhi kielie gie. Pse ta shiheni gou wilie giezhi gou kielien kieliekude tande nenli ogi gie.
2TH 3:1 Gaijiula, zuihoude kielieye, ta bijiende ingiezhi onxian gie, tai dundashiku mutun Ezhanyi kielienyi gochude ghujighan chonji keidene famashigha gie.
2TH 3:2 Mouxien kun, doghun kunlase bijienyi jiui gie. Ene xinyanshi dajianughun pusho.
2TH 3:3 Ezhanshi kekaoni wo, tai khiduzheghazhi doghunnise bouine.
2TH 3:4 Bijien Ezhanyi miende tai xianxin giezho. Bijien tande fenfulasanyi ta giezho, ihouye giene.
2TH 3:5 Ezhan tai zhughei uduruzhi Hudai orekude, Mexihani rennai giekude echigha gie!
2TH 3:6 Gaijiula, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani niereghala tande minlin xiaiye, langande giezhi bijien chonjisan daolini ulie zunjisan gaijiulase gholodo.
2TH 3:7 Bijienyi daghazhi indan matui giekuni ta goyane mejiene. Bijien tai dunda bikude langanrazhi ese giezho.
2TH 3:8 Kunlai budanyi belien ese ijiezho. Tande achan ulie ogine giezhi xieni udu wilie giezhi khishulazhi ku shouizho.
2TH 3:9 Eneshi bijiende qienli wikuni pusho, taye bijien mutun gie giezhi bijien tande yanzi uzheghawo.
2TH 3:10 Bijien tai hhende bikude kien wilie ulie giene giese budan bu ijie giezhi tande minlin xiaizhi daowo.
2TH 3:11 Bijien chenliese tai dunda niezhan kunla langanrazhi wilie ulie giene. Da ulie gonjiku shiqinyi gonjine.
2TH 3:12 Bijien Ezhan Ersa Mexihani miende ene izhun kunlade minlin xiaizhi sughazhi kielieye, undande wilie giezhi goya budanne ijie.
2TH 3:13 Gaijiula, ta gouni giekude zhughene bu sularagha.
2TH 3:14 Kien bijienni ene xin jieredu kielienyi ulie chenliese hhei zhiidene laiwon bu giezhi shizhegha.
2TH 3:15 Ingieliuzhe hhei duitou bu danlagha. Gaijiune mutun uzhezhi sughazhi kielie.
2TH 3:16 Pinnan ogisan Ezhan qinsi yan shiqindeliuzhe suishisui tande pinnan ogi gie. Ezhan chan ta ashighalare hhantu bi gie!
2TH 3:17 Bi Baolo qinsi huaizhi kielien asazho. Mini alinie xin jiereliuzhe bi nierene ingiezhi huaizhi hao giezho.
2TH 3:18 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani nenjien tanre man hhantu bi gie!
1TI 1:1 Mai jiuichen Huda, matan xiwon giesan Mexiha Ersai minlinyi zunjizhi Mexiha Ersade shitu danlasan Baolo
1TI 1:2 xinyan jiere made zhenzhen kewon danlasan Qimotaide xin huaizho. Huda Ada, mai Ezhan Mexiha Ersa chade nenjien, ubali xiiku, pinnan ogi gie!
1TI 1:3 Bi Maqidunde echikude chade goude fenfulazhi Ifusode feilieghakushi niezhan kunla psedu daolii surughase bu surugha giezho.
1TI 1:4 Pse yama genzi witu guhuade, ulie baraku xienrenlai niere jilasande hhelai izhigie bu miigha giezho. Ene shiqinlade zi jianjindune, xinyanghala chengun oluku Hudai jihuade yama zoin uwo.
1TI 1:5 Bi surughasan daolini mujishi oreku wo. Ene orekushi ganjin zhughe, gou lianxin, jia witu xinyanse khizhezho.
1TI 1:6 Niezhan kunla enezighanse wiruladene yama biyo witu jianjindukude echiwo.
1TI 1:7 Hhela jinwun loushi danlane giezhoma, goya yan kieliesanne ulie mejiene, kenjin giezhi ijien qilasanneye ulie mejiene.
1TI 1:8 Guijinni heshide injise gouni bikui matan mejiene.
1TI 1:9 Guijinni gou kunde ese jinjizho. Mouxien kun, kielienyi ulie chenliechen, zhigui witu, zui fanjichen, zannanni giechen, hharamu giechen, ana adane alachen, kun alachen,
1TI 1:10 lon kijiechen, tunxinlien giechen, kun huichen, ghudan kieliechen, jiani fayen giechen, pse olusan daolini duizhi yanyanji giechen kunlade jinjizho.
1TI 1:11 Ene olusan daolishi famatu gouxioxise iresan wo. Enei indan doulaku Huda made jiuizhi ogiwo.
1TI 1:12 Made nenli ogisan mai Ezhan Mexiha Ersade bi mafan kieliezho. Hhe mii xianxin giedene nanpei giezhi goyadene wilie gieghazho.
1TI 1:13 Eqighandei bishi Mexihai sugiechen, heichen, qifulachen wo. Ingieliuzhe Huda made ubali xiikushi bi xianxin ese giekude mejie dazhi giezho.
1TI 1:14 Mai Ezhan made nenjien texien olon ogizho. Ingiese Mexiha Ersai miende made xinyan, oreku olodozhi moizho.
1TI 1:15 Mexiha Ersa duyade zuirenlani jiuile irewo giesan ene kielienyi xianxin giezhi man jienliekughon wine. Bishi zuiren dunda zui mouxienni wo.
1TI 1:16 Eneshi Ezhan made ubali xiisan yenyin wo. Mexiha Ersa bi ene zui mouxien kunni jiere hende rennai giezhi yanzi uzheghakushi khuinashi xianxin giechen kunlade chanqiku amin ogine.
1TI 1:17 Hhe chanqiku Honshan, ulie fuguku, chanla daku, zi niekozi Hudade zhigui, kuaikui chanqi izhi ogi. Amine!
1TI 1:18 Mii kewon Qimotaiya, zhao melieshida kunla Hudai kielienyi deilazhi chade kieliesan mutun bi ene minlinni chade ogiye. Hhe kielienghala gou zhan eghi.
