1PE 1:3 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai ada Hudade doulaye! Hhe matande hende ubali xiidene Ersa Mexihai fugusan kun dundase aminne olughakughala matanyi erchan olughazhi zhenzhenji xiwon ogizho.
1PE 1:4 Pse ulie xiuqiraku, ulie zannantuku, ulie widaku jiachanyi tande oluzhi asiman jiere sunjizho.
1PE 1:5 Huda ta xianxin giekui tungo giezhi nenlighalane tai baohu giedene duya barakude xienjizhi khizhene giesan jiuikui tande ogine.
1PE 1:6 Ingiese ta hende bayasuzho. Ta bixi zhanshi jiere yanyanji kunnande yuchou giezhoma,
1PE 1:7 enezighan kunnan tai xinyanshi zhenni bikui mejieghane. Khande tuliesan antanliuzhe huailunema, tai xinyan antanse da guizhunde Ersa Mexiha xienjikude tande kuaiku, fama, zhiguii ireghane.
1PE 1:8 Ta Ersai chanlazhi ese daozhoma, hhende orezho. Edeliuzhe hhei chanla danema, hhei xianxin giezhi kielienghala kielie daku, hashu witu bayasukughala bayasuzho.
1PE 1:9 Ta xinyanni jiegoi jienliezho. Hheshi goyane jiuiku wo.
1PE 1:10 Ene jiuikui kieliese xienzhila xianxide chaizhi yenjiu giezhi daozho. Tande ogine giesan ene nenjienni hhela melie kieliezhi daozho.
1PE 1:11 Hhela Mexihashi kien bikui, yan xienzide irekui yenjiu giezho. Mexiha shouku giedene khuinashi fama irekui Mexihani ruhher hhelai sudoro melie kieliezho.
1PE 1:12 Hhela ene wiliei giese goyadene ese giezho, tande oluzhi giesei Huda hhelade mejieghazho. Ene gouxioxishi chonjichen kunla asiman jierese peizhi ireghasan Shenlinyi nenlighala ede tande chonjizhi ogiwo. Ene shiqinlai qienxienlaye hende uzheku duran wo.
1PE 1:13 Ingiese ta zhughedene zhunbei giezhi jinxin giedene Ersa Mexiha xienjikude tande deilazhi ireku nenjienyi goude panji.
1PE 1:14 Ta shunjiku kewosi danlazhi eqighanku mutun yama mejie dazhi nefuxin giekulai bu dagha.
1PE 1:15 Tai urusan Hudashi zhigui mutun taye yan shiqin giese zhiguide gie.
1PE 1:16 Jinwun jiere jilazhi kieliezho, "Bishi zhiguitu wo, taye zhiguishi."
1PE 1:17 Ta xiahua giekude kunni pienxin ulie giezhi kunni giekughala panjichen Ezhanni Ada giezhi uruse ta zhanshi jiere duyade bikude hhei zunjizhi udu dao.
1PE 1:18 Ta mejiene. Tai xienrenla tande chonjizhi ogisan yama zoin witu xigonse tai shuisanshi huailuku antan, miengughala pusho,
1PE 1:19 Mexihani zhiguitu chusunghala wo. Hoxian goujida uye chaizhi ese cheiqisan ghoni ghughanyi chusunyi xianli.
1PE 1:20 Huda Mexihai duya zhayaghaku melie jinjiwoma, duya barakude tande oluzhi xienjizhi khizheghawo.
1PE 1:21 Ta Mexihai tungo giezhi hhei fugusan kun dundase aminne olughazhi hhende kuaikui ogisan Hudai xianxin giezho. Ingiese ta xianxin giesan, panjisanne man Hudade kouizho.
1PE 1:22 Ta zhendaoi shunjizhi goyane ganjinraghazhi kunlade zhenzhenji orezho. Ingiese xiacha giezhi zhughesene nieniedene orendu.
1PE 1:23 Tai erchan olusanshi huailuku fureghala pusho, ulie huailuku fureghala wo. Hudai chanqi ulie widaku, amitu kielienghala wo.
1PE 1:24 Jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Kun osun niekielien wo. Kunni fama osun jieredu chizhe niekielien wo. Osun ghone, chizheye xiniene.
1PE 1:25 Zinie Hudai kielien chanqi wine." Ene kielienshi tande chonjisan gouxioxi wo.
1PE 2:1 Ingiese soyuji doghunni, piendaku, jiazhon gieku, dubilieku, sugieku enelai ta man widagha.
1PE 2:2 Yeliwa neizii neiiku mutun taye qingiezhi zhenni, pse gou daolini neii. Ruhherni ganjin neizii neii. Daolide kouizhi izhi fugiedase jiuine.
1PE 2:3 Ta Ezhan gou bikui mejiese qingiezhi gie.
1PE 2:4 Ta Ersai shida ire. Hheshi amitu tashi wo. Kunla hhei bendawoma, Huda hhazeliezhi sunghuwo.
1PE 2:5 Taye amitu tashi mutun nienieji luizhi ruhhertu gie gholu. Ingie zhiguitu buwa danladene Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi Huda bayasuku mutun jiomuntu mure ogi.
1PE 2:6 Jinwun jiere kieliezho, "Uzhe, bi zhiguide sunghusan tashii Xiwunde teizhi jichu tashi gholughawo. Hhei xianxin giesanla jiuren ulie giene."
1PE 2:7 Ingiese ene tashi xianxin giesan tande zhigui woma, ulie xianxin giesan kunlade, "Jianrenla bendasan tashi giei zhunyo tashi gholuwo"
1PE 2:8 pse hheshi kunyi banjighaku tashi wo. Unaghaku fugie tashi wo giezho. Hhela banjikushi kielienyi uye shunjizho. Eneshi hhelai amin wo.
1PE 2:9 Ingieliuzhe tashi sunghusan bexin, honshan mutun buwa, zhiguitu minzu, bexin wo. Tai kharanise uruzhi khizheghadene goyai ghudureqitu gonqi dunda ireghasan Hudai famatuni kunlade kielieghane giezho.
1PE 2:10 Melieshida tashi bexin pusho. Ede Hudai bexin wo. Melieshida tande ubali ese xiizho. Ede ubali xiizho.
1PE 2:11 Mii orentula, tashi duyade zhanshi jiere sousan niman kun wo. Bi tande goude fenfulaye, ruhherghala eghinduku beyeni nefuxinni bu gie.
1PE 2:12 Ta niman kunlai dunda goude gie. Ingiese ta doghunni giezho giezhi sugiesan kunla ta goude giesei uzhedene Huda panjiku udude hhei kuaine.
1PE 2:13 Ta Ezhanyi yenyinghala soyuji kunni zhiduni shunji. Zui fugie qienlitu honshan,
1PE 2:14 pse noyenlai shunji. Noyenlashi doghunni giesan kunlai faizhi gounii giesan kunlai kuaighane giezhi honshan peisan wo.
1PE 2:15 Hudai isishi ta gouni giezhi bende yama ulie mejiechen kunlai amanyi duigha giezho.
1PE 2:16 Tashi ziyutui woma, ziyughala doghunni gieku jiekou bu gholughadene Hudai hoji mutun gie.
1PE 2:17 Jien kunlai zunzhun gie. Xianxin giesan kunlade ore. Hudai zunji. Honshanyi zunzhun gie.
1PE 2:18 Hoji danlasan kunla, ta zunzhun gieku zhugheghala ezhanne shunji. Zinie gou, renyitui pusho, mouxiennilaiye shunji.
1PE 2:19 Kien hanhanji shouku giedene Hudai sumulazhi rennai giese kuaikui wine.
1PE 2:20 Zui fanjidene eghikui rennai giese yan kuaikui wine? Gouni giedene shouku giekui rennai giese Hudai melie kuaikui wine.
1PE 2:21 Shouku gieliuzhe gouni giekude Huda tai uruzho. Mexihaye tande oluzhi shouku giezhi yanzi uzheghawo. Tai goyane korolon mutun yoghane giezho.
1PE 2:22 Hhe zui fanjizhi ese daozho, ghudanye kieliezhi ese daozho.
1PE 2:23 Hhei sugiekude khareizhi ese sugiewo, shouku giekude ayighaku kielien ese kieliewo, khareidene goyane gundande panjichen Hudade jiuiwo.
1PE 2:24 Hhe qinsi beyeghalane shizijia jiere mai zuini danjidene mai zui dunda udu ulie daoghazhi gounide udu daoghawo. Hhe shan deiladene ta goudawo.
1PE 2:25 Ta eqighandei miisan ghoni niekielien wo. Ede ruhhertai adulachen, baohu giechen hhei shida khareizhi irewo.
1PE 3:1 Biereila, taye qingiezhi zhanguijine shunji. Ingiese Hudai daolii ese xianxin giesan zhanguijiliuzhe ta kieliesanlai pusho, giesanlai uzhedene zhugheini gojiolughane.
1PE 3:2 Yenyinshi ta zunzhun giezhi ganjinde udu daosei hhela chanlawo.
1PE 3:3 Ta mienzide usunne bienjizhi antan zhozhi seighan jien musizhi bu dabala.
1PE 3:4 Khareidene ta renyi, undantughala sudorone dabala. Eneshi ulie xiuqiraku seighanni wo, Hudai melie zhigui wo.
1PE 3:5 Hudai kouisan eqighanku zhiguitu biereilaye ingiezhi zhanguijine shunjizhi goyane dabalazho.
1PE 3:6 SareIburaheimui shunjizhi ezhan giezhi uruzho. Ta yama ulie ayidene gounii giese Sare mutun gholuwo.
1PE 3:7 Zhanguijila, taye qingiezhi biereighalane hhantu udu daokude hhelai gonxin gie. Hhelashi zholien oqitula wo. Hhelashi tanre hhantu aminni nenjienyi jienliechen wo giezhi zunzhun gie. Ingiese tai onxian giekui ulie duine.
1PE 3:8 Zuihoude kielieye, ta man nie zhughe gholuzhi nieniedene ubali xii, nieniedene ore, renyide giezhi goyane meilade uzhe.
1PE 3:9 Doghunnide doghunnii, sugiekude sugiekui bu kharuludene hhelade oluzhi gouni kielie. Huda tai zhen enende uruzhi fuqi jienlieghane giezho.
1PE 3:10 Jinwun jiere kieliezho, Kien goude udu daoghane giezhi xianshou giene giese Kielienne gonjizhi doghun kielien bu kielie. Amanne gonjizhi ghudan bu kielie.
1PE 3:11 Doghunnise likai giezhi gouni gie, heqishikui xiacha giezhi gie.
1PE 3:12 Ezhanni nudun gou kunyi uzhene, hhei chighin hhela waradasei chenlienema, Doghunni giesan kunlade Ezhan uxinne boughane.
1PE 3:13 Ta goude gouni giese kien tai heine?
1PE 3:14 Ta gouni giedene shouku giese tande fuqi wine. Kunla ayighakuse bu ayi, ye bu jinda.
1PE 3:15 Zhughedene Mexihai zunjizhi hhei ezhan danlagha. Kunla ta zhughedene panjisei asase suishisui huida giekui zhunbei gie.
1PE 3:16 Huida giekude renyide zunzhun giezhi gie. Ta lianxin bu ghudandu. Ingiese kunla tai uru giekude ta Mexihai xianxin giezhi giesan gounii sugiesan kunla shizhene.
1PE 3:17 Gouni giezhi shouku giekushi Hudai isi enbese doghunni giezhi shouku giekuse gou wo.
1PE 3:18 Mexihaye zuini yenyinzhe 1 huide duya ijiewo. Ingiezhi gou kun gou witu kunyi deilawo. Ingiekushi Hudai melie tai echighane giezho. Beyeghala kieliese hhe duya ijiewo, ruhherghala kieliese aminne oluwo.
1PE 3:19 Hhe echidene ruhherghalane bafanzide khasan ruhherlade daoli chonjizho.
1PE 3:20 Hhelashi eqighandei Nuhha chon gieku shihoude Huda rennai giezhi sagheikude uye shunjisan kunla wo. Hhe shihoude chon jiere khizhi ususe jiuisan kun jian neiman wo.
1PE 3:21 Ene usushi xilini melie mejieghasan jihao wo, ede Ersa Mexihani aminne olughakughala tai jiuine. Hheshi beye jieredu goujiani widaghakui pusho, ulie ghudanduku lianxinghala Hudade fayen giekui wo.
1PE 3:22 Ersa asiman jiere khireizhi Hudai borun miende wo, qienxien, qienlitu, nenlitula man hhende shunjizho.
1PE 4:1 Mexiha ingiezhi beyedene shouku giezhoma, taye imutu zhugheghala goyane ku shouikui zhunbei gie. Beyede shouku giesan kun zuise gonxi sirazho.
1PE 4:2 Ingiedene feiliesan udude kunni nefuxinyi pse ulie daghazhi Hudai isi mutun udu daone.
1PE 4:3 Ta daosandei niman kunla xiqi bikulai daghazhi hu gieku, nefuxin gieku, jiu ochizhi sudoku, lon naduzhi ochiku, nigiedalai beiizhi hanzhan gieghakui pse bu gie.
1PE 4:4 Ene shiqin jiere ta hhelare hhantu qingiezhi hashu witu lon ulie giekui hhela chanladene ghudurezhi tai sugiezho.
1PE 4:5 Jianlai hhela amitu kun, fugusan kunyi panjiku Ezhanyi melie zhan jiuine.
1PE 4:6 Ene yenyin jiere fugusan kunladeye gouxioxini chonjikushi beye miende hhelai kun mutun panjine giezhoma, ruhher miende Huda mutun amituraghane giezho.
1PE 4:7 Duya baraku ghujinlawo. Ingiese ta zhughesene xioxin giezhi jinxin giedene onxian gie.
1PE 4:8 Zui zhunyonishi nieniedene shixinde ore. Oreku olon zuini khazhi widaghane.
1PE 4:9 Ta bayasuku zhugheghala nieniene giedene goude jienlie.
1PE 4:10 Ta zhao Huda tande ogisan nenjien mutun nieniene ushilazhi Huda ogisan yanyanji nenjienni gou gonjia danla.
1PE 4:11 Jianjichenla indan Hudai kielienyi jianjikuni wo. Ushilachenla indan Huda ogisan lilianghala ushilakuni wo. Ingiese yan gieliuzhe Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi Hudade kuaikui ireghane. Kuaiku, qienlini chanqi izhi hhende ogi. Amine.
1PE 4:12 Mii orentula, shiiku khan mutun tai jiere irese goyade yama shiqin penjiwo giezhi ghudure wo giezhi bu jindadene
1PE 4:13 Mexiha mutun hhere hhantu shouku giezho giezhi bayasundu. Ingiese Mexihai famatui khizheghakude ta hende bayasuzhi jiuline.
1PE 4:14 Mexihai yenyin jiere kunla tai sugiese tande fuqi wine. Famatu ruhher, yejiushi Hudai Ruhher tai jiere wo.
1PE 4:15 Tai dunda kienliuzhe kun alaku, ghulaku, doghun shiqin gieku, ulie gonjiku shiqinyi gonjikughala shouku bu gie.
1PE 4:16 Mexihani tuji danlazhi shouku giese bu shizhedene ene nierei yenyinzhe Hudai kuai.
1PE 4:17 Panjiku shihou kuzhewo. Hudai bexinse panjizhi qiine. Matanse kaishi giese gouxioxini ulie shunjisan kunlai jiego matui gholune?
1PE 4:18 Pse, "Gou kunyi jiuiku chijiashi xienlian witu kun, zuirenla matui gholune?"
1PE 4:19 Ingiese Hudai isi mutun shouku giesan kunla izhi gouni giezhi duyai zhayaghasan kekaotu Ezhande goyane ogikui wo.
1PE 5:1 Tai dunda zhanlao danlasan kunlade bi sughazhi kielieye. Biyeshi zhanlao wo, Mexiha shouku giekude ganzhen beizhi jianlai khizheku famade hhantu xianshou giechen kun wo.
1PE 5:2 Tai dundadu Hudai ghonilai qiezhe. Hudai isi mutun hhelai zhaogu gie. Mienqian bu giedene yenyizhe gie. Baerde oluzhi bu giedene bayasuzhi gie.
1PE 5:3 Tande ogisan ghonilai gofende bu gonjizhi gieku yanzi uzhegha.
1PE 5:4 Ingiese Zui Fugie Adulachen xienjikude ibeizi ulie qida oluku famatu maghalai tande ogine.
1PE 5:5 Nasuchighan kunla, taye qingiezhi zhanlaolai shunji. Ta man nieniedene oluzhi goyane meilade uzhekui wiqin danlaghazhi pixilie. "Huda goyane undude uzhesan kunlai fandui giene. Goyane meilade uzhesan kunlade nenjien ogine."
1PE 5:6 Ingiese ta Hudai nenlitu kha doura goyane boghonide uzhe. Shihou kuzhese hhe tai undudaghane.
1PE 5:7 Ta munan giekulane man Hudade echigha, hhe tai gonjine.
1PE 5:8 Ta xioxin giezhi jinxin gie. Tai duitou Ibilisi onghonosan shizi mutun eneman hhemanji yozhi ijieku kun ereizho.
1PE 5:9 Ta xianxin giesan zhughene khiduzheghazhi hhei dui. Duyani gaijiula niekielienji shouku giesei ta mejiene.
1PE 5:10 Nenjien durusan Huda, Mexihai tungo giezhi tai uruzhi hhei chanqiku famade ireghasan hhe zhanshi jiere shouku giesan tai qinsi hulunshighazhi khiduzheghane, lilian ogizhi undanlaghane.
1PE 5:11 Qienlini chanqi izhi hhende ogi. Amine!
1PE 5:12 Bi Seilai tungo giezhi ene okho xinni tande huaiwo. Bi uzhese hheshi nie kekaotu gaijiu wo. Bi xin huaikushi eneshi Hudai zhenzhenji nenjien wo giezhi tande sughazhi kieliezhi ganzhen beine giezho. Ta ene nenjien jiere bei.
1PE 5:13 Tanre hhantu sunghusan Babilunni jiohui tande kielien asazho. Mii kewon Makeye kielien asazho.
1PE 5:14 Ta oreku zhugheghala nieniedene kielien asa. Mexihai miende bisan tande man pinnan ogi gie!
2PE 1:1 Ersa Mexihade hoji, shitu danlasan Ximun-Beduru mai Huda, jiuichen Ersa Mexihai gundanni tungo giezhi bijien mutun zhiguitu xianxin gieku bisan kunlade xin huaizho.
2PE 1:2 Nenjien, pinnan Huda, mai Ezhan Ersani tanikui tungo giezhi tande olon ire gie!
2PE 1:3 Huda tebieji nenlighalane matan xienliande udu daokude keresanlai man ogizho. Goya famatu, gounighalane mai urusan hhei tanikughala ingiezho.
2PE 1:4 Enezighanyi tungo giezhi Huda zhiguitu, fugie dainni matande ogizho. Ingiedene nefuxinse iresan duyani qida olukuse tai likai gieghazhi Hudai tejiende hhantulaghazho.
2PE 1:5 Zhen ene yenyinde oluzhi ta xiacha giezhi xianxin gieku jiere gounii, gouni jiere erlini,
2PE 1:6 erlin jiere goyane kunzhi giekui, goyane kunzhi gieku jiere rennaini, rennai jiere xienliantui,
2PE 1:7 xienliantu jiere gaijiulade orekui, gaijiulade oreku jiere kunlade orekui olodogha.
2PE 1:8 Enela tande bizhi olodose mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani taniku jiere tai yama oronde wizhi xiogo witui ulie gholughane.
2PE 1:9 Kunde ene giedun uwoshi zinie chadashikui chanlazhi gholoshikui chanla dane, sugho niekielien wo. Daosan zuinini arughasei matazho.
2PE 1:10 Ingiese gaijiula, ta genjia xiacha giezhi Huda tai urusan, sunghusanyi khidunde gholugha. Ta enei giese ulie furane.
2PE 1:11 Ingiezhi giese mai Ezhan, yeshijiu jiuichen Ersa Mexihani chanqiku gojiade sunfande orone.
2PE 1:12 Ta ijin enelai mejiezhi ede bisan zhendao jiere khidunde beizho, ingieliuzhe bi enelai chan tande jilaghaye.
2PE 1:13 Bi sumulase bi amitu xienzide enelai tande jila ireghase indanji wo.
2PE 1:14 Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha made mejieghasan mutun mii shihou oloncha widakui bi mejiene.
2PE 1:15 Bi duya ijiedene ene shiqinlai tai chan jilaghane giezhi bi jinlianji xiacha giene.
2PE 1:16 Bijien mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani fugie nenli, hhe ireku shiqinlai tande kieliekushi goude bienjisan yama genzi witu guhualai ese daghazho. Bijien hhei famatui qinsi uzhezhi daozho.
2PE 1:17 Zui famatu hhense shenqi irezhi "Eneshi bi oresan mii kewon wo, bi hhende xiqi wo." giezhi hhende kieliekude hhe ada Hudase zhigui, famani jienliewo.
2PE 1:18 Bijien hhere zhiguitu ulade bikude ene shenqi asiman jierese iresanyi qinsi sonosuwo.
2PE 1:19 Matande pse xienzhila melie kieliesan genjia kekaotu kielien wine. Ta hhei zhuyi giese oluzho. Hheshi kharanide zhouisan zhula niekielien wo, ogheizhi eqiemaghaku hodun tai zhughede khizhetula zhouine.
2PE 1:20 Ta mejieku zui zhunyonishi ene wo, jinwun jieredu soyuji melie kieliesan kielienlai goyane isighala jieshi giese ulie olune.
2PE 1:21 Melie kieliesan kielienshi kunni isighala kieliesan pusho, Shenlin kunni zhughei gojiolughadene Hudai isii kielieghazho.
2PE 2:1 Eqighandei bexinlai dunda jia xienzhila khizhesan mutun jianlai tai dundaye jia loushila khizhene. Hhela ghulazhi kunni widaghaku daolini ireghane. Hhela goyai shuisan Ezhanni ulie renjizhi widakude holune.
2PE 2:2 Ingieliuzhe olon kunla hhela lon kijiezhi hu giesanyi daghane. Hhelai yenyinghala zhendaoni sugiene.
2PE 2:3 Hhela tanxin giezhi ghudanghala tai jierese haochu ereine giezho. Huda hhelade eqighanse zui jinjizho, hhelai widaghakui danwu ulie giene.
2PE 2:4 Huda zui fanjisan qienxienlai ese rouliedene dozoheini khara nokiende bendazhi panjikui sagheighazho.
2PE 2:5 Pse eqighanku duyani ese rouliedene xienlian witu kunlai duyade hunshui ireghazhi zinie gundanni chonjisan Nuhhani nie gie neiman kunyi feilieghawo.
2PE 2:6 Pse Sodoma, Emola ghua chenshide zui jinjidene sideragha funiesun gholughazhi 1 houku xienlian witu kunlade jingao giezho.
2PE 2:7 Zinie mouxien kunla hu giesande yuchou giesan gou kun Luteini jiuiwo.
2PE 2:8 Hhe gou kun hhelai dunda niudunie souzhi hhela giesan mouxiennilai chanlazhi sonosuse hhei gou zhugheni otuzho.
2PE 2:9 Ingiese Ezhan xienliantu kunyi shiikuse matugie jiuizhi gou witu kunyi feilieghadene panjiku udude faikui mejiene.
2PE 2:10 Tebieshi beyeni zannan nefuxinni daghasan kunla, pse qienlini yamacha ulie teisan kunlai genjia ingiene. Hhela jionaoghazhi goyane fugiede uzhezhi asiman jieredu famatulase ulie ayidene sugienema,
2PE 2:11 qienxienliuzhe fugie lilian, nenli bidene sugieku kielienghala Ezhanyi melie asiman jieredu famatulai ulie zhane.
2PE 2:12 Enezighan jia loushila olusanse alaku, yama sumula daku chushen mutun goya sugiesanne ulie mejiene, chushen mutun widane.
2PE 2:13 Hhela gou wini giedene goyai jiere gou wini ireghazho. Hhela udu hu giese bayasukui wo giezho. Tanre hhantu ijiekude piendakui giezhi bayasuzho. Hhelashi goujia, cheiqisan wo.
2PE 2:14 Hhela jin piofen giekui ereizho, ulie beidene zui fanjine. Bixin kunlai miine. Hhelai zhughede tanxin gieku gon oluwo. Hhelashi kharakui wo.
2PE 2:15 Hhela zhen moni bendadene Bierni kewon Balanni moni daghazhi xiemacha echiwo. Balan zhendan witu baerde xiqi bidene
2PE 2:16 goya codasandene kheilaghawo. Enzheghe kielien kielie danema, kunni shenqighala kielien kieliezhi ene xienzhi fenjiulisei danlawo.
2PE 2:17 Enezighan kunlashi usu witu bula wo, honfen kei feiliesan u niekielien wo. Zui khara oronni hhelade zhunbei giezho.
2PE 2:18 Hhela yama oronde wiku fugie kielien kieliezhi hu gieku nefuxinghala hhezighan codasan shenhose jian likai giesan kunlai miizho.
2PE 2:19 Hhela kunlade ziyu ogine giezhi dain giezhoma, goyane qida olukude hoji danlazho. Kunni yan hanshiliese yande hoji danlazho.
2PE 2:20 Kunla mai Ezhan, yeshijiu jiuichen Ersa Mexihai tanikughala duyani zannannise andadene zannanni pse hhelai jiohoro giezhi hanshiliese hhelai khuinashiku qinkon eqighankude ulie kurune.
2PE 2:21 Hhela zhen moni tanidene jienliesan zhiguitu minlinni bendase ulie mejiekuse da gou wo.
2PE 2:22 Kunla kieliesan kielien shuhua wo, hhelai jiere gholuwo, "Noghei kharei ire goya benzhesanne ijiene." "Wagha arughasan khighei pse shuwade ghoghoreine."
2PE 3:1 Mii orentula, eneshi bi tande huaisan ji 2 hui xin wo. Ene ghua xin dunda tai qixin giezhi loushi zhugheitai olodoghane giezho.
2PE 3:2 Zhiguitu xienzhila melie kieliesan kielienyi, pse tai shitulai tungo giezhi Ezhan, yeshijiu jiuichen ogisan minlinyi tai jila ireghane giezho.
2PE 3:3 Ta mejieku zui zhunyonishi ene wo, duya baraku xienzide uzhezhi xiniechen kunla khizhedene duranghalane giezhi uzhezhi xiniezhi
2PE 3:4 "Ersa irene giezhi dain giesan khala wine? Mai xienrenla fugusanse eli kutula yanyanjila man wine, zui melieshida zhayaghasanghala niekielien wo." giezhi kieliene.
2PE 3:5 Hhela eqighandei Hudai kielienghala asimanni giesei, pse zemin ususe khizhezhi usughala gholusei nanxighan matazho.
2PE 3:6 Hhe shihouku duyani usughala manjidene widaghawoma,
2PE 3:7 edeku asiman, zeminni yen Hudai kielienghala feilieghazhi xienlian witu kunlai panjizhi widaghaku hhe udu kurune. Hhe shihoude asiman, zeminni khanghala tulie widaghane.
2PE 3:8 Mii orentula, enei ta bu mata, Ezhan uzhese niudushi 1000 nien wo, 1000 nienshi niudu wo.
2PE 3:9 Ezhan niezhan kunla sumulasan mutun dain giesanne danwu giezhi ulie chenjighakui pusho. Shijishan hhe tai rennai giezhi nieda ulie widaghadene jien kunlai geizhen gieghaku duran wo.
2PE 3:10 Ezhanni udu ghughei mutun irene. Hhe udude nie fugie shenqi irese asiman wida khine. Asiman jieredulai khanghala tulie widaghane. Zemin, zemin jiere giesanlai man widaghane.
2PE 3:11 Yanyanjila man ingie widase ta matunie kun danlane? Ta indan zhiguide, xienliande udu daokuni wo.
2PE 3:12 Hudai udui panjizhi ghujighan ire gie. Hhe udu kuzhese asimanyi khan tulie widaghane, asiman jieredulai tulie xiui widaghane.
2PE 3:13 Matan Huda dain giesan mutun gundanni durusan shini asiman, shini zeminni sagheizho.
2PE 3:14 Ingiese mii orentula, ta ene shiqinlai sagheise xiacha giezhi goyane bu zannanshighadene yama kheilakui wizhi Hudare heqishi.
2PE 3:15 Mai Ezhan rennai giekushi jiuiku jihui wo giezhi sumula. Zhen matan oresan gaijiu Baolo zhao Huda hhende ogisan aghelighala tande xin huaisan mutun wo.
2PE 3:16 Hhei xinla jiere man enezighan shiqinlai kieliezho. Xin jiere niezhanlai dunjireku chijiashi erlin witu, undan witu kunla psedu jinwun mutun codazhi lijie giedene goyane widaghawo.
2PE 3:17 Ingiese mii orentula, ta enei eqighan mejiese goude xioxin gie. Pse mouxien kunlai codasan tai miidene goya undanlasan oronsene anda boune.
2PE 3:18 Ta mai Ezhan, yeshijiu jiuichen Ersa Mexihani nenjien, taniku jiere henda. Kuaikui edese chanqi hhende ogi. Amine!
1JO 1:1 Hhe dei qiikude bisan aminni kielien giezhi urusan hhei tande kielieye. Bijien hhei chenliezhi daowo, nudundene chujieghezhi daozho, qinsi uzhezhi khaghalane maqizhi daowo.
1JO 1:2 Ene amin xienjizhi bijien uzhezhi daowo. Ganzhen beizhi ene chanqiku aminni tande kielieye. Hhe Huda Adaghala izhi hhantu wo, ede bijiende xienjighazho.
1JO 1:3 Bijien chanlasan, chenliesanne tande kieliekushi tai bijienre laiwon gieghane giezho. Matanyi laiwonshi Ada, hhei kewon Ersa Mexihare laiwon giekuni wo.
1JO 1:4 Ene kielienni tande huaizhi ogikushi matanyi hende bayasughane giezho.
1JO 1:5 Hudashi gon wo. Hheni sudoro kharani goujida uwo. Eneshi bijien Ezhanse chenliedene tande chonjizhi ogisan xioxi wo.
1JO 1:6 Matan Hudaghala laiwon giezho giezhi kieliedene kharanide yose ghudan kieliezho, zhendaoi ese zunjizho.
1JO 1:7 Hhe goyane gon dunda biku mutun matanye gon dunda yose matan nienierene laiwon giezho. Pse hhei kewon Ersani chusun mai zuini man waghazhi arughane.
1JO 1:8 Matande zui uwo giezhi kieliese goyane piendazho, mai sudoro zhendao uwo.
1JO 1:9 Matan zuine renjise Huda kekao, gundan wo, mai zuini mienliene. Mai codasanlai man arughane.
1JO 1:10 Matan zui uye fanjizho giezhi kieliese Hudai ghudanchi danlaghazho. Hhei kielien mai sudoro uwo.
1JO 2:1 Mii kesilaya, bi enei tande huaikushi tai zui ulie fanjighane giezho. Kien zui fanjise Adai melie matande nie banjichen wine. Hheshi nie gundan kun, Ersa Mexiha wo.
1JO 2:2 Hhe mai zuini deilazhi fuguwo. Zi mai zuide pusho, qienxiani kunlai zuide oluzhi fuguwo.
1JO 2:3 Matan Hudai minlinyi zunjise matan Hudai tanikui mejiene.
1JO 2:4 Kien "Hhei tanine." giezhi kieliedene hhei minlinyi ulie zunjise ghudan kieliezho, zhendao hhei sudoro uwo.
1JO 2:5 Kien Hudai kielienyi zunjise Hudade zhenzhenji orezho. Ingiese matan hhei sudoro bikui mejiene.
1JO 2:6 Kien goyane Hudai sudoro beizho giezhi kieliese indan Ersa Mexiha mutun giekuni wo.
1JO 2:7 Mii orentula, ede bi tande huaisanshi shini minlin pusho. Eneshi ta dei qiikude jienliesan khuichen minlin wo. Ene khuichen minlinshi ta chenliezhi daosan kielien wo.
1JO 2:8 Ingieliuzhe bi tande nie shini minlin huaizho, Mexihai miende tai miende zhenni wo. Kharani lalaghan widazhi zhenzhenji gon zhouizhi qiiwo.
1JO 2:9 Kien goyane gon dunda wo giezhi kieliedene gaijiulane henjise da kharanide wo.
1JO 2:10 Kien gaijiuladene orese gon dunda wo. Hhei sudoro zui gieghakui uwo.
1JO 2:11 Kien gaijiulani henjise kharanide wo. Hhe kharanide yozho, khala echikune ulie mejiene. Hhe kharanide yose kharani hhei sugho gholughawo.
1JO 2:12 Kewosila, bi tande xin huaikushi Mexihai niereghala tai zuini mienliewo.
1JO 2:13 Oqio kunla, bi tande xin huaikushi ta dei qiikude bisan hhei tanine. Nasuchighan kunla, bi tande xin huaikushi ta Ibilisise injiwo.
1JO 2:14 Kewosila, bi tande xin huaikushi ta Adai tanine. Oqio kunla, bi tande xin huaikushi ta dei qiikude bisan hhei tanine. Nasuchighan kunla, bi tande xin huaikushi ta khidun wo. Tai sudoro Hudai kielien wine. Ta hhe doghunnise injiwo.
1JO 2:15 Duya, duya jieredu ojienlai bu ore. Kien duyai orese hhei sudoro Adade oreku zhughe uwo.
1JO 2:16 Duya jieredulashi man beyeni nefuxin, nudunni nefuxin, baerni kuaiku wo. Enelashi Adase iresan pusho, duyase irezho.
1JO 2:17 Ene duya, duya jieredu nefuxin giekula man widane, zinie Hudai isii zunjizhi giesan kun chanqi amitu wo.
1JO 2:18 Kewosila, ede duya baraku shihou wo. Mexihani duitou irekui ta chenliezhi daozho. Ede Mexihani duitoula olon khizhewo. Ingiese matan duya baraku shihoui mejiene.
1JO 2:19 Hhela matanyi dundase khizhi echise matannughun pusho. Matanughun enbese izhi matanre hhantu wo. Hhela khizhi echise matannughun pusho bikui zhenmin giewo.
1JO 2:20 Ta hhe zhiguituse tebieji nenjienni jienliezho. Ingiese ta man mejiene.
1JO 2:21 Bi tande xin huaikushi ta zhendaoni mejie dakui pusho, ta zhendaoni mejiene, zhendaose jiani ulie khizhene.
1JO 2:22 Kienshi ghudan kieliechen wo? Ersashi Mexiha bikui chenren ulie giechen pushonu? Kien Ada, kewonni chenren ulie giese hheshijiu Mexihani duitou wo.
1JO 2:23 Kien kewonyini chenren ulie giese hhende Adaye uwo. Kewonyini chenren giese Adaye wine.
1JO 2:24 Tai kieliese ta dei qiikude chenliesanne zhughedene ghura. Ingiese ta kewon, Adai sudoro beine.
1JO 2:25 Eneshi hhe qinsi matande dain giesan chanqiku amin wo.
1JO 2:26 Bi ene shiqinlani tande huaise tani piendachen kunlai zhiizhi huaizho.
1JO 2:27 Tai kieliese tai sudoro Ezhanse jienliesan tebieji nenjien wine. Ingiese tande kiema surughaku biyo uwo. Hhei tebieji nenjien tande man surughane. Surughasanshi jiani pusho, zhenni wo. Ingiese hhe surughasan mutun ta hhei sudoro bei.
1JO 2:28 Ingiese mii kesila, ta Ersa Mexihai sudoro bei. Ingiese Ersa Mexiha xienjikude matan hhei melie yamase ayizhi shizhekui uwo.
1JO 2:29 Hhe gundan bikuni ta mejiene. Ingiese gundande giesan kunlashi man Hudase iresan kewosi bikuiye mejiene.
1JO 3:1 Ta uzhe, Ada matande matugiezhi orezho. Huda matanyi goyane kewosi wo giezhi uruzho. Matanshi hhei kesila enbene. Duyani kunla matanyi tani dakushi Hudai tani dazho.
1JO 3:2 Mii orentula, ede matanshi Hudai kesila wo. Jianlai matan matui gholukuni da ulie mejienema, Ersa Mexiha xienjikude matan hhei zhen yanziini chanlase matan hhe mutun gholukui mejiene.
1JO 3:3 Kien hhei kouizhi enei panjise goyane Ersa Mexiha mutun ganjinraghane.
1JO 3:4 Kien zui fanjise guijinni fanjizho. Guijinni fanjise jiushi zui wo.
1JO 3:5 Ersa Mexiha zuini widaghale iresanyi ta mejiene. Hhende yama zui uwo.
1JO 3:6 Hhei sudoro beisan kun zui ulie fanjine. Zui fanjisan kun hhei uzhezhi ese daozho, taniye dane.
1JO 3:7 Kewosila, ta goyane bu piendagha. Gundande giesan kunshi Ersa Mexiha mutun gundan kun wo.
1JO 3:8 Zui fanjisan kunshi Ibilisinughun wo. Ibilisi dei qiisanse zui fanjizho. Ibilisini giekuni widaghane giezhi Hudai Kewon irezhi daozho.
1JO 3:9 Hudase iresan kesila zui ulie fanjine. Hhelai sudoro Huda ogisan fure wine. Hhelashi Hudase iresan kesila wo, ingiese zui fanji dane.
1JO 3:10 Kienshi Hudai kesila, Ibilisii kesila bikui ingiezhi mejiene. Gundande ulie giezhi gaijiuladene ulie orese Hudanughun pusho.
1JO 3:11 Matan nieniedene orekuni wo. Eneshi ta dei qiikude chenliesan daoli wo.
1JO 3:12 Jiabini bu dagha. Hheshi Ibilisinughun wo. Jiune alazho. Yangiezhi alazho? Hheni giekushi mouxienni wo. Jiuni giekushi gouni wo.
1JO 3:13 Gaijiula, duyai kunla tani henjise ta bu ghanira.
1JO 3:14 Matan gaijiulade orese fugukuse amitude iresei mejiene. Ulie orechenla fugukude beizho.
1JO 3:15 Kien gaijiulani henjise kun alaku niekielien wo. Kun alasan kunni sudoro chanqiku amin wikuni ta mejiene.
1JO 3:16 Ersa Mexiha matande oluzhi aminne sheiwo. Ingiese matan yanshi orekuni mejiene. Matanye indan gaijiulade aminni sheikuni wo.
1JO 3:17 Kiende baer olon bidene nanxin jiulani uzhedene zhughene khidunde giezhi ulie gonjise Hudade oreku zhughe hhei sudoro matugie wine?
1JO 3:18 Kesila, matan orese zi amande bu kieliedene xindun giezhi shixinde gieye.
1JO 3:19 Ingiezhi giese matanshi zhendaose iresei mejiene. Matan zhughedene gui gieliuzhe mai zhughe Hudai melie undan wo. Hudashi mai zhughese pse fugie wo. Yan shiqinyiliuzhe man mejiene.
1JO 3:21 Mii orentula, mai zhughede gui ulie giese Hudai melie yama ayikui uwo,
1JO 3:22 pse hhense yan xiahua giese yan ogine. Matan hhei zunjizhi hhe bayasukui giezho.
1JO 3:23 Hhei minlinshi matan hhei kewon Ersa Mexihai niereni xianxin giekuni wo. Pse hhe ogisan minlin mutun nieniedene orekuni wo.
1JO 3:24 Kien Hudai minlinyi zunjise hhe Hudai sudoro beizho. Hudaye hhei sudoro beizho. Huda mai sudoro beisei hhe ogisan Shenlinghala mejiene.
1JO 4:1 Mii orentula, ta ruhherlani man xianxin giezhi ulie olune. Hhelashi Hudanughun enbenu pusho bikui ta shiizhi uzhekuni wo. Duya jiere ede olon jia xienzhi khizhezho.
1JO 4:2 Hudai ruhherni ingiezhi mejiene, Ersa Mexiha kun gholudene iresei chenren giese hheshi Hudase iresei enbene.
1JO 4:3 Ersa Mexihani chenren ulie giese hheshi Hudase iresan pusho. Eneshi Mexihani duitouni ruhher wo. Hhe irene giekuni ta eqighanse chenliezhoma, ede ijin duya jiere wo.
1JO 4:4 Kewosila, tashi Hudanughun wo. Tani sudoro bisan hhe duyade bisan hhense hen wo. Ingiese ta jia xienzhilase injiwo.
1JO 4:5 Hhelashi duyanughun wo. Duyani shiqinyi kieliese duyai kunla hhelani kielienni chenliene.
1JO 4:6 Matanshi Hudanughun wo. Hudai tanichen kun mai kielienni chenliene. Hudanughun pushoshi manughunni ulie chenliene. Ingiezhi hhelashi zhenni onu piendachen bikui mejiene.
1JO 4:7 Mii orentula, matan nieniedene oreye. Orekushi Hudase irezho. Orechen kunshi Hudase iresan kewosi wo, Hudai tanine.
1JO 4:8 Ulie orechen Hudai tani dane. Hudashi oreku wo.
1JO 4:9 Huda orekune matande ingiezhi uzheghawo. Huda niekozi kewonne peizhi duyade ireghadene hhei tungo giezhi matanyi amituraghawo.
1JO 4:10 Eneshijiu oreku wo. Matan Hudade oresan pusho. Huda matande orezho. Hhe matande orezhi kewonne peizhi ireghadene mai zuini deilazhi fuguwo.
1JO 4:11 Mii orentula, Huda matande ingiezhi orezho. Matanye indan nieniedene orekuni wo.
1JO 4:12 Kun Hudai uzhezhi ese daozhoma, matan nieniedene orese Huda mai sudoro beizho. Hhei oreku mai dunda chengun oluwo.
1JO 4:13 Huda matande Shenlinne ogizho. Ingiese matan Hudai sudoro, Huda matanyi sudoro beisei mejiene.
1JO 4:14 Ada kewonne peizhi duyani kunlai jiuighale iresei bijien chanlawo, ye ganzhen beine.
1JO 4:15 Kien Ersashi Hudai Kewon giezhi renjise Huda hhei sudoro beizho. Hheye Hudai sudoro beizho.
1JO 4:16 Huda matande orekui matan mejiezho, xianxinye giezho. Hudashi oreku wo. Orechen kun Hudai sudoro beizho. Hudaye hhei sudoro beizho.
1JO 4:17 Oreku mai dunda ingiezhi chengun oluwo. Ersa Mexiha matugiese matanye duyade qingiene. Ingiese matan panjiku udude yamase ayikui uwo.
1JO 4:18 Orekui sudoro ayikui uwo. Zhenzhenji orese ayikui man widaghane. Ayichen kun faikuse ayizho. Ayichen kunni sudoro orekui chaizho.
1JO 4:19 Matan orekushi Huda xien matande orezho.
1JO 4:20 Kien, "Hudade orene." giezhi kieliedene gaijiulane henjise ghudan kieliezho. Chanla shidaku gaijiuladene ore dase chanla daku Hudade ore dane.
1JO 4:21 Hudade orechen kunla gaijiuladeneye orekuni wo. Eneshi hhe matande ogisan minlin wo.
1JO 5:1 Kien Ersashi Mexiha wo giezhi xianxin giese hheshi Hudase iresan kewosi wo. Adade oresan kun hhei kewosideye orene.
1JO 5:2 Matan Hudade orezhi hhei minlinyi zunjise matan Hudai kesilade orekui mejiene.
1JO 5:3 Matan Hudai minlinni zunjise Hudade orezho. Hheni minlinni zunjiku hende chijia uwo.
1JO 5:4 Hudase iresan kesila duyase inji shidane. Mai xianxin giekughala injine.
1JO 5:5 Duyase injisanshi kien wine? Ersashi Hudai Kewon wo giezhi xianxin giesanla pushonu?
1JO 5:6 Hheshijiu usu, chusunghala iresan Ersa Mexiha wo. Zinie usughala iresan pusho. Usu, chusunghala irewo. Enende Shenlin ganzhen beine. Shenlinshi zhendao wo.
1JO 5:7 Ganzhen beisanshi ghuran wo.
1JO 5:8 Shenlin, chusun, usu wo. Ene ghurulie niekielien ganzhen beine.
1JO 5:9 Matan kunni ganzhenni jienliese Hudai ganzhenni genjia jienliekuni wo. Ene ganzhenshi Huda kewondene oluzhi beisan wo.
1JO 5:10 Hudai Kewonni xianxin giechen kunyi sudoro ene ganzhen wine. Hudai xianxin ulie giechen kun Hudai ghudanchi danlaghazho. Huda kewondene ganzhen beisanyi hhe xianxin ese giezho.
1JO 5:11 Eneshijiu ganzhen beisan wo, "Huda chanqiku aminni matande ogiwo. Ene chanqiku hheni kewonni sudoro wine."
1JO 5:12 Kewon bichen kunde amin wine. Hudai Kewon wichen kunde amin uwo.
1JO 5:13 Bi enezighanyi tande huaikushi Hudai Kewonni niereni xianxin giesan tande chanqiku amin bikuni mejieghane giezho.
1JO 5:14 Matan Hudai melie echikude ulie ayine. Zhao hhei isi mutun xiahua giese hhe chenliene.
1JO 5:15 Matan xiahua giesei hhe chenliekui mejiese yan xiahua giese yan ogikuiye mejiene.
1JO 5:16 Kien gaijiula ulie fuguku zui fanjisei chanlase hhende oluzhi onxian gie. Huda ulie fuguku zui fanjisan kunlade amin ogine. Fuguku zui fanjise bi hhende onxian gie giezhi ulie kieliene.
1JO 5:17 Gou winilashi man zui woma, man fuguku zui pusho.
1JO 5:18 Hudase iresan kesila zui ulie fanjikui matan mejiene. Hudai kewon hhelai bouise Ibilisi hhelai hei dane.
1JO 5:19 Matanshi Hudanughun bikui, duyashi man Ibilisii kha doura bikui matan mejiene.
1JO 5:20 Matan Hudai Kewon irezhi matande agheli, lijie gieku nenli ogidene zhenzhenji Hudai tanighasei, pse matan hhe zhennii sudoro, yejiushi hhei kewon Ersa Mexihai sudoro bikui mejiene. Hheshijiu zhenzhenji Huda wo, chanqiku amin wo.
1JO 5:21 Kesila, ta nigiedalase gholodo.
2JO 1:1 Bishi nie zhanlao wo. Huda sunghusan funi pse hhei kesilade xin huaizho. Bi tande shixin orezho. Zinie bi pusho, zhendaoni mejiesanla man tande orezho.
2JO 1:2 Tande orekushi zhendaoni yenyin wo. Ene zhendao mai sudoro wine, chanqi matanre hhantu wo.
2JO 1:3 Ada Huda, Adai Kewon Ersa Mexiha zhendao, orekuni zunjisan matande nenjien, ubali xiiku, pinnan ogi gie!
2JO 1:4 Bi uzhese chii niezhan kesila Adani minlinyi zunjizhi zhendaode yozho. Ingiese bi hende bayasuzho.
2JO 1:5 Ingiese funi, bi chade goude fenfulaye. Matan indan nieniedene orekuni wo. Eneshi nie shini minlin pusho, matan dei qiikude jienliesan minlin wo.
2JO 1:6 Matan Hudai minlinni zunjizhi giese eneshijiu oreku wo. Hhe ogisan minlinshi nieniedene orekuni wo. Enei ta eqighanse chenliezhi daowo.
2JO 1:7 Duya jiere olon piendachen kun khizhezho. Hhela Ersa Mexiha beye gholuzhi iresei ulie renjine. Hhelashi piendachen kun wo, Mexihani duitou wo.
2JO 1:8 Ta xioxin giezhi bijien giesan wilielai belien bu gholughadene Huda ogiku soyuji jianlini man linla.
2JO 1:9 Kien Mexihani sughasande ulie beizhi gholodose hhei sudoro Huda uwo. Sughasande beise hhei sudoro Ada Huda, kewonni Ersa Mexiha wine.
2JO 1:10 Kien Mexihani ene izhun sughasanghala ulie irese giedene bu jienlie. Kielienye bu asa.
2JO 1:11 Hhelade kielien asase hhelai doghunnide hhantulazho.
2JO 1:12 Bi tande huaiku shiqin da olon woma, meshuighala giejie jiere huaiku duran uwo. Bi xiwon giese tani hhende echizhi danmien kielieku duran wo. Ingiese matan hende bayasune.
2JO 1:13 Huda sunghusan eghechiichii kesila chade kielien asazho.
3JO 1:1 Bishi nie zhanlao wo, zhughe jieredu Gaiyude xin huaizho. Bi chade shixin orezho.
3JO 1:2 Mii orentu, ruhherchii gou biku mutun shiqinlachii, beyechii man gou woshijiu.
3JO 1:3 Gaijiula kharei iredene chii zhughede zhendao wine, pse chi zhao zhendao mutun giezho giezhi zhenmin giese bi hende bayasuzho.
3JO 1:4 Bi chenliese kesilami zhao zhendao mutun giezho giese enense bayasukui uwo.
3JO 1:5 Mii orentu, chi gaijiulade tani daseye shixinde zhaogu giezho.
3JO 1:6 Hhela iredene ene jiohuini kunlade chi hhelade oresei kieliezho. Hhela mo yokude Huda bayasuku mutun ta izhi hhelai khughose gou wo.
3JO 1:7 Hhela Ersa Mexihani nierede oluzhi ghadane khireiwo, xianxin uye giechen niman kunlase yama ese kerewo.
3JO 1:8 Matan indan imutu kunlade banman giese oluzho. Ingiese matan zhendaode oluzhi hhelare lienshou gholune.
3JO 1:9 Ene shiqinde melieshida bi jiohuide xin huaizhoma, touzi danlakude xiqi bitu Jiutefei bijiennughunyi ese chenliezho.
3JO 1:10 Ingie bi echise hhe giesan shiqinlani kielie khizheghane. Hhe doghun kielienghala bijienni heizho. Dou enende ese kuruzhi mo yozhi chonjisan gaijiulani goya ulie jienliene, jienliene giesan kunyi ulie jienlieghane, da jiohuise tou khighane.
3JO 1:11 Mii orentu, doghunnii bu dagha, gounii dagha. Gouni giesanlashi Hudanughun wo, doghunni giesanla Hudai uzhezhi ese daozho.
3JO 1:12 Olon kunla Jimijiushi gou kun wo giezho, zhendao benshen hhende ganzhen beine. Bijienye hhende ganzhen beine. Bijien beisan ganzhenshi zhenni bikuni ta mejiene.
3JO 1:13 Bi chade huaiku shiqin da olon woma, meshui, bighala huaiku duran uwo.
3JO 1:14 Bi xiwon giese ghujighan chii chujieghedene danmien kielieku duran wo.
3JO 1:15 Chade pinnan ogi gie. Zhanlienla man chii asazho. Chii hhendedu zhanlienlai zhao nierezhe kielien asa.
JUD 1:1 Ersa Mexihani hoji, Yagebuni gaijiu Yuda tande xin huaizho. Tashi Ada Huda orezhi urusan wo, Ersa Mexihade oluzhi baohu giesanla wo.
JUD 1:2 Tande ubali xiiku, pinnan, orekui ologhonni ogi gie!
JUD 1:3 Mii orentula, matan hhantu jienliesan jiuiku shiqinni fanmiende bi yenlai tande xin huaiku hende duralazhoma, ede bi sumulase ta xianxin giekune goude bareizhi baohu gie giezhi xin huaizhi fenfulaku biyo wine. Ene xianxin giekushi Huda shentulade 1 huide ogisan wo.
JUD 1:4 Niezhan kunla tai dunda ghulazhi orozhezho. Enelashi xienlian witu kun wo, hhelai zuini jinjikui eqighanse huaizho. Hhela Hudai nenjienni lon kijiezhi hu giekui gholughazho. Da mai zi niekozi zhanguiji, Ezhan Ersa Mexihai ulie renjine.
JUD 1:5 Ta ene shiqinyi 1 huide man mejiewoma, bi tande pse jilaghaye giezho. Ersa bexinlane Aijise jiuidene khuinashi niezhan xianxin ulie giechen kunlai widaghawo.
JUD 1:6 Pse goya wizidene ulie beizhi sousan oronsene likai giesan qienxienlani fugie panjiku udu kuzhetula qieshenghala chanqi soziladene zui kharanide khazho.
JUD 1:7 Pse Sodoma, Emola, zhouwidedu chenshini kunlaye hhela mutun kunlare lon kijiezhi zhenchan wini naduzho. Ingiese hhelai faizhi ibeizi ulie xinieku khande teidene kunlade jingao giezho.
JUD 1:8 Hhe ghulazhi iresan jia loushilaye niekielien wo. Oruntan zhoujiliedene qienli wine giezho. Beyene zannanshighazho, qienlini yamacha ulie teine, da asiman jieredu famatulai sugiene.
JUD 1:9 Fugie qienxien Mijialeliuzhe qingiezhi ese giezho. Hhe Ibilisighala Musani fugusan beyede oluzhi jianjindukude sugieku kielienghala hhende zui ese jinjiwo. Zi ezhan chii kheila gie giewo.
JUD 1:10 Enela goya mejie dasanlane suibiende sugiezho. Sumula daku chushen mutun duranghala giezhi goyane qida olughazho.
JUD 1:11 Hhelade gou widawo! Hhela Jiabini mode yozho. Balan mutun baerde oluzhi codasande holu orowo. Kela mutun zodui giedene fuguwo.
JUD 1:12 Ezhanni orekui jilazhi hhantulazhi ijiekude hhelashi xi jieredu zannanni wo. Ulie shizhezhi ijiene, zi goyane chudughachen yanbashi wo. Ghura witu olien mutun kei feilie yozho. Baye xienzii alima ulie souku mutunghala niekielien wo. Icha fuguwo, lien genzi xi khizhese liancha fuguwo.
JUD 1:13 Haini fugie lan mutun goya shizheku momozine xirei khizheghane. Jiujia yoku hodun niekielien wo, zui khara oronni hhelade chanqi jiezho.
JUD 1:14 Jiushi enezighan kunlai zhiizhi Adanni 7 dai sunzi Idileisi Hudai kielienyi deilazhi ingiezhi melie kieliewo, "Uzhe, ezhan qienwon zhiguitu qienxienlarene iredene
JUD 1:15 kunlai man panjine. Xienlian witu kunla giesan xienlian witu wilielani, pse xienlian witu zui fanjichen kunla Hudai fandui giezhi hu kieliesan kieliende zui jinjine."
JUD 1:16 Ene kunlade ibeizi kuru dazhi chan boxin kieliene. Yan duralase yan giene. Fugie kielien kieliene. Goya haochudene oluzhi kunlai bajie giene.
JUD 1:17 Mii orentula, mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihani shitula melieshida kieliesan kielienyi ta jila. Hhela tande ingiezhi kieliezho,
JUD 1:18 duya barakude xienlian witu kunla khizhese goya duranghalane suibiende giezhi kunlai uzhezhi xiniene giezho.
JUD 1:19 Hhe jia loushilashi kunlai danxinraghachen kun wo. Hhelade Shenlin uwo, zinie ganxi beilieku zhughe wo.
JUD 1:20 Mii orentula, ta zui zhigui xianxin gieku jierene goyalane hendagha. Shenlinyi kouizhi onxian gie.
JUD 1:21 Huda matande oresanni chan jila. Mai Ezhan Ersa Mexiha ubali xiizhi chanqiku aminni ogikui panji.
JUD 1:22 Niezhan kunla zhughedene inxin giese ta ubali xii.
JUD 1:23 Niezhan kunlai khan dundase qianlazhi jiuiku mutun jiui. Pse niezhan kunlade ubali xii. Qingiezhi giekude xioxin gie. Hhelai zuide bu hhantula.
JUD 1:24 Huda tai baohu giezhi ulie hhengereighane, tai zannannilai man widaghazhi bayasughazhi goyane fama melie beigha shidane.
JUD 1:25 Mai jiuichen niekozi Hudade mai Ezhan Ersa Mexihai tungo giezhi kuaiku, wifen, nenli, qienli zui melieshida, ede, pse chanqi izhi wine gie! Amine.
REV 1:1 Eneshi Ersa Mexiha mejieghasan wo. Deigo fashen giene giesan shiqinni hojiladene uzheghane giezhi Huda Ersade mejieghasan wo. Ingiese Ersa Mexiha qienxienne peizhi Yaheiya hojidene qinchude mejieghawo.
REV 1:2 Yaheiya chanlasanlane man ganzhen beiwo. Jiushi Hudai kielien, pse Ersa Mexiha hhende mejieghasanlai ganzhen beizhi kieliewo.
REV 1:3 Ene shu jiere melie kieliesanlai onshizhi chenliezhi hhende jilasei zunjisanlade fuqi wine. Shihou chadashiwo.
REV 1:4 YaheiyaYaxiyani dolon jiohuide xin huaizho. Edeku, eqighanku, jianlai ireku Huda, hhei baozo meliededu dolon ruhher, pse shixinji ganzhen beisan, fugusan kun dundase tou 1 giede aminne olusan, duyai honshan dunda touzi danlasan Ersa Mexiha tande nenjien, pinnan ogi gie! Hhe matande orezhi goya chusunghalane zuise mai andaghazhi
REV 1:6 gojia gholughazhi hhei ada Hudai melie buwa danlaghawo. Kuaiku, qienlini Ersa Mexihade chanqi izhi ogi! Amine.
REV 1:7 Uzhe, hhe olien jiere irene. Jien kunla hhei uzhene. Hhei chujisan kunlaye uzhene. Duya jieredu minzula man hhei yenyinzhe wilane. Shuhuajia ingiene. Amine!
REV 1:8 Ezhan Huda kieliezho, "Bishi Alafa wo, Emeiga wo. Bishi edeku, eqighanku, jianlai ireku, nenlitu Huda wo."
REV 1:9 Bishi tai gaijiu Yaheiya wo. Ersai miende tanre hhantu kunnan shouiku, Hudai gojia, rennai giekude guzide wine. Bi Hudai kieliende oluzhi Ersade ganzhen beiku yenyinghala Bamo giesan haini dao jiere bafanzi souzho.
REV 1:10 Ezhanni udude Shenlin mii zhughei gojiolughazhi mii khuina laba tunguliesan mutun fugie shenqii bi sonosuwo.
REV 1:11 Hhe shenqi kieliezho, "Chi chanlasanne man shu jiere huaizhi Ifuso, Shimeina, Biejiamo, Tuiyatuila, Saji, Feilaqiefei, Laojijia ene dolon jiohuide khugho!"
REV 1:12 Bi ochira kien made kielien kieliesei uzhene giezho. Ochira daozhese dolon antanni zhula teizii chanlawo.
REV 1:13 Zhula teizi dunda niekozi kun hoxian kunni kewonni xianli. Fudu jien musizhi konde bouzho, antanghala echanne huighazho.
REV 1:14 Hhei qiorun, usun chighande ghonini noghosun, chasunyi xianli. Nudunni khan giedai xianli.
REV 1:15 Konni hoxian luzide siderasan gieghan tunni xianli. Shenqini olon usu usurusan shenqii xianli.
REV 1:16 Hhei borun khade dolon hodun wine. Amanseni niekozi ghua renzitu xidu khudogho khizhezhi ungieni gon faisan hherei naranni xianli.
REV 1:17 Bi hhei chanladene fugusan mutun hhei kon kondei fura bouwo. Hhe borun khane mii jiere teizhi kieliewo, "Bu ayi! Bishi tou 1 gie wo, zuihouku wo,
REV 1:18 chanqi biku wo. Uzhe, bi fuguzhi daozhoma, ede chanqi izhi amiturazho. Dou fugukuji dozoni yeshi made wine.
REV 1:19 Chi chanlasanlane man huaizhi jila. Jiushi edeku shiqinji khuina gholuku shiqin wo.
REV 1:20 Chi chanlasan mii borun khani dolon hodun, pse dolon antanni zhula teizini mimishi ene wo. Dolon hodunshi dolon jiohuini qienxien wo, dolon zhula teizishi dolon jiohui wo."
REV 2:1 "Chi Ifuso jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Borun khadene dolon hodunni bareizhi dolon antanni zhula teizi dunda yosan hhe kieliezho.
REV 2:2 Chi giesan, khishulasan, rennai giesei bi mejiene. Doghun kunlai ulie roulieseiye mejiene. Goyaneshi shitu wo giezhoma, shijishan pushotulai chi kaoyen giedene jianini khizheghazho.
REV 2:3 Chi rennai giezhi mii nierede oluzhi jienchi giezhi hhechekune mejie dazho.
REV 2:4 Ingieliuzhe ene nie shiqinde bi chii kheilane, dei qiikude orekui chi widaghazho.
REV 2:5 Ingiese chi nie sumula. Khalase banjizhoshi hhense geizhen giezhi dei qiikude giesan wilielai gie. Chi geizhen ulie giese bi chii hhende iredene zhula teiziichii yenlaiku oronse agi echine.
REV 2:6 Ingieliuzhe chade intu nie gou shiqin wine. Nigela paini giesanlai bi henjisan mutun chi henjizho.
REV 2:7 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu. Injisan kunlade Hudai qientanyi aminni mutunni alimai ogizhi ijieghane.'"
REV 2:8 "Chi Shimeina jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Tou 1 gie, zuihouku, fugudene aminne olusan hhe kieliezho.
REV 2:9 Chii kunnan, nanxinni bi mejiene. Shijishan chi bayan wo. Hhezighan goyalaneshi Yutai kun wo giesan kunla tai sugiesanyi bi mejiene. Shijishan hhelashi Yutai kun pusho, Ibilisire hhantuku kun wo.
REV 2:10 Chade kuzhene giesan kuse chi bu ayi. Uzhe, Ibilisi tai dundadu ezighan kunlai bafanzide khazhi tai shiine. Tai hharudu zayalane. Chi fugutula shixinji giese bi chade aminni maghalai ogine.
REV 2:11 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu. Injisan kunlai ji 2 gie fuguku hei dane.'"
REV 2:12 "Chi Biejiamo jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Ghua renzitu xidu khudogho winetu hhe kieliezho.
REV 2:13 Chi sousan oronni bi mejiene, Ibilisii baozo hhende wo. Made shixinji ganzhen beisan Anqipai tai hhende, jiushi Ibilisi sousan oronde alakude chi mii nierei goude zunjizhi mii xianxin giesanni ese bendawo.
REV 2:14 Ingieliuzhe giedun shiqin jiere bi chii kheilane. Tai dundadu niezhan kunla Balan sughasei shunjizho. BalanBalede sughazhi Isilie bexinlai zui fanjighazhi nigiedade teisan dunxii ijieghazhi lon kijieghazho.
REV 2:15 Niekielien wo, chii hhende niezhan kunla Nigela paini surughasei shunjizho.
REV 2:16 Ingiese chi geizhen gie. Pse bi chii hhende irezhi amanne khudoghoghala enelai eghine.
REV 2:17 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu. Injisan kunlade bi niuighasan manani ogizhi pse chighan tashii ogine. Tashi jiere shini niere huaizho. Jienliesan kunse chugo tanichen kun nieda uwo.'"
REV 2:18 "Chi Tuiyatuila jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Nudunni khan gieda mutun, konni gieghan tun mutun Hudai kewon kieliezho.
REV 2:19 Chii gieku, oreku, xianxin gieku, kunlade oluzhi gieku, rennai giekui bi mejiene. Chi khuinashi giesan melieshi giesanse da olon bikuiye mejiene.
REV 2:20 Ingieliuzhe ene nie shiqinde bi chii kheilane. Goyaneshi xienzhi wo giesan bierei Yexibieni chi renjizho. Hhe mii hojilade sughazhi hhelai miidene lon kijieghazhi nigiedade teisan dunxii ijieghazho.
REV 2:21 Bi hhende geizhen gieku jihui ogizhi daozhoma, hhe lon kijiekune geizhen ulie geine.
REV 2:22 Bi jingao gieye. Bi deigo hhei giemereghazhi chonban jiere bendane. Hhere hhantu piofen giesanlaye hhe giesanlai geizhen ulie giese fugie zeinan dunda bendane.
REV 2:23 Bi hhere niekielienji giesan kunlai alane. Ingiese soyuji jiohuila man bishi kunni sumuladanji zhughei uzhechen bikui mejiene. Bi tai giekuzhe jien kunde kharulune.
REV 2:24 Ta Tuiyatuiladedu hhe sughasei ese shunjisan, kunla kieliese Ibilisini chijia isi wo giesanni ese surusan kunlade bi kielieye, bi psedu achanni tai jiere ulie teine.
REV 2:25 Zinie bi iretula ta bisanne goude barei.
REV 2:26 Injisan, mii isii zunjizhi zuihou kusan kunlade bi soyuji gojialai gonjiku qienli ogine.
REV 2:27 Hhe kun qiemu zhugunghala waganganyi ghalughaku mutun hhelai gonjine.
REV 2:28 Eneshi bi adasene linlasan qienlighala niekielien wo. Bi pse eqiemaghaku hodunni hhende ogine.
REV 2:29 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu!'"
REV 3:1 "Chi Saji jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Hudai dolon ruhher, dolon hodun winetu hhe kieliezho. Chi giekui bi mejiene, zhao niereghala chi amitu woma, shijishan chi fuguzho.
REV 3:2 Chi xiereidene deigo fugune giezhi goujinie feiliesanlai khiduzhegha. Bi mejiese chi giesanla mii Hudai melie hulunni nieda uwo.
REV 3:3 Ingiese chi daolini matugie jienliezhi chenliesei jiladene zunjizhi geizhen gie. Chi ulie xiereise bi ghughei mutun irene, bi yan xienzide chii hhende irekui chi jiedui ulie mejiene.
REV 3:4 Ingieliuzhe Sajide niezhanla jienne ese zannanshighazhi hhela pei shidadene chighan jien musizhi bighala hhantu yone.
REV 3:5 Injisan kunla ingiezhi chighan jien musizhi hhelai nierei aminni jilasan benzi jierese ulie widaghane. Bi adane melie, hhei qienxienlai melie hhelai nierei chenren giene.
REV 3:6 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu!'"
REV 3:7 "Chi Feilaqiefei jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Dawudeni yeshii bareizhi niese kiemada kha dane, khase kiemada nie daku hhe zhiguitu, zhenni kieliezho.
REV 3:8 Chi giekui bi mejiene. Chade goujinie lilian bizhi mii kielienyi zunjizhi mii nierei ese ghudanduzho. Uzhe, bi chii melie nie keighasan wijienni teiwo, kiemada kha dane.
REV 3:9 Hhezighan Ibilisire hhantuku kunla, goyaneshi Yutai kun wo giezhoma shijishan pushotu ghudanchilai bi chii kon melie xiutulieghazhi bi chade oresei hhelade mejieghane.
REV 3:10 Chi mii kielienyi zunjizhi rennai giezho. Ingiese duyai kunlai man kaoyen gieku shihoude bi chii baohu giene.
REV 3:11 Bi ghujighande irene. Chi bisanlane goude barei, pse jianli giesan maghalai kunla qianla echine.
REV 3:12 Injisan kunlai mii Hudai dajiende tuhua danlaghazhi pse likai ulie gieghane. Bi Hudane nierei, Hudai chenshii nierei, pse mii shini nierei man hhei jiere huaine. Ene chenshishi asimanse, mii Hudai hhense bouzhesan shini Yelusalen wo.
REV 3:13 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu!'"
REV 3:14 "Chi Laojijia jiohuini qienxiende xin huaizhi kielie, 'Hhe Amine giesan, shixinji shuhua ganzhen beisan, Huda zhayaghasan genzi kieliezho.
REV 3:15 Chi giekui bi mejiene, chi kuiqienye uwo, hhereiye uwo. Mii duranshi chi kuiqien onu hhereishijiu.
REV 3:16 Chi unchu usu mutun kuiqien wiji hherei uwoshi bi chii amansene nunpu khighane.
REV 3:17 Chi kieliese bi bayan wo, facai giezhi yama ese chaizho giezhoma, chade lolien, ubali, nanxin, sugho, hulan muchughun bikui chi ulie mejiene.
REV 3:18 Bi chade sughaye, chi mase khanghala tuliezhi daosan antanni agizhi goyane bayazhegha. Chighan jien agizhi musidene hulan muchughun shizhekune bu khizhegha. Pse nienye agizhi teidene nudunne chanlagha.
REV 3:19 Jien bi oresanlade kheilazhi gonjine. Ingiese chi rexinne khizhegha, geizhen gie.
REV 3:20 Uzhe, bi ghadane beidene wijienyi eghizho. Mii shenqii sonosudene wijienyi niese bi hhei hhende orozhi bi hheghala, hhe bighala hhantu ijiene.
REV 3:21 Injisan kunlai bi baozo jierene goyarene hhantu soughane. Hoxian bi injidene adane baozo jiere hhere hhantu souku niekielien wo.
REV 3:22 Chighin bitu kunla Shenlin jiohuilade kieliesan kielienni chenliendu!'"
REV 4:1 Enense khuinashi bi chanlase asiman jieredu wijien niezho. Bi eqighandei sonosusan laba feiliesan shenqi mutun made kieliezho, "Chi mii enende khizhe. Ihou kenjin gholuku shiqinlai bi chade uzheghaye."
REV 4:2 Shenlin deigo mii zhughei gojiolughazhi bi chanlase asiman jiere nie baozo wine. Hhende niekozi souzho.
REV 4:3 Hhe sousei uzhese noghon ishi, hulan boushini xianli. Pse baozoni lun sulasan wiqizhi noghon boushini xianli.
REV 4:4 Baozoni izhonde 24 gie zowi wo. Zowi jiere 24 gie zhanlao souzho, chighan jien musizhi qiorun jiere antanni maghala zhozho.
REV 4:5 Shanjien, olien tunguliesan fugie shenqi baozose khizhezho. Pse dolon hoba baozo melie siderazho. Ene dolon zhulashi Hudai dolon ruhher wo.
REV 4:6 Baozo melie nie boli mutun hai, shuijinyi xianli. Baozo zhouwini simiende jieran amitu ojien wo, beyeni melie khuina nudun duruzho.
REV 4:7 Tou 1 gie shizini xianli, ji 2 gie fughereini xianli, ji 3 gieni ungie kunni ungiei xianli, ji 4 gie musisan inni xianli.
REV 4:8 Jieran amitu ojiende niede zhighon siban wo, beye jiereni nudun duruzho. Hhela udu xieniji ese beidene kieliezho, "Zhigui! Zhigui! Zhigui! Ezhan, Fugie Nenlitu Hudashi eqighanku, edeku, jianlai ireku wo."
REV 4:9 Jieran amitu ojien kuaiku, zhigui, mafan giekui baozo jiere sousan, chanqi izhi amituku hhende niefanie ogikude,
REV 4:10 24 gie zhanlao baozo sousan chanqi izhi amituku hhende papaladene beiizhi goya maghalane baozo konde teidene kieliezho,
REV 4:11 "Mai Ezhan, mai Huda kuaiku, zhigui, nenlini pei shidane. Chi yanyanjilai zhayaghazho. Yanyanjilashi chii isighala zhayaghadene bisan wo."
REV 5:1 Bi chanlase baozo sousei borun khade horosan shu wine. Ghadane, sudoroji uru huaizhi dolon fenqioghala fenjizho.
REV 5:2 Bi pse chanlase nie lilian fugietu qienxien fugiede waradazhi kieliezho, "Kien fenqioni keighazhi shuni keighakui pei shidane?"
REV 5:3 Asiman jiere, zemin jiere, zemin doura hhe shuni keighazhi onshichen uwo.
REV 5:4 Peizhi keighazhi onshichen wise bi hende wilazho.
REV 5:5 Zhanlao dundase niekozi made kieliezho, "Bu wila! Uzhe, Yuda paini shizi, jiushi Dawudeni houdei ijin injiwo. Hhe shuni keighazhi dolon fenqioni keigha shidane!"
REV 5:6 Bi pse chanlase baozo, jieran amitu ojien, zhanlao dunda nie ghoni ghughan beizho. Alazhi daosei xianli. Hhende dolon gocha, dolon nudun wine, eneshi duyai gochude peizhi echighasan Hudai dolon ruhher wo.
REV 5:7 Ene ghoni ghughan yo dao baozo sousei borun khase shuni agiwo.
REV 5:8 Shuni agise jieran amitu ojien, 24 gie zhanlao ghoni ghughanyi melie papalawo. Manla qin, xian durusan antanni luzii bareizho. Ene xianshi shentulai onxian wo.
REV 5:9 Hhela shini donghala doulazho, "Chi shuni agizhi pei shidane. Dolon fenqioni keighazhi pei shidane. Chii alazhi daozho, goya chusunghalane Hudade oluzhi go pai, go kielien, go minzu, go gojialase kunlai agizho.
REV 5:10 Hhelai mai Hudade oluzhi buwatu gojia gholughawo, Zemin jiere qienli bareine."
REV 5:11 Bi chanlazhi sonosuse baozo, amitu ojien, zhanlaolai zhouwide olon qienxienlai shenqi wine, hhela olonde shuzi uwo.
REV 5:12 Qienxienla fugie shenqighala kieliezho, "Alazhi daosan ghoni ghughan nenli, bayan, agheli, lilian, zhigui, kuaiku, doulakui peizhi jienlie shidane."
REV 5:13 Bi sonosuse asiman jiere, zemin jiere, zemin doura, hainughun, asiman zemin dunda yanyanji zhayaghasanla man kieliezho, "Doulaku, zhigui, fama, qienlini man baozo sousanji ghoni ghughande chanqi izhi ogi!"
REV 5:14 Jieran amitu ojien amine giezho. Zhanlaolaye papaladene beiizho.
REV 6:1 Bi chanlase ghoni ghughan dolon fenqio dundadu ji 1 giei keighakude sonosuse jieran amitu ojien dundadu niekozii shenqini olien tunguliesan mutun, "Chi ire." giezhi kieliezho.
REV 6:2 Bi chanlase nie chighan morei wine. Morei jiere unusan gunjien bareizhi jianli giesan maghalai hhende ogizho. Hhe khizhedene injizhi pse injine giezho.
REV 6:3 Ji 2 gie fenqioni keighakude bi sonosuse ji 2 gie amitu ojien, "Chi ire." giezhi kieliezho.
REV 6:4 Pse nie morei khizhewo, hulanni wo. Morei unusande qienlini ogizhi zemin jierese pinnanni agi echise kunla nieniene alandune. Nie fugie khudoghoni hhende ogizho.
REV 6:5 Ji 3 gie fenqioni keighakude bi sonosuse ji 3 gie amitu ojien, "Chi ire." giezhi kieliezho. Bi chanlase nie khara morei wine! Morei jiere unusan khadeni shizhi bareizho.
REV 6:6 Bi sonosuse jieran amitu ojien dunda shenqi biku mutun kieliezho, "Niuduku gunzighala 2 jin boudei agine, niuduku gunzighala caigie 6 jin damai agine. Tosun, jiuni zaota bu gie!"
REV 6:7 Ji 4 gie fenqioni keighakude bi sonosuse ji 4 gie amitu ojien, "Chi ire." giezhi kieliezho.
REV 6:8 Bi chanlase nie boro morei wine! Morei jiere unusei niereini Fugu giene, dozohei hhei daghazho. Hhelade qienli ogizhi khudogho, oliesuku, inzhaku gien, yewo enelaghala zemin jieredu 4 fenzhi 1 ni oronde kunlai alane.
REV 6:9 Ji 5 gie fenqioni keighakude bi chanlase sidagha gieku teizi doura Hudai daolide oluzhi, pse hhende ganzhen beisande oluzhi alasan kunlai ruhher wine.
REV 6:10 Hhela fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Zhiguitu zhenzhenji Ezhan, chi zemin jiere sousan kunlai ulie panjizhi bijienyi kuighazhi usurusan chusunde bouchou ulie giezhi yan xienzi kune?"
REV 6:11 Ingie hhe jien kunde chighan fudu jien ogidene fenfulazhi tanre hhantu hoji danlasan gaijiulai ta mutun deigo alazhi shuzi kutula pse gouji hhamura giezho.
REV 6:12 Ji 6 gie fenqioni keighakude bi chanlase zemin hende gojioluzhi naran kharaladene khara bosii xianli, sara hulande chusunyi xianli.
REV 6:13 Hodunla asimanse zemin jiere bouzhezho, hoxian kei feiliezhi gojiolughasan uhuago mutunse ese shalasan alima bouzhesan niekielien wo.
REV 6:14 Asiman horosan shu mutun horo widawo. Jien ula, haini daoni oronseni noighawo.
REV 6:15 Duyani honshan, fugie noyen, jianjin, bayan kun, lilian fugietu kun, pse jien hoji, hoji ese danlasan kun, man ulai dunde, tashi fenzide niuidene
REV 6:16 ulade tashide kieliezho, "Bijienyi jiere bouzhe! Baozo sousei ungiese, ghoni ghughan hokusanse bijienyi niuigha!
REV 6:17 Hhelai hokusan zhunyoni udu kuzhewo, kien bei shidane?"
REV 7:1 Enense khuinashi bi chanlase jieran qienxien zeminni jieran gozide beidene simienni keini duizhi zemin, hai, soyuji mutunlai jiere ese feilieghazho.
REV 7:2 Bi pse chanlase dou nie qienxien naran khizheku oronse khizhezho, chanqiku Hudai zhanzini bareizho. Zemin, haini hei shidaku nenlini jienliesan jieran qienxiende fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho,
REV 7:3 "Bijien matai Hudai hojilai manlou jiere zhanzi taitula ta zemin, hai, mutunlai bu hei."
REV 7:4 Bi sonosuse Isilieni go paise zhanzi taisan shuzishi 144000 wo.
REV 7:5 Yuda paise zhanzi taisan 12000, Libien paise zhanzi taisan 12000, Jiade paise zhanzi taisan 12000,
