REV 7:8 Xibulun paise zhanzi taisan 12000, Yusufu paise zhanzi taisan 12000, Bienyamin paise zhanzi taisan 12000 wo.
REV 7:9 Enense khuinashi bi chanlase tebieji olon kun wine. Kiema toulazhi baragha dane. Go gojia, go pai, go minzu, go kielien kieliechen kunlase man irezhi baozo, ghoni ghughani melie beizho, chighan jien musizhi zunshu mutun chalalai bareidene
REV 7:10 fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Jiuiku baozo sousan mai Hudaji ghoni ghughande wine!"
REV 7:11 Qienxienla man baozo, zhanlao, jieran amitu ojienlai zhouwide beidene baozo melie papala Hudai beiizhi
REV 7:12 kieliezho, "Amine! Zanjiku, kuaiku, agheli, mafan gieku, zhigui, nenli, lilianni Mai Hudade chanqi izhi ogi! Amine!"
REV 7:13 Zhanlao dunda niekozi made asazho, "Enezighan chighan jien musisanshi kien wo? Hhela khalase irezho?"
REV 7:14 Bi hhende kieliewo, "Mii gujiu, chi mejiene." Hhe made kieliewo, "Enezighan kunla zeinan dundase khizhezhi ghoni ghughanyi chusun hhelai jienni waghazhi chighanshighazho."
REV 7:15 Ingiese "Hhela Hudai baozo melie xieni udu Hudai dajiende hhei beiizho. Baozo sousan hhe zhanfanghala hhelai huizho.
REV 7:16 Hhela pse ulie oliesune, ulie undasune. Naran, pse hhereini hhelai tulie dane.
REV 7:17 Ingiekushi baozo dundadu ghoni ghughan hhelai chezhezhi udurudene aminni usui bula konde echine, Huda hhelai nunpusunyi saine."
REV 8:1 Ghoni ghughan ji 7 gie fenqioni keighakude asiman jiere bangie xioshi yama shenqi uwo.
REV 8:2 Bi chanlase Hudai melie dolon qienxien beizho. Hhelade dolon laba ogizho.
REV 8:3 Da nie qienxien iredene antanni xianlu bareizhi sidagha gieku teizi kanzide beizho. Olon xianni hhende ogizhi shentulai onxianghala hhantu baozo kondedu antanni sidagha gieku teizi jiere ogine giezho.
REV 8:4 Hhe xianni funi shentulai onxianghala hhantu qienxienni khase Hudai melie khireiwo.
REV 8:5 Ingie qienxien xianluni bareizhi sidagha gieku teizi jieredu khanni zhonlozhi durughadene zemin jiere kiese olien tunguliezho, fugie shenqi, shanjien, zemin gojioluzho.
REV 8:6 Dolon laba bareisan dolon qienxien feiliene giezhi zhunbei giezho.
REV 8:7 Ji 1 gie qienxien labani feiliese mendou, chusunghala huisan khan zemin jiere bouzhezho. Zeminni 3 fenzhi 1, mutunni 3 fenzhi 1 ni sidera widaghawo, pse noghon osunlai man sidera widaghawo.
REV 8:8 Ji 2 gie qienxien labani feiliese khan siderasan xianlitu fugie ulai haide bendawo. Haini 3 fenzhi 1 chusun gholuwo,
REV 8:9 Haini amitu ojien 3 fenzhi 1 fuguwo, chonni 3 fenzhi 1 qida oluwo.
REV 8:10 Ji 3 gie qienxien labani feiliese hoba mutun siderasan fugie hodun asimanse moron, bulai 3 fenzhi 1 de bouzhewo.
REV 8:11 Ene hodunni nierei Kou giene. Usuni 3 fenzhi 1 kouni gholuwo. Usu koudase olon kunla fuguwo.
REV 8:12 Ji 4 gie qienxien labani feiliese naranni 3 fenzhi 1, sarani 3 fenzhi 1, hodunlai 3 fenzhi 1 ni eghizhi naran, sara, hodunlani 3 fenzhi 1 kharalawo. Uduni 3 fenzhi 1 de gon widawo, xieniye niekielien wo.
REV 8:13 Bi chanlazhi sonosuse asimande musisan nie in fugie shenqighala kieliezho, "Gou widawo! Gou widawo! Duyade sousan kunlade gou widawo! Da ghuran qienxien labani feiliene giezho!"
REV 9:1 Ji 5 gie qienxien labani feiliese bi chanlase nie hodun asimanse zemin jiere bouwo, jizi witu nokienni yeshii hhende ogizho.
REV 9:2 Hhe nokienni niese funi ojiede mouizhi fugie luzini funii xianli. Ene funi naran, asimanni kharalaghawo.
REV 9:3 Machazi funise khizhedene zemin jiere luiwo. Hhelade nenli ogizhi hoxian zemin jieredu xiezini nenlii xianli.
REV 9:4 Hhelade fenfulazhi zemin jieredu osunji yanyanji noghon dunxi, mutunlai bu shanjidene zinie manlou jiere Hudai zhanzii ese taisan kunlai shanji giezho.
REV 9:5 Hhelai bu alazhi tawun sara tendun shouigha giezho. Ene tendun xiezi kunyi jinjisan niekielien wo.
REV 9:6 Hhezighan udude kun fugune giezhoma fugu dane. Fuguku duran biliuzhe fuguku hhelase piizho.
REV 9:7 Machazini yanzi hoxian zhan eghindune giezhi zhunbei gie goudaghasan moreii xianli. Qiorun jiere zhosan antanni maghalai xianli, ungienni ere kunyi ungiei xianli,
REV 9:8 usunni biereini usunyi xianli, shidunni shizii shidunyi xianli.
REV 9:9 Echan jiereni qiemu majiai xianlitu huiku majia wine. Hhelai sibanyini shenqi hoxian olon mache holuzhi zhanchan jiere khireiku shenqii xianli.
REV 9:10 Hhelai xien xiezii xianli, xien jieredu duni kunyi tawun sara shanji shidane.
REV 9:11 Jizi witu nokienni qienxien hhelade honshan danlazho. Xibolai kielienghala kieliese niereini Yabadun giene, Xila kielienghala Yabolun giene.
REV 9:12 Ji 1 gie zeinan daowo. Uzhe, pse ghua zeinan irene.
REV 9:13 Ji 6 gie qienxien labani feiliese bi sonosuse nie shenqi Hudai meliedu antanni sidagha gieku teizii jieran gochase khizhezho.
REV 9:14 Ene shenqi laba bareisan ji 6 gie qienxiende kieliezho, "Yufalaji fugie moronde banlasan jieran qienxienni andagha."
REV 9:15 Ingie jieran qienxienni andaghawo. Hhela alinie hon, sara, udu, zhuntoude kunni 3 fenzhi 1 ni alakui zhunbei gie goudaghazho.
REV 9:16 Bi shuzii sonosuse hhelade morei unusan budui lianyi wine.
REV 9:17 Bi zhoujin mutun hhezighan morei, morei unusanlai chanlawo. Morei unusanlai echan jiere huiku majia wine. Majiani yenshei khan mutun hulan, manou mutun kugie, liuhon mutun shira wo. Moreini qiorun shizini qiorunni xianli. Khan, funi, liuhon, moreini amanse khizhezho.
REV 9:18 Amanseni khizhesan khan, funi, liuhon ene ghuran zeinanghala kunni 3 fenzhi 1 ni alawo.
REV 9:19 Moreilai nenli amandeji xiende wo. Xienni mogheini xianli, qiorun bizhi qiorunghala kunni heine.
REV 9:20 Enezighan zeinanghala ese alasan psedu kunla goya khaghalane giesanne geizhen ese giedene da sheitanlai, pse hhezighan uzhe daku, sonosu daku, yo daku, antan, miengu, tun, tashi, muzhaghala giesan nigiedalai beiizho.
REV 9:21 Hhela kun alaku, fashu shuaiku, lon kijieku, ghulaku shiqinlasene geizhen ese giezho.
REV 10:1 Bi pse chanlase dou nie fugie liliantu qienxien asimanse bouzhezhi olienni nanbezho, qiorun jiereni lun sulasan wine, ungienni naranni xianli, ghua konni khantu tuhuai xianli.
REV 10:2 Hhei khade keighasan ga shu wine. Borun konni haini taizho, soghei konni zeminni taizho.
REV 10:3 Fugie shenqighala waradase hoxian shizi onghonosei xianli. Waradakude dolon olien tunguliesan shenqi khizhezho.
REV 10:4 Dolon olien tunguliesan shenqi khizhekude bi hhei huaine giezho. Ingiekude bi sonosuse asimanse shenqi kieliezhi dolon olien tunguliesan kieliesei bu huaidene fenji giezho.
REV 10:5 Bi chanlasan hai, zeminni taisan qienxien asimande borun khane zhadeighadene
REV 10:6 zhiizhi asiman, asiman jieredu ojien, zemin, zemin jieredu ojien, hai, hai dundadu ojienlai zhayaghasan chanqi izhi amituku hhende fayen giezhi kieliezho, "Pse danwu ulie giene.
REV 10:7 Ji 7 gie qienxien labani feiliekude Hudai mimi Huda xienzhi hojiladene chonjizhi ogisan gouxioxi mutun chenjine."
REV 10:8 Bi melieshi asimanse sonosusan shenqi pse made kieliewo, "Chi echidene hai, zeminni taisan qienxienni khase keighasan shuni agi."
REV 10:9 Bi qienxienyi hhende yo dao horosan ga shuni made ogi giezhi kieliewo. Hhe made kieliewo, "Chi bareidene ijie agi. Kielidechii koudanema, amandechii qiende shimei niekielien wo."
REV 10:10 Bi qienxienyi khase ga shuni jienlie daozhedene ijie agise mii amande zhenzhenji qiende shimei niekielien wo, kielidemi kou wo.
REV 10:11 Pse made kieliezho, "Chi olon minzu, gojia, yanyanji kielienyi kieliechen kun, honshanlai fanmiende kieliesan Hudai kielienyi indan pse kieliekuni wo."
REV 11:1 Made nie zhugunyi xianlitu chizii ogizhi kieliezho, "Bosizhedene Hudai dajien, sidagha gieku teizi, pse hhende libai giesan kunlai nanji.
REV 11:2 Dajienni ghadanedu yenzii bu nanji, hhei niman kunlade ogizho. Hhela zhiguitu chenshini 42 gie sara tai pindaghane.
REV 11:3 Bi ghua ganzhen beisan kundene madei jien musighazhi qienli ogidene 1260 qien Hudai daolini kielieghane."
REV 11:4 Hhelashi duyai Ezhanyi melie beisan ghua ganlan mutun, ghua zhula teizi wo.
REV 11:5 Kien hhelai heine giese hhelai amanse khan khizhezhi duitoulai sidera widaghane. Hhelai heine giesanlai kenjin ingiezhi alane.
REV 11:6 Ene ghualade Hudai kielienyi kielieku udude asimanni menjighadene ghura ulie boughaku nenli wine. Pse usulai chusun gholughazhi da goyane isizhe yanyanji zeinanghala duyai eghiku nenli wine.
REV 11:7 Hhela ganzhen bei balukude jizi witu nokiense khizhesan yewo hhelare eghinduzhi injidene hhelai alane.
REV 11:8 Hhelani fugusan beyeni fugie chenshini geidoude jiene. Ene chenshini bilazhi kieliese Sodomaye giene, Aijiye giene, jiushi hhelai Ezhanni shizijia jiere ghada alasan oron wo.
REV 11:9 Go minzu, go pai, go kielien, go gojialase iresan kunla hhelai fugusan beyei ghurudu zharun xihan uzhezhi mezade ulie teighane.
REV 11:10 Ene ghua xienzhila zemin jiere sousan kunlai tendun shouighazhi daozho, ingiese zemin jiere sousan kunla hhela fugusande bayasuzhi nieniedene mure khughone.
REV 11:11 Ghurudu zharun daodene amin bitu ho Hudai hhense hhelai sudoro orose hhela bosizhewo. Hhelai chanlasan kunla hende ayizho.
REV 11:12 Ghua xienzhi sonosuse asimanse fugie shenqi hhelade kieliezho, "Enende khizhe." Hhela olienre hhantu asimande khiwo. Duitoulaniye chanlawo.
REV 11:13 Zhen ingiekude zemin hende gojioluzhi chenshini 10 fenzhi 1 tairezho. Zemin gojioluzhi fugusan kun 7000 gie wo. Feiliesan kunla ayizhi kuaikui asiman jieredu Hudade ogizho.
REV 11:14 Ji 2 gie zeinan daowo. Uzhe, ji 3 gie zeinan deigo irene.
REV 11:15 Ji 7 gie qienxien labani feiliese asimande fugie shenqila bizhi kieliezho, "Duyani gojia mai Ezhanji hhe teisan Mexihani gojia gholuwo. Hhe chanqi izhi honshan danlane."
REV 11:16 Hudai melie goya wizide sousan 24 gie zhanlao papaladene Hudai beiizhi
REV 11:17 kieliezho, "Edeku, eqighanku Ezhan, nenlitu Huda, bijien chade mafan kielieye. Chi fugie nenli bareizhi honshan danlawo.
REV 11:18 Gojiala noiwoma, chii hokuku irewo. Fugusan kunni panjiku shihou, chii hoji, xienzhi, shentu, jien chii jilasan kun fugiei gajiniji jianli linlaku shihou, Pse duyani pohai giesanlai chi widaghaku shihou irewo."
REV 11:19 Ingiekude asimandedu Hudai dajien keizhi sudoroni kielien yenjisan xianzini uzhe shidane. Pse shanjien, fugie shenqi, olien tunguliesan, zemin gojiolusan, fugie mendou wine.
REV 12:1 Asimande fugie zunji xienjizhi nie bierei naranni musizhi sarani taizho. Qiorun jierene 12 gie hoduntu honshan zhoku maghala zhozho.
REV 12:2 Hhe kewosi laizhi olukude otuzhi tendun shouizhi waradazho.
REV 12:3 Asimande pse nie zunji xienjizhi nie hulan lunde dolon qiorun, hharan gocha wo. Dolon qiorun jiereni dolon honshan zhoku ga maghala zhozho.
REV 12:4 Hhe xienghalane asimanni hodunlai 3 fenzhi 1 ni laizhi zemin jiere bendawo. Pse kewosi olune giesan biereini melie beidene hhe oluse hhei kewosii ijiene giezho.
REV 12:5 Bierei nie kewon oluwo. Ene kewon jianlai qiemu zhugunghala gojialai man gonjine. Hheni kewosii Hudai baozoi hhende qila echiwo.
REV 12:6 Bierei hontande holuzhi echise Huda hhei hhende 1260 qien qiezhene giezhi zhunbei giesan oron wine.
REV 12:7 Asiman jiere zhan eghindu qiiwo. Mijiale qienxienlarene lunghala eghinduzhi lunye kha douradedularene hhantu bosizhezhi eghinduzho.
REV 12:8 Lun inji dase asiman jiere hhelade oron widazho.
REV 12:9 Fugie lunshi gushihouni moghei wo, niereini Sheitan giene, pse Ibilisiye giene. Duyade sousan kunlai man miizho. Hhei zemin jiere bendawo, hhei kha douradedulaiye hhantu bendawo.
REV 12:10 Bi sonosuse asimanse fugie shenqi kieliezho, "Ede mai Hudai jiuiku, nenli, gojia irezho, hhe teisan Mexiha qienli bareizho! Mai Hudai melie xieni uduji mai gaijiulai zhasan hhei benda boughawo.
REV 12:11 Gaijiula lunni injikushi ghoni ghughanyi chusun, pse goyalane ganzhen beisan daolighala wo. Hhela amindene ulie orezhi fugukude kuzho.
REV 12:12 Ingiese asiman, pse hhende sousanla bayasundu! Zemin, haide gou widawo! Ibilisi goyade shihou oloncha widakui mejiedene Hende hokuzhi tai hhende bouwo."
REV 12:13 Lun goyai zemin jiere bendasei mejiedene kewon olusan biereini fenjiezhi biizho.
REV 12:14 Ingiese fugie inni ghua sibanni biereide ogise hhe musidene mogheise piizhi hontanni goya orondene echiwo. Hhende biereini nie shihou, ghua shihou, olie shihou qiezhezho.
REV 12:15 Moghei biereini khuinase amansene moron mutun usuni nunpuzhi biereini chunji yolaghane giezho.
REV 12:16 Zemin biereide banman giezhi amanne keighadene lun amansene nunpusan usuni yenjiwo.
REV 12:17 Lun biereide hokudene biereini psedu kesilare eghindule echizho. Ene kesilashi Hudai minlinyi zunjizhi Ersade ganzhen beisanla wo.
REV 12:18 Qingiekude lun haibienzini shazi jiere beizho.
REV 13:1 Bi chanlase nie yewo haise khizhezhi hharan gocha, dolon qiorun wine. Hharan gocha jierene hharan honshan zhoku ga maghala zhozho. Dolon qiorun jiereni Hudai sugieku niere wine.
REV 13:2 Bi chanlasan yewo laohuni xianli, konni gouxinni konni xianli, amanni shizini amanni xianli. Lun goya nenli, wizi, fugie qienline hhende ogiwo.
REV 13:3 Bi chanlase yewoni dolon qiorun dunda niekozi hoxian fuguku shan deilazhoma goudazho. Zemin jieredula man ghanirazhi yewoni daghazho.
REV 13:4 Hhela lunni beiikushi lun qienline yewode ogizho. Pse yewoni beiizhi kieliezho, "Kien ene yewoghala bilane, kien hheghala eghindu shidane?"
REV 13:5 Yewode tungulieku, Hudai sugieku aman ogizho. Pse 42 gie sara durare gieku qienli ogizho.
REV 13:6 Yewo amanne keighazhi Hudai sugieku kielien kieliezho. Hudai nierei, hhei zhanfan, jiushi asiman jiere sousanlai sugiezho.
REV 13:7 Pse shentulare eghinduzhi injiku dainni jienliezhi go pai, go minzu, go kielien, go gojialai hanshilieku qienlini jienliezho.
REV 13:8 Jien zemin jiere sousan, niereini duyai zhayaghasanse alasan ghoni ghughanyi aminni jilasan benzi jiere ese jilasan kunla man hhei beiine.
REV 13:9 Chighin bitu kunla chenliendu!
REV 13:10 Qianla echiku kunyi kenjin qianla echine. Khudoghoghala alaku kunyi kenjin khudoghoghala alane. Ingiese shentulade bixi rennai, xianxin gieku bikui wo.
REV 13:11 Bi chanlase da nie yewo zeminse khizhezhi ghua gocha bisan ghoni ghughanyi xianli, kielien kieliese lunni xianli.
REV 13:12 Hhe tou 1 gie yewoni nenlini hhei melie man khizheghazhi zemin, zemin jiere sousanlai, fuguku shanni goudaghasan tou 1 gie yewoni beiighazho.
REV 13:13 Pse fugie ghudureqilai giezhi da kunlai melie khanni asimanse zeminde bouzheghazho.
REV 13:14 Ene yewo qienlini jienliedene tou 1 gie yewoni melie ghudureqilai giezhi zemin jiere sousan kunlai miizho. Pse khudoghoghala shan deiladene ese fugusan yewode nie nigieda gie giezhi hhelade kieliezho.
REV 13:15 Hhe nenlini jienliedene nigiedade ho ogizhi kielien kielieghazho, pse soyuji nigiedai ese beiisan kunlai man alaghazho.
REV 13:16 Pse soyuji kunlai bugon fugiei, gajii, nanxinyi, bayanyi, hoji ese danlasan, hoji danlasanlai borun kha jiere onu manlou jiere zhanzi taighadene
REV 13:17 zhanzi uwochenlai meimei ese gieghazho. Ene zhanzishi yewoni niere, pseshi yewoni nierei daibio giesan shuzi wo.
REV 13:18 Enende agheli kerene. Jienzha kun ene yewoni shuzii sana khizhegha. Ene shuzi nie kunni nierei daibio giezho, 666 wo.
REV 14:1 Bi chanlase ghoni ghughan Xiwunshande beizhi 144000 kun hhere hhantu wo! Hhelai manlou jiere hhei nierei, adaini nierei huaizho.
REV 14:2 Bi sonosuse asimanse iresan shenqi hoxian olon usuni shenqi, fugie olien tunguliesan shenqii xianli. Bi sonosusan shenqi hoxian qin tanjisan kunla tanjisan shenqii xianli.
REV 14:3 Hhela baozo melie pse jieran amitu ojien, zhanlaolai melie shini don doulazho. Zemin jierese shuizhi iresan 144000 kunse chugo kiemada ene donni suru dane.
REV 14:4 Enezighan kunla biereini shighazhi ese daozho, biereilare kijiezhi ese daozho. Ghoni ghughan khala echise hhela hhei daghazho. Hhelashi kun dundase shuizhi iredene Hudaji ghoni ghughonde ogisan tou 1 ban kun wo.
REV 14:5 Hhelai amanse ghudan ereizhi olu dane, hhelade jienjien goujida uwo.
REV 14:6 Bi chanlase da nie qienxien asimande musizhi zemin jiere sousan go gojia, go pai, go kielien, minzulade chonjiku chanqiku gouxioxii bareizho.
REV 14:7 Hhe fugie shenqighala kieliezho, "Hudai zunji! Kuaikui hhende ogi! Hhe panjiku shihou kuzhezho. Asiman, zemin, hai, bulai zhayaghasei beii!"
REV 14:8 Pse nie qienxien irezhi kieliezho, "Soyuji gojialade lon kijiezhi hokukui ireghasan Babilun fugie chenshi furawo, furawo!"
REV 14:9 Pse nie, jiushi ji 3 gie qienxien irezhi fugie shenqighala kieliezho, "Kien yewo, hhei yanzii beiizhi manlou jiere, kha jiere zhanzi taise
REV 14:10 kienye Hudai hokukui shouine. Huda zui fugiede hokukune ireghane. Ene kunla zhiguitu qienxien, ghoni ghughanyi melie khan, liuhon dunda tendun shouine.
REV 14:11 Hhela tendun shouisan funi chanqi izhi ojiede mouizho. Hhezighan yewo, yewoni nigiedai beiizhi hhei niereni zhanzii taisanlade udu xieniji nanran uwo."
REV 14:12 Ingiese Hudai minlinyi zunjizhi Ersai xianxin gieku bisan shentulade bixi rennai bikui wo.
REV 14:13 Bi sonosuse asimande shenqi bizhi kieliezho, "Enedu khuinashi Ezhanni miende fugusan kunlade fuqi wine giezhi chi huai." Ingiese Shenlin kieliezho, "Enbene, hhela khishulasansene xiine, giesande huibao wine."
REV 14:14 Bi pse chanlase niegieda chighan olien wo! Olien jiere hoxian kunni kewon souzhi qiorun jierene honshan zhoku antanni maghala zhozho, khadene xidu liendao bareizho.
REV 14:15 Pse nie qienxien dajiense khizhezhi olien jiere sousande fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Ghuraku shihou kuruzho. Zemin jieredu zhonjiala bolu momoreizho. Liendaoghalane ghura!"
REV 14:16 Ingiese olien jiere sousan liendaoghalane nie ghaduliese zemin jiereshiku zhonjiani ghurawo.
REV 14:17 Pse nie qienxien asiman jieredu Hudai dajiense khizhezhi xidu liendaoye bareizho.
REV 14:18 Pse nie qienxien sidagha gieku teizise khizhezhi nenli bizhi khanni gonjizho. Xidu liendao bareisande fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Putou bolu momoreizho. Xidu liendaoghalane ghaduliezhi zemin jieredu putoui ghura."
REV 14:19 Hhe qienxien liendaoghalane ghaduliezhi zemin jiereshiku putouni ghuradene Hudai hokuku fugie jiu gieku chizide bendawo.
REV 14:20 Chenshi ghadane jiu gieku chizide putouni taizho. Hhense chusun usuruzhi khizhezhi undude morei ghada undu wo, gholode 1600 sitaji wo.
REV 15:1 Bi pse chanlase asimande da nie zunji wine. Fugie, ghudure no wo. Dolon qienxien dolon zeinanni bareizho. Eneshi zuihouku zeinan wo. Hudai hokuku eneghala barane.
REV 15:2 Bi chanlase khan huisan boli mutun hai wine. Yewo, yewoni nigieda, yewoni nierei daibio giesan shuzise injisan kunla boli hai jiere beizhi Hudai qinni bareidene
REV 15:3 Hudai hoji Musai don, ghoni ghughanyi donni doulazhi kieliezho, "Ezhan Huda, fugie nenlituya, chii gieku fama wo, ghudure wo! Soyuji gojiani honshanya, chii mo gundan wo, zhen wo!
REV 15:4 Ezhan, zinie chishi zhiguitu wo. Kien chii ulie zunjizhi chii nierei ulie kuaine? Soyuji gojiala irezhi chii beiikushi chi gundande giekune khizheghazho."
REV 15:5 Enense khuinashi bi chanlase asiman jiere dajien keizho. Eneshi ganzhen beiku zhanfan wo.
REV 15:6 Dajiense dolon zeinanni gonjisan dolon qienxien khizhewo. Ganjin, gieghantu gou jien musizhi echan jierene antanni popu banlazho.
REV 15:7 Jieran amitu ojien dundadu niekozi chanqi izhi amituku Hudai hokukui zhonlozhi durughasan dolon antanni ighai dolon qienxiende ogiwo.
REV 15:8 Hudai fama, nenlighala dajiende funi duruzho. Dolon qienxien dolon zeinanni bouzhezhi baraghatula kiema dajiende oro dane.
REV 16:1 Bi sonosuse dajiense fugie shenqi khizhezhi dolon qienxiende kieliezho, "Ta echidene Hudai hokuku dolon ighai zeminde pojie."
REV 16:2 Ji 1 gie qienxien echidene ighani zeminde pojiese yewoni zhanzi taisan, yewoni nigiedai beiisanlai beye jiere zannan, du yara khizhezho.
REV 16:3 Ji 2 gie qienxien ighani haide pojiese hai fugusan kunni chusun mutun gholuwo. Haini amitu ojienla man fuguwo.
REV 16:4 Ji 3 gie qienxien ighani moron, bulade pojiese usu chusun gholuwo.
REV 16:5 Bi sonosuse usuni gonjisan qienxien kieliezho, "Eqighanku, edeku zhiguitu Huda, chi ingiezhi panjise gundan wo.
REV 16:6 Hhela shentu, xienzhilai chusunyi usurughazhi daozho. Ede chi hhelade chusun ochighazho. Ingiezhi giese hhelade indanji wo!"
REV 16:7 Bi pse sonosuse sidagha gieku teizise shenqi bizhi kieliezho, "Enbene, Ezhan Huda, fugie nenlituya, chii panjiku zhen wo, gundan wo!"
REV 16:8 Ji 4 gie qienxien ighani naran nudunde pojiese nanran kunni khanghala kouine.
REV 16:9 Kunlai hende hhereide kouise nenli bizhi zeinanni gonjisan Hudai nierei sugiezhi, da geizhen ulie giezhi kuaikui Hudade ulie ogine.
REV 16:10 Ji 5 gie qienxien ighani yewoni zowide pojiese yewoni gojia kharalawo. Kunla tendun shouizhi shidunne zhouzho.
REV 16:11 Tendun shouiku, yara khizheku yenyinghala hhela asiman jieredu Hudai sugiezhi da giesansene geizhen ulie giene.
REV 16:12 Ji 6 gie qienxien ighani Yufalaji fugie moronde pojiese moron ghozhi dunbangiese iresan honshanlade mo zhunbei giezho.
REV 16:13 Bi pse chanlase baghai xianlitu ghuran zannan ruhher lun, yewo, jia xienzhilai amanse khizhezho.
REV 16:14 Hhelashi sheitanni ruhher wo, ghudureqi gie shidane, duyani honshanlai hhende echizhi hhelai Fugie Nenlitu Hudai famatu udude hhantulaghazhi eghindughane giezho.
REV 16:15 Uzhe, bi ghughei mutun irene. Jinxin giezhi jienne musisan kunde fuqi wine. Hulan muchughun ulie yozhi shizhekune ulie uzheghane.
REV 16:16 Hhe zannan ruhherla honshanlai nie oronde hhantulaghazho, ene oronni Xibolai kielienghala Hamagiedun giene.
REV 16:17 Ji 7 gie qienxien ighani asimande pojiese fugie shenqi dajiendedu baozo jierese khizhezhi kieliezho, "Chenjiwo!"
REV 16:18 Ingiese shanjien, shenqi, olien tunguliesan, fugiede zemin gojioluku wine. Imutu fugie yenzhunde zemin gojioluku kun zemin jiere bisanse uwo.
REV 16:19 Hhe fugie chenshi ghaluzhi ghuran gholuzhi go gojialani chenshilaye man furawo. Huda Babilun fugie chenshini sumula iredene goya hokukune hhei jiere bouzheghawo.
REV 16:20 Go haini daola piizhi ulalaiye chanla dane.
REV 16:21 Pse fugie mendoula asimanse kunyi jiere bouzhezhi niekozi gundude 70 jin wo. Ene mendouni zeinan hende fugieshi kunla Hudai sugiezho.
REV 17:1 Dolon ighai bareisan dolon qienxien dundadu niekozi made kieliezho, "Chi ire, olon usu jiere sousan fugie biozini faikui bi chade uzheghaye.
REV 17:2 Zemin jieredu honshanla hhere kijiezhi daozho, zemin jiere sousan kunla biozini lon kijieku jiuni ochizhi sudozho."
REV 17:3 Shenlin mii zhughei gojiolughazhi qienxien mii uduruzhi hontande echise nie bierei dahunse yewo jiere unusei bi chanlawo. Hhe yewode dolon qiorun, hharan gocha wo, hunshendeni Hudai sugieku niere wine.
REV 17:4 Hhe bierei zishei, dahunseni jien musizhi antan, boushi, zhenzhughala dabalazho. Khadene antanni beizi bareizho. Beizide hanzhan gieghaku, lon kijieku zannannii zhonlo durughazho.
REV 17:5 Manlou jiereni fugie Babilun wo, zeminni biozila, yanyanji hanzhan gieghakulani Ana wo giezhi mimitu niere huaizho.
REV 17:6 Bi pse chanlase hhe bierei shentulani chusun, Ersade oluzhi ganzhen beisan kunlai chusunyi ochi sudozho. Bi hhei chanlase hende ghanirazho.
REV 17:7 Qienxien made kieliezho, "Chi yale ghanirazho? Bi ene biereini, pse hhei achisan dolon qiorun hharan gochatu yewoni mimii chade kielieye.
REV 17:8 Chi chanlasan yewo eqighandei wine, ede uwo, jianlai jizi witu nokiense khizhezhi widakude echine. Jien zemin jiere sousanla, jiushi niereini duyai zhayaghasanse aminni jilasan benzi jiere ese jilasanla hhe eqighandei wine, ede uwo, jianlai ireku yewoni chanlase ghanirane.
REV 17:9 Enende aghelitu zhughe kerene. Hhe dolon qiorunshi bierei sousan dolon ula wo, dolon honshan wo.
REV 17:10 Tawulie ijin furawo, niekozi da wine, da nie dou ese irezhoma, irese goujicha beine.
REV 17:11 Eqighandei biku, ede uwoku yewoshi ji 8 gie honshan wo, yeshi dololie mutun nie wo, widakude echine.
REV 17:12 Chi chanlasan hharan gochashi hharan honshan wo. Hhela dou gojiani sou dazhoma, niecha jiere yewore hhantu honshan danlaku qienli bareine.
REV 17:13 Hhela nie zhugheghala goya nenli, qienline yewode ogizho.
REV 17:14 Hhela ghoni ghughanre eghindune. Ghoni ghughan hhelase injikushi ghoni ghughanshi ezhan dundadu Ezhan wo, honshan dundadu Honshan wo. Hhezighan urusan, sunghusan, shixinji giesan kunlaye ghoni ghughanre hhantu injine."
REV 17:15 Qienxien pse made kieliezho, "Chi chanlasan biozi sousan usushi olon minzu, bexin, gojia, kielien wo.
REV 17:16 Chi chanlasan hharan gocha, yewo hhe biozini henjine. Hhei yanyanjilai qianlazhi hulan muchughun gholughadene mighaini ijiezhi khanghala sidera widaghane.
REV 17:17 Ingiekushi Huda hhelai zhughede goyane isii gieghakui teizho. Hhela nie zhugheghala goya gojialane yewode ogizhi Hudai kielien man gholuku shihou kune.
REV 17:18 Chi chanlasan biereishi zemin jieredu honshanlani gonjisan fugie chenshi wo."
REV 18:1 Enense khuinashi bi chanlase nie fugie nenlitu qienxien asimanse bouzhezho, hhei fama zemin jiere gon zhouizho.
REV 18:2 Hhe fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Babilun fugie chenshi furawo, furawo! Sheitan souku oron gholuwo. Yanyanji zannan ruhherni ho, yanyanji zannan bunzhuni galun, yanyanji zannan, hanzhan gieghaku yewoni oron gholuwo.
REV 18:3 Soyuji gojiala hhei lon kijieku fugie nefuxinde sudozho. Zemin jieredu honshanla hhere kijiezhi daozho. Hhe gofenji baer lon huaise zemin jieredu meimei giechen kunla facai giewo."
REV 18:4 Bi pse sonosuse asimanse da nie shenqi kieliezho, "Mii bexinla, hhe chenshise khizhe! Pse hhere hhantu zui bizhi hhe shouiku zeinanni shouine.
REV 18:5 Hhei zui zemin jiere duruzhi Huda hhei codasanyi ese matazho.
REV 18:6 Hhe kunlade matugie giese hhendeye qingiezhi gie. Zhao hhe giesande shonbeide kharulu. Hhe huighasan jiuni beizide shonbeide huighadene hhende ogizhi chenfa gie.
REV 18:7 Hhe goyane matugie kuaizhi matugie gofende baerni lon huaizhoshi hheiye qingiezhi tendun shouighazhi nango giegha. Hhe zhughedene kieliezhi bi honshan mutun wizide souzhi guafu pusho. Zhughede yama nango gieku uwo giezho.
REV 18:8 Ingiese hhei zeinanla man niudude irene. Jiushi fuguku, nango gieku, oliesuku wo. Hhei khanghala sidera widaghane. Hhei panjiku Ezhan Hudade fugie nenli wine."
REV 18:9 Hhere hhantu lon kijiezhi gofende lon baer huaisan zemin jieredu honshanla hhei tuliesan funii chanladene hhende oluzhi hende wilane.
REV 18:10 Hhela hhe tendun shouisanse ayizhi gholode beidene, "Gou widawo! Gou widawo! Babilun fugie, famatu chenshiya, Niecha jiere chii faiku irewo." giezhi kieliene.
REV 18:11 Zemin jieredu meimei giesan kunla hhende oluzhi hende wilakushi hhelai dunxilai agichen kun pse widawo.
REV 18:12 Ene dunxilashi antan, miengu, boushi, zhenzhu, gou bosi, zisheini seiliu, donzi, dahunseni seiliu, yanyanji xian winetu mutun, daxianni shidunghala giesan yanyanji dunxi, guizhuntu mutun, tun, qiemu, guizhuntu tashighala giesan yanyanji dunxi,
REV 18:13 rougui, doukou, xian, xianshui, andatu osun, jiu, tosun, ghurun, boudei, fughe, ghoni, morei, mache, pse hoji wo.
REV 18:14 Meimei giesan kunla kieliezho. "Babilunya, chi oresan dunxila man widawo. Chii yanyanji seighan, gou dunxila chii dundase widazhi pse chanla dane!"
REV 18:15 Hhe chenshide meimei giezhi facai giesan kunla hhe tendun shouisanse ayizhi gholode beidene hende wilazhi kieliezho,
REV 18:16 "Gou widawo! Gou widawo! Ene fugie chenshiya, Yenlai zishei, dahunni gou jienni musizhi antan, boushi, zhenzhughala dabalazho.
REV 18:17 Niecha jiere imekie bayannila wida khiwo!" Jien chonzhan, chon sousan kun, chon jiere wilie giesan, soyuji haini kouizhi udu daosanla gholode beizhi
REV 18:18 hhei tuliesan funii chanladene waradazhi kieliezho, "Yan chenshi ene chenshise fama wo?"
REV 18:19 Hhela pse turani qiorun jierene teidene hende wilazhi waradazhi kieliezho, "Gou widawo! Gou widawo! Ene fugie chenshiya, Jien hai jiere yosan chonla hhei bayanni kouizhi bayazhezho! Hhe niecha jiere hontan gholuwo.
REV 18:20 Asimanya, shentu, shitu, xienzhilaya, ta man hhei yenyinzhe bayasundu! Huda tande oluzhi hhei panjiwo!"
REV 18:21 Nie fugie liliantu qienxien nie fugie qiemansha mutun tashini qila haide bendadene kieliezho, "Babilun fugie chenshini ingiezhi hende benda boughase pse chanla dane.
REV 18:22 Qin tanjisan, don doulasan, xiu feiliesan, laba feiliesan shenqini chii dunda pse sonosu dane. Yanyanji mujianlai chii dunda ereizhi olu dane. Qieman sidasan shenqini chii dunda sonosu dane.
REV 18:23 Zhulani gon chii dunda pse ulie zhouine. Shini khughon, shini biereini shenqii pse chii dunda sonosu dane. Chare meimei giesan kunla yenlaishi duya jieredu zui henni wo. Soyuji gojialai chii fashu miizhi daozho.
REV 18:24 Xienzhi, shentu, da zemin jieredu soyuji alasan kunlai chusunni ene chenshise ereizhi oluwo."
REV 19:1 Enense khuinashi bi sonosuse hoxian olon kunla asiman jiere fugie shenqighala kieliezho, "Haliluya! Jiuiku, kuaiku, nenlishi mai Hudanughun wo.
REV 19:2 Hhei panjiku zhenni wo, gundan wo! Lon kijiezhi duyani qida olughasan fugie biozini panjiwo. Hojilaini chusunni usurughasan biozini panjizhi hhelade bouchou giewo!"
REV 19:3 Pse kieliezho, "Haliluya! Biozini tuliesan funi chanqi izhi mouizho."
REV 19:4 24 gie zhanlao, jieran amitu ojienla baozo sousan Hudade papaladene beiizhi kieliezho, "Amine! Haliluya!"
REV 19:5 Pse shenqi baozose khizhezhi kieliezho, "Hudai hojila, jien hhei zunjisan fugiei, gajii, man mai Hudade doula!"
REV 19:6 Bi pse sonosuse hoxian olon kunlai shenqi, olon usuni shenqi, fugie olien tunguliesan shenqi kieliezho, "Haliluya! Ezhan mai Huda Hhe Fugie Nenlitu manlai gonjizho.
REV 19:7 Matan hende bayasuzhi kuaikui hhende ogiye. Ghoni ghughan ghurun ijieku shihou kuzhewo, Shini biereini zhunbei gie goudawo.
REV 19:8 Gieghan, ganjintu gou jienni hhende ogizhi musighawo. Ene gou jienshi shentula giesan gou wilie wo."
REV 19:9 Qienxien made kieliezho, "Chi ingiezhi huai, 'Ghoni ghughanyi ghurunde xinlazhi iresan kunlade fuqi wine.'" Pse made kieliezho, "Eneshi Hudai shuhuajia kielien wo."
REV 19:10 Ingie bi hhei kon konde papaladene hhei beiine giese hhe kieliezho, "Ulie olune! Biye chighala, pse chii hhezighan Ersade ganzhen beisan gaijiulare hhantu hoji danlasan wo. Chi Hudai beii. Hudai kielienyi jianjiku dunda zui zhunyonishi Ersade ganzhen beiku wo."
REV 19:11 Bi pse chanlase asiman keizhi nie chighan morei wo! Jiereni unusei Kekao, Zhenni giezhi uruzho. Hhe panjizhi eghinduse gundanghala giezho.
REV 19:12 Nudunni khan giedai xianli, qiorun jierene honshan zhoku ga maghala olon zhozho. Jiereni hhense chugo kiema ulie mejieku niere huaizho.
REV 19:13 Hhe chusun xireighasan jienni musizho, niereini Hudai Kielien giene.
REV 19:14 Asiman jieredu buduila chighan, ganjintu gou jien musidene chighan morei unuzhi hhei daghazho.
REV 19:15 Amanseni xidu khudogho khizhezhi gojialani eghizhi beiighane. Qiemu zhugunghala hhelai gonjine, putou chizide jiu daruku mutun Fugie Nenlitu Hudai hokukui ireghane.
REV 19:16 Hhei fudu jien jiere, datui jiere honshan dundadu Honshan, ezhan dundadu Ezhan giezhi niere huaizho.
REV 19:17 Bi pse chanlase nie qienxien naran nudun dunda beizhi asiman jiere musisan soyuji bunzhulade fugie shenqighala waradazhi kieliezho, "Ta hhantuladene Hudai fugie xini soule ire.
REV 19:18 Honshan, jianjin, lilian fugietu, morei, morei unusan, pse soyuji ziyutu, hoji danlasan, fugie, meilani kunlai mighai ijie."
REV 19:19 Bi pse chanlase yewo, zemin jieredu honshanla, pse hhelai buduila hhantuladene chighan morei unusan, da hhei buduilare eghindune giezho.
REV 19:20 Yewoni bareiwo. Pse yewore hhantuku jia xienzhiiye bareiwo. Jia xienzhi eqighandei yewoni melie ghudureqi giedene hhezighan yewoni zhanzii taizhi yewoni nigiedai beiisan kunlai miizho. Hhe ghualai amitu siderasan liuhonni khantu haide bendawo.
REV 19:21 Psedulai morei unusei amanse khizhesan khudogho alawo. Soyuji bunzhula hhelai mighai ijie chuduwo.
REV 20:1 Bi pse chanlase nie qienxien asimanse bouzhezhi khadeni jizi witu nokienni yeshi, fugie qielien wine.
REV 20:2 Qienxien lunni bareiwo. Hheshi gushihouni moghei, sheitan, Ibilisi wo. Hhei 1000 nien banladene
REV 20:3 jizi witu nokiende bendazhi nokienyi khadene fenjizhi 1000 nien kurutula gojialai pse ulie miighane. Ene shiqinla daose hhei bixi zhanshi jiere andaghane.
REV 20:4 Bi pse ezighan baozo, baozo jiere sousanlai chanlawo. Hhelade panjiku qienlii ogizho. Bi pse hhezighan Ersade ganzhen beizhi Hudai kieliende oluzhi qiorunni pienjisan kunlai ruhherni chanlawo. Hhelashi yewo, yewoni nigiedai ese beiizhi manlou kha jiereni zhanzi ese taisan kunla wo. Hhela aminne oluzhi Mexihare hhantu 1000 nien honshan danlawo.
REV 20:5 Eneshi tou 1 hui fuho wo. Psedu kunla 1000 nien olutula aminne ese oluzho.
REV 20:6 Tou 1 hui fuhode guzi bichen kunlade fuqi bizhi zhiguitu wo. Ji 2 hui fuguku hhelai gonji dane. Hhela Huda, Mexihaghalade buwa danlazhi Mexihare hhantu 1000 nien honshan danlane.
REV 20:7 1000 nien daose Ibilisini bafanzise andaghase
REV 20:8 khizhedene zemin jieredu simienni gojialai miine. Ene gojialashi Gaoge, Mage wo. Hhelai hhantulaghazhi eghindughane giezho. Hhelai shuzi olonde haini shazi niekielien wo.
REV 20:9 Hhela khizhezhi nie zemin jiere dudene shentulani zhanfan, Huda oresan chenshini wiqise khan asimanse bouzhezhi hhelai sidera widaghawo.
REV 20:10 Hhelai miisan sheitanni liuhontu khantu haide bendawo. Hhende yewo, jia xienzhi wine. Hhela xieni uduji chanqi izhi tendun shouine.
REV 20:11 Bi pse nie chighan fugie baozo, baozo jiere sousanyi chanlawo. Hhei meliese asiman, zemin piizhi hhelai pse chanla dawo.
REV 20:12 Bi pse chanlase fugusan kun gajii fugieiji baozo melie beizho. Shulani man keighawo. Da nie shuniye keighawo, hheshijiu aminni jilasan benzi wo. Fugusan kunlai zhao hhela giesanzhe shu jiere jilasan mutun panjine.
REV 20:13 Pse hai haide fugusan kunlai ogiwo. Fuguku, pse dozohei hhelai hhende fugusan kunlaiye ogiwo. Hhelai zhao hhelai giesan mutun panjine.
REV 20:14 Fuguku pse dozoheini khantu hude bendawo. Ene khantu hushi ji 2 hui fuguku wo.
REV 20:15 Kienyi niere aminni benzi jiere uwoshi hhei khantu hude bendawo.
REV 21:1 Bi pse shini asiman, zemin chanlawo. Eqighanku asiman, zemin widawo, haiye widawo.
REV 21:2 Bi pse chanlase zhiguitu chenshi shini Yelusalen asimanyi Hudai hhense bouzhezho. Hoxian shini bierei zhanguijidene oluzhi dabala goudasei xianli.
REV 21:3 Bi pse sonosuse fugie shenqi baozose khizhezhi kieliezho, "Uzhe, Hudai zhanfan kun dunda wo! Huda kunlare hhantu soune. Hhela hhende bexin danlane. Huda qinsi hhelare hhantu wine.
REV 21:4 Hhelai nughunsunyi man saine. Pse fuguku uwo, pse nango gieku, wilaku, tendun uwo. Melieshidaku shiqinla daowo."
REV 21:5 Baozo sousan kieliewo, "Uzhe, bi soyujilai shinishighazho." Pse kieliewo, "Chi huai, enezighan kielienshi kekao, zhenni wo."
REV 21:6 Hhe made pse kieliewo, "Chenjiwo! Bishi Alafa wo, Emeiga wo, jiushi keitou wo, baraku wo. Bi aminni bula usuni undasusan kunde belien ughane.
REV 21:7 Injisan kunla enezighanyi jienliezhi caichan giene. Bi hhende Huda danlane, hhe made kewon danlane.
REV 21:8 Danzi meilatu, xianxin ulie giechen, hanzhan gieghachen, kun alachen, lon kijiechen, fashu shuaichen, nigieda beiichen, da soyuji ghudan kieliechen kunlai guzi siderasan liuhontu khantu hude wo. Eneshi ji 2 hui fuguku wo."
REV 21:9 Zuihouku dolon zeinanni zhonlo durughasan dolon antan ighani bareisan dolon qienxien dundadu nie made kieliewo, "Chi ire, bi chade shini biereii uzheghaye, ghoni ghughanyi bierei wo."
REV 21:10 Shenlin mii zhughei gojiolughazhi qienxien mii uduruzhi nie undu fugie ulade echi, asimanni Hudai hhense bouzhesan zhiguitu chenshi Yelusalenni made uzheghawo.
REV 21:11 Chenshide Hudai fama wine. Faisan gon guizhuntu boushi, ishini xianli, gieghantu shuijin niekielien wo.
REV 21:12 Hhende fugie undu dan wine, 12 gie wijien wo. Wijien jiere 12 gie qienxien wine. Wijien jiere Isilieni 12 gie paini nierei huaizho.
REV 21:13 Dunmiende ghuran wijien, beimiende ghuran wijien, nanmiende ghuran wijien, ximiende ghuran wijien wo.
REV 21:14 Chenshini dande 12 gie jichu wo, jichu jiere ghoni ghughanyi 12 gie shituni niere wine.
REV 21:15 Made kielien kieliesan qienxien antanni ghulusunyi bareizhi chenshi, wijien, danni nanjine giezho.
REV 21:16 Chenshishi jieran mien wo, fudu, aghui niekielien wo. Qienxien ghulusunghala chenshini nanjise man 12000 sitaji wo. Fudu, aghui, unduni niekielien wo.
REV 21:17 Hhe zhao kunni chicun, yeshijiu qienxienni chicunghala danni nanjise 144 zhou wo.
REV 21:18 Danshi ishighala giesan wo, chenshishi gou antanghala giesan wo, gieghande boli niekielien wo.
REV 21:19 Danni jichui yanyanji boushighala dabalaghazho. Ji 1 gie jichushi ishi wo, ji 2 gieshi kugie boushi wo, ji 3 gieshi noghon manou wo, ji 4 gieshi noghon boushi wo,
REV 21:20 ji 5 gieshi hulan manou wo, ji 6 gieshi hulan boushi wo, ji 7 gieshi shira boushi wo, ji 8 gieshi noghon ishi wo, ji 9 gieshi shira ishi wo, ji 10 gieshi feicui wo, ji 11 gieshi zishei manou wo, ji 12 gieshi zishei shuijin wo.
REV 21:21 12 gie wijienshi 12 gie zhenzhughala giesan wo, nie wijienshi nie zhenzhu wo. Chenshini geidoushi gou antanghala giesan wo, gieghande boli niekielien wo.
REV 21:22 Bi chenshi sudoro dajien chanla dakushi Fugie Nenlitu Ezhan Hudaji ghoni ghughanshi chenshini dajien wo.
REV 21:23 Chenshide naran, sarani gonni ulie kerekushi Hudai fama zhouizho, ghoni ghughanshi chenshini zhula wo.
REV 21:24 Gojiala hhe gon dunda yone. Zemin jieredu honshanla famanine deilazhi hhe chenshide echine.
REV 21:25 Chenshini wijienyi izhi ulie khane, hhende xieni uwo.
REV 21:26 Kunla gojialani fama, zhiguini deilazhi hhende echine.
REV 21:27 Jien ganjin witu, pse hanzhan gieghachen, ghudan kieliechenlai hhende ulie oroghane. Zinie ghoni ghughanyi aminni jilasan benzi jiere nierei jilasanlai oroghane.
REV 22:1 Qienxien pse made nie amin winetu moronni uzheghazho, gieghande shuijinni xianli. Huda, ghoni ghughanyi baozose usuru khizhezhi
REV 22:2 chenshini geidou dundase daozho. Moron lianmiende aminni mutun wine. 12 yan alima soune, nie sara 1 hui soune. Mutun lachen gojialai goudaghane.
REV 22:3 Kharasanla pse uwo. Chenshide Huda, ghoni ghughanyi baozo wine. Hhei hojila hhei beii
REV 22:4 hhei ungiei chanlane. Hhei niere hhelai manlou jiere wine.
REV 22:5 Pse xieni uwo, zhula, naranyi gonyi ulie kerene. Ezhan Hudai gon hhelai zhouizho. Hhela chanqi izhi honshan danlane.
REV 22:6 Qienxien pse made kieliewo, "Enezighan kielienshi kekao, zhenni wo. Ruhherghala xienzhilai zhughei gojiolughasan Ezhan Huda qienxienne peizhi deigo fashen giene giesan shiqinni hojiladene mejieghawo."
REV 22:7 "Uzhe, bi deigo irene. Jien ene shude melieshi kieliesei zunjisanlade fuqi wine!"
REV 22:8 Enezighan shiqinshi bi, Yaheiya sonosuzhi chanlasan wo. Bi sonosuzhi chanlase enezighanni made uzheghasan qienxienni kon konde papaladene hhei beiine giese
REV 22:9 hhe made kieliewo, "Ulie olune! Chi Hudai beii. Bishi chi, xienzhila, jiushi chii gaijiula, pse ene shude melieshi kieliesei zunjisanlare hhantu hoji danlasan wo."
REV 22:10 Hhe pse made kieliewo, "Ene shude melieshi kieliesei bu fenji. Shihou chadashiwo.
REV 22:11 Gou witu kun gou wini giegha, zannantu kun zannanni giegha, gou kun gouni giegha, zhiguitu kun zhiguini giegha."
REV 22:12 Ersa kieliewo, "Uzhe, bi deigo irene! Jianli ogiku, faiku made wo, jien kun giesanzhe bi kharulune.
REV 22:13 Bishi Alafa wo, Emeiga wo. Bishi zui melieshiku wo, zui kuinashiku wo, keitou wo, baraku wo."
REV 22:14 Goya jienne waghazhi arughasanlade fuqi wine. Qienli bizhi aminni mutunyi hhende echine, wijiense chenshideye oro shidane.
REV 22:15 Nogheila, fashu shuaichen, lon kijiechen, kun alachen, nigiedai beiichen, pse soyuji ghudan kieliekude xiqi bichen, jiani giechenla man chenshi ghadane wo.
REV 22:16 "Bi, Ersa jiohuilade oluzhi qienxienne peizhi enezighan shiqinyi tande ganzhen beighane. Bishi Dawudeni houdei wo, eqiemaghaku gieghan hodun wo."
REV 22:17 Shenlin shini biereighala, "Ire." giezhi kieliezho. Sonosusanlaye, "Ire." giezhi kielie. Undasusan kunla man ire. Duran bichen kunla man aminni usui belien jienlie.
REV 22:18 Bi ene shude melieshi kieliesei soyuji sonosusanlade jingao gieye. Kien ene melieshi kieliesande jiaise Huda ene shude huaisan zeinanni hhei jiere ireghane.
REV 22:19 Ene shude melieshi kieliesei kien widaghase Huda ene shude huaisan aminni mutun, pse zhiguitu chenshide hhei bisan guzini widaghane.
REV 22:20 Ene shiqinlade ganzhen beisan kieliezho, "Enbene, bi deigo irene." Amine! Ezhan Ersaya, ire!
REV 22:21 Ezhan Ersani nenjien shentulare man hhantu bi gie. Amine!
